Bhṛgusaṃhitā

atha prathamo adhyāyaḥ

śrīyainamaḥ śrīrāmacandrāyanamaḥ śrīmadvikhanasamahāguravenamaḥ śrīmadbhyobhṛgumarīcyatrikaśyapebhyonamaḥ prakīrṇādhikāraḥ athaprathamo adhyāyaḥ

śrautasmārtādikaṅkarma nikhilaṃyenasūtritam ।
tasmaisamastavedārthavide vikhanasenamaḥ ।।

śrutismṛtinadīpūrṇaṃ śāstrakallolasaṃkulam ।
viṣṇubhaktyudakaṃśuddhaṃ vandevaikhānasārṇavam ।।

ṛṣipraśyottaram

ṛṣaya ūcuḥ-
brahmaputramuniśreṣṭha namastedehināṃvara ।
tvamevasarvavettāsitvamevavadatāṃvaraḥ ।।

tatojñātuṃhiviṣṇorvai bhūparīkṣādiṣukramam ।
icchāmastvatprasādena dīnāśśiṣyajanāḥprabho ।।

vistārajñohisarveṣāṃ vistarādvaktumarhasi ।
kenamārgeṇakairmantraiḥkaṃ devaṃpūjayannaraḥ ।।

kānlokānsamavāpnoti tattvametadvadasvanaḥ ।
bhṛguruvāca-
praṇamyadevadeveśaṃ cakrapāṇiṃkhaḍgadhvajam ।।

vistāreṇapravakṣyāmi śruṇudhvaṃsusamāhitāḥ ।
muhūrtavicāraḥ
sarvāraṃbhepraśastaṃsyād ādityecottarasthate ।।

apraśastamitikhyāta mayanedakṣiṇetathā ।
puṣyamāsādiṣaṇmāsā devānāntudivāsmṛtāḥ ।।

yasminmāsekṛtaṃsarvaṃ vivṛddhyarthamitismṛtam ।
rātrirāṣāḍamāsādi rayuktassarvakarmasu ।।

prathamācadvitīyāca tṛtīyāpañcamītathā ।
ṣaṣṭhīcasaptamīcāpi daśamyekādaśītathā ।।

trayodaśīcatithayaḥ paurṇamāsīśubhāssmatāḥ ।
prājāpatyāśvayukcaumya tiṣyapauṣṇatriruttarāḥ ।।

maitrādityamaghāsvātī hastāścaśravaṇaṃśubhāḥ ।
rāśayaścaravarjyās syurubhītacchobhanaṃsthiram ।।

gurubhārgavasaumyendu vārāśśreṣṭhatamāsmṛtā ।
eṣāmaṃśaścadrekkāṇahorādarśanamiṣyate ।।

eṣāmevodayaṃśastaṃ tatrasomodayaṃvinā ।
krūrecatuṣyanakṣatre vyādhipīḍāṃkarotihi ।।

sūryasauriścasaumyaścatriṣaḍāyasthitāśśubhāḥ । tadhaivalagnagāḥkuryur vyādhiśokabhayānitu।।

aṣṭamasthāgrahāssarve kartuḥkurvantidusthitim ।
ekādaśagatāssarve kṣemārogyakarāsmṛtāḥ ।।

bhayakṛdbhārgavaḥproktodvisaptadaśamasthitaḥ ।
dvisaptapañcanavama sthitojīvassuśobhanaḥ ।।

rāṣṭrasyayajamānasya mahatsaukhyaṅkarotihi ।
sūryavāreśubhoviṣṇu hastapauṣṇatriruttarāḥ ।।

mandavāreśubhauproktā brāhmasvātyaucatattathā ।
varjayedbudhavāreṇa hastamāśvayujantathā ।।

guruvāreṇa varjyautu tathāsaumyottarā ubhau ।
śravaṇañcaivapuṣyañca śukravāreṇavarjayet ।।

uttarāṣāḍhānakṣatraṃ somavāretu śobhanam ।
dvitīyābudhayuktāca ṣaṣṭhījīvasamāyutā ।।

soma ekāvaśīyuktaḥ karotiprāṇasaṃśayam ।
pauṣṇastusaptamīyukto dahatyagnirivaprajāḥ ।।

kāṇastūṇāndhanakṣatra guruviṣīrvivarjayet ।
bhūmikaṃpediśāndāhe durdinecaṇḍamārute ।।

aśanidhvaniyogeca ninditandivasaṃsmṛtaṃ ।
ayaneviṣuvecaiva saṃtyājaṅgrahaṇītathā ।।

ṣaḍaśītimughevāpi kṛtaṃvāstuvinaśyati ।
evaṃparīkṣyakartavya miccheccecchreya ātmanaḥ ।।

karṇādipratiṣṭhāntaṃ karmakuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ ।
athabhūmiṃparīkṣyaiva pūrvaṅkarṣaṇamārabhet ।।

bhūparīkṣā
śvetātubrāhmaṇībhūmī daktātu kṣatriyātathā ।
pītātuvaiśyākṛṣṇātu śūdrābhūmirudāhṛtā ।।

mokṣadābrāhmaṇīproktā kṣatriyāvijayapradā ।
vaiśyātudhanadābhūmi śśūdrāputrasamṛddhidā ।।

pratilomādibhirjuṣṭāṃ valmīkāḍhyañcavarjayet ।
hastamātraṅkhanitvātu pūrayet tattupāṃsunā ।।

adhikepuṣkalābhūmir nyūnevarjyāsamesamā ।
guptantrirātreṃ'kurati grāhyabhūmistunānyathā ।।

padmaṅkuṃbhasthatoyena pūritetatkṛtāvale ।
mukhyaṃpradakṣiṇāvarta mudakaṃśāstabudbudaḥ ।।

savyāvartantathāneṣṭa mudakaṃbahubudbudaḥ ।
uttānapadmakaṅgrāhyaṃ natvadhomukhapadmakam ।।

evaṃparīkṣyagṛhṇīyātpuṇyāhamapivācayet ।
evaṃparīkṣyabahudhā kuryātkarṣaṇamuttamam ।।

karṣaṇam
śvetau vākapilau vātha nāṅgaṅaīnauvṛṣautathā ।
athavānānyavarṇau vā arogaubalaśālinau ।।

kṣīravṛkṣayugaṃbaddhvā śamīvṛkṣayutantathā ।
asanaṅkhadiraṃvātha halaṅkṛtvāsanehakaṃ ।।

yantrayitvāyugenātha govālakṛtarajjunā ।
tasyapaścimadeśetu prapāṅkṛtvāvidhānataḥ ।।

dhānyapīṭhānikṛtvaiva trivedisahitaṅkramāt ।
purvandeveśamabhyarcya cakraṃpaścātsamarcayet ।।

viṣvakcenañcagaruḍaṃ samabhyarcyanivedayet ।
vāstuyajñañcahutvātu puṇyāhamapivācayet ।।

toyadhārāṃpuraskṛtya prādakṣiṇyavaśenatu ।
acāryo ahatavastreṇa cottarīyāṅgulīyakai ।।

alaṅkṛtyavidhānena śvetamālyānulepanaiḥ । samādāyavṛṣantatra "tvaṃvṛṣabha'' itibruvan।।

vṛṣabhandakṣiṇeyojya"saurabheya'' itibruvan ।
tatassaṃyojayetpaścād balīvardaibalānvitā ।।

"yugaṃyugaśruṅgam'' itiyojayeccahalaṃpunaḥ ।
"ṛṣiṅgṛhṇā'' mitimantreṇa ṛṣiṃsamyak pragṛhyaca ।।

"viṣṇurmāṃrakṣa''tvitica svātmarakṣāṃsamācaret ।
"ye asmindeśejīvanta'' ityāśritāṃścavisarjayet ।।

"halakṛṣṭe''timantreṇa dārayettāmilāṃśubhām ।
karṣayedvaiṣṇavairmantraiḥ prāgudakpṛvaṇāṃmahīm ।।

tataḥkarṣakamāhūya sarvatraivatukarṣayet ।
ayāryaṃpūjayitvātu tathaivasahalauvṛṣau ।।

prathamaṅkarṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā dvitīyaṃ karṣaṇañcaret ।
bījaṃsarvaṃsamādāya prokṣaṇaiḥprākṣaṇañcaret ।।

"imebījāḥpraro''heti saptagrāmyāṇyataḥparam ।
vāpayitvātubījāni "devitvayi'' samuccaran ।।

"duhatāṃuhadiva'' mityuktvāto yantatrasamarpayet ।
rakṣāṃsamyagvidhāyātra cācāryamabhipūjayet ।।

"sasyā'' imetimantreṇa sasyaṃpakvaṃpraṇamyaca ।
viṣvakcenādibhirmantraiśśāntañcāpisamarcayet ।।
"śuddhā'' imetimantreṇa gobhyassamyaṅnivedayet ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre prathamo adhyāyaḥ

atha dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ

athadvitīyo adhyāyaḥ 
śaṅkusthāpanam
ataḥparaṃpravakṣyāmi śaṅkusthāpanamuttamam ।
meṣantathaivavṛṣabhaṅgate sūryedinetathā ।।

kṛtvāsamatalāṃbhūmiṃ gomayenatulevayet ।
tadbahibhrāmayetsū tradvayantenai vamānataḥ ।।

prācīsādhanam
pūrvāhṇecāparāhṇeca śaṅkuchāyāntulāñchayet ।
tatassūtratrayaṃvāthapāti yecchaṅkumathyame ।।

bhrāmayedadhiker'ṣantu nyūnetāvadvivardhayet ।
prācīntatsūtramānena madhyamenai vakalbayet ।।

udaksūtraṃbhavettatra kṛtvātucaturaśrakam ।
pañcagavyenasaṃprokṣya puṇyāhamapivācayet ।।

vāstupada devatāpūjanam
ekāśītipadānkṛtvāvāstu devānprapūjayet ।
īśānādi samabhyarcya dvātriṃśatbadabhāginaḥ ।।

īśānañcaivaparjanyaṃ jayastañcamahendrakam ।
ādityaṃsatyakaṃbhṛśamanta rikṣañcapūrvagān ।।

agniḥpūṣācavitatha grahākṣatayamāstathā ।
gantharvobhṛṅgarājarṣī dakṣiṇepadadevatāḥ ।।

paścimenir ṛtiścaiva dauvārikastathaivaca ।
sugrīvaḥpuṣpadantaśca varuṇaścāsurastathā ।।

śoṣaṇaścaivarāgaścate cāṣṭaukadhitāssurāḥ ।
uttarejavanonāga mukhyaubhallāṭa evaca ।।

somor'galo aditiścaiva sūridevastathaivaca ।
brahmānavapadaṃbhuṅkai vāstumadhyeviśeṣataḥ ।।

aryamādaṇḍa bhṛccaivapāśabhṛddhanadastathā ।
brahmaṇaścacaturdikṣu sthitāṣṣaṭpadabhāginaḥ ।।

apaścaivāpavatsaśca savitāsāvitra evaca ।
indraścaivatathendrājo rudrorudrāja evaca ।।

etedvipadabhoktāro vidikṣaṣṭausthitāssurāḥ ।
carakīdevatāriśca pūtanāpāparākṣasī ।।

īśānādiṣukoṇeṣu bāhyasthāḥpadavarjitāḥ ।
evaṃ vinyasyadevāṃntu vāstu devaṃ prakalpayet ।।

vāstupuruṣalakṣaṇam-pūjā
vāstunaśśira īśānepādau nairṛtikecaret ।
hastausaritpataujñeyāvagnau bāhurudāhṛtaḥ ।।

apikaṇṭhaitiproktaṃ hṛdayañcāpavatsake ।
nābhirbrahmaṇisaṃkhyātā kukṣassavitṛsaṃjñake ।।

indraindrājake guhyamūrumūlevidhānataḥ ।
pārśvantudakṣiṇaṃ proktaṃvāmamevaṃ prakalpayet ।।

śetevāstubhuvaṃ prāpyavāstudevastvadhomukhaḥ ।
puṇyāhaṃvācayitvātu prokṣaṇaiḥprokṣaṇañcaret ।।

puṣpairgandhaistathādhūpairdī paiścāpiprapūjayet ।
namaskāraiścasaṃyuktaiḥ praṇavādyaissvanāmabhiḥ ।।

śalyaparīkṣā pūjanāntespṛśetkartā yamaṅgantannirīkṣayet ।
vāstudehe apitatraivaśalyaṃ brūyādyathārthataḥ ।।

astiśalyaṃśirassparśe taddhastadvayamānataḥ ।
kaṇṭhasparśegalecaiva hastamātresamādiśet ।।

upasparśāttribhirhāstai śśruṅkhalāśalyamādiśet ।
hastamātraikarasparśāt khaṭyāpādaṃsamādiśet ।।

bahusaṃsparśanātkartu raṅgārastutrihastataḥ ।
gulbhaisarpādibhirduṣṭaṃ vitastidvayamānataḥ ।।

pādekaṇṭakamityuktaṃ ṣaḍvitastipramāṇataḥ ।
kaniṣṭhāṅguṣṭhayosspṛrśāddhastantatrasamācaret ।।

vyayādhikecaturhāste jānusparśāttataḥparam ।
śalyaṃviśodhyabhūmintāṃ talaṅkṛtvāsamānataḥ ।।

pañcagavyenasaṃprokṣya vāstudevānprapūjayet ।
vāstudevatābaliḥ
droṇandroṇārthakaṃvāpitaṇḍulānpācayettataḥ ।।

dadhiguḍājyasaṃyuktaṃ sarveṣāñcabalindadet ।
brahmadīnāṃnamostaṃvā svāhāstaṃvābalirbhavet ।।
kṛtvātu balidānañca puṇyāhamapivācayet ।।
itiśrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre dvitīyo adhyāyaḥ

atha tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ

atha tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ 
vimānabhedāḥ
athavinyāsarūpāṇi pravakṣanteyathākramam ।
śrīvatsaṃprathamaṃproktaṃ nandyāvartandvitīyakam ।।

tṛtīyaṃsvastikaṃvindyāccaturthaṃbhadrakaṃsmṛtam ।
daṇḍakaṃpañcamantvāhur vedikaṃṣaṣṭhamucyate ।।

kuṃbhakaṃsaptamaṃvindyā daṣṭamaṃpadmakantathā ।
navamaṃsyādrathapadaṃ daśamantuprakīrṇakam ।।

eteṣāmākṛtiṃvakṣye yathāvadanupūrvaśaḥ ।
nyatradaṇḍakātsarvaṃ bahirvīdhīsamanvitam ।।

tasyacāstagantaiścihnaiśśrīvatsādyaṃvidhīyate ।
ekaprācīnavīdhīka mudīcīnānyavīthikam ।।

śrīvatsamitivijñeyaṃ sarvavidyāsamaṃmatam ।
madhyekoṇaṃ caturdvāraṃ prāgīśādipradakṣiṇam ।।

tannigantojavīthīkaṃ nandyāvartamitismṛtam ।
svastikantvojavīthyantaṃ bhadraṃmadhyapratolikam ।।

ekaprācīnakandaṇḍaṃ caturaśrantuvedikam ।
vṛttaṅkuṃbhakamuddiṣṭaṃ padmakaṃsyāddvivedikam ।।

brahmakośāṣṭakadvāravīthīrathapadākṛtiḥ ।
prāgudakpravaṇañcaiva prakīrṇakamudāhṛtam ।।

dvidvāraṃvācatudvānraṃ manastoyuktitobhavet ।
ayuktadvāradevasya bhajanaṃnābhidhīyate ।।

daṇḍakastenamānena yonigrahaṇamucyate ।
śarīramaṅgaṃpratyaṅgaṃ jñātvāyoniṃprakalpayet ।।

grāmaṃśarīramaṅgaṃssyād devadvijaparigraham ।
pratyaṅgamaṅgaṃsaṃvṛttaṃ vimānabhavanādikam ।।

daṇḍenapūrvayorvādaṃ hastenānyatradhīyate ।
daṇḍevistāramāyāma mekaikaṅguṇayettribhiḥ ।।

ekaikaṃṣaṣṭibhihintvā śiṣṭaṃyoniṃsamādiśet ।
hastenadvayasaṃsarge triguṇaṃvasubhihanret ।।

śeṣaṃyoniṃvijāniyāddhvajadhūmādikaṅkramāt ।
sarvatrakalpayedyoniṃ tayorvargaphalenavā ।।

yonermahādiśāśreṣṭhā divisaptatrigahintā ।
pravīṇañcaturaśraṃsyāc ceṣāṇāmāyataṃviduḥ ।।

aṣṭaṣaṭcaturaṃśāssyu ritareṣāṃyathākramam ।
evamāyāmayogastu pratyaṅgasyaivakalpayet ।।

aṅgedviguṇamāyāmaṃ pādanyūnamadhādhikam ।
ardhaṃnavāhayennyūna madhikantuvidhīyate ।।

ātmāvāstuśarīrasya vistārādadhikaṃviduḥ ।
pādāyāmaśikhāvāpi dviguṇaṃvāviśeṣataḥ ।।

samaṃvāsarvataḥkuryāc carīrandaṇḍakādṛte ।
vardhayedadhikāyāmaṃ daṇḍaṣoḍaśakenavā ।।

daṇḍe aṣṭaguṇaṅkuryā dāyāmaṃyuktito athavā ।
aṅgamāgamavistāro daṇḍabhedo apiyojyate ।।

anyatradaṇḍanechindyāccareṣutuviśeṣataḥ ।
pātaṃvistārasūtreṣu vidussūtradvaye apivā ।।

kaṇṭhasūtradvayevāpi pratyaṅgenaiva kārayet ।
vidhibhedantukartavyaṃ brahmabhāgeviśeṣataḥ ।।
evaṅkrameṇa śāstrajñaśśarīraṃ saṃprakalpayet ।।
viṣṇusthāpanam
sahasrabhūsurādūrdhve brahmāṃśevāyudeśake ।
pañcamūrtividhānena sthāpayitvā janārdhanam ।।

vaikhānasai mahābhāgair vaidikārcanatatparaiḥ ।
vedāntavedibhirviprairañcayet puruṣottamam ।।

śaṅkarādi sthāpanam īśāna īśvarañcaiva someśānāvathāpivā ।
paścimekeśavasthāna maiśānyāṃśaṅkarālayam ।।

anukalpaṃvikalpañca kalpañcaivatridhābhavet ।
bhūparīkṣādiyatkarma anukalpamitismṛtam ।।

devādīnāṃmunīnāñca kalpayettuvikalpakam ।
gabhenmṛdālayeyatra pratiṣṭhāyāntukalpakam ।।

evandeśaṃviniścitya mūlasthānañcanirdiśet ।
nirmite atravimānasyaco tsedhārthaṃsamantuvā ।।

jalāstaṃvāśilāntaṃ vākhānayeducitaṃsudhīḥ ।
vistārāyāmasīmāntādbāhyekhātvādṛḍhāyaca ।।

ekahastandvihastaṃvā trihastaṃvādhikaṅkramāt ।
vālukairviśvataḥpūrya dṛḍhīkaraṇamādiśet ।।

bālālayantuśaktānāmaśaktānāṃvinābhavet ।
dhruvārcāyāḥpratiṣṭhāce dbālāgāraṃnakalpayet ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre tṛtīyo adhyāyaḥ

atha caturtho adhyāyaḥ

athacaturtho adhyāyaḥ 
adyeṣṭakā sthāpanam
athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi vāstunaḥprathameṣṭakām ।
sādhayitvāpūrvarātrau catasraḥprathameṣṭakāḥ ।।

śilāyāṃmṛṇmayevātha kuryāllakṣaṇasaṃyutāḥ ।
śailādoṣavinirmuktās supakvā athamṛṇmayāḥ ।।

vistāreṇeṣṭakāḥproktā ṣaṭpañcacaturaṅgulāḥ ।
uttamādikriyādeva vistāradviguṇāyatāḥ ।।

vistārārthaṅghanaṃprokta miṣṭakānāṃpramāṇataḥ ।
ālayābhimukhecaiva prapāṅkṛtvāvicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

tanmadhyevedikāṅkṛtvā hastamātrapramāṇataḥ ।
vistārantatsamañcauna mutsethantutadardhakam ।।

sabhyāgniṃ vidhivatkṛtvātu vidhināghoramācaret ।
bhūmiyajñañcakṛtvātu kalaśaissaptabhiḥkramāt ।।

saṃsnāpyanavavastreṇa cācchādyaśayanopari ।
kautukaṃbandhayitvātu śayaneśāyayettataḥ ।।

hutvātupauruṣaṃsūktaṃ viṣṇusūktamataḥparam ।
caturvedādimantrāṃśca śrībhūsūkteyajetkramāt ।।

iṣṭakāvāśilāvātha tannāmādyakṣaraṃsmaret ।
nṛttaigenyaiścavādyaiścarātriśeṣaṃnayetkramāt ।।

prabhātepūjayetpūrvamācāryaṃśilpibhissaha ।
ācāryomantrayogyastu śilpibhiḥkarmayogyakaiḥ ।।

dvārasyadakṣiṇepāśenvsthānamasyapraśasyate ।
sumuhūrtenyasedvidvāniṣṭakāṃścaturaḥkramāt ।।

vinyāsetucaturdikṣu caturvedādimastrataḥ ।
teṣāṃmadhyetadāgarte pūrayedudakenatu ।।

tatraivanavaratnāni vilyasedanupūrvaśaḥ ।
gabhannyāsavidhiḥ
athavakṣyeviśeṣeṇa gabhannyāsavidhikramam ।।

prāsādogabhansaṃyuktaḥ kurutesarvasaṃpadam ।
tasmādādauprakartavyaḥ gabhannyāsassamṛddhidaḥ ।।

trayaḥprāsādamūlesyāt pūrvantuprathameṣṭake ।
upānoparimadhyaṃsyāt prateruparicāntataḥ ।।

bhūgataṃśūdrajātīnā mupānenṛpavaiśyayoḥ ।
praterupariviprāṇā mānulomyenakārayet ।।

sarveṣāṃbhūgataṅkāryaṃ sarvasiddhikaraṃśubham ।
aindrapāvakayormadhye prāgdvāreṣuprakalpayet ।।

dvārasyadakṣiṇekuryātpaścimaipitadhaivahi ।
kavāṭārgalayogevānya stavyaṅgabhanbhāyanam ।।

phelā
tathātāmramayīphelā sphāṭikāvāpraśasyate ।
pādaviṣkaṃbhavistārāṃ phelāntattvapadāñcitāṃ ।।

khaṇḍasphuṭitavajānysā ।
ghanaṃviṃśatibhāgaikaṃ tadardhārdhāṃśamevavā ।।

vistārasyacatubhāngaṃ koṣṭhabhittyucchrayaṃbhavet ।
uttamantusamotsedhaṃ tripādaṃmadhyamaṃsmṛtaṃ ।।

athamañcārdhamutsedhaṃ trividhantatpracakṣate ।
tribhāgaikavidhānaṃsyād dvibhāgaṃbhāgikaṃbhavet ।।

antarecāṃgulāyāmaṃ tadardhaṃbhinnattikam ।
saṃyogārdhavihīnaṃsyād vidhāne abhyantaretathā ।।

prakṣālyapañcagavyena viśuddhaṅgabhanbhājanam ।
ālayātpramukhecaiva maṇṭapesamalaṅkṛte ।।

gomayenopalipyaiva puṇyāhaṃvācayettataḥ ।
raktabījānidhātūṃśca sannyasenmastravittamaḥ ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃviṣṇusūktañca pauruṣaṃsūktamuccaran ।
"viṣṇuryoni'mityuktvātu gabhaṃntranidhāpayet ।।

itiśrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstrebhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre caturtho adhyāyaḥ

atha pañcamo adhyāyaḥ

prāsādalakṣaṇam
athavakṣyeviśeṣeṇa prāsādānāntulakṣaṇam ।
prasādaṅkuruteyena prāsādair atikīrtitam ।।

aṅgulabhedaḥ
trividhantusamākhyātamaṅgulaṃsyātpramāṇataḥ ।
mānāṅgulantuprathamaṃ mātrāṅgulamataḥparam ।।

tṛtīyantusamākhyātaṃ dehalabdhapramāṇataḥ ।
rathareṇvaṇuraṣṭābhirīkṣāyū kāyavāstathā ।।

kramaśo aṣṭakuṇairviddhi mānāṅgulamitismṛtam ।
madhyamāṅgulimadhyantu paryamātrāṅguliṃsmṛtam ।।

pratimāyāvibhāgena tālagaṇyena? bhājanam ।
aṅgulantu samākhyātaṃ dehalabdhapramāṇataḥ ।।

prāsādamaṇḍapānāñca mānāṅgulavidhānataḥ ।
yāgopakaraṇānāstu mātrāṅgulavidhānataḥ ।।

dehalabdhapramāṇena pratimāṅkārayettathā ।
aṅgulaiḥkiṣkurityuktaṃ caturviṃśatibhistathā ।।

pañcaviṃśatibhiścaiva prājāpatyamudāhṛtam ।
ṣaḍvintiśadhannurmuṣṭhi saptaviṃśaddhanugranhaḥ ।।

hastānāṃlakṣaṇaṃproktaṃ mānāṅgulavidhānataḥ ।
ekatalādikalpanam
trihastādisamārabhya navahastāntamevaca ।।

ayugmairathahastaistukuryādekatalaṃbudhaḥ ।
dvitalantutataḥkuryātsatrayodaśahastakaiḥ ।।

pañcādhikadaśaihanstaiprāsādassyāttribhūmikaḥ ।
talaṃpratyadhikaṅkuryāt ṣaḍḍhastantuviśeṣataḥ ।।

ādvādaśatalādevaṃ kuryādvistāramānakam ।
vistāradviguṇotsedha muttamantupracakṣate ।।

vistāraṃsaptadhākṛtvā dvādaśāṃśantumadhyamam ।
ekādaśāṃśamadhamaṃ vistāresaptadhākṛte ।।

ādvādaśatalādevamutsedhantuvidhīyate ।
prāṅmukhodaṅmukhaissūtraiḥ padaṅkuryāttuṣoḍhaśam ।।

gabhangehassamākhyāto madhyamantucatuṣpadam ।
bāhyatodvādaśapadaṃ bhittyarthamupakalpayet ।।

ṣaḍbhiṣṣaḍbhistadhāsūtraiḥ padānāṃpañcaviṃśatiḥ ।
navagabhangṛhaṃmathyebhittyarthaṃ śeṣamucyate ।।

trividhantusamākhyātaṃ? prāsādākṛtayastathā ।
nāgarandrāviḍañceti vesarañcatridhābhavet ।।

nthūpyantañcaturaśraṃsyān nāgaraṃsamudāhṛtam ।
kaṇṭhaprabhṛticāṣṭāśraṃ prāsādandrāviḍaṃbhavet ।।

kaṇṭhaprabhṛtivṛttaṃya dvesarantatpracakṣate ।
beraḥpūrvaṃsthitoyatra tatraberavaśādbhavet ।।

yāvadberantribhāgaikaṃ vistāraṃpīṭhamevahi ।
pīṭhasyatriguṇaṅgabhaṃn garbhārdhaṃbhittirucyate ।।

gabhangehatribhāgaikaṃ bhittiṃvātatrakārayet ।
agratomaṇḍapaṅkuryāt prāsādasamavistṛtam ।।

prāsādasya samāyāmaṃ daśāṃśaṃmukhamaṇḍapam ।
prāsādasyāgratodvāraṃ prakuryāllakṣaṇānvitam ।।

vrateruparisīmāntaṃ dvārasyotsedhaucyate ।
uttamandvāravistāramutsethārdhamudāhṛtam ।।

utsedhārdha daśāṃśena hīnaṃmadhyamamucyate ।
viṃśatyāparihīnaṃsyā dvistāramadhamaṃbhavet ।।

kāyañcāpyanukāyañca kuryādutsedhamānataḥ ।
bhāgamekamadhiṣṭhānamutse dhovasudhābhavet ।।

pādāyāmodvibhāgassyād bhāgaḥprastāraucyate ।
bhāgaḥkaṇṭhaitiproktaṃ dvibhāsaṃśikharaṃbhavet ।।

bhāgasthyūpiritikhyāta mevamutsedhaucyate ।
kāmamevaṃsamākhyāta manukāyamadhocyate ।।

kuryātprāsādavistāraṃ caturviṃśatibhāgikam ।
ekabhāgastuvistāraṃ bhāgamekantalantathā ।।

daśāṅgulaṃscāddvitale tritaledvādaśāṅgulam ।
yugāṅgulavivṛddhyātu kartavyaṃsyāttalaṃprati ।।

pādamasyatuviṣkaṃbha maṣṭabhāgaṃvihīnakam ।
staṃbhāgreṇaivagartavya manukāyapramāṇataḥ ।।

upānasyatuviṣkaṃbha magrepādadvayaṃbhavet ।
adhiṣṭhānantridhākṛtvā bhāgovaijagatībhavet ।।

kumudantudvitīyena bhāgenaivatukārayet ।
kṛtvāśeṣañcataṃbhānga mekāṃśainapaṭcaṭikām ।।

kuryātsārdhenakaṇṭhantu śeṣaṃvājinamucyate ।
pādabandhamitikhyātaṃ sarvakāryeṣupūjitam ।।

pratikramaṃvākartavya madhiṣṭhānapramāṇataḥ ।
jagatīntadvadevātha kumudaṃpṛttamucyate ।।

bhāgenapūrvavatkṛtvā caturthaṃśeṣamācaret ।
paṭṭikenaivakartavya megamastarikantathā ।।

dvābhyāṃpratimukhaṅkuryāt pratikramamidaṃbavet ।
adhiṣṭhānamitikhyātaṃ pādamānaṃpravakṣyate ।।

caturaśramathāṣṭāśraṃ vṛttañcaivatridhābhavet ।
kuṃbhayuktantathāke citkecitkuṃbhavihīnakam ।।

kaicidvaikuṃbhamaṇībhyāṃ yuktaṃpādaṃsmarantihi ।
vistāreṇasamaṃvāpi dviguṇaṃvāpimūlataḥ ।।

caturaśramadhohitvā vṛttamaṣṭāśramevavā ।
kartavyantuyadhāyukta mathavāṣoḍaśāśrakam ।।

pādānāmākṛtiḥproktā kuṃbhalakṣaṇamucyate ।
pādādhikamadhādhyarthaṃ pādonandviguṇantuvā ।।

dviguṇantusamutsedhaṃ pādaviṣkaṃbhamānataḥ ।
śrīkarañcandrakāstañca saumukhyaṃpriyadarśanam ।।

yathākrameṇanāmāni kartavyāniviśeṣataḥ ।
śrīkaraṃvṛttapādānāṃ kalāśrāṇāntathaivaca ।।

caṃndrakāntamathāṣṭāśraṃ somakhaṇḍamitismṛtam ।
atibhāreṣu staṃbheṣu priyadarśanamucyate ।।

kṛtvānavāṃśakaṅkuṃbhaṃ bhāgamekaṃhṛducyate ।
kuṃbhañcaturbhiraṃśaistu kaṇṭhabhāgamudāhṛtam ।।

āsyamekāṃśamityuktaṃ śeṣaṅkuryāddvidaṇḍam ।
ekenapadmakenaiva vṛttamekenavātathā ।।

vistṛtau staṃbhavistārau dviguṇaukuṃbhamucyate ।
adhyarthamāsyavistāraṃ hārodhāmūlapādavat? ।।

vistāramevamuktaṃsyānmaṇḍailankṣaṇamucyate ।
maṇḍaistripādamutsedhaṃ vistārantucatugunṇam ।।

tribhāgaikaṃbhavetpadmaṃ vetramekantathaivaca ।
bhāgāvāphalakārāmā vetrāvāpādarūpavat ।।

pādāgrakarmamānena skandhaṅkuryādvidhānataḥ ।
staṃbhāgrasamavistāraṃ vīrakāntantripādataḥ ।।

tadūrdhvepādatāṅkuryādvistāraṃpādavistṛtam ।
samantripādamardhaṃvā bodhikotsedhaucyate ।।

tridaṇḍamadhamāyāme caturdaṇḍantumadhyamam ।
uttamaṃpañcadaṇḍaṃsyā dbodhikotsedhaucyate ।।

jagatyantekumudānte paṭṭikānte athavāpunaḥ ।
jalaniryāṇamāgaṃnca nālaniganmanaṅkriyāt ।।

haṃsapādantripādaṃvā vitastirvāviśeṣataḥ ।
pratebānhyaviniṣkrāntyā nālīṃśailamayīntathā ।।

gajoṣṭhasadṛśākārāṃ siṃhākṛtimukhottarām ।
bhūtasiṃhopamāmūrdhvasāravārādhikārayet ।।

dvidaṇḍañcatridaṇḍaṃvā gabhangehetuveśmanaḥ ।
berodayasamaṃvātha dviguṇaṃvādhyarthamevavā ।।

praṇālamūlavistāraṃ tribhāgaikāgravistaram ।
vyāsatribhāgaṃbhāgonaṃ bahulantutribhāgabhām ।।

vārisaṃcāragaṃbhīratāraṃ jhajhanralakṣaṇam ।
animnonnatamābhitte stadātyaśraṅkramānnatam ।।

sarvavādyasamāyuktaṃ tadāmaṅgalavācakaiḥ ।
vāstuhomantataḥkṛtvā ācāryavūjayettataḥ ।।

śilpinaṃpūjayetpaścātsumuhūrtesulagnake ।
ācāryassuprasannātmā vāruṇaṃsūktamuccaret ।।

takṣakasthsāpayennālīṃ susnigdhāṃsudṛḍhāṅkramāt ।
beraprāsādagabhansya yāvattālasyacāvadhi ।।

dhārāntukevalaṅkuryād bhittautālasyadhīmataḥ? ।
śreṣṭhamadhyakaniṣṭhāni berasyasthāpanantridhā ।।

dhārādalasamāptautu sthāpanañcottamaṃbhavet ।
dvārabandhasyapūrvetu sthāpanaṃmadhyamaṃbhavet ।।

mūrdhopalasyapūrvetu sthāpanaṃsyātkanīyasam ।
yaḥkarotyanyathācāsmā dabhicārāyacaivahi ।।

evaṃnālañcasaṃsthāpya prastarañcottarādikam ।
viṣkaṃbhaṃpādavistāra mutsedhantrividhaṃbhavet ।।

uttamantusamotsedhaṃ tripādaṃmadhyamaṃbhavet ।
adhamañcārdhamutsedha muttamaṃsyādvidhānataḥ ।।

staṃbhāgraikatribhāgaikaṃ tasyordhvepaṭṭikābhavet ।
tatsamaṃniganmaṃproktaṃ paṭṭikālakṣaṇantvidam ।।

dvibhāgenatadūrdhvetu kartavyaṃpadmapaṭṭikam ।
dvidaṇḍantukapotaṃsyā dupānasamaniganmam ।।

śeṣaṃprastāramānantu kartavyaṃpañcabhāgikam ।
ekenapaṭṭikāṅkuryāt kaṇṭhamekenakārayet ।।

dvābhyāntadūrdhve kartavyamekāṃśenatupaṭṭikām ।
evaṃprastāramākhyātaṃ toraṇaṃvakṣyate athunā ।।

pāśvanyoḥpṛṣṭhataścāpi kartavyanto raṇantathā ।
prateruttarasīmānte toraṇasyāśrayobhavet ।।

vistārantutadardhaṃsyā dvistāraṃpañcabhāgikam ।
makarāṃśantriyaṃśena śeṣaṃpādamitismṛtam ।।

pādāntarāgramadhavāvistārantoraṇasyatu ।
pūrvoktamevakartavyaṃ makarāṃśapramāṇataḥ ।।

pramāṇanto raṇasyoktaṃ nāsikāyāstulakṣaṇam ।
vakṣyatetupramāṇena yathāśāstraviniścitam ।।

gabhangehārdhavistāraṃ mahānāsītikīrtyate ।
niganmantutadardhaṃsyāt tripādaṃsamamevacā ।।

śikhareṣu caturdhikṣu kuryādekāntunāsikām ।
vistārantutadardhaṃsyātka poteṣvaṣṭanāsikāḥ ।।

kūṭasyalakṣaṇaṃproktaṃ kūṭaśālaṃvidhīyate ।
kṛtvāprāsādaṣaḍbhāgamekabhāgaṃvidhīyate ।।

bhāgenakūṭaśālaṃ syādbhāgārdhaṃpañcamaṃbhavet ।
caturguṇaṃbhavetkūyaṃ śālāsyādgopurākṛtiḥ ।।

śālāvistāramānena pāśvanyonānsikābhavet ।
ekanāsikayāyuktaṃ pañjaraṃsamudāhṛtam ।।

tataḥkaṇṭhārdhamānena śikharaṃvardhayettataḥ ।
kaṇṭhāddvidaṇḍamityuktaṃ śikharasyatuniganmam ।।

niganmādvartanādbāhye vardhanantutadardhakam ।
sthūpiṅkubhasamāyuktaṃ kuryāddaṇḍaṃvidhānataḥ ।।

vistārantatpramāṇena śikharantatracocyataṃ ।
tadūrdhvekaṇṭhamityuktaṃ phalakācatadūrdhvataḥ ।।

krameṇakṛśatāṃ kuryādyānadantastumākṣmataḥ

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre pañcamo adhyāyaḥ

atha ṣaṣṭho adhyāyaḥ

athaṣaṣṭho adhyāyaḥ 
mūdhenṣṭakāvidhiḥ
athavakṣyeviśeṣeṇa kramaṃmūrdheṣṭakāvidheḥ ।
pramukheyāgaśālāñca kṛtvācaivavicakṣaṇa ।।

madhyevediṃprakalpyaiva sthūpikīlapramāṇataḥ ।
sabhyaṃprakalpyacaprācyā māghāraṃvidhivadyajet ।।

vedimadhyenyasedvidvān susnigdhānirvraṇādṛḍhāḥ ।
vaiṣṇavañcajapitvaivacatasraśceṣṭakāḥkramāt ।।

kiñcidagraṃbhavennimnaṃ mūlevaikiñcidunnatam ।
adhobhāgebhavetpṛṣṭa mūrdhvabhāgemukhaṃbhavet ।।

śālipiṣṭamayenātha lekhayedakṣarāṇitu ।
yakāraṃpūrvatolekhya rakārandakṣiṇenyaset ।।

lakāraṃpaścimelekhyavakāre cottarelikhet ।
lohajāndārujāṃvātha sthūpintatranyasedbudhaḥ ।।

pādāyāmasamandīghaṃn vistāraṃpādasammitam ।
agramaṅgulavistāra mānupūrvyātkṛśantathā ।।

caturaśraṃbhavenmūlaṃ tribhāgai kaṃsamaṃyathā ।
vṛttantadūrdhvataḥkuryāc chīlīpādamadhonyaset ।।

vistāratriguṇāyāmaṃ vistārasamavistaraṃ ।
taddvayenasamāyojya namaṃśūlaṃsthitaṃyadhā ।।

pañcagavyaissamabhyukṣya puṇyāhamapivācayet ।
vāstujomañcahutvaiva paryagnikaraṇañcaret ।।

mūrdheṣṭakāvidhānena homaṅkṛtvāvicakṣaṇaḥ ।
punaḥprabhātedharmātmā yajamānayutoguruḥ ।।

śilādīn saṃpragṛhyaiva vimāneropayettadhā ।
pāṇibhyāṃsaṃpragṛhyaiva prāṅmukhodaṅmukho apivā ।।

caturvedādimantraiśca śilā indrādiṣunyaset ।
dhruvasūktañjapitvātu mathyesthūpiṃnyasettadhā ।।

kāleśilpinamāhūya pūjayitvā viśeṣataḥ ।
śilādyuparivinyasya dṛḍhīkaraṇamācaret ।।

pādabandhegalecaiva vimāne paritaḥkramāt vimānadevāḥ ।
prācyāṃ viṣṇuṃ prakurvīta yasya garbhagṛhesthitiḥ ।।

dakṣiṇesatyamūrtestu paścimecā cyutasya ca ।
uttarecāniruddhasya sthitimevaṃ prakalpayet ।।

galepuruṣamūrtistu dakṣiṇe nārasiṃhakaḥ ।
paścime tu varāhaśca hayagrīvastathottare ।।

sukhasanasamāluktaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam ।
vyāloddhvakoṇakañcaiva vīśaṃ vātha mṛgeśvaram ।।

vakratuṇḍaṃ ca durgāṃ cāpyagramaṇḍapabhittiṣu ।
sthitamevaṃ susaṃsthāpya yathālābhaṃ samarcayet ।।

dvāreṣu dvārapālānāṃ sthitimevaṃ prakalpayet ।
prāsādalakṣaṇaṃproktaṃ maṇḍapānāmathocyate ।।

staṃbhaiṣṣoḍaśabhiryuktaṃ maṇḍapaṃ śrīpratiṣṭhitam ।
dvādaśastaṃbhasaṃyuktaṃ bījāsanamiti smṛtam ।।

dvātriṃśadgātrasaṃyuktaṃ jayabhadretikīrtyate ।
ṣaṭtriṃśadgātrasaṃyuktaṃ nandyāvartaṃ suśobhanam ।।

caturbhiṣṣaṣṭibhistsaṃbhair yuktaṃśrībhadrakaṃ smṛtam ।
staṃbhānāṃ tu śatairyuktaṃ viśālamiti saṃjñitam ।।

prāsādavatsamākhyātaṃ prastāraṃ tatpramāṇataḥ ।
vājinopari kartavyaṃ dhārakastu kalāstathā ।।

staṃbhaviṣkaṃbhamutsedhaṃ caturbhāgenavistṛtam ।
tulāvistāramānena jayantīsyātsamonnatā ।।

tato daṇḍārdhabāhulya manumārgaṃ tadūrdhvataḥ ।
iṣṭakābhistadūrdhvaṃ tu chādayedgala kānvitam ।।

pādādhikamadhādhyardhaṃ dviguṇaṃ pādahīnakam ।
caturvidhamathāyāmaṃ kartavyaṃ maṇḍapasyatu ।।

āyāme tu yathāyuktaṃ staṃbhānāṃ vidhirucyate ।
dvihastaṃ vātrihastaṃ vā caturhastamathāpivā ।।

staṃbhāntaraṃ prakartavyaṃ yathāyukti viśeṣataḥ ।
evaṅkramātsamākhyātaṃ prākāramadhunocyate ।।

pākāraṃ paritaḥ kuryāt prāsādasya pramāṇataḥ ।
prākārasyatuvistāraṃ tasyadaṇḍamihocyate ।।

antarmaṇḍalamityāhu radhyardhaṃ daṇḍamānataḥ ।
antarbhāramitiprostaṃ madhyabhāraṃ dvidaṇḍata ।।

caturdaṇḍapramāṇena yuktā maryādabhittikā ।
mahāmaryādabhittissyātsaptadaṇḍapramāṇataḥ ।।

adhyardhadviguṇaṃ vāpi triguṇaṃ vā caturguṇam ।
mukhāyāmamiti proktaṃ prākārāṇāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

kapotā ntaṃsamutsedhaṃ bhittihastapramāṇataḥ ।
kūṭaśālāyutaṃ vāpi kuryātprākārasaṃyutam ।।

mūlajaṃ tu talotsedhaṃ hastamevaṃ vidhīyate ।
yathālābhonnataṃ vāpi pradhamāvaraṇaṃ smṛtam ।।

ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ kramātkuryānnyūnaprākārakaṃviduḥ ।
jalaniryāṇamārgaṃ syātpadānte taṭake apivā ।।

pradhamāvaraṇadvāraṃ pramukhekalpayettathā ।
dvitīyāvaraṇadvāro vyastaśchennāstidūṣaṇam ।।

vimānotsedhaturyaṃ vā podonaṃ cārthameva vā ।
pṛdhaggopurasaṃyukta mucchritaṃ tu samantuvā ।।

pañcaprākāramityevaṃ triprākāramathāpivā ।
triprākāreṣaḍaṅgulyaṃ tridhādhastalanimnagam ।।

prākārehucchrayaṃ vindyātkapotāntaṃ taduttamam ।
madhyamaṃ cotkarāntena kalaśāntaṃ tathādhamam ।।

evaṃ prākārasaṃgena tūtsedhaṃ trividhaṃ kramāt ।
utsedhātpañcabhāgaikaṃ caturaṃśakameva vā ।।

ṣaḍbhāgaikena vākuryāttrividhaṃ bhittivistaram atha vā ।
prāsādabhittistu tatsamaṃ bhittimeva ca ।।

garbhe aṣṭāṃśocchrayaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ saptabhāgedvimadhyamam ।
pañcabhāgaikamadhamaṃ balipīṭhaṃ tathābhavet ।।

garbhapañcatribhāgaikaṃ ।
navāṃśeṣaṭcaturbhāgaṃ madhyamādhamamuttamam ।।

tridhā paiśācikaṃ pīṭhāddhastamātraṃ kramādbhavet ।
dvihastāntaṃ trihastāntaṃ caturhastāntamucyate ।।

adhamaṃ madhyamaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ tridhā paiśācapīṭhakam ।
saptaviṃśatibhāgaiśca samamevaṃ samunnatam ।।

dvyaṃśaṃ ca pādukā jñeyaṃ caturaṃśaṃ janiṃ viduḥ ।
tṣaṃśaṃ tu kuṃbhamityāhu ścaturthaṅkaṇṭhameva ca ।।

ṣaḍbhāgaṃ karaṇetyāhurdvyaṃśaṃ valakameva ca ।
caturaṃśe kapotāśca aṃśecaivāgrapaṭṭikā ।।

adhyardhaṃ padmapuṣpantu ekārdhaṃ padmapuṣpakam ।
evaṃ samyagviditvātu bhāgebhāge vinirdiśet ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavaccāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre ṣaṣṭho adhyāyaḥ

atha saptamo adhyāyaḥ

atha saptamo adhyāyaḥ 
parivārālayalakṣaṇam
athātaḥ parivārāṇāmālayasya ca lakṣaṇam ।
vimānātpādahīnaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā samācaret ।।

varṇayuktaṃ tataśśreṣṭhaṃ kaniyovarṇahīnakam ।
someśānadvayormadhye viṣvaksenaṃ prakalbayet ।।

dvārasya dakṣiṇe cendra māgneyyāṃ pacanālayam ।
tasya paścimadeśetu pānīyasthānamevaca ।।

yāmye śayanamuddiṣṭaṃ tatpūrve yāgamaṇḍapam ।
aiśānye puṣpadeśantu dakṣiṇe vastrasaṃcayam ।।

īśānasomayormadhye sthāpanaṃ tathā ।
indrāgnyormadhyamecaiva dhānyasthānaṃ praśasyate ।।

sopānamadhye śrībhūtamarcayedbahirānanam ।
purastādgaruḍaṃ tasya devābhimukhamarcayet ।।

vimānapālān dikpālān bhāskareṇa samāyutam ।
cakraṃ dhvajaṃ ca śaṅkhaṃ ca bhūtaṃ vai bhūtanāyakam ।।

prathamāvaraṇe dehustattaddeśe samarcayet ।
utsavaṃ balimārabhya anapāyiviśeṣataḥ ।।

amitasyāpi tantatra pradakṣiṇamathācaret ।
devasya kaṇṭhasīmāntaṃ bāhyantaṃ stanasammitam ।।

nābhyantaṃ vā viśeṣeṇa parivārodayaṃ kramāt ।
dhātrādibhūtaparyantaṃ parivārānviśeṣataḥ ।।

varṇavāhanaketvādyairnāmanakṣatrapūrvakam ।
mayākriyādhikāre tu vyaktamuktantulakṣaṇam ।।

beralakṣaṇam- 

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa beralakṣaṇamuttamam ।
śailajaṃ ratnajaṃ caiva dhātujaṃ dāravaṃ tathā ।।

mṛṇmayaṃ syāttathaiveti pañcadhāberamucyate ।
caturvidhaṃ tu śailaṃ syātsaptadhā ratnajaṃ tathā ।।

aṣṭadhā dhātujaṃ proktaṃ dārujaṃ ṣoḍaśocyate ।
mṛṇmayaṃ dvividhaṃ proktaṃ kramāllakṣaṇamucyate ।।

śailajalakṣaṇam
śvetaṃ raktaṃ tathā pītaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ caiva catuṣṭayam ।
śailajaṃ bhedamākhyātaṃ tasya lakṣaṇamucyate ।।

gokṣīrasannibhācaiva śaṅkhakundendu sannibhā ।
śīlā śvetā samākhyātā sā tu vaśyapradāyikā ।।

japākusumasaṃkāśā śilā śoṇitasannibhā ।
bandhūkapuṣpapratimā jātihiṅgulikopamā ।।

śilā raktā samākhyātā jayadā lakṣaṇānvitā ।
pītā suvarṇasadṛśā rajanīcūrṇasannibhā ।।

śilā lakṣaṇasaṃyuktā dhanadhānyasukhapradā ।
māṣamudgala?saṃkāśā tathājaṃbūphalopamā ।।

bhṛṅga? mutpalasaṃkāśā prajāvṛddhikarāsmṛtā ।
śilā kṛṣṇā tu sarveṣāṃ sarvasiddhipradāyikā ।।

viprakṣatriyavaiśyānāṃ śūdrāṇāñca yadhāvidhi ।
śvetā raktā tathā pītā kṛṣṇā caiva yathākramam ।।

dvijānāṃ ca trivarṇānāṃ śilā raktā jayapradā ।
śvetā mokṣapradā proktā brāhmaṇānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

etaintudhruvaberantu kārayedyadibhaktitaḥ ।
māṇikyaṃ ca pravālaṃ ca vaidūryaṃ sbhaṭikaṃ tathā ।।

maratakaṃ puṣyarāgaṃ ca nīlaṃ caiteṣuratnajāḥ ।
māṇikyaṃ śrīkaraṃ proktaṃ pravālaṃ vaśyakārakam ।।

ākarṣaṇaṃ tu vaiḍhūryaṃ sphāṭikaṃ putravṛddhidam ।
vidveṣaṇaṃ maratakaṃ staṃbhanaṃ pūṣyarāgakam ।।

nīlaṃ turamaṇaiḥ kāryaṃ ratnajānāṃ phalaṃ bhavet ।
eteṣāṃ kautukaṃ kuryā danyeṣāṃ ca vidhīyate ।।

haimaṃ raipyaṃ tathātāmraṃ kāṃsyaṃ caivārakūṭakam ।
āyasaṃ sīsakaṃ caiva trapukaṃ ceti dhātujam ।।

haimantu śrīpradaṃ proktaṃ raupyaṃ rājyapradāyakam ।
tāmraṃ putrasamaddhyarthaṃ kāṃsyaṃ vidveṣakārakam ।।

proccāraṇe cārakūṭa māyasaṃ kṣayakāraṇam ।
sīsaṃ nīraugakaraṇaṃ trapurāyurvināśanam ।।

evaṃ tu lohajaṃ proktaṃ tato dārujamucyate ।
devadāruśśamīvṛkṣaṃ pippalaṃ nandanaṃ tathā ।।

asanaṃ khadirañcaiva vakulaṃ śaṅkhi vātanam ।
mayūrapadmaḍuṇḍūka karṇikāraṃ tathaiva ca ।।

nibūkāñjanikācaiva plakṣamauduṃbaraṃ tathā ।
etairvarjyāstu? catvāro dvijātikramayogataḥ ।।

mṛṇmayaṃ dvividhaṃ proktaṃ pakvāpakvaṃ tathaiva ca ।
pakvaṃ ca nāśakaṃ caivam apakvaṃ sarvasiddhitam ।।

nimittadarśanam- 

yasmin deśe śilāstīti gacchenniścitamānasaḥ ।
prayāṇakāle śakunā śśubhāśśubha phalapradāḥ ।।

śubhavākyodakuṃbhāsthi gajarājadvijottamāḥ ।
carmamāṃsadadhikṣīra dundabhidhvanayaśśubhāḥ ।।

aśobhanāṃstathāvakṣyeśapamānā yathāyati ।
vikīrṇakeśāvipraikyaghṛtatailāktadarśanam ।।

riktakuṃbhanirodhokti tailabhājanadarśanam ।
prayāṇakāle naṣṭāstu viparītaphalapradāḥ ।।

śubhe prayāṇaṃ kartavyaṃ sthitvā śobhanalakṣaṇam ।
śilāṃ prāpya śubhesthāne vāstuhomaṃ samācaret ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ śrībhūsūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।
pariṣekaṃ tataḥkṛtvā kalaśān pañca sunyaset ।।

mṛdgandhākṣatajapyāṃśca sarvauṣadhyudakantathā ।
saṃsthāpyābhyarcya pādyādyai ntattaddevāṃ tsamarcayet ।।

abhiṣiñcecchilāṃ sūtre? muhūrtekaraṇānvite ।
atodevādimantreṇa śilāṃ chitvāvicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

adhobhāgaṃ mukhaṃ tatra śira ūrdhva prakalpayet ।
pūrvataścottare vātha śirobhāgaṃ prakalpayet ।।

mukhaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ tathāpādaṃ pārśvaṃ caiva śirastathā ।
lāñchayitvā vidhānena tatastakṣaṇa mācaret ।।

bālā ca yuvatī vṛddhājñātavyā lakṣaṇānvitā ।
snigdhā mṛdvī natā caiva bālā kṣīrasvarātathā ।।

susvarā kā ntisaṃyuktā yuvatī sā śilā smṛtā ।
asitā jhargharā rūkṣā vṛddhā yā nissvarāśilā ।।

bālā kṣayapradā proktā yuvatī susamṛddhidā ।
kāryanāśakarī vṛddhā grāhyā jñātvāśilāstathā ।।

mūrdhanastakṣaṇaṅkṛtvā śilādoṣāṃntu lakṣayet ।
śilāṃ pralipyakṣīreṇa sarpiṣā sīsagairikaiḥ ।।

ekarātroṣitaśilāṃ saṃprakṣālyāṃbhasātataḥ ।
śilādoṣaṃ parīkṣyaiva kartavyaṃ vidhicoditam ।।

rekhābinduḥ kalaṅkaśca śilādoṣāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।
maṇḍalaṃ tu bhavettatra yatra garbhaṃ vinirdiśet ।।

site tu maṇḍale sarporaktetu kṛkalāsakam ।
pīte tu maṇḍale godhā mañjiṣṭhe darduro bhavet ।।

kapile mūṣikā proktāsitavarṇe tu vṛścikaḥ ।
śvetaraktavimiśretu vṛścikaśśvetaraktake ।।

raktamiśretu maṇḍūko maṇḍalobhavet ।
siṃdūravarṇe khadyotaḥ kapote gṛhagaulikā ।।

guḍavarṇetu pāṣāṇaṃ nissvaśobhe jalaṃ bhavet ।
varjayedgarbha saṃyuktāṃ vimalair añcintāṃ tathā ।।

vimalaṃ hemakāṃsyākhyaṃ lohākhyaṃ catridā smṛtam ।
parīkṣyaivaṃ prakartavyameva meva pramāṇataḥ ।।

prāsādagarbhamānaṃ vā hastamānamathāpi vā ।
pratyekaṃ tritribhedaṃ syāddvāramānaṃ pravakṣyate ।।

dvārādadhyardhakaṃ caiva dvārātpādādhikaṃ tathā ।
madhyamaṃ ca kanīyassyāddvāramevaṃ vidhīyate ।।

adhamottamayormadhye tvaṣṭadhā kārayedbudhaḥ ।
kanīyastrīṇi vijñeyaṃ trīṇi madhyamakaṃ tathā ।।

trīṇi cottamakaṃ vidyādutsedhaṃ navathā bhavet ।
staṃbhādadhyardhakaṃ tuṅgamuttamaṃ tu viśeṣuḥ ।।

uttamādhamayormadhye dvāramānena yojayet ।
garbhagehasamaṃ madhyaṃ tripādaṃ cādhamaṃ bhavet ।।

pādādhikaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ śreṣṭhamevaṃ vidhīyate ।
।
hastamānaṃ tadhāvakṣye navahastaṃ tadhottamam ।।

ṣaḍaṅgulaissahānyāntu sārdhadvihastakāvadhi ।
evamutsedhamānantu sthāvarasya praśasyate ।।

jaṅgamānāṃ bhavennāma mūlaberavaśāttathā ।
biṃbodayaṃ caturviṃśadbhāgānaṣṭāṃśakaṃ tathā ।।

biṃbodayaṃ caturviṃśadbhāgānaṣṭāṃśakaṃ tathā ।
vedāṃśaṃ tu bhaveduccaṃ jaṅgamasya prakīrtitam ।।

mānāṅgulena saptādi dvidvyaṅgulavidhānataḥ ।
pañcāśatsavanāṅgulyā vidhissarvovidhīyate ।।

mūlaberāṃgulānmānamārabhyaikādaśāṃgulam ।
dvidvyaṅgulavivṛddhyātu saṣaṣṭitṣaṅgulaṃ? bhavet ।।

pratyekaṃ tu tribhedaṃ syāduttamādhamamadhyataḥ ।
utkṛṣṭaṃ navatuṅgaṃ syānmadhyamaṃ navatuṅgakam ।।

nikṛṣṭaṃ tu tathā proktaṃ saptaviṃśatituṅgakam ।
etairuttamamānaṃ syāsmadhyamaṃ ca tathaiva hi ।।

karmārcotsavasnānācca yojyaṃ syādanyadhā natu ।
adhamaistu bhavedyatra baliberaṃ vidhīyate ।।
mātrāṃgulena yanmāraṃ gṛhārcāṇāṃ tu nānyathā ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre saptamo adhyāyaḥ

athāṣṭamo adhyāyaḥ

athāṣṭamo adhyāyaḥ 
pīṭhamānam
atha pīṭhodayaṃ paścātthsānakasya viśeṣataḥ ।
bhuvaṅgasya samaṃ vātha adhyarthaṃ triguṇaṃ tu vā ।।

paritaḥ pāvayorasya nītvāvai bhāgamaṅgulam ।
dhruvārcāyāmaśeṣeṇa ṣaṇmānasahitaṃ śubham ।।

vakṣyāmi devyormānaṃ tatkaṇṭhāntaṃ nāsikāntakam ।
hanvastaṃ bāhusīmāntaṃ nābhyantaṃ vādha kārayet ।।

caturdhaikāṃśakaṃ vāpi tṛtīyaikāṃśakaṃ tu vā ।
dhruvārcāyāṃ viśeṣeṇa pīṭhamevaṃ prakalpayet ।।

caturaśraṃ suvṛttaṃ vā dalaiṣṣoḍaśabhiryutam ।
sthānakaṃ cāsanaṃ vāpi yānakaṃ vā samācaret ।।

garbhāgāratribhāgaikaṃ caturaśraṃ trimekhalam ।
tasyordhvavedivistāraṃ caturaṅgulameva hi ।।

utsedhaṃ tasya cārdhantuparitaścaturaṅgulam ।
vistārotsedhamānantu madhyenimnaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulam ।।

udīcyāntu pratīcyāntu vārimārgantu kārayet ।
prāṅmukhodaṅmukhaṃ sūtraṃ daśa sapta samarcayet ।।

madhye kalāpadaṃ brāhmaṃ parito daivikaṃ tathā ।
vaidāthikāśītipadaṃ mānuṣaṃ ca tathaiva ca ।।

padaṃ syāt ṣaṇnavatikaṃ ṣaṣṭiḥpaiśācikaṃ bhavet ।
arcāsthānaṃ tu brahmāṃśaṃ tridhā kṛtya ca daivikam ।।

tathaiva paścime bhāge madhye vā sthānakāya ca ।
asanaṃ vāpi ca tadhā devamānuṣamadhyame ।।

śayānaṃ mānuṣe pīṭhe sthāpayitvā viśeṣataḥ ।
dhruvārcane viśeṣeṇa nāgasūtrān samarpya ca ।।

koṣṭamekāna pañcāśadbhavati brāhmamandiram ।
daivikaṃ cāṣṭabhāgantu mānuṣaṃ cārtvijaṃ padam ।।

śeṣaṃ paiśācamevaṃ syācchāntipauṣṭikadaivikam ।
brahmasthāne viśeṣaṇa sthāpayedyogavīrakau ।।

bhogameva dhruvārcāyāṃ devamānuṣamadhyame ।
vīrakaṃ sthāpayedvidvān paiśāce kramaśassudhīḥ ।।

grāmamadhye dhruvārcāyāṃ sthāpayed bhogameva tu ।
yogapīṭhe dhruvārcā cettadgrāmasya vipadbhavet ।।

anyeṣāṃ tu dhruvārcāyāṃ bhogaṃ vā yogameva vā ।
ālayoddakṣiṇe vāpi vūrve vāpi prapāṃ tathā ।।

vediṃ tanmadhyame kuryādbiṃbādhyardhapramāṇataḥ ।
sabhyāgnikuṇḍaṃ tatprācyāṃ snānavediṃ tathottare ।।

bhūmiyajñaṃ ca kṛtvātu paryagni prokṣaṇaṃ caret ।
kalaśaissaptabhissnāpya vedyāmāropayettathā ।।

ācchādya navavastreṇa kautukaṃ bardhayettathā ।
prākṣīraśśāyayettatra śrībhūmyorubhayorapi ।।

mahākāyakṛte bere prokṣayetpañcagavyakaiḥ ।
anyatsarvakriyāṃ kṛtvāhautraśaṃsanamācaret ।।

ādimūrtyādi sarvāstamāvāhanamathācaret ।
avāhanakrameṇaiva nirupyājyāhutīryatet ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ pauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।
śrībhūsūktaṃ tato hutvā brāhmaṃ raudrantathaivaca ।।

nṛttairgeyaiśca vādyaiśca rātriśeṣaṃ vinīya ca ।
snātvā prabhāte tvācāryo devamutthāpya cādarāt ।।

garbhāgāraṃ praviśyaiva sthāpite vihite api vā ।
nyasya pīṭhantu tanmadhye ratnādīnvinyasettadā ।।

dhruvasūktena saṃsthāpya ato devādimuccaran ।
tattanmantreṇa devyādīn sthāpayedvihite pade ।।

vidhinā cāṣṭabandhantu saṃyojyaiva tu pūrayet ।
antahomaṃ tato hutvā dadyādācāryadakṣiṇām ।।

śilbinaṃ ca samāhūya śarkarāṃ lepayetkramāt ।
śilāpratiṣṭhā caivaṃ syāddārusaṃgrahaṇaṃ tataḥ ।।

dārusaṃgrahaṇam candanaṃ khadiraṃ tālamasanaṃ ।
raktacandanam
rājānaṃ ciribilvañca aśokaṃ stimitaṃ tathā ।।

khādiraṃ dhanvinaṃ caivaśirīṣaṃ padmakaṃ tathā ।
ityevamādayo vṛkṣā gṛhyante berakarmaṇi ।।

caṇḍālasthānapārśve tu duṣṭaprāṇiniṣevite ।
mātṛsthānasamudbūte? śmaśāne devamandire ।।

kūpavāpītaṭākānte munivāse sahālaye ।
yogasthānapade dharmaśālāyāṃ mārgamadhyame ।।

pretabhūtālaye corasattvānāṃ ca niṣevite ।
prasthānaśalabhasthāne kalpāsdhinilaye api ca? ।।

sauṣṭābhūtasamudbhūtadeśe? rauṇika deśake ।
evaṃ sthāne samudbhūtaṃ na gṛhṇanti drumaṃ tataḥ ।।

pādānapāvanaṃ tardhi maśaneryātipīḍanam ।
asākṣikaṃ sarpanilayaṃ bahuvalmīka saṃyutam ।।

sujanaṃ taruṇaṃ rūkṣaṃ bahupakṣasamākulam ।
asthiraṃ bahucakraṃ ca suśākhaṃ caikaśākhinam ।।

karmāntaragṛhitaṃ ca karmāntaraprayojanam ।
evamīdṛgvidhaṃ vṛkṣaṃ varjayedberakarmaṇi ।।

āmūlāgraṃ samaṃ vṛttamṛjuṃ caiva pradakṣiṇam ।
vistārayāmasaṃpannaṃ śubhāyaiva samāyutam ।।

sumadhyavayasopetaṃ kālapuṣpaphalapradam ।
īdṛgvidhaṃ mahāvṛkṣaṃ śūlārthaṃ parigṛhṇate ।।

evaṃ lakṣaṇa saṃpannaṃ drumaṃ gatvā prasannadhīḥ ।
tanmūle gomayenāpi lepayeccaturaśrakam ।।

divyalakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ drumaṃ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇam ।
"vanarājebhya' ityuktvāpāyasaṃ ca baliṃ dadet ।।

paraśaṃ ca samādāya secayetpañcagavyakaiḥ ।
mūlamantraṃ japitvā tu dhmāyedviṣṇuṃ parātparam ।।

paraśuñca samādāya bhedayettu vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
payaḥ parisrave tatra śubhamevaṃ vidhīyate ।।

śoṇitaprasrave tatra nirdaśedaśubhaṃ punaḥ ।
pūrvaṃ tupatanaṃ śastamāgneyyāṃ tu bhayāvaham ।।

yāmyāyāṃ maraṇaṃ vindyānnairṛtyāṃ vyādhimādiśet ।
paśmimetu janānāṃ tu kṣutpipāsāvivardhanaṃ ।।

vāyavye ca bhavellābha uttare dhanadhānyakaṃ ।
aiśānyāṃ śāntikaṃ tatra sarvavṛddhikaraṃ nṛṇām ।।

tadvṛkṣapatane kālekośassarvomṛdurbhavet ।
sihavyāghragajādīnāṃ sarvasaṃpatkaraṃ bhavet ।।

vṛkṣāgraṃ bhevayitvā tu tvacaṃ samyagvyapohya ca ।
prakṣālyavāriṇā śvetacandanenānulepayet ।।

śvetavastreṇa saṃdeṣṭya jayamaṅgalaghoṣaṇaiḥ ।
rathevā śakaṭe vāthaskanthe vā kṣipya veśayet ।।

grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṅkṛtyā svastisūktaṃ samuccaran ।
śiṣṭacchāyesame deśetālukopariśāyayet ।।

hemarūpyakṛtaṃ śūlaṃ sarvasaṃpatsamṛddhidam ।
lohairanyairnakartavya mabhicārasya kāraṇam ।।

viṣṇuśūlaṃ tu keśānāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ paṭṭikameva ca ।
dhyeyaṃ meḍhrādayaśbordhvaṃ samaṃ bhāgasya yattrayam ।।

ūrukeśāntaparyantaṃ tasyārthaṃ ca takaṃ mukham ।
sarandhrayavakaṃ cordhve mānaśūlaṃ śirodharam ।।

hikkāyāṃ ṣaḍyavaṃ pañcāṅgulaṃ nābhyantakaṃ matam ।
trayodaśāṅgulayavaṃ tato meḍhrantu nābhyadhaḥ ।।

yonernābhesturyādaśraṃ brāhmamaṣṭaumataṃ tataḥ ।
hikkāstaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ bhāgaṃ tato vṛttaṃ śivāṃśakam ।।

uṣṇīṣaṃ mātṛkaṃ śūlaṃ sthānādīnāṃ sanātanam ।
sthānāsanaśayānānāṃ caturaśrāṣṭavartulam ।।

yathākrameṇa yuñjīyādevaṃ vā pūrvamuktavat ।
sarveṣāṃ devatānāṃ ca sāmānyaṃ ca turaśrakam ।।

caturmātrārdhavistāraṃ śūlamūlaviśālakam ।
agratāraṃ caturmātramaṣṭāṃśonamathāpi vā ।।

dvātriṃśadaṅgulāyāmaṃ vakṣodaṇḍasya cocyate ।
tarma? vistṛtayorbāhye mātṛsūtrasamordhayoḥ ।।

vakṣodaṇḍāyataṃ svena mukhena dviguṇaṃ matam ।
uktvāsamantu bāhyagretatsaptāṃśavihīnakam ।।

tāraṃ saptāṅgulaṃ teṣāṃ yena sārthaṃ trimātrakam ।
ṣoḍhaśāṣṭa caturmātrāyāmatārasamanvitam ।।

kaṭidaṇḍaṃ bhavettasya pārśvamadhyamanimnakam ।
kṛtvaiva nimnakaṃ vakṣodaṇḍamadhye prakalpayet ।।

śeṣayorvaṃśadaṇḍe tu nābhyantaṃ nimnamadhyakam ।
dakṣiṇe mūlamadhye tu agraṃ kuryāddvayorapi ।।

vakṣodaṇḍasyamūlāgre śikhā sūdasradāyatam ।
kālāṅgulakalātāraṃ kalārdhavipulaṃ matam ।।

evaṃ caturbhujaṃ kṛtvādvibhuje dviśikhaṃ tathā ।
catasraśśibikā stasmāttasyā mevāṣṭabāhuke ।।

yāvanto bāhavastasmiṃ stāvatyaśca śikhā matāḥ ।
adhyardhāṅgulavistāraṃ śikhāyāmaṃ tadeva hi ।।

kaṭidaṇḍaṃ śikhāyāmaṃ tāre dvitṣaṅgule kramāt ।
vina?dvimātrameva syāddviśikhaṃ kaṭidaṇḍakam ।।

śroṇibhāgādadhastena śeṣayedvaṃśadaṇḍakam ।
ūrudaṇḍālayaṃ saptaviṃśadaṅgulamucyate ।।

jānubhāgaṃ tato jaṅghā pyūrdhvadaṇḍasamāyatā ।
pādabhāgābhave dūrurjaṅghayorjhānumānakam ।।

āropya mānayejjānudaṇḍasyāsaṃbhavādapi ।
pādadaṇḍe samāropya mānayettalatuṅgakam ।।

ūrudaṇḍaviśālaṃ syānmūlebhāgaṃ tadaśrake ।
kalāṅgulaṃ tadekaṃ syājjaṅghāmūlaviśālakam ।।

kalāviśālaṃ jaṅghāgraṃ kalāyāmaṃ daśāṅgulam ।
trimātrakalamūlasya tāramagre adhikāṃgulam ।।

saptaviṃśati vāgroṣaṃ daṇḍadīrghaṃ tataḥ kalā ।
korparassyātprakoṣṭhasya dīrghaṃ daśakalāṅgulam ।।

prakoṣṭhabāhvairāropya korparaṃ jānuvadbhavet ।
tṣaṅgulaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ bāhudaṇḍamūlāgravistaram ।।

prakoṣṭhaṃ daṇḍamūlasya viśālaṃ cadvimātrakam ।
adhyardhāṅgulamagrasya viśālaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam ।।

vakṣodaṇḍaśikhāmadhye bāhumūlagate śikhe ।
bāhumūlagatābhyāṃ tu vakṣodaṇḍaśikhāgatām ।।

śeṣayedagrabhāgebhyaḥ korpare śeṣayettataḥ ।
prakoṣṭhamūlagābhyāṃ tu vakṣodaṇḍaśikhāgatām ।।

kaṭidaṇḍorudaṇḍābhyāṃ taccheṣaṃ bāhudaṇḍavat ।
jānukorparamuddiṣṭaṃ tasyatu dviśikhematam ।।

śeṣayennalakānāntu prakoṣṭhe tu bhavedbudhāḥ ।
prasāritānāṃ pādānāṃ jānusandhautu gṛhyatām ।।

tathaiva visṛjānāṃ ca budhānāṃ korparaṃ matam ।
sthānādīnāṃ kramāschūlasaṃghātaṃ vakṣyate api ca ।।

vaṃśadaṇḍaṃ tathā vakṣye daṇḍaṃ ca kaṭidaṇḍakam ।
jānudaṇḍadvayaṃ caiva pādadaṇḍadvayaṃ tathā ।।

bāhudaṇḍāśca catvāra ścatvāraśca prakoṣṭhakāḥ ।
tathā caraṇadaṇḍau dvau daṇḍāssapta daśa smṛtāḥ ।।

kaṭidaṇḍārdhamārabhya yāvadāsīnarapi ।
tārassyātpṛṣṭhaphalakā tāramūrau ca bandhayet ।।

kaṭidaṇḍādadhastācca vakṣodaṇḍadharas tathā ।
yojayedupayānīlaṃ? pṛṣṭhato vṛttameva vā ।।

vaṃśadaṇḍaṃ tathā tena kleśayedviśikhena tu ।
śikhāgrasuṣīre kīlaṃ lohaṃ vā skāmathāpi vā ।।

dārḍhyārthaṃ yojayecchūlaṃ sthitaṃ vai śūlakarmaṇi ।
anyatkīlaṃ tu suṣiraṃ kartavyaṃ kathañcana ।।

evaṃ sthānasya saṃproktamāsanasya pravakṣyate ।
meḍhramūlādadhomūlaṃ nāhamaṣṭāṃgulaṃ bhavet ।।

bhāgamāsanamānasya bhāgaṃ śvabhrapraveśanam ।
meḍhrasūtrasame samyak śeṣayetkaṭidaṇḍakam ।।

kaṭidaṇḍaśikhāhyūru daṇḍamūlaśikhāni ca ।
āsane śayane caiva jānusandhiḥ praśasyate ।।

ekonaviṃśatiśśūladaṇḍānāṃ tu samākṛtiḥ ।
neṣyate korpare saṃdhiśayane daṇḍahastake ।।

tasmādatha daśa proktā śūlasaṃkhyā caturbhuje ।
pañcānye dvibhuje daṇḍa daṇḍā haste caturdaśa ।।

dakṣiṇe vakṣodaṇḍasyāyatamekādaśāṃgulam ।
śikhā pūrvavaduddiṣṭā bāhumūlaśikhānvitā ।।

tayorupari cābhogaṃ chāyayecchāstravittamaḥ ।
kaṭīḍaṇḍadvayādanyat sthānasyoktavadācaret ।।

uktaṃ hi śayane yāne vakṣyatetha trivikramam ।
uddaṇḍasyorudaṇḍasya śikhā bhāgāyate smṛte ।।

tāvatyaḥ kaṭidaṇḍasya śikhāyāssamyaganvaye ।
tadāyataṃ tu kāryārthaṃ taladaṇḍaṃ tu taddvitam ।।

sthitāṅghristhsitimān proktaśśeṣaṃ cedaṃ śayānavat ।
evamaṣṭabhujopetaṃ caturbhujasamanvite ।।

śūlasaṃkhyānurūpeṇa yojayettu vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
śūlaṃ cakratanau vakramavakre vakratāṃ nayet ।।

strīṇāṃ śūlavibhāgantu lakṣmyādīnāṃ pravakṣyate ।
nāsāmānavibhāgaṃ ca śūladaṇḍāyataṃ matam ।।

bhāgatāraṃ bhavedvaṃśaṃ daṇḍaṃ taccaturaśrakam ।
yaduktaṃ bāhuparyantaṃ tāraṃ tasmāddvipārśvayoḥ ।।

bāhumūlaviśālārdhaṃ tyaktvā yāvattadantaram ।
tāvattu paramaṃ vakṣodaṇḍasyāyāmamucyate ।।

kacchāṃśonaṃ karākāraṃ kaṭidaṇḍāyataṃ matam ।
ūrutāraṃ tu turyāṃśā dūrudaṇḍaviśālakam ।।

jaṅghādaṇḍaṃ
tribhāgaikaṃ tāvaśce?daṣṭāṃśadaṇḍakam ।
mūlameva mataṃ caiṣāmagramaṣṭāṃśahīnakam ।।

pārśvadaṇḍaṃ na yoktavyaṃ strīṇāṃ śūle kathaṃ cana ।
puruṣāṇāṃ prayoktavya madhyardhāṅgulivistaram ।।

sarveṣāmasi tālānāṃ śūlamevaṃ vidurbudhāḥ ।
bhuvaṅgasya samaṃ proktaṃ sthānake pīṭhakonnatam ।।

bhuvaṅgoparitālaṃ syāddhruvapīṭhasya connatiḥ ।
dhruvaberasya pādasya pratidikcaturaṅgulam ।।

vistāramūrdhvavedyāntu padmapatradalair yutam ।
maṇḍalaṃ caturaśraṃ vā pīṭhaṃ kuryāttadarhakam ।।

daivikaṃ tu tridhā kṛtvā dvibhāgaṃ puratastyajet ।
apare sthānakaṃ sthāpya madhyabhāge atha vā pulaḥ ।।

devamānuṣayārmadhye vā'sanaṃ saṃprakalpayet ।
kiṃ ciddaivikasaṃyukte mānuṣe śayanaṃ smṛtam ।।

evaṃ samyagviditvaiva māsane ca pravakṣyate ।
dhruvaberaṃ tathā kṛtvā cordhvaṃ siṃhāsanocchrayam ।।

tadarhavistṛtaṃ prokta mupadhānena saṃyutam ।
pādāśrayeṇa pīṭhena padmākārau? ca saṃyutam ।।

yathāsaindaryakaṃ kṛtvā śeṣaṃ yuktyā samācaret ।
berāyāmaṃ caturbhāgaṃ śayanocchrāyamucyate ।।

tatturīyāṃśakotsedhaṃ śirobhāge viśeṣataḥ ।
pādayorubhayoścaiva samaṃ tatraiva mūhya ca ।।

śeṣabhogaṃ trirāveṣṭya pañcavarṇasamāyutam ।
adhaḥpucchaṃ śiraścordhvaṃ sarpadehe tu veṣṭite ।।

tadutsaṃgagataṃ devaṃ śayānaṃ saṃpracakṣate ।
phaṇānāṃ pañcakaṃ kuryādviṣavegasamanvitam ।।

evameva prakurvīta sthānāsanaśayānakān ।
pīṭhaṃ kṛtvā prayatnena sthāpanāraṃbhamācaret ।।

aṅkurānarpayitvaiva yāgaśālāṃ prakalpayet ।
śilāsthāpanasārgeṇa sarvaṃ kṛtvāprayatnataḥ ।।

athācāryaḥprabhāte tu snātvā nityaṃ samāpya ca ।
yajamānasamāyukto garbhagehaṃ praviśya ca ।।

sthānāsanaśayānānāṃ padamuktaṃ vicārya ca ।
pīṭhaṃ tadarhakaṃ kuryādyuktenaiva vidhānataḥ ।।

pratiṣṭhoktakrameṇaiva ratnanyāsaṃ samācaret ।
ācāryasthāpakādīnāmṛtvijāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ dadet ।।

śūle sārthaṃ samādāya gāyatrīṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ japan ।
sthāpayeddevadevasya śūlaṃ devyostataḥkramāt ।।

ādhāradaṇḍayoḥ paścācchiṣṭadaṇḍānniyojayet ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvātu sabhyamagniṃ visṛjya ca ।।

tataśśilpinamāhūya śāstrīyaṃ priyadarśanam? ।
vastrairābharaṇaiścāpi pūjayitvānvavekṣya ca ।।

rajjubandhādikaṃ karma beroktaṃ tatra kārayet ।
atrānuktaṃ tataḥ kuryācchilpaśāstroktamārgataḥ ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛsuproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre aṣṭamo adhyāyaḥ

atha navamo adhyāyaḥ

atha navamo adhyāyaḥ 
rajjubandhanam
athātas saṃpravakṣyāmi rajjubandhavidhiṃ kramāt ।
yathoktaṃ ca mṛdassarvāssamāhṛtya vidhānataḥ ।।

saṃpiṣya śodhayitvaiva yathoktaṃ sarva mauṣadham ।
cūrṇāni ca yathoktāni kaṣāyāṇi vidhānataḥ ।।

yojayitvā yathābhāgaṃ gavyairapi ihaivaca ।
niryāsena kapiddhasya yuktaṃ nādeyavāriṇā ।।

peṣayitvā mṛdā samyaksaṃpiṣya ca vidhānataḥ ।
sādhayitvātha vā vāmaṃ sārdhaṃvāpi nidhāya ca ।।

nālikerasya sāreṇa trivṛtāṃ rajjumāharet ।
sarajjuṃ bandhayec chūlaṃ yathātatsudṛḍhaṃ tathā ।।

bandhayitvāṣṭabandhaṃ ca śūlamālipya sarvaśaḥ ।
mṛdaṃ ca tāṃ samādāya śūla mālopayettathā ।।

śūlopari pramāṇaṃ yaccaturbhāgaṃ vibhajyaca ।
tattribhāgaṃ mṛdākuryā drajjubandhasamāyutam ।।

ghaṭaśarkarayā vastramauktikair varṇakair yutam ।
pūraye danyabhāgaṃ ca tatpramāṇavidhānataḥ ।।

śarkarāṃ ca samālipya paṭaṃ saṃyojya pūrvavat ।
mauktikākṛti mālipya bhūṣaṇāni prakalpyaca ।।

yathoktena vidhānena varṇānapi suyojayet ।
mṛṇmayaṃ dhravaberaṃ cetkāraye devamaiva tat ।।

ardhacitraṃ na kurvīta dhruvaberaṃ tu mṛṇmayam ।
śūlārdhaṃ tu dvayaṃ kuryāttāmranālasamāyutam ।।

khādiraṃ tāmradaṇḍaṃ vābhittisthaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ caret ।
chidraṃ kṛtvātadādhāre śūlaṃ yantreṇa yojayet ।।

dṛḍhaṃ tadyojayitvaiva berapṛṣṭhasya madhyame ।
tatpṛṣṭheskandhamadhye ca tadādhāreṇa yojayet ।।

śūle chidraṃ nakartavyaṃ kuryācchetsa vinaśyati ।
tāmreṇa dhruvaberaṃ cenmadhūcchiṣṭavidhānataḥ ।।

mṛṇmayaṃ dvividhaṃ prokta mapakvaṃ pakvamityapi ।
pūrvoktaṃ mṛṇmayaṃ yattadapakva mabhidhīyate ।।

mṛdākṛtvāgvinādagdhaṃ yattatpakvamitīritam ।
apakvaṃ mṛṇmaye viṣṇoḥ kārayettu vidhānataḥ ।।

yadi pakvaṃ tu kuryācchettadvināśakaṃ bhavet ।
yogādisthānāni
sthānaṃ caturvidhaṃ vindyādyogaṃ bhogaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

sṛṣṭiḥ saṃhāra ityeṣāṃ sthānabhedaḥ pravakṣyate ।
sarvato bhadrakaṃ nandyāvartakaṃ śrīpratiṣṭhitam ।।

svastikaṃ parvatākāraṃ vṛttabhedaṃ tathaivaca ।
pralīnaka mathodyogaṃ padmañcaiva caturmukham ।।

brahmādīśānaparyantaṃ krameṇaiva niveśayet ।
yogakāntaṃ bhavedyogaṃ sthānakasya vidhīyate ।।

caturaśraṃ vṛttagehaṃ prāsādaṃ sthānakasya tu ।
āsanānāṃ caturbhedaṃ pūrvoktena krameṇa tu ।।

pralīnaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ vimānaṃ vā caturmukham ।
viṣṇuchandavimānaṃ ca śrīpratiṣṭhitakaṃ tathā ।।

parvatākṛtikañcaiva nandyāvartaṃ tathaiva ca ।
mahāpadmavimānaṃ ca pralīnaka vīmānakam ।।

aṣṭāṅgaṃ sarmatobhadraṃ citraśilpaṃ tathaiva ca ।
mahāpadmaṃ ca vṛttaṃ ca caturmukhavimānakam ।।

evaṃ vimānakaṃ caiva āsanasya vidhīyate ।
svastikaṃ vṛttabhadraṃ ca vṛttagarbha mavedikam ।।

prekṣya gṛhālpabhūrājachandaṃ ca śrīpratiṣṭhitam ।
martalaṃ ca śanairyogaṃ mārtāṇḍaṃ ca catuṣphuṭam ।।

gaṇikāviśālaṃ saṃśuddhaṃ svastikaṃ dhvajamānakam ।
evamākhyāya tantrāṇi vartulādyāyutāni ca ।।

śayānakena yogyāni kathitāni manīṣibhiḥ ।
āyādivicāraḥ
āyavyayādi ṛkṣāṃścayoniḥ paścādvidhīyate ।।

berodayaṃ triguṇitaṃ śiṣṭamāyaṃ nage hṛte ।
caturbhirguṇitaṃ sapta sauravārādikaṃ dinam ।।

berocca maṣṭaguṇitaṃ saptaviśadibhirhṛtam ।
śiṣṭa maśvyādibhaṃ vindyāttaccheṣaṃ syāccaturguṇam ।।

randhrehṛte navāṃśaṃ taccheṣaṃ bhāṃśayugairhṛtam ।
berodayaṃ triguṇitaṃ yonissyā daṣṭabhirhṛtam ।।

āyādhikye śubhaṃ prokta mṛṇavṛddhir vyayādhike ।
vāreṣu saurisūryārairvinānye śubhadāssmṛtāḥ ।।

taskaraṃ bhuktiśaktī ca dhanaṃ rājyaṃ klibādi ca ।
nirhṛtya cādhanaṃ preṣyaṃ tannāmasadṛśaṃ phalam ।।

nāmakartṛnṛparkṣādyā nāmarkṣānuguṇaṃ bhavet ।
yadākāraṃ dhruvākāraṃ tadākāraṃ ca kautukam ।।

āsane sthānakaṃvāpi śayāne sthāna māsanam ।
deve sthite na devyau ca āsīne sthānakāsane ।।

viparītaṃ na kurvīta sarvaśāstraviśāradāḥ ।
tālaniyamaḥ
śreṣṭhaṃ prādurbhavaṃ tālaṃ kevalaṃ keśavasya tu ।।

taddevīnāṃ sarasvatyā madhyamaṃ daśatālakam ।
candrendrānalakīnāśavaruṇānilaśūlinaḥ ।।

ṛṣayo vasavo rudrā mārkaṇḍeyo amito bhṛguḥ ।
āryāścaiva guho hīnadaśatālamitā matāḥ ।।

maruto api ca yakṣeśadevavadhvaśśubhāgrahāḥ ।
tadhānyetu tridhā sādhyā navatālamitā matāḥ ।।

daityayakṣeśa? randhāśca siddhagandharvacāraṇāḥ ।
kujārkarāhava śśreṣṭhanavatālena sammatāḥ ।।

navatālair munīṃścaiva gaṇāṃścaiva tu mānayet ।
uṅgāścāraṇāścānye navatālamitodayāḥ ।।

martyāścāṣṭāyatāḥ proktāḥ pretānāṃ saptatālakam ।
ṣaḍyamāḥ kubjakāḥ proktā vāmanāḥ pañcatālagāḥ ।।

bhūgatānāṃ catustālaṃ kinnarāstu tritālakāḥ ।
kūśmāṇḍā dvitayāścaiva kabandhā stvekatālakā? ।।

śreṣṭhamadhyakaniṣṭhāni tritālānāntu tatra nai ।
pravakṣyāmi madhūcchiṣṭakriyāṃ pratividhānataḥ ।।

yajamānagṛhevāpi ālaye vā manorame ।
alaṅkṛtya vitānādyaiḥ kuṇḍa maupāsanaṃ kriyāt ।।

āghāraṃ vidhivatkṛtvā vaiṣṇavaṃ ca yajettathā ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ ca hutvātu brāhmaṃ raudraṃ tathaiva ca ।।

vīśaśaiṣikacakrāṃśca vighneśaṃ ca suhūyate ।
tasyāgner dakṣiṇe kuryā dvrīhibhi sthsaṃḍilaṃ tathā ।।

caturaśraṃ tato vṛttaṃ samāstīrya yathā śubham ।
cakraśaiṣikavīśāṃśca krameṇaiva supūjayet ।।

śodhitaṃ tu madhūcchiṣṭa mādāya praṇavena tu ।
"iṣetvorje'tveti mantreṇa pradhānāṃgaṃ prakalpayet ।।

akṣarāṇi ca sannyasya caivaṃ dhyātvābhimṛśya ca ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ ca tato hutvā devā nanyān visṛjya ca ।।

devyādīn pārṣadāṃ statra tattanmantreṇa hūyatām ।
tatsiddhaṃ śilpihaste tu nidhāyaiva hariṃsmaran ।।

yathā nagendriyaṃ grāhyaṃ yoniṣveva samarpayet ।
tathā tantu gṛhītvaiva sthāpanīyantu garbhakam ।।

mānonmānapramāṇena matimān śilpinācaret ।
śanairālipya saṃśoṣya mṛdbhiśca bahirāyasaiḥ ।।

paṭṭairābaddhya vidhinā punarālipya śoṣayet ।
yajamānānukūlarkṣe pūrvavaddhoma mācaret ।।

tathā tulyaṃ ca saṃsthāpya jalatulyakrameṇa vai ।
yuktāṃ siddhiṃ ca saṃprāpya taṃ ca garbhaṃ pratāpayet ।।
śanair mṛdbhedanaṃ kṛtvā vidhinā beramāharet ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase phagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre navamo adhyāyaḥ

atha daśamo adhyāyaḥ

atha daśamo adhyāyaḥ 
aṅkurārpaṇam
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhūparīkṣādikarmaṇām ।
devadevasya viṣṇortu vidhinā cāṃkurārpaṇam ।।

navame saptamevāpi pañcame vātṣahe atha vā ।
ālayābhimukhe vāpi aiśānye cottare api vā ।।

rudrahastaṃ dvijātīnāṃ nṛpāṇāṃ navahastakam ।
vaiśyānāṃ munihastantu śūdrāṇāṃ pañcahastakam ।।

ṣoḍaśastaṃbha saṃyuktaṃ caturdvārasamāyutam ।
maṇḍapaṃ vāta kūṭaṃ vā prapāṃ vā vidhinā caret ।।

gomayālepanaṃ kṛtvā "śāmya'ntviti ca? mantrataḥ ।
śvetatanttulacūrṇaṃ vā sudhācūrṇa mathāpi vā ।।

sūkṣmacūrṇaṃ ca kṛtvā tu vālukairmiśritaṃ tathā ।
prāgragaṃ cottarāgraṃ ca "somaṃrā'jeti mantrataḥ ।।

yugmaṃ ca srāyitvātu darśanīyaṃ ca sundaram ।
cakravālādyalaṅkṛtya pālikāṃkuraśobhitaiḥ? ।।

madhyecakraṃ ca kṛtvātu darśanīyaṃ ca kārayet ।
vitānais staṃbhaveṣṭaiśca darbhamālādyalaṅkṛtam ।।

dharmaṃ jñānaṃ ca vairāgya maiśvaryaṃ ca catuṣṭayam ।
antastsaṃbha catuṣkośe sthāpayedadhidevatāḥ ।।

bāhyānāṃ dvādaśādityā dvādaśānāntu devatāḥ ।
arcayitvā yadhānyāyyaṃ tattadvidhimadhācaret ।।

pañcahastaṃ trihastaṃ vā ekahasta mathāpivā ।
pañcaviṃśatpadaṃ kṛtvā madhye brahmāsanaṃ caret ।।

saṃcārārthaṃ phavantyaṣṭa paritaśca padāni vai ।
prāgādimadhyamāḥ proktā dvārā ścatvāra evaca ।।

śeṣitārkapade dhīmān pālikānāṃ sthitiṃ caret ।
vrīhibhi staṇḍulairvāpi paṅktiṃ kuryā dvidhānataḥ ।।

ṣoḍaśāṃgula māyāmaṃ yathālābhasamunnatam ।
trivedisahitaṃ kuryā dvedāśraṃ brāhma māsanam ।।

pūrvadvārottare śeṣaṃ dakṣiṇadvārapūrvake ।
vakratuṇḍasya pīṭhaṃ syāt paścimadvāradakṣiṇe ।।

paṅktīśa muttaradvāra paścime somapīṭhakam ।
kuṃbhe vātha samabhyarcyet tatpūrveśānta marcayet ।।

ṣaṇṇāṃ pīṭhaṃ prakalpyaiva brahmaṇa ścoktavaccaret ।
aindrādica tathaiśāntaṃ jayādyapsarasor'cayet ।।

āḍhakaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā pādaṃ vā taṇḍuraiḥ pṛthak ।
bāhye aṣṭāṃgulivistāre pīṭhe vā sthaṇḍile apivā ।।

caturaśraṃ suvṛttaṃ catrikoṇaṃ dhanurākṛti ।
daṇḍākāraṃ ca padmābhaṃ vasvaśraṃ samavṛttakam ।।

jayādīnāṃ kramātpīṭhaṃ pālikābāhyata ścharet ।
dikpālānāntuśaktaśce nmaṇḍalāni tu kārayet ।।

bhūmyāṃ vā pūjayet tadvatkuśakūrceṣu satvaraḥ ।
caturaśraṃ trikāṇaṃ ca suvṛttaṃ vajrameva ca ।।

ardhacandraṃ ca ṣaṭkoṇaṃ vṛttaṃ nūpurameva ca ।
digīśamaṇḍalākāra manyeṣāṃ caturaśrakam ।।

aśvadthapallavaṃ dūrvāṃ kuśaṃ cābaddhya madhyame ।
pālikādīn krameṇaiva mṛdā vāpūrayec chuciḥ ।।

gāyatrīmantramuccārya praṇavenādāyamantravit ।
medinīmantra muccārya caiśānyādiṣu pālikāḥ ।।

sannyasyaiva tataḥ kuṃbhān dvāravāme ca sannyaset ।
"rākāmahaṃ' samuccārya dvāradakṣiṇataḥ punaḥ ।।

"sinīvā'līti mantreṇa ācāryaḥ sannyasetkramāt ।
jātikrameṇa caiśāstaṃ pālikānāṃ pade pade ।।

brahmaṇo dakṣiṇe pārśva ācārya ścottarāmughaḥ ।
brāhmamāsana māsthāya devadeva manusmaran ।।

brahmādyān hṛdayātpūrvaṃ praṇidhyāṃ sanniveśayet ।
sthaṇḍilopari kūrceṣu pātrā dāvāhayetkramāt ।।

caturmukhaṃ caturbāhuṃ sarvābharaṇa būṣitam ।
abhayaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ vāmamūrupratiṣṭhitam ।।

kuṇḍikā makṣamālāñca vahantaṃ dakṣavāmayoḥ ।
padmāsanasthaṃ hemābhaṃ śyāmavastrañca padmajam ।।

mūrtimantraissamāvāhya brahmāṇaṃ prāṅmukhaṃ yajet ।
prāgdvāre prāṅmukhaṃ caiva dakṣiṇadvārake tathā ।।

pratyagdvāravimāne api cottaradvārake tadhā ।
abjajaṃ prāṅmukhañcānyān yathāvidhi ca saṃsmaret ।।

bhavanaṃ prāṅmukhādīnāṃ prāṅmukhaśca prajāpatiḥ ।
paṅktimadhye samabhyarcye dbrāhmamantraṃ samuccaran ।।

hemāṅgaṃ pītavastraṃ ca dvibhujaṃ padmadhāriṇam ।
sdhitaṃ karaṇḍikāmauliṃ śeṣaṃ tatpaścimāmukham ।।

anantaṃ sarvanāgānā madhipaṃ vāruṇīpatim ।
phaṇasaptakasaṃyuktaṃ sitābhaṃ prāñjaliṃ smaret ।।

pravālābhaṃ gajamukha māsīnaṃ cottarāmukham ।
kadalīcūtapanasapāśāṃkuśadharaṃ prabhum ।।

ekadaṃṣṭraṃ caturbāhuṃ vagratuṇḍaṃ smaredbudhaḥ ।
pītāṃbare taṃ śyāmābhaṃ khaḍgakheṭakadhāriṇam ।।

dvibhujaṃ
karaṇḍikāmauliṃ paṅktīśaṃ prāṅmukhaṃ smaret ।
sitaṃ śyāmāṃbaraṃ saunyuṃ dvibhujaṃ daṇḍadhāriṇam ।।

karaṇḍamakuṭasaṃyuktaṃ susthitaṃ dakṣiṇāmugham ।
abhrābhāṃraktavastrāntāṃ dvihastāṃbujadhāriṇīm ।।

sarvabhūṣābhūṣitāṅgāṃ jayāmaindrapader'cayet ।
nīlābhāṃ pītavastrāṃ tāṃ dvikarāṃbujadhāriṇīm ।।

bhūṣābhūṣitasarvāṅgāṃ vijayā manaler'cayet ।
kumudābhāṃ haridvastrāṃ dvikarāṃpaṅkajāṅkitām ।।

nānābhūṣābhūṣitāṅgāṃ vindāṃ yāmyapader'cayet ।
dhātakīpatra saṃkāśāṃ nīlanīlāṃbarāvṛtām ।।

dvikarāmaṃbujadharāṃ nandāṃnairṛtipader'cayet ।
dhautābhāṃ pītavastrāṃ tāṃ dvihastāṃbujadhāriṇīm ।।

puṣpābharaṇasaṃyuktāṃ puṣṭikāṃ vāruṇer'cayet ।
svarṇābhāṃ raktavastrāṃ tāṃ dvihastāṃbujadhāriṇīm ।।

kumudvatīṃ bhūṣitāṅgāṃ vāyavye cārcayetkramāt ।
raktābhā mabhrasaṃkāśavasanāṃ bhūṣaṇairvṛtām ।।

dvikarā maṃbujadharāṃ saumye cotbalakāṃ yajet ।
hāṭakābhāṃ haridvastrāṃ padmasaṃyutabāhukām ।।

sarvālaṅkāra saṃyuktāṃ viśogā marcayettataḥ) ।
raktābhāṃ hāṭakābhāṃ ca hariṇīṃ nīlavarṇakām ।।

dhātakīpadra saṃtāśāṃ kumudotpalasannibhām ।
aśokābhāṃ kramādetā dvibhujāḥ padmadhāriṇīḥ ।।

viparītāṃbaradharāḥ sukhāsīnā stadāsanāḥ ।
jayādyāssarvabhūṣāṃgā dhyāyedatreti kecana ।।

medinīṃ caiva rākāṃ ca sinīvālīṃ smaredbudhaḥ ।
medinīṃ pīdavastrāntāṃ śyāmāṅgīṃ dvibhujāṃ sthitām ।।

hastayoḥ pālikāṃ dhṛtvā sukeśīṃ taddigānanām ।
pūrṇacandrapriyāṃ devīṃ pūrṇacandranibhānanām ।।

hemāṅgīṃ raktavastrāntāṃ rākāṃ kuṃbhadharāṃ sthitām ।
śeṣaṃ tadvacchinīvālīṃ sitāṃgīṃ śyāmalāṃbarām ।।

śarāvaṃ dadhatīṃ manye medinīsadṛśāṃ tathā ।
dhyātvātattatpade samyagāsīnāṃ vātha cār'cayet ।।

bījesomaṃ tathā dhyātvā hastābhyāṃ bījadhāriṇam ।
sthānakaṃ vāthacāsīvaṃ cottare dakṣiṇāmukham ।।

evaṃ dhyātvā tatodeva māsanādibhirarcayet ।
haviḥ samyaṅmi vedyaiva baliṃ vā dāpaye dbudhaḥ ।।

jayādīnāṃ kramādvarṇaḥ prādakṣiṇyakrameṇatu ।
vitastiḥ pālikotsedhaṃ tadardhaṃ vipulaṃ mukham ।।

adhovipulanāhena madhyanāhaṃ daśāṃgulam ।
kuṃbhodayaṃ tu tattulyaṃ rasamātraṃ mukhāyatam ।।

kuṃbhoṣṭhamiva vaktavyaṃ kuṃbhakukṣirdaśāṃgulam ।
āśramadvāra saṃyuktaṃ śeṣaṃ tatpālikāsamam ।।

tārotsedhaṃ śarāvaṃ syānmukhaṃ tatpālikāsamam ।
ālayasyottare vāpi aiśānye vā viśeṣataḥ ।।

gomayenopalipyaiva medinīṃ tu samarcayet ।
cakraṃ śāntaṃ samabhyarcya harettajjaṭhare mṛdam ।।

kāṃsyapātre nusannyasya śiṣyasya śirasi nyaset ।
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā ālayaṃ vā pradakṣiṇam ।।

pālikādīn prapūryaiva gāyatrīmantra muccaran ।
aiśānyādiṣu koṇeṣu sthāpayet tāśca pālikāḥ ।।

dvāravāme tu kuṃbhaṃ syāccharāvaṃ dvāradakṣiṇe ।
navavastraissamāveṣṭya pālikādīn samarcayet ।।

kaṅkumudgayavāścāpiniṣpāvāḥ sarṣapāstathā ।
caṇakā stilatilvāśca pātredhānyānicāharet ।।

haviḥpātraṃ tu saṃgṛhya vāyavye soma marcayet ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācya tatkāle tūryaghoṣaṇa mācaret ।।

"imebī'jeti mantreṇa vāpayedaṅkurāṃ stataḥ ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ samuccārya yajamānayuto guruḥ ।।

"somaṃ rā' jeti mantreṇa vāpayedaṅkurāṃ stataḥ ।
vāruṇaṃ mantramuccārya jalanekaṃ tu kārayet ।।

śūdrastu yajamānaścen napapastrairguruṃ punaḥ ।
saṃpūjya dakṣiṇāṃ datvātatastenaiva vāpayet ।।

praṇavenār kapatrairvātathā cairaṇḍapatrakaiḥ ।
ācchādaye dyāvadantaṃ trikālābhyarcanaṃ matam ।।

atra devān visṛjyaiva guptedeśe nidhāpayet ।
vastrairnavaiḥ samācchādya pālikādīn samarcayet ।।

amāvāsyāvyavahite kuryāt sadyā eṃkurārpaṇam ।
saṃkramavyavadhāne api sadya eveti ke ca na ।।

sadyā eṃkuraścedrātrau vā divāvāpi ca kārayet ।
tathā sarvakriyāṃ kṛtvā puṣpairvā taṇḍurais tathā ।।

vāpayetkarmaṇa stasyasadya evatu kārayet ।
pātrālābheśarāvevā yathālābhaṃ ca kārayet ।।

arcayettaṇḍulān śuddhān sadyaḥkālāṃkurārpaṇe ।
gṛhṇīyāt pālikā eva navapañcaikakalpane ।।

brahmaṇo abhimukhecaikaṃ śeṣāntu paritodiśi ।
tattaddigīśa mabhyarcya tattanmantreṇacār'cayet ।।

eṣa eva viśeṣassyā danyatsarvaṃ khiloktavat ।
lakṣaṇaṃ ca tathaivoktaṃ tatraiva ca guṇāguṇāḥ ।।

ajasradīpadānaṃ tu sarvatra vidhinā caret ।
karmānte jalamadhyetu nikṣipe dvijayāṃkurān ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre daśamo adhyāyaḥ

athaikādaśo adhyāyaḥ

athaikādaśo adhyāyaḥ 
bhagavatpratiṣṭhāvidhiḥ
athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi pratiṣṭhāvidhimuttamam
supraśaste muhūrte vai pratiṣṭhāṃ kārayedbudhaḥ ।।

ācāryalakṣaṇam
vaikhānasena sūtreṇa niṣekādikriyānvitān ।
viprān vedavidaśśreṣṭhān dhārmikān jñāpatatparān ।।

saumyān jitendriyān śuddhān viṣṇorārādhane parān ।
ūhāpohavidhānena dhvastasaṃśayamānasān ।।

patnyapatyayutān śāntān snānaśīlān surūpiṇaḥ ।
āhūya pūjyatatraikaṃ sarvakāryopadeśakam ।।

ācāryaṃ varayitvaiva tenoktaṃ sarva mācaret ।
bhūmiḥ parīkṣitā yena guruṇā vidhipūrvakam ।।

karṣaṇādipratiṣṭhāntaṃ karma tenaiva kārayet ।
ūrdhvepyācāryakarmāṇi tatra tenaiva kārayet ।।

tadabhāve tu tatputraṃ pautraṃ naptārameva vā ।
tasyaiva bhrātaraṃ śiṣyaṃ praśiṣyaṃ gurumeva vā ।।

sabrahmacāriṇaṃ vāpi pūrvābhāve tathottaram ।
tadanujñāta mitara mācāryatve niyojayet ।।

anyadhā ce nmahāndoṣo rājā rāṣṭraṃ ca naśyati ।
kṣīyante varṇadharmāśca jāyate varṇasaṃkaraḥ ।।

agnihotrā na sīdanti svādhyāyo na pravartate ।
viparītāni cānyāni bhaviṣyantyadharottaram ।।

tasmācchāstroktavidhinā sarvakarmāṇi kārayet ।
śvetagandhānulepaiśca śvetapuṣpāṃgulīyakaiḥ ।।

ācāryādīn samaphyarcya namaskṛtya svadaivavat ।
"karmedaṃ me kuru'ṣveti yāce dācārya mādarāt ।।

śiṣyaḥ samarpayetsarvaṃ bharamācāryapādayoḥ ।
ācāryaḥ suprasannātmā śiṣyānugrahatatparaḥ ।।

tathaiveti susaṃkalpya kuryāccaivāṃkurārpaṇam ।
aṅkurārpaṇakādūrdhva māraṃbhadivasādadhaḥ ।।

kūśmāṇḍahoma mabjāgnaukārayedgururatvaraḥ ।
śuddhadantanakhaścaiva śvetavastrottarīyakaḥ ।।

triṣavaṇasnānanirato haviṣyāśī jitendriyaḥ ।
evaṃ krameṇavai vidvān ṛtvigbhiḥ sārthamācaret ।।

araṇīṃ srukcruvaucaiva juhūmupabhṛtaṃ tathā ।
maṅgalāni ca darvīṃ ca toraṇāni yathākramam ।।

nyagrodhaplakṣā paśvadthaṃ pitṛvṛkṣayutaṃ tathā ।
toraṇārthaṃ samāhṛtya lakṣaṇena samanvitam ।।

athāṣṭamaṅgalaṃ vakṣyedvitālāyatameva ca ।
prādeśavistṛtaṃ kuryāt ṣaḍaṅgula mathāpi vā ।।

ghanaṃ syāc caturaṅgulya? mata vā dvyaṅgulaṃbhavet ।
tasya madhye likhe dvidvān tattadrūpaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।।

śrīvatsaṃ pūrṇakuṃbhaṃ ca bherī mādarśanaṃ tathā ।
matsyayugmāṅkuśau śaṅkha māvartaṃ cāṣṭamaṅgalam ।।

āvartalakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye pañcaviṃśatpadaṃ tathā ।
īśādinairṛtāntantu padaṃ tristriḥkrameṇa ca ।।

pūrvamadhyamapāścātyapadānyevatu yojayet ।
vāyuvye tvagnikoṇānta mudaṅmadhyamadakṣiṇe ।।

antarālapadāṃścāṣṭau vinaiva tu vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
etaiśca saptadaśabhi rāvarta mabhidhīyate ।।

śaṅkhacakragadācāpā asiḥ pañcāyudhānyapi ।
srucaḥ sruvasya daṇḍaṃ tu prādeśatraya māyatam ।।

mūlaṃ prādeśamātraṃ syā dagranāhaṃ tadardhakam ।
agre bilvaphalākāraṃ prādeśa pratimaṇḍalam ।।

dvyaṅgulaṃ syāttadāsyantu kartaṃ māṣadvayāvadhi ।
sruvamevaṃ prakurvīta dviprādeśa mathāpivā ।।

juhūdaṇḍasamāyāmaṃ caturviṃśatakāṅgulam ।
nāhaṃ tadardha mityuktaṃ padmasya mukulopamam ।।

ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ tu tasyāgraṃ nāhaṃ tasya vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
yugāṅgulāgravistāra maṣṭāṃgula mathāyatam ।।

śeṣaṃ tu tṣaśra mityuktaṃ vistṛtonnata maṅgulam ।
madhyagartānupūrvyeṇa juhvāścaivakramaṃ viduḥ ।।

paścādupabhṛtaṃ kuryāt prādeśatraya māyatam ।
prādeśaṃ nāhamityuktaṃ mūlādagraṃ tadardhakam ।।

ānupūrvyātkṛśaṃ daṇḍaṃ galāntamiti saṃjñitam ।
ūrdhve prādeśamāyāmaṃ caturaśraṃ ṣaḍaṅgulam ।।

tadūrdhver'dhāṅgulāyāmaṃ kaṇṭha mevaṃ pracakṣate ।
śeṣaṃ tu tṣaśrakaṃ kuryāt tatra tenaiva kārayet ।।

unnatāsyāṅgulārdhaṃ syādbhittyuccamiti kathyate ।
oṣṭha mekāṅgulaṃ jñātvā tanmadhyenimna mācaret ।।

pūrṇacantrākṛtiṃ kṛtvā prādeśaṃ tasya nāhakam ।
nimnaṃ caturyavāgāḍha magrāntastu kramādbudhaḥ ।।

atha darvyāstathāyāmaṃ caturviṃśatikāṃgulam ।
ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ tadagraṃ syāt pucchaṃ pañcāṃgulaṃ bhavet ।।

śeṣaṃ trayodaśāṃgulyādaṇḍa mityucyate kramāt ।
mūlasthūlaṃ bhavennārī agrasthūlaṃ napuṃsakam ।।

mūlādagraṃ kramādvṛttaṃ puṃrūpa mītikathyate ।
darbhairmālāṃ ca kṛtvaiva tasyāṃ parvaṇi parvaṇi ।।

dvaudvaudarbhau vivikṣipya dvitālaṃ laṃbayetkramāt ।
dvitālāyāmasaṃyuktaṃ khādiraṃ daṇḍameva ca ।।

daśāṃgulaparīṇāhaṃ samavṛttaṃ tathaiva hi ।
śākhāṃgulasamāyuktaṃ mūlādagraṃ tu bandhayet ।।

tattāmrāyasapaṭṭairvābandhayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
tanmūle suṣiraṃ kṛtvā golakaṃ tatpramāṇakam ।।

evantu manthadaṇḍassyāt kuryāt tacchāstrapāragaḥ ।
śamījāta mathāśvadtha maraṇyarthaṃ pragṛhya ca ।।

ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ tu vistāraṃ golakaṃ tu ghanaṃ bhavet ।
dairghyaṃ tasya dvitālaṃ syātphalakāṃ kārayedbudhaḥ ।।

tathaivopari paṭṭiṃ ca kṛtvā tatra vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
maiñjyaiva trivṛtāṃ rajjuṃ manthanārthāya kārayet ।।

daśāṣṭanavabhirhastairvastra māyata mucyate ।
tricatuḥpañcatālaṃ vāvistṛtaṃ vastramucyate ।।

gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ cāhareta kāpilaṃ tu gavādiṣu ।
ājaṃ ca māhiṣaṃ tyājyaṃ pakṣātītaṃ ca varjayet ।।

pādauprakṣālyacācamya pūrvodaṅmukha evavā ।
brāhmamāsasa māsthāya vaiṣṇavaṃ mantramuccaran ।।

paristaraṇakūrcādīn samithādīn pragṛhyaca ।
kūrcaṃ pradakṣiṇāvartaṃ gṛhṇīyā dvidhivittamaḥ ।।

pramukhe dakṣiṇe vāpi yāgaśālāṃ prakalpayet ।
yāgaśālā
ṣoḍaśastaṃbhasaṃyuktaṃ maṇḍapaṃ kūṭamevavā ।।

prapāṃ vā tatra kurvīta madhye kūṭaṃ ca kārayet ।
nimnonnataṃ vibhajyaiva jalasthalasamīpakam ।।

pūrvoktena vidhānena alaṅkṛtya yathākramam ।
madhye vediṃ prakalpyaivabiṃbādhyardha pramāṇataḥ ।।

tadbahiḥpūrvabhāgetu sabhyakuṇḍaṃ prakalpayet ।
sabhyasya pūrvabhāgetu kuṇḍa māhavanīyakam ।।

uttarevāpunaḥ kuryā daupāsanavidhānataḥ ।
sabhyasya dakṣiṇe kuṇḍaṃ paiṇḍarīkaṃ prakalpayet ।।

vedyāstu dakṣiṇekuṇḍamanvāhāryaṃ prakalpayet ।
nairṛte devatāsthānaṃ kalpayetta dvicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

vaidyāntu paścime bhāge gārhapatyaṃ prakalpayet ।
vāyavye saṃcayasthānaṃ kalpayet tadvidhānataḥ ।।

vedyāstathottare bhāge tvāvasadhyaṃ prakalpayet ।
aiśānye snāpanaśvabhraṃ kalpayet tadvidhānataḥ ।।

sabhyasya paiṇḍarīkasya maikhalātrayamucyate ।
anyeṣāṃ caiva kuṇḍānāṃ mekhalādvayameva hi ।।

ekaikavedyā vistāra munnataṃ caturaṅgulam ।
sabhyasya madhyamaṃ pañca padmasyādhaṣṣaḍaṅgulam ।।

aupāsananorthvavedyāssyā dunnataṃ tu dviyaṅgulam ।
dakṣiṇottarayoścaiva saṃsthānaṃ brahmasomayoḥ ।।

dvādaśāṃgulasaṃyuktaṃ caturaśraṃ suvṛttakam ।
śalyaloṣṭatuṣāṃgāratṛṇabhasmādihīnayā ।।

mṛdā vā vālukais tatra pṛthakkuṇḍaṃ prakalpayet ।
yāgasthānasya pūrvetu prapāṃ kṛtvā vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

nayanonmīlanār'thāya yāgaśālāṃ prakalpayet ।
nayanonmīlanam
uktakriyāvasāne tu beramādāyacātvaraḥ ।।

śilpinā śāstramārgeṇa kārayedakṣimocanam ।
devasya pramukhe kuryād dhānyarāśiṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

hemaśruṅgāṃ raupyakhurāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyadohanām ।
savatsāṃgāṃ samādāya devasya pramukhe nyaset ।।

ghṛtaṃ madhudadhikṣīraṃ gṛhītvā kāṃsyabhājane ।
rukmantatraiva nikṣipya dīpayuktaṃ tu vinyaset ।।

hemapātraistu sūcībhyāṃ rajatairvāpi cāharet ।
hūlikāṃ tāṭanīñcaiva śīlāṃ lohamayasyavai ।।

biṃbasya cottare pārśve vāstuhomaṃ yajettataḥ ।
paryagni caiva kṛtvātu prokṣayet pañcagavyakaiḥ ।।

uttarābhimukho dehaghuddhiṃ kṛtvā gurustataḥ ।
hūlikāṃ tāṭanīñcaiva gṛhītvā mantrapūrvakam ।।

"viṣṇustvāṃ rakṣa'tvityuktvā viṣṇusūktaṃ ca saṃsmaran ।
paṭasya cāntardevasya mūrdhādīn saṃspṛśetkramāt ।।

viṣṇugāyatrī muccārya tatra karma samācaret ।
devībhyāṃ ca krameṇaiva tattanmastraṃ japettadā ।।

paścāttupātre sūcībhyāṃ kṛhītvā cākṣimocanam ।
ṣaṇmaṇḍalāni saṃskuryādadhideva manusmaran ।।

pakṣmavarma ca raktañca śvetaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ca taijasam ।
etaistu maṇḍalaṃ dhyātvā dṛḍhīkṛtvātvaraḥ kramāt ।।

hitvār'karāhusaurāṇā mudayantu dvilocane ।
nayanonmīlanaṃ kuryātsarvasaṃpatsamṛddhaye ।।

andhanakṣatrake kuryātsarvanāśaṃ na saṃśayaḥ ।
puruṣasūktaṃ japitvaiva dakṣiṇe nayane nyaset ।।

tadhaiva vāmanetretu vaiṣṇavaṃ mantra muccaran ।
tatsūktābhyāṃ viśeṣeṇa śrībhūmyośca samācaret ।।

devasyāṃgaṃ spṛśan hutvā maulimālādipūrvakam ।
tathā devyośca hutvātu dadbhyassyāhādinā pṛthak ।।

vimānaṃ nūtanaṃ cettu sdhūpyādīnāṃ hutaṃ caret ।
parṣadāṃ mūrtimantreṇa kārayenmantravittamaḥ ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktañca sviṣṭākāraṃ ca hūyatām ।
godānasūkta muccārya kavādīnabhimṛśya ca ।।

paṭaṃ paścā dvisṛjyaiva gavādīn saṃpradarśayet ।
gavādidravya mādāya dadyācca gurave tataḥ ।।

kautukādī nviśeṣeṇa pūrvoktena krameṇavai ।
berapīṭhe ca saṃpādya ratnādīni vinikṣipet ।।

ratnaṃ dhātūṃśca bījāni suvarṇaṃ cā atra nikṣipet ।
evaṃ saṃsthāpya matimān saṃtāpyaiva dṛḍhaṃ yathā ।।

dhruvaberoktavatkṛtvā nayanonmīlanaṃ caret ।
paścājjalādhivāsādīn kuryāt tanmantrapāragaḥ ।।

pañcagavyaṃ pragṛhyaiva prokṣayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
vasoḥpavitramityuktvātatra kāryaṃ samcaret ।।

paścāt kṣīraṃ samādāya prokṣayitvā samāhitaḥ ।
"śanno devī'ritiprocya tena karma samācaret ।।

arthadarśī pragṛhyaiva devasyāgre nidhāyaca ।
pradīpa marpaye dvadvān jale tatrādhivāsayet ।।

evañcātrādhivāsyaiva cāsyabereṣuvai punaḥ ।
pañcagavyādhivāsaṃ ca tathā kṣīrādhivāsanam ।।

etaddvayaṃ vinā tatra kuryāttoyādhivāsanam ।
grāme sarvatra tadrātrau prabhūtaṃ nikṣipedbalim ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre ekādaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha dvādaśo adhyāyaḥ

bhagavatpratiṣṭhāvidhiḥ
athapradoṣe dharmātmā jalasthaṃ devamuddharet ।
snānadravyāṇi cāhṛtya devaṃ saṃsnāpya mantravit ।।

kṣaumapaṭṭādinā chādya maṇihemādikaiḥ punaḥ ।
vividhaiḥ puṣpamālādyair alaṅkṛtya manoharam ।।

yāna māropya deveśaṃ svaktisūktaṃ samuccaran ।
toyadhārāṃ puraskṛtya nītvā grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇam ।।

śvabhrasya paścime bhāge sthāpayitvā viśeṣataḥ ।
uttare yāgaśālāyāṃ vāstu homaṃ samācaret ।।

mathitvāgniṃ pragṛhṇīyā dvāstu homāgnimeva vā ।
saṃskṛtya vidhinādāya praṇaye dgārhapatyake ।।

trissaṃskṛto laukikāgnir mathitāgnisamo bhavet ।
āghāraṃ vidhivatkṛtvā vaiṣṇavāntaṃ samācaret ।।

tato anvāhāryakuṇḍe ca paścādāhavanīyake ।
āvasathyetatassabhye tataḥpadmānalekramāt ।।

sūtroktena vidhānena sarvatrāghāramācaret ।
dvātriṃśatprasthasaṃpūrṇaṃ ghaṭamādāyacātvaraḥ ।।

"iṣe tvorje'tvādi japan tantunā pariveṣṭya ca ।
"śucī vo havya' ityuktvā kuṃbhaprakṣālanaṃ caret ।।

nadītoyaṃ samādāya samutpūya ca pūrayet ।
vastrayugmena cāveṣṭya alaṅkuryāt prayatnataḥ ।।

elātakkolakarpūrair gandhośīrākṣataiḥkramāt ।
anyairgandhayutaiḥ puṣpairvāsayitvā vidhānataḥ ।।

suvarṇaratnadhātūṃśca nyasitvā mantravittamaḥ ।
govālakuśadarbhaiśca kṛtaṃ kūrcaṃ tu nikṣipet ।।

atha vā nikṣipet kūrcaṃ kṛtaṃ darbhaistu kevalaiḥ ।
asthi ratnaṃ sirā stantur māṃso mṛtsnā prakīrtitā ।।

śoṇitaṃ raktamṛdbhintu jalaṃ medastathaiva ca ।
śukrantu kūrcamityuktaṃ vastraṃ syāccarma vaiṣṭitam ।।

sapta dhātava ityete kuṃbheṣu karakeṣu ca ।
eteṣvekaṃ vinākuryānnāsti tatrāsya sannidhiḥ ।।

devasya dakṣiṇe pārśve kuṃbhaṃ tatra niveśya ca ।
alaṅkṛtastathācāryo vastrābharaṇakuṇḍalaiḥ ।।

sraggandhairveṣṭito dhṛtmā mukhasyoṣṇīṣabandhanam ।
kuṃbhasya dakṣiṇe bhāge prāṅmukhodaṅmukho apivā ।।

svastikāsana māsthāya ṛjukāyaḥ samāhitaḥ ।
lalāṭādiṣu sthāneṣu keśavādīn praṇamyaca ।।

akārādyakṣaraṃ sarvaṃ nyasitvā sarvasandhiṣu ।
paścātkuṃbhaṃ susaṃtpṛśya kramātsūktādikaṃ japet ।।

ātmasūktantato japtvā pauruṣaṃ sūktameva ca ।
sūktamekākṣaraṃ japtvā viṣṇusūkta mataḥ param ।।

śrībhūsūktaṃ tato japtvā "sahasraśīrṣaṃ'samuccaran ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ tu tatojaptvā dhyāyet samyaksamāhitaḥ ।।

prāṇāyāmaṃ tataḥ kuryāt recapūrakakuṃbhakaiḥ ।
etatphalaṃ kramādvakṣye trividhaṃ tatpṛthagvidham ।।

tatraiva recakaṃ pūrvaṃ sarvapāpasyadāhakam ।
paścāttu pūrakaṃ kuryā damṛtāpyāyanaṃ tataḥ ।।

tṛtīyaṃ kuṃbhakaṃ kuryā damṛtatvaṃ ca saṃsmaret ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena recakādīni kārayet ।।

kuṃbhagantu jalaṃ smṛtvā vāruṇaṃ maṇḍalaṃ budhaḥ ।
ardhacandrākṛtiṃ smṛtvā tasya bījākṣaraṃ nyaset ।।

tamoṅkāreṇa saṃveṣṭya bandhayuktaṃ? tu niśmalam ।
ādityamaṇḍalāntasthaṃ devaṃ tatraiva cāhvayet ।।

ādibījaṃ suvarṇābhaṃ praṇavaiḥ pariveṣṭitam ।
paścāddevaṃ samabhyarcya kuryā darghyānta marcanam ।।

biṃbaṃ kuṃbhaṃ ca saṃgṛhya snānaśvabhre niveśayet ।
śvabhrasya pūrvabhāge tu daṇḍapaṅktiṃ ca kārayet ।।

kalaśaiḥ snāpayetsamya kcaturdaśabhirevatu ।
devaṃ sarvatra saṃsnāpya dīpāntaṃ ca samarcayet ।।

nairṛte viṣṭare nyasya nameddevāṃ tsamāhitaḥ ।
evaṃ devyau samādāya snāpaye datvaraṃ budhaḥ- ।।

pādyamācamanaṃ datvā devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।
pātraṃ tu taṇḍulaiḥ pūrṇaṃ gṛhītvātra viśeṣataḥ ।।

sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi kautukaṃ tatra nikṣipet ।
atha vā tantu māhṛtya nyasitvā taṇḍulopari ।।

tāṃbūlasahite pātre? devasyāgre nidhāyaca ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācya tatkālesvastisūktaṃ samuccaran ।।

devasya dakṣiṇehaste devyoryai vāmahastayoḥ ।
"svastidā' vītimantreṇa kautukaṃ bandhayetkramāt ।।

vedamantrajña ācāryo rakṣāmantraṃ samuccaran ।
ṣaḍdroṇaṃ dhānyamardhaṃ vā vedikopari cāstaret ।।

tadardhaṃ taṇḍulāṃścaiva tadagdhaṃ tu tilānapi ।
tadagdhaṃ yavamādāya tadardhaṃ tilvameva ca ।।

aṇḍajaṃ muṇḍajaṃ caivaromajaṃ vāmajaṃ tathā ।
carmajaṃ cāstaretpañca śayanaṃ vedikopari ।।

alābhe tu tathaitaiṣāṃ pañcavastrāṇi vāstaret ।
mūrdhopadhānaṃ kartavyamūrdhve anastaṃ samarcayet ।।

devaṃ devyau samādāya yaddigdvāraṃ tathā śiraḥ ।
śāyayecchayane vidvān "yadvaiṣṇava'miti bruvan ।।

devyoścāpi tathā kuryāttattatsūktaṃ japetkramāt ।
uttarācchādanaṃ kuryādgalāntaṃ tatra nikṣipet? ।।

śayyāvedyāstuparitassarvān devāntsamarcayert ।
iśānādikramāddevān balyantantu samarcayet ।।

śaṅkaraṃ balirakṣaṃ ca vāgdevīṃ baliśrakrakau ।
agniṃ pavitraṃ śailūṣaṃ prācyāṃ pratyaṅmukhān kramāt ।।

bhaumaṃ guhaṃ ca durgāṃ ca yamaṃ mandaṃ ca nairṛtim ।
rohiṇīṃ saptamātṝśca dakṣiṇe cottarāmukhān ।।

paścime nairṛtādyādīnarcayettadanukramāt ।
vaiṣṇavīṃ puruṣaṃ caiva budhaṃ jyeṣṭhāṃ tathaiva ca ।।

puṣparakṣakavāyū ca prāṅmukhāṃśca samarcayet ।
vāyavyādīśaparyastaṃ dakṣiṇābhimūkhān kramāt ।।

śukraṃ caiva bhṛguṃ śāntaṃ tathā sapta ṛṣīnapi ।
bhāgīrathīṃ kuberaṃ ca candraṃ bhūtāni cār'cayet ।।

dvāre dvāre ca dhātrādīn dvāradevāntsamarcayet ।
vimānaṃ parito bhyarcya nyakṣādīnarcayetkramāt ।।

devasyāgre prasannātmā pūjayedanapāyinaḥ ।
bhūtadvayaṃ tathā tārkṣyaṃ tathā caivāmitaṃ budhaḥ ।।

cakraśaṅkhāravindāni devasyāgrer'cayedbudhaḥ ।
vedānadhyāpayeddikṣu "ṛcāṃ prā'cīriti śrutiḥ ।।

saṃbhāravedyāmāstīrya dhānyaṃ vastrovarikramāt ।
hemādipātre ratnādīṃ tsannyasyaivādhidaivatam ।।

viṣṇumabhyarcya vidhinā kārayitvādhivāsanam ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ samuccārya vastreṇācchādayedbudhaḥ ।।

paścāddhotāramāhūya yathoktaguṇasaṃyutam ।
pādauprakṣālya cācamya kūrcayuktaṃ samāhitam ।।

alaṅkuryācca puṣpādyaiḥ pañcāṅgocitabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।
sabhyasya pūrvabhāge tu paścimābhimukhaḥsthitaḥ ।।

sabhyādhvaryuṃ samīkṣyaiva hotā praṇavamuccaret ।
"hotarehi' pade uktetato hotā samuccaret ।।

"adhvaryo deva'tetyuktvā pādau prakṣālya cācamet ।
pūrvavattatra casthitvā "oṃ namaḥ pravaktre' bruvan ।।

hotā ca nāma śarmāntaṃ saṃyojyaiva samuccaret ।
"bhūte bhaviṣya'tītyuktvā brūyād "dhiṃ'kārapūrvakam ।।

"bhūrbhuvassuva' rityeva prāṅmukhaśca pradakṣiṇam ।
adadhyātsamidho adhvaryuḥ pratyoṅkāraṃ tato anale ।।

hotrā"gne mahā'mityukteprabhauḥ pravara iṣyate ।
rājño vā rājapatmyā vā tathāmātyasya vā bhavet ।।

grāmaścedyajamānastu vasiṣṭhapravaraṃ vadet ।
atha vā kārayedvidvān kāśyapravaraṃ vadan ।।

vaiśyādanyatra jātīyo yajamāno bhavedyadi ।
tasya tu pravaraṃ hitvā kāśyapapravaraṃ vadet ।।

tata "āyātu bhagavā'nuktvā paścimadiṅmukhaḥ ।
viṣṇvādi bhūta paryantaṃ sarvamūrtī stadāhvayet ।।

nanadhoktena mārgeṇa pārṣadānāhvayedbudhaḥ ।
āvāhana krameṇaiva nirupyā'jyāhutīryajet ।।

sabhyāgniṃ ca paristīrya prāṇāyāmādipūrvakam ।
"svasticai'veti hutvātu tathā caiva "prajāpateḥ' ।।

"agnirdhīmata'yetyuktvā "ādityebhya'stathaiva ca ।
"viśvebhyo devebhya'ścaiva "marudgaṇebhya'eva ca ।।

"bhūragnaye'caivamādyāścatasro vyāhṛtīryajet ।
daśabhiśsataśastvetaissahasrāhutirucyate ।।

sruveṇa srāvayan vidvānavicchinnaṃ samācaret ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ samuccārya sūktaṃ pauruṣameva ca ।।

śrīsūktaṃ bhūmidaivatya matodevādi vaiṣṇavam ।
ekākṣarādisūktaṃ tu viṣṇugāyatriyā yutam ।।

etaintu saptabhissūktaiścaturāvartya hūyatām ।
etatkartumaśaktaścetsakṛdvātra samācaret ।।

aṣṭākṣareṇa mantreṇa dvādaśākṣarakeṇa vā ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇugāyatrīṃ juhuyāditi ke cana ।।

tataścāhāvanīyāgnikuṇḍe samyagyathākramam ।
yajetpuruṣasūktaṃ tu ṣoḍaśāvartya yatnataḥ ।।

anvāhārvāgnikuṇḍe tu viṣṇusūktaṃ suhūyatām ।
brāhmañca vyāhṛtīścaiva jayādīn juhuyātkramāt ।।

śrīsūktaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ caiva juhuyādgārhapatyake ।
āvasadthye viśeṣeṇa vaiṣṇavaṃ rudrasūktakam ।।

mahīsūktaṃ ca juhuyatsūktamekākṣarādikam ।
paiṇḍarīke tu juhuyātpāramātmikasaṃyutam ।।

raktābjaṃ bilvapatraṃ ca śvetābjānāmasaṃbhave ।
ghṛtenāplutya juhuyādviṣṇugāyatriyā budhaḥ ।।

samidājyaṃ carur lājāḥ sarṣapāśca yavāstathā ।
tilaṃ tilvaṃ tathā mudgā māṣāssakturguḍaṃ tathā ।।

madhvapūpā dadhi kṣīraṃ homadravyamitīritam ।
etaissaptadaśadravyair vaiṣṇavaṃ juhuyādbudhaḥ ।।

juhvācaivopajuhvā ca viṣṇusūktaṃ suhūyatām ।
sabhye ca vaiṇḍarīke ca sviṣṭākāraṃ vinā caret ।।

agniṣvāhavanīyādiṣvantahomaṃ samācaret ।
ṛgādīṃśca caturdikṣu vedānadhyāpayetkramāt ।।

evamadhyayanaṃ prokta"mṛcāṃ prācī'riti śrutiḥ ।
nṛttaigenyaiśca vādyaiśca rātriśeṣaṃ nayatkramāt ।।

tataḥprabhāte dharmātmā snātvāsnānavidhānataḥ ।
brahmayajñaṃ ca kṛtvā tu japetsūktāni dvādaśa ।।

pādau prakṣyālya cācamya devānuddhāpya mantravat ।
pūrvavastraṃ visṛjyaiva punaranyadvibhūṣya ca ।।

brahmasthāne viśeṣeṇa pīṭhaṃ samyak prakalpayet ।
tadūrdhve kalpayedvidvān navabhāgaṃ vibhajya ca ।।

pūrvoktena krameṇaiva ratnanyāse samācaret ।
sudhayā paripūryaiva kṣaumenācchādayedbudhaḥ ।।

yajamānastu tatkāle ācāryādīn praṇamyaca ।
sapādanavaniṣkaṃ ca gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadet ।।

pratyekaṃ sthāpakādīnāṃ pañcaniṣkaṃ dadettadā ।
sabhyādhvaryorviśeṣeṇa hotuścāpi tathaiva ca ।।

paiṇḍarīkasya cādhvaryoḥ pratyekaṃ pañcaniṣkakam ।
anyeṣvāhavanīyādiṣvadhvaryūṇāṃ catubhanvet ।।

paṣanddhāmasu cādhvaryoranyeṣāṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak ।
niṣkaṃ pādādhikaṃ dadyātsaṃpūrṇamiti paṭhyate ।।

ācāryasya niyogena dakṣiṇādānamīritam ।
yajamānassvatantreṇa na kuryāditi śāsanam ।।

hantyalpadakṣiṇo yajño yajamānaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
adakṣiṇaṃ tu yajanaṃ niṣphalaṃ tviti śāsanam ।।

muhūrte samanuprāpte vādyaghoṣasamanvitam ।
toyadhārāsamāyuktaṃ svastisūktaṃ samuccaran ।।

ācāryaḥ kuṃbhamādāya vrajetpūrvaṃ tataḥkramāt ।
nayeyusthsāpakāḥ paścāddevaṃ depyādisaṃyutam ।।

pradakṣiṇaṃ śanaigantvā devāgāraṃ praviśya ca ।
pīṭhasya dakṣiṇe bhāge dhānyapīṭhe prakalpite ।।

ācāryassannyasetkuṃbhaṃ devaṃ cādāyacātvaraḥ ।
kautukaṃ brahmasthāne tu sthāpayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

"bhūrasi bhūṃ' ityuktvā pīṭhe devaṃ suyojayet ।
tasya dakṣiṇapāśenv tu śrīdevīṃ sthāpayedbudhaḥ ।।

tathaiva vāmapāśenv tu bhūmiṃ kuryātpratiṣṭhitām ।
devasya vāmabhāge tu sthāpayedbiṃbamotsavam ।।

snāpanaṃ baliberaṃ ca dakṣiṇe sthāpayedbudhaḥ ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ ca japtyaiva puruṣasūktayutaṃ tathā ।।

dhruvasūktaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca devībhyāṃ ca pṛthak pṛthak ।
śrībhūsūktaṃ pṛthak japtvā paścānnyāsaṃ samācaret ।।

"suvabhunvabhūn'rityuktvā cākṣarāṇi viśeṣataḥ ।
pādayorantare vidvān yakāraṃ vinyasettataḥ ।।

biṃbasya hṛdaye samyaṅnyasedbījākṣaraṃ param ।
rukmābhaṃ paramaṃ bījaṃ sarvakāraṇakāraṇam ।।

taruṇārka sahasrābhaṃ brahmeśābhyāṃ namaskṛtam ।
padmāsanasthaṃ deveśaṃ śrīvatkālaṅkṛtorasam ।।

śaṅkhacakradharaṃ saumyaṃ sarvābharaṇa bhūṣitam ।
"o'mityekākṣaraṃ brahma praṇavaḥ paripaṭhyate ।।

"śrī'kāraṃ śriya ityuktvā "la'kāraṃ bhuva ityapi ।
kūrcenādāya tattoyaṃ kuṃbhasthaṃ śaktisaṃyutam ।।

"idaṃ viṣṇu'ssamuccārya samādāya samāhitaḥ ।
"āyātu bhagavā'nuktvādhruvaberasya mūrdhavi ।।

viṣṇuṃ ca puruṣaṃ satyamacyutaṃ cāniruddhakam ।
acale devadeveśo vyāpya tiṣṭhatīti śrutiḥ ।।

"śriye jā'teti mantreṇa śriyamāvāhayedbudhaḥ ।
"medi'nīti ca mantreṇa hariṇīṃ samyagāhvayet ।।

kautukecautsavecaiva snāpane baliberake ।
praṇidhimuddhṛtya tatkāle dīpāddīpamiva kramāt ।।

dhruvaberātsamāvāhya kūrcenāvāhayetkramāt ।
navadhā mārgamālokya yatheṣṭaṃ karturicchayā ।।

avicchinnār'canaṃ nityaṃ vidhinaiva prakalpayet ।
aśaktaścettathākartuṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ naiva kārayet ।।

āḍhyassarvasamastyāgī cikīrṣurviṣṇumandiram ।
svārthaṃ kṛtvā tridhaikāṃśaṃ kuṭuṃbārthe vidhāya ca ।।

aṃśābhyāmavaśiṣṭābhyāṃ vimānārcanamārabhet ।
āpadyapi ca kaṣṭāyāṃ na druhyedātmane budhaḥ ।।

avicchinnā yathā pūjā vidhinā saṃpravartate ।
tathā prakalpayedvidvān bhūmibhogena vai sthitim ।।

arcakasyār'canār'thaṃ ca kuṭuṃbārthaṃ ca yatnataḥ ।
atyantapuṣkalāṃ bhūmiṃ bahusasyocitāṃ tathā ।।

karagrahādi rahitāmarcakāya samarpayet ।
tataśca tāmrapaṭṭādau lekhya sīmāviniścayam ।।

devanāmnaiva tāṃ bhūmiṃ dadyādarcakajīvikām ।
idamagre prakurvīti tadadhīnā sthitirhareḥ ।।

pitā haristu bhagavānarcakaḥ putra ucyate ।
putrasyana likhennāma sannidhāne pituḥkramāt ।।

arcakassuprasannātmā harideva hi kevalam ।
atha vā vilikhedvidvān nāmnā vā pūjaka sya ca ।।

tathār'cakasya cāvāsamālayasya samīpataḥ ।
śilābhissudṛḍhaṃ kṛtvā vāsāyāsya praśasyate ।।

akleśena yathā jīvedarcakassusamāhitaḥ ।
yāvaccandradivānāthaṃ tathā kuryātprayatnataḥ ।।

arcake kleśayuktetu kliśyate bhagavān hariḥ ।
arcake tu susaṃtuṣṭe tadā tuṣṭo janārdanaḥ ।।

rūpadvayaṃ hareḥ proktaṃ biṃbamarcaka evaca ।
biṃbe tvāvāhanādarvāksadā sannihitor'cake ।।

punarvicintya dharmātmā yajamāno mudānvitaḥ ।
śaktilobhamakṛtvaiva karoti vibhavāntaram ।।

pañcaparvasu saṃkrāntau puṇyāheṣvitareṣu ca ।
viśeṣa pūjanārthañca havirarthaṃ ca yatnataḥ ।।

snapanārthaṃ cotsavārthaṃ prāyaścittārthameva ca ।
naṭanartakadāsīnāṅgāyakānāṃ caśaktitaḥ ।।

vidyārthināṃ ca bhaktānāmanyasya vibhavasya ca ।
vṛttiṃ tuparikalpyaiva bhūrūpāṃ purato hareḥ ।।

dadātyācāryahaste tu mantrodakapurassaram ।
anyeṣāṃ vibhavānāṃ catathaivānyapadārthinām ।।

tattannāmnaiva bhūmyādiṃ dāpayeddeśikottamaḥ ।
ācāryasyāpi tannāmnā kalpayedvṛttimuttamām ।।

evaṃ yaḥ kurute bhaktyā aihikāmuṣmikaṃ phalam ।
paśubhṛtyādibhogāṃśca vāhanādīn viśeṣataḥ ।।

suvarṇaratnadhānyādīnatyantaṃ samavāpnuyāt ।
tasya kāyakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva naśyati ।।

yaṃ yaṃ kāmayate sarvantaṃ tamāpnotyasaṃśayam ।
pūrvajātigatāstasya pitaraḥ pituranvaye ।।

mātṛpakṣe ca yejātāstasya mātāmahādayaḥ ।
sarvepi tridivaṃ yānti modante tridive ciram ।।

tato yāsyanti vaikuṇṭhaṃ nissamābhyadhikaṃ mahaḥ ।
yassamyakpālayedetadadhikaṃ yaśca vardhayet ।।

ādyeṣṭakādi nirmāṇaphalameva prapadyate ।
sarvāśubhavināśaṃ ca labdhvāceṣṭamavāpya ca ।।

ante vimānamāruhya viṣṇoryāti paraṃ padam ।
kiṃ bahūktena vidhinā na daivaṃ keśavātparam ।।

taṃ viṣṇuṃ pūjayennityaṃ sarvasādhanasādhanam ।
sarvamuktipradaṃ nityaṃ sarvakāmaphalapradam ।।

grāmāgrahārayossamyagarcanaṃ tatra vāsinām ।
sarvasiddhipradaṃ nityaṃ putrapautrapravardhanam ।।

sāmānyamagni hotraṃ syādanagnīnāṃ tapodhanāḥ ।
sāgnīnāmapyavijñātaprāyaścittāya kalpate ।।
tasmātkuryādavicchinnamarcanaṃ sarvayatnataḥ ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre dvādaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha trayodaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha trayodaśo adhyāyaḥ 
navaṣaṭpañcamūrtividhānam
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi navaṣaṭpañcamūrtikam ।
viṣṇuṃ ca puruṣaṃ satyamacyutaṃ cāviruddhakam ।।

naranārāyaṇābhyāṃ tu vārāhaṃ nārasiṃhakam ।
evaṃ tu navamūrtistu sthāpayitvā yadhāvidhi ।।

viṣṇvādipañcamūrtīstu adimūrtintathākramāt ।
sthāpayet tatkrameṇaiva ṣaṇmūrtikamihocyate ।।
