viṣṇvādīnāṃ tu pañcānāṃ sthāpanaṃ pañcamūrtikam ।
daśāvatārakalpaḥ
matsyaḥ kūrmovarāhaśca nārasiṃho atha vāmanaḥ ।।

rāmo rāmaśca rāmaśca kṛṣṇaḥ karkirime daśa ।
sargakāle tu bhagavān sṛṣṭvā vikhanasaṃ gurum ।।

vedānupādiśattasmai lokasaṃrakṣaṇakṣamān ।
purā madhvādayaḥ kāle saṃbhūya bhuvi rākṣasāḥ ।।

apāharaṃstu tān vedān balātkṛtva vidhiṃ muhuḥ ।
tadā tu somakaṃ hantuṃ rākṣasaṃ raṇavikramam ।।

antarhitamakūpāre mātsyaṃ bhāvaṃ gato hariḥ ।
hatvā tu somaṅkaṃ paścādvedānabjabhuve dadau ।।

grāmādiṣu ca sarvatra madhyame paścime apivā ।
hastipṛṣṭhavimāne tu kuṃbhākāravimānake ।।

dvitālenottamaṃ kuryānmānametadudāhṛtam ।
avatārasya sarvasya kautukaṃ syācchaturbhujam ।।

viśeṣamatra vakṣyāmi pradhāne abjāvale kramāt ।
hautrapraśaṃsanaṃ kṛtvā devatāvāhanaṃ caret ।।

"matsyaṃ ca jalajaṃ ceti bhadraṃ krīḍātmakaṃ'tathā ।
evamādibhirāvāhya cānyatpūrvavadācaret ।।

"yassvayaṃ sṛṣṭa'mityuktvā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ yajet ।
yathoktenaiva mārgeṇa saṃsthāpya vidhinār'cayet ।।

kūrmaḥ devāsurārthaṃ mṛte kṛtayuge hariḥ ।
kacchapassamabhūddhartuṃ mandharaṃ taṃ mahācalam ।।

grāmādau vāstumadhye ca parvatāgre viśeṣataḥ ।
nandyāvartavimāne vā phelākāravimānake ।।

ekatālena mānena kūrmarūpaṃ vidhīyate ।
kūrmarūpaṃ dhruvaṃ kuryāt kautukaṃ tu caturbhujam ।।

pratiṣṭhāṃ pūrvavatkuryādgārhapatye viśeṣataḥ ।
hautramatra praśaṃsanti mūrtimastramathocyate ।।

"akūpāraṃ kūrmarūpaṃ viṣṇuṃ ca vasudhādharam' ।
"akūpāraṃ jalaṃ kūrmaṃ kacchapaṃ'tviti ke ca na ।।

samāvāhya tu taireva nirupyājyāhutīryajet ।
"rāyāmīśa'ssamuccārya śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ yajet ।।

uktavatthsāpayedvidvān vidhinā samyagarcayet ।
matsyakūrmau dvidhā proktaukiṃ cidbhedaṃ pracakṣate ।।

dvibhujau kecidicchanti kecidiṣṭabhujau budhāḥ ।
varāhaḥ
devamānuṣatiryañca sthāvarā jaṅgamās tathā ।।

purāsṛṣṭā yathā sarve catvāro bhuvi jantavaḥ ।
jarāyujāṇḍajodbhijjanvedajāśceti jātitaḥ ।।

evaṃ pravartamāne tu hiraṇyākṣo mahābalaḥ ।
rasātalamagāddhṛtvā carācaradharāṃ mahīm ।।

mahāvarāhavapuṣā tāṃ tadoddhṛtavān hariḥ ।
varāhastrividhaḥ prokto devasyāviṣkṛtau punaḥ ।।

kramādādivarāhaśca varāhaḥ pralayātmakaḥ ।
yajñavārāha ityevaṃ trividhissaṃprakīrtitaḥ ।।

vimāne parvatākāre śrīpratiṣṭhitake tathā ।
daśatālena mānena devaṃ sūkaramācaret ।।

catubānhusamāyuktaṃ śaṅkhacakradharaṃ param ।
vāmapādaṃ samākuñcya mahīmuddhṛtya sādaram ।।

dakṣiṇaṃ caṇḍitaṃ kuryānmahīmūrau samācaret ।
mahīṃ ca śyāmavarṇāṃ tu kuryāccaiva vidhānataḥ ।।

evamādivarāhantu kārayellakṣaṇānvitam ।
avāntaramanuprāpya yadā tu pralayaṃ hariḥ ।।

tattoyamupasaṃhartuṃ varāhaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ ।
tataḥ pralayavārāhaṃ purābhūtaṃ ca kārayet ।।

śaṅkhacakradharaṃ saumyaṃ pītāṃbaradharaṃ harim ।
dakṣiṇaṃ cābhayaṃ hastaṃ vāmaṃ kaṭyavalaṃbitam, ।।

mahīṃ tu dakṣiṇe kuryātsaśyāmanibhāṃ tathā ।
sukhāsanakrameṇaiva cāsīnāṃ vā svalaṅkṛtām ।।

evaṃ pralayavārāhaṃ kārayettu vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
hiraṇyākṣaḥpurā rakṣo balavān balināṃ varaḥ ।।

vareṇa garvāddurbuddhiryajñavidveṣako avṛdhat ।
avātarattadā viṣṇuvan rasūkaramūrtimān ।।

hatvā sadaityaṃ sabalaṃ paścādyajñānnyavartayat ।
tasmādyajñavarāhaṃ tu tañca kuryādvidhānataḥ ।।

śvetaṃ yajñavarāhaṃ tu śrībhūmibhyāṃ sahaiva vā ।
sukhāsane samāsīnaṃ kuryāllakṣaṇasaṃyutam ।।

trayāṇāṃ ca varāhāṇāṃ sthāpane bheda ucyate ।
pūrvoktena krameṇaiva sarvaṃ kṛtvā viśeṣataḥ ।।

sabhyāgnikuṇḍe rātrautu hautraśaṃsanamācaret ।
"varāhaṃ varadaṃ viṣṇumurvīsaṃdhāraṇaṃ tathā ।।

vajradaṃṣṭra'miti procya devamādivarāhakam ।
"mahīṃ tāṃ pṛthulāmurvī'miti devīṃ mahīṃ kramāt ।।

āvāhayedyathānyāyamanvatsarvaṃ samācaret ।
"vārāhaṃ pralayaharaṃ bhūteśaṃ viṣṇumeva ca ।।

jagattrayātmakaṃ' coktvā varāhaṃ pralayātmakam ।
"varāhaṃ devarūpaṃ ca yajñeśaṃ yajñavardhakam ।।

viṣṇuṃ' ceti tathā devaṃ yajñavārāhamāhvayet ।
āvāhanādisarvatra pūrvavatkārayedbudhaḥ ।।

"kṣmāmekā'miti mantreṇa yajedaṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।
hareruktavidhānena sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret ।।

nārasiṃhaḥ
hiraṇyakaśipurnāma daityānāṃ prabalo abhavat ।
vareṇa garvāddaityendro hiraṇyakaśipustadā ।।

devairmṛgairmanuṣyairvā jīvibhirvāpyajīvibhiḥ ।
divā vā yadi vā rātrau vadho me na bhavediti ।।

lokānudvejayamāsa tadā taṃ daityasattamam ।
hantukāmaḥ kṛtodyogaścintayitvā hariḥ prabhuḥ ।।

tatpālitapurādbāhye mahāparvatamastake ।
rakṣasā pīḍitairdevaiḥ prārthitaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ ।।

narasiṃhavapurbhūtvā divā rātriṃ vyapohya ca ।
saṃdhyākāle avadhīttantu bhuvaṅge sa nakhāyathaḥ ।।

bāhyamābhyastaraṃ hitvā jīvājīvairnakhaiśśubhaiḥ ।
evaṃ daityavadhaṃ kṛtvā parvate antarabhūt hariḥ ।।

tatastamarcayedbhaktyā vijayārthaṃ vivṛddhaye ।
parvatākṛtike vāpi śrīpratiṣṭhitake apivā ।।

daśatālena mānena narasiṃhaṃ prakalpayet ।
girijaṃ sthūṇajaṃ caiva sudarśananṛsiṃhakam ।।

tathā lakṣmīnṛsiṃhaṃ ca pātālanarasiṃhakam ।
tathā pucchanṛsiṃhaṃ ca nṛsiṃhaṃ ṣaḍvidhaṃ viduḥ ।।

siṃhāsane samāsīnaṃ sarvābharaṇa bhūṣitam ।
nārasiṃhaṃ caturbāhuṃ śaṅkhacakradharaṃ param ।।

pādau dvau ca samākuñcya nyasya siṃhāsane sthitam ।
prasārya hastau dvau jānvostayorūrdhve nidhāya ca ।।

vastreṇa corū baddhvaivamāsīnaṃ girijaṃ tathā ।
śriyaṃ kanakavarṇābhāṃ medinīṃ śyāmasannibhām ।।

brahmeśau vandamānau tu dakṣiṇottarayoḥ kramāt ।
vāhanaṃ sāmavedaṃ ca pramukhe saṃprakalpayet ।।

sāma śyāmanibhaṃ kuryātsarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।
bhūmīśo nāmagandharvo śaiṣikasthānamāśritaḥ ।।

kārayeduktavarṇantaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।
sthūṇajaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi sthūṇādāvirbabhau hariḥ ।।

vāmapādaṃ samākuñcya dakṣiṇaṃ saṃprasārya ca ।
caturbhujadharaṃ devaṃ śaṅkhacakreca kārayet ।।

hastaṃ tu dakṣiṇaṃ pūrvaṃ kuryāddānakaraṃ tadhā ।
vāmahastaṃ prabaddhyaiva ūrau ca tu suvinyaset ।।

saṭākandharasaṃyuktaṃ tīkṣṇadaṃṣṭraṃ bhayānakam ।
śaṅkhakundendudhavalaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣetam ।।

sudarśananṛsiṃhasya lakṣaṇaṃ saṃpravakṣyate ।
sūryakoṭipratīkāśaṃ cakraṃ vimalamujjvalam ।।

bṛhadbhānupuradvandvaṃ cakramadhye prakalpayet ।
cakramadhye samāsīnaṃ nṛsiṃhamaruṇaprabham ।।

atyantabhīṣaṇākāraṃ bhaktānāmabhayapradam ।
cakrāyudhaṃ caturbāhuṃ devadevaṃ prakalpayet ।।

vakṣyelakṣmīrṛsiṃhasya lakṣaṇaṃ munisattamāḥ ।
vāmapādaṃ samākuñcya dakṣiṇaṃ saṃprasārya ca ।।

vāmorau śriyamāsīnāṃ prāṃjalīkṛtavāstakām ।
vāmahastena dehyaśca kurvantamupagūhanam ।।

dakṣiṇaṃ tvabhayaṃ kuryātparābhyāṃ śaṅkacakrake ।
pātālanārasiṃhākhyamāsīnaṃ pūrvavattathā ।।

phaṇaistu pañcabhissamyak channamūrdhānameva ca ।
dakṣiṇādakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ varadaṃ kaṭīkaṃ tathā ।।

vakṣye pucchanṛsiṃhastu pucchayuktaṃ tu kārayet ।
abhayaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ vāmamūrupratiṣṭhitam ।।

dakṣiṇaṃ pādamākuñcya sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।
nārasiṃhamidaṃ kṛtvāsthāpanāraṃbhamācaret ।।

tatracāhavanīyāgnau hautraśaṃsanamācaret ।
"nārasiṃhaṃ taponāthaṃ mahāviṣṇuṃ mahābalam ।।

bhaktavatsala' mityuktvā narasiṃhaṃ samāhvayet ।
"taponidhiṃ' samuccārya śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ yajet ।।
snāpanaṃ cotsavaṃ caiva hareriva vidhānataḥ ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre trayodaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha caturdaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha caturdaśo adhyāyaḥ daśāvatārakalpaḥ 

athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi vāmanasya kramaṃ yathā ।
vairocanasutohyugro balī ca balināṃ varaḥ ।।

tadbalasyāpahārārthaṃ kāśyapājjāyate hariḥ ।
harirvāmanarūpo abhūcchatrī daṇḍī ca vedavit ।।

vaṭabījena sadṛśaḥ kevalaṃ sūtradaṇḍabhṛt ।
vartamāne mahāyajñe balervairocaneḥ purā ।।

tadyajñaśālāṃ saṃprāpya vaṭurūpo mahāhariḥ ।
tvaṃ dehi tripadīṃ mahyaṃ gāmityūce svamāyayā ।।

baliśca tripadaṃ tasmaiprādāttoyasamanvitam ।
hastejale patatyāśu bhadraṃ rūpamavāpya ca ।।

devastraivikramaṃ rūpaṃ sarvaṃ lokaṃ tadāgrahīt ।
trivikramapratiṣṭhāyāṃ viśeṣassaṃpravakṣyate ।।

vasantvimāne vā bhadrake hastibhadrake ।
dīrghaśāre mahākūṭe sthāpanaṃ sarvasiddhidam ।।

daśatālena mānena devadevaṃ prakalpayet ।
savyaṃ pādaṃ sthitaṃ kuryāddakṣiṇaṃ codthitaṃ bhavet ।।

caturbhujaṃ prakurvīta saṃyutaṃ vāṣṭabhirbhujaiḥ ।
dakṣiṇe śārṅgamālaṃbya bhūmyāṃ caiva prasrya ca ।।

śaraṃ ca dakṣiṇe haste khaḍgaṃ caiva tathā bhavet ।
gadā vāmakare proktā tathā kheṭakameva ca ।।

cakraśaṅkhetathā kuryādūrdhvabāhorvicakṣaṇaḥ ।
evameva prakurvīta vasuhastaṃ prakalpayan ।।

sasyaśyāmanibhaṃ kuryāddharṣa vegasamanvitam ।
sarvābharaṇa saṃyuktaṃ kīrīṭādivibhūṣitam ।।

indraṃ sasyanibhaṃ kuryādvāmapārśve ca susthitam ।
dakṣiṇe dharmarājaṃ ca puṣpamālādharaṃ punaḥ ।।

dakṣiṇe bhittiporśve tu brahmāṇaṃ ca prakalbayet ।
hastābhyāṃ kuṃbhayoścaiva pādaprakṣālanaṃ caret ।।

tasyapādāṃbuje caiva jātāṃ gaṅgāṃ ca sundarīm ।
prāñjalīkṛtya hastābhyāṃ nābherūlrāvaṃ śarīragau ।।

pārśvayorubhayoścāpi candrādityau ca pūrvavat ।
jāṃbavantaṃ tathā bherīṃ tāḍayastaṃ narākṛtim ।।

indraṃ śyāmanibhaṃ kuryādyamamañjanasannibham ।
ādityaṃ cāgni varṇaṃ ca candraṃ śtetaṃ tathā caret ।।

pītavarṇaṃ baliṃ kuryānnīlābhaṃ jāṃbavantakam ।
brahmāṇaṃ pītavarṇaṃ ca śyāmavarṇāṃ ca jāhnavīm ।।

evaṃ varṇakrameṇaiva citrābhāsaṃ ca kārayet ।
pūjakau tu prakurvīta tathā śakrabṛhaspatī ।।

śaṅkhaṃ dakṣiṇataḥ kuryāccakraṃ vāme samarcayet ।
amūrtaṃ vā samūrtaṃ vā kalpayitvā yathākramam ।।

śukraṃ śuklanibhaṃ kuryātpītavarṇaṃ bṛhaspatim ।
mahīṃ dakṣiṇataḥ pārśvesthitāmevaṃ prakalpayet ।।

udaṅmukhīṃ ca kurdīta padmahastāṃ ca dakṣiṇe ।
vāme prasāritāṃ caiva sarvaratna vibhūṣitām ।।

tasyāḥpūrve tathā kuryātprahlādaṃ cottarāmukham ।
jaṭāmukuṭasaṃyuktaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।।

hṛdayeṃjalisaṃyuktaṃ śukavatranibhāṃbaram ।
tasyacottarapārśve tu brahmāsūtrasya dakṣiṇe ।।

asurendraṃ tathāsīnaṃ vinataṃ paścimāmukham ।
brahmāñjali samāyuktaṃ kīrīṭādivibhūṣitam ।।

evaṃ vairocaniṃ kuryātpuṣpāṃbaradharaṃparam ।
namuciṃ ca samāsīnaṃ pādapīṭhāvalaṃbinam ।।

vāmapārśve samāsīnaṃ pūrvabhittisamāśrayam ।
kalpayitvā yathāmārgaṃ śukraṃ caiva samāgatam ।।

vāmapādaṃ samāsīnaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ kuñcitaṃ tathā ।
abhayaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ vāmaṃ kaṭyavalaṃbitam ।।

sarvābharaṇa saṃyuktaṃ paścimāmukhameva ca ।
tasya cottarapārśvetu pakṣirājaṃ prakalpayet ।।

dakṣiṇāmukhasaṃyuktaṃ śukremuṣṭiprahāriṇam ।
evaṃ garbhagṛhe proktaṃ vidhinā kārayedbudhaḥ ।।

maṇḍape nimnitasthāne anantaṃ cottarāmukham ।
hṛdayeṃjalisaṃyuktaṃ sthitamevaṃ prakalpayet ।।

phaṇaistu pañcabhiryuktaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।
uttare bhittipārśvetu vāsukīṃ ca prakalpayet ।।

ana ntavattathā kuryāddharṣa vegasamanvitam ।
evameva vidhānena kalpayitvā yathākramam ।।

śyāmavarṇāṃ tathā devīṃ prahgādaṃ pītameva ca ।
kanakābhaṃ baliñcaiva namuciṃ ca tathai va ca ।।

śakraṃ tu pūrvavatkuryātpañcavarṇaṃ khagādhipam ।
anantaṃ pītavarṇaṃ ca vāsukiṃ śyāmameva ca ।।

evaṃ sthānakrameṇaiva kūṭayuktena kārayet ।
atha vā bhittipārśve tu citrābhāse adhamādhamam ।।

trivikramaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathā kuryājjagattraye ।
ekaṃ jānusamaṃ kuryāddvitīyaṃ nābhitassamam ।।

tṛtīyaṃ tu lalāṭāntaṃ trividhaṃ syāttrivikramam ।
mahīṃ devīṃ tathā caiva prahlādaṃ tu baliṃ tathā ।।

namuciṃ ca tathā śukraṃ garuḍaṃ ca tathā caret ।
anantaṃ vāsukīṃ caiva maṣṭāṃgasthāpanaṃ caret ।।

viṣṇuṃ trivikramaṃ ceti trilokeśamataḥ param ।
viśveśvaraṃ trimūrti ca sarpādhāra' mitīrayet ।।

"pītavarṇaṃ guruṃ caiva taiṣyaṃ caiva bṛhaspatim' ।
"samuciṃ kanakābhaṃ ca pītavāsasamityapi ।।

śyāmalāṅgamiti proktaṃ' mūrtimantraṃ yathākramam ।
"hariṇīṃ ca tathā pauṣṇīṃ kṣauṇīñcaiva tathā mahīm' ।।

"prahlādaṃ vīryavittaṃ ca viṣṇu bhaktaṃ mahābalam' ।
"asurendraṃ baliṃ ceti vadānyaṃ vīra'meva ca ।।

śukrasya pūrvamevoktaṃ garuḍasya vidhānataḥ ।
"kāśyapaṃ garuḍaṃ caiva vainateyaṃ khagādhipam ।।

"sahasraśīrṣaṃ śeṣaṃ ca nāgarājamitīrya ca ।
anastaṃ' ca samuccārya śeṣasyāvāhanaṃ caret ।।

"vāsukīṃ nāgarājaṃ ca kādraveyaṃ manoramam ।
evaṃ mūrtikramaścaiva maṣṭāṃgasthāpane caret ।।

pratiṣṭhoktakrameṇaiva sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret ।
trivikramapratiṣṭhāyāmanvāhārye viśeṣataḥ ।।

tathā hautraṃ praśaṃsyaiva mūrtyāvāhanamācaret ।
juṣṭākāraṃ ca kṛtvaiva pūrvavatsarvamācaret ।।

"yo vā trimūrti'rityevaṃ śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ yajet ।
karṣaṇādipratiṣṭhāntaṃ pūrvavatsamyagācaret ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre caturdaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha pañcadaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha pañcadaśo adhyāyaḥ daśāvatāra kalpaḥ bhārgavaḥ

ataḥ paraśurāmasya sthāpanaṃ vakṣyate adhunā ।
bahubhirbalavadbhistu rājabhirdharaṇī hatā ।।

tadvadhāya kṛtodyogo jamadagnisuto hariḥ ।
bhūtvāvatīrṇo lokesmin bhāranirharaṇāya vai ।।

paraśuṃ ca gṛhītvorvyāṃ nṛpān sarvān pragṛhya ca ।
jaghāna kilabhūyo api rāmo bhīmaparākramaḥ ।।

sthāpayecchatrunāśāya rāmaṃ paraśudhāriṇam ।
śrīpratiṣṭhitake caiva aṅganākāra eva ca ।।

madhyamaṃ daśatālena rāmaṃ dvibhujamācaret ।
paraśaṃ dakṣiṇe haste dhṛtvācaiva vicakṣaṇam ।।

vāmamuddeśahastaṃ ca jaṭāmukuṭaśobhitam ।
raktavarṇayutaṃ caiva śvetāṃbaradharaṃ tathā ।।

sarpābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sthānakaṃ tatra kārayet ।
tadrūpaṃ kautukaṃ kuryādatha vā taṃ caturbhujam ।।

anvāhārye pradhānāgnau hautraśaṃsanamācaret ।
"rāmaṃ ṛṣisutaṃ viṣṇuṃ paraśupāṇi'mitīrayet ।।

ityevamuktvā cāvāhya nirupyājyāhutīryajet ।
"viṣṇurvariṣṭha' ityuktvā śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ yajet ।।

utsavasnapanādīni viṣṇuvatsarvamācaret dāśaradhiḥ ।
rāvaṇo bahubhiḥ krūrai rākṣasaiśca mahābalaiḥ ।।

trīn lokān pīḍayāmāsa varadānena garvitaḥ ।
devāssaṃpīḍitāssarve munayaścākhilāstathā ।।

tairdevairmunibhissarvaiḥ saṃstuto hariravyayaḥ ।
tadvadhāya kṛtodyogo mānuṣaṃ rūpamāsthitaḥ ।।

avatīrṇassuto bhūtvā rājño daśarathasya ca' ।
rāmastu rākṣasān hatvā sarvān lokānapālayate ।।

puṣṭyarthī vijayārthī ca vīrārthī ca viśeṣataḥ ।
kūṭāgāreṃganākāre phelākāraṃ catuṣphuṭam ।।

svastikaṃ vā vimānastu kṛtvācaiva vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
rāghavaṃ tu pratiṣṭhāpya yathā vatsaṃprapūjayet ।।

athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi rāmalakṣmaṇa lakṣaṇam ।
sītāyā vāyuputrasya bharatasyāsujasya ca ।।

mānonmānapramāṇāni vakṣye saṃkṣepataḥ kramāt ।
uttamaṃ daśatālena madhyamena yathākramam ।।

uttamaṃ rāghavendrasya madhyamaṃ lakṣmaṇasya ca ।
antenai va tu māsena sītāyāstūcchrayo bhavet ।।

navatālena mānena vāyuputraṃ prakalpayet ।
adhamaṃ daśatālena bharatasyānujasya ca ।।

evaṃ yuktiyutenaiva kriyate śāstravittamaiḥ ।
garbhadvāravimānābhyāṃ beramānamihocyate ।।

utsava pratimāyāntu sarveṣāmālayeṣu vai ।
taddevabhedaṃ mūrtīnāṃ tatpramāṇena yojayet ।।

iṣyate garbhamānantu puṣyamānaṃ? vibhajya ca ।
uttamaṃ pañcabhāgaṃ tu caturbhāgaṃ tu madhyamam ।।

tribhāgamadhamaṃ proktaṃ yathāvacchāstravittamāḥ ।
garbhamānaṃ pravakṣyanti dvāramānantu vakṣyate ।।

saptabhāge caturbhāgamuttamaṃ tu vidhīyate ।
tṣaṃśaṃ tu madhyamaṃ proktamarthāṃśamadhamaṃ bhavet ।।

dvāramānamidaṃ proktaṃ kriyāyāntu viśeṣataḥ ।
rāmasyātha lalāṭāntaṃ nāsāntaṃ lakṣmaṇocchrayam ।।

āsyāntamatha vā kuryādvāyuputrasya lakṣaṇam ।
bharatasyāmajasyāpi tathā galasamaṃ bhavet ।।

uṣṇīṣātpādaparyantaṃ caturviṃśacchatāṅgulam ।
ṣaṣṭidvigolagaṃ vidyādekatṣaṃśatribhāgīkam? ।।

tālāni daśabhāgaikamuttamaṃ daśatālakam ।
caturbhāgāṣṭabhāgaṃ syāccatustālaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

daśatālasya tṣaṃśena uttamaṃ madhyamādhamam ।
madhyamādadhamaṃ hīnaṃ mukhe vārdhāṅgulakṣayam ।।

uṣṇīṣamaṅgulaṃ netraṃ śirastṣaṅgulamiṣyate ।
lalāṭe hanuparyantaṃ trayodaśārdhāṅgulaṃ bhavet ।।

galaṃ caturyavāḥ proktāgrīvā sārdhatriyaṅgulā ।
hikkā hṛdayānābhyantaṃ meḍhramūlaṃ mukhatrayam ।।

mukhāyāmaṃ caturmātraṃ liṅgaṃ pañcāṅgulāyatam ।
nābhirardhāṅgulaṃ jñeyaṃ nimnārdhavaritālakā ।।

śroṇī bhāgārdhamevaṃ syātkaṭiḥ pañcāṅgulaṃ bhavet ।
meḍhramūlādijānvantaṃ saptaviṃśatikāṃgulam ।।

jānubhāgamiti proktaṃ jaṅghorū susamāyutau ।
caraṇaṃ caturaṅgulyaṃ manordeśavidhānataḥ ।।

brahmāṅgulamūkhāyāmaṃ trayodaśāṃgulameva ca ।
kaniṣṭhāṃgulamāyāmamekādaśāṃgulaṃ bhavet ।।

akṣṇāmuṣṇīṣaparyantaṃ bhāgārdhāṅgulamucchrayam ।
hikkāsūtrāntamevaṃ svātskandhamūladvayaṃ bhavet ।।

skandhaṃ bhujasamotsedhaṃ bhujordhvaṃ golakaṃ bhavet ।
bhujadvimukhamāyāmaṃ kūrparaṃ ca kalāyatam ।।

prakoṣṭhaṃ viṃśadaṅgulyaṃ hastāyāmamiti smṛtam ।
nāsyāni nābhivāmebhyo rakṣāntaṃ sūtradakṣiṇam ।।

ādisūtramidaṃ proktamanyatsūtraṃ ca kārayet ।
īṣatkuñcitamātrantu mātrārdhaṃ samakuñcitam ।।

dvikalākuñcitaṃ jñeyaṃ trividhaṃ kuñcitaṃ bhavet ।
pāṣṇonyrantarasaṃyuktaṃ pañcāgulasamanvitam ।।

pādāṅguṣṭhāntaraṃ caiva trayodaśāṃgulamīritam ।
uṣṇīṣātpārśvakarṇāntaṃ vāmahastocchrayaṃ bhavet ।।

nīvraṃ kaṇṭhayavānānta dvimukhaṃ vistaraṃ bhavet ।
dakṣiṇe laṃbahastantu ūrumūlau samaṃ bhavet ।।

nīvraṃ pañcāṃgulaṃ caivatrayodaśāṃgulamīritam ।
hastantu dvyaṅgula ceti kaṭībāhū ṣaḍaṅgulam ।।

triyujā kuñcitaṃ sthityā tribhaṅgāgra virājitam ।
dakṣiṇe kaṭideśe tu vāmamakṣānvitaṃ bhavet ।।

dakṣiṇaṃ mukhamāśritya tribhaṅgāṅga mathocyate ।
śruṅgāraguṇasaṃyuktaṃ kirīṭaṃ vā viśeṣataḥ ।।

vajraṃ pulliṅgavāyuktaṃ makarakuṇḍalamaṃyutam ।
kirīṭamukuṭau jñeyo hārakeyūrasaṃyutam ।।

uṣṇīṣaṃ keśapṛṣṭhānte trayodaśāṃgulamāyatam ।
grīvāyāṃ madhyamaṃ bhāgaṃ kakudbhāgātkramonnatiḥ ।।

jānakīṃ samabhaṅgena vāmahasteva puṣpadhṛt ।
dakṣiṇaṃ saṃprasāryaiva rukmavarṇāntu kārayet ।।

śyāmavastradharāṃ caiva divyastrīmaṇḍanopamām ।
lakṣmaṇaṃ samabhaṅgena taptakāñcanasannibham ।।

bharataṃ śyāmavarṇantu śatrughnantu suvarṇakam ।
lakṣmaṇasyātha vāme tu sthitau bāṇadhanurdharau ।।

hanūmantaṃ piṅgalābhaṃ vārtāvijñāpane param ।
evaṃ sāyudhavargantu vakṣyate atra nirāyudham ।।

prasāri dakṣiṇaṃ pādamitaraccaiva kuñcitam ।
dakṣiṇe nābhayaṃ hastaṃ vāmaṃ kaṭikamucyate ।।

sthāpanādikriyāssarvāḥ pūrvavatkārayettataḥ ।
dakṣiṇāgnau pradhānetu hautraśaṃsanamācaret ।।

"rāmaṃ dāśarathiṃ viṣṇuṃ kākutstha'miti cāhvayet ।
"sītāmayonijāṃ lakṣmīṃ vaidehī'miti cāhvayet ।।

"rāmānujaṃ ca saumitriṃ lakṣmaṇaṃ lakṣmivardhanam' ।
"bharataṃ rāmapriyaṃ ceti kaikaiyīsutameva ca ।।

sadvṛtta'miti cāvāhya bharatasya viśeṣataḥ ।
"śatrughnaṃ sumanaskaṃ ca lakṣmaṇānujameva ca ।।

daśarathodbhava'mityeva śatrughnaṃ ca samāhvayet kapirājaṃ hanūmantaṃ śabdarāśiṃ mahāmatim, ।।

juṣṭākārādisarvaṃ ca pūrvavatkārayedbudhaḥ ।
"rāyāmī'śeti mantreṇa śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ yajet ।।

"śriye jāta'śca sītāyā home mantra udīritaḥ ।
"tanmā yaśogra' mantreṇa bharatasya ca hūyate ।।

"śanno nidhattā'muccārya lakṣmaṇasya hunetsudhīḥ ।
"bhūmānantogra' ityuktvā śatrughnasya samācaret ।।

"marutaḥ paramā'tmeti mārutasyeva mārute ।
sarvatra juhuyānmantraṃ śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ budhaḥ ।।

arcanaṃ cotsavaṃ caiva snapane ca hareriva ।
halī
daityānāṃ tu vadhārthāya yaduśreṣṭhaṃ malābalam ।।

balabhadraṃ vidusso api vasudevasya saṃbabhau ।
bhūbhāramocanārthāya viṣṇussabalabhadrakaḥ ।।

hatvānarakakaṃsādīn sarvān lokānapālayat ।
evaṃ sthāpayituṃ rāmamicchetkārayitaṃ ca yaḥ ।।

somachandavimāne vā hastipṛṣṭhe atha vābudhaḥ ।
tṛtīyaṃ rāmamāsthāpya dvibhujaṃ svetavarṇakam ।।

daśatānena mānena kṛtvā rūpaṃ samāhitaḥ ।
dakṣiṇetarahastābhyāṃ musalaṃ khaḍgameva ca ।।

śroṇīnūtrasamenaiva muṣṭiṃ samusalaṃ dṛḍham ।
bāhusūtrasamaṃ kuryāddhalaṃ vāme tathaivaca ।।

tasya dakṣiṇapārśvetu lakṣmīvadrohiṇīṃ caret ।
evaṃ tu sāyudhaṃ kuryādvakṣye ahaṃ tu nirāyudham ।।

vāmapādaṃ samākuñcya dakṣiṇaṃ saṃprasārya ca ।
abhayaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ vāmamūrau ca vinyaset ।।

agnāvāhavanīyetu hautraṃ tatra praśaṃsayet ।
"rāmaṃ yaduvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ halāyudha'mitikramāt ।।

"indirāṃ revatīṃ caiva lakṣmīṃ rāmapriyā'miti ।
evamāvāhanaṃ kṛtvājuṣṭākārādi pūrvavat ।।

"kṣmāmekā'miti mantreṇa śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ yajet ।
arcanaṃ cotsavaṃ caiva snapanaṃ ca hareriva ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇa'dhikāre pañcadaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha ṣoḍaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha ṣoḍaśo adhyāyaḥ daśāvatārakalpaḥ 

athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi kṛṣṇasya sthāpanaṃ budhāḥ ।
kṛṣṇasyālayamuddiṣṭaṃ kuṃbhākāravimānake ।।

kūṭe vā gopure vāpi parvatākṛtike apivā ।
kṛṣṇasya bālarūpasya vayasā tālamānakam ।।

ekavarṣaṃ samārabhya yāvatbañcābdamādarāt ।
tālatrayakrameṇaiva yathāyogaṃ prakalpayet ।।

vedavarṣaṃ samārabhyaṣaṭtālatrayameva vā ।
saptavarṣaṃ samārabhya saptatālatrayaṃ tathā ।।

daśavarṣaṃ samārabhya aṣṭatālatrayaṃ tathā ।
trayodaśa samārabhya navatālatrayaṃ tathā ।।

evaṃ vayaḥkrameṇaiva tālamānaṃ tathocyate ।
tiṣṭhantamekapīṭhasthaṃ rukmiṇyā satyabhāmayā ।।

kṛṣṇaṃ ca bālavapuṣaṃ śyāmalaṃ pītavāsasam ।
rukmiṇīṃ kanakābhāṃ tāṃ satyabhāmāṃ ca śyāmalām ।।

vāsudevaṃ guḍākeśaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।
krīḍayaṣṭidharaṃ devaṃ tribhaṅgadhyānasaṃyutam ।।

svastikaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ vāmapādaṃ tu kuñcitam ।
tiṣṭhantamaṅgulisthāne cāṃguṣṭhasthitimācaret ।।

kiñcitkuñcitajānvantavāmapādasthitirbhavet । vaktraṃ caiva tathā gātraṃ kaṭibhāgaṃ tathaiva ca।।

triṣumārgeṣu bhaṅgitvāttribhaṅgitvaṃ vidhīyate ।
vaktraṃ dakṣiṇato bhāge madhyabhāgaṃ tu vāmataḥ ।।

kaṭīrdakṣiṇato bhāge bhaṅgatrayamudāhṛtam ।
dakṣiṇaṃ kaṭikaṃ hastaṃ krīḍāyaṣṭisamanvitam ।।

dakṣiṇe yaṣṭihastantu nābhisūtrādadhonnatam ।
bhūtavedaguṇāṅgulyā vidhinā sahitālataḥ? ।।

vāmaṃ devyorbhujāsaktaṃ vāmahastamadhomukham ।
hikkāsūtrādadho vāmaṃ kūrparaṃ syāddaśāṅgulam ।।

ṣaṭsaptāṣṭāṃgulādhikyonnataṃ vā kālayetkramāt ।
vāmahastatalāgrantu nābhimātrantu yojayet ।।

veṇuṃ ca taravegaṃ tu hastābhyāṃ pīḍayetkramāt ।
ūrdhvakāyasamaṃ veṇuṃ krīḍāyaṣṭiṃ tu tatsamam ।।

triṇataṃ śyāmalāṅgaṃ ca dvibhujaṃ raktavāsasam ।
caturbhujaṃ vā kurvīta śaṅkhacakradharaṃ param ।।

susthitaṃ vāmapādena dakṣiṇenaiva bandhayet ।
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ sundaraṃ saumyalocanam ।।

devībhyāṃ sahitaṃ kuryā drahitaṃ vātra kecana ।
devasya vāme garuḍaṃ prāñjalīkṛtya nusthitam ।।

pakṣadvayayutaṃ kuryāttālapatrasya mūlavat ।
navanītanaṭaṃ kuryāttathā kālīyamardanam ।।

pārthasārathirūpaṃ tu devyośca rahitaṃ kramāt ।
pīṭhaṃ ca pratimotsethaṃ pañcabhāgaṃ tribhāgikaṃ ।।

navāṃśātsaptabhāgaṃ catribhāgadvayamucyate ।
laukikapratimotsedhaṃ mānāṃgulamiti kramāt ।।

prathamaṃ tu navāṅgulyaṃ dvadvyaṅgulavivardhanam ।
navasaṃkhyamiti proktaṃ mānamevaṃ vidhīyate ।।

etena tu tribhedaṃ syāduttamādhamamadhyamam ।
mānaṃpramāṇamunmānaṃ laṃbamānopamānakam ।।

pañcatālamiti proktaṃ laṃbamānaṃ vidhīyate ।
sāttvikaṃ rājasaṃ caiva tāmasaṃ tu vivarjayet ।।

dakṣiṇaṃ mānamuddhṛtya nābhisūtrapramāṇakam ।
kaṭiyonisamaṃ vātha dakṣiṇaṃ pādameva hi ।।

daṇḍahastantu mānena mūrdhni keśākṣameva vā ।
abhayaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ hastaṃ bhrūmātraṃ kūrparādayaḥ ।।

dakṣiṇena mukhaṃ caiva kiñcitprahasitānanam ।
keśakaṃbalamityuktaṃ sūtraṃ vāmāśrayaṃ bhavet ।।

uṣṇīṣasthapade madhye nāsāgre puṭavāmake ।
nābhimadhyagate vāpi muṣkamālorudakṣiṇe ।।

pāde dakṣiṇapāṇyante agrānmakuṭavāmake ।
laṃbayenmadhyasūtraṃ cedanyatsūtraṃ na kārayet ।।

uṣṇīṣamaṅgulārdhaṃ ca mukhamaṣṭāṃgulaṃ bhavet ।
galamarthāṃgulaṃ tasya grīvāntaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ bhavet ।।

hikkāntaṃ hṛdayāntaṃ ca nābhyantaṃ meḍhramūlakam ।
aṣṭādaśāṃgulaṃ caiva mūrdhvakāyaṃ vidhīyate ।।

trayodaśāṃgulaṃ caiva mūrudīrṅaṃ vidhīyate ।
jānussyāddvyaṅgulaṃ caiva jaṅghā coruśca tatsamā ।।

caraṇaṃ dvyaṅgulaṃ caiva mānameva na saṃśayaḥ ।
hīkkāsūtrāntato bāhurdaśāṅgulamiti smṛtam ।।

prakoṣṭhamaṣṭāṅgulāyāmaṃ saptāṅgulatalāyatam ।
mukhaṃ mukhaviśālaṃ syātkarṇavistāramaṅgulam ।।

grīvāvistāramevaṃ syāccaturaṅgula caturyavam ।
abhayaṃ bāhumānaṃ caturviṃśatiraṅgulam ।।

kakṣayorantaraṃ caiva caturdaśāṃgula vistaram ।
ūrurdaśāṃgulaṃ caiva śroṇirekādaśāṃgulam ।।

kaṭivistāramevaṃ syāttrayodaśāṃgulamiṣyate ।
ūrumūlasuvistāramaṣṭāṃgulamiti kramāt ।।

ṣaḍaṅgulaṃ jānutāraṃ jaṅghātāraṃ ca saptakam ।
tṣaṅgulārdhaṃ ca vijñeyaṃ nālikāvistaraṃ bhavet ।।

pādavistāramevoktaṃ sarvalakṣaṇasaṃyutam ।
kalāpakusumaśyāmaṃ śaṅkhacakragadāmbujam ।।

anekaratnaṃ sa channaṃ kaustubhodbhāsi vakṣasam ।
tārahārāvalīramyaṃ garuḍopari saṃsthitam ।।

devībhyāṃ sahitaṃ kuryātkṛṣṇaṃ bṛndāvane ratam ।
ālola kuntalodbhāsi mukhacandra virājitam ।।

atiraktādharoṣṭhaṃ ca raktapāṇidvayāṃcitam ।
vāmapādaṃ samākuñcya cottānīkṛtya dakṣiṇam ।।

dakṣiṇaṃ cābhayaṃ hastaṃ navanītayutaṃ tathā ।
vāmaṃ prasārya cottānaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।।

sāṃbaraṃ tu prakurvīta vigatāṃbarameva vā ।
evaṃ tu vidhinā kuryānnavanitanaṭaṃ budhaḥ ।।

evameva prakurvīta kālīyāhiphaṇopari ।
nṛtyantaṃ paramātmānamuttānākuñcitāṅghrikam ।।

dakṣiṇe tu kare kuryānnavanītasya khaṇḍakam ।
ahipucchaṃ kare vāpi kuryātkālīyamardanam ।।

nīlotpaladalaśyāmaṃ pītāṃbarasuśobhitam ।
caturbhujaṃ śaṅkhacakramūrdhvapāṇidvaye dhṛtam ।।

adhaḥpāṇidvaye veṇuṃ vādayantaṃ mudānvitam ।
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ garuḍopari saṃsthitam ।।

devībhyāṃ sahitaṃ devaṃ munibhiḥ pariveṣṭitam ।
kṛṣṇamevaṃ prakurvīta santānārthī viśeṣataḥ ।।

kalāpakusuma śyāmaṃ pūrṇacandranibhānasam ।
barhibarhakṛtottaṃsaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam ।।

yuvatīveṣalāvaṇyaṃ śrīvatsāṃkitavakṣasam ।
smerāruṇādharanyastaveṇuṃ trailokyamohanam ।।

akṣamālāṃ ca vidyāṃ ca kuryādūrdhvakaradvaye ।
veṇuṃ karadvaye kuryāccaturbhujayutaṃ harim ।।

tapanīyalasatkāntyābhrājatkamalahantayā ।
nirīkṣyamāṇacaraṇaṃ vāmapārśvasthayā śriyā ।।

hemasiṃhāsane ramye rājñībhistu niṣevitam ।
candramaṇḍalasaṃkāśaśvetachatreṇaśobhitam ।।

nāradādyairmunigaṇaijñānnārthibhirupāsitam ।
indrādidevatābṛndhaiḥ praṇataṃ parameśvaram ।।

evaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ prakurvīta jaganmohanavigraham ।
gopībhirāvṛtaṃ gobhiḥ paramānandavigraham ।।

vyatyasya dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ vāme nyasya ca susthitam ।
caturbhujaṃ śaṅkhacakradharamūrdhvakaradvaye ।।

dhṛtvā vedamayaṃ veṇumanyahastadvayena ca ।
aṅgulībhirmudā veṇusuṣirāṇi ca pūrayan ।।

divyagāndharvagītārtaṃ tribhaṅgena ca saṃsthitam ।
evaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ prakurvīta veṇunādanaṭaṃ budhaḥ ।।

sarvabhūṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ brahmasūtrasamanvitam ।
raktāṃbaradharaṃ caiva śyāmalaṃ kamalekṣaṇam ।।

rukmiṇīsatyabhāmābhyāṃ pārśvayorupaśobhitam ।
rukmiṇīṃ rukmavarṇābhāṃ satyāṃ śyāmanibhāṃ tathā ।।

vasudevaṃ devakīṃ ca purato dakṣiṇe tathā ।
yaśodāṃ nandagopaṃ ca deveśaṃ vīkṣya susthitam ।।

pradyumnaṃ ca tathā sāṃbaṃ vāme kuryātsalakṣaṇam ।
dāmaṃ sumanasaṃ caiva kuryādanyāṃ ca gopikām ।।

karṇāgrāntantu kṛṣṇasya sumantuṃ vāmamāśritam ।
kakṣabāhusamaṃ vāpi kārayedyuktitaḥ kramāt ।।

navatālena mānena kuryāttān samalaṅkṛtān ।
devakīṃ vasudevaṃ ca kṛṣṇavarṇau prakalpayet ।।

yaśodāṃ gauravarṇāñca karburaṃ nandamācaret ।
pradyumnaṃ śyāmavarṇaṃ ca sāṃbaṃ kālāñjanaprabham ।।

dāmaṃ raktanibhaṃ caiva gauraṃ sumanasaṃ tathā ।
sumantuṃ śvetavarṇaṃ ca kalbayedvidhinā budhaḥ ।।

evaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ prakurvīta līlāmānuṣavigraham ।
caturmūrtikramaścaiṣāṃ vāsādhikaraṇoktavat ।।

dhṛtvā puṣpamayīṃ yaṣṭiṃ dakṣiṇevatu pāṇinā ।
nyasyānyaṃ caiva bhūmistharājadaṇḍasya mūrdhavi ।।

rājārhābharaṇairyuktaṃ rukmīṇyā sahitaṃ prabhum ।
eve kṛṣṇaṃ prakurvīta rājagopālavigraham ।।

pītāṃbaradharaṃ devaṃ jñānamudrālasatkaram ।
veṇumanyakare dhṛtvā sukhāsīnaṃ śucismitam ।।

upāsyamānaṃ munibhirdevībhyāṃ rahitaṃ harim ।
kṛṣṇamevaṃ prakurvīda jñānagopālavigraham ।।

svarṇaprabhamudārāṅgamaṣṭabāhuṃ jagatprabhum ।
ikṣucāpāṃkuśānveṇuṃ śaṅkhārisumasāyakān ।।

bibhrantaṃ ramayā śliṣṭadivyamaṅgalavigraham ।
sarvābharaṇasaṃyuktaṃ yogināmamṛtapradam ।।

evaṃ sammohanaṃ kuryātkṛṣṇaṃ gopālavigraham ।
gavāṃ gopakumārāṇāṃ gopīnāṃ rakṣaṇāyavai ।।

nagaṃ govardhanaṃ nāma dadhāra bhagavān hariḥ ।
vāmenoddhṛtahastena bibhrantaṃ nagamuttamam ।।

kaṭinyastānya hastaṃ ca padmahastamadhāpi vā ।
śaṅkhacakradharaṃ devaṅkuryāccaiva caturbhujam ।।

evaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ prakurvīta govardhanadharaṃ harim ।
purā mahati saṃgrāme pārthaṃ rakṣitavān hariḥ ।।

pārthaṃ rathasthitaṃ kuryāccharatūṇīrasaṃyutam ।
samīkṣamāṇaṃ deveśaṃ syandanasthaṃ svapārśvagam ।।

śyāmavarṇaṃ mahābāhu kṛṣṇamudbaddhakuntalam ।
bibhrantaṃ dakṣiṇe pāśaṃ śaṅkhaṃ vāmakare tadhā ।।

arjunasya mukhaṃ vīkṣya smayamānaṃ mahāratham ।
evaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ prakurvīta pārthasārathivigraham ।।

vāmajānusamākuñcya dīrghamanyaṃ prasārya ca ।
tathai vāvithya sannyasya bhūmyāṃ vāmakaraṃ puraḥ ।।

ākuñcitānyapādeva cāsanasthitiśobhinā ।
anyahastena saṃdhārya navanītaṃ navaṃ navam ।।

muhurālokayantaṃ taddarśanīyaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
evaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ prakurvīta bālagaupālavigraham ।।

purā saṃdartasamaye saṃhṛteṣu jagatsu ca ।
vaṭapatre vinidrāṇo babhūva bhagavān hariḥ ।।

vaṭapatre śayānaṃ tu bālarūpaṃ parātparam ।
ākṛṣya dakṣiṇaṃ pādaṃ vāmahastena līlayā ।।

pādāṅguṣṭhaṃ mukhe nyasya dhāsyantaṃ hasitānanam ।
dakṣiṇena tu hastena vahantaṃ dakṣiṇorukam ।।

prasāritetarapadaṃ divyālaṅkāraśobhitam ।
vaṭapatraṃ prakurvīta viśālaṃ cādharāgrakam ।।

vaṭapatraśayānaṃ tu kṛṣṇamevaṃ prakalpayet ।
śaṅkhacakragadāpadma pāśāṃkuśalasatkaram ।।

karābhyāṃ veṇumādāya dhamantaṃ sarvamohanam ।
sūryāyutaśatābhāsaṃ pītāṃbarasuśobhitam ।।

nānālaṅkārasubhagaṃ sūryamaṇḍalasaṃsthitam ।
evaṃ prakalpayetkṛṣṇaṃ mahāntaṃ sarvamohanam ।।

kṛṣṇarūpamasaṃkhyātaṃsvecchārūpaṃ tu kārayet ।
kālīyamardanādau tu nāgakanyādikalpanam ।।

kalpanaṃ bhogabhedasya caivamādīn prakalpayet ।
yuktyā buddhyā ca bhaktyā ca yathā syānmanasaḥ priyam ।।

evaṃ rūpaṃ ca kṛtvā tu tadrūvaṃ kautukaṃ caret ।
athavākautukaṃ biṃbaṃ caturbhujasamanvitam ।।

abhayaṃ varadaṃ pūrvaṃ śaṅkhacakradharaṃ param ।
evaṃ caturbhujaṃ kṛtvā sthāpanāraṃbhamācaret ।।

pūrvoktayāgaśālāyāṃ pañcāgnīn parikalpya ca ।
paiṇḍarīke pradhānāgnau hautraśaṃsanamācaret ।।

"kṛṣṇaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ tridaśādhipa'matyapi ।
"rukmiṇīṃ suṃdarīṃ devīṃ ramā'miti ca rukmiṇīm ।।

"satyarūpāṃ satīṃ caiva sannatīṃ ca kṣamā'miti ।
ityevamuktvā cāvāhya garuḍaṃ pūrvavattadhā ।।

āvāhanakrameṇaiva nirupyājyāhutīryajet ।
"satyassatyastha' ityuktvā śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ yajet ।।

śrībhūmyoriva kuryācca rukmiṇīsatyabhāmayoḥ ।
pūrvoktena vidhānena sthāpanādīni kārayet ।।

karkī
yugāntasamaye viṣṇuḥ karkī nāma bhaviṣyati ।
khaḍgakheṭakahastastu mlecchādīn sa haniṣyati ।।

kūṭe vā gopure vāpi parvatākṛtike api vā ।
kalkirūpaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya vimāne tu samarcayet ।।

madhyamaṃ daśatālena bhinnāṃjanacayaprabham ।
aśvānanaṃ mukhaṃ kuryādanyaccaiva narākṛti ।।

caturbhujaṃ ca hasteṣu kramāccaivāyudhānyapi ।
cakraṃ śaṅkhaṃ ca khaḍgaṃ ca dadhānaṃ kheṭakaṃ tathā ।।

athavā kalpayeddevamaśvārūḍhaṃ dvibāhukam ।
śuddhasphacikasaṃkāśaṃ khaḍgakheṭaka dhāriṇam ।।

atraiva kautukaṃ kuryādviṣṇurūpaṃ caturbhujam ।
pūrvoktayāgaśālāyāṃ pañcāgnīn parikalpya ca ।।

paiṇḍarīke pradhānāgnau hautraśaṃsanamācaret ।
"karkiṇaṃ kāmarūpaṃ ca viṣṇuṃ saṃhārakāraṇam' ।।

evamāvāhya vidhinā nirupyājyāhutīryajet ।
"dhūrno vahantā' mityuktvā śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ yajet ।।

utsavasnapanādīni viṣṇoriva samācaret ।
viṣṇordaśāvatārāṇāmevaṃ proktaṃ tu lakṣaṇam ।।

anādirbhagavān kālo nāsya cānto api dṛśyate ।
cakravatparivartante sṛṣṭisthityantasaṃyamāḥ ।।

avatārāśca kīrtyante bhūyāṃsaḥ paramātmanaḥ ।
dharmasaṃrakṣaṇārthāya duṣṭasaṃśikṣaṇāya ca ।।

sadya āvirbhavedviṣṇuryatra bhaktānukaṃpayā ।
āvirbhāvaṃ tu taṃ vindyātprādurbhāvamathetarat ।।

āvirbhāvantu matsyādyāḥ pañca pañcetarāssmṛtāḥ ।
gajendramokṣaṇādīnapyāvirbhāvān pracakṣate ।।

antarāle tathā viṣṇordakṣiṇottarapārśvayoḥ ।
kalpayedrāmakṛṣṇau tu mukhamaṇḍapa eva vā ।।

athāntarmaṇḍape vāpi tathāvaraṇa maṇḍape ।
saṃsthāpya kautukaṃ beraṃ dvayameveti ke ca na ।।

nārasiṃhaṃ varāhaṃ ca vāmanaṃ ca trivikramam ।
dhruvaberaṃ vinā kṛtvā kautukaṃ lakṣaṇānvitam ।।

sthāpayitvā tathā viṣṇoḥ pūjayedagramaṇḍape ।
matsyakūrmavarāhāṇāṃ vāmanasya viśeṣataḥ ।।

kautukaṃ viṣṇurūpaṃ tu kuryāccaiva caturbhujam ।
dhruvarūpaṃ na kurvīta yatheṣṭamitaratratu ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre ṣoḍaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha saptadaśo adhyāyaḥ

atha saptadaśo adhyāyaḥadimūrtikalpaḥ
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa keśavādivinirṇayam ।
keśavaṃ tu prakurvīta saumyarūpaṃ caturbhujam ।।

śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ svarṇābhave va ca ।
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ muktāhāravibhūṣitam ।।

sthitamevaṃ prakurvīta devībhyāṃ sahitaṃ prabhum ।
nārāyaṇaṃ prakurvīta ghanaśyāmaṃ caturbhujam ।।

śaṅkhapadmadhakaṃ devaṃ bibhrantaṃ ca gadāmasim ।
bhūṣitaṃ maṇibhūṣābhiḥ vītavāsasamacyutam ।।

prakuryācca viśeṣeṇa lakṣmīnārāyaṇaṃ śubham ।
uttamaṃ daśatālena mānonmānapramāṇataḥ ।।

siṃhāsane samāsīnaṃ dakṣiṇāṃghriṃ prasārya ca ।
āsane nihitaṃ vāmaṃ lakṣaṇaṃ pūrvavattathā ।।

lakṣmīṃ sannyasya vāmorau mukhe harṣasamanvitām ।
prasāritakarāṃ devīṃ pañcatālapramāṇataḥ ।।

prāñjalīkṛtahastāṃ tāṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitām ।
vāmena tāṃ pariṣvajya dakṣiṇenābhayapradam ।।

anyābhyāṃ ca karābhyāṃ ca śaṅkhacakradharaṃ param ।
tārkṣyaṃskandhāsanasthaṃ vā anyatsarvaṃ ca pūrvavat ।।

tārkṣyaṃ navārdhatālena ardheṣadbhṛkuṭiṃ? mukham ।
dakṣiṇorau sthitāṃ lakṣmīṃ kecidicchantisūrayaḥ ।।

nāgabhoge samāsīnamevaṃ kuryāttu vā harim ।
saptabhiḥ pañcabhirvāpi phaṇairvistāritairyutam ।।

śeṣaṃ samyakprakurvīta samuttuṅgaśarīriṇam ।
mādhavaṃ cotpalanibhaṃ cakracāvagadāsibhiḥ ।।

caturbhujadharaṃ kuryāccitramālyāṃbaraṃ harim ।
govindaṃ pāṇḍurābhaṃ ca caturbhujadharaṃ harim ।।

gadāśaṅkhāripadmāni bibhrantaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ ।
viṣṇuṃ nīlotpalābhantu śaṅkhāryabjagadābhṛtam ।।

sarvābharaṇa saṃyuktaṃ pītavāsasamacyutam ।
raktotpalābhaṃ kurvīta devaṃ tu madhusūdanam ।।

śaṅkhāryabjagadāpāṇiṃ caturbhujamanāmayam ।
trivikramaṃ nīlavarṇaṃ śaṅkhāryabjagadābhṛtam ।।

caturbhujadharaṃ devaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।
vāmanaṃ meghavarṇaṃ tu caturbāhuṃ mahābalam ।।

gadāśaṅkhāripadmāni bibhrantaṃ chalarūpiṇam ।
atha vā kārayetkuṃbhaṃ dadhyannaṃ ca karadvaye ।।

dadhivāmanamāhustaṃ śvetābhaṃ dvibhujaṃ harim ।
atha vā vaṭurūpaṃ tu dhṛtvā daṇḍakamaṇḍalū ।।

svarṇacchami bālarūpaṃ dvibhujaṃ kārayeddharim ।
sitāsitābhaṃ kurvīta śrīdharaṃ tu caturbhujam ।।

kaumodakīśaṅkhacakrapadmadhāriṇamīśvaram ।
hṛṣīkeśaṃ prakurvīta śyāmābhaṃ ca caturbhujam ।।

gadāśaṅkhāripadmāni bibhrantaṃ harimavyayam ।
sitamecakavarṇantu padmanābhaṃ prakalpayet ।।

kaumodakīcakrapadmaśaṅkhapāṇiṃ ramādhavam ।
dāmodaraṃ prakurvīta sitagaurābhamīśvaram ।।

padmaśaṅkhagadācakradharaṃ devaṃ caturbhujam ।
saṃkarṣaṇaṃ tu kurvīta śvetavarṇaṃ caturbhujam ।।

śaṅkhāryabjagadāpāṇiṃ sarvādhāraṃ sanātanam ।
vāsudevaṃ prakurvīta taruṇādityasannibham ।।

śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ sarvadharaṃ vibhum ।
candrābhaṃ navakundābhamatha vā kālayeddharim ।।

pradyumnaṃ tu suvarṇābhaṃ kuryāddevaṃ caturbhujam ।
cakraśaṅkhagadāpadmadharaṃ devaṃ mahābalam ।।

aniruddhaṃ hiraṇyābhaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam ।
śaṅkhacakradhanuḥkhaḍgadharaṃ deveśvareśvaram ।।

sitāsitābhaṃ kurvīta deveśaṃ puruṣottamam ।
śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ devaṃ caturbhujam ।।

athokṣajaṃ prakurvīta śaṅkhābhaṃ ca caturbhujam ।
cakraśaṅkhagadāpadmadharaṃ bhūṣaṇabhūṣitam ।।

nārasiṃhaṃ tu meghābhaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam ।
śaṅkhapadmagadācakradharaṃ bhaktābhayapradam ।।

sitamecakavarṇaṃ tu kurvīta vibhumacyutam ।
gadābjacakraśaṅkhāṅkaṃ caturbhujavirājitam ।।

janārdanamudārāṅgaṃ nīlavarṇaṃ samācaret ।
cakraśaṅkhagadāpadmadharaṃ devaṃ sanātanam ।।

atha vā kaṭivinyastavāmahastaṃ prakalpayet ।
upendraṃ ghanakṛṣṇābhaṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitam ।।

śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ devaṃ jagatprabhum ।
hariṃ pāṇḍurakṛṣṇābhaṃ sarvālaṅkāraśobhitam ।।

śaṅkhapadmagadācakradharaṃ kuryānmanoharam ।
kṛṣṇaṃ tu nīradaśyāmaṃ puṇḍarīkanibhekṣaṇam ।।

śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadharaṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ ।
sarveṣāṃ tu vimānāni viṣṇoruktavadācaret ।।

sabhyakuṇḍe pradhānāgnau hautraṃ tatra praśaṃsya ca ।
"keśavaṃ kleśasaṃhāraṃ viṣṇuṃ caiva parātparam' ।।

"nārāyaṇaṃ naraṃ viṣṇuṃ narakāntaka' mityapi ।
"mādhavaṃ puṇḍarīkākṣaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarvātmakaṃ' tviti, ।।

"govindaṃ paramānandaṃ viṣṇuṃ caiva sanātanam' ।
viṣṇuṃ vyāpinamīśānaṃ sarvalokādhipaṃ tathā ।।

"madhusūdanamudyogaṃ mahāntaṃ viṣṇu'mityapi ।
"trivikramaṃ trilokeśaṃ lokādhāraṃ sanātanam' ।।

"vāmanaṃ varadaṃ caiva kāśyapiṃ cāditipriyam' ।
"śrīdharaṃ puruṣaṃ ceti viṣṇuṃ śrīvatsavakṣasam' ।।

"hṛṣīkeśaṃ jagannāthaṃ viṣṇuṃ viśvamayaṃ' tathā ।
"padmanābhaṃ sureśaṃ ca viṣṇuṃ caiva jagatpatim' ।।

"dāmodaraṃ sadādhāraṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇavarūpiṇam' ।
"saṃkarṣaṇaṃ yaduvaraṃ viṣṇuṃ haladhara'ntathā ।।

"vāsudevaṃ puṇyamūrtiṃ bhadreśaṃ puṇyarūpiṇam' ।
"pradyumnaṃ jagadīśānaṃ viṣṇu puṇyātmakaṃ' tathā ।।

"aniruddhaṃ mahāntaṃ ca vairāgyaṃ sarvatejasam' ।
"puruṣottamamānandaṃ viṣṇuṃ pañcātmakaṃ' tathā ।।

"adhokṣajamanādiṃ ca viṣṇuṃ vyāpaka' mityapi ।
"nārasiṃhaṃ taponāthaṃ mahāviṣṇuṃ mahābalam' ।।

"acyutaṃ cāparimitamaiśvaryaṃ śrīpatiṃ' tathā ।
janārdanamanādyantaṃ viṣṇuṃ tejomayaṃ' tathā ।।

"upendramindrāvarajaṃ viṣṇuṃ vaikuṇṭha'mityapi ।
"hariṃ pāpaharaṃ ceti viṣṇuṃ maṅgalavigraham ।।

"kṛṣṇaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ puṇyaṃ tridaśādhipa'mityapi ।
āvāhya tu krameṇaiva nirupyājyāhutīryajet ।।

"viṣṇornukā'dabhiṣṣaḍbhi"ratodevā'dabhistathā ।
keśavādidvādaśānāṃ mantrairdvādaśabhirhunet ।।

nārasiṃhasya kṛṣṇasya mantraḥ pūrvamudīritaḥ ।
itareṣāṃ daśānāṃ tu daśamantrāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।

"viṣṇussarveṣā'mityādi "yaṃ yajñai'rantamīritāḥ ।
taṃ taṃ devaṃ samuddiśya tattanmantreṇa cātvaraḥ ।।

śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ hutvā śeṣaṃ pūrvavadācaret ।
evaṃ sarvatra kurvīta devībhyāṃ sahitaṃ vibhum ।।

tadrūpaṃ kautukaṃ kuryātsarvalakṣaṇalakṣitam ।
karṣaṇādikriyāssarvā viṣṇorina samācaret ।।

lakṣmīkalpaḥ
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa lakṣmīsthāpanamuttamam ।
aṣṭadhā procyate lakṣmīḥ prathamā tvanapāyinī ।।

viṣṇorvakṣasthsalekāryā sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutā ।
dakṣastanasyordhvabhāge vahnyaśredivyamaṇḍale ।।

padmamadhye samāsīnāṃ padmadvayakarāñcitām ।
varadābhayahastāṃ ca mandasmita mukhāṃbujām ।।

evaṃ rūpāṃ prakurvīta yogalakṣmīstusā matā ।
yogalakṣmīṃ pratiṣṭhāpya śrīkāmassamyagarcayet ।।

deveśena samaṃ kuryādasyāsthcāpanamuttamam ।
kālāntare prakuryāccheddhemarūpyādinā punaḥ ।।

kṛtvā śrīvatsarūpaṃ tu dhārayedviṣṇumavyayam ।
tattadbiṃbānurūpaṃ ca kuryācchrīvatsalakṣaṇam ।।

bhogalakṣmyassamākhyātā śśrībhūnīlāḥ kramādimāḥ ।
dhruvādiṣu tu bereṣu śrībhūmyau devapāśanvge ।।

vaikuṇṭhamārgasaṃcārā nīlā nityasamāśritā ।
śrībhūmyosthsāpanaṃ pūrvaṃ deveśena sahoditam ।।

devībhyāṃ rahite deve kuryātkālāntare punaḥ ।
pṛdhakpratiṣṭhāṃ śrībhūmyoḥ kuryādāṅgirasoktivat ।।

vīralakṣmīriti proktā pṛthagālayasaṃgatā ।
alayāddakṣiṇe pārśvekuryāttu pṛthagālayam ।।

daśatālena mānena kuryāddevīna salakṣaṇām ।
padmadvayakarāṃ caiva vandā bhayadhāriṇīm ।।

kirīṭamukucopetāṃ sarvālaṅkāraśobhitam ।
padmāsane samāsīnāṃ hemābhāṃ sarvamaṅgalām ।।

godāmanyāṃ prakurvīta lakṣmīṃ tu vijayābhidhām ।
navatāleṃ mānena kuryādanyālayāśritām ।।

dakṣiṇena tu hastena kalhāraṃ dadhatīṃ tathā ।
prasāritetarakarāṃ baddhadhammillaśobhinīm ।।

sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktāṃ tiṣṭhantīmeva kārayet ।
godā bhūmyaṃśajā proktā tanmantreṇācaretkriyāḥ ।।

pākalakṣmīssamākhyātā pacanālayasaṃgatā ।
aṣṭatālena mānena kuryāttāṃ pacanālaye ।।

padmadvayāñcitakarāṃ varadābhayadhāriṇīm ।
āsīnāṃ vātha tiṣṭhantīṃ kuryādbhūṣaṇabhūṣitām ।।

dvitīya maṇḍapadvāre dvāralakṣmīṃ samācaret ।
pataṅgapaṭṭikāmadhye sarvālaṅkāraśobhitām ।।

padmadvayāñcitakarāṃ varadābhayadhāriṇīm ।
padmāsane samāsīnāṃ kirīṭādivibhūṣitām ।।

gajai tu pāśanvyoḥkuryāddhemakuṃbhakarau punaḥ ।
siṃcantau tau mahālakṣmīṃ kuryātkuṃbhajalaistathā ।।

śrībhūmyorvīravijayalakṣmyoreva vidhīyate ।
dhravaberānurūpeṇa berāntarasamarcanam ।।

tadrūpaṃ kautukaṃ kuryādutsavādi yathecchayā ।
anyāsāṃnaiva kurvīta dhruvārcāmeva kārayet ।।

paiṇḍarīke pradhānāgnau hautraṃ tatra praśaṃsya ca ।
śrībhūmyormūrtimantraiśca krameṇāvāhanādikam ।।

"godāṃ kṛṣṇapriyāṃ lakṣmīṃ rukmiṇī'miti cāhvayet ।
āvāhanakrameṇaiva tanmantrairjuhuyātkrarūt ।।

pratiṣṭhoktakrameṇaiva sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret ।
navaṣaṭpañcamūrtīnāṃ vimānasyālayasya ca ।।

dvimūrtisthāpanaṃ tadvatrimūrtasthāpanaṃ tathā ।
anyeṣāṃ parivārāṇāṃ sthāpanaṃ vidhivaccaret ।।

yadyatsamarpyate vastu deveśasya tu mandire ।
tattatsarvaṃ vidhānena pratiṣṭhāpya samarpayet ।।

asaṃskṛtaṃ tu na grāhyaṃ na taddevapriyaṃ bhavet ।
bhūṣaṇāni ca vā sāṃsi pātrāṇyanyatparicchadam ।।

berālaṅkārayogyāni dhāmālaṅkaraṇāni ca ।
yathāhaṃn saṃskṛtānyeva gṛhṇīyātsaphalaṃ bhavet ।।

tattaddravyādhidaivatyaṃ devatāmūrtimantrakam ।
juhuyātsarvamanyacca pratiṣṭhoktavadācaret ।।
dravyādhidevatākalbassamyagukto mayākhile ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛsuproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre saptadaśo adhyāyaḥ

athāṣṭādaśo adhyāyaḥ 
bhagavadarcanam
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa viṣṇorarcanamuttamam ।
"pravaḥ pāntama'ndhetyādi śrutibhirvihitaṃ tathā ।।

yaccoktaṃ guruṇā sūtre samāsena maharṣiṇā ।
tenaiva vivṛtaṃ śāstre sārdhakoṭī pramāṇataḥ ।।

asmābhistu susaṃkṣiptaṃ cāturlakṣapramāṇataḥ ।
tadarcanakramaṃ vakṣye śruṇudhvamṛṣisattamāḥ ।।

vaikhānasena sūtreṇa niṣekādi kriyānvitaḥ ।
ṛtviguktaguṇopetassupuṣṭāṅgassamāhitaḥ ।।

gṛhastho brahmacārī vā bhaktyaivār'canamācaret ।
dravyairanekaissaṃpādyaṃ tathānantopacārakaiḥ ।।

āśakyaṃ vidhivatkartuṃ brahmādyairapi pūjanam ।
manuṣyaiḥkimuvaktavyaṃ daridrairadṛḍhātmabhiḥ ।।

yathāśakti tataḥ kuryāttasmādbahubhirarcakaiḥ ।
bahubhiḥ paricāraiśca tathai vānyapadārthibhiḥ ।।

nirvartyaṃ pūjanaṃ viṣṇośśraddhābhaktisamanvitaiḥ ।
tasmānnavavidhā grāhyā arcakāḥ paricārakāḥ ।।

uttame tūttamaṃ proktamarcakānāntu viṃśatiḥ ।
aśītiḥ paricārāṇāmuttame madhyamaṃ tataḥ ।।

paricārāṇāṃ catuṣṣaṣṭidarcakāṣṣoḍaśa smṛtāḥ ।
uttame tvadhamaṃ proktamarcakā dvādaśa smṛtāḥ ।।

pañcāśatparicārāśca madhyame cottamaṃ punaḥ ।
catvāriṃśatparicarāḥ pūjakāścāṣṭakīrtitāḥ ।।

madhyame madhyamaṃ proktamacankāṣṣaḍudīritāḥ ।
pañcaviṃśatparicarā madhyame tvadhamaṃ punaḥ ।।

catvāraḥ pūjakāstatra paricārāstu ṣoḍaśa ।
trayor'cakāḥ paricarā nava syuradhamottame ।।

pūjakau dvauparicarāścatvāro adhamamadhyame ।
ekor'cakaḥ paricarau dvauproktāvadhamādhame ।।

ācāryassyādupadraṣṭā devassānnidhyakārakaḥ ।
arcanādyakhilaṃ kāryaṃ tanniyogena kārayet ।।

sa hi kāryasya nirṇetā goptādharmasyadeśikaḥ ।
arcako devadevasya kuryānmantrāsanādiṣu ।।

upacārānanantāṃśca vidhinā śāstracoditān ।
arcakasya sahāyantu kiṅkaraḥ paricārakaḥ ।।

bahukāryakarāścaite grāhyāstu paricārakāḥ ।
sammājannakaraścaiva tathā syādupalepakaḥ ।।

dīpoddīpayitā cauva potraśodhanakārakaḥ ।
pānīya vāhakaścaiva puṣpāpacayakārakaḥ ।।

dhūpadīpādikartā ca gandhapeṣaṇatatparaḥ ।
tattatparicchadāhartā tathaiva balivāhakaḥ ।।

evamādīni kāryāṇi kurvanti paricārakāḥ ।
pācakaḥ paricārassyātpacanālayasaṃgataḥ ।।

haviṣpākavidhānajñaśśaucācāraparāyaṇaḥ ।
etānvaikhānasāneva vṛṇetsarvān padārthinaḥ ।।

alābhe tatra sarveṣāmācāryaṃ cārcakānpusaḥ ।
vaikhānasāneva vṛṇannakyudaryādanyasūtriṇaḥ ।।

avaikhānasa viprastu pūjayedālaye harim ।
sa vai devalako nāma sarva karmabahiṣkṛtaḥ ।।

paricārāṃntu vṛṇuyādalābhe tvanyasūtriṇaḥ ।
dīkṣitānevasadvṛttānāgamoktavidhānataḥ ।।

yajamānassadādhyātmarato mokṣārthacintakaḥ ।
dhanī sarvasamastyāgī bhaktiyuktaḥ prasannadhīḥ ।।

śāstroktena vidhānena viṣṇulāñchanalāñchitaḥ ।
devasya nityapūjārthamutsavārthaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

tathānyavibhavārthaṃ ca dāpayeddhanasaṃcayam ।
ācāryājñāpratīkṣassyātṝjake hitacintakaḥ ।।

paricāre prasannaśca kiṅkareṣu dayāparaḥ ।
tīrthaprasādasevī ca nirmālyeṣu kṛtādaraḥ ।।

iti lakṣaṇasaṃpannāḥ prabhavantyālayārcane ।
athārcakaḥ pramannātmā pañcakālaparāyaṇaḥ ।।

brāhmemuhūrte codthāya nārāyaṇamanusmaret ।
kṛtvā sūtroktavidhinā śaucādīni yathāvidhi ।।

snātvā snānavidhānena dhṛtvā dhautāṃbare punaḥ ।
ūrdhvapuṇḍrāṇi saṃdhārya vidhinā keśavādibhiḥ ।।

dhṛtvā pavitrapadmākṣatulasīmaṇimālikāḥ ।
dhṛtvobhayapavitre ca tathā sandhyāmupāsya ca ।।

uṣṇīṣeṇa ca pañcāgabhūṣaṇainsuvibhūṣitaḥ ।
samāpya nityakarmāṇi mahāmantrādikaṃ japan ।।

aruṇaṃ tu japitvaiva nārāyaṇamataḥ param ।
praṇamya yantrikāñcaiva karābhyāṃ parigṛhya ca ।।

bāhvośśirasi vā nyasya bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ ।
saṃgataḥ paricāraiśca yajamānena sādaram ।।

sarvavādya samāyuktaḥ sarvamaṅgalaśobhitaḥ ।
kramamāṇaśśanairvidvān devāgāraṃ prati vrajet ।।

"pratadviṣṇu'riti procya cālayaṃ paritaḥkramāt ।
yugmapradakṣiṇaṃ kuryāddeva devamanusmaran ।।

yugmapradakṣiṇaṃ kuryādayugmaṃ tvābhicārikam ।
āyugmaṃ tu parītyāpi tathāyugmaṃ praṇamya ca ।।

prekṣetodyantamādityaṃ japeddvādaśasūktakam ।
chāyālaṅghanadoṣantu na tatra syātpradakṣiṇe ।।

devāgāraṃ praviśyaiva tattanmantramanusmaran ।
dvāradevān praṇamyātha nirastaṃ rakṣamastrataḥ ।।

gṛhītvā yantrikāṃ caiva "hiraṇyapāṇi' muccaran ।
kavāṭe tu susaṃyojya "divaṃ' vīti samuccaran ।।

kavāṭodghāyanaṃ kṛtvā praviśedantaraṃ budhaḥ ।
"ato devā' itiprocya devaṃ vīkṣyapraṇamya ca ।।

paricārakamāhūya dīpānuddīpayetkramāt ।
praṇavaṃ mantramuccārya tatra kāryaṃ samācaret ।।

trissaṃprahārya pāṇibhyāṃ "śāmyantvi'tyādi coccaran ।
ādarśaṃ gāśca kanyāśca hastyaśvādīn śubhodayān ।।

brāhmaṇānvedaviduṣo nartakāṃścaiva gāyakān ।
devasya puratasthsāpya mukhamaṇḍapa evacā ।।

pracchanna paṭamudvāsya kṛtvā nīrājanaṃ tathā ।
sarvavādyasamāyuktaṃ darśayeddharaye mudā ।।

dhāroṣṇaṃ caiva gokṣīraṃ navanītaṃ saśarkaram ।
deveśāya nivedyātha kuryādyavanikāṃ punaḥ ।।

"bhūḥ prapadye' samuccārya deveśaṃ praṇamenmuhuḥ ।
"paraṃ raṃ'hīti mantreṇa śayanasthaṃ śriyaḥpatim ।।

"bhūrasī bhū'riti procya jīvasthāne niveśayet ।
tasmin kāletu ye bhaktyā sevante puruṣottamam ।।

teṣāṃ puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyaṃ tridaśairapi ।
tataśśiṣyaṃ samāhūya vinayānvitamādarāt ।।

sammārjanādikarmāṇi gurustasmai samādiśet ।
"ava dhūti'miti procya garbhagehādi sarvataḥ ।।

mārjanyā mārjayecchiṣyaḥ prādakṣiṇyakrameṇa vai ।
pāṃsvādīn parihṛtyāpi prākārāntaṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।।

"āśā'sviti samuccārya gomayenopalepayet ।
pañcagavyaistu saṃprokṣya raṅgavallīssamācaret ।।

"ā mā vājasya' mantreṇa yathoktena vidhānataḥ ।
sarvaṇyapi ca pātrāṇi śodhayetsumanorame ।।

to yasaṃgrahaṇārthaṃ tu niyuktaḥ pūjakena tu ।
ghaṭamādāya śiṣyastu "duhatāṃ diva'muccaran ।।

nadītaṭākakūpānāṃ pūrvālābhe paraṃ vrajet ।
upasthāya jalaṃ smṛtvā jāhnavīṃ lokapāvanīm ।।

"ājyamabhigṛhṇā'mīti cāppavitreṇa vāsasā ।
gṛhītvotpūtamādhāvaṃ gāyatrīmuccaran punaḥ ।।

alaṅkṛtyaghaṭaṃ samyak kṣaumenācchādya tanmukham ।
gaje śirasi vā kṣiptvā sarvavādyasamāyutam ।।

punarālayamāviśya kṛtvā caiva pradakṣiṇam ।
somaṃ rājānamuccārya garbhagehe tu dakṣiṇe ।।

vinyasecca tataḥ kuṃbhaṃ tripādopari śobhite ।
elośīrādicāhṛtya gandhadravyaṃ yathāvidhi ।।

dadyādarcakahaste tu gṛhītvā tattu pūjakaḥ ।
pūrṇakuṃbhe tu nikṣipyatoyaṃ tadadhivāsayet ।।

alābhe kuśadūrvairvā tulasīdalamiśritaiḥ ।
abhimṛśya tataḥ kuṃbha "midamāpaśśivā'iti ।।

sūtroktavidhinā kṛtvā puṇyāhaṃ vidhivattadā ।
"śuci vo havya'mantreṇa saṃbhārān prokṣayetkramāt ।।

śodhayitvātu nirmālyaṃ "naśyastu jagatā'miti ।
"ahameveda'muktvā tu pīṭhapuṣpaṃ ca śodhayet ।।

"pūtastasya' samuccārya vedimadbhissuśodhayet ।
dhruvasya pādapuṣpastu viṣṇugāyatriyā tathā ।।

pañcabhirmūrti mantraiśca datvā devaṃ praṇamya ca ।
devanirmālyaśeṣeṇa viṣvaksenaṃ vibhūṣya ca ।।

anyannirmālyamādāya śucisthāne apsu vā kṣivet ।
pūjanārthāṃśca saṃbhārān yathāśakti susaṃbharet ।।

tatassamāhito bhūtvāsaṃbhārārcanamārabhet ।
tattatthsāneṣu pātrāṇi yathārhaṃ sthāpayedbudhaḥ ।।

snānārthamagnikoṇe syādarghyarthaṃ nairṛte api ca ।
pādyārthaṃ vāyudeśe syādācamārthamatheśake ।।

śuddhyarthamekaṃ madhye tu pañcapātramidaṃ kramāt ।
tripādopare nikṣipte viśāle tāmrabhājane ।।

"agniśśu'cīti mantreṇa sthāpayecca hariṃ smaran ।
kuryācca pātrasaṃskāraṃ śoṣaṇādi yathāvidhi ।।

uddhariṇyāṃ gṛhītvātu praṇavena jalaṃ tadā ।
nikṣipya tulasīṃ tasyāṃ puṣpaṃ vā dhāraṇaṃ caret ।।

vārikuṃbhamukhe brahmā tadadho rudra īritaḥ ।
varuṇastu jale dhyeyastathai vāvāhanaṃ caret ।।

tripāde candramāvāhya cādityaṃ cordhvabhājane ।
vasiṣṭhasomayajñāṅgāninduṃ mandraṃ krameṇavai ।।

āgneyādikrameṇaiva pañcapātreṣu cāhvayet ।
karpūrośīrakaṃ caiva gandhānelālavaṅgakam ।।

snānadravyamidaṃ proktaṃ snānapātre tunikṣipet ।
viṣṇuparṇaṃ padmadalaṃ dūrvāṃ śyāmākameva ca ।।

prādyadravyāṇisaṃpādya pādyapātre tu nikṣipet ।
kuśākṣatatilavrīhiyavamāṣāṃstathaiva ca ।।

priyaṅgūṃścaiva siddhārthānarghyapātre tu nikṣipet ।
elośīralavaṅgādiṃ stakkolānīti ca kramāt, ।।

kṣipedācāmapātre tu śuddhatoye tataḥkramāt ।
puṣpāṇi gandhānvinyasyedyathālābhamathāpivā ।।

alābhetattaduccārya tulasīṃ vā vinikṣipet ।
"dhārā'sviti ca mantreṇa pātrāṇyadbhiḥ prapūrayet ।।

"idamāpaśśivāḥ' procya surabhimudrāṃ pradarśya ca ।
pātrābhimantraṇaṃ kuryāddasadigbandhanaṃ caret ।।

viṣṇugāyatrīmuccārya tatrakāryaṃ samācaret ।
ghaṇṭāyāṃ caiva brahmāṇaṃ nāde vedānsamarcayet ।।

tajjihvāyāṃ ṣaḍāsyastusūtrenāgāntsamarcayet ūrdhvevīśaṃ ca śaṅkhārī pārśvayostasyacārcayet ।।

nāle caiva mahādevamiti ghaṇṭādhidevatāḥ ।
tripādasyottaresthāpya vimalantu patadgrahe ।।

varuṇaṃ śaṅkhakukṣau tu mūle tu pṛthivīṃ tathā ।
dhārāyāṃ sarvatīrthāṃśca śaṅkhe candraṃ samarcayet ।।

uddhariṇyāṃ ca pānīyapātre somamathārcayet ।
āsane dharmamāvāhyaplote tvaṣṭārameva ca ।।

aṃbare sūryamāvāhya cottarīye niśākaram ।
bhūṣaṇe ṣaṇmukhaṃ caiva yajñasūtre niśākaram ।।

puṣpe pullaṃ tathā gandhe mukhavāse ca medinīm ।
akṣate kāśyapaṃ dhūpe bṛhaspatimadhāhvāyet ।।

dīpe śriyaṃ ghṛte sāmataile pitṝntsamarcayet ।
upadhāne tathāchatre pāduke śeṣamarcayet ।।

yantrikāyāṃ ca mārtāṇḍaṃ siddhārthe somamarcayet ।
kuśāgre jāhnavīṃ caiva tileṣu pitṛdevatāḥ ।।

taṇḍule ravimāvāhya dadhni cāvāhayedyajuḥ ।
kṣīre atharvāṇamāvāhya madhuparke ṛcaṃ tathā ।।

mātrāyāṃ śarvamāvāhya haviḥpātre divākaram ।
haviṣṇu padmagarbhaṃ ca pānapātre niśākaram ।।

upahārādipātreṣu divākaramathārcayet ।
jyeṣṭhāmāvāhya mārjanyāṃ nartakeśarvamarcayet ।।

gāyake sāmavedaṃ ca nandīśaṃ vādaker'cayet ।
pāñcajanyaṃ ca śaṅkhe tu gaṇikāsvapcarastsriyaḥ ।।

garuḍaṃ paricāreṣu samāvāhya tataḥ kramāt ।
anukteṣu tu dravyeṣu viṣṇumāvāhya kārayet ।।

tattaddravyādhipe smṛtvātattaddravyasamīpataḥ ।
tattaddravyadharatvena caturbhirvigrahairyajet ।।

tattatkarmasu kāle vai yathārhamupayojayet ।
tatkāle pyatha vāvāhyatasmin karmaṇi yojayet ।।

tator'cakaḥ prasannātmādhyātvātmānaṃ janārdanam ।
devasya dakṣiṇebhāge kūrmapīṭhe samāhitaḥ ।।

biṃbārhaṃ saṃsthito vāpi samāsīno atha vā punaḥ ।
dhyātvā dhyānavidhānena japtvācāryapalaṃparām ।।

yogaśāstroktamāgenṇa prāṇāyāmādikaṃ caret ।
bhūtaśuddhiṃ vidhāyādau nyāsānanyāntsamācaret ।।

akārādikṣakārāntamakṣarāṇi yathāvidhi ।
sarvatra sandhiṣu nyasya brahmanyāsaṃ samācaret ।।

"brahma brahmantarātme'ti hṛdayaṃ cābhimarśayet ।
"dyaurdyaira'sīti coccārya mūrdhānaṃ cābhimarśayet ।।

"śikhe udvartayā'mīti spṛśeccaiva śikhāṃ tathā ।
"devānāmāyudhai'ruktvā kavacaṃ bandhayettataḥ ।।

"nārāyaṇāya vidmaha' iti daśadigbhandhanaṃ caret ।
"sudarśanama'bhītyuktvā dakṣiṇe tu sudarśanam ।।

"ravipā'miti vāme ca śaṅkhaṃ ca bibhṛyātkare ।
"sūryosi ca dro asī'tyuktvā netrayordakṣavāmayoḥ ।।

sūryācandramasoścaiva maṇḍale sannyasedbudhaḥ ।
"ahuraṇyaṃ vidhiṃ yajñaṃ brahmāṇaṃ devendra'mityapi ।।

aṅguṣṭhādikaniṣṭhāntaṃ karanyāsaṃ samācaret ।
"antarasminnima'iti brahmāṇaṃ ca hṛdi nyaset ।।

prāṇānāyamya saṃkalpya tithivārādikīrtayet ।
tato mantrāsanaṃ vidvān saṃkalpya ca yathāvidhi ।।

"pratadviṣmussavata'iti iti ta"thāstvāsana'mityapi ।
puṣpadabhankuśeṣvekaṃ pīṭhānte cāsanaṃ dadet ।।

"viśvādhikānā'mityuktvā svāgataṃ tu samācaret ।
"mano abhimantā'mantreṇa deveśamanumānya ca ।।

"trīṇi pa'deti mantreṇa dadyātpādyaṃ padadvaye ।
"āmāvājasya'mantreṇa spṛśyamaghaṃny pradāya ca ।।

devasya dakṣiṇe haste spṛśyaṃ ssṛśyāghanymucyate ।
"śannodevī'riti procya dadyādācamanīyakam ।।

"devasya'tveti mantreṇa cādarśaṃ darśayettataḥ ।
annādyāya samuccārya dantadhāvanamācaret ।।

hiraṇmayaṃ vā raupyaṃ vā dantakāṣṭhaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulam ।
jauduṃbaraṃ vā saṃpādya yathālābhaṃ samācaret ।।

"idaṃ bra'hmeti mantreṇa jihmāśodhanamācaret ।
"yanme garbhe'samuccārya gaṇḍūṣaṃ kṣālanaṃ tathā ।।

"śannodevī'riti procya dadyādācamanaṃ tataḥ ।
"vicakrame' namuccārya mukhavāsaṃ pradāpayet ।।

pūrvavastraṃ visṛjyaiva paridhāpyānyavāsasā ।
grīvāyāḥ pṛṣṭhataḥ kuryādavakuṇṭhanamādarāt ।।

keśānvikīrya mantrajño vāmabhāge ca susthitaḥ ।
"uvānahā'viti procya purastātpādukenyaset ।।

"bhūḥprapadye' samuccārya praṇamya jagatāṃ patim ।
"para bra'hmeti mantreṇa samādāya tu kautukam ।।

svastisūktaṃ tato japtvā "pratadviṣṇu'riti bruvan ।
snānapīṭhe susaṃsthāpya pādyamācamanaṃ dadet ।।

ato devādimantraistu tailamālipya mūrdhani ।
tathaiva viṣṇugāyatṣā sarvāṃgāṇyanulepayet ।।

"parilikhita'miti mantreṇa sarvāṅgamapi śodhayet ।
āmlena khaṇḍaśīkena śarkarābhiryathocitam ।।

alāśodhanaṃ kuryācchrīpatrāmalakāṃbunā ।
śālipiṣṭena gandhādyairaṅgaśodhanamācaret ।।

viśadaṃ śodhayitvātu saṃsnāpyoṣṇena vāriṇā ।
"vārīścatasra'ityuktvā śuddhodairabhiṣecayet ।।

"namo varuṇa'ityuktvā gokṣīrairabhiṣecayet ।
"bhūrānilaya'mantreṇa snāpayedgandhavāriṇā ।।

"agnimīle'samuccārya madhunā snānamācaret ।
"sīnīvā'līti mantreṇa hāridrodakasecanam ।।

tattaddravyāntare caiva bhavecchuddhodakāplapaḥ ।
punargandhodakenaiva "gandhadvārā' mudīrya ca ।।

snāpayeddevadeveśaṃ tūryaghoṣapurassaram ।
caturvedādimantraiśca śuddhodaissnāpayetpunaḥ ।।

"mitrassuparṇa'ityuktvā vimṛjya plotavāsanā ।
pūrvavastraṃ visṛjyaipa parīdhāpya tathetarat ।।

pādyamācamanaṃ dadyātpūrvoktena vidhānataḥ ।
praṇamya devadeveśaṃ datvāpuṣbāñjaliṃ tataḥ ।।

"bhūrasi bhū'rityuccārya jīvasthāne niveśayet ।
"trirdeva'mantramuccārya dṛśyāghanyntu samarpayet ।।

tataḥprokṣya dhruvasthānaṃ gāyatrīmantramuccaran ।
"saṃyuktameta'duccārya dhruvakautukayontataḥ ।।

saṃbandhārthaṃ nyasetkūrcaṃ kautukāgraṃ vidhānataḥ ।
gāyatṣā dhruvapīṭhantu prokṣya śuddhena vāriṇā ।।

"viṣṇave nama'ityuktvā devadevamanusmaran ।
dhruvasya pādayormadhye puṣpanyāsaṃ samācaret ।।

prāgādi ca nyasettatra pādakṣiṇyakrameṇa vai ।
caturthyantena puṣpāṇipuruṣaṃ satyamacyutam ।।

aniruddhamiti rocya mahādikṣu caturṣu ca ।
āgneyādi tathā nyanyedvidikṣu ca krameṇa vai ।।

kapilaṃ caiva yajñaṃ ca nārāyaṇaṃ puṇyameva ca ।
prathamāvaraṇaṃ caitaddvitīyāvaraṇe tataḥ ।।

pūrvoktena krameṇaiva vārāhaṃ nārasiṃhakam ।
vāmanaṃ trivikramaṃ caiva subhadraṃ ca tataḥ param ।।

īśitātmānamityuktvā sarvodvahamataḥ param ।
sarvavidveśvaraṃ ceti samabhyarcyedbahirmukhān ।।

tṛtīyāvaraṇe tattaddigīśāṃśca samarcayet ।
śrīphūmyormūrtimantraiśca devyorapi samācaret ।।

evaṃ dhruvasya pīṭhe tu puṣpanyāsa udāhṛtaḥ ।
atha kautukapīṭhe tu pūrvoktena krameṇa vai ।।

prācyāṃ subhadramāvāhya hayātmakamataḥ param ।
rāmadevaṃ puṇyadevaṃ sarvaṃ caiva sukhāvaham ।।

saṃvahaṃ suvahaṃ ceti prathamāvaraṇer'cayet ।
dvitīyāvaraṇe tadvanmitra matriṃ śivaṃ tataḥ ।।

viśvaṃ sanātanaṃ caiva sanarthanamataḥ param ।
sanatkumāraṃ sanakamarcayecca bahirmukhān ।।

tṛtīyāvaraṇe tadvallokapālāntsamarcayet ।
praṇavādi namo antaṃ syādarcanaṃ nyāsa ucyate ।।

ekādaśabhiraṣṭābhirupacārais tathārcayet ।
tatra devyośca vidhinā dhruvatevyorivācaret ।।

mārkaṇḍeyaṃ bhṛguṃ caiva devadakṣiṇavāmayoḥ ।
brahmāṇaṃ śaṅkaraṃ tadvadbhittipārśve samarcayet ।।

deveśābhimukhānetānyathāvidhi samarcayet ।
dvārārcanaṃ samārabhya śiṣyaḥ kuryādgurūditaḥ ।।

dvāre dvāre dvāradevān dvārapālāntsamarcayet ।
vimānapālān lokeśāṃs tathā caiva'napāyinaḥ ।।

parivārāṃs tathānyāṃśca viṣṇubhūtāntameva ca ।
tattannāmnā samabhyarcya "bhūrānilaya' mantrataḥ ।।

dvāraprakṣālanaṃ kṛtvā dakṣiṇe madhyavāmayoḥ ।
dharmaṃ jñānamathaiśvarya māvāhya susamarcayet ।।

sarvatra dvāravāme tu rakṣārthaṃ śāntamarcayet ।
tato yavanikāṃ kuryāddvāre kṣaumādinirmitām ।।

striyaśśūdrāntu patitāḥ pāṣaṇḍā vedanindakāḥ ।
devatāntara bhaktāśca pāparogādipīḍitāḥ ।।

abhiśastāśca ye pāpāśśāstreṣu tu vininditāḥ ।
pūjākāle tu nārhanti sevituṃ harimavyayam ।।

dhyānamāviśya tatkāle pūjakassusamāhitaḥ ।
ātmasūktaṃ japitvaiva sākṣānnārāyaṇo bhavet ।।

viṣṇuṃ vyāpinamātmāna makhaṇḍānandacinmayam ।
rukmābhaṃ raktanetrāsyapāṇipādaṃ sukhodvaham ।।

kirīṭahārakeyūrakuṇḍalāṅgadabhūṣitam ।
śaṅkhacakradharaṃ devaṃ varadābhayacihnitam ।।

śrīvatsāṃkaṃ mahābāhuṃ kaustubhodbhāsitorasam ।
śukapiñchāṃbaradharaṃ pralaṃbabrahmasūtriṇam ।।

divyāyudhaparīvāraṃ divyabhūṣāvibhūṣitam ।
devībhyāṃ parivāraiśca sevyamānaṃ jagatpatim ।।

dhyāyetsannihitaṃ biṃbe nārāyaṇamanāmayam ।
yathāberaṃ tathā thātvā nyāsakarma tataścaret ।।

suvarbhuvarbhūr ityuktvā mūrdhni nābhau ca sādayoḥ ।
biṃbasya vyāhṛtīrnyasyedvyāhṛtinyāsa ucyate ।।

pādayorantare pīṭhe yakāraṃ ca tatonyaset ।
akāraṃ hṛdayenyasya cādibījaṃ tataḥpunaḥ ।।

āveṣṭya praṇavenaitān praṇāmaṃ punarācaret ।
puṣpagandhākṣatairyuktaṃ śuddhodairabhipūritaṃ ।।

praṇidhiṃ caurdhvamuddhṛtya dīpāddīpamivakramāt ।
"idaṃ viṣṇuriti'procya "cāyātu bhagavā'niti ।।

praṇavātmakamavyaktaṃ divyamaṅgalavigraham ।
dhruvātpraṇidhitoye tu kūrcevāvāhayeddharim ।।

tadvyāptaṃ to yamādāya kautukasya tu mūrdha ni ।
praṇavena samāsrāvya kūrcevāvāhayedguruḥ ।।

mūrtimantrāntsamuccārya tatra kāryaṃ samācaret ।
devyau caiva tathāvāhya samyagabhyarcayedbudhaḥ ।।

tathaivāvāhayedvidvān vidhinā cotsavādiṣu ।
kaitukādbaliberasya kecidāvāhanaṃ viduḥ ।।

alaṅkārāsanaṃ paścātsaṃkalsya ca yathāvidhi ।
asanaṃ mantravaddadyāddeveśamanumānayet ।।

pādyamācamanaṃ cāpi dadyātpūrvoktamantrataḥ ।
"tejovatkyāva'vamantreṇa vastraṃ kṣaumādicārpayet ।।

"bhūto bhūteṣu' mantreṇa bhūṣaṇaiśca vibhūṣya ca ।
"somasya tanūra'sītyuktvādhārayeduttarīyakam ।।

aṣṭākṣareṇa mantreṇa cordhvapuṇḍraṃ ca dhārayet ।
"agniṃ dūtami'ti procya yajñasūtraṃ samarpayet ।।

"tadviṣṇoriti mantreṇa puṣpādyaiḥ pūjayettataḥ ।
mūrtimantrāntsamuccārya keśavādibhireva vā ।।

aṣṭottaraśataistadvadaṣṭottarasahasrakaiḥ ।
anantainānmabhiḥ pūjyo anantanāmā bhavān hariḥ ।।

"tadviprāsa' iti procya candanenānulepayet ।
"paromātra'yetyuccārya dhūpamāghrāpayettataḥ ।।

"viṣṇoḥ karmāṇi' mantreṇa dīpaṃ tasmai pradarśayet ।
"trirdeva'iti mantreṇa dadyādaghaṃ ca pūrvavat ।।

upacāreṣu sarveṣu priyamaghaṃny haressmṛtam ।
tasmānnivedayeddhīmān madhupakonpamaṃ śubham ।।

acamanantu tasyānte pūrvamantreṇa kārayet ।
droṇataṇḍulamādāya tadardhaṃ pādamevavā ।।

taṇḍulārthatilairyuktaṃ mukhavāsaphalānvitam ।
gṛhītvā kāṃsyapātretu devasyāgre nidhāya ca ।।

daśanyeddevadevasya "somaṃ rājāna'muccaran ।
devārpitaistu nirmālyaiḥ pūjayitvār'cakaṃ tataḥ ।।

"ghṛtātpa'rīti mantreṇa daśanyitvākaraṃ hareḥ ।
arcakāya pradeyaṃ syānmātrādānamiti smṛtam ।।

bahuśo dakṣiṇāṃ dadyāddānasādguṇyasiddhaye ।
"devasya'tveti mantreṇa parigṛhya tadarcakaḥ ।।

upayuñjyātkuṭuṃbārthe sa hi dāyaharo hareḥ ।
devadravyovabhoge tu yaśśāstraidonṣa īritaḥ ।।

vaikhānasānāṃ taddoṣā nāsti devaprasādataḥ ।
praṇamya devadeveśaṃ mantrairvedādisaṃbhavaiḥ ।।

strotraiśca vividhaintsutvā pāde puṣpāñjaliṃ kṣipet ।
daśanyedvividhākārān dīpānmantreṇa tatra tu ।।

kuṃbhadīpaṃ samādāya devāgre tu vinikṣipet ।
vārāhaṃ nārasiṃhaṃ ca cāmanaṃ ca trivikramam ।।

daleṣvabhyarcya vidhinā dīpe lakṣmīṃ samarcayet ।
vartikāyāṃ śriyaṃ caiva dhūme abhyarcyabhavaṃ tathā ।।

prokṣyopacārairabhyarchya puṣpagandhādibhiḥ kramāt ।
"śubhrā jyoti'riti procya karābhyāṃ parigṛhya ca, ।।

pradakṣiṇaṃ trivāraṃ tu darśayan bhrāmayeddharim ।
sarvavādyasamāyuktaṃ taṃ dīpaṃ parigṛhya ca ।।

śiṣyo vā gaṇikā vāpi devāgāraṃ parītya ca ।
visṛjeccaiva taṃ dīpaṃ pṛṣṭhe yūthādhipasya ca ।।

taddīpadarśanānnṝṇāmāyuśśrīputrasaṃvadaḥ ।
saṃbhavanti na sandeho viṣṇornī rājanaṃ hī tat ।।

citraiścavālavyajanais tatkāle vījayedguruḥ ।
darbaṇaṃ cāmaraṃ chatraṃ vyajanaṃ caturaṅgakam ।।

nṛttaṃ gītaṃ ca vādyaṃ ca vaiṣṇavaṃ mantramuccaran ।
devasya darśayitvātu stotraṃ vedaiḥkramāccaret ।।

tathā nānāvidhaistotraiśśrāvayedacyutaṃ harim ।
anuktaṃ caiva yatsarvamūhayitvā samācaret ।।

śrībhūmyohṛndaye nyasya tattadbījākṣaraṃ pṛthak ।
tatsūktābhyāṃ ṣoḍaśopacārairabhyarcayetkramāt ।।

utcavādeśca pūrvoktaṃ sarvamarcanamācaret ।
tatobhojyānanaṃ caiva saṃkalpya ca yathāvidhi ।।

ghṛtaṃ madhu guḍaṃ caiva payo dadhi samanvitam ।
prasthamātraṃ tu saṃgrāvyāṃ madhupakanmihocyate ।।

"yanmadhuneti mantreṇa madhupākaṃ nivedayet ।
paścādācamanaṃ datvāśiṣyaṃ kārye niyojayet ।।

"athāvanīda'mantreṇa śodhayitvā sthalaṃ tataḥ ।
maṇḍalaṃ caturaśraṃ ca kārayetbaricārakaḥ ।।

haviḥ pātrāṇi saṃśodhya ravimabhyarchya teṣu vai ।
abhighārya ghṛtenaiva havistatra tu nikṣipet ।।

"amṛtopastaraṇama'sītyatra kāryaṃ samācaret ।
upadaṃśādikaṃ tatra guḍaṃ dadhi phalāni ca ।।

nikṣipya viṣṇugāyatṣā pṛthakpātreṣvasaṃkaram ।
"yatte susīma' mantreṇa goghṛtenābhighārya ca ।।

devasyāgre tu nikṣipya tripādeṣu yathāvidhi ।
havirarpaṇakāle tu na sevyo harirucyate ।।

tasmādvaikhānasān hitvā brāhmaṇā anyasūtriṇaḥ ।
na viśeyustathānye ca tatkāle viṣṇumandiram ।।

kavāṭaṃ bandhayetpaścāt ghaṇṭānādaṃ ca kārayet ।
tūryaghoṣādikaṃ kuryānmṛḍuvādyapriyo hariḥ ।।

tator'cakaḥ prasannātmā devadevamanusmaran ।
haviḥpātreṣu tulasīṃ nikṣipyāṣṭākṣareṇa tu ।।

puṣpairabhyarcya saṃprokṣya praṇavaiḥ pariṣicya ca ।
abhimṛśyānnasūktena surabhimudrāṃ pradarśya ca ।।

"tadasya priya'mityuktvā haviruṣṇaṃ nivedayet ।
"subhūssvayaṃbhūṃ'tyuktvā apūpaṃ ca nivedayet ।।

pṛthukādīni cānyāni "viśvabheṣaja'mantrataḥ ।
apakvāni ca vastūni sarvamaṣṭākṣareṇa tu ।।

"idaṃ viṣṇu'ssamuccārya pānīyaṃ svādu śītalam ।
nivedayitvā gaṇḍūṣaṃ pādyamācamanaṃ dadet, ।।

"ghṛtātba'rīti mantreṇa mukhavāsaṃ pradāpayet ।
viṣṇugāyatrīmuccārya dadyātpuṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ ।।

nityāgnikuṇḍe chullyāṃ vā pariṣicya ca pāvakam ।
caruṇājyena juhuyāsmūrtimantraiḥkramādbudhaḥ ।।

devyādibhyastathā hutvā vaiṣṇavaṃ ca yajetkramāt ।
puṣpanyāsoktadevebhyaḥ pāṣandānāṃ tathaiva ca ।।

trikāleṣūttamaṃ proktamadhamaṃ prātarevahi ।
prātarmadhyāhnayoścaiva madhyamaṃ homalakṣaṇam ।।

rakṣedagnimavicchinnamaśakto yaśca rakṣitam ।
samidhyātmani vāropya praṇīyāharaharyajet ।।

tatoyātrāsanaṃ vidvān saṃkalpya vidhinā budhaḥ ।
prokṣyālaṅkṛtya cādāya rathaṃ vā caturantaram ।।

baliberaṃ samāropya sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam ।
"rathantaraṃ' samuccārya tatra kāryaṃ samācaret ।।

"yogeśaṃ paraṃbrahmāṇaṃ paramātmānamityapi ।
bhaktavatsala'mityuktvā mūrtimantraistathā harim ।।

nārācarajjvā nudṛḍhaṃ bandhayedrahasikramāt ।
"viṣṇustvā'miti mantreṇa pādau sṛṣṭvā namenmuhuḥ ।।

"somaṃ rājāna'muccārya chatraṃ mūrdhani dhārayet ।
"marutaḥ paramā'tmeti pārśvayoścāmare dadet ।।

"vāyupa'rīti mantreṇa vyajanairvījayeddharim ।
tathānyaissumahāhainśca yuktodivyaparicchadaiḥ ।।

ghaṇṭāraveṇa saṃyuktaṃ śaṅkhabherīnināditaiḥ ।
bherīmṛdaṅgapaṇavanissālaiḥ kāhalairapi ।।

mardalairdivyavādyaiśca layaśrutisamanvitaiḥ ।
upatiṣṭhejjagadyoniṃ nārāyaṇamanāmayam ।।

śiṣyamāhūya tatkāle soṣṇiṣaṃ sottarīyakarm ।
ūrdhvepuṣpaṃ ca sannyasya prokṣayitvā ca mantrataḥ ।।

tasyoṣṇīṣoparisthāpya balipātraṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
alaṅkṛtya ca mālyādyaiḥpūjayettākṣanyvatsmaret ।।

vāhayitvā baliṃ tena balipātreṇa caiva hi ।
sarvadvāreṣu sarvatra puṣpanyāsoktamāgantaḥ ।।

pūrvāntamuttarāntaṃ ca nikṣipettu baliṃ kramāt ।
toyaṃ puṣpaṃ baliṃ toyaṃ catvārastatra vigrahāḥ ।।

tato devaṃ samānīya kramamāṇāśśanaiśsanaiḥ ।
vāhakā vāhayeyustaṃ rathaṃ sarvaṅgasundaram ।।

krameṇa namrakāyastu kṣipecchiṣyo baliṃ kramāt ।
baliṃ datpāgrato gaccheddevena saha vā pṛthak ।।

tato devaṃ kramānnītvā prādakṣiṇyakrameṇa vai ।
tatkāle tu balirdeya statkramastupravakṣyate ।।

maṇikaṃ ca tatassandhyāṃ pradhamadvārapālakau ।
tāpasaṃ siddhidaṃ caiva dvitīya dvārapālakau ।।

nyakṣendrāvantarāle ca yathāvidhi samarcayet ।
prathamāvaraṇadvāre kiṣkindhaṃ tīrdhameva ca ।।

dditīyāvaraṇadvāre gaṇeśaṃ śeṣamarcayet ।
tṛtīyāvaraṇadvāre śaṅkhapadmanidhī tathā ।।

tuhiṇaṃ ca balindaṃ ca caturthāvaraṇe tathā ।
pañcamāvaraṇe caiva khaḍgaṃ śāṅkhaṃ samarcayet ।।

ṣaṣṭhe cāvaraṇa śaṅkhacakracūḍau samarcayet ।
caṇḍaṃ tathā pracaṇḍaṃ ca saptamāvaraṇer'cayet ।।

sopānamadhye śrībhūtaṃ garuḍaṃ ca samarcayet ।
havīrakṣakamagniṃ ca āgneyyāṃ samyagarcayet ।।

vimānadakṣiṇe pārśve vivasvantaṃ yamaṃ tathā ।
nairṛtyāṃ vādya'rakṣaṃ ca nirṛtiṃ ca samarcayet ।।

paścime mitramabhyarcyettathā varuṇameva ca ।
vāyavyāmarcayeccaiva puṣpeśamarutau tathā ।।

uttarasyāṃ tu kṣattāraṃ kuberaṃ ca samarcayet ।
īśānaṃ bhāskaraṃ caiva tathaiśānye samarcayet ।।

bhūtapīṭhe samabhyarcya cakraṃ caiva dhvajaṃ tathā ।
śaṅkhaṃ yūthādhipaṃ caiva akṣahantaṃ tathārcayet ।।

pīṭhasya dakṣiṇe bhāge "ye bhūtā' iti mantrataḥ ।
bhūtayakṣapiśācebhyo baliśeṣaṃ tu nirvapet ।।

pādau prakṣālya cācamya tatra kāryaṃ samācaret ।
nṛttageyādiyuktaṃ tu divyastotraissamanvitam ।।

pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā bhrāmayitvā jagadgurum ।
sopānamadhye saṃsthāpya rajjubandhaṃ visṛjya ca ।।

jayaśabdaistathāmantrairdadyānnī rājanaṃ tataḥ ।
tato devaṃ samādāya svasthāne tu niveśayet ।।

viṣṇusūktaṃ samuccārya praṇāmaṃ muhurācaret ।
dadyātpuṣpāñjaliṃ caiva dvādaśāṣṭaṣaḍakṣaraiḥ ।।

pauruṣaṃ sūktamuccārya praṇavaṃ ca samuccaran ।
mukhavāsaṃ samarpyaiva śaktito dakṣiṇāṃ dadet ।।

tataḥpatadgrahāttīrthamādāyaiva tu pūjakaḥ ।
triḥpibenniyato bhūtvā tulasīmapi bhakṣayet ।।

pratyūṣaśca prabhātaśca madhyāhnaścāparāhmakaḥ ।
sāyaṅkālo niśīthaśca pūjākālāntu ṣaṭ smṛtāḥ ।।

prātaḥkālercanaṃ kuryājjapahomābhivṛddhaye ।
rājarāṣṭrābhivṛddhyarthaṃ madhyāhnārcanamiṣyate ।।

sāyaṅkāler'canaṃ caiva sarvasasyābhivṛddhaye ।
uṣaḥkālār'canaṃ proktaṃ prajāpaśuvivṛddhaye ।।

aparāhṇārcanaṃ caiva daityanāśanahetave ।
ardharātrār'canaṃ proktaṃ catuṣpādabhivṛddhaye ।।

evaṃ ṣaṭkālapūjāyāṃ phalamuktaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
ṣaṭkālaṃ vā trikālaṃ vā dvikālaṃ kālameva vā ।।

pūjanaṃ devadevasya tvaihikāmuṣmikapradam ।
ṣaṭkāla pūjane kuryādādāvāhanaṃbudhaḥ ।।

tathāntya velārcanāyāṃ kuryādudvāsanaṃ param ।
upasandhyāsu deveśamāsanādyaṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।।

samabhyarcya havirdadyādvinā homaṃ baliṃ tathā ।
puṣpanyāsaṃ ca homaṃ ca parivārārcanaṃ balim ।।

nityayātrotsavaṃ caivetyupasandhyāsu varjayet ।
trikālamarcane anyatra mnapanaṃ prātareva hī ।।

prokṣaṇaṃ cānyakāle tu mantreṇetyāha pūjanam ।
śiṣyāṇāmapyabhāve tu varṣādyupahatau tathā ।।

tathā vādyādyabhāve vā balikāle samāgate ।
tadā devāntsamāvāhya dvārāgre nikṣipedbalim ।।

sūryastvāmantramuccārya kavāṭaṃ bandhayettataḥ ।
madhyāhne caiva sāyāhne kāle kāle tathācaret ।।

tathaivodghaṭayetkāle sarvaṃ pūrvavadarcanam ।
puṣpaṃ dvārārcitaṃ śodhya punardvāre samarcayet ।।

dhruvapīṭhetu puṣpāṇi na śodhyāni punaḥpunaḥ ।
tāni puṣpāṇyanuddhṛtya tadūrdhve nyāsamācaret, ।।

sāyārcane tu tāni syuninrmālyāni na cānyataḥ ।
kautukādyarcitaṃ puṣpamādāya vidhinā budhaḥ ।।

pīṭhe pārśve nidhāyānyairarcayettu navairnavaiḥ ।
antyavelārcanānte tu saṃkalbya śayanāsanam ।।

vimucya vastramālyādīn sūkṣmavastraṃ samarpya ca ।
abhyarcya puṣbagandhādyairdevadevaṃ śriyaḥpatim ।।

sarvauṣadhivimiśraṃ ca kaṣāyaṃ toyameva ca ।
nivedya devadevasya mukhavāsaṃpradāpayet ।।

"yadvaiṣṇava'miti procya mṛduvādyairmanoramaiḥ ।
divyopadhānasahite divyālaṅkāraśobhite ।।

pariṣkṛte vitānādvairdivyadhūpaiḥ sudhūpite ।
mahāhānstaraṇopete śayane śāyayeddharim ।।

śrībhūmyau ca samādāya tanmantrābhyāṃ kramādguruḥ ।
śāyayeddevapāśenv tu "dhruvanta'iti coccaret ।।

"aricitassuṣṭutaścāsi suparṇagaruḍadhvaja ।
cakrapāṇe mahābāho yatheṣṭaṃ vasa oṃ namaḥ' ।।

iti mantraṃ samuccārya bhaktyā paramāyā yutaḥ ।
prātarāvāhitāṃ śaktiṃ dhruvabere avaropayet ।।

pradakṣiṇaṃ praṇāmaṃ ca kṛtvā mantreṇa deśikaḥ ।
stutvā puruṣasūktena viṣṇugāyatriyā tathā ।।

vyāpakatrayamantraiśca tathā "viṣṇornukā'dibhiḥ ।
"ato devā'dibhirmantrairmantrairanyaiśca vaiṣṇavaiḥ ।।

ekākṣarādisūktaiśca dvādaśāṣṭaṣaḍakṣaraiḥ ।
muhuḥpuṣpājaliṃ datvākṣāmayeddoṣasaṃcayam ।।

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa pūjanaṃ cautsavādiṣu ।
brahmasthānaṃ kautukasya pūrvameva samīritam ।।

pāśanvyoḥkautukasyātha sthāpayetsnāpanautsavau ।
uttare kautukasyaiva baliberasya saṃsthitiḥ ।।

garbhālayasya saṃkoce tvatha vā mukhamaṇḍape ।
antarāle atha vā sthāpya pūjayetsnāpanautsavau ।।

snāpanautsavayoḥkuryātpūrvoktārcanamuttamam ।
āsanādyupacārāṃśca kalpayet ṣoḍaśātha vā ।।

trayodaśopacāraiśca śāntaṃ samyaksamarcayet ।
navopacārairabhyarcyedanapāyigaṇāṃs tathā ।।

dvāradevān dvārapālān lokapālāṃstathaiva ca ।
aṣṭopacārairabhyarcyenmūrtimantraiḥ samācaret ।।

itarān parīvārāṃśca yajet ṣoḍaśavigrahaiḥ ।
tathaiva pākalakṣmyāśca dvāralakṣmyāśca kārayet ।।

śrīvatsalakṣmyāśca tathā devena saha cācaret ।
avatārapratiṣṭhāyāṃ dhruvarcāṃ vātha kārayet ।।
trivikramapratiṣṭhāyāṃ dhruvārcāmarcayettataḥ ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre aṣṭādaśo adhyāyaḥ

zählung bei ???

athaikonaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

athaikonaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ 
bhagavadarcanam
ata ūrdhvaṃ dhruvārcāyām arcanaṃ saṃpravakṣyate ।
mūrdhādi pīṭhātsannyastapuṣpādīnyapi śodhayet ।।

yogavīrārcanaṃ syāccettrikālaṃ snānamācaret ।
prātarmadhyāhnayorvātha yogapīṭhedhruvār'canam ।।

bhogameva dhruvārcāyāṃ prātarmadhyāhna yorapi ।
trikālaṃ vātha saṃsnāpya dhruvārcāyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

vastrādīnyapi saṃśodhya puṣpanyāsaṃ ca pūrvavat ।
śivādīnarcayitvātu pādapīṭhe samantataḥ ।।

tathāsanādyaissarvaiśca trisaṃdhyaṃ cārcayedbudhaḥ ।
ardhayāme tu pūrvāntamarcayitvā ca pūrvavat ।।

havirni vedayeccaivānuktamasyacca pūrvavat ।
āvāhanavisargau tuna kuryāditi śāsanam ।।

atha vakṣyer'canāntetu vidhānaṃ prati karmaṇām ।
sauvarṇamuttamaṃ pātraṃ rājataṃ madhyame bhavet ।।

adhamaṃ tāmrapātraṃ tu trividhaṃ pātra mucyate ।
tritālamuttamaṃ proktaṃ dvitālaṃ madhyamaṃ bhavet ।।

adhamaṃ tvekatālaṃ syāttrividhaṃ pātravistaram ।
vistāreṇa samākhyātaṃ tayormadhyamamadhyamam ।।

tasya madhye tribhāgaikaṃ karṇikāṃgulamucchrayam ।
pareto aṣṭadalaṃ kuryātkarṇikocchrayamānataḥ ।।

dvyaṅgulaṃ mūlanāhaṃ syāttadagraṃ tvardhanāhakam ।
kiñcitphalāṃbujākāramagraṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

dviprasthataṇḍulaiḥ pakvamannaṃ tatraiva nikṣipet ।
abhighārya ghṛtenaiva aṣṭāṃgulasamunnatam ।।

daśāṅgulaṃ vā utsedhaṃ dvādaśāṃgulamevavā ।
tatpātrañca samādāya kautukāgre nidhāya ca ।।

kautukācchaktimādāya cārcayedaṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।
"parabrahmāṇa mityuktvā paramātmānamityapi ।।

bhaktavatsalaṃ yogeśaṃ' caturmūrtibhirarcayet ।
prātaḥpuṣpabaliṃ kuryānmadhyāhnennabaliṃ tathā ।।

sāye tvarghyabaliṃ kuryātpūrvameva pracoditam ।
taṇḍulaiḥ kuḍubaiścāpi yathālābhamathāpi vā ।।

śrutaṃ cārghyabaliṃ kuryātpuṣbaṃ tu caturaṅgulam ।
śiṣyamāhūya tatkāle soṣṇīṣaṃ sottarīyakam ।।

śiṣyaṃ garuḍa vatsmṛtvā pātramuddhṛtyatatra vai ।
"udutya'miti mantreṇa śiṣyastacchirasi nyaset ।।

pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kuryātkur yācchabdaravairyutam ।
vitānachatrasaṃyuktaṃ piñchacāmarasaṃyutam ।।

dhūpadīpasamāyuktaṃ śanaiḥkuryātpradakṣiṇam ।
pradakṣiṇatrayaṃ kṛtvā praviśedālayaṃ bhudhaḥ ।।

bhūtapīṭhāntare tiṣṭhedgṛhṇīyāttu tadarcakaḥ ।
kautukāgretu sannyasya oṅkāreṇa niveśayet ।।

balyagraṃ khaṇḍayitvātu seneśāya nivedayet ।
taccheṣaṃ sodakaṃ caiva bhūtapīṭhe tu nikṣipet ।।

utsavaṃ kartukāmaścettrisaṃdhiṣvevamuttamam ।
sāyaṃ prātarmadhyamaṃ syātsāyaṃ caivādhamaṃ bhavet ।।

baliṃ ca baliberaṃ vā kārayediti ke ca na ।
balyarthaṃ klaptadevasya cordhvamānamudāhṛtam ।।

mahāberasya hastena caikaviṃśatikāṃgulam ।
saptadaśāṅgulaṃ vidyāddvādaśāṃgulameva vā ।।

śreṣṭhamadhyakaniṣṭhāni trividhaṃ mānamācaret ।
arcāberatribhāgai kamuttamapratimābhavet ।।

tanmānasya daśāṃśena tvekonaṃ madhyamaṃ bhavet ।
madhyamasya daśāṃśena tvekonamadhamaṃ bhavet ।।

mahato mūlaberasya mukhāyāmaṃ praśasyate ।
balyarthaṃ pratimāṃ kuryātsarveṣāṃ sthāpanaṃ bhavet ।।

sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ śreṣṭhamadhyamagauṇataḥ ।
ratnajapratimāṃ kuryānmānonmānaṃ na vidyate ।।

uṣṇīṣaṃ golakaṃ jñeyaṃ śiromānaṃ trimātrakam ।
keśāntārcā samaṃ bhāgaṃ saṃgamātpuṭasūtrakam ।।

puṭasūtrāddhanuparyantamekamekantu bhāgaśaḥ ।
galamardhāṅgulaṃ vindyānmātrārdhaṃ grīvamucyate ।।

hikkāhṛdayaparyantaṃ mukhaṃ mātrādhikaṃ bhavet ।
hṛdayaṃ nābhi tathaivoktaṃ tadadhastāttu tatsamam ।।

ūrū ca dvimukhāyāmaṃ golakotsedhamiṣyate ।
caraṇaṃ jānumānaṃ ca kālāyapurato param? ।।

hikkāsūtrādadhastāttu bāhudvimukhanetrakam ।
prakoṣṭhaṃ mukhabandhaṃ ca mukhamardhādhikaṃ bhavet ।।

maṇibandhāṅgulasyāgre mukhayāmaṃ praśasyate ।
caturbhujaṃ ca kṛtvā tu mānamevamudāhṛtam ।।

vakuryātpadmākāraṃ tu golakam ।
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa haviṣpākaṃ vidhānataḥ ।।

paktvā vittānusāreṇa havīṃṣyapi ca kalpayet ।
alpe mahati vā tulyaṃ phalamāḍhyadaridrayoḥ ।।

nivedayitvā deveśaṃ kalyāṇaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ ।
avadatvā? ghṛtaṃ yattu kalyāṇamaśubhāyavai ।।

alābhe caiva sarveṣāṃ vrīhīṇāṃ taṇḍulāṃ ḥs tathā ।
śatadvayaṃ pañcaviṃśadvrīhibhiḥ pūritaṃ tu yat ।
śuktimātramiti khyātaṃ mānaṃ tenaiva kārayet ।।

taddvayaṃ tilamityuktaṃ prakuñcaṃ syāttiladvayam ।
prasṛtistaddvayaṃ proktaṃ kuḍubaṃ prasṛtidvayam ।।

añjali staddvayaṃ proktaṃ prasthaṃ syādañjalidvayam ।
pātraṃ prasthadvayaṃ proktamāḍhakaṃ taddvayaṃ bhavet ।।

caturāḍhakasaṃyuktaṃ droṇamityabhidhīyate ।
droṇadvayaṃ bhavetkhārī bhāraṅkhārīdvayaṃ bhavet ।।

droṇataṇḍulasaṃyuktamuttamaṃ havirucyate ।
tadardhaṃ madhyamaṃ proktantadardhamadhamaṃ bhavet ।।

uttamottamamityuktamaṣṭadroṇaintu taṇḍulaiḥ ।
adhikaṃ yadbhavettasmātproktaṃ sarvaṃ mahāhaviḥ ।।

tadardhaistaṇḍulaiḥ siddhaṃ madhyamaṃ havirucyate ।
ṣaḍdroṇaistaṇḍulaiḥ siddhaṃ haviruttamamadhyamam ।।

droṇahīnaṃ bhavettasmāduttamādhamamucyate ।
madhyamottamamityuktaṃ caturdreṇaistu taṇḍulaiḥ ।।

droṇatrayaṃ bhavedyatra kṛtaṃ madhyamamadhyamam ।
madhyamādhamamityuktaṃ droṇadvayakṛtaṃ haviḥ ।।

droṇena taṇḍulenaiva nivedya'madhamottamam ।
tasya madhyamamityuktamāḍhakadvaya sammitam ।।

āḍhakena tu saṃyukta madhasūdhamamucyate ।
taṇḍulānāḍhakārdhaṃ tu devīnāṃ tu prakalpayet ।।

caruprasthadvayaṃ proktaṃ havirāḍhakamucyate ।
prasthaṃ kuḍubasaṃyuktaṃ piśācānāṃ balirbhavet ।।

gandhavarṇarasairjuṣṭāḥ pragrāhyāstaṇḍulāstathā ।
prakṣālya taṇḍulān samyak niṣbīḍya ca punaḥpunaḥ ।।

catuḥ prakṣālanaṃ kṛtvā "prajāsthā'līti mantrataḥ ।
"ūrjasva'tīti mantreṇa pātre prakṣipya taṇḍulān ।।

chullyāmāropayetpaścā "dviṣṇave juṣṭa'mityapi ।
"vācaspa'tīti mantreṇa havissvinnantu pācayet ।।

dhūmagandharasaṃ svinnamatipakvaṃ ca śītalam ।
keśakīṭāpaviddhantu tyajetparyuṣitaṃ tathā ।।

mudgaṃ caiva mahāmudgaṃ kūṭasthaṃ rājamāṣakam ।
kadalī panasaṃ caiva kūśmāṇḍaṃ bṛhatī tathā ।।

kandamūlaphalānyanye sārāḍhyā upadaṃśakāḥ ।
guḍaṃ dadhi samāyuktamājyayuktaṃ ।।

haviḥkṛtvā caturbhāgamūrdhvabhāge nivedayet ।
adhastādekabhāgena homārthaṃ balaye tathā ।।

yadaṃśaṃ pātrasaṃśiṣṭaṃ pūjāyaiva ca nirmitam ।
sauvarṇe rājate pātre kāñcye tāmre nivedayet ।।

agni kāryāvaśiṣṭaṃ ca baliśiṣṭaṃ ca yaddhaviḥ ।
tatsarvaṃ pūjakāyaiva proktamevaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।।

dvitīyāvaraṇe proktamāgneyyāṃ pacanālayam ।
arcakasya gṛhe vāpi pācayitvā nivedayet ।।

praṇidhiṃ cājyasthālīṃ ca prokṣaṇīpātrameva ca ।
arghyapradānapātraṃ ca kuḍubena prapūritam ।।

haviḥpātrapramāṇantaṃ balipātrapramāṇataḥ ।
pānīyadānapātraṃ ca kāṃsyaṃ śuktijameva vā ।।

hiraṇmayaṃ vā raupyaṃ vā yadhāśobhamalaṅkṛtam ।
tāṃbūladāne pyevaṃ syātsauvarṇaṃ kāṃsyameva hi ।।

dapanṇaṃ ca pradātavyaṃ dhruvānasasamaṃ bhavet ।
āvāhanārthapraṇithiṃ prasthamātra prapūritam ।।

kaluṣaṃ kṛmiśaivālayuktaṃ sūtravivarjitam ।
gandhavarṇarasairjuṣṭamaśucisthānamāśritam ।।

paṅkāśmadūṣitaṃ caiva sāmudraṃ palvalodakam ।
agrāhyamudakaṃ grāhyamebhirdeṣairvivarjitam ।।

uttamaṃ triguṇair adbhissānaṃ cāthamamucyate ।
abhiṣeko nadībhnantu madhyame madhyamaṃ bavet ।।

uśīracandanopetaṃ yajjalaṃ pādyamucyate ।
elālavaṅgatakkolajātīphalasamanvitam ।।

āpa ācamanīyārthamuśīrāmayacandanaiḥ ।
āpaḥkṣīrakuśāgrādi yavasiddhārthataṇḍulaiḥ ।।

tilavrīhi samāyuktairarghya maṣṭāṅga mucyate ।
candanaṃ cāguruścaiva kuṅkumaṃ gandha ucyate, ।।

ekaṃ dvayaṃ trayaṃ vāpi karbūreṇa catuṣṭayam ।
uśīracanṭanopetaṃ ghṛtayuktaṃ ghṛtāplutam ।।

kiñcitkarbūrasaṃyuktaṃ dhūpamityucyate budhaiḥ ।
goghṛtena kṛtaṃ yattu dīpamuttamamucyate ।।

caturaṅgulamāyāmaṃ rājasaṃ dīpameva hi ।
dīpaṃ tattṣaṅgulāyāmaṃ madhyamaṃ dīpamucyate ।।

adhamaṃ tu bhaveddīpamaṅguladvayasammitam ।
kāpilena gṛtenāpi kṛtaṃ karbūravartikam ।।

dīpaṃ viṣṇupriyaṃ proktaṃ sarvasiddhipradāyakam ।
tāmasaṃ tu bhaveddīpaṃ māhiṣeṇa tu sarpiṣā ।।

vṛkṣabījodbhavasnehadīpaṃ paiśācamucyate ।
tāmasaṃ vāpi paiśācamayogyaṃ dīpamucyate ।।

kṣaumaṃ kārpāsajaṃ vastraṃ vakṣabhedāṅgasaṃbhavam ।
daśahastāyataṃ caiva vistāraṃ tu dvihastakam ।।

manoharaṃ tu suślakṣṇaṃ viśeṣaṃ vastramucyate ।
berāyāmārdhamānena vastravistāra mucyate ।।

vistārāṣṭaguṇāyāmaṃ sadaśaṃ tu salakṣaṇam ।
mayūrapiñchaiḥkuryāttu catustālaṃ tu vistṛtam ।।

adhomukhaṃ tu kartavyamata ūrdhvamukhaṃ tathā ।
pañcāratnipramāṇeva daṇḍassyādadhamaṃ tathā ।।

adhikaṃ dvādaśāṅgulyaṃ madhyamecottamepi vā ।
evaṃ piñchaṃ samākhyātaṃ chatralakṣaṇamucyate ।।

ṣaṭtānaṃ chatravistāramuttamaṃ samudāhṛtam ।
madhyamaṃ pañcatālaṃsyācca tustālamathādhamam ।।

mauktikaṃ tu bhavecchatraṃ vastreśāpi hitaṃ tathā ।
vastreṇa vā tathā kuryāttālapatramathāpi vā ।।

chatraṃ tvadhomukhaṃ proktaṃ daṇḍaṃ piñchasya daṇḍavat ।
suvarṇaratnasaṃyuktaṃ kuryādābharaṇādikam ।।

mukuṭaṃ kuṇḍalaṃ caiva hāraṃ kaiyūrakaṃ tathā ।
kaṭakaṃ kaṭisūtraṃ ca puṣpaṃ vai hāranūpure ।।

kuryādudarabandhaṃ ca ratnahāraṃ ca mekhalām ।
hāraṃ ca karṇapuṣpaṃ ca pratimāyā yathārhakam ।।

cāmarai ścāmaraṃ kuryātpiñchairvāpi mayūrajaiḥ ।
daṇḍaṃ haktapramāṇaṃ syādbāladaṇḍapramāṇakam ।।

hemaratnamayaṃ daṇḍaṃ tāratāmramayaṃ tathā ।
atha vā dārudaṇḍaṃ syānmayūrapiñchaṃ ca yojayet ।।

evaṃ tu cāmaraṃ proktaṃ pracchannapaṭamucyate ।
kṣaumakārpāsasaṃyuktaṃ dvāramānantu kārayet ।।

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa sahasradhārāvidhikramam ।
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ vāpi tāmraṃ vāpi svaśaktitaḥ ।।

uttamaṃ ṣoḍaśāṅgulyaṃ madhyamaṃ dvādaśāṃgulam ।
aṣṭāṃgulaṃ tadadhamaṃ yathāśakti ca kārayet ।।

etairaṅgulibhissamyak bhramīkṛtya ca candravat ।
bhāgaṃ bhittyunnataṃ proktaṃ golakaṃ vā viśeṣataḥ ।।

sīmāvṛttaṃ tu vistāramaṣṭāṅgulamiti smṛtam ।
karṇi kāyāmavistāraṃ golakaṃ tu yavonnatam ।।

madhye ratnaṃ suvarṇaṃ vā yathā śakti samarpayet ।
karṇikāmabhitaḥ kuryāddalānyaṣṭa susaṃgatam ।।

paritaṣṣoḍaśadalaṃ dvātriṃśatkarṇikaṃ bahiḥ ।
catuṣṣaṣṭisamāyuktaṃ dalaṃ bāhye prakalpayet ।।

dale yavadvayaghanaṃ rekhāmapi ca kārayet ।
sahasrasuṣirairyuktaṃ samānoktaṃ ca kārayet ।।

ṣoḍaśadvādaśāṣṭābhiraṅgulyāyāmavistṛtam ।
mālaṃ taddhastavistāraṃ śaṅkhāntarasamīkṛtam ।।

padmākṛtiṃ ca kṛtvā tu tau ca nālasamāyutau ।
śeṣaṃ yuktyā prakurvīta jalanirgamanaṃ budhaḥ,, ।।

sarvasaindaryasaṃyuktaṃ tathākāraṃ ca kārayet ।
prakṣālya pañcagavyena śodhanīyena śodhayet ।।

devālayasya purito gomayenopalipya ca ।
thānyarāśiṃ samāstīrya vastraṃ copari vinyaset ।।

uttare vāstuhomaṃ ca paryakniṃ caiva pūrvavat ।
ācāryaṃ pūjayettatra navavastrāṅgulīyakāḥ, ।।

tantrendumaṇḍalaṃ dhyātvā padme padmanidhiṃ tathā ।
śaṅkhe śaṅkhanidhiṃ tadvadāvāhyaiva samarcayet ।।

puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvā tu dakṣiṇāṃ ca dadetpunaḥ ।
biṃbaśuddhiṃ ca kṛtvātu mantreṇaivābhiṣicya ca ।।

devadevaṃ samabhyarcya havistatra nivedayet ।
evaṃ vai kṛtapātrāṇi devārthaṃ ca pradāpayet ।।

tasya kāyakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tat kṣaṇādeva naśyati ।
sarvadoṣopaśamanaṃ viṣṇubhaktivivardhanam ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛsuproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre ekānaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha viṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha viṃśo adhyāyaḥ 
rakṣādīpavidhiḥ
ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi rakṣādīpavidhikramam ।
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃvāpi tāmraṃvāpi svaśaktitaḥ ।।

dvātriṃśadaṅgulaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ madhyamaṃ pādahīnataḥ ।
adhamaṃ viṃśadaṅgulyaṃ samavṛttantu kārayet ।।

aṣṭadikṣu ca madhyeca caturdikṣu ca vā tathā ।
kevalaṃ karṇikāṃ vātha karṇikāyāntu vistṛtam ।।

tadardhamunnataṃ vindyādgaṇḍāyāmaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulam ।
dvyaṅgulaṃ tu parīṇāhaṃ tadūrthve bhāgavistṛtam ।।

tadardhaṃ vistṛtotsedhaṃ dīpabātraṃ prakalpya ca ।
alabheśālipiṣṭaṃ vā gomaye vā samāharet ।।

tattatthsāne tu vinyasya pātresaṃyojayettataḥ ।
āḍhakaṃ vā tadardhaṃ vā piṇḍārdhaṃ ca caruṃpacet ।।

hāridracūrṇa saṃyuktaṃ pātre prakṣipya mantravit ।
ājyena srāvya saṃmṛjya muṣṭimātraṃ dṛḍhīkṛtam ।।

daśapiṇḍāṃ stadardhaṃ vā sākṣate ca samāharet ।
jalena kuṃbhamāpūrya sarvagandhasamāyutam ।।

kuśakūrcānvinikṣipyapallavairapi bhūṣayet ।
aṣṭamaṅgalasaṃyuktaṃ pādyācamanasaṃyutam ।।

puṣpagandhasamāyuktaṃ dhūpadīpārghya saṃyutam ।
pṛdhakpātre samāhṛtya devadevaṃ ca pūjayet ।।

śaṅkhadhvanisamāyuktaṃ vaṃśadhvanisamāyutam ।
bherīmṛdaṅgasuṣiravādyaghoṣasamāyutam ।।

stotradhvanisamāyuktaṃ svaktisūktasamanvitam ।
dāsībhiścātha vā bhaktaissvahastopari dhārayet ।।

pradakṣiṇaṃ śanairgatvā devālayamupāvrajet ।
ācāryaṃ pūjayitvātu devadevaṃ praṇamyaca ।।

rakṣādīpaṃ samādāya "śriye jāta' iti bruvan ।
biṃbamūrdhni tu saṃyojyatriḥ pradakṣiṇamācaret ।।

dikpiṇḍaṃ tu visṛjyaiva prokṣayitvā ca mantravit ।
pradakṣiṇaṃ praṇāmaṃ ca kārayedaṣṭamaṅgalaiḥ, ।।

pādyamācamanaṃ datvāgandhapuṣpādibhiryajet ।
mukhavāsaṃ ca datvātu stutimantraiśca vaiṣṇavaiḥ ।।

samālabhyaiva hastābhyāṃ puṣpadūrvāṅkurākṣataiḥ ।
pādepuṣpāñjaliṅkuryātkuryāddevasya mantrataḥ ।।

ālayāttu bahirgatvā pīṭhapārśvetu nikṣipet ।
kautuke baliberepi snāpane pyautsave api ca, ।।

prādurbhāve ca sarveṣāmāvirbhāve tathaiva ca ।
evameva tu kṛtvā tu bhrāmayitvā vicakṣaṇaḥ, ।।

cakravīśāmitādīnāmindrādīnāṃ tathaiva ca ।
darśanaṃ bhrāmaṇaṃ caivamācarecchāstravittamaḥ ।।

mohādajñānataḥ kuryātsarvahānirbhaviṣyati ।
sāyāhne catripūjānte cotsavānte ca nityaśaḥ ।।

evameva vidhānena kārayeduttamaṃ viduḥ ।
sarvaśāntikaraṃ cāpi sarvakaṃpatsamṛddhidam ।।

dāridṣādivināśena sarvān kāmanavāpnuyāt ।
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi śibikānāṃ tu lakṣaṇam ।।

mātrāṅgulena vākuryācchibhikādīnvidhānataḥ ।
āvṛtaṃ tadardhavistāramuttamaṃ tuvidhīyate ।।

tat ṣaḍaṅgulahīnantu madhyamantuprakīrtitam ।
vistārādhyardhapādena ?ayāmadviguṇaṃ bhavet ।।

uttamādhamamadhyānāṃ śibikāvistaro bhavet ।
tribhāgaikasya bhāgaṃ syāccaturbhāgaikabhāgikam ।।

pañcabhāgaikabhāgaṃ syādvistārasya ghanaṃ bhavet ।
taccaturbhāgamevaṃ syādekaikaṃ vamanaṃ bhavet ।।

śeṣabhāgaṃ tu padmoktaṃ talāyukti viśeṣataḥ ।
śibikāvistṛtaṃ caivaṃ bhāgaikaṃ bhāgameva ca ।।

taccaturbhāgamevoktaṃ bhittyutsedhaṃ vidhīyate ।
dvitalaṃ tritalaṃ caiva gulikāphalakābhavet ।।

gulikāpādatalotsedhaṃ madhyordhvatalavatsamam ।
caturbhāgaikamevantu navabhāgaikameva vā ।।

aṅgulaṃ cāṅgulārthaṃ ca ūrthvapaṭṭyā ca saṃyutam ।
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi rathādīnāṃ vidhikramam ।।

pañcaṣaṭsaptatālaṃ vā cāṣṭatālamathāpi vā ।
vistārāyamamevaṃ syādutsedhaṃ dviguṇaṃ bhavet ।।

maṇḍapadvārayuktaṃ vā kūṭākāramathāpi vā ।
adharādharamāyāmaṃ rathāyāmatrayaṃ bhavet ।।

chatrasyāyāmavistārādutsedārdhapramāṇataḥ ।
evaṃ tu parikalpyaiva śibikāyāmamucyate ।।

rathāyāmasamaṃ vāpi pādahīnamathārthakam ।
vistāraṃ tattribhāgai kamāyāmaṃ cocchrayaṃ bhavet ।।

vistārārdhasamutsedhaṃ vistārārthādhikāyatam ।
śayanaṃ saṃprakalpyaiva pūrvoktenaiva dāruṇā ।।

sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ sarvasaindaryasaṃyutam ।
śilpaśāstroktamārgeṇa śilpibhiḥ kālayedbudhaḥ ।।

pañcagavyaissusaṃśodhya vāstuhomaśca hūyatām ।
paryagni caiva kṛtvātu kalaśaissnāpayet tataḥ ।।

maṇḍape vā prapāyāṃ vā sthaṇḍile vātra vinyaset ।
navairvastraissamāveṣṭya puṇyāhamapi vācayet ।।

jaupāsanāgnikuṇḍaṃ ca kārayitvā vidhānataḥ ।
āghāraṃ pūrvavatkṛtvā kuṃbhapūjāṃ samācaret ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca tattaddevāṃśca mūrtibhiḥ ।
vyāhṛtyantaṃ ca hutvā tu antahomaśca hūyate ।।

yānādiṣu ca tanmadhye tattaddevāṃ stathaiva ca ।
āvāhyaiva samabhyarcya devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।।

pādyādyarghyāntamabhyarcya havissamyaṅnivedayet ।
