sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ sarvavādyasamanvitam ।।

yānādiṣu samāropya "pratadviṣṇu'riti bruvan ।
grāmaṃ vā pyālayaṃ vāpi pradakṣiṇamadhācaret ।।

mandiraṃ saṃpraviśyaiva svesvesthāne niveśayet ।
evaṃ yaḥkurute bhaktyā vaiṣṇavaṃ padamāpnuyāt ।।

ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi prapāmaṇḍapalakṣaṇam ।
maṇḍapaṃ trividhaṃ jñeye vimānasamavistṛtam ।।

ardhaṃ pādaṃ tu pādaṃ vā hīnantu trividhaṃ bhavet ।
pramukhe tasyasopānamālayārdhamiti smṛtam ।।

pūrvetu snapanārthāya maṇḍapaṃ saṃprakalpayet ।
ṣoḍaśastaṃbhayuktaṃ vā dvādaśastaṃbhasaṃyutam ।।

aiśānye vā prakurvīta snapanārthaṃ prakalpayet ।
prathamāvaraṇe vātha dvitīyāvaraṇe atha vā ।।

ekādaśena hastena samaṃ samyak prakalpayet ।
navahastaṃ saptahastaṃ pañcahastamiti tridhā ।।

prathamāvaraṇe bāhye maṇḍapantu vidhīyate ।
āsthānavṛttageyādidarśanārthaṃ prakalpayet ।।

pūrvavatpramukhe kuryādyathāvibhavavistaram ।
yajamānasya hastena dvihastantu vivardhayet ।।

pūrvavat staṃbhasaṃyuktaṃ yathāyogyaṃ prakalpayet ।
tatbūrvadiśi śālāyāṃ nṛttārthantu vidhīyate ।।

viṣkaṃbhaṃ navahastaṃ vā āyāmaṃ dviguṇīkṛtam ।
yajamānecchayā tatra dvihastantuvivardhayet ।।

ayādilakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye yajamānānukūlataḥ ।
hastaṃ pādaṃ tadardhaṃ vā vistārāyādisaṃyutam ।।

tathaiva nūnaṃ kṛtvā tu ayādīn lakṣayedbudhaḥ ।
śilābhiriṣṭakābhirvā hastocchrayasamaṃ talam ।।

dvitalaṃ vā prakurvīta tālaṃ samyak prakalpayet ।
śailajaṃ dārusāraṃ vā staṃbhamāhṛtya yatnataḥ ।।

vṛttaṃ vā caturaśraṃ vā ṛjuṃ vakravivarjitam ।
staṃbhānāṃ viṃśatiṃ gṛhya bāhyastaṃbhaṃ pragṛhya ca ।।

tanmadhye dvādaśastaṃbhaṃ pūrvavatkārayedbudhaḥ ।
staṃbhāyāmaṃ yathāyogaṃ kṛtvā tatra vicakṣaṇaḥ ।।

dvitālaghana saṃyuktaṃ staṃbhamānena svastikam ।
stalatyordhve vibhajyaiva samaṃ vandatyaprakalpayet ।।

tasyāmeva tu staṃbhārthaṃ pādaṃ saṃsthāpya svastikam ।
dṛḍhaṃ kṛtvā tadūrdhveta staṃbhaṃ saṃsthāpya vai budhaḥ ।।

dvyaṅgulaṃ ca bhavairvātha vedikāṃ kārayedbudhaḥ ।
nānālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ nānācitrasamanvitam ।।

uttaraṃ tatsamaṃ kṛtvā bodhiketu suyojayet ।
staṃbhādūrdhvantu saṃsthāpya tadūrdhve prastaraṃ nyaset ।।

abhlantarottarādūrdhve abiṣṭakādhānapādayoḥ ।
bālottaraṃ yathāyogyaṃ sthāpayetsudṛḍhaṃ kramāt ।।

tadbilvako yathāmārgaṃ yogyaṃ tatpadmamucchrayam ।
evaṃ lakṣaṇasaṃyuktaṃ darśanīyaṃ ca kārayet ।।

yajamānecchayātattanmaṇḍapena sahaiva tu ।
ṣoḍaśastaṃbhasaṃyuktaṃ dvādaśastaṃbhamevavā ।।

bhaktiyuktaṃ prakalpyaiva prapāṃ yuktyaiva kārayet ।
apare dvārasaṃyuktaṃ pūrvavat staṃbhameva vā ।।

kavāṭaṃ tatra vā kuryāccheṣaṃ yaktyaiva kārayet ।
śilpaśāstroktamārgeṇa śilpibhiḥ kārayedbudhaḥ ।।

maṇḍapasya samāptautu aṅkurānarpayetkramāt ।
śuddhyarthaṃ vāstuhomaṃ ca puṇyāhaṃ caiva kārayet ।।

brāhmaṇān bhojayetpaścāttaddeśamupalakṣayet ।
carodaye ca nakṣatre sthirarāśiṃ pragṛhya ca ।।

maṇḍapasya tu madhye vai dhānyapīṭhāni kalpayet ।
pratiṣṭhoktakrameṇaiva kuṃbhanyāsāti kārayet ।।

paścime gārhapatyāgnāvāghāraṃ juhuyātkramāt ।
hotā hautrakrameṇaiva hautraṃ tatra praśaṃsayet ।।

tattaddevasya cāvāhya juṣṭākāraṃ hutaṃ caret ।
śrīsūktaṃ vaiṣṇapaṃ caiva vaiṣṇavaṃ caikaviṃśatiḥ ।।

indrādilokapālānāṃ pratyekaṃ juhuyātkramāt ।
tattatsthānetu kūrce vā sthaṇḍile vā samarcayet ।।

prabhūtaṃ tu nivedyaiva droṇandroṇārchameva vā ।
ācāryasyārcakādīnāṃ dakṣiṇāṃ ca dadetkramāt ।।

sauvarṇairutpalaiḥ puṣpairalaṅkuryātprapāṃ tataḥ ।
padmairvākumudairvātha puṣpairanyaissvaśaktitaḥ ।।

devadevamalaṅkṛtya vastramālyādibhiḥ punaḥ ।
prapāṃ saṃyojya deveśaṃ dhyānenaiva tu sannayet ।।

deveśaṃ sthāpayettatra pādyādyairarcayetkramāt ।
mahāhaviḥ prabhūtaṃ vā yathāśakti nivedayet ।।

evaṃ yaḥ kurute bhaktyā viṣṇuloke mahīyate

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre viṃśo adhyāyaḥ

anthaikaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

viśeṣārcanam
athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi viṣṇupañcadināni ca ।
śravaṇaṃ dvādaśī śukle kṛṣṇe cārdhe ca dvādaśī ।।

pūrṇimā cāpyamāvāsyā pañcaitāni dināni vai ।
pūrvoktena vidhānena aṅkurānarbayetkramāt ।।

baddhvā pratisaraṃ tatra pūrvarātrautu śāyayet ।
prātassandhyārcanāntetu snāpanoktakrameṇavai ।।

samabhyarcya nivedyaiva pūrvasthāne niveśayet ।
mārgaśīrṣākhyamāse tu pūrvapakṣe viśeṣataḥ ।।

prātassandhyāvasānetu pūrvamāsthānamaṇḍape ।
saṃsthāpya caturo vedān krameṇādhyāpayetsadā ।।

pūjayeddevadeveśaṃ saptaviṃśativigrahaiḥ ।
ekādaśīmupopyaiva mahāpātakanāśinīm ।।

tataḥprabhāte dvādaśyāṃ snātvāsnānavidhānataḥ ।
mṛṇmayāni tu bhāṇḍāni purāṇāni parityajet ।।

mṛṣṭasiktopalepādyaiśśodhayitvā yathārhakam ।
snāpanoktakrameṇaiva snāpayitvā yathāvidhi ।।

āsanādibhirabhyarcya pāyasaṃ ca nivedayet ।
pānīyācamanaṃ datvā mukhavāsaṃ tataḥparam ।।

puruṣasūktena saṃstūya gkāmaṃ caiva pradakṣiṇam ।
dhāmapradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā jīvasthāne niveśayet ।।

saṃvatsarer'cane hīne nityanaimittikādiṣu ।
tatsarvaṃ pūrṇamityāhurdvāśīpūjane kṛte ।।

pauṣe tu pūrṇimāyāṃ vai viṣṇupañcadinoktavat ।
arcayitvātu deveśaṃ gavyaṃ kṣīraṃ nivedayet ।।

so api saṃvatsaraphalaṃ labhate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
māghamāse punarvasvo rāghavo ajāyata svayam, ।।

tattastasyāmapoṣyaiva rāmaṃ vā viṣṇumeva vā ।
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā snāpayitvā nivedayet ।।

tilapadmavidhiṃ vakṣye śruṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।
māghamāse tu pañcamyāṃ pūrvapakṣe viśeṣataḥ ।।

pūrvarātrai tu deveśamarcayitvā yathāvidhi ।
havīṃṣyapi nivedyaiva baddhvā pratisaraṃ punaḥ ।।

pūrvavacchāyayitvaiva rātriśeṣaṃ nayetkramāt ।
prabhāte devamuddhāpya kalaśaissnāpayetpunaḥ ।।

maṇḍapaṃ vātha kūṭaṃ vā prapāṃ vātha yathocitam ।
gomayenopalipyaiva pañcavarṇairalaṅkṛtam ।।

tasmin saṃsthāpya deveśaṃ praṇamyaivānumāsya ca ।
pramukhe dhānyarāśau tu dvihastāyatavistṛte ।।

kṛṣṇājinaṃ samāstīrya navavastressamāstaret ।
tadūrdhvetu vikīryaivaṣaḍdroṇaṃ tilameva hi ।।

droṇatrayaṃ dvaye vāpi maṇḍalākālavattathā ।
aṣṭabhiścadalairyuktaṃ tilapadmaṃ samālikhet ।।

triṇiṣkena tadardhena niṣkamātreṇa vā punaḥ ।
svarṇapadmaṃ ca kṛtvātu tilapadme tu vinyaset ।।

āḍhakaiśśālidhānyaiśca pūrṇapātrāṇi ṣoḍaśa ।
indrādīśānaparyantaṃ śālirāśyupari nyaset ।।

aḍhakaṃ tailamāhṛtya tadardhañca ghṛtaṃ tathā ।
paścime dadhimannyasya devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।।

ātmasūktaṃ ca japtvātu pūjayedaṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।
praṇamya devadevāya padmamadhyetu pūrvavat ।।

prācyādi puruṣādīṃśca caturmūrtibhirāhvayet ।
ekādaśopacāraiśca pūjayitvā yathārhakam ।।

indrādyaiśāntamāvāhya degdevānarcayettata ।
"atodevā'disaṃyuktaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ japetpunaḥ ।।

biṃbe devaṃ samāropya cānyānudvāsayetkramāt ।
yajamāno atha tatkāle dadyādācāryadakṣiṇām ।।

viṣṇubhaktiyutaṃ śāstaṃ dayādyātmaguṇairyutam ।
vedapārāyaṇaparaṃ sarvāvayavasaṃyutam ।।

vipramāhūya tatkāle devasya niyato agrataḥ ।
dhyātvā deveśamācāryo devadevasya sannidhau ।।

tilapadmaṃ dadettasmai sarvalokahitāya vai ।
stotrairgeyaiśca vādaiśca stutvā devaṃ samarcayet ।।

devaṃ yāne samāropya sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam ।
devālayaṃ parītyaiva jīvasthāne niveśayet ।।

eve yaḥkurute bhaktyā viṣṇave paramātmane ।
sarvān kāmānavāpnoti vaiṣṇavaṃ lokamaśnute ।।

phālgune māsi phalgunyāṃ śriyā sārthaṃ janārdanam ।
snāpayitvotsavaṃ kṛtvā samabhyarchya nivedayet ।।

caitremāsi tathā caitṣāṃ kuryāddamanakotsavam ।
pūrvasminneva divase rātripūjāvasānake ।।

bhaddhvā pratisaraṃ tatra deveśāya nivedayet ।
vasastaṃ kāmamabhyarcya pāyasānnaṃ nivedayet ।।

desasya dakṣiṇe pārśve mālāṃ damanakīṃnyaset ।
prabhāte devamuddhāpya snāpayitvār'cayettathā ।।

devasya puṣpamantrābhyāṃ dadyādbhakti samanvitam ।
sarveṣāṃ parivārāṇāṃ dadyāttanmantramūrtibhiḥ ।।

grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā saṃsthāpyāsthānamaṇḍape ।
samabhyarcya nivedyaiva mukhavāsaṃ dadettataḥ ।।

vaiśākhyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ vai snāpayitvā samarcayet ।
jyeṣṭhe tu snāpayeddevaṃ navavastraṃ pradāpayet ।।

so api saṃvatsaraphalaṃ prāpnuyādeva mānavaḥ ।
arghyadānaṃ praśastaṃ syāddevasyāṣāḍhamāsake ।।

śrāvaṇe māsi sakṣatre śravaṇe tu viśeṣataḥ ।
utsavasnapanādīni pūrvavatkārayedbudhaḥ ।।

ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi jayantyutsavalakṣaṇam ।
jayantī śrāvaṇe māsi kṛṣṇapakṣe aṣṭamī śubhā ।।

rohiṇīsahitā jñeyā sarvapāpaharā tithiḥ ।
tasyāṃ jāto jacagannātho jagatpālana kāṅkṣayā ।।

candrasyodayakāletu madhyarātre svalīlayā ।
tasmin vai divase kṛṣṇamarcayitvā prayatnataḥ ।।

utsavaṃ kārayedyastu viṣṇossālokyatāṃ vrajet ।
aṣṭamī rohiṇīyuktā rahitāvā vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

aviddhaiva sadā grāhyāsaptamyā sarvadā tidhiḥ ।
ādityodayavelāyāṃ kalāmātrāṣṭamī yadi ।।

sātithissakalā jñeyā niśīthavyāpinī bhavet ।
nāgaviddhā yathā nandā varjitā śravaṇānvitā ।।

tathāṣṭamīṃ pūrvaviddhāṃ sarkṣāṃ vāpi parityajet ।
aviddhaivāṣṭamī grāhyā tāṃ supuṇyāmupāvaset ।।

rohiṇīsahitā kṛṣṇā māsi bhādrapade aṣṭamī ।
ardharātrādadhaścordhvaṃ galayā vāpi pūrvavat ।।

jayantī nāma sā proktā sarvapāpapraṇāśinī ।
tasmāttu divasātpūrvaṃ navame vātha saptame ।।

pañcame vā tṣahe avāpi vidhivā cāṅkurārpaṇam ।
pūrvedyureva śarvaryāṃ rātripūjāvasānake ।।

baddhvā pratisaraṃ tatra śayane śāyayeddharim ।
tasyāṃ tithāvardharātre kṛṣṇamevaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

puṣpāñjaliṃ tataḥ kuryācchriyā yukto janārdanaḥ ।
bhūmibhārāpahārāya lokejāto jagatpatiḥ ।।

iti saṃcintayeddevaṃ vaiṣmavaṃ mantramuccaran ।
sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ maṇḍapaṃ ca pradakṣiṇam ।।

purastānmadhyame vāpi cāsthāne vāpyalaṅkṛte ।
tanmadhye viṣṭare sthāpya devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।।

tailaṃ haridracūrṇaṃ ca kalaśān saṃprapūrya ca ।
sthaṇḍile vinyasettatra devadevaṃ samarcayet ।।

tailenābhyañjanaṃ kṛtvā cūrṇenodyartanaṃ caret ।
nādeyaṃ gandhatoyaṃ ca puṣpodaṃ cākṣatodakam ।।

kuśodakaṃ tu saṃbhṛtya kalaśān pañca vinyaset ।
"ato devā'dibhirmantraissnāpayetpuruṣottamam ।।

pādyādyarṅyāntamabhyarcya devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।
"hiraṇyagarbha' ityuktvāgavāṃ kṣīraṃ nivedayet ।।

mukhavāsaṃ ca datvaiva praṇāmaṃ ca tataścaret ।
niveditaṃ tu tat kṣīraṃ vandhyāputrapradaṃ bhavet ।।

pītvāprasūte putraṃ ca āyuṣmantaṃ balānvitam ।
nītvā ghṛtaṃ ca tailaṃ ca mukhavāsayutaṃ tathā ।।

devasya darśayitvā tu brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pradīyatām ।
devadevamalaṅkṛtya bhaktānāmāttacetasām ।।

yathā vai yajamānasya tathā priyakaraṃ bhudhaiḥ ।
sarvavādyasamāyuktaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam ।।

grāmaṃ vāpyālayaṃ vāpi pradakṣiṇamathācaret ।
ālayaṃ saṃpraviśyaiva kalaśaissnāvayedbudhaḥ ।।

ācāryadakṣiṇāṃ datvā sodakaṃ devasannidhau ।
prabhūtaṃ tu nivedyaiva mukhavāsaṃ dadetpunaḥ, ।।

evamevaṃ tathā kuryādutsavaṃ prativatsaram ।
bhuktimuktipradamidamṛṣibhiḥ parīkīrtitam ।।

apare atha dine vāpi kārayedutsavaṃ bhudhaḥ ।
yadyanmantrakriyālopo vaiṣṇavair hūyate tathā ।।

ekasmin vatsare hīne devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।
snapanaṃ pañcaviṃśadbhiḥ kalaśaiśśuddhamānasaiḥ ।।

śāntihomaṃ ca hutvātu puṇyāhamapi vācayet ।
utsavaṃ dviguṇaṃ kuryāddakṣiṇāṃ ca svaśaktitaḥ ।।

śrāvaṇe dvādaśīyoge māpi bhādrapade tathā ।
saṃvatsarārcādoṣasya śāntyarthaṃ keśavasya tu ।।

asmin māse viśeṣeṇa pavitrāropaṇaṃ hareḥ ।
sarvadoṣopaśamanaṃ sarvakāmābhivṛddhidam, ।।

māse asmīnnārabhetaiva śravaṇavratamuttamam ।
tribhirvarṣaistribhirmāsairupoṣya ca mahatpalam ।।

āśvayujamāse cāśvyarkṣe deveśaṃ snāpayettataḥ ।
arghyadānaṃ praśastaṃ syāddevadevasya śārjiṇaḥ ।।

athātaḥ kṛttikādīpadānalakṣaṇamucyate ।
kārtikyāṃ pūrṇimāyāntu yadṛkṣantu pravartate ।।

tadṛkṣaṃ dīpaṛkṣaṃ syātkālāpekṣā na vidyate ravyastamayavelāyāṃ ।
dīpāropaṇamācaret ।।

devasya sannidhau staṃbhe devālayasamocchraye ।
adhike vā mahādīpaṃ mahāsnehaṃ prakalpayet ।।

tripādaṃ vā tadhardhaṃ vā dīpadaṇḍaṃ samāharet ।
veṇuṃ vā kramukaṃ vāpi tālaṃ vā nālikerakam ।।

madhūkaṃ tintriṇīkaṃ cetyanyaissāradrumaistathā ।
śatāṣṭadīpasaṃyuktaṃmuttamottamamucyate ।।

utme madhyamaṃ dīpaṃ ।
śatasaṃkhyākramaṃ viduḥ ।
uttamādhamadīpaṃ syānnavatirdvyadhikā tathā ।।

madhyamottamamuktaṃ syādaśītiścaturastathā ।
madhyame madhyamaṃ caiva ṣaṭsaptatirathocyate ।।

madhyamādhamadīpantu aṣṭaṣaṣṭiriti smṛtam ।
adhamottamadīpantu ṣaṣṭisaṃkhyāṃ vadantihi ।।

dvipañcāśatpradīpāṃśca kuryādadhamamadhyame ।
adhamādhamamevedaṃ catvāriṃśatpradīpakam ।।

aśaktānāṃ yathāśakti dīpaṃ tatraiva yojayet ।
daṇḍetu suṣire yojyaṃ caturdikṣu krameṇa vai ।।

bhūtapīṭhasya pūrvetu dīpasthānaṃ vidhīyate ।
"padmakośapratīkāśa' iti śrutyāmudāhṛtam ।।

tasmātsarvaprayatnena padmaṃ kuryātsalakṣaṇam ।
vistārāyāmatulyaṃ syāccatustālapramāṇataḥ ।।

golakāṅgulamutsedhaṃ caturaśraṃ prakalpayet ।
tatraiva śālibhi stiryakpadmamaṣṭadalānvitam ।।

tanmadhye tālamātreṇa samavṛttaṃ sakarṇikam ।
ekāṅgulasamutsedhaṃ tatraivopari taṇḍulaiḥ ।।

sati padmaṃ samutphullaṃ navavastraṃ samāstaret ।
puṣpaṃ tasyopari nyasya kalbayetpadmamaṇḍalam ।।

daleṣvabhyarcya ca vasūn madhye dharmaṃ samarcayet ।
ālayābhimukhe kuryātprapāṃ caivātisundaram ।।

āsthānamaṇḍape vāpi kalpayetpadmamaṇḍalam ।
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ mṛṇmayaṃ vāsvaśaktitaḥ ।।

śarāvaṃ prasthasaṃpūrṇaṃ samāhṛtya vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
kiñcitkarpūrasaṃyuktaṃ picuvartisamanvitam ।।

gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ samādāya sthāpayetpadmamadhyame ।
ācāryassuprasannātmā navavastrottarīyakaḥ ।।

"śriyaijā'teti mantreṇa dīpasyoddīpanaṃ caret ।
pratīcyāṃ padmamadhyetu śriyaṃ dhyātvā samāhvayet ।।

ekādaśopacāraiśca pūjayitvā samāhitaḥ ।
śrīdevīṃ manasā dhyātvā śrīsūktaṃ ca samuccaran ।।

dīpamādāya hastābhyāmapsarobhirviśeṣataḥ ।
dīpānanyāntsamādāya to yadhārāsamanvitam ।।

geyadhvanisamāyuktaṃ nṛttavādyasamanvitam ।
pradakṣiṇaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā garbhāgāraṃ praveśayet ।।

depasya dakṣiṇe pārśvesthāpayenmantravittamaḥ ।
devadevaṃ samānīya maṇḍale sthāpya cātvaraḥ ।।

kuryāddaśopacārāṃśca samabhyarcyedvidhānataḥ ।
"śrīye jā'teti mantreṇa dīpānuddīpayedbudhaḥ ।।

garbhageheca sopāne prāsāde mukhamaṇḍape ।
prāsādaśikhare vāpigrīvāyāṃ caraṇe api ca ।।

prākāreṣu ca sarvatra tathaiva snapanālaye ।
puṣpasaṃcayadeśe ca dvāre cāsthānamaṇḍape ।।

anyeṣvapi ca sarvatra dīpānuddīpayetkramāt ।
kārpāsatūlaṃ saṃbaddhya śarāveṣughṛtena vai ।।

pūrvoktenaiva mantreṇa coddīpanamathācaret ।
nṛttageyādivādyaiśca ghoṣayitvā prayatnataḥ ।।

taccharāvasthadīpaṃ ca balipīṭhasya paścime ।
adhidevaṃ samārādhya nikṣipeddīpamaṇḍape ।।

"śubhrājyoti'riti procya daṇḍrāgre anyāṃśca nikṣipet ।
nivedya bahūdhā devaṃ pṛthukādīnviśeṣataḥ ।।

bhakṣyāṇi guḍamiśrāṇiprabhūtaṃ ca mahāhaviḥ ।
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam ।।

punardevaṃ samādāya jīvasthāne niveśayet ।
so api saṃvatsaraphalaṃ prāpya gacchetparaṃ padam ।।

grahaṇārādhanam
athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi sūryasomoparāgayoḥ ।
arcanādividhiṃ samyak devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ।।

sūryagrahe caturyāmaṃ triyāmaṃ tu vidhugrahe ।
nāśnanti havyakavyāni devatāḥ pitarastathā ।।

ālaye tu hareḥ pūjāṃ na tyajanti maharṣayaḥ ।
havirnivedanaṃ hitvāpūjāṃ sarvāṃ samācaret ।।

grahaṇe vartamānetu snāpayetpuruṣottamam ।
koṭiyajñaphalaṃ prāpya brahmaloke mahīyate ।।

grastāstagrahaṇe kuryātsnapanaṃ tu pare ahani ।
tathā grastodaye kuryāditi śātātapo abravīt ।।

sarvadhā varamāne tu grahaṇesnapanaṃ caret ।
grahaṇaṃ saṃkramo hasticchāyā ca viṣuvādikam ।।

yugādi va mādyāstu puṇyakālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।
niṣethaḥ kathitaḥ prājñairhavirdāsavadutsave ।।

nityārcanaṃ cotsavaṃ ca snapanātpūrvamācaret ।
snāpayitvā hṛṣīkeśaṃ havirdānaṃ praśasyate ।।

vāstuśuddhiṃ sadā kuryādgrahaṇe candrasūryayoḥ ।
purāṇāni ca bhāṇḍāni tyaktvānyāni samāharet ।।

kuśāgrāṇāṃ samutkṣepādvāsasāṃ śuddhiriṣyate ।
apakvānāṃ ca vastūnāṃ na pakvaṃ parigṛhṇate ।।

adṛśyamuparāgantu noparāgaṃ pracakṣate ।
dīkṣitasya tathānyasya snānaṃ syātsparśamokṣayoḥ ।।

yāvānādyantakālassyāttāvatākīrtayeddharim ।
maunī japādikaṃ kuryādūrdhvapuṇḍradharaśśuciḥ ।।

saptavātāhataṃ vastramārdraṃ dhṛtvā na doṣabhāk ।
grahaṇe bhagavatsevā sarvāśubhavināśinī ।।

dadyāddhānāni śaktyā vai sakāmo harimandire ।
tadanantaṃ bhavetsākṣī yatrānanto harissvayam ।।

prabhūtaṃ tu nivedyātha bhuñjīyāttadanantaram ।
rātrau śrāddhaṃ prakurvīta grahaṇe tannadoṣakṛt ।।

dūṣite tūktakāle tu tasyāpagama eva ca ।
viparīte mahān doṣa iti śāstravido viduḥ ।।

na niśīthātparaṃ śrāddhamāpatsvapi vidhīyate ।
snānamāśaucināṃ nityaṃ te api dānaṃ ca kurva ।।

na japo na tapasteṣāmaśuddhā mokṣaṇe punaḥ ।
yadā rāśyantaraṃ rāśeḥ kāle saṃkramate raviḥ ।।

tadā tu puṇyakālassyātsnapanādyatra kārayet ।
kaṭakeviṃśatiḥ pūrvaṃ makare viṃśatiḥ pare ।।

puṇyāntu ghaṭikāḥ proktā statra grahaṇavaccaret ।
yadāstamayavelāyāṃ saṃdhyāyāṃ saṃkramoraveḥ ।।

pūrve ahṇi puṇyakālassyādaparāhṇātparassmṛtaḥ ।
ardhāstamita āditye tathā cār'dhodite sati ।।

pāścātyapūrvaghaṭīkāstisrassaṃdhyā prakīrtitāḥ ।
uparāge api kuryādvai utsave avabhṛthaṃ hareḥ ।।

vidhugrahe niśāṃ sarvāmahorātraṃ ravigrahe ।
tyajecchubhe tadā kuryānnaiva dīpotsavaṃ hareḥ ।।

paścānniśīthādgrahaṇe dīpaṃ dāsyanti ke ca na ।
aviddheparvaṇi proktaṃ dīpadānaṃ śubhāvaham ।।

grahaṇe api bhaveddīpamaviddhā pūrṇimā na cet ।
aparvaṇyarpitaṃ dīpaṃ hanti puṇyaṃ purātanam ।।

māsarkṣeṣvanyapuṇvarkṣe viṣṇupañcadine tathā ।
arcanārthāya devasya kālo madhyāhna ucyate ।।

kāmye tu sumuhūrte syātpūjanaṃ nānyadhā caret iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre ekaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha dvāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha dvāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ snapanam

athātassnapanāgāraṃ pramukhe cottare tathā ।
aiśānyāṃ vā viśeṣaṇa prapāṃ vā maṇḍapantu vā ।।

vitānopari saṃvītaṃ laṃbamānaṃ pariṣkṛtam ।
staṃbhāntsaṃveṣṭya vastraiśca dukūlaistāntavairapi ।।

muktādāmasamāyuktaṃ pūrṇakuṃbhasamanvitam ।
satvaṃ rajastamaścaiva aiśvaryaṃ cādhidaivatam ।।

caturvedādikairmantraistoraṇāṃsthsāpayetkramāt ।
ubhayoḥ pārśvayoścaiva kadalīkramukānvitam ।।

pūrvāstamuttarāntaṃ ca ṣaṭsūtraṃ saṃprasārya ca ।
kalpayedāyatasamaṃ padānāṃ pañca viṃśatim ।।

madhyebrāhmaṃ padaṃ hitvā caryārdhaṃ parito aṣṭa ca ।
pūrvādi catvāri padaṃ dvārārthaṃ parikalpayet ।।

śiṣṭāṃśca dvādaśapadān dravyanyāsārthamāharet ।
madhyeśvabhrantu kartavyamaupāsanavidhānataḥ ।।

madhyenimnaṃ ca kṛtvā tu tālamātrapramāṇataḥ ।
śvabhrasya madhyame caiva bilvajaṃ phalakaṃ nyaset ।।

tatpramāṇādhikaṃ pīṭhaṃ paritaścaturaṅgulam ।
madhyehitvā pratiṣṭhāpya dvivedisahitaṃ kramāt ।।

tataḥpāvanamārgeṇa jalaṃ gacchedudaṅmukham ।
maṇḍapāttu bahisthsāne jalasthānaṃ tu khānayet ।।

ācchādya kadalīpatraiḥ padmapatrairathāpi vā ।
hāridraiścātha patrairvāpatraiḥ kramukajaistu vā ।।

"atodevā'dimantreṇa kuśadarbhāṃntu śodhayet ।
yāvacchvabhrapramāṇantu tāvatkṛtvāsamāharet ।।

hastamātraṃ tathāyāme prokṣaṇārthaṃ tu kūrcakam ।
mārjanārthantu kūrcaṃ ca ṣaḍaṅgulamiti smṛtam ।।

pañcabhirvātribhirvātha dvādaśāṃgulamāyatam ।
kalaśārthaṃ tu kurvīta yathākalaśasaṃkhyayo ।।

taṇḍulairvrīhibhiścaiva satilaiścatrivedikam ।
vrīhyardhaṃ taṇḍulaṃ proktaṃ tadardhaṃ ca tilānapi ।।

uttamaṃ droṇamityuktaṃ madhyamaṃ tu tadardhakam ।
adhamaṃ cāḍhakaṃ caiva paṅktiṃ kuryādvicakṣaṇaḥ, ।।

samyak dagdhvātu kalaśānabhinnāntsaṃpragṛhya ca ।
śarāvāṇāṃ pramāṇaṃ tu kuḍubaṃ samudāhṛtam ।।

ṣaṭprasthamātraṃ karakaṃ kuṃbhaṃ tu droṇameva ca ।
"devasya'tveti kalaśān kuṃbhādīntsaṃpragṛhya ca ।।

yavāntaraṃ tu tantūnāṃ saṃveṣṭya kalaśānapi ।
pūrvarātrau viśeṣeṇa deveśaṃ saṃpraṇamya ca ।।

samabhyarcya nivedyaiva mukhavāsaṃ dadettataḥ ।
pūrvoktena vidhānena baddhvāpratisaraṃ tataḥ ।।

śayanaṃ sopadhānaṃ ca kālayitvātu pūrvavat ।
śayane śāyayeddevamuttarācchādanaṃ caret ।।

nṛttairgeyaiśca vādyaiśca rātriśeṣaṃ nayetkramāt ।
tataḥ prabhāte dharmātmā yajamānayuto guruḥ ।।

śvabhramadhye pratiṣṭhāpya kūrcāntsamyaṅnyasetkramāt ।
jayādīrapi tatraiva caindrādyaiśāntamarcayet ।।

paṅktīśamarcayetpūrvaṃ nīlavāruṇamadhyame ।
viṣvakcenaṃ samabhyarcya someśānāntarepi ca ।।

lokapālāntsamabhyarcye dvigrahairdaśabhistribhiḥ prāgdravyāṇi ।
nadītire mṛdaṃ gṛhya sasyaṅe tretaṭākake ।।

darbhamūle ca saṃgṛhya gajadante tathaivaca ।
gośruṅge karkaṭāvāse valmīkasya tu madhyame ।।

mahīṃ devīmanujñāpya tāścāhṛtya pṛthak pṛthak ।
ātapenātha saṃśoṣya viśvāmitrān parihraset ।।

śarāveṣu mṛdaṃ caiva pūrayityā pṛthak pṛthak ।
indrādīśānaparyantaṃ pradakṣiṇavaśena tu ।।

"udutya'miti mantreṇa prathamaṃ sannyasenmṛdaḥ ।
mṛdupasnānamekaṃ tu aiśānyāṃ vipyasettadā ।।

aśvadthena palāśena bilvena khadireṇa vā ।
kuryādaṣṭāṃgulotsedhaṃ caturaśraṃ samastataḥ ।।

mūlaṃ ṣaḍaṅgule cāgrāttṣaṅgulaṃ samudāhṛtam ।
anena vā mṛdā vāpi kuryādvai parvatān kramāt ।।

himavānūrjavānvindhyo vidūro vedaparvataḥ ।
mahendraśca puraścandraśśataśruṅgāśca parvatāḥ ।।

eṣāṃ varṇastathaivoktaḥ kuryādvarṇena saṃyutān ।
śvetaṃ pītaṃ ca kṛṣṇaṃ ca raktaṃ vai śvetameva ca ।।

pītaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ ca raktaṃ ca kramādvarṇa udāhṛtaḥ ।
prāgādīśānta metāṃśca "idaṃ viṣṇu'riti nyaset ।।

śailānāṃ cāpyupasnāmekamīśānyagocaram ।
śālivrīhiyavā mudgatilamāṣa priyaṅgavaḥ ।।

godhūmaścaṇakastilvomasūraścādthasī tathā ।
kuluddhamāṣakāścaiva ṣaṣṭirniṣpāva eva ca ।।

etānyāhṛtya dhānyāni śarāveṣu pṛthak pṛthak ।
prakṣipya tāṃśya saṃpūrṇān kramāddvau dvaunyakettathā ।।

indrādīśānaparyantaṃ "śukranta' iti mantrataḥ ।
nyasedekamupasnānaṃ dhānyānāmagnidiśyapi ।।

śarāvāṇāmalābhe tu kalaśeṣu pṛthak pṛthak ।
"soma oṣadhīnā'mucchārya pūrvavaccāṃkurānapi ।।

yamanīlāntare cāpi śarāvetu suvinyaset ।
aṅkurāṇāmupasnānamekamatraiva vinyaset ।।

parvatārthaṃ samaṃ proktavṛkṣairyatnena vā mṛdā ।
maṅgalāni prakuryācca dārupakṣāṇyanukramāt ।।

śrīvatsaṃ pūrṇakuṃbhaṃ ca bherīmādarśanaṃ tathā ।
matsyayugmāṃkuśaṃ śaṅkhamāvartamiti cāṣṭavai ।।

śrīvatsaṃ tattu rukmābhaṃ ghaṭoraktābha ucyate ।
raktāṃ bherīṃ suvarṇābhaṃ tasya pārśve asitaṃ?tathā ।।

ādarśanaṃ ca śvetaṃ syādvṛttaṃ candravadiṣyate ।
matsyayugmaṃ tathā śvetamūrdhvānanamitīritam ।।

aṅkuśasya tu daṇḍaṃ ca raktaṃ kṛṣṇaghṛṇīyutam ।
śaṅkhaṃ śaṅkhanibhaṃ proktaṃ raktamāvartamiṣyate ।।

saptāṅgulasamutsedhameṣāṃ pīṭhaṃ dvigolakam ।
yathā vṛkṣaistathā kuryātpañcavarṇairmṛdā tadhā ।।

evaṃ lakṣaṇamuddiṣṭaṃ śeṣaṃ yuktyā samācaret ।
pradakṣiṇakrameṇaiva caindrādīśāntamarcayet ।।

dikṣvaṣṭasu mahādikṣu tattaddvārasya dakṣiṇe ।
"śaṃ sā niyaccha'tvityuktvāmaṅgalānyatra vinyaset ।।

maṅgalānāmupasnānamendrādyecaikamevahi ।
evaṃ prakaraṇaṃ proktaṃ kalaśānāṃ ।।

dvādaśa pradhānadravyāṇi
pañcagavyakramaṃ vakṣye devasya snapanaṃ prati ।
kapilāyā varaṃ kṣīraṃ śvetāyā dadhi cocyate ।।

raktavarṇāghṛtaṃ grāhyaṃ kṛṣṇāyā gośśakṛdbhavet ।
mūtraṃ tu nīlavarṇāyāḥ pañcagavyamiti smṛtam ।।

prasthapādaṃ ghṛtaṃ caiva dviguṇaṃ dadhi saṃyutam ।
gṛhītvā triguṇaṃ kṣīraṃ gomayantu caturguṇam ।।

ṣaḍguṇaṃ caiva gomūtraṃ pañcagavyayutaṃ kramāt ।
apātitaṃ tu gomūtraṃ patitaṃ gomayaṃ bhavet ।।

dhāroṣṇaṃ kṣīramādāya sadyastsaptaṃ ghṛtaṃ bhavet ।
aśuktaṃ dadhi gṛhṇīyādetatsarvatra lakṣaṇam ।।

"gāṅgeyaṃ' mantramuccārya gomūtraṃ pūrvamāharet ।
tatparaṃ tu śakṛdgrāhya "mīśāna'miti mantrataḥ ।।

"hiraṇyapāṇi'mityuktvā paya ādāya nikṣipet ।
"iṣe tve'ti dadhi yañjyādghṛtaṃ "cāyanta' ityapi ।।

ityevaṃ pañcabhirmantraiḥ pañcagavyaṃ samāharet ।
etadāḍhakapūrmantu kalaśedṛśyate pṛthak ।।

sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ kāṃsyaṃ mṛṇmayameva vā ।
dvādaśāṃgulavistāraṃ ṣoḍaśāṃgulanāhakam ।।

dvyaṅgulaṃ saṃbharetkaṇṭhaṃ mukhaṃ pañcāṅgula bhavet ।
pakvabiṃba phalākāraṃ khaṇḍasbhuṭītavarjitam ।।

evaṃ kalaśamādāya pañcagavyaiḥprapūrya ca ।
"rudramasya'miti procya nyasedīśānagocare ।।

āḍhakārdhaghṛtenaiva saṃpūrṇaṃ kalaśaṃ tathā ।
"ghṛtapratīka' ityuktvā i dreśānāntarenyaset ।।

kalaśaṃ madhusaṃyuktaṃ sukuśaiḥ pūritaṃ tathā ।
"madhu vā'teti mantreṇa indrāgnyorantare nyaset ।।

na śuktaṃ dadhi gavyaṃ ca? saṃpūrṇakalaśaṃ tathā ।
"dadhi krāv ṇna' ityukvā āgneyyāṃ dadhi vinyaset ।।

sadyo dugdhaṃ payogrāhya makṣataiḥ pūritantathā ।
"aṇoraṇīyā' nityuktvā yamāgnyormadhyame nyaset ।।

uśīrāgaruparṇairvā saṃyuktaṃ candanena vā ।
śuddhokena saṃgṛhya kalaśaṃ paripūritam ।।

yamanīlāntare tatra "apsara'ssviti vinyaset ।
vrīhimāṣayavairyuktaṃ sarṣapañcākṣataṃ viduḥ ।।

tūryaghoṣasamāyuktaṃ miśritaṃ cākṣatodakam ।
tatrākṣatodakenaiva saṃpūrṇaṃ kalaśaṃ tataḥ ।।

"imā oṣadhaya' ityuktvā nyasennī le akṣatodakam ।
kadalīmātuluṅgāmra panasernālikerakaiḥ ।।

ārdrādibhiḥ phalaiścānyairyathālābhaṃ samāhṛtaiḥ ।
phalair ardhāṃśasaṃyuktaṃ śeṣaṃ toyena pūritam ।।

phalodakamiti proktaṃ kalaśaṃ saṃprasāthitam ।
nīlavāruṇayormadhye "somaṃ rā'jeti vinyaset, ।।

kuśāgrairatha vā dūrvairakṣataiśca samanvitam ।
kuśodakamiti proktaṃ kalaśaṃ tena pūritam ।।

varuṇodānayormadhye "yatassva'miti vinyaset ।
vajraṃ nīlaṃ pravālaṃ ca śaṅkhajaṃ śuktijaṃ tathā ।।

etāni pañcaratnāni tato maratakaṃ tathā ।
vaiḍūryaṃ puṣyarāgaṃ ca gomedhikamiti kramāt ।।

ratnodakamiti proktaṃ kalaśaṃ tena pūritam ।
vāyavye sannyasedvidvā"nato devādi'muccaran ।।

yathālābhaṃ tathā ratnasuvarṇasahitaṃ kramāt ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣasūktayutaṃ japet ।।

tathābhimantritaṃ toyaṃ japyodakamiti smṛtam ।
kuberodānayormadhye "brahmā devānā'miti nyaset ।।

phalānte tu vitunnāssyuroṣadhyassamudāhṛtāḥ ।
sarvauṣadhisamāyuktaṃ sarvauṣadhyudakaṃ bhavet ।।

taryāṃśeṣu gṛhītaṃ ca kalaśaṃ pūrṇamaṃbhasā ।
someśānāstarecaiva "citraṃ devānā'miti nyaset ।।

eṣāṃ pratyekamekaṃ tu kalaśaṃ śuddhavāriṇā ।
gṛhītvā tadupasnānaṃ vāmapārśvetu vinyaset ।।

upasnāne tu kalaśā"nato devā'dinā nyaset ।
evaṃ pradhānakalaśāścaturviṃśatirīritāḥ ।।

anudravyāṇi
nandyāvartaṃ ca padmaṃ ca tulasī viṣṇuparṇikā ।
bilvaṃ ca karavīraṃ ca padmaṃ kumudameva ca ।।

aṣṭavai puṇyapuṣpāṇi grāhyāṇi tu yathākramam ।
divāśuddhaṃ tu bilvaṃ ca kapidthaṃ bilvavanniśi ।।

karavīraṃ divā śuddhaṃ niśi sitaṃ? tathā śuci ।
śarāveṣu samāhṛtya puṣpāṇi tu pṛthak pṛthak ।।

"imāssumanasa' iti mantreṇa yamanīlāntare nyaset ।
tasyopasnānamekantu tatpārśve kalaśaṃ nyaset ।।

śrīveṣṭakaṃ yavaṃ mudgamuśīraṃ caiva ratnakam ।
tathā masūraṃ damanaṃ jātīphalayutaṃ tathā ।।

lavaṅgaṃ ca samāhṛtya cūrṇayitvākrameṇa vai ।
samārādhyaiva taccūrṇaṃ śarāveṣu ca pūrayet ।।

paṅktīśāddakṣiṇe cūrṇaṃ "vandyo na'iti vinyaset ।
eṣāmalābhe cūrṇānāṃ grāhyamailādicūrṇakam ।।

upasnānaṃ tu tatpārśve tvekaṃ vai kalaśaṃ nyaset ।
aśvadthasya madhūkasya khadirasya vaṭasya ca ।।

vañjulāsanayoścāpi citravṛkṣasya ca tvacaḥ ।
hṛtvolūkhalamadhye ca "udutya'miti vinyaset ।।

ukta carmaṇyalābhe tu aśvadthasya vidhīyate ।
kaṣāyaṃ parikalpyaiva "ye te śata'miti bruvan ।।

varuṇodānayormadhye kaṣāyakalaśaṃ nyaset ।
upasnānaṃ tu tatpārśve ekaṃ vai kalaśaṃ nyaset ।।

siṃhī ca nakulavyāghranandādityaṃ ca puṣkaram ।
dūrvā ca sahadevī ca pāṭhā sāhvayameva ca ।।

evaṃ vanauṣadhīrgṛhya somavāyvontu madhyame ।
upasnānaṃ tu tatpārśve ekaṃ vai kalaśaṃ nyaset ।।

nadītaṭākakūpānāṃ palvalasya ca vāribhiḥ ।
pṛthaksaṃpūrya kalaśāṃścaturastu samāharet ।।

tasyaikaṃ kalaśaṃ pārśve upasnānaṃ tu vinyaset ।
hareṇukaṃ ca sthauṇeyaṃ patraṃ vyāghranakhaṃ tathā ।।

parṇāgaruṃ ca dyāmākaṃ kacoraṃ ceruvālakam ।
māñcī jātiphalailāṃśca lavaṅgaṃ candanaṃ tathā ।।

karpūraṃ ca balośīrasthiranāradameva ca? ।
kastuṃburuṃ tathānyāni sugandhīni śucīni ca ।।

prāṇyaṅgaṃ ca purīṣaṃ ca varjayitvā samāharet ।
eteṣāmapi yaccūrṇaṃ sūkṣmamutpīḍya kalpitam ।।

sarvagandhamiti proktaṃ śarāveṣu prapūrayet ।
nyase"ttrātāra'mityeva yakṣarājeśamadhyame ।।

tattatpārśvenyasetteṣāmupasnānaṃ tathaiva ca ।
navasya snigdhavarṇasya hāridrasya prakalpayet, ।।

cūrṇaṃ tu kalaśe kṣiptvā saṃpūrṇaṃ kalaśaṃ caret ।
paṅktīśasyaiva pārśvetu "sinī vā'līti vinyaset ।।

tasya pārśve nyasedekamupasnānantu pūrvavat ।
pālāśadūrvāpāmārganandyāvartadalāni ca ।।

karavīrasya patrāṇi kuśapatrāṇi caiva hi ।
mūlagandhārthamāhṛtya tasya pārśve nyasedbudhaḥ ।।

śuddhodakalaśaṃ sthāpyedupasnānaṃ ca pūrvavat ।
vastrayugmaṃ navaṃ sūkṣmaṃ kṛtaṃ kārpāsatantunā ।।

plotārthantu samāhṛtya śuddhapātre tu nikṣipet ।
viṣṇugāyatriyā sthāpya yakṣarājeśamadhyame ।।

plotapārśvenyasettāni "brahmajajñāna'mityapi ।
jātiṃ hiṅgulikaṃ caiva añjanaṃ ca manaśśilām ।।

gorocanaṃ ca girikamiti dhātūntsamāharet ।
etāni cūrṇayitvātu śarāveṣu pṛthak pṛthak ।।

prakṣipya "jātave'deti nyasettatraiva pūrvavat ।
ekādaśānukaraṇe kalaśāṃścaiva pūrayet ।।

ahataṃ ca sumākṣmaṃ ca vastrayugmamakhaṇḍitam ।
vastraṃ yajñopavītaṃ ca pavitraṃ bhūṣaṇādikam ।।

evamādīni saṃgṛhya someśānāntare nyaset ।
vinyasya kalaśāṃścaiva tathā cūrṇān pṛthak pṛthak ।।

vastrairāveṣṭya tāntsarvān punaḥkūrcāni nikṣipet ।
utkūrcaṃ vāpyadhaḥkūrcaṃ prāgagraṃ vodagagrakam ।।

vinyasya teṣu kūrcāni śarāve rapidhāya ca ।
praṇamya devadeveśaṃ dravyārcasamathārabhet ।।

tataścaryāpadānteṣu jayādyapsarasor'cayet ।
jayāṃ ca vijayāṃ vindāṃnandakāṃ puṣṭikāmapi ।।

kumudvatīmutpalakāṃ viśokāṃ ca samarcayet ।
prāgādivedyāḥ paritaḥ paṅktau paṅktīśamarcayet ।।

viṣvaksenaṃ tataḥ paścādindrādīṃśca samarcayet ।
dravyadevārcanam
mṛddevatā tu bhūdevī parvateśastu pāvakaḥ ।।

vāyurvaidhānyadevassyādgaruḍā oṃkuradevatā ।
maṅgalādhipatiśśakraḥpañcagavyādhipaśśivaḥ ।।

tathaiva viśvedevāśca upasnānādhidevatāḥ ।
sāmavedo ghṛteśassyādupasnāne tu vatsarāḥ ।।

ṛgvedo madhudevassyādupasnāne tu vāyavaḥ ।
yajurvedo dadhīśo abhūdupasnā kapardinaḥ ।।

kṣīre tvadharvavedaśca upasnāne aśvinau tathā ।
gandhodake ṣaḍṛtavo marutastadanantare ।।

akṣatode viśvamūrtirupasnāne bṛhaspatiḥ ।
somaḥ phalodakeśassyādanantastadanantare ।।

kuśodake ca munaya upasnāne tu takṣakaḥ ।
viṣṇūratnodakeśassyādgandharvāstanadantare ।।

mantroratnodakeśassyādupasnānetu puṣpajāḥ ।
sarvauṣadhyudake bhānurupasnāne apsarogaṇāḥ ।।

puṇyapuṣpeṣu dhātāraṃ cūrṇeṣvapyanapāyinam ।
varuṇaḥ
kaṣāyadevassyāttīrthe caiva jagadbhuvaḥ ।।

vanauṣadhīśo rudro abhūcchinīvālī haridrake ।
upasnāni tu rākā syātsarvagandhe śatakratuḥ ।।

brahmāṇaṃ mūlagandhetu plotavastre purandaram ।
dhātuṣvapi ca durgāṃ ca tattaddravyadharaṃ smaran ।।

trayodaśopacāraiśca mūrtimantrairathār'cayet ।
upasnāneṣu cānyeṣu varuṇaṃ ca tathār'cayet ।।

ācārya pūjayitvātu vastrairābharaṇais tathā ।
śiṣyaṃ ca pūjayetpaścādyajamānassvaśaktitaḥ ।।

tato guruḥprasannātmā deveśaṃ saṃpraṇamya ca ।
aṣṭopacārairabhyarcya snapanāvasaraṃ tataḥ ।।

vijñāpya haraye samyak paścātkāryaṃ samācaret ।
"rakṣasva tva'miti procya dravyadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।।

śiṣyastunamrakāyassannācāryājñāṃ pratīkṣate ।
ājñāpayedguruśśiṣyaṃ "harasveda'miti bruvan ।।

tattaddravyaṃ samādāya śiṣyastasmai nivedayet ।
adbhiḥprokṣya samādāya taddravyaṃ gururatvaraḥ ।।

pvaṇavaṃ tu samuccārya tatra kāryaṃ samācaret ।
lalāṭāntaṃ samuddhṛtya devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।।

taddravyeṇa sakṛttrirvā deveśasya pradakṣiṇam ।
taddravyanāma saṃyojya tanmantrānte tu kārayet ।।

"ato devā'ditimantreṇa devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।
viṣṇuṃ ca puruṣaṃ satyamacyutaṃ cāniruddhakam ।।

evaṃ mantraṃ samuccārya tatra kāryaṃ samācaret ।
kriyānte pātramādāya pūrvasthāne niveśayet ।।

snapanaprayogaḥ "ekākṣareṇa' mantreṇa prokṣyaṃ gṛhya pradakṣiṇam ।
kūrcenādāya saṃsrāvya mūrdhnivai snāpayenmṛdā ।।

"viśve nimagna'ityuktvāparvatena pradakṣiṇam ।
dhānyena snāpayeccaiva "prāṇaprasūti'muccaran ।।

"vitatya bāṇa'mityuktvā aṅkuraireva cār'cayet ।
"tvaṃ ya'jñeti ca mantreṇa maṅgalaiśca pradakṣiṇam ।।

"vasoḥ pavitra'mityuktvā pañcagavyābhiṣecanam ।
"vārīścatasra'ityuktvā sarvopasnānamācaret ।।

"agna āyāhi' mantreṇa ghṛtenaivābhiṣe cayet ।
"agnimīleti mantreṇa madhunaivābhiṣecayet ।।

dadhmābhiṣecayetpaścā"diṣe tve'ti samuccaran ।
"śanno devīra'bhītyuktvā kṣīreṇaivābhiṣecayet ।।

"abhi tvā śūra'ityuktvā snāpayedgandhavāriṇā ।
"imā oṣadhaya'ityuktvā snāpayedakṣatodakaiḥ ।।

"japan da'tveti cocchārya phalodaiścābhiṣecayet ।
"catvā'rīti ca mantreṇa kuśodaiścābhiṣecayet ।।

"tatpuruṣā'yeti mantreṇa ratnodaiścābhiṣecayet ।
"pūta sta'nyeti mantreṇa japyodairabhiṣecayet ।।

"catvāri śruṃgetyuccārya saryauṣadhyudakaiścaret ।
"dhātā vidhā'tetyuccārya puṇyapuṣpairathārcayet ।।

"ṛco yajūṃṣi' mantreṇa cūrṇena snāpayedguruḥ ।
"sa eṣa deva' uccārya udvarteta kaṣāyakaiḥ ।।

"sa sarvavettā'mantreṇa tīrthodeścābhiṣecayet ।
"sāmaiśca sāṃga'mityuktvā mārjayecca vanauṣadhīḥ ।।

hāridracūrṇaissaṃsnāpya "ato devā' iti bruvan ।
"tvaṃ strīpumā'nityuccārya lepayetsarvagandhakaiḥ ।।

snāpayeduṣṇatoyena "āpo hi'ṣṭheti coccaran ।
nityasnānoktamārgeṇa śuddhodairabhiṣecayet ।।

tattaddravyābhiṣekānte snānavastraṃ visṛjya ca ।
dhautaṃ samarpayeccaiva pūjayedaṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।।

"mitrassuvarṇa'ityuktvā plotena parimṛjya ca ।
vastrādyaissamalaṅkṛtya pūrvoktenaiva kārayet ।।

"tvaṃ bhūrbhuvastvaṃ'mantreṇa mūlagandhena mārjayet ।
"buddhimatā'mityuccārya cālaṅkuryācca dhātubhiḥ ।।

pādyamācamanaṃ dadyādālayasya pradakṣiṇam ।
svastisūktādisūktaṃ ca japtvācaivātha kārayet ।।

arcāsthāne tu saṃsthāpya pūjayitvoktamārgataḥ ।
mahāhāviḥ prabhūtaṃ vā yathāśakti nivedayet ।।

niṣkādhikaṃ suvarṇaṃ ca savatsāmapi gāṃ tathā ।
gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadyātsnāpakānāṃ tathaiva ca ।।

tatrānyakarmakartṝṇāṃ yathāśaktyāca dakṣiṇām ।
dadyātkarmaphalaṃ prāpya yajamāno atha bhaktimān ।।

snapanāyattamuddiṣṭadhānyadravyāṃbarāṇi ca ।
pātrāṇi ca tathānyāni snapanānte dhṛtāni ca ।।

nivedayitvā gurave praṇamecca muhurmuhuḥ ।
dhruvārcanā yadi syāttu pramukhe snapanaṃ caret ।।

vitānastaṃbhaveṣṭādipūrvavatkārayettataḥ ।
pañcahastābhedeṣu paṅktiṃ kuryādvidhānataḥ ।।

madhye kubhaṃ ca snyasya arcayitvā ca pūrvavat ।
dhruvapīṭhasya paritaḥ kūrcayuktaṃ caturdiśam ।।

jayādīrarcayitvātu mṛdādīn pūrvavatkramāt ।
tatpātraṃ saṃpragṛhyaiva pāṇibhyāṃ kṣālanaṃ caret ।।

atha vā pātramādāya pūrayitvātu sannyaset ।
dravyaṃ prati viśeṣeṇa pūrayitvār'cayetkramāt ।।

pādyaṃ cācamanaṃ puṣpaṃ gandhaṃ dhūpaṃ tathaiva ca ।
dīpamarghyaṃ tathācāmamarcayitvāṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।।

devadevaṃ namaskṛtya pradakṣiṇamathācaret ।
devasya puratastiṣṭheddravyamādāya pāṇinā ।।

gauśṛṅgāgraṃ samuddhṛtya pūrvoktavidhinā kramāt ।
punaḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā pūrvasthāne tu vinyaset ।।

dhruveṇābhyastare caiva biṃbairanyaissahaivatu ।
pūrvamuktaṃ dhruvārcā cetsnapanaṃ samyagācaret ।।
yathoktenaiva mārgeṇa yathāvidhi samarcayet catvāriṃśat ।।gavyaṃ śrutaṃ dadhi madhu kṣīre syādratna toyakam ।।japyaṃ dvādaśaitān samāhṛtya ।।ntu upasnānamekaṃ hāridra madhyamottamam ।।upasnānavi mādhamaṃ caiva snapanaṃ tu vidhīyate ।।stathā kuryātkalaśaistu caturdaśaiḥ ।।madhyame madhyamaṃ caiva madhyamādhama vidhīyate ।।saptabhiḥ kalaśaiḥ madhyamaṃ teṣāṃ ṣaḍbhiḥ kala ।।dhamamucyate caturdaśaiḥ ।।gavyaṃ ghṛtaṃ kṣīramakṣa pasnānaṃ tathaiva ca ।।etai daśaitān kalasyācetkra? ta ।।pūrvoktenaiva kalaśasyacet ।।dikṣaṣṭa gavyaistu aindre ghṛtami ।।myegandhodakaṃ tathā payo tyāṃ vāruṇyāmakṣatodakam ।।saumye japyodakaṃ kramāt vyastusaptabhiḥ kalaśaiḥ ।।catriṣaṭyoṇasthalaṃ saptabhiḥ kalaśoktavat ।।navakoṣṭhantu tatra vai ma bhaśca kuśāṃbhasā ।।japyā vinyaset evamevaṃ yet ।।dakṣiṇāyanakāletu uttarāyaṇakāletu paścāt ।।ye tu saṃprāpte tatsūryeṃdūparāgeṣu snapanaṃ devadevasya kṛtvā ta ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre dvāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

athatrayoviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

athatrayoviṃśo adhyāyaḥ 
utsavacakram
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi pūrvoddiṣṭaṃ sudarśanam ।
sudarśanasya coddiṣṭaṃ pramāṇaṃ ca viśeṣuḥ ।।

mahāberasya mānena navāṅgulamiti smṛtam ।
tasya vṛttaṃ samuddiṣṭamarāścaiva tu tṣaṅgulam ।।

vṛttaṃ paṭṭasya vistāramekāṅgulamudāhṛtam ।
tanmadhye cārakūṭaṃ syādekāṃgulamudāhṛtam ।।

arā dvādaśa uddiṣṭā etaccakrasya vai tathā ।
adhamaṃ mārgamālokya proktametatpramāṇakam ।।

tatra madhyaṃ pramāṇantu vakṣyāmi śruṇutādarāt ।
mahāberasya hastena dvādaśāṃgulamucyate ।।

tadvṛttaṃ tasya hastena dvādaśāṃgulamucyate ।
vṛttaṃ tasya samuddiṣṭamārakūṭaṃ dviyaṅgulam ।।

vṛttapaṭṭasya vistāramekāṃgulamudāhṛtam ।
aṣṭau ca caturaṅgulyā? duddiṣṭāśca samāsataḥ ।।

arāṣṣoḍaśa uddiṣṭāścakrasyaiva tu madhyame ।
kūrmaṃ vāpyatha siṃhaṃ vā padmaṃ vāpyatha kālayet ।।

adhastādyogadaṇḍaṃ ca ekāṅgulamudāhṛtam ।
ubhayoḥ pādayoścaiva siṃhenaiva tu kārayet ।।

āyasenaiva vā kuryāddāruṇā vā tathaiva ca ।
sarvatra suṃdaraṃ kuryātsajānana? vidhīyate ।।

etallakṣaṇamudgiṣṭaṃ cakrasyaiva pramāṇataḥ ।
madhūcchiṣṭena vidhinā kuryādvai tatra tatra tu ।।

vidadhyāddeva devasya heti pravaramuttamam ।
pramāṇaṃ ca tu sarvatra tattribhāgaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

sthāpanāṃ mūrtimantraṃ ca cakrasya śruṇutarṣayaḥ ।
athātassaṃpravakṣyāmi vaiṣṇavaṃ cakramuttamam ।।

trividhaṃ cakramuddiṣṭaṃ brahmaṇā parameṣinā ।
kālacakraṃ vīracakraṃ sahasravikacaṃ kramāt ।।

karoddhṛtaṃ vīracakraṃ devasya mukhamānataḥ ।
sarvājināṃ samūhanta bajaṃ khatrayamantataḥ? ।।

devasya mukhamānaṃ syāddvādaśāṣṭāracihnitam ।
jvālāpañcakasaṃyuktaṃ karāgre dakṣiṇe caret ।।

mayaṃ mahīmayaṃ divyamaṣṭāraṃ dvādaśārakam ।
ebhirmantraissamabhyarcya rakṣārthaṃ mokṣaśāntaye ।।

kālacakraṃ pravakṣyāmi autsavaṃ sarvaśāntidam ।
dhruvaberamukhāyāmaṃ dviguṇāyāmavistṛtam ।।

vṛttaṃ ca ṣaḍguṇaṃ proktaṃ kṣatāntaṃ tatsuvṛttakam ।
vṛttasya paṭṭavistāraṃ triyaṅgulamiti smṛtam ।।

ṣaḍaṅgulasamāyāmamārakūṭaṃ tu tṣaṅgulam ।
yavā kārakarā jñeyā ubhayatra praveśatā ।।

arakūṭe atha siṃhaṃ vā makaraṃ vātha padmakam ।
jvālātrikaṃ vā kartavyaṃ jvālāpañjakameva vā ।।

śatāṣṭāraṃ niṃśatiṃ vā uttame samyagācaret ।
catuṣpañcadvipañcāśanmadhyame samudāhṛtam ।।

dvātriṃśadvā caturviṃśadadhame saṃprayojayet ।
evaṃ syātkālacakrantu utsavārthaṃ prakalpayet ।।

cakrādhastāttathā nālaṃ dvādaśāṃgulamācaret ।
cakradviguṇadaṇḍantu khadiraṃ cāsanaṃ bhavet ।।

yājñikairatha vā vṛkṣaiḥ kārayedatra śāsanam ।
ṣaḍaṅgulāyatavistārāṃ phalakāṃ saṃprakalpayet ।।

vṛttaṃ vā caturaśraṃ vā laṃbadāmasamāyutam ।
triyaṅgulasamutsedhaṃ saṃdhayettarikopari ।।

tadadhastāttu tāṭiṃ ca kuṃbhalaṃbakasaṃyutam ।
aṣṭāṃgulasamutsethaṃ kārayediti śāsanam ।।

antassuṣirasaṃ kṛtvā?daṇḍāgre cādha eva vā ।
kūradaṇḍena saṃyojya phalakophalapadmakam ।।

latā prasthataraṃ vāpi kārayediti śāsanam ।
padmaṃ tu tṣaṅgunāyāmaṃ vistāramadhikāṃgulam ।।

pālikopari siṃhau dvāvubhayoḥ pārśvayoścaret ।
cakraṃ saṃvahamānau tau yāvattatra ca kālayet ।।

tayormānaṃ samuddiṣṭaṃ pañcāṃgulamiti smṛtam ।
daṇḍamadhyena kuryāttaddaṇḍamūle ṣaḍaṅgulam ।।

pīṭhaṃ ṣaḍaṅgulotsedhaṃ caturaṅgulameva vā ।
vṛttaṃ vā caturaśraṃ vā sarojadalakarṇayuk ।।

ṣāḍhaśāṃgulamāyāmaṃ vistāraṃ saṃprakīrtitam ।
karṇikāmadhyame nālamaṣṭāṃgula samāyutam ।।

nāladaṇḍena saṃyojya bandhayedaṣṭabandhanaiḥ ।
hāravatsudṛḍhaṃ kuryādavakramṛjusaṃyutam ।।

evaṃ kṛtvā yathāmārgaṃ sthāpanaṃ samyagācaret ।
sahasravikacaṃ cakraṃ puruṣākāramācaret ।।

raktābhaṃ nīlavarṇaṃ ca navatālena mānataḥ ।
dvibhujaṃ mukuṭodbandhaṃ cakracūlinamācaret ।।

sudarśanaṃ tathā cakraṃ sahasravikacaṃ tathā ।
anapāyinamityevaṃ mūrtimantraissamarcayet ।।

śatadhāraṃ kālacakraṃ sarvāsuravimardanam ।
sarvavighnaharaṃ ceti kālacakraṃ samarcayet ।।

kālacakraṃ pravakṣyāmi sarvāsuravināśanam ।
ṣaṭṭriṃśadaṅgulaṃ vāpi ṣaṭ pañcāśacchatāṣṭakam ।।

vistārāyāmatomānamuttamādhamamadhyamam ।
mānāṃgulena tadgrāhyaṃ takṣakaṃ vartulaṃ bhavet ।।

sahasrārā aṣṭaśataṃ triśataṃ ṣaṣṭimeva vā ।
arāḥkrameṇa saṃyuktā uttamādhamamadhyamāḥ ।।

caturviṃśattathā jvālāṣṣoḍaśa dvādaśātha vā ।
daśasaptāṅgulaṃ pañca vṛttaṃ paṭṭasya saṃyutam ।।

cakraprabhehakaṃ bhāgaṃ pīṭhaṃ padmakamācaret ।
daṇḍādīni vinā tasya padmaṃ pīṭhasyayojayet ।।

etaduktaṃ mahaccakraṃ sarvāriṣṭavināśanam ।
cakrasya sthāpanaṃ mārgaṃ pravakṣyāmi tapodhanāḥ ।।

aṅkurānarpayitvātu kārayedakṣimocanam ।
tathādhivāsanaṃ kṛtvā gavyānāmadhivāsanam ।।

yāgaśālāṃ tathā kṛtvā bhūṣayettoraṇānvitam ।
śayyāvediṃ ca tanmadhye cādhyardhāyāmavistṛtam ।।

tatturyāṃśodayāṃ vediṃ kṛtvā tāṃ caturaśrakam ।
prācyāmāhavanīyaṃ ca kuṇḍamaupāsanāgnivat ।।

prācyāṃ tu snānavediṃ ca kṛtvācaiva vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
athādhivāsitaṃ cakramādāyevābhiṣicya ca ।।

agniṃ saṃsādhya pūrvoktaṃ kuṃbhaṃ saṃsāthayetpunaḥ ।
cakrasyābhimukhe kuṃbhaṃ dhānyapīṭhoparikramāt ।।

sannyasya tu gururdhīmān yaditaṃ bhāvayettathā ।
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā śālāyāṃ sthāpayettathā ।।

hṛtpadmamadhye cakreśaṃ dvibhujaṃ prāṃjalīkṛtam ।
raktābhaṃ kṛtavastrābhaṃ dhyātvāsamyak prapūrya ca ।।

tasmātkuṃbhe samāvāhya pūrvoktamabhipūjya ca ।
vedyāṃ saṃsnāpya taccakraṃ kalaśaisnāpayettadā ।।

samala kṛtya vaktrādyairdhānyapīṭhoparikramāt ।
sannyasya kuṃbhaṃ saṃyuktaṃ baddhvā pratisaraṃ tataḥ ।।

śāyayitvā tathā cakraṃ hautraṃ samyak praśaṃsya ca ।
cakrāṅgānyāyadhāṃgāni mūrtimantrān pracakṣate ।।

paścādagniṃ paristīrya vaiṣṇavairmantra saṃyutaiḥ ।
"bhūmānano agre vandyāna'hutvā gāyatrisaṃyutam ।।

śatamaṣṭottaraṃ hutvā rātriśeṣaṃ vyapohya ca ।
snātvā prabhāte pūrvoktaṃ cakramādāya pūrvavat ।।

grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā kuṃbhenāsādayettathā ।
maṇḍape dakṣiṇe pārśve kṛtapīṭhe viśeṣataḥ ।।

ratnaṃ nikṣipya pūrvoktamantreṇa sthāpayettadā ।
cakramantrau susannyasya bījān sannyasya pūrvavat ।।

kuṃbhācchaktiṃ tathāvāhya pūjayedāsanādibhiḥ ।
pāyasādyairni vaidyātha guruṃ samyak prapūjayet ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛsuproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre trayoviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha caturviṃśo adhyāyaḥ 
utsavaḥ
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi deveśasyotsavakramam ।
varṣadaṃ sarvalokasya śāntidaṃ sarvapuṣṭidam ।।

rājñāṃ vijayadānāya śatrūṇāṃ nāśahetave ।
vyādhidurbhikṣaśā ntyarthamutsavaṃ kārayedbudhaḥ ।।

kālaśraddhānimittārthā utsavāstrividhāssmṛtāḥ ।
māsetu yasmin kasmiṃśchitpratisaṃvatsaraṃ caret ।।

ekasmin samayecaiva sa tu kālotsavo bhavet ।
iṣṭamāse dine ceṣṭe śraddhayā kriyate tu yaḥ ।।

sa tu śraddhotsavojñeya stasmātkālotsavo guruḥ ।
bhayapradanimitteṣu tathānāvṛṣṭikādiṣu ।।

kriyate tatra śāntyarthaṃ sa nimittotsavassmṛtaḥ ।
pratiṣṭhādivase tīrthaṃ prati saṃvatkaraṃ caret, ।।

kālotsava itijñeyaśśāntyarthaṃ saprakīrtitaḥ ।
rājarāṣṭrābhivṛddhyarthaṃ rājñāṃ caivābhivṛddhaye ।।

atmanaścaiva putrāṇāṃ kuryādukteṣu maṅgalam ।
rājño janmadine caiva yassa śraddhotsavo bhavet ।।

adbhutādyudbhaveśāntissatu naimittikotsavaḥ ।
grāmādau cotsavassyāccetkrameṇaivaṃ tu kārayet ।।

sarvaduḥkhārtiśāntyarthamādau kālyutsavaṃ caret ।
anveṣāṃ krūradevānāṃ śiṣṭabhūtagaṇasya ca ।।

śāntyarthaṃ kārayetpaśchāstroktaṃ śaṅkarotsavam ।
viśastrigaṇasāntyarthaṃ saumyamārgeṇa vāstuṣu ।।

cakraseneśa saṃyuktaṃ kuryāddurgotsavaṃ punaḥ ।
sarveṣāmapi devānāṃ munīnāmapi sarvaśaḥ ।।

pitṝṇāṃ ca grahāṇāṃ ca tatpatnīnāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।
dvijānāmapi śāntyarthaṃ lokānāmapi sarvaśaḥ ।।

puṣṭyarthaṃ kārayetpaścāddeveśasyotsavaṃ kramāt ।
anyadhā cedvināśassyātsarveṣāṃ ca na saṃśayaḥ ।।

tasmātpariharedvidvān grāmādautaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
viṣuvāyanabhūparkṣapratiṣṭhākartṛbheṣu ca ।।

grahaṇemāsanakṣatre viṣṇupañcadineṣu ca ।
utsavasyāntadivase teṣu tīrthaṃ prakalpayet ।।

eteṣvekaṃ parigrāhyaṃ yajamānasya cecchayā ।
viṣuve cāyane caiva grahaṇe somasūryayoḥ ।।

tattatkāle prakurvīta tīrthasnārantu nānyadhā ।
anyarkṣeṣvatha pūrvāhṇemadhyāhne vā guṇānvite ।।

ekasminneva māsetu yadi tīrthadinadvayam ।
tayorantyadine tīrthamiti pūrvajadarśanam ।।

tadeva yadi sūryasya viddhaṃ cetsaṃkramādibhiḥ ।
varjanīyaṃ tathā pūrvaṃ praśastamabhidhīyate ।।

vāradvayānuṣakte cet tithau syāttupare tathā ।
adhimāsaḥ parityājyaḥ kālotsavavidhauhareḥ ।।

arkavārarkṣa saṃyogassarvadā saṃpraśasyate ।
śravaṇadvādaśīyogassarvakarmaphalapradaḥ ।।

yogāśca supraśastāssyussiddhāmṛtavarāhvayāḥ ।
tithidvayānuṣaktaṃ ce annakṣatraṃ syātpare ahani ।।

parasmin divase syāccedyāvacca daśanāḍikāḥ ।
hīnaṃ cet pūrvadivase saṃkalpyāvabhṛthaṃ caret ।।

uttamaṃ tu trisaptāhaṃ madhyamaṃ syāccaturdaśa ।
navāhaṃ vāthasaptāham adhamaṃ paricakṣate ।।

triguṇānyutsavāhāni kṛtvādau ghoṣaṇaṃ caret ।
madhyame dviguṇādau syādutsavādi dine adhame ।।

athavāvabhṛthātpūrvamekaviṃśatike dine ।
dhvajasyārohaṇaṃ kṛtvā sarvamutsavamācaret ।।

rāhudarśanasaṃkrāntyoḥ snānaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ niśāsvapi ।
kriyāṃ samāpya madhyāhne rātraucetsakalaṃ budhaḥ ।।

tāvatkālaṃ vinodeva nītvā tattīrthamācaret ।
pakṣantrayodaśāhaṃ vā dinānyekādaśa kramāt ।।

navāhaṃ vātha saptāhaṃ pañcāhamatha vā punaḥ ।
tridinaṃ dvidinaṃ caiva kuryādekāhameva vā ।।

na dhvajārohaṇaṃ kuryāttṣahādautu viśeṣataḥ ।
utsavasya dinādautu ghoṣaye dvidhipūrvakam ।।

ghoṣaṇādivasātpūryaṃ kālayedaṅkurār'paṇam ।
dhvajadaṇḍaṃ tatovakṣye viprādīnāṃ yathākramam ।।

veṇuṃ ca jātivṛkṣaṃ ca caṃpakaṃ kramukaṃ tathā ।
dhvajadaṇḍārthamāhṛtya sarveṣāṃ kramukaṃ tu vā ।।

anyairvāśubhavṛkṣairvākārayediti ke ca na ।
caturviṃśāṅgulaṃ nāhaṃ dhvajadaṇḍamathottamam ।।

tasmāttu dvyaṅgulaṃ hīnaṃ dhvajadaṇḍantu madhyamam ।
viṃśatyaṅgulanāhe tadadhamaṃ daṇḍamucyate ।।

yathālābhaparīṇāhamavakraṃ parigṛhya ca ।
dhvajadaṇḍamṛjuṃ kurvādvimānasamayāyatam ।।

vimānasyādhikaṃ kuryāt pādahīna mathār'dhakam ।
adhyarthaṃ vādhipādaṃ vā mūlādagraṃ kramātkṛśam ।।

veṇukaṃ yadi saṃgrāhyaṃ bhūtavedāṃgulāyatam ।
ṣaḍaṅgulaparīṇāhaṃ veṇudaṇḍaṃ susaṃsthitam ।।

tanmadhye dviyamaṃ hitvā tanmadhye valayaṃ dṛḍham ।
tāladvayamathāyāmaṃ yamamātrantu vistṛtam ।।

utsedhaṃ bhāgamuddiṣṭaṃ dārubhiryājñikaistuvā ।
taccaturthāṃśakaṃ kṛtvā mūle agredvyaṃśakantyajet ।।

madhye dvyaṃśaṃ tu kartavyaṃ suṣiradvayasaṃyutam ।
śakalāni trīṇiyojya mūlamadhyāgrataḥkramāt ।।

prakṣālyamūlamantreṇa tanmantraiḥprokṣaṇaṃ caret ।
daśadarbhayutaṃ kūrcamagrecaiva tu yojayet ।।

darbhamālāntarāveṣṭya daṇḍocāśvadthapatrayuk ।
madhyāṅguliparīṇāhaṃ daṇḍadviguṇamāyatam ।।

daṇḍāgre tatra saṃyojya rajjuṃ tatraiva bandhayet ।
saṃvyapohya catustālaṃ pṛṣṭhe yūdhādhipasyatu ।।

khānayitvā dhvajasthānaṃ tritālaṃ gāḍhayeva ca ।
medinīṃ tu samabhyarcya ratnaṃ bījāni ca kṣipet ।।

sthāpayitvā dhvajaṃ tatra dhvajamantreṇa mantravit ।
devadevaṃ samīkṣyaiva yaṣṭiṃ tatpra mukhe nyaset ।।

dhvajadaṇḍamṛjuṃ kuryāddṛḍhaṃ tatraiva kārayet ।
mūlaṃ tritālamutsedhaṃ tadadhyardhantu vistṛtam ।।

tadūrdhve ratnimātrantu sāṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam ।
śuddhakārpāsavastrantu samāhṛtya navaṃ dṛḍham ।।

uttamaṃ ṣoḍaśaṃ hastaṃ madhyamaṃ tithihastakam ।
adhamaṃ caturdaśaṃ hastaṃ trividhaṃ vastramucyate ।।

pañcatālaṃ catustālaṃ tritālaṃ vistṛtaṃ kramāt ।
agraṃ pādaṃ viditvā tu mukhaṃ pṛṣṭhaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

caturbhāgaṃ paṭaṃ kuryādekabhāgaṃ śiro bhavet ।
vīśasthānaṃ dvibhāgaṃ tu pucchamekāṃśamucyate ।।

madhyamasyāgramūlaṃ ca yaṣṭiṃ samyak prayojayet ।
tanmadhye tu likhedvīśaṃ pañcavarṇairalaṅkṛtam ।।

dhruvaberasya kaṇṭhāsta muttame cottamaṃ bhavet ।
adhame antyantu nābhyantaṃ tayormadhyeṣṭadhā bhavet ।।

ekai magathamāntaṃ ca navadhā mānamucyate ।
dhvajadaṇḍasya vīśasya ṣaṭ śubhāni nirīkṣayet ।।

yajamānānukūle ca nakṣatre ca viśeṣataḥ ।
navārdhatālamānaṃ vā navatālamathāpi vā ।।

atibhaṅgaṃ nataṃ caiva bhaṅgatrayasamanvitam ।
vāmapāde samākuñcya dakṣiṇaṃ saṃprasārya ca ।।

kiñcitsaṃkucitaṃ pīṭhātparṣṇīpārśvaṃ samuddhṛtam ।
pakṣadvayasamāyuktaṃ karaṇḍamukuṭānvitam ।।

śyāmaṃ śvetaṃ tathā kṛṣṇaṃ raktaṃ pītaṃ tathaiva tu ।
etaistu pañcabhirvarṇairanurūpaistu śobhanaiḥ ।।

garuḍaṃ prāñjaliṃ kuryātkiñcitkaṃ prekṣayedbudhaḥ ।
bhūṣaṇair aṣṭanāgaiśca vāmahaste tvanantakaḥ ।।

vāsukiryajña sūtrantu kaṭīsūtrantu takṣakam ।
hāraṃ karkoṭakaṃ caiva padmaṃ dakṣiṇakarṇake ।।

mahāpadmaṃ vāmakarṇe śaṅkha ca śirasi kramāt ।
gulikaṃ dakṣiṇe haste kramātsarvavibhūṣaṇam ।।

mūrdhnaścopari kartavyaṃ śvetachatraṃ tu sundaram ।
pārśvayorubhayoścāpi cāmaradvaya saṃyutam ।।

pādapārśvadvayecaiva dīpadvaya samanvitam ।
pūrṇakuṃbhaṃ tayormadhye likhitvā tu viśeṣataḥ, ।।

tasyādhasśaṅkhacakre ca samālikhya viśeṣataḥ ।
muktādāmādyalaṅkṛtya pārśvayoḥ kadalīkṛtam ।।

pūrvasminneva divase kṛtvā nayanamokṣaṇam ।
devālayasyābhimukhe prapāyāṃ maṇḍape-tha vā ।।

pañcavarṇairalaṅkṛtya vitānastaṃbhaveṣṭanaiḥ ।
śālirāśiṃ ca kṛtvaiva tatpaṭantu susannyaset ।।

vāstuhomaṃ tataḥkṛtvā paryagnīkaraṇaṃ caret ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvaiva prokṣayetpañcagavyakaiḥ ।।

aiśānyāmagnikuṇḍe tu cauvāsana vidhānataḥ ।
āghāraṃ vidhivaddhutvā vaiṣṇavaṃ ca suhūyate ।।

haimapātrasthavarṇena haimatūlyā viśeṣataḥ ।
tanmantraṃ ca samuccārya nayanonmilanaṃ caret ।।

aṅgahomaṃ tataḥkṛtvā darśanīyaiśca darśayet ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ ca hutvātu tathā puruṣasūktakaiḥ ।।

vyāhṛtyaṃntaṃ ca hutvātu tataḥ kuṃbhaṃ pragṛhyaca ।
tantunā pariveṣṭai va kūrcayuktaṃ sahākṣatam ।।

vadanvai viṣṇugāyatrīṃ gāyatrīṃ garuḍasya ca ।
"iṣe tvorjye'tvādi japan "āpa undantvi'ti kramāt ।।

tataḥ puruṣasūktaṃ ca mantrānapi ca vaiṣmavān ।
kūrcenaiva tu tattoyamabhimṛśya samāhitaḥ ।।

tadaṃbunā kuśāgreṇa prokṣaṇaiḥ prokṣaṇaṃ caret ।
apo hiraṇyavarṇābhiḥ pavamānādibhistribhiḥ ।।

"śanno devī'rabhītyuktvā puruṣasūktena vaiṣṇapaiḥ ।
śuddhyarthaṃ prokṣayitvā tu puṇyāhamapi vācayet ।।

pariṣicya pāvakaṃ paścāttanmantreṇa suhūyatām ।
sāyamarcāvasāne tu kuṃbhapūjāṃ samācaret ।।

kalaśaissaptabhiḥ prokṣya baddhvāpratisaraṃ tataḥ ।
aṇḍajādīni pañcaiva dhānyānyāstīrya vastrayuk ।।

śayane śāyayeccaiva devavāde śirastathā ।
hautraṃ praśaṃsya tatkāle hotā hautrakrameṇa vai ।।

vainateyasya mantreṇa tanmūrtyāvāhanaṃ caret ।
mūrtimantraissamāvāhya nirupyājyāhutīryajet ।।

"śatadhāraṃ kadā'vīti vīśamantramudāhṛtam ।
tathādvādaśaparyāyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca suhūyatām ।।

vyāhṛtyantaṃ ca kṛtvā tu rātriśeṣaṃ vyapohya ca ।
āgneyyāṃ nyasya bheryāṃ ca nandikeśvaramāhvayet ।।

punaḥ prabhāte dharmātvāsnātmāsnānavidhānataḥ ।
muhūrte samanuprāpte hṛdi bījākṣaraṃ nyaset ।।

kuṃbhācchaktiṃ samāvāhyacār'cayitvā vidhānataḥ ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvaiva samabhyarca vivedayet ।।

agniṃ prajvālya tanmantrairjuhuyāddaśaśaḥkramāt ।
antahomaṃ vācayitvaiva samabhyarcya nivedayet ।।

upalipya paṭaṃ paścātpañcavarṇairalaṅkṛtam ।
dhūpadīpairalaṅkṛtya śālipīdhaṃ prakalpayet ।।

caturaśraṃ samaṃ kṛtvā vistāraṃ caikabhāgakaṃ ।
śālyardhaṃ taṇḍulaṃ proktaṃ tadardhaṃ tilamāharet ।।

cakraṃ paścimato nyasya dhānyapīṭhopari sthitam ।
tasyaivot tarataḥ pārśveviṣvaksenaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

dhānyapīṭhe susaṃsthāpya garuḍaṃ paścimāmukham ।
nyasya bherīṃ ca pārśve yaṣṭiṃ susannyaset ।।

devadevaṃ susaṃpūjya dviguṇaṃ pūjayettataḥ ।
dviguṇaṃ havirevoktaṃ devībhyāṃ ca tathā bhavet ।।

cakrādīnāṃ pṛthakkuryādāsanādīn pṛthak pṛthak ।
nandīśvaraṃ tathābhyarcya havirbhiśca nivedayet ।।

ācāryo yaṣṭimādāya "bhūrbhuvassuva' rīrayan ।
"upa śvāsaya' mantraṃ ca japtvā bherīṃ sutāḍayet ।।

vādakastu śucirbhūtvā vastramālyādyalaṅkṛtaḥ ।
sarvavādyasamāyuktaṃ bherīmādāya śāstravit ।।

śāstroktena vidhānena cakrāgretāḍayettadā ।
droṇairdreṇārdhakairvāpi āḍhakairvātha taṇḍulaiḥ ।।

pācayitvā kaṭāhetu prakṣipedbalimuttamam ।
mudganiṣpāvatilvāṃśca lājāpūpaupragṛhya ca ।।

kaṭāhe tu susannyasya śiṣyastaṃ śirasā vahet ।
abhivandya dhvacaṃ pūrvamādāya samalaṅkṛtam ।।

rathe vā śibikāyāṃ vā mantreṇāropya maṅgalaiḥ ।
saha puṣpaṃ baliṃ pātre saṃgṛhyānugataṃ punaḥ ।।

cakravīśāmitān paścānnāthavadgamayettadā ।
ācāryaḥ purato gatvā sarvavādyasamāyutam ।।

garbhagehasthadevānāṃ brahmādīnāṃ yathākramam ।
dvāreṣu dvārapālebhyo dhāmapālebhya eva ca ।।

anyeṣāṃ parivārāṇāṃ svesvesthāne baliṃ kṣipet ।
ālayasya bahirgatvā grāme sarvatra ghoṣayet ।।

madhyame cālayaṃ yatra brahmādīśāntamācaret ।
yasyāṃ diśi bhaveddhāma taddigādi baliṃ kṣipet ।।

utsavabhramaṇaṃ kuryātprādakṣiṇyakrameṇa nai ।
grāmaṃ gatvātu saṃprāpya saṃdhau saṃdhau viśeṣataḥ ।।

dhyātvā buddhvādhipānmantrī bhūmyāmāvāhya pūrvavat ।
arghyāntaṃ ca samabhyarcya muṣṭyannaṃ nāmabhirdadet ।।

saṃdhau tatsaṃdhimādāya prācyāṃ "bhūtebhya'ityapi ।
devebhyo dakṣiṇe paścā drākṣanebhyaśca paścime ।।

nāgebhyaścottare cātha ūrdhvāyāṃ diśi cakramāt ।
"ye bhūtā'iti mantreṇa pūrvaṃ dadyājjalaṃ punaḥ ।।

puṣpaṃ baliṃ tathādhāvaṃ saṃdadyāccakrasannidhau ।
yasyāṃ diśi vimānaṃ vā brahmādyeva baliṃ dadet ।।

ācaredatha vā tasya digīśādyaṃ baliṃ kramāt ।
paścimastha vimānaṃ cedvaruṇādi baliṃ kṣipet ।।

atha vā grāmamadhye ceddatvā brahmabaliṃ puraḥ ।
tatodikpālakānāṃ ca tathā bhūtabaliṃ kṣipet ।।

digīśayordvayormadhye mahāvīthyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
saṃdhiryadi bhavettatra bhūtānāṃ ca baliṃ kṣipet ।।

saṃdhyantaragatāṃ saṃdhimācaredyadi mohataḥ ।
karmaṇo vāstujātānāmanardhaṃ bhavati dhruvam ।।

prāgantaṃ paścimādyaṃ ca ekavīthiṃ ca daṇḍakam ।
kuryāttatraiva cakrādyaiḥ paścimādyaṃ baliṃ tataḥ ।।

varuṇanirṛti vāyubhyaḥ paścime tu baliṃ tathā ।
dhātre yamakuberābhyāṃ sadhau madhye baliṃ kṣipet ।।

indravāpakarudrebhyaḥ prācyāṃ dadyāttataḥ kramāt ।
udagantaikavīthiśceddakṣiṇādyaṃ baliṃ kṣipet ।।

yamanīlānalebhyaśca dakṣiṇe madhyame api ca ।
brahmavāruṇa śakrebhyaścottare ca baliṃ tathā ।।

kubila pavane śebhyo baliṃ dadyātkrameṇa ca ।
nadyādiṣu vimānaṃ cetparitaḥ prāṅgaṇe dadet ।।

pūrvaṃ kṣiptvā baliṃ dhīmān punastasya ca tasya ca ।
mantramuccārya pūrvoktaṃ gadyapadyaiśca ghoṣayet ।।

nagarādau tu gadyaiśca praśaṃsyopāṃśunā budhaḥ ।
tattanmantraṃ samuccārya ghoṣayetpaṭahādibhiḥ ।।

"priyatāṃ bhagavānviṣṇussarvalokeśvaro hariḥ ।
brahmeśābhyāṃ ca sahitaścotsave naḥ prasīdatu ।।

devāśca ṛṣayassarve pitaraśca grahādayaḥ ।
viṣṇulokagatāssarvenānālokanivāsinaḥ ।।

sarvenye devatāssarvāḥ parivāragaṇaissaha ।
viśve te viṣṇuyāge arsmi samāgacchantu sādarāḥ ।।

havyaṃ baliṃ samādāya bhuñjantu śubhadāyinaḥ' ।
ityuktvā ghoṣayetsaṃdhau cakrasyābhimukhe punaḥ ।।

brahmādyān svasvatālaiśca ghoṣayedvādakaḥ punaḥ ।
balimevaṃ ca nirvāpya pradakṣiṇava śena tu, ।।

japanvai śākunaṃ sūktaṃ praviśedālayaṃ punaḥ ।
baliśiṣṭaṃ bhūtapīṭhe "sarvabhūtebhya' ityapi ।।

baliṃ tattoyaśeṣaṃ ca prakṣipeccakrasannidhau ।
dhāmapradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā dhvajādyairanapāyibhiḥ ।।

śāntaṃ cakraṃ ca cat sthāne sthāpayenmatimān punaḥ ।
dhvajasthānaṃ praviśyaiva dhvajamādāya mantravit ।।

"svasti dā'iti mantreṇa badhnīyādrajjunā saha ।
mantreṇa matimān paścātprāṅmukho vā pyudaṅmukhaḥ ।।

daṇḍāgre yojayetpaścācchaṅkhakāhalasaṃyutam ।
samābaddhya punassnigdhaṃ "bhūri'sīti japaṃ stataḥ ।।

abhimantṣa dhvajaṃ paścādāsanādyaissamarcayet ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayetpaścānmudgānnaṃ tu dhvajasya ca ।।

nivedya mukhavāsaṃ ca praṇāmamapi kārayet ।
tatkāle maudgikaṃ cānnaṃ garuḍasya niveditam ।।

striyassatbutrakāmā stadaśnīyurbhaktisaṃyutāḥ ।
āyaṣmantaṃ balārogyavantaṃ dāntaṃ sulakṣaṇam ।।

buddhimantaṃ yaśovantaṃ prasūyeyussutaṃ dhruvam ।
(tatantu toṣayedvīśaṃ stotrairdhyānayuto guruḥ ।।

"namo namaste pakṣīndra svā'dhyāyavapuṣe namaḥ ।
vāhanāya mahāviṣṇostārkṣyāyāmita tejase ।।

garuḍāya namastubhyaṃ sarvasarpendramṛtyave ।
vainateya mahābāho mahābala vayo adhipa ।।

vihagendra namaste astu samutpāṭītakalpaka ।
āhṛtāmṛtakuṃbhāya jananīdāsyamocine ।।

surāsurendrajayine nāgendrābaraṇāya te ।
yadādhāramidaṃ sarvaṃ tadādhārāya te namaḥ ।।

pakṣau yasya bṛhatsāma rathantaramapi dvayam ।
akṣiṇī cāpi gāyatrī trivṛtsāma śirassvayam ।।

stoma ātmā namastasmai vāmadevyāṅgasampade ।
namaḥprāṇādivāyūnāmīśāya garuḍātmane ।।

pakṣīndra pakṣavikṣepataraṅgānilasaṃpadā ।
nirastāsurasannāha samare śatrusūdana ।।

pratiṣṭhitaḥ paṭe tubhyaṃ namaḥpraṇavamūrtaye ।
karmaṇāṃ siddhimāhūtaḥ kuruṣva vihageśvara ।।

doṣānapanayāsmākaṃ guṇānāvaha sarvaśaḥ ।
vighnāni jahi sarvāṇi ātmasātkuru māmapi' ।।

stutvaivaṃ gāruḍaṃ mantraṃ japedekāgramānasaḥ) ।
dhvajasyārohaṇe yāvattāvasmūrtyā viśeṣataḥ ।।

trikālaṃ vā dvikālaṃ vā eka kālamadhāpi vā ।
havissamyaṅnivedyaiva saptaviṃśati vigrahaiḥ ।।

pūjayitvā dhvajaṃ paścādrātrau bhūtabaliṃ kṣipet ।
"jiyamatyucchrayaṃ dhanyaṃ dhvajaṃceti dhvajaṃ tathā ।।

dhvajamūle tathendrādīn daṇḍe brahmāṇamityapi ।
sūryendvagnīṃstu phalakatraye yaṣṭyāṃ sudarśanam ।।

valaye vānukiṃ rajjvāṃ trimūrtīrarcayettataḥ ।
ghaṇṭāyāṃ caiva brahmāṇaṃ darbhadāmni sarasvatīm ।।

itikrameṇa cāvāhya tanmantrairarcanaṃ caret ।
dhvajārohaṇamārabhya cotsavādidinādadhaḥ ।।

sāyaṃ prātaśca vūjānte dhvajārohaṇavadbalim ।
śiṣyeṇa guruṇā cātha cakrasyābhimukhe tathā ।।

nityaṃ rātrau viśeṣeṇa tathā bhūtabaliṃ kṣipet ।
vīśāmitau vinā dhīmān tīrthāntaṃ sarvarātriṣu ।।

cakrameva nayedvidvān balirakṣaṇahetave ।
dhvajasyāropaṇaṃ yāvattāvannityaṃ samāhitaḥ ।।

trikālaṃ vā dvikālaṃ vāpyekakālamathāpi vā ।
pūrvoktena krameṇaiva samabhyarcya nivedayet ।।

dhvajasyārohaṇaṃ rātrāvapi kurvanti ke ca na ।
utsavāraṃbhadivasāttatra ye grāmavāsinaḥ ।।

anyakāryasamāsaktāna gaccheyusthsalāntaram ।
gaccheyuratha vā tīrthe nivarteyurasaṃśayam ।।

bahirvīthyāṃ tu tadgrāme janāssarve tathaiva ca ।
tāvānna teṣāṃ nirbandhassamīpastheṣu yassmṛtaḥ ।।

ahūtavyā utsavārthe devāssamyak prakīrtitāḥ ।
devādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ teṣāṃ sthānaṃ pravakṣyate ।।

indrādayo mahādikṣu vidikṣu ca samāśritāḥ ।
tathaikādaśa rudrāśca dvādaśāhaskarā api ।।

vasavassyurathāṣṭau ca oṅkāraśca vaṣaṭkṛtam ।
ete devāstrayastriṃśāḥ kathitā brahmaṇā purā ।।

aśvināvapi tatreti kecidāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।
trayastriṃśaddevatānāṃ sthānamaiśānyamucyate ।।

apare cāpi kartavyā nadīpārśve viśeṣataḥ ।
aṣṭādaśagaṇānāntu bhutapīṭhasya dakṣiṇe ।।

devāśca ṛṣayassarve pitaro daityadānavāḥ ।
asurāścaiva gandharvā stathaivāpsarapāṅgaṇāḥ ।।

yakṣāśca rākṣasāścaiva nāgābhūtāḥ piśācakāḥ ।
anāvṛṣṭigaṇāścaiva tathāmṛtamucāṃ gaṇāḥ ।।

mātaraścaiva rohiṇyaḥ sūryā aṣṭādaśa smṛtāḥ ।
aṣṭādaśagaṇāścaite proktā vai devayonayaḥ ।।

anuktānanyadevāṃśca indrapārśve samarcayet ।
devānāṃ caiva patnīśca tattatpārśve samarcayet ।।

skando vighnaśca durgā ca jyeṣṭhā caiva sarasvatī ।
tadālaye baliṃ dadyātprākāre cottare api vā ।।

parivāroktadeśe tu rohiṇyo mātarastathā ।
ṛṣipatnīśca tāssapta ṛṣibhissaha cār'cayet ।।

siddhān vidyādharāṃś caiva garuḍagandharvakinnarān ।
kipūruṣāṃś cāraṇān devān mahādikṣu samarcayet ।।

bhūtebhyaścātha yakṣebhyaḥ piśācebhya stathaiva ca ।
rākṣasebhyaśca nāgebhyassaṃdhau saṃdhau baliṃ dadet ।।

rājaveśmāṅgaṇe madhye indraṃ caiva samarcayet ।
tasya dakṣiṇapārśve tu jayaśrīkīrtīssamarcayet ।।

utsavārthaṃ viśeṣeṇa saṃbhārānāharettataḥ ।
rathaṃ ca śibikāṃ caiva yantraḍolādikāṃs tathā ।।

kārayitvā ca śilpoktaṃ dīpānanyān pragṛhya ca ।
bheryādīnyapi vādyāni śaṅkhakāhalakāni ca ।।

tālavṛntaṃ dhvajānanyān chatracāmarabarhiṇaḥ ।
nartakān gāyakānanyān yathoktaṃ pūrvamāharet ।।

ālayaṃ samalaṅkṛtya toraṇādyairvibhūṣya ca ।
paricārān samāhūya svasvakarma nivedayet ।।

maṇṭapādīni sarvāṇi prapādīni ca sarvaśaḥ ।
āstānārthaṃ ca nṛtyārthaṃ kārayecchilpaśāstravit ।।

"ava dhū'teti mantreṇa grāmavīthīrviśeṣataḥ ।
viprā vedavidaśśuddhāśśodhayeyurmanoramam ।।

"āśāsu sapta'ityuktvā gavyādyaiḥ sarvataśśubham ।
samabhyukṣyopalipyaiva taṇḍulānavakīrayet ।।

kadalīpūgakuṃbhādyairalaṅkuryādgṛhāṃgaṇam ।
vitānādyairviśeṣeṇa phūṣayetsarvataśśubham ।।

tadgrāmavāsinaḥ sarve alaṅkṛtā nānyatatparāḥ ।
naimittikādikaṃ hitvā dhyāyeyurmanasā harim ।।

tadgrāmasīmanyantasthsā nityakarmakriyāṃ vinā ।
naimittikāni kāmyāni tīrthāntaṃ nācaredbudhāḥ ।।

pravṛtte cotsave viṣṇossaumyamārgeṇa vāstuṣu ।
anyadevotsavaṃ tatra nācarediti śāsanam ।।

asmin devotsave yāge tadvāstuṣu viśeṣataḥ ।
saṃkalpya cottarāṃ vediṃ pravṛtte anyāni nācaret ।।

yadi cetsarvanāśassyātkartābhartā vinaśyati ।
tasmātparihareddhīmān tīrthāntaṃ teṣu vāntuṣu ।।

utsavādidinātpūrvaṃ saptame pañcame atha vā ।
saṃsnāpya devadeveśamaṅkurār'paṇamācaret ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāste bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre caturviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha pañcaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

utsavavidhiḥ

athotsavavidhiṃ vakṣye devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ।
āraṃbhadivasātpūrvaṃ yajamāno mudnvitaḥ ।।

pūrvoktaguṇasaṃpannaṃ varayitvā guruṃ tathā ।
dviguṇārādhanāyaikamekaṃ kuṃbhārcanāya ca ।।

homārthaṃ balidānārthaṃ tathā sthānārcanāya ca ।
vṛṇetpadārthinaḥ pañca tāvataḥ paricārakān ।।

ācāryamupasaṃgamya saṃpūjya ca vidhānataḥ ।
"karmedaṃ me kuru'ṣveti yācayedvinayānvitaḥ ।।

ācāryaḥ saha śiṣyaistu kṛtvā keśādivāpanam ।
snātvā snānavidhānena dhṛtvā dhautaṃ yathāvidhi ।।

ūrdhvapuṇḍradharassamyak saṃdhyādīn samupāsya ca ।
brahmayajñaṃ ca kṛtvaiva tathā devarṣi tarpaṇam ।।

japeddvādaśasūktāni nārāyaṇamathāruṇam ।
ālaye saṃpraviśyaiva deveśaṃ saṃpraṇamya ca ।।

devaṃ viśeṣato abhyarcya kāryaṃ tasmai nivedayet ।
yajamāno api dharmātmā nityakarma samāpyaca ।।

devālayaṃ praviścaiva puṇyāhaṃ kārayettataḥ ।
śrīvaikhānasa sūtrokta madhuparmavidhānataḥ ।।

ācāryamṛtvijaścaiva saṃpūjya vidhinā tataḥ ।
alaṅkuryācca ganthādyairdhūpadīpādibhistathā ।।

navavastrottarīyādyaistathā pañcāṅgabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।
pañcāṅgabhūṣaṇaṃ vakṣye yathā kuryādatandritaḥ ।।

daśaniṣkapramāṇena kuṇḍalābharaṇaṃ pṛthak ।
ṣaṇṇiṣkamānaṃ kaṭakamaṅgadaṃ cāṃgulīyakam ।।

ekaviṃśatiniṣkāḍhyaṃ kaṭīsūtraṃ salakṣaṇam ।
tadardhāṃśapramāṇeva grīvālaṅkaraṇaṃ pṛthak ।।

aṣṭaniṣka pramāṇeva yajñasūtraṃ ca kārayet ।
anena vidhinā kuryādgurorardhārdhamṛtvijām ।।

ācāryaḥ prokṣyacātmānaṃ yajamānamathartvijaḥ ।
prāśnīyātpañcagavyaṃ ca padārthibhyaścasādaram ।।

yajamānāya dadyācca mantrapūrvaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
tataḥ padmāgnimādhāya pariṣicya ca pāvakam ।।

yaddevādi catussūktānyājyena juhuyādguruḥ ।
vaiśvānareṇa sūktena copatiṣṭheddhutāśanam ।।

kṣapayitvā tataḥ pāpaṃ karmārhāste bhavantyataḥ ।
kūśmāṇḍahoma ityuktassarvapāpapraṇāśanaḥ ।।

tatkāne dīkṣitāssarve vidhimantrapurassaram ।
baddhvā pratisaraṃ haste paścātkuryuḥkriyāmapi ।।

tataḥprabhṛti sarve te śuddha dantanakhāstathā ।
haviṣyabhojino dāntā strikālasnāyino api ca ।।

jitendriyā bhaveyuste tathā adhaśsāyino api ca ।
strīśūdrābhyāmasaṃbhāṣya nārāyaṇaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

yāvatkālaṃ bhaveddīkṣā tāvacchuddhā ime smṛtāḥ ।
sūtake mṛtake vāpi teṣāṃ nāśauca iṣyate ।।

athavakṣyeṃkurārthantu mṛttikāgrahaṇe vidhim ।
śānta cakre samabhyarcya havīṃṣyapi nivedya ca ।।

viṣvaksenaṃ samādāya yānamāropya nāthavat ।
ācāryaḥ puratogacche "dviṣṇurmā'miti coccaran ।।

cakrasya paścādgaccheyurācāryeṇa samanvitāḥ ।
ādarśahemakalaśapūrṇakuṃbhāṃkurādibhiḥ ।।

dhvajatrayādikān sarvān puraskṛtya padārthinaḥ ।
prācyāṃ sarvasamṛddhissyādāgneyyāṃ dhānyanāśanam ।।

yāmye janavināśassyānnairṛtyāṃ dhananāśanam ।
anāvṛṣṭiśca vāruṇyāṃ rājakopaśca pāvane ।।

saumye putrasamṛddhissyā daiśānyāṃ sukhadaṃ bhavet ।
etānāṃ tu diśāṃ madhye praśastāṃ śuddhamṛttikām ।।

ācāryassādhanairyukto diśaṃ gatvā saśiṣyakaḥ ।
grāmadevālayādārādārāme atra manorame ।।

nadītaṭākatīre vā sīmāmanatilaṅghya ca ।
prārdhya bhūdevatāmantrai śśuddhe deśe mṛdaṃ haret ।।

vīśāmitau ca cakraṃ ca sthāpayetprāṅmukhān budhaḥ ।
prāṅmukhaścopalipyaiva vṛttākāraṃ samullikhet ।।

tatra sthānaṃ ca saṃprokṣya "dadhi krāvṇṇa'uccaran ।
bhūrūpaṃ tu likhitvaiva "bhūmirbhū'mneti ca bruvan ।।

ūrdhvavaktrāṃ ca śayitāmaiśānyāṃ nyastamaulikām ।
devīṃ mahīṃ tāmabhyarcya prokṣaṇaiḥ prokṣaṇaṃ caret ।।

ekādaśopacāraiśca mūrtimantraissamarcayet ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvātu medinyādi samuccaran ।।

khanitre śeṣamabhyarcya vastrādyaissamalaṅkṛte ।
lalāṭe sarvadoṣaghnaṃ bāhvorbahusukhapradam ।।

stanadvaye vayovṛddhirjaṭhare sarvasaṃpadaḥ ।
adhobhāge mṛdaṃ tasyā nāhareta kadācana ।।

evaṃ saṃkalpya manasā medinyādi tadā bruvan ।
"tvāṃ khanā'mīti mantreṇa vārāhaṃ manasā smaran ।।

ubhābhyāñcaiva hastābhyāṃ khanitreṇa khanedbudhaḥ ।
mahīṃ devīmanujñāpya khanitvā tālamātrakam ।।

apohyaiva ca tatsarvaṃ tadadhasthsāṃ mṛdaṃ haret ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ mantramuccārya tatrakāryaṃ samācaret ।।

pātramadhye susannyasya pūrvavacchirasinyaset ।
paścāddevīṃ samudvāsya cāpaṭaṃ tatra pūrayet ।।

śirasā dhārayitvātu purastāccakraśāntayoḥ ।
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā devālayamupāvrajet ।।

pūrvasminnuttare pārśve vāṃkurānarpayettadhā ।
cakrādīnabhiṣicyaiva havissamyaṅnivedya ca ।।

svesvesthāne tu saṃsthāpya paścādyāgaṃ samārabhet ।
alayābhimukhe vāpi dakṣiṇe vā manorame ।।

yamapāvakayormadhye pāvakāṃśe atha vā caret ।
aiśānyāṃ vātha vā kecitsomeśānāntare tathā ।।

kalpayedyāgaśālāṃ ca pratiṣṭhoktavidhānataḥ ।
vediṃ tanmadhyame paṅktau vedimānena kārayet ।।

pratiṣṭhādyardhamānaṃ vā ratnimātrodayaṃ kramāt ।
pañcāgnīn kalpayeddhīmānutsave cottame tathā ।।

tretāgnīn kalpayedvidvānmadhyame cotsavekramāt ।
adhamaṃ yadi cetsabhyaṃ kalpayetpūrvavatsudhīḥ ।।

tretāgnikalpanaṃ yatra pradhānaṃ gārhapatyakam ।
ubhayoranyayossabhyaṃ pradhānaṃ kalpayettathā ।।

bhūmiyajñeva sarvatra śodhayecca yathāvidhi ।
devaṃ devyau samādāya snānaśvabhre gurūttamaḥ ।।

"paraṃ raṃ'heti mantreṇa sthāpayecca viśeṣataḥ ।
nityasnānoktamārgeṇa snāpayitvā hariṃ param ।।

āsthāne viṣṭaraṃ nyasya tadūrdhve vastramāstaret ।
devaṃ devyau samādāya śvetavastrairvibhūṣya ca ।।

kuṇḍalāṃgadahārādibhūṣaṇairapi bhūṣayet ।
śvetamālyairalaṅkṛtya śvetagandhānulepanaiḥ ।।

pavitraṃ cottarīyañca gatvā devaṃ praṇamya ca ।
rājavaccopacārādīnācareddeśikottamaḥ, ।।

navakubhāropaṇam
pūrvoktavidhinā dhīmān nava kuṃbhān pragṛhyaca ।
"indraṃ naro na'ityuktvātantunā veṣṭayettathā ।।

vedyāmuparipūrvoktadhānyānyāstīrya mantravit ।
catussūtrairnavapadaṃ kṛtvā kuṃbhāṃśca vinyaset ।।

kuṃbhānadbhiḥ ppapūryaiva kuśakūrcākṣatādikān ।
maṅgalānyāyudhaṃ ratnaṃ pratikuṃbhaṃ pṛthak pṛthak ।।

gāyatṣā caiva nikṣivya madhyakuṃbhe viśeṣataḥ ।
dvyaṅgulena pramāṇena srugādīnyapi pūrvavat ।।

hānakenaiva kṛtvā tu viṣṇusūktena nikṣipet ।
āveṣṭya vastrayugmena sarvānapi pṛthak pṛthak ।।

vedyā madhastātpūrvetu vīśaṃ vai paścimāmukham ।
sannyasya dakṣiṇe paścāccakraṃ caivottarāmukham ।।

paṅktīśaṃ prāṅmukhaṃ paścātpaścime cottare atha vā ।
dakṣiṇābhimukhaṃ śāntaṃ sthaṇḍilopari sannyaset ।।

abhāve garuḍādīnāṃ sthāne tatra ca tatra ca ।
kuṃbhāntsannyasya tanmadhye dhyātvaivāvāhayetkramāt ।।

yāvattīrthāvasānaṃ syāttāvatkuṃbhetu pārṣadān ।
sāyaṃ prātarviśeṣeṇa pūjayedvidhivatsudhīḥ ।।

paścātsabhyāgnikuṇḍe tu vidhināghāra mācaret ।
uttarābhimukha stiṣṭhan kururvedyāstu dakṣiṇe ।।

prāṇāyāmaṃ tataḥkṛtvā pūrvavaddhyānamācaret ।
pradhānakuṃbhamadhye tu viṣṇuṃ devyau ca sānvayau ।।

dhruvādāvāhayenmantrī prāgādiṣu yathākramam ।
puruṣaṃ kapilaṃ satyaṃ yajñamacyutameva ca ।।

nārāyaṇaṃ cāniruddhaṃ tataḥ puṇyaṃ samarcayet ।
taṃ rukmavarṇaṃ raktāsyaṃ raktanetraṃ sukhodvaham ।।

kirīṭahārakeyūralaṃbayajñopavītinam ।
kaustubhodbhāsitoraskaṃ śrīvatsāṃkaṃ caturbhujam ।।

dakṣiṇenaikahastena bhaktānāmabhayapradam ।
vāmenāpyanyahastena svakaṭyāmavalaṃbitam ।।

parābhyāṃ tu karābhyāṃ tu śaṅkhacakradharaṃ param ।
śukapiñchāṃbaradharaṃ viṣṇuṃ praṇavarūpiṇam ।।

taptahāṭakasaṃkāśāṃ padmapatrāyatekṣaṇām ।
tisṛbhiḥpuṣpacūḍūbhirlalāṭopari śobhitām ।।

sapadmavāmahastāntāṃ kakṣyābaddhaghanastanīm ।
prasāritetarakarāṃ prasannendunibhānanām ।।

śrīvatsāṃkitabījāntāṃ phālgunecottarodbhavām ।
viṣṇordakṣiṇapārśvasthāṃ haṃsaniryākhyavāhinīm ।।

vāmabhāge mahīṃ śyāmāṃ sarvābharaṇabhūṣitām ।
vaiśākhe revatījātāṃ dadhatīṃ dakṣiṇe aṃbujam ।।

prasāritetarakarāṃ prasannendunibhānanām ।
mahācātakamārūḍhāṃ lakṣnīpūrvākṣarānvitām ।।

puruṣaḥ prāṅmukho acchābhaḥ pītavāsāścaturbhujaḥ ।
śaṅkhacakradharaśśrīmān sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।।

varado abhayadaḥ prācyāṃ śrībhūmisahito hariḥ ।
kapilaḥ prāṅmukho acchābho raktavastro aṣṭabāhuyuk ।।

dakṣiṇenaikahasteva bhaktānāmabhayapradaḥ ।
anyaiścakrāsihalabhṛtsarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।।

vāmenāpyanyahastena svakaṭyāmavalaṃbya ca ।
anyaiśsaṃkhadhanurdaṇḍadharassuṃdara vigrahaḥ ।।

āgneyyāṃ diśi gāyatṣā sāvitṣā ca yuto hariḥ ।
satyoyāmyamukhaśśrīmānañjanābhaścaturbhujaḥ ।।

śaṅkhacakradharasyaumyassarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।
varado abhayadassādhūraktavāsā mahāhanuḥ ।।

devībhyāṃ dhṛtipauṣṇībhyāṃ yuto yāmyadiśi prabhuḥ ।
yajñaḥ paścimadigvaktrastaptacāmīkaraprabhaḥ ।।

saptahastaścatuśśruṅgo raktavāsā dviśīrṣakaḥ ।
śaṅkhacakrājyapātrasruksruvānupabhṛtaṃ juhūm ।।

bibhrattripādo nairṛtyāṃ devassvāhāsvadhāyutaḥ ।
acyutaḥ paścimāśāsyaḥ kanakābhaścaturbhujaḥ ।।

śaṅkhacakradharaśśrīmān sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।
varado abhayadassākṣī sarvakarmaphalapradaḥ ।।

yuktaḥpavitrīkṣoṇībhyāṃ pratīcyāṃ śyāmalāṃbaraḥ ।
nārāyaṇaḥ paścimāsyassphaṭikābhaścaturbhujaḥ ।।

śaṅkhacakradharaśśrīmān sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।
varado abhayadaśśyāmāṃbaraśśrīvatsacihnitaḥ ।।

saṃyutaḥ kamalelābhyāṃ vāyavyāṃ jagatāṃ patiḥ ।
aniruddha udīcyāsyaḥ pravālābhaścaturbhujaḥ ।।

anantotsaṃga āsīnaḥ puṣpāṃbaradharo hariḥ ।
śaṅkhacakradharaśśrīmān sarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।।

dadhatsvadakṣiṇe vāme pramodādāyinīṃ mahīm ।
varado abhayado deva udīcyāṃ sarvasiddhidaḥ ।।

puṇyaḥprāgānanaśśrīmāṃ staruṇādityasannibhaḥ ।
śrīvatsavakṣā nityaśrīssarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।।

caturbhujaśśaṅkhacakravaradābhayacihnitaḥ ।
śvetavastrottarīyopavītādyaissamalaṅkṛtaḥ ।।

indirādharaṇīnāthar iśānyāṃ puṇyapūruṣaḥ ।
etān devān samāvāhya samabhyarcyāṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।।

vīśānasāyipaṅktīśaśāntān dikṣvarcayetkramāt ।
sāyaṃ prātarvinā kuṃbhairdevaṃ vīśāmitaissaha ।।

vedyāmeva pratiṣṭhāpya pūjayediti ke ca na ।
hotrapraśaṃsanam
hotā paścātpradhānāgnau hautraśaṃsanamācaret ।।

pratiṣṭhoktakrameṇaiva tadālayagatān surān ।
avāhya tatkrameṇaiva nirupyājyāhutīryajet ।।

pariṣicya pāvakaṃ paścādvaiṣṇavaṃ juhuyātkramāt ।
vedyāntu paścime vātha vāyavyāṃ vā viśeṣataḥ ।।

sthiṇḍilaṃ kalpayitvātra cāstaredaṇḍajādikān ।
yajamānasamāyukto gururdevaṃ praṇamya ca ।।

kusumāñjali mutsṛjya "pratadviṣṇuṃ'riti bruvan ।
devībhyāṃ saha deveśamādāya sthaṇḍilopari ।।

prāṅmukhaṃ caiva saṃsthāpya pūjayedaṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।
utsavapratimābhāve snāpane vā viśeṣataḥ ।।

snapanasyāvyabhāve tu kautuke cācarettu vā ।
kautuke yadi ceddevyau naivādāya tathā caret ।।

nādarennityavaikalyaṃ visargāvāhane tathā ।
ācaredutsavaṃ vidvānnityārcāntu yathākramam ।।

kuryāccennityavaikalyaṃ sarvanāśo bhaveddhruvam ।
snāpayedyadi cedvidvān madhyame cotsavasya tu ।।

snapane yadi saṃprāpte kautuke snapanaṃ caret ।
snāpanapratimābhāve snapanaṃ yadi cotsave ।।

saṃprāste snapane cātra kautuke cotsavaṃ vinā ।
acaredeva sāṃkaryaṃ nācaredubhayorapi ।।

utsave vartamāne tu kautuke snapanaṃ yadi ।
saṃbhaveduktakāle tu karmaṇī dve samācaret ।।

purāpravṛttakārye tu doṣo nānena saṃbhavet ।
kātuke cedyathai kāgnau bahukarmavadācaret ।।

gṛhe tretāgni vannityaṃ praṇīyāropaṇaṃ vinā ।
snāpanotsavabhede tu kautukena dinaṃ dinam ।।

arohaṇaṃ yadi bhaveddruve tatkarma pūrvataḥ ।
āvāhya karmamāmante tathā sāye visarjayet ।।

pātra rāvāhanaṃ nityamarcanādau viśeṣataḥ ।
visargaṃ sāyamarcānte kautuke tu yathā tathā ।।

tathaivautsavadīkṣānte samāvāhya dhruvātsudhīḥ ।
visargaṃ nācarenmadhye dīkṣāntetu samācaret ।।

arcanānte viśeṣeṇa puṇyāhamapi vācayet ।
hemapātre tu sauvarṇaṃ kautukaṃ taṇḍulopari ।।

sannyasya pūrvavaddhīmān bandhayeddakṣiṇekare ।
kuṃbhān devyauca cakrādīn samābaddhya samarcayet ।।

pariṣicya pāvakaṃ paścādvaiṣmavaṃ viṣmusūktakam ।
juhuyātpauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ śrībhūsūkta samanvitam ।।

dinasaṃdhyādhidaivatyaṃ tithivārarkṣadaivatam ।
tathā māsādhidai vatyamabdadai vatyameva ca ।।

tadālayagatānāṃ ca juhuyānmūrtibhiḥ kramāt ।
vyāhṛtyantaṃ pradhāne syāttata āhavanīyake ।।
nṛsūktaṃ dakṣiṇāgnau ca vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।।
avasathye mahīsūktamekākṣaramato yajet ।
juhuyātpaiṇḍarīkāgnā "vato devādi' vaiṣṇavam ।।

viṣṇusūktaṃ puruṣasūktaṃ "yaddevādi'samanvitam ।
pāramātmika mantrāṃśca brāhmamaindraṃ ca vāruṇam ।।

juhuyādviṣṇugāyatṣā śvetābjaṃ ca ghṛtāplutam ।
aṣṭottaraśataṃ caiva sarvadoṣopaśāntaye ।।

ekāgnimatha vādhāya juhuyādadhamādhamam ।
sabhya homaṃ ca pūrvoktaṃ vaiṣṇavādi vidhānataḥ ।।

athotsavādhidaivatyaṃ viśeṣeṇa pravakṣyate ।
brāhmamārṣaṃ tathā raudramaindraṃ saumyaṃ ca vaiṣmavam ।।

sarvadaivatyayāmye ca vāruṇaṃ ca navāhnike ।
āgneyaṃ prājāpatyaṃ ca kauberaṃ vaighnameva ca ।।

śrīdaivatyaṃ ca kaumāramādityaṃ raudrameva ca ।
daurgamaindraṃ tathā yāmyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ skāngameva car ।।

iśānyaṃ saumyamityetattithidaivatyamucyate ।
tattaddvāre tu juhuyānmatrairdvārādhipocitaiḥ ।।

tathā nakṣatradaivatyaṃ juhuyādvidhinā budhaḥ ।
trisaṃdhiṣu hunedaindraṃ sauraṃ bārhaspataṃ kramāt ।।

māsarkṣādhipadaivatyaṃ māsadaivatyamucyate ।
yāmyaṃ ca vaiṣṇavaṃ saumyaṃ brāhmaṃ bārhaspataṃ tathā ।।

saumyamaindraṃ vāruṇaṃ ca śeṣāgnyādityabhautikam ।
mārutaṃ bhṛgudaivatyaṃ vāruṇaṃ vaighnameva ca ।।

raudraṃ kauberakaṃ tvāṣṭraṃ maitraṃ kaumārameva ca ।
sāvitrīṃ śrīdaivatyaṃ caiva gaurīdaivatyameva ca ।।

ādityaṃ paitṛkaṃ caivāditi daivatyameva ca ।
yogadaivatyametatkyājjuhuyādvidhinā budhaḥ ।।

aindraṃ ca prājāpatyaṃ ca maitramāryamaṇaṃ tathā ।
bhūta śrīyāmyadaivatyaṃ bhārgavaṃ vṛṣadaivatam ।।

kauberaṃ vāyudaivatyaṃ juhuyātkaraṇeṣu vai ।
devebhyaḥ pitṛbhyaśceti pakṣayośśuklakṛṣṇayoḥ ।।

sauraṃ cāndraṃ ca juhuyātkramādayanayordvayoḥ ।
"madhuśca mādhava'śceti juhuyādṛtuṣu kramāt ।।

viṣṇuḥ prajāpatiśśūlī vighneśassapta carṣayaḥ ।
aṣṭau lokādhipāḥ pañca bhūtā viśvaṃbharādayaḥ ।।

vasavo aṣṭau ca rohiṇyassapta śrīścaṇḍikā guhaḥ ।
sūryassomaścirañjīvī kāśīvīśapurardarāḥ ।।

cakraśśānto gururbhaumabudhaśukraśanaiścarāḥ ।
haviḥpālo hyanastaśca gaṅgā jyeṣṭhā ca mātaraḥ ।।

prabhavādi kramādete vijñeyā vatsarādhipāḥ ।
tathotsavādhidaivatyaṃ tithivārarkṣadaivatam ।।

caturdaivatyamātrantu juhuyāditi ke ca na ।
palāśabilvaśāmīlanya grothoduṃbarāstathā ।।

aśvaddhakhadirapla kṣabrahmavṛkṣāḥ kramādime ।
samidhāṃ grāhya vṛkṣāntu parṇamaśvadthameva vā ।।

padmaṃ ca bilvapatraṃ ca karavīraṃ kumudaṃ tathā ।
nandyāvartaṃ ca tulasī tathaiva sthalapaṅkajam ।।

viṣṇukrāntāravinde tu puṣpāṇyetānyanukramāt ।
alābhe tulasīṃ vātha karavīraṃ ca paṅkajam ।।

mudgaṃ niṣpāvakaṃ caiva kuluddhaṃ māṣayeva ca ।
tilānapūpān lājāṃśca yavān saktūn yathākramam ।।

balidravyāṇi coktāni sarvābhāve tu maudgikam ।
evameva vidhānena dvikālaṃ homamācaret ।।

prātassaṃdhyāvasānetu sāyamarcāvasānake ।
homaṃ kṛtvā baliṃ dadyāddvikālaṃ cotsavaṃ caret ।।

utsavabhramaṇaṃ vakṣye devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ।
balinirvāpaṇānte tu sāyaṃ prātarviśeṣataḥ ।।

devadevamalaṅkṛtya vastrādyairbhūṣaṇaiśśubhaiḥ ।
sugandhipuṣpamālābhirgandhairapi manoharaiḥ ।।

rathe vā śibikāyāṃ vā vīśaskandhe api vā tathā ।
gajāśvāṃdolikādau vā vāhane samalaṅkṛte ।।

"ahameveda'mantreṇa devamāropya niścalam ।
aṣṭopacārairabhyarcya lājāpūpādikāṃs tathā ।।

saṃkkṛtān guḍasaṃmiśrān nivedya mukhavāsakam ।
datvā vādyaissamāyuktaṃ sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam ।।

dāsībhirvādakaiśyaiva nṛttageyasamanvitaiḥ ।
brāhmaṇairvedavidbhiśca samāyuktaṃ śanaiśsanaiḥ ।।

dhvajaiścatrairātapatraistoraṇaiśca tathaiva ca ।
saṃbhṛtaiḥ saṃyutaṃ cānyaissarvaiśśṛṅgāralakṣmabhiḥ ।।

vālavyajanahastābhirdāsībhiḥ pārśvayordvayoḥ ।
vījyamānaṃ viśeṣeṇa tathā bhaktavarairapi ।।

vāhaye yurdvijā devaṃ brāhmaṇā vedapāragāḥ ।
dīpairudagrairbahubhiḥ pariṣiktairghṛtādinā ।।

parassahasraissarvatra dīpayecca śatāvaraiḥ ।
vipraistrayīmadhīyānair japastutiparāyaṇaiḥ ।।

nṛtyatā gāyatā māpi gāṇikyena susevitam ।
vīṇādivādibhiścaiva vandibhiśca tathā paraiḥ ।।

ṣaḍjādigītanipuṇair vādyavādakakovidaiḥ ।
gadyaṃ padyaṃ tathā miśraṃ pathadbhistsotramujjvalam ।।

vai taṇḍikais tathā jalpairnipuṇairvādaśikṣitaiḥ ।
tathā tattvakathāniṣṭhaiḥ padārdhajñaiśca tārkikaiḥ ।।

mīmāṃsakairyājñikaiśca chāndasaissāṃkhyakovidaiḥ ।
yogajñaiśca purāṇajñaiśśābdikais tattvavedibhiḥ ।।

mauhūrtikaiśca gaṇaśaḥparasparajīgīṣubhiḥ ।
tattacchāstrokamārgeṇa prameyaṃ ca bahusthitam ।।

uccairbruvāṇairvidvadbhiḥ pañcakālaparāyaṇaiḥ ।
vāsudevasya māhātmyaṃ kathayadbhiścasāttvikaiḥ ।।

śāstreṣu naipuṇaṃ sarvaṃ pradarśayitumudyataiḥ ।
devasya purataḥpṛṣṭhe pārśvataścasthitairjanaiḥ ।।

senayā sarvato dikṣu caturaṅgabalāḍhyayā ।
devasya pārśvayoḥ pūrde lākṣārañjitamaskaraiḥ ।।

yatrairdārumayaiścitraiḥ pakṣyākārairitastataḥ ।
devatākṛtiyantraiśca tathā yantrairgajādibhiḥ ।।

niṣādibhissamārūḍhais strībhiśca bharatoditaiḥ ।
mārgairbahuvidhairnṛttaṃ darśayantībhiradbhutam ।।

lekhāyantraistsriyārūḍhairyantrairanyaistathā vithaiḥ ।
gatāgatāni kurvāṇair anuyātaṃ samākulaiḥ ।।

śanairnayejjagannāthaṃ yathāśakti samanvitaiḥ ।
ārabhyāvaraṇādādyādeṣā parivṛtirbhavet ।।

devena sārthamācāryo yānamāruhya tatra tu ।
rakṣārthaṃ devadevasya dhyāyannupaviśeddharim ।।

arcakaśca tathāsīnassamyagarcanamācaret ।
ārohaṇe gajendrasya devadevaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

vastrābharaṇapuṣbādyairalaṅkṛtya yathārhakam ।
deveśaṃ pūrvamāropya hastenādāyacāṃkuśam ।।

niṣīdedgajapṛṣṭhe tu deśikassvayamatvaraḥ ।
arcakaśchatramādāya tathā devasya dhārayet ।।

toyadhārāṃ puraskṛtya kuryādbhramaṇamācarāt ।
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kuryādbaliryena padhā kṛtaḥ ।।

tatkāle devamāyāntaṃ bhaktā bhāgavatā janāḥ ।
spagṛhaprāṃgaṇe caiva pratyudthāya punaḥpunaḥ ।।

praṇamya copahārāṃśca dadyurbahuvidhān bahūn ।
patraṃ puṣpaṃ phalaṃ pūgaṃ nāgavallīdalānyapi ।।

dakṣiṇāṃ ca viśeṣeṇa yathāśakti yathāruci ।
nīrājanādi kuryuśca bālavṛddhāturāstadā ।।

tapobhirbahubhirgamye svayameva parātpare ।
bhaktānukaṃpayā deve spagṛhadvāramāgate ।।

ko na nandati mūḍhātmā tasya kā niṣkṛtirbhavet ।
tatkāle cārpitaṃ dravyaṃ yadapakvaṃ pragṛhya ca ।।

āmantraṃ tu nivedyaiva bhagavatpriyamācaret ।
upahāreṣu tatrārdhaṃ gṛhṇīyādbhāgamarcakaḥ ।।

nāgavallīdalaṃ puṣpaṃ kramukaṃ dakṣiṇādikam ।
sarvamarcakasarvasvaṃ gṛhṇīyādarcakassvayam ।।

tatkāle bhaktinamrebhyassaṃprāptebhyaśca sannidhim ।
bhagadatpādukāṃ dadyācchirasi śraddhayā guruḥ ।।

śirasā dhāraṇe martyaisspṛṣṭidoṣo na vidyate ।
na nayetpādukāṃ viṣṇordūrīkṛtya tu sannidhim ।।

na gṛhadvārasīmāntaṃ nayettāṃ gṛhiṇāṃ guruḥ ।
iṣṭaṃ rājagṛhe strībhiḥ pādukādhāraṇaṃ yadi ।।

dehalīmanatikramya neyāttāṃ dīpikānvitām ।
tadā dīpaistathānyaiśca rājārhaiśca paricchadaiḥ ।।

neyā syātpādukā viṣṇoḥ praṇidhissā yato hareḥ ।
tassannidhimatikramya pūjakastu na jātu cit ।।

ādānāyopahārāṇāṃ prayāyādgṛhiṇāṃ gṛhān ।
nāpi kāryāntarāsaktaḥ pañcahastānati kramet ।।

eṣa śreṣṭhopacārassyādyatassammānyate hariḥ ।
evaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ nītvā nivartetālayaṃ prati ।।

gopurāgretu deveśaṃ kṛtvā devonmukhaṃ kramāt ।
arghyapādyādinābhyarcya nivedya pṛthukādikam ।।

dhāmapradakṣiṇaṃ nītvā punarāviśya cālayam ।
avaropya ca deveśaṃ sthāpya cāsthānamaṇḍape ।।

pādyamācamanaṃ datvā mukhavāsaṃ pradāya ca ।
kautukaṃ tu visṛjyaiva śuddhodaissnāpayetprabhum ।।

vimṛjya plotavastreṇa samalaṅkṛtya pūrvavat ।
kautukaṃ punarābaddhya haviḥpaścānnivedayet ।।

kuryādrājopacārāṇi sa hi rājā jagatprabhuḥ ।
vinodaṃ kārayeccaiva nṛttagītādibhirbahu ।।

tataḥ praṇamya deveśaṃ pūrvasthāne niveśayet ।
prathame ahani sāyetu kartavyamidamīritam ।।

dvitīyāhaḥprabhṛtyeva sāyaṃ prātaśca nityaśaḥ ।
nityārcanānte dviguṇamarcayecca nivedayet ।।

kuṃbhadevān samārādhya dhvajadevārcanaṃ caret ।
homaṃ baliṃ ca datvātu kārayedutsavaṃ tathā ।।

tṛtīye pañcaye avāhni prātassyādgaruḍotsavaḥ ।
ṣaṣṭhe ahani tu madhyāhne devībhyāṃ sahitaṃ harim ।।

pīṭhamadhye samāropya samabhyarcyāṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।
jalakuṅkumamādāya kārayedutsavaṃ tathā ।।

navavastrādikaṃ datvā pṛthukāni nivedya ca ।
datvā tāṃbūlamācāmamarcayedrājavatprabhum ।।

saptame prātararcānte kuryātsaptarṣipūjanam ।
vṛṇuyādṛtvijassaptatadācāryapurassarān ।।

dhyātvā saptarṣivattāṃstu svarṇaṃ gāmājyameva ca ।
taṇḍulodakakuṃbhādīn dūrvāgraṃ kramukaṃ tathā ।।

dadyātprabhūtaṃ tebhyantu brāhmaṇebhyaḥ pṛthak pṛthak ।
tatsāyaṃ ca viśeṣeṇa kṛṣṇagandhānulepanam ।।

sadyaḥ pratisaraṃ baddhvā devāgre sthaṇḍilaṃ caret ।
kṛṣṇāguru samādāya sarvavādyasamāyutam ।।

grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā sthaṇḍilopari vinyaset ।
puṇyāhaṃ vidhivatkṛtvā śriyamāvāhya tatra ca ।।

saṃskṛtya vidhivadgandhān samabhyarcya hariṃ tataḥ ।
"gandhadvāre'ti mantreṇa sarvāṅgaṃ lepayedguruḥ ।।

devyādīnāṃ tathā kuryāttattanmantrairyathāvidhi ।
taccheṣagandhaṃ bhaktyaiva bhaktebhyo dāpayedguruḥ ।।

tadgandhadhāraṇānnṝṇāṃ bhadeyussarvasaṃpadaḥ ।
sāyamarcāvasāne tu rathayātrāṃ samācaret ।।

aṣṭame divase prāpte samāpte prātarutsave ।
alaṅkṛtya tu deveśaṃ mṛgayotsavamācaret ।।

madhyāhne devadevasya jalakrīḍotsavaṃ caret ।
prapāṃ kṛtvā vidhānena nadyādīnāṃ taṭe budhaḥ ।।

vitānādyairalaṅkṛtya jalakrīḍārthamaṇṭapam ।
biṃbādhyardhāyatāmardhavistārāṃ biṃbadaghnikām ।।

jaladroṇīmathācchidrāṃ nyasya lohamayīṃ ghanām ।
nādeyādbhissamāpūrva "dhārāsvi'ti ca mantrataḥ ।।

elācandanakarbūraiḥ kuṅkumenādhivāsayet ।
kalhāraketakīpuṣpairuśīrāgurubhistathā ।।

āstīrya navavastrāṇi "vedāha'miti mantrataḥ ।
"puṇyatīrthaṃ śivaṃ puṇyaṃ devāvāsa'miti bruvan ।।

adhidevaṃ samāvāhya vigrahairaṣṭabhiryajet ।
maṇḍape paścimārdhe tu viṣṭare sottarachade ।।

devadevaṃ samāsthāpya śakunasūktaṃ samuccaran ।
navavastrottarīyādyairalaṅkṛtya manoharam ।।

pādyādibhissamabhyarcya sthāpagaissahito guruḥ ।
"bhūḥ prapadye'ti mantreṇa devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।।

"paraṃ raṃhe'ti mantreṇa devamādāyacādarāt ।
"pratadviṣṇustsavata'iti jaladroṇyāṃ niveśya ca ।।

indrādī śca jayādīśca taṇḍulaiḥkj ptamaṇḍale ।
samāvāhya samabhyarcyejjaladroṇyabhito guruḥ ।।

"apo hi ṣṭhā'di mantrāṃ strīnanuvākāntsamuccaran ।
"idamāpaśśi'vetyuktvā "āpo vā ida'muccaran ।।

abhimantṣa jaladroṇyāṃ devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।
pauruṣaṃ sūktamuccārya viṣṇusūktaṃ ca vaiṣṇavam ।।

"iṣe tvorje'tvādi japan "bhūrānilaya' ityapi ।
maṅjayitvā jaladroṇyāṃ devaṃ prākchirasaṃ harim ।।

adhivāsyatu yāmārdhaṃ yāmadvayamathāpi vā ।
"paraṃ raṃ'heti mantreṇa tata uddhṛtyavai punaḥ ।।

alaṅkṛtya ca vastrādyairyathārhaṃ paripūjya ca ।
yānamāropya deveśaṃ grāmamālayameva vā ।।

pradakṣiṇaṃ kramānnītvā sarvālaṅkālasaṃyutam ।
grāmavīthyāmupahṛtamupahālamagṛhya ca ।।

punarālayamāviśya saṃsthāpyāsthānamaṇḍape ।
sugandhitailenābhyajya devaṃ saṃsnāpya pūrvavat ।।

jīvasthāne samāsthāpya samabhyarcya nivedayet ।
tadrātrāvutsavāntetu devaṃ devīyutaṃ harim ।।

pratiṣṭhoktavidhānena baddhvā pratisaraṃ tataḥ ।
adhivāsavidhānena śayane śāyayedguruḥ ।।

prabhāte devasutthāpya pādyādyarghyāntamarcayet ।
tasmin tīrthadine prātarhemādyaṃ prātarutsavam ।।

kṛtvā havirvinā devamabhyarcyāsthānamaṇḍape ।
pramukhe garuḍaṃ paścāddakṣiṇe cakrameva ca ।।

amitaṃ cottaredhīmān dhānyapīṭhopari nyaset ।
nityapūjāṃ havirdānaṃ dhruvabere samācaret ।।

pūrvālaṅkṛtavastrādīn visṛjyaiva prayatnataḥ ।
anyavastrāṇicācchādya yathārhaṃ bhūṣya bhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।

aṣṭopacārairabhyarcya devaṃ cakrādidevatāḥ ।
vrīhibhisthsaṃḍilaṃ kṛtvā dvihastāyatavistṛtam ।।

ulūkhalaṃ ca musalaṃ sthāpya vastreṇa saṃyutam ।
tayorīśau krameṇaiva brahyeśāvarcayedbudhaḥ ।।

pātre haridrāṃ saṃgṛhya sinīvālīmathār'cya ca ।
ulūkhale haridrāṃ ca tanmantreṇa vinikṣipet ।।

gṛhītvā vaiṣṇavairmantrairācāryo musalaṃ tathā ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ samuccārya kiñcittadavaghātayet ।।

bhaktairvā devadāsībhiścūrṇīkṛtya viśeṣataḥ ।
ekasminvādvayorvātha triṣu vā kalaśeṣuvai ।।

gandhoṣitaṃ ca vādailamāḍhakaṃ parigṛhyaca ।
pidhāya ca pidhānaiśca sthaṇḍilopari vinyaset ।।

ācchādya navavastreṇa somaṃ taile samarcayet ।
sinīvālīṃ ca taccūrṇe cakrādīṃśca prapūjayet ।।

devamabhyarcya puṇyāhaṃ vācayanvaiṣṇavaṃ guruḥ ।
saṃsrāvya mūrthni tattailaṃ "vedāha'miti mantrataḥ ।।

hāridracūrṇaissaṃsnāpya cakrādīn snāpayettataḥ ।
tacchiṣṭaṃ dhārayan bhaktassarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।।

atha yāne samāropya devaṃ cakrādibhissaha ।
cūrṇotsavamimaṃ kṛtvā tīrthotsavamathācaret ।।

devakhātaṃ yadi phavettīrthaṃ tatra praśasyate ।
nadyāditīre saṃsthāpya devībhyāṃ saha vā vinā ।।

cakrādīn pūrvavat sthāpya pramukhe sthaṇḍilaṃ caret ।
dravyeṇāpūrva kalaśān gāyatrīmantramuccaran ।।

madhye siddhārthakaṃ nyasya prācyāṃ syādakṣatodakam ।
dakṣiṇe gandhatoyaṃ syātpaścime tu kuśodakam ।।

japyodakaṃ cottare syādvidiśāsu ca madhyataḥ ।
upasnānāni vinyasya kramāttadadhipān guruḥ ।।

ādityānapsarasaśca kāśyapaṃ ca guruṃ tathā ।
ṛtūṃśca marutaścaiva munīṃ stakṣakameva ca ।।
