mantrānvidyādharāṃścaiva krameṇāvāhyacārcayet ।
"pūtasta'syeti mantreṇa "imā oṣadhaya'ityapi ।।

"abhi tvā śūra'"catvāri'"pūtastanye'ticakramāt ।
kalaśaiḥ pañcabhissnāpyatattaddravyāntare kramāt ।।

"vārīścatasra'ityuktvā copasnānaṃ samācaret ।
śiṣṭābhiḥ kalaśādbhiśca cakrādhīnabhiṣicya ca ।।

praviśya tu jalaṃ tatra varuṇaṃ cārcayetkramāt ।
hastābhyāṃ cakramādāya devaṃ bhaktaissamanvitaḥ ।।

ācāryaḥ prathamaṃ tīrthe cakraṃ ssṛṣṭyāvagāhayet ।
nābhidaghnajale tatra jalamadhye tu susthitaḥ ।।

cakraṃ devaṃ hṛdi sthāpya hastābhyāṃ dhārayan dṛḍham ।
"ye te śataṃ' samuccārya prāṅmukho vāpyudaṅmukhaḥ ।।

nimajjayettadā cakraṃ sarvavādyayutaṃ guruḥ ।
janāssarve ca tattīrthe snātvā vigatakalmaṣāḥ ।।

bhaveyuraśvamedhasya phalaṃ ca samavāpnuyuḥ ।
tatastīre pratiṣṭhāpya viṣṭare cakramuttame ।।

kuryādavabhṛthasnānaṃ śuddhasnānoktamārgataḥ ।
tato visṛjya vastrādīn devaṃ cānyairvibhūṣya ca ।।

tatraiva nasasnāṃbhārān saṃbhṛtya vidhinā guruḥ ।
devībhyāṃ saha deveśaṃ snāpayetpūrvavatprabhum ।।

alaṅkṛtya viśeṣeṇa kuryādarghyāntapūjanam ।
paścāddevaṃ samādāya sarvālaṅkārasaṃyutam ।।

śākunaṃ sūktamuccārya nītvā grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇam ।
devālayaṃ praviśyāthasthāpya cāsthānamaṇḍape ।।

pādyādibhissamabhyarcya vedānadhyāpayetkramāt ।
muhuḥpuṣpāṃjaliṃ datvājīvasthāne niveśayet ।।

cakrādīnapi cādāya tattatthsāne niveśya ca ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvātu prokṣaṇeḥ prokṣaṇaṃ caret ।।

nityapūjaṃ samāpyaiva havirdadyādviśeṣataḥ ।
yāgaśālāṃ samāsādya hutvāgniṣu ca vaiṣṇavam ।।

kuṃbhasthāṃ śaktimādāya dhruvabere avaropayet ।
antahomaṃ ca hutvāgniṃ nityakuṇḍepraṇīya ca ।।

tadrātrau nityahomānte baliṃ datvā ca pūrvavat ।
paścāccakraṃ vinā dadyādbaliṃ śuddhānna kalpitam ।।

pūrvoktenaiva mārgeṇa sarvatra balimācaret ।
caityasthāne prapāyāṃ tu utyāne vṛkṣamūlake ।।

taṭāke nirjhare kūpavāpīvalmīkapārśvake ।
śmaśāne anyatra devāgre vīthyanteṣu ca nikṣipaset ।।

punarālayamāviśya snātvā cāpyagnisannidhau ।
dhvajamūlaṃ samāsādya sarvavādya samāyutam ।।

dhvacāvarohaṇaṃ kuryāddhvajamatraṃ samuccaran ।
taddhvajaṃ tu samādāya prādakṣiṇyakrameṇa vai ।।

parītya mandiraṃ paścātpraviśyābhyantaraṃ punaḥ ।
devasya pādamūle tu nyasya puṣpāñjaliṃ dadet ।।

kṣamāmantraṃ samuccārya daṇḍavatpraṇamedbhuvi ।
phalaśrutiḥ
evaṃ yaḥ kurute bhaktvā viṣṇorutsavamādarāt ।।

sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā sarvān kāmānavāpya ca ।
ante vimānamāruhya viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।

puṣpayāgaḥ ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi puṣpayāgaṃ sukhāvaham ।
dvitīyadivase tīrthātpuṣpayāgaṃ samācaret ।।

śāntidaṃ puṣṭidaṃ ceti kāmyadaṃ ca tridhā bhavet ।
prātarmadhyāhnāparāhṇāḥ kramātkālāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।।

nyūnaṃ vāpyadhikaṃ caitaddoṣopaśamanāya vai ।
āsthānamaṇḍape vātha snapanālaya eva vā ।।

caturdiśaṃ caturhastaṃ gopayenopalipya ca ।
pañcaviṃśatpadaṃ kṛtvā ṣaṭsūtraiḥ prāgudgagataiḥ ।।

madhye nanapade padmaṃ sāṣṭapatraṃ sakarṇikam ।
ratnadhānyādikairvāpi taṇḍulairvrīhibhistilaiḥ ।।

bahisteṣu padeṣvagre vīśamekatra pūjayet ।
dakṣiṇe cakramabhyarcya paṅktīśaṃ paścime tathā ।।

udīcyāṃ śāntamabhyarcya śeṣeṣu ca padeṣu vai ।
pūjādravyāṇi saṃbhṛtya pratyekaṃ vinyasedbudhaḥ ।।

daleṣvaṣṭasu padmasya suvarṇaśakalopari ।
lokapālāntsamabhyarcya vastropari yathādiśam ।।

niṣkatrayasuvarṇeva kalpite karṇikopari ।
ādityamaṇḍalaṃ tatra rājate candramaṇḍalam ।।

tasmin suvarṇarūpe tu vahni maṇḍalamarcayet ।
viṣṭaraṃ tatra saṃsthāpya tadantargatapaṅkaje ।।

tatra devaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya yāvaddivasamutsavam ।
tāvatkṛtvassamabhyarchya saptaviṃśativigrahaiḥ ।।

tatra pūjāvasānetu tattatpuṣpāñjaliṃ dadet ।
paṅkajaṃ tulasī bilvaṃ karavīramathotpalam ।।

nandyāvartaṃ ca kumudamapāmārgaṃ tathaiva ca ।
viṣṇukrāntaṃ ca dūrvāṃ cakramādetānyanukramāt ।।

evaṃ puṣpājaliṃ datvā ṛtvijassahatairguruḥ ।
nṛttairgeyaiścavādyaiśca caturvedastavairapi ।।

parātparataraṃ pāraṃ guhyādguhyataraṃ gurum ।
sarvavedārthasāraṃ taṃ dvādaśāṣyākṣaraṃ tathā ।।

japanto viṣṇugāyatrīṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tataḥ ।
dadyuḥ puṣpāñjali bhaktyā devadevasya pādayoḥ ।।

pañcāgniṣvatha vāgnīṃstrīn paiṇḍarīkamathāpi vā ।
devasya paritaḥ kuryāduttamādikrame kramāt ।।

uttame sabhyakuṇḍe tu madhye tvāhavanīyake ।
hautrapraśaṃsanaṃ kuryāttadālayagatāntsurān ।।

āvāhyājyaṃ nirūpyaiva tatkrameṇāhutīryajet ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca samyagghutvā viśeṣata ।।

tataścāhavanīyāgnau nṛsūktaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ yajet ।
dakṣiṇāgnau viṣṇusūktaṃ śrīsūktaṃ ca yajetkramāt ।।

juhuyādgārhapatyāgnau gāyatrīṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ tataḥ ।
āvasaddhye tu juhuyātsūktamekākṣarādikam ।।

ājyena samidhā tattaddhavirbhedaiśca hūyatām ।
etaduttamamuddiṣṭaṃ madhyamaṃ tu pravakṣyate ।।

yathālābhapramāṇena pūrvoktārdhena vā hareḥ ।
padmamaṇḍaladevānāṃ kārayetpratimādikam ।।

tattaddinārcanānte tu śuddhānnaṃ vā nivedya ca ।
sarvārcānte pañcahavirdadyādityāha pūrvajaḥ ।।

caturvedādighoṣaṃ ca caturdikṣu prakalpayet ।
abjahomaṃ krameṇaiva juhuyānmantra vittamaḥ ।।

puṣpanyāsakrameṇaiva sarvavidyeśvarāntakam ।
abhyarcya prathamaṃ paścātpaṣpayāgokta pūjanam ।।

kṛtvā yathālābhahavirbhakṣyāṇi vividhāni ca ।
nivedya mukhavāsānte parivārabaliṃ kṣipet ।।

ityevaṃ madhyame proktaṃ pravakṣyāmyadhame punaḥ ।
vinā diśādibhirbhedairhemaiśca pṛthagarcanaiḥ ।।

maṇḍale devamāropya pūjayitvā yadhāvidhi ।
havīṃṣi pañca coktāni nivedya ca tataḥ param ।।

dadyātpuṣpāṃjaliṃ mantraissamastadivasoditaiḥ ।
jānvantaṃ ca tathorvantaṃ kaṭyantaṃ ca samarcayet ।।

nābhyantaṃ ca stanāntaṃ ca bāhyastamiti cakramāt ।
grīvāntaṃ ca lalāṭāntaṃ maulyastamiti cakramāt ।।

tattatpūjāvasānetu havissamyaṅni vedayet ।
utsavājñātadoṣāṇāṃ prāyaścittamidaṃ smṛtam ।।

atassarvaprayatnena puṣpayāgaṃ samācaret ।
dvādaśārādhanam
kuryādyathoktavidhinā dvādaśārādhanaṃ tathā ।।

dadyādācāryapūrvebhyo dakṣiṇāṃ vidhivattataḥ ।
ekaviṃśatiniṣkantu dadyādācāryadakṣiṇām ।।

padārthināṃ ca sarveṣāṃ tadardhaṃ syātpṛthak pṛthak ।
gobhūmibhyāṃ viśeṣeṇa datvācāryaṃ prasādayet ।।

ācāryassuprasannātmā sarvāgniṣu yathākramam ।
antahomaṃ samāpyaiva devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।।

jīvasthāne pratiṣṭhāpya deveśaṃ samyagarcayet ।
brāhmaṇān bhojayeccaiva pradadyādbhūridakṣiṇām ।।

puṣpayāgotsavaḥ prokto devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ।
śāntikādividhāne tu kuryādaṅkurapūrvakam ।।

evaṃ yaḥkurute bhaktyāpuṣbayāgaṃ hareḥ priyam ।
sarvān kāmānavāpyaiva sarvaiśvaryamavāpya ca ।।

sarvān śatrūn vijitvaiva prajāpaśusamanvitaḥ ।
ante vimānamāruhya viṣṇusāyujyamāpnuyāt ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre pañcaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha ṣaḍviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha ṣaḍviṃśo adhyāyaḥ prāyaścittam

ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi bhūparīkṣādiniṣkṛtim ।
nyūne atirikte vyāghāte prāyaścittaṃ samācaret ।।

prāyodoṣassamuddiṣṭaścittaṃ tasya nivāraṇam ।
prāyaścittaṃ samākhyātaṃ kuryātkarmasamṛddhaye ।।

prāyaścittamakurvāṇassati doṣe vinaśyati ।
tasmātsarmaprayatnena kuryādyatnena niṣkṛtim ।।

ālayasya ca nirmāṇaṃ pūjādyāstatra yāḥkriyāḥ ।
asmācchāstrādatikramya niṣphalāḥprabhavantihi ।।

taddoṣaśamanāyaiva mahāśāntipurassaram ।
sarvāḥkriyāḥkrameṇaiva punaśśāstroktavaccaret ।।

yacchāstravidhimutsṛjya kriyate kāmakārataḥ ।
noktaṃ dadyātphalaṃ karma pratyutānarthadaṃ bhavet ।।

śilpaṃ ca jyotiṣaṃ vāstu tada'nye cāgamāḥ pare ।
tāvatā hi pramāṇaṃ syādyāvadetena nāntaram ।।

vaikhānasamidaṃ śāstra manyaśāstrānapekṣitam ।
praṇivāyābjajaḥ pūrvaṃ sarvaśāstrārthasaṃgraham ।।

mohādajñānato vāpi vicikitsāpadeṣu yaḥ ।
śāstrānta rānurodhena śāstrametadvimānayet ।।

sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।
tasmānniṣkāsya taṃ mūḍhaṃ śāstroktaṃ samyagācaret ।।

yadāgacchedbahirdvāraṃ bhūmiṃ samyak parīkṣitum ।
apatedantarāyaścetprāyaścittaṃ hunedbudhaḥ ।।

japecca vaiṣṇavaṃ vaighnaṃ śataśaḥ punarācaret ।
durdarśane japetsauraṃ hunetpūrvoktavadbudhaḥ ।।

durvākye tu śrute brāhmaṃ japetsārasvataṃ tathā ।
tatkāle kalahe caiva śoṇitaprasrave tathā ।।

agnidāhādike caiva vaiṣṇavaṃ saumyasaṃyutam ।
vaiṣvaksenaṃ tathā saudarśanaṃ gāruḍameva ca ।।

laukikāgnau huneddhyātvā devaṃ paścātsamācaret ।
bhūparīkṣaṇakāle tu yadi pāṃsukṣayo bhavet ।।

pūrṇāhutiṃ ca juhuyāttathā mindāhutī budhaḥ ।
parīkṣitā yadā bhūmiḥ pūrvamevānyavartmanā ।।

aupāsanāgnimādhāya vyāhṛtyantaṃ tu vaiṣṇavam ।
juhuyāddaśaśaḥ kuryāttataḥ karmāṇi mantrataḥ ।।

vṛṣabhasyāṅgahānautu karṣaṇe doṣaśāntaye ।
raudraṃ brāhmaṃ ca juhuyāttato anyaṃ vṛṣamāharet ।।

halādīnāṃ tu nirmāṇe yajñavṛkṣetaraiḥ kṛte ।
tathā pramāṇahīne ca juhuyādvaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।।

saumyaṃ caiva tathāgneyaṃ prājāpatyaṃ ca deśikaḥ ।
rajjabhede vāruṇaṃ ca sītābhedeśriyaṃ tathā ।।

dātrabhede tu juhuyājjyeṣṭhāmantraṃ vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
ṛṣibhede tu vāyavyaṃ kṣiṇīye vāsavaṃ tathā ।।

yuge nāgaṃ pratode tu yāmye vyāhṛtisaṃyutam ।
kapālāsthituṣāṅgārakeśavalmīkakharparāḥ ।।

dṛṣṭāḥkarṣaṇakāle cettadvyapohyāvilaṃbitam ।
abhyukṣya pañcagavyena saumyāgneyau hunetkramāt ।।

tatra cedarcane hīne śāntavīśānapāyinām ।
vaiṣṇapaṃ juhuyāttattaddaivatyaṃ cār'cayetpunaḥ ।।

bījāvāpanahīne tu juhuyādvaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।
saumyaṃ hutvā ca vāyavyaṃ punarbījāni vāpayet ।।

gavāṃ nivedane hīne vaiṣṇapaṃ cāmitaṃ hunet ।
gāruḍaṃ cakramantraṃ ca daśaśassusamāhitaḥ ।।

palālabhārānāhṛtya gogaṇebhyo nivedayet ।
padadevabalau hīne hunettanmantrapūrvakam ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmamaindraṃ ca yāmyaṃ vāruṇameva ca ।
kauberaṃ ca kramāddhutvā baliṃ tatra samarpayet ।।

brahmapadmakriyāhānau vaiṣṇavabrāhmavāruṇān ।
bhūdaivatyaṃ ca juhuyātpunaḥ kāryaṃ samācaret ।।

dikpharicchedahīne tu digdaivatyaṃ ca vaiṣṇavam ।
sauraṃ caiva punarhutvā kuryāddiksādhanaṃ tataḥ ।।

vimānārthaṃ yadā bhūmiḥkhanyate tatra saṃbhave ।
śarkarāśalyaloṣṭādau vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmameva ca ।।

pañcabhūtādhidai vatyaṃ vyāhṛtīśca hunetkramāt ।
hīne adhike vā māne tu śīlāyā iṣṭakasya vā ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca hutvā vidhivadācaret ।
viparyāse tu vinyāse digdaivatyaṃ ca vaiṣṇavam ।।

hutvā yathoktavatkṛtvājapedvedādikānmanūn ।
ratnanyāsavihīne tu hunettadadhipānmamān ।।

viṣṇusūktantato hutvā ratnanyāsaṃ samācaret ।
garbhanyāsavihīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

hutvā śrībhūmi daivatyaṃ garbhanyāsaṃ punaścaret ।
pramāṇahīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

sauraṃ saumyamathāgneyaṃ yajetkuryādvidhāvataḥ ।
nirmāṇakāle dravyāṇāṃ sthāpane saṃkareṇavai ।।

viparyāse ca saṃprāpte vaiṣṇavaṃ juhu yātkramāt ।
tattatthsānādhidaivatyaṃ hutvā vidhivadācaret ।।

anuktadeśe nyāse ca viṣṇusūktaṃ ca pauruṣam ।
hunecchrībhūmidaivatyaṃ tattatthsāne niveśayet ।।

apramāṇe śilāyāṃ vā tathā mūrdheṣṭakādiṣu ।
juhuyānniṣkṛtiṃ vidvānādyeṣṭakavidhānataḥ ।।

sthūpikīle tadādhāre pramāṇaparivarjite ।
alābhe coktadārūṇāṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ saumyapāvake ।।

bhūdaivatyaṃ ca hutvā tu vidhinā kālayedbudhaḥ ।
vimāne nirmite paścātsudhākarmaṇyakalpite ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca sūktaṃ pauruṣameva ca ।
hunecchrībhūmidaivatyaṃ vidhinā punarārabhet ।।

āgneyaṃ bhūmidaivatyaṃ hutvā kāryaṃ samācaret ।
hīne dhāmnaḥkavāṭādau dhātrādīn juhuyācca ṣaṭ ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ śrīmahīmantrān hutvā nirmāpayetpunaḥ ।
prākāre gopure hine doṣo bhūyānmahattaraḥ ।।

vaṃśahānirdviṣadvṛddhirarthanāśo mahadbhayam ।
śāntehine mahāpatsyātkulaṃ cotsīdati dhruvam ।।

bhūtapīṭhavihīne tu dhanadhānyāyuṣāṃ kṣayaḥ ।
kūpārāmahaviśśālapuṣpasaṃcayavāṭikāḥ ।।

snānapānīyaśālā ca tathaivāsthānamaṇḍapam ।
nṛttagītaprapāścaivaṃ maṇḍapādāvanirmite ।।

saṃpadyeta mahān doṣaḥ kṛtaṃ syādakṛtaṃ punaḥ ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena kārayecchaktito budhaḥ ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusuktaṃ ca pauruṣaṃ sūktameva ca ।
hutvā śrībhūmidaivatyaṃ tattaddaivatyameva ca ।।

yathoktaṃ tu prakurvīta vittaśāṭhyaṃna kārayet ।
prathameṣṭakāṃ samārabhya sthūpikīlāvasānake ।।

ānuktānāṃ ca doṣāṇāmiyaṃ syātsarvaniṣkṛtiḥ ।
ālayātpuratovātha dakṣiṇe vā manorame ।।

śucau deśe pratiṣṭhāpya padmāgnau juhuyātkramāt ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca pauruṣaṃ sūktameva ca ।।

hunecchrībhūmidai vatyamaṅga homaścahūyate ।
sthūpyādyupānaparyantavimānāṅgāni nāmataḥ ।।

"dadbhyassvā'hādi juhuyādbrāhmaṃ raudraṃ vināyakam ।
āgneyaṃ durgāsūktaṃ ca prājāpatyaṃ ca hāvayet ।।

samāpite vimāne tu dhanalobhādinā punaḥ ।
dhruvaberaṃ vinākṛtvā kautuke sthāpite yadi ।।

ābhicārikametatsyādrāja rāṣṭravināśanam ।
taddoṣaparihārārthaṃ mahāśāntiṃ tṣahaṃ caret ।।

vaiṣṇavāṃśca susaṃpūjya bhojayedbrāhmaṇān bahūn ।
"kṣama'sveti namaskṛtya devadevaṃ tu kautukam ।।

bālālaye pratiṣṭhāpya dhruvaberaṃ samācaret ।
dhruvārcāberamatha vā kṛtvā sthāpanamācaret ।।

vimānasya samāptau tu māsādūrdhvaṃ tu tatra vai ।
dhruvasthāpanahīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ juhuyāttataḥ ।।

viṣṇusūktaṃ tathā raudramaindramāgne yameva ca ।
vāruṇaṃ bārhaspatyaṃ ca śrībhūdaivatyameva ca ।।

śāntiṃ hutvā vidhānena dadyādācāryadakṣiṇām ।
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvaiva pūjayitvā tu vaiṣṇavān ।।

dhruvaberaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya vidhinā samyagarcayet ।
evaṃ māsadvaye atīte dviguṇaṃ niṣkṛtirbhavet ।।

māsatraye tu triguṇamevamāvatsaraṃ bhavet ।
saṃvatsare vyatīte tu doṣo bhūyānmahattaraḥ ।।

saptāhaṃ tu mahāśāntiṃ hutvābjāgnau vidhānataḥ ।
brāhmaṇān bhojayetpaścādvidhinā sarvamācaret ।।

saptavarṣeṣu saptāhaṃ prathamādikrameṇa vai ।
kecidicchanti munayassaptāhāntamidaṃ caret ।।

ata ūrdhvaṃ karṣaṇādi punassaṃskāramācaret ।
jalādhivāsanātpūrvamaṅgahānau dhruvasyatu ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca sūktaṃ pauruṣameva ca ।
hunecchrībhūmidaivatyaṃ "dadbhyassvāhā'dikaṃ tathā ।।

ācāryadakṣiṇāṃ dadyādberaṃ samyak parīkṣayet ।
saṃdhānayogyaṃ saṃdadhyātpunaḥ kāryaṃ samācaret ।।

śaktaścennūtanaṃ beramāhṛtya tu samācaret ।
śilāgrahaṇasaṃskāramakṛtvā śilpinā kṛtam ।।

beramādāya juhuyācchāntiṃ vaiṣṇavamantrataḥ ।
bhūmau pidhāya tadberaṃ vāstuhomaṃ samācaret ।।

paryagnipañcagavyābhyāṃ beraṃ saṃśodhya yatnataḥ ।
paritaḥ pūrvavadgatvā baliṃ devaṃ samarcya ca ।।

paścātsamantrakaṃ kṛtvāvidhinā sthāpayedbudhaḥ ।
jalādhivāsanādarvākthsāpanātpūrvameva ca ।।

devasya devyādīnāṃ vā aṅgahānirbhavedyadi ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca pauruṣaṃ sūktameva ca ।।

śrīsūktaṃ ca mahīsūktaṃ brāhmaṃ raudraṃ tathaiva ca ।
munyormantramathānyeṣāṃ tattanmatraṃ suhūyatām ।।

saṃdhānayogyaṃ saṃdadhyādayogyaṃ vidhivattyajet ।
saṃdhāya vānyaṃ cāhṛtya punasthsāpanamācaret ।।

sthāpite tu mahābere māsādūrdhvamasaṃskṛte ।
abjāgnau vaiṣṇavaṃ caiva viṣṇusūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

sūktaṃ tu pauruṣaṃ hutvā śrībhūdaivatyameva ca ।
brāhmaṃ raudraṃ pārṣadaṃ ca hutvā kāryaṃ samācaret ।।

māsadvaye tu dviguṇaṃ trimāse triguṇaṃ bhavet ।
saṃvatsarāntamevaṃ syāttadante sthāpayetpunaḥ ।।

atīte dvādaśe varṣe karṣaṇādi punaḥ kriyāḥ ।
śilāsaṃgrahaṇādyanyatkṛtvā sthāpanamācaret ।।

atha vakṣye karṣaṇādau punassaṃskāra mācaret ।
tṛṇagulmalatādīni śodhayetpūrvamālaye ।।

kuryācchileṣṭakādāruprakṣepaṇavidhiṃ kramāt ।
sudhāvarṇānulepādīn samāpya gurutvaraḥ ।।

alayasyottare kuryādvāstuhaumaṃ yathāvithi ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayedvidvān paryagniṃ caiva kārayet ।।

pañcagavyaissamabhyukṣya tatassaṃkarpya karṣaṇam ।
ālayābhimukhe kṛtvā vrīhibhisthsaṃḍilaṃ budhaḥ ।।

śāntānapāyinau vīśaṃ cābhyarca ca nivedayet ।
suvarṇena halaṃ kṛtvā garbhāgārādi sarvaśaḥ ।।

gṛhītvā dakṣiṇe haste mantrairviṣṇornukādibhiḥ ।
karṣayitvā yathoktāni bījānyāhṛtya deśikaḥ ।।

abhyukṣya somamabhyarcya viṣṇugāyatrimuccaran ।
abhimantṣa tato bījān "somaṃ rājāna'muccaran ।।

sarvatra vāpanaṃ kuryāddūrvādīṃścāharettṛṇān ।
āstīryopari tā ntṛrvān sūktaṃ gaudānikaṃ punaḥ ।।

uccārya gogaṇebhyastānnivedya ca pradāpayet ।
ālayaṃ tu susaṃśodhya brahmādīnāṃ dadedbalim ।।

droṇaistadardhairvā paktvā taṇḍulaissaghṛtaṃ carum ।
pūrvaṃ toyaṃ tataḥ puṣpaṃ baliṃ to yaṃ samarpayet ।।

punassaṃśodhayeddhāma śāntihomapurassaram ।
tattatsaṃskārahomaṃ ca hutvā kuryātkriyāstataḥ ।।

ādyeṣṭakārthamāsādya kuṇḍamaupāsanaṃ budhaḥ ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca pauruṣaṃ sūktameva ca ।।

degdaivatyaṃ ca juhuyāddevaṃ dhyāyan samāhitaḥ ।
japedvedādimantrāṃstu saṃspṛśyādyeṣṭakāsthalam ।।

kṛtvāntaḥ pariṣekaṃ ca pariṣicyānalaṃ punaḥ ।
garbhanyāsārthamāgūrya vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

puruṣasūktaṃ ca śrīsūktaṃ mahīsūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।
degdaivatyaṃ ca juhuyā"nnāgarājāya'setyapi ।।

"sarvaratnebhya'ityuktvā "sarvadhātubhya'ityapi ।
"sarvabījebhya'ityuktvā"sarvalohebhya'ityape ।।

"nadībhyaḥpātālebhya'śca "nāgebhyo'juhuyāttataḥ ।
"diggajebhyo viṣṇave' ca svāhāntaṃ juhuyātkramāt ।।

tata ābhyantaradvāradakṣiṇantaṃbhadakṣiṇe ।
medinīṃ tu samabhyarcya japetsūktaṃ tu pauruṣam ।।

medinyādīṃstato japtvātattatthsāvaṃ spṛśedbudhaḥ ।
kṛtvāntaḥ pariṣekantu tatra kāryaṃ samācaret ।।

naṣṭe garbhe ca hutvaivaṃ saṃpādya sthāpayetpunaḥ ।
anyaiṣṭakārthaṃ juhuyādvaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

puruṣasūktaṃ ca hutvātu juhuyādvidhinā budhaḥ ।
vimānapāladaivatyaṃ japan vedādikānmanūn ।।

vimānasyopariṣṭāttu sthūpikīlādadhastathā ।
japanvaiviṣṇusūktaṃ ca kuryāccaivābhimarśanam ।।

dhruve pramāṇahīne ca paristīrya ca pāvakam ।
dhruvasthāpanavaddhutvā ratnanyāsoditānmanūn ।।

japetthsāpanasūktaṃ ca navīkṛtya prayatnataḥ ।
kautukādīṃśca kṛtvaiva pratiṣṭhāṃ kārayedbudhaḥ ।।

naṣṭe dhruve punaḥkuryādutkṛṣṭadravyanirmitam ।
atha vā vūrvavatkṛtvā sthāpayedvidhinātvaraḥ, ।।

narairvṛṣairmṛgādyairvāberamutpāṭitaṃ yadi ।
ahīnāṅgaṃ tu saṃgṛhya śuddhyarthamadhivāsayet ।।

jalādhivāsaṃ kṛtvā tu tatthsāne vidhinā budhaḥ ।
ratnanyāsaṃ ca kṛtvaiva pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।।

anyālayādapahṛtamaniṣpannakriyaṃ tathā ।
śilāberaṃ yadi syāttadbhūmau samyak pidhāya ca ।।

vidhināhṛtya saṃskāryaṃ kṛtvā sthāpanamācaret ।
śilpinā vithipūrvaṃ tu kṛtaṃ belaṃ tathā caret ।।

yathāvidhi yathāsthānaṃ sthāpitaṃ doṣavarjitam ।
beraṃ na cālayedyasmādrājarāṣṭravināśanam ।।

taddoṣaśamanārthāya padmāgnau juhuyātkramāt ।
saptāhaṃ tu mahāśāntiṃ kuryādbrāhmaṇabhojanam ।।

dadyātsuvarṇaṃ gāṃ bhūmiṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।
avidhijñairathācāryair ṛtvigbhisthāpagais tathā ।।

sthāpitaṃ beramājñāya cālayitvā yathāvidhi ।
vidhijñaisthpāpanaṃ vidvān kārayedatvaraṃ tathā ।।

vidhijñaisthsāpitaṃ beramajñānāccālitaṃ yadi ।
śāntiṃ hudvā vidhānena vidhijñaisthsāpayetpunaḥ ।।

nadītaṭākapāthodhipravāhairvātyayādha vā ।
daivātpracālite tatra vimāne vā dhruve api vā ।।

bhūmau pidhāya tadberaṃ nirmāya punarālayam ।
acalaṃ sthāpayedberaṃ śāstroktenaiva vartmanā ।।

sāpāye tu sthale tasmin sannikṛṣṭe sthale caret ।
grāmādau vā vivikte vā pradeśe sumanorame ।।

vimānaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ kṛtvā devamādāya tatra vai ।
sarvaiśca pārṣadairyuktaṃ saṃsthāpya vidhinār'cayet ।।

grāmādīnāmabhāve tu śatadaṇḍātparaṃ tataḥ ।
vimānaṃ vistṛte deśe kṛtvā saṃsthāpya cārcayet ।।

rājārāṣṭrāntaraṃ jitvā beramāhṛtya yatnataḥ ।
svarāṣṭresthāpituṃ cecchedyadi grāmaṃ vidhāya ca ।।

tadvāstvaṅgālaye beraṃ vidhinā sthāpya cārcayet ।
apauruṣālayābhyāśe vimānaṃ pauruṣaṃ yadi ।।

kartumicchettadā kuryāttatprākārāntare punaḥ ।
bhūśuddhyādīnvinā kṛtvā prākāraṃ pratimādikam ।।

pratiṣṭhāpyār'cayettasya mūlasthānār'canaṃ phalam ।
pramādādathavā daivā dālaye snapanālaye ।।

āsthānamaṇḍape pākasthānaprākārayorapi ।
govuresnānapānīyaśālādau vahnidūṣite ।।

mahāvātahate akasmādaśanyādihate tathā ।
pāramātmikamabjāgnāvīṅkārādīṃs tathā hunet ।।

vicchinnaṃ mindāhutīcaiva āgneyaṃ vyāhṛtīstathā ।
punaranyannavaṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāṃ kārayetkramāt ।।

śilāgrahaṇa kāle vā tadā dārugrahe api ca ।
kriyāṅgīne viparyāse vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

mindāhutī ca vicchinnaṃ vyāhṛtyantaṃ hunedbudhaḥ ।
dvārastaṃbhe bhuvaṅgādau hīne māne agnidūṣite ।।

jīrṇe vā kṛmidaṣṭe vānupayuktaṃ tyajedbudhaḥ ।
anyamāhṛtya vidhinā saṃyojyaiva ca pūrvavat ।।

nityāgnau vaiṣṇavaṃ saumyamāgneyaṃ śāntimācaret ।
garbhanyāsārthamathavā pīṭhanyāsārthameva vā ।।

ratnānāmapyalābhe tu suvarṇaṃ tatra nikṣipet ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ tu juhuyātprāyaścittaṃ tu tadbhavet ।।

dhātūnāṃ pāradaṃ prāktamalābhapraṇidhintu tat ।
pāradaṃ tatra nikṣipya brāhmaṃ raudraṃ ca niṣkṛtiḥ ।।

yavā bījapratinidhirmudgānvā tatra nikṣipet ।
vāyavyaṃ vaiṣmavaṃ ceti juhuyāttatra niṣkṛtiḥ ।।

dhruvabelasya nirmāṇe śūlagrahaṇakarmaṇi ।
sthāpane vā viparyāse brāhmaṃ raudraṃ ca vaiṣṇavam ।।

vāhṛtyantaṃ ca hutvaiva vidhinā yojayetpunaḥ ।
apramāṇe vimāne tu beraṃ mānavivarjitam ।।

ajñānāt sthāpitaṃ cettadrājarāṣṭravināśakṛt ।
taddoṣaśamanārthaṃ ca mahāśāntiṃ hunedbudhaḥ ।।

tadvimānaṃ ca tadberaṃ sthāpayedvidhivatpunaḥ ।
tattadberoktaśūlānāṃ pramāṇaṃ yadi hīyate ।।

pūrṇaṃ kṛtvā vaiṣṇavaṃ ca pauruṣaṃ sūktameva ca ।
"dadbhyassvā'hetyaṅgahomaṃ hutvātu sthāpayetpunaḥ ।।

snehacūrṇakaṣāyādau hīne yogaviparyaye ।
rajjubandhāṣṭabandhādau śarkarālepane tathā ।।

tathā mṛdālepane ca paṭācchādanakarmaṇi ।
bhūṣādau kramahīne vā varṇādīnāṃ vyatikrame ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmaraudrāgnimahābhūtāthipāṃstathā ।
prājāpatyaṃ vyāhṛtīśca hutvā vidhipadācaret ।।

mahāberaṃ cārdhacitraṃ mṛṇmayaṃ naiva kārayet ।
sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ śailaṃ dāravamevavā ।।

ratnajaṃ vārdhacitrastu kuryādberaṃ salakṣaṇam ।
kṛtrimeṇāpyanuktena varṇenālepitaṃ punaḥ ।।

beraṃ prakṣālya nirvāsavāriṇā parimārjyaca ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca hutvābjāgnau jayādikān ।।

paścādyathoktavarṇena yathārhamanulepayet ।
dhravaberaṃ sudhāyukta miṣṭakākalpitaṃ tathā ।।

duṣṭadravyakṛtaṃ vātha sthāpitaṃ cābhicārikam ।
tacchīghramapahāyeva padmāgnau vaiṣmavaṃ tathā ।।

viṣṇusūktaṃ pauruṣaṃ ca śrībhūdaivatyameva ca ।
yaddevādīṃs tathā brāhmaraudrapāvakavāruṇān ।।

sarvadaivatyamantrāṃśca pāramātmikameva ca ।
mahāśānti ca hutvaitāṃ sarvadoṣavināśinīm ।।

paścatsaṃskṛtya vidhivadberaṃ saṃsthāpya cārcayet ।
vṛttalohārakūṭādyairanuktadravyasaṃbhavaiḥ ।।

nirmitaṃ kautukaṃ beramabhicārāya kalpate ।
taddoṣaśāntyai padmāgnau mahāśāntiṃ samācaret ।।

beraṃ salakṣaṇaṃ kṛtvā vidhinā sthāpayetpunaḥ ।
kautukaṃ sthitamāsīnamatha vā kārayedbudhaḥ ।।

śayānaṃ nācaredārṣaṃ yathāvasthitamarcayet ।
nirduṣṭe kautukādau tu pūjyamāne tu vigrahe ।।

naiva praveśayedberamutkṛṣṭadravyakalpitam ।
nikṛṣṭadravyajaṃ cāpi pūjyamānaṃ na saṃtyajet ।।

arcyamāne kautukādau virūpe varṇavarjite ।
yuktevā jharjhurādyaiśca dhruveśaktiṃ samarpya ca ।।

navīkṛtya punarbiṃbaṃ saṃśodhya sthāpayetpunaḥ ।
kautukaṃ cedarcyamānaṃ daivādrājādibhirhṛte ।।

taddeśaśuddhiṃ kṛtvaiva mahāśāntiṃ puroditām ।
kṛtvā nyasyātra ratnaṃ vā suvarṇaṃ kūrcameva vā ।।

dhruvādvā hṛdayādarka maṇḍalādvā vidhānataḥ ।
devamāvāhya tatkāle paścādberaṃ yathāvidhi ।।

pūrvadravyeṇa votkṛṣṭadravyeṇāpi prakalpayet ।
kālāpekṣāmakṛtvaiva pratiṣṭhāṃ pūrvavaccaret ।।

madhūcchiṣṭakriyāhīnaṃ beramādāya vaiṣṇavam ।
śāntiṃhutvā raudrasaurapāvakān punarācaret ।।

anyālaye sthāpitaṃ tu dhruvaṃ kautukameva vā ।
anyālaye sthāpayeccenmahāśāntiṃ hunedbudhaḥ ।।

vaiṣṇavāṃntu susaṃpūjya brāhmaṇān bhojayedbahu ।
tattatthsāne tu vidhinā saṃsthāpyārcana mācaret ।।

grāmādīnāmālayasya nāśeberaṃ tu tadgatam ।
anyasminnālaye sthāpya yathārhaṃ tu samarcayet ।।

kṛte tu pīṭhasaṃghāte bere tvavanate kramāt ।
dakṣiṇādi bhavenmṛtyurarthanāśo abhivardhanam ।।

putrahāni stundabhede dhyānyānāṃ tu vināśanam ।
uraśchidrer'thanāśaśca kṛśe kārśyaṃ bhajennaraḥ ।।

sthūle ca mahatīvyādhirdīrghe anāyuṣyameva ca ।
hrasve adurbhikṣamāpnoti nyūnādhikyasamudbhave ।।

anyeṣvaṅgeṣu hānissyācchāstroktaṃ samyagācaret ।
dhruvasya sthāpanādarvāk prākpratiṣṭhāvidhestathā ।।

anuktaniṣkṛtiṃ vakṣye kāpilena ghṛtena vai ।
padmāgnau vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ suktaṃ ca pauruṣam ।।

śrībhūdaivatyamantrāṃśca juhuyādvyāhṛtīrbunaḥ ।
tattatkarmapunaḥ kuryādanyathā niṣphalaṃ bhavet ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre ṣaḍviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha saptaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

prāyaścittam
ācāryasyartvijāṃ caiva pūjakasya viśeṣataḥ ।
yathoktavaraṇe hīne śāntiṃ kuryādyathāvidhi ।।

abjāgnau tu mahāśāntiṃ daśavāraṃ hunettataḥ ।
yathoktaṃ varaṇaṃ kṛtvā paścātkarma samācaret ।।

aṅkurārpaṇakāle tu brahmādīnāmathār'cane ।
havirnivedane vāpi hīne śāntiṃ samācaret ।।

taddaivatyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca hutvā-bhyarcya nivedayet ।
aṅkurārpaṇahīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

puruṣasūktaṃ ca brāhmaṃ ca vyāhṛtīśca hunettathā ।
punarapyaṅkurān kṛtvā paścātkāryaṃ samācaret ।।

kṛtvāṃkurārpaṇaṃ paścānnācaretkarma cettataḥ ।
rājarāṣṭravināśassyānmahāśāntiṃ samācaret ।।

"kṣama'sveti praṇamyaiva punaraṅkuṃmācaret ।
akṣyunmeṣāttu pūrvaṃ cetpīṭhasaṃghātakarmaṇi ।।

alābhe caiva ratnānāṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।
sūktaṃ tu pauruṣaṃ brāhmaṃ saumyaṃ caiva tu vyāhṛtiḥ ।।

hutvā suvarṇaṃ bahuśa stattatthsāne vinikṣipet ।
akṣyunmeṣaṇakāle tu gavādīnāmasaṃbhave ।।

darśanadravyarūpāṇāṃ yathālābhaṃ pragṛhya ca ।
tattaddravyādhidaivatyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ juhuyātkramāt ।।

tattaddravyaṃ ca saṃpādya vidhivaddarśayetpunaḥ ।
akṣyunmeṣaṇahīne vā rāhusaurodaye atha vā ।।

andhakecaiva nakṣatre kṛte caivākṣimocane ।
sarvanāśo bhavettasmādvaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

navagrahādimantrāśca hutvākṣyunmīlanaṃ caret ।
pañcagavyādiṣu dravyeṣvadhivāse vivarjite ।।

hutvā vaiṣṇavamārṣañca viṣṇusūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।
jalādhivāsaṃ triyahamekāhaṃ vāpi kālayet ।।

yajñālaye mahāvedyāṃ kṛtāyāmapramāṇataḥ ।
anyadeśakṛtāyāṃ vā vihīnāyāṃ ca śobhanaiḥ ।।

tattaddeśādhidaivatyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।
śrībhūdaivatyaṃ ca hutvaiva yathoktaṃ punarācaret ।।

dhruvaberākṣimokṣānte yadi beraṃ na śodhayet ।
viparīte api vā hutvā vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

puruṣasūktaṃ raudramārṣaṃ vāruṇaṃ ca punaścaret ।
agnikuṇḍānyavidhinā kṛtānyālakṣya satvaram ।।

brāhmaṃ saumyamathāgneyaṃ vidhinā kārayettataḥ ।
apramāṇeṣu kūrcādiṣvājyapātra sruvādiṣu ।।

mindāhutī ca sāvitraṃ vyāhṛtīśca hunedbadhaḥ ।
pañcāgniṣu yathāsthānaṃ prokṣaṇollekhane kṛte ।।

mathitāgnāvalābhe tu prāpya cācāryamandiram ।
atha vā śrotriyāgārādāhṛtyāgniṃ samācaret ।।

nidhāya gārhapatyegnimāghāraṃ juhuyādbudhaḥ ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ bhūmidaivatyamāgneyaṃ ca hunetkramāt ।।

tamagniṃ vardhayitvātu dakṣiṇāgnau praṇīya ca ।
tata āhavanīyāgnāvāvasadhye tataḥ param ।।

sabhye padmānale caivaṃ kramātpraṇayanaṃ caret ।
viparīte praṇayane tattanmantravivarjite ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ pāvakaṃ brāhmaṃsaumyaṃ hutvā punaścaret ।
tattadagniṣu cāghārātpūrvaṃ teṣāmathāntarā ।।

nagacchedyadi gacchettu tattaddikpāladaivatam ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ pāvakaṃ ceti prāyaścittaṃ hunaitkramāt ।।

utpanne mathitāgnau tu śānte tatra pramādataḥ
ādau praṇayanādarvāgathavāgniṣu sarvaśaḥ śāntiṃ yathoditāṃ kuryādagni sūktaṃ sahasraśaḥ) ।
taṇḍulair ekajātīyairdviprasthaiḥ pācayeccarum gavyaṃ ca navanītaṃ ca laukikānalasaṃskṛtam ।।

saṃskārakāle saṃskuryāttadagniṃ mantravattadā ।
ājyasthālyāmatha carau makṣikādiḥ patedyadi ।।

tadvyapohyānyadādāya prājāpatyaṃ ca pāvakam ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ ca hunedājye tvalabdhe nūtane pūnaḥ ।।

vyapohya doṣaṃ taṃ darbhairuddīpyotpūya cācaret ।
āghārite agnau naṣṭe tu "ayaṃ te yoni' muccaran ।।

āropayecca samidhaṃ tadbhasmani yathārhataḥ ।
"udbuddhya'sveti nikṣipya vidhinā laukike anale ।।

vicchinnaṃ mindāhutī ca vaiṣṇavaṃ vyāhṛtipūrvakam ।
paristarādidravyāṇāṃ dāhe bhede atha nāśane ।।

punastattacca saṃyojya mahāvyāhṛtipūrvakam ।
āgneyaṃ mindāhutī ca vaiṣṇavaṃ ca hunedbudhaḥ ।।

pātre anukte sruvaṃ pātraṃ gṛhṇīyāddhomakarmaṇi ।
havirviśeṣe anu ktetu ghṛtaṃ vā saghṛtaṃ caru ।।

dravye pramāṇahīne tu kāpilena ghṛtena vai ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṃśatirhutvā paścātkāryaṃ samācaret ।।

prāyaścittānale anukte chullyāṃ nityānale api vā ।
kriyāhīne viparyāse mantrāṇāṃ saṃkare api vā ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ vyāhṛtīścaiva vyāhṛtyantaṃ hunetkramāt ।
puṇyāhahīne puṇyāhamantrān dvādaśaśo japet ।।

vāstuhomavihīne tu tanmantrān daśaśo hunet ।
prāyaścittaviśeṣe yadyanukte vaiṣṇavaṃ tataḥ ।।

viṣṇusūktaṃ pauruṣaṃ ca sūktaṃ hutvā samācaret ।
ratnapratinidhī rukmaṃ dhātūnāṃ pāradaṃ tathā ।।

bījānāṃ ca yavāḥ proktāḥ pūrvālābhe parassmataḥ ।
ratnānāṃ praṇidhiṃ gṛhya vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

digdaivatyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca dhātūnāmatha tatparam ।
bījānāṃ praṇidhiṃ gṛhya vāyavyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।।

hune dviṃśativāraṃ tu pratyekaṃ doṣaśāntaye ।
vastrelakṣaṇahīne vā yukte chedādinā tataḥ ।।

tattyaktvānyaṃ samāhṛtya śrīdaivatyaṃ ca vaiṣṇavam ।
aṇḍajādidvalabdheṣu vastraṃ pratyekamāharet ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ śrībhūdaivatyaṃ hutvā kāryaṃ samācaret ।
pramāṇahīneṣu punastoraṇādiṣu cātvaraḥ ।।

pṛthagdvārādhidaivatyaṃ juhuyādviṃśatiṃ budhaḥ ।
darbharajjvāṃ vihīnāyāṃ hunaidārṣaṃ ca vaiṣṇavam, ।।

kuṃbhe pramāṇahīne vā doṣayukte api vā tathā ।
vastrābhyāṃ varṇacihnaiśca hīne nātravaseddhariḥ ।।

yatnena tāni nikṣipya vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।
puruṣasūktaṃ brāhmaṃ ca munimantrāṃśca pāvakam ।।

juhuyāddaśakṛtvantu viprāṇāṃ bhojanaṃ caret ।
ācāryadakṣiṇāndadyātsaphalaṃ bhavati dhruvam ।।

bhinne tu sādhite kuṃbhe vaiṣṇapaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।
puruṣasūktaṃ brāhmamaindramāgneyaṃ cārṣameva ca ।।

hutvā viṃśatikṛtvantu dadyādācāryadakṣiṇām ।
brāhmaṇān bhojayitvaiva saṃpūjyaiva ca vaiṣmavān ।।

anyatkuṃbhaṃ samāhṛtya pūrvavatsādhayedbudhaḥ ।
spṛṣṭe tu sāthite kuṃbhe patitaiḥ kukkuṭādibhiḥ ।।

tadvyapohyāryadādāya pūrvavatsādhayettathā ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣasūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

brāhmaṃ sauramathāgneyamaṣṭādhikaśataṃ yajet ।
ācāryadakṣiṇāṃ dadyādvaiṣṇavān pūjayedvidhiḥ ।।

sparśaduṣṭe tathā bere snapanaṃ śāstrataścaret ।
pūrvoktāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ kṛtvā paścātkāryaṃ samācaret ।।

nruvādīnāmalābhetu sruveṇaiva huneddhaviḥ ।
śvakukkuṭādyaissaṃspṛṣṭe kuṇḍe taṃ taṃ vyapohya ca ।।

kuṇḍaṃ tu pūrvavatkṛtvā kṛtvāghāraṃ yathāvidhi ।
āgneyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ pañcavāruṇaṃ mūlahomakam ।।

śataśo juhuyātkuryādbrāhmaṇānāṃ ca bhojanam ।
alābhe samidhāṃ kṛhya pālāśīrvaṭasaṃbhavāḥ ।।

āgneyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmaṃ hutvākāryaṃ samācaret ।
darbhān kuśānvā samidho māsātītān pragṛhya ca ।।

vāruṇaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmaṃ saumyamāgneyameva ca ।
ādityaṃ juhuyāccaiva doṣa śāntirbhavettathā ।।

dadhi kṣīraṃ gṛhītaṃ cedājaṃ māhiṣameva vā ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmamāgneyaṃ sauraṃ ca vyāhṛtīrhunet ।।

anuktadeśādānītā mṛdo vā vālukās tathā ।
agnikuṇḍārthamāhṛtya vāruṇaṃ vaiṣṇave hunet ।।

ārdraṃ sadhūmaṃ durgandhaṃ lepayuktaṃ sakaṇṭakam ।
jantuyuktaṃ kṣipedvahnāvindhanaṃ tatparityajet ।।

anyatprakṣipya cāgneyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ vyāhṛtīrhunet ।
vastrādidravye darbheṣu prapāyāṃ kūṭa eva vā ।।

dagdhāyāmagninā brāhmaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ saurameva ca ।
āgneyaṃ vaiṣṇavamiti pratyekaṃ daśaśo hunet ।।

kalaśanyāsaracanāviparyāne tu vaiṣṇavam ।
paṅktīśadaivatyaṃ ca hunettataśśāstravadācaret ।।

snapane tu viparyāne berasya juhuyādbudhaḥ ।
pañcavāruṇamantrāṃśca vaiṣṇavaṃ ca yathāvidhi ।।

śayane cedviparyāso vaiṣṇavaṃ śrīmahīmanūn ।
kalaśasnānaśayane pratyekaṃ daśaśo hunet ।।

hīne vā viparīte vā tatra hautrapraśaṃsane ।
brāhmaṃ munīndramantrāṃścahunetpāriṣadāmapi ।।

avāhanādāvarcāyāṃ viparīte vivarjite ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca brāhmaṃ raundraṃ huneddaśa ।।

sarveṣāmuktahomānāṃ viparīte vivarjite ।
padmāgnau vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ sūktaṃ ca pauruṣam ।।

śayānamuddhareddevamakāle cāpyamantrakam ।
hutvā śrībhūmidaivatyaṃ catuṣkṛtvantu śāyayet ।।

hīne cādhyayane sārasvatamaṣṭādhikaṃ śatam ।
prāyaścittaṃ ca hutvaiva yathāśāstraṃ samācaret ।।

yathālābhaṃ ca gṛhṇīyādalābhe ṣoḍaśartvijām ।
tantreṇa kārayetsarvameṣa śāstravidhissmṛtaḥ ।।

pratiṣṭhāyāmutsavevā tathānyacchubhakarmaṇi ।
kurvatāṃ tu puraścaryāmācāryasya rtvijāṃ tathā ।।

āsnānāddīkṣitānāṃ tu nāśaucaḥparikīrtitaḥ ।
mohādanuṣṭhitāśaucāḥpatantinarake aśucau ।।

gṛhṇīyā tsaṃskṛtāṃstānvā punaranyānathāpi vā ।
ācārya sthsāpakādīṃstu bhartsanādikamācaran ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca sūktaṃ pauruṣameva ca ।
brāhmaṃ sārasvataṃ hutvā tānanujñāpya cācaret ।।

ācāryadakṣiṇākāle atīte hutvā tu vaiṣṇavam ।
munimantrañca juhuyātpṛthagaṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।।

yathoktadakṣiṇāṃ dadyādarthalobhaṃ na kārayet ।
brāhmaṇānāmannadāne vihīne śāntimācaret ।।

triyahaṃ tu mahāśānti staddoṣavinivāriṇī ।
hantyalpadakṣiṇo yāgaḥ phalaṃ dadyātsadakṣiṇaḥ ।।

yajñasya dakṣiṇā jīvastasmādyatnena pālayet ।
iyaṃ tātkālikījñeyā bhūmimagre pradāpayet ।।

arcakasyārcanārdhaṃ ca kuṭuṃbārthaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
bhūmibhogamakalpyaiva mahāśāntiṃ samācaret ।।

asaṃkalpitavṛttistu devāvāso na vardhate ।
arcakaḥ praṇidhiryasmādrājño rāṣṭrasya kalpate ।।

tasmātsamāhitaḥ kuryādyathā pūjā na lupyate ।
āpadyapi ca kaṣṭāyāṃ pūjāmetāṃ na lopayet ।।

yadaiva lupyate pūjā yena kenāpi hetunā ।
agrer'cakamiyāddoṣa ārdrameṣo aparādhyati ।।

tasmāddāyena bhūmyādi sthiradānena sādaram ।
rūḍhādhikāra evāgre pravartetār'caner'cakaḥ ।।

yasmādarcanahīne tu rājarāṣṭrādisaṃkṣayaḥ ।
tadgrāmavāsinastasmādrājā rāṣṭragatā api ।।

bhagavatpūjanāheto rupakuryuḥ prayatnataḥ ।
ārdrāparādho bhavati yasmāddoṣeṣu pūjakaḥ ।।

taṃ vṛttikarśitaṃ dṛṣyvā rājā ca grāmavāsinaḥ ।
sukhitaṃ taṃ tathā kuryuryathā devastathārcakaḥ ।।

datvṛttimadhikāṃ cāpina śaṅkeyurasūyavaḥ ।
yathārhamupayuñjīran svaśaktiṃ tatsukhāya vai ।।

pratiṣṭhānte tu vidhivadarcake tvaprakalpite ।
āsurī sā bhavedarcā kartā naivāpnu yātphalam ।।

devena sārthamuddiṣṭaṃ yatkulaṃ pūjakasya tu ।
tadatikramya pūjāṃ tu kārayeditareṇa cet ।।

rauravaṃ narakaṃ yāti kartā kārayitā ca yaḥ ।
tasmā tsarvaprayatnena śāstroktaṃ paripālayet ।।

śvaḥ kāryamadya kurvīta pūrvāhṇe cāparāhṇikam ।
na hi pratīkṣate mṛtyuḥ kartavyo dharmasaṃgrahaḥ ।।

na tya ktavibhavo jātu bhavecca vibhave sati ।
yathāśakti prakurvīta vibhavāṃśca na lobhayet ।।

alābhe kautukādīnāṃ suvarṇaṃ nyasya vaiṣmavam ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ nṛsuktaṃ ca vāyavyaṃ digadhīśvaram ।।

sabhye antahomahīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ pāvakaṃ tathā ।
vyāhṛtīśca hunedvidvān daśakṛtvassamāhitaḥ ।।

agnigrahaṇahīne tu hutvā pūrvoktaniṣkṛtim ।
śrotriyāvasathādagnimāhṛtyāghāravūrvakam ।।

nityahomaṃ ca juhuyāttataḥ prabhṛti cācaret ।
dhruvādāvāhayedyasmātkautukādi caturṣvapi ।।

pramādātkuṃbhatīrthena teṣāmāvāhane kṛte ।
"iṣetve'tyādinā snāpya śīghraṃ śuddhena vāriṇā ।।

anumānya ca deveśaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।
juhuyātpauruṣaṃsūktaṃ dhruvādāvāhayetpunaḥ ।।

athanityārcanāyāntu prāyaścittaṃ pravakṣyate ।
sūryodayācca madhyāhnātpūrva mastamayādapi ।।

kavāṭodghāṭane hīne nityāgnau vā mahānane ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ dhātrādidaivatyaṃ hutvā dauvārikaṃ tathā ।।

śīghramudghāṭayeddvāraṃ devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।
amantrakamathānyairvā kavāṭodghāṭane kṛte ।।

pūrvoktaṃ juhuyācchāntiṃ japeddvādaśasūktakam ।
mārjanādiṣu hīneṣu nirmālyecāpyaśodhite ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ vāruṇaṃ hutvā vāyavyaṃ śāntameva ca ।
yathāvatkārayetsarvaṃ mantreṇaiva punarguruḥ ।।

dravyapratinidhistoyamalābhe tena cācaret ।
devasya snapane hīne vaiṣṇave vāruṇaṃ hunet ।।

"apo hi'ṣṭhādibhirmantraissnāvayen niṣkṛtirbhavet ।
paśnānnityaṃ prakurvīta snānaṃ nityārcanoditam ।।

aśaktausnāpane prokṣyaṃ mantreṇa kuśavāribhiḥ ।
vastrādīṃśca vyapohyaiva dhautavastraṃ samarpayet ।।

nityaṃ snānamaśakyaṃ cedviṣṇupañcadineṣu vai ।
snāpayeddevadeveśamiti kecidvadantihi ।।

dhruvapīṭhetu nirmālyaṃ saṃśodhya punareva ca ।
puṣpanyāsaṃ prakurvīta dhruve nityārcanaṃ bhavet ।।

puṣpanyāsaṃ vinākuryātkautukasyārcanaṃ yadi ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣasūktaṃ tadhaiva ca ।।

hutvā ca viṣṇugāyatrīṃ puṣbanyāsaṃ kramāccaret ।
saṃbandhakūrcahīnetu vaiṣṇavaṃ munimantrakam ।।

hutvāsannyasya kūrcaṃ tu paścātkāryaṃ samācaret ।
dhātrādyarcanahīne tu taddaivatyaṃ savaiṣṇavam ।।

hutvārcayed dhātṛmukhān tathā pariṣadaḥ kramāt ।
upacāraviparyāse "kṣama'nveti praṇamya ca ।।

anumānyārcayed devaṃ hīne caiva tu vigrahe ।
taddevatāmanuṃ japtvā vaiṣṇavaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

punastadupacārādi pūjaye tsarvavigrahaiḥ ।
uktadravye ṣvalabdheṣu puṣpaṃ toyamathākṣatam ।।

gṛhītvā caiva tatsarvaṃ dhyātvā devaṃ samarcayet ।
arcākāle anyakālaṃ vā smaye vā mūṣikādibhiḥ ।।

marutā vāpi vicchinnamajasraṃ dīpamādarāt ।
dviguṇaṃ tu samuddīpya sauraṃ raudraṃ ca pāvakam ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ ca tathāhutvā punararcanamācaret ।
tatkāle sarvadīpānāṃ nāśe doṣo mahattaraḥ ।।

devaṃ śuddhodakaissnāpya kuśodairabhiṣicya ca ।
pūrvoktāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ hutvā dviguṇaṃ tu nidevayet ।।

bahudīpeṣucaikasminnaṣṭe tenana duṣyati ।
mantrāṇāṃ skhalane mūrtyāpraṇavena sahācaret ।।

arcākāle yavanikāhīne caiva prajāpatim ।
vaiṣṇapaṃ caiva hutvā tu paṭaṃ kṛtvār'cayetpunaḥ ।।

vedadūṣaka pāṣaṇḍa pāparogānvitairjanaiḥ ।
pratilomādibhirlmecchairantyajātibhireva ca ।।

tatkāle darśane hutvā vaiṣṇavaṃ brāhmameva ca ।
raudraṃ ca pāvakaṃ hutvā vyāhṛtīśca tator'cayet ।।

yadi cāvaraṇādbāhye pañcāśaddaṇḍakāntare ।
manuṣyāṇāṃ mṛtissyāttaduddhṛtyaivārcayeddharim ।।

naivārcanaṃ havirdānaṃ tataḥ pūrvaṃ samācaret ।
dhruvakautukayoḥ kuryātpuṣpanyāsāvasānakam ।।

paścātkālātyaye śāntiṃ hutvā dviguṇamarcayet ।
ekakālārcane hīne dvitīye dviguṇaṃ caret ।।

tṛtīye triguṇaṃ kuryādekāher'cāvivarjite ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣa sūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

hunecchrībhūmidaivatyaṃ dvyahe tu dviguṇaṃ bhavet ।
tṣahe triguṇamevantu dvādaśāhāntamācaret ।।

atīte dvādaśāhetu saṃdhāyaupāsanānale ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣasūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

ālaye pariṣaddeva mantrān hutvā ca śaktitaḥ ।
kalaśaissnāpya deveśamabhyarcya havirarpayet ।।

māsaṃ hīner'cane kuryādālayābhimukhe guruḥ ।
sabhyāgnau vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ sūktaṃ ca pauruṣam ।।

hutvā śrībhūmidaivatyaṃ sarvadaivatyameva ca ।
kalaśairaṣṭabhiśca tvāriṃśadbhissnāpayeddharim ।।

viśeṣeṇa havirdadyāddvitīyedviguṇaṃ tathā ।
tṛtīye triguṇaṃ caivaṃ vatsarānantu vardhayet ।।

atīte vatsare caivaṃ padmāgnau saptavāsaram ।
mahāśāntiṃ tu hutvaiva kṛtvā vaiṣṇavapūjanam ।।

brāhmaṇān bhojayitvaiva śatāṣṭakalaśaiḥ punaḥ ।
saṃsnāpya devadeveśaṃ punasthsāpana mācaret ।।

akṣyunneṣādhivāsau tu punasthsāpanakarmaṇi ।
hitvānyatsakalaṃ karma pūrvavattu samācaret ।।

havirhīne janāssarvetadgrāmasthāssamīpagāḥ ।
pīḍitāḥ kṣutpipāsādyairbhaveyurvyādhitā api ।।

tasmādatiprayatnena havissamya ṅnivedayet ।
hīne haviṣyeka kāle dvitīye dviguṇaṃ bhavet ।।

tṛtīye triguṇaṃ kuryādekasmin divase gate ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ śrīmahīmantrān mūrti homaṃ tathā hunet ।।

devaṃ śuddhodakaissnāpya prabhūtaṃ tu nivedayet ।
sopadaṃśamapakvaṃ ca śītaṃ paryuṣitaṃ tathā ।।

pātrāntareṣvanikṣiptaṃ sāvaśeṣaṃ ca laṅghitam ।
vivṛtaṃ srāvitaṃ caiva vikṛtaṃ dṛṣṭi dūṣitam ।।

aprokṣitamathāspṛṣṭa magṛhītamamudritam ।
havirnivedayeccettu vaiṣṇavaṃ śrīmahīmanūn ।।

āgneyaṃ vāruṇaṃ caiva vāyavyaṃ daśaśo hunet ।
dviguṇaṃ tu punaḥkṛtvā prabhūtaṃ tu nivedayet ।।

nivedya cāśumispṛṣṭaṃ devaṃ saṃsnāpya mantrataḥ ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇugāyatrīṃ trayastriṃśatkramāddhunet ।।

juhuyādvidhināśāntiṃ prokṣaṇairapi prokṣayet ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvaiva dviguṇaṃ cārcanaṃ haviḥ ।।

vrīhyaṅgāratuṣairyukteśarkarādivimiśrite ।
nivedite tu haviṣi mantreṇāṣṭākṣareṇa tu ।।

vaiṣṇapyā caiva gāyatṣā mantraissaṃstūya vaiṣṇavaiḥ ।
"kṣama'svetyanumānyaiva praṇamayaiva ca yācayet ।।

makṣikādyairjantubhiśca keśādyairapi dūṣite ।
nivedite tu haviṣi śuddhodaissnāvyavai harim ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca śrībhūdaivatyameva ca ।
aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā dviguṇaṃ tu nivedayet ।।

mahāhaviṣi caitaintu saṃyukte tatra dūṣitam ।
puruṣāśanamātraṃ tu vyapohya tadanantaram ।।

bhasmāṃbhasākuśai "rāpo hiraṇya pavamāna'kaiḥ ।
prokṣya devaṃ susaṃprārdhya tadgṛhītvā nivedayet ।।

pūrvamarkodayātpakva mupadaṃśamatho haviḥ ।
koṣṇaṃ cedarpayet prātararcanāntena doṣabhāk ।।

pūrva mastamayātpakvaṃ tathā sāyaṃ nivedayet ।
asaṃskṛtaṃ tu tāṃbūlaṃ lepakeśānvitaṃ tathā ।।

jantuspṛṣṭaṃ nivedyaiva vaiṣṇavaṃśrīmahīmanun ।
hutvā saṃskṛtya tāṃbūlaṃ punaranyannivedayet ।।

arcanāṃgeṣu cānyeṣu padārtheṣvevameva hi ।
dūṣiteṣvadha hīneṣu tasya tasyādhidaivatam ।।

mantraṃ sa vaiṣṇavaṃ hutvā punaranyaissamarcayet ।
alābhe caiva sarveṣāṃ puṣpaṃ toyaṃ pragṛhyaca ।।

saṃkalpyaiva pratinidhiṃ tattatsmṛtvā samarcayet ।
nityahome vihīnetu vaiṣṇavaṃ daśaśo hunet ।।

yathoktahomaṃ dviguṇamācarettadanantaram ।
agnisaṃrakṣaṇe aśaktā "vayante yo'nimuccaran ।।

samidhyāropayetkuṇḍātpaścātsaṃsthāpya laukike ।
nyasya "copāvaro'hetipratyahaṃ juhuyātkramāt ।।

surarṣimanujānāṃ tu balaṃ yasmātpṛvardhate ।
tasmādbalissamākhyātastadarthaṃ pratyahaṃ harim ।।

uktadravyeṣu cāvāhya triṣu kāleṣu deśikaḥ ।
abhyarcya bhrāmayedevamaśaktaḥ kartumuttamam ।।

yathoktapātre nikṣipya balidkavyantu kevalam ।
tasyopari yathoktaṃ tu baliberaṃ ca vinyaset ।।

śirasā dhārayan pātraṃ trirdvirvā sakṛdeva vā ।
dene tataḥ parīyācca devāgāraṃ pradakṣiṇam ।।

atha hitvā balidravyaṃ śibikādau gaje athavā ।
aropya yāne vidhivatkārayecca pradakṣiṇam ।।

prātarbhramaṇahīne tu vaiṣmavaṃ saurasaumyakam ।
prājāpatyaṃ ca juhuyāddhīne coktapradakṣiṇe ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ gāruḍaṃ hutvā balibhramaṇamācaret ।
hīne prātarbalau kuryānmadhyāhne dviguṇaṃ balim ।।

tathā hīne ca madhyāhne rātrau triguṇamācaret ।
ekāhe tu balau hīne nityāgnau vā mahānane ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣasūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।
digdaivatyaṃ ca hutvā tu pradakṣiṇanuthācaret ।।

devālaṅkārahīne tu śrīdaivatyaṃ yajedbudhaḥ ।
chatrapiñchādyalābhe tu vāruṇaṃ juhuyāttathā ।।

alābhe cāmarādīnāṃ vāyavyaṃ caiva hūyate ।
dīpālābhe pāvakaṃ ca vyāhṛtyantaṃ yajettrayam ।।

dvyahe tu dviguṇaṃ kurvāttṣahe triguṇameva ca ।
dvādaśāhāntamevaṃ syāddvādaśāhe gate tataḥ ।।

aupāsanāgnimādhāya vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।
puruṣasūktaṃ ca śrībhūmidaivatyaṃ brāhma meva ca ।।

raudraṃ digdevatāmantraṃ hutvaiva bhramaṇaṃ caret ।
māne atīte tu padmāgnau vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktam ।।

nṛsūktaṃ pāramātmīkamīṅkārādīṃ stadālaye ।
pariṣaddevamantrāṃśca hutvā bhramaṇamācaret ।।

dvimāse dviguṇaṃ kuryāttrimāse triguṇaṃ caret ।
vardhaye dvatsarāntaṃ cāpyatīte vatsare punaḥ ।।

sabhyaṃ saṃsādhya devābhimukhe vā dakṣiṇe nalam ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca sūktaṃ pauruṣameva ca ।।

śrībhūmyoścaiva daivatyaṃ sarvadaivatyameva ca ।
hutvā cāryaṃ ca saṃpūjya balyuddharaṇamācaret ।।

patite annabalau bhūmyāṃ bhinne jīrṇe ca pūrvavat ।
balimāpādya hutvā ca vaiṣṇavaṃ gāruḍaṃ tathā ।।

prājāpatyaṃ tu vidhinā tataḥ kuryātpradakṣiṇam ।
balyuddharaṇakāle tu vighnaścedāpatettadā ।।

sauraṃ saumyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ ca hutvā punarathācaret ।
pātrālābhe haviḥpātraṃ hunaidādāya vaiṣṇavam ।।

pramāṇahīne annabalau vaiṣṇavaṃ ca prajāpatim ।
juhuyāddoṣaduṣṭe tu havirniṣkṛtimācaret ।।

āvāhanaṃ vinā cānnabalau tu bhramaṇekṛte ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣasūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

hutvā śrībhūmidaivatyaṃ vidhinā bhramaṇaṃ caret ।
balyagrakhaṇḍe vidhinā śāntāya tvanivedite ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ mūrtimantraṃ ca hutvaiva daśaśaḥ kramāt ।
nivedya viṣvakcenāya pradāya mukhavāsanam ।।

punaśca balyuddharaṇaṃ vidhinā kārayettataḥ ।
akṛte balidāne tu prāśya pādodakaṃ hareḥ ।।

prasādaṃ cāpi saṃprāśya punardviguṇamarcayet ।
pravṛttāyāṃ tu pūjāyāṃ havirdānāntameva ca ।।

tīrthaprasādadānaṃ vā pādukāgrahaṇaṃ tathā ।
naśastamanyathā kṛtvā śāntihomaṃ samācaret ।।

pūjānte pūjakātpūrvamanyastīrthādikaṃ pibet ।
prasādaṃ vāpi gṛhṇīyāttatpūjā niṣphalā bhavet ।।

mahāśāntiṃ tathā hutvā punaḥpūjāṃ samācaret ।
tīrthaṃ puṣpaṃ tataḥ kṣīraṃ gandhaṃ ca tadanantaram ।।

sarvāṇvapi havīṃṣyatra nāgavallīdalānyapi ।
yadyanniveditaṃ deve dadyādagrer'cakāya ca ।।

arcakastu harissākṣāccararūpo yatassmṛtaḥ ।
nitye karmaṇi sarvatra pūjakaṃ pūrvamarcayet ।।

ācārya marcakaṃ vātha tathā naimittiker'cayet ।
yadyavaikhānaso vipraḥ kadāpi harimandire ।।

samicchedagrasanmānaṃ taddevasya vimānanam ।
yajamāno vipannassyādrājarāṣṭraṃ vinaśyati ।।

ajñānādatha vā mohādācale danyathāyadi ।
dviguṇaṃ tu samabhyarcya cānyaddviguṇa mācaret ।।

aśucirvāpyanācāraḥ sadāvaikhānasa śśuciḥ ।
pitā mṛṣyati putrāṇāṃ viśaṅkaṃ doṣasaṃcayam ।।

pitā hi bhagavān viṣṇuputrāssyuḥ pūjakā hareḥ ।
tasmātteṣu na kupyeta dīrghamāyurjijīviṣuḥ ।।

ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi niṣkṛtiṃ snapanāśritām ।
nityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ trividhaṃ snapanaṃ bhavet ।।

viṣuve cāyanadvandve snapanaṃ nityamucyate ।
candra sūryoparoge yannaimittikamiti smṛtam ।।

śeṣeṣu snapanaṃ yattatkāmyaṃ tu parikīrtitam ।
nityasnāpanahīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

puruṣasūktaṃ vāruṇaṃ ca daśakṛtvo hunetpunaḥ ।
snapanaṃ vidhivatkuryānni tyasnapana niṣkṛtiḥ ।।

grahaṇe snapane hīne pūrvavanniṣkṛtiṃ caret ।
kāmye ca pūrvavatkṛtvā śuddhodairabhiṣecayet ।।

anyathā cenmahādoṣo yajamāno vinaśyati ।
ālayātpurataścaiva uttare vā manorame ।।

uttamaṃ snapanāgāramaiśānyāṃ madhyamaṃ bhavet ।
paścime dakṣiṇe caivamadhamaṃ saṃprakīrtitam ।।

āgneyyādiṣu koṇeṣu snapane vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ nṛsūktaṃ ca digīśānāṃ manuṃ hunet ।।

snapanaṃ kārayetpaścādeṣā vyatyaya niṣkṛtiḥ ।
saṃdhyākāletu saṃprāpte nimittasnapane tathā ।।

naimittikaṃ samāpyaiva nityapūjaṃ samācaret ।
anyathā vaiṣṇavaṃ mantraṃ śatavāraṃ japetsudhīḥ ।।

pūrvarātrau pratisare hīne ca śayane tathā ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ śrīmahīmantrān hutvā saudarśanaṃ tathā ।।

śayyādhivāsanaṃ hitvā bandhayetkautukaṃ punaḥ ।
emabere kautuke tu kartavye śayanaṃ vinā ।।

baddhvā pratisaraṃ sadyassnapanaṃ samyagācaret ।
kṛte aṃkurārpaṇe hīne snapane vaiṣṇapaṃ tathā ।।

saumyaṃ śrībhūmidaivatyaṃ vaighnaṃ hutvābhiṣecayet ।
vināṃkurārpaṇaṃ cātha snāpayediti kecana ।।

pramāṇahīne adhike vā paṅktau snānāvaṭe api ca ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ bhūmidaivatyaṃ paṅktīśasya manuṃ yajet ।।

hīne śāntādyarcane ca vaiṣṇavaṃ śāntameva ca ।
paṅktīśasyārcane hīne tanmantraṃ ca jayādīkān ।।

indrādyarcanahīne tu tanmantraṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ hunet ।
kalaśeṣvapramāṇeṣu vaiṣṇavaṃ vāyudaivatam ।।

āgneyaṃ juhuyānmṛtsu hīnāsvatra ca vaiṣṇavam ।
bhūdaivatyaṃ ca juhuyānmṛtsu sarvāsvayaṃ vidhiḥ ।।

parvateṣyapramāṇeṣu vaiṣṇavaṃ pāvakaṃ hunet ।
dhānyeṣu vaiṣṇavaṃ caiva vāyavyaṃ ca hunedbudhaḥ ।।

aṅkureṣu vihīneṣu vaiṣṇavaṃ gāruḍaṃ tathā ।
juhuyādvyāhṛtīścaiva yathārhaṃ saṃbharetpunaḥ ।।

varṇahīneṣvamāneṣu maṅgaleṣu tu vaiṣṇavam ।
aindraṃ ca juhuyātkuryādyathārhaṃ saṃbharedapi ।।

pañcagavye mantrahīne vihīne yogakarmaṇi ।
juhuyādvaiṣṇavaṃ raudraṃ mantreṇaiva suyojayet ।।

uktapramāṇahīneṣu pañcagavyādiṣu kramāt ।
pradhāneṣu jalaiḥpūrva dravyādhipamanuṃ tathā ।।

vaiṣṇavenaiva mantreṇa saha hutvā samācaret ।
prāśanaṃ prokṣaṃ vāpi śāstre asmin yatra codyate ।।

ayameva vidhirjñeyaḥ pañcagavyasya sarvataḥ ।
sādhite kalaśebhinne tvanyamādāya pūrvavat ।।

āpūryābhyarcya daśaśo vaiṣṇavaṃ juhuyāttataḥ ।
kalaśānāṃ viparyāme taddhṛtenaiva cāplute ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ dravyadaivatyaṃ hutvā saṃśodhya tatpunaḥ ।
śuddhodaissnāpayec caiva yathāvacca punarnyaset ।।

kṛte tu kalaśanyāse śvakākādibhireva vā ।
aspṛśyairvāpi saṃsparśe saṃsādhyānyattu pūrvavat ।।

śāntiṃ vaiṣṇavamantrāṃśca hutvā kāryaṃ samācaret ।
kṛmikīṭādipatane tattaddravyaṃ parityajet ।।

anyadādāya juhuyādvaiṣṇavaṃ dravyadaivatam ।
ratnālābhe vaiṣṇavaṃ tu hutvā svarṇaṃ tu nikṣipet ।।

vastrālābhe vaiṣṇavaṃ ca śrīdaivatyaṃ ca hāvayet ।
yathoktasnapane hīne kathaṃ citsnapanaṃ caret ।।

atha vā kārayec chuddhasnapanaṃ vā vidhānataḥ ।
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi prāyaścittamathotsave ।।

kālādibhedanteṣāṃ ca lakṣaṇaṃ ca puroditam ।
puraskṛtya tithiṃ kecit kecinnakṣatrapūrvakam ।।

saṃkalpayantyavabhṛthaṃ varamṛkṣāpavargakam ।
akṛte niyate kālaṃ kṛte vāniyate tathā ।।

kālotsave mahān doṣastatra kuryāttuniṣkṛtim ।
utsavātpūrvamuddisya mahāśāntiṃ tṣahaṃ caret ।।

vijñāpya devadeveśaṃ tataḥ kālotsavaṃ caret ।
anyathā tu kṛtaṃ kāryamakṛtaṃ syādasaṃśayam ।।

anyasmin vāpi māse tu na kuryādyadi cotsavam ।
eṣa eva vidhiḥ proktaḥ parasminvatsare kṛte ।।

evaṃ trivatsarebhyassyādata ūrdhvaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
saptāhantu mahāśāntiṃ kṛtvā tūtsava mācaret ।।

eve dvādaśavarṣāntaṃ tataścasthāpanaṃ punaḥ ।
tatra devo na ramate yo asāvutsava daivatam ।।

yatra devālaye viṣṇusthsāpyate prathamaṃ tataḥ ।
tenaiva kārayetsarvamācāryeṇār'cakena ca ।।

tadabhāve tu tatputraiḥpautrais tadvaṃśajaistathā ।
tanniyuktais tadīyairvāpūrvābhāve paraiścaret ।।

anyathā kriyate cettu yajamāno vinaśyati ।
utsavāhassu hīneṣu prāyaścittaṃ samācaret ।।

vardhayedvaiṣṇavaṃ kāryaṃ hrāsayenna kadā cana ।
pramādādvāpyaśaktau vā kṛtvā saṃprārthayeddharim ।।

mahāśāntiṃ tu hutvaiva śeṣaṃ kuryātprayatnataḥ ।
eṣa eva vidhirvṛddhau sa tu śreyo abhivṛddhidaḥ ।।

yadā tvavabhṛthedaivātkṛte vinimayena tu ।
asaṃkalpitavatkuryāttatra pūrvokta niṣkṛtiḥ ।।

pramādādbuddhipūrvaṃ vā tattadvelotsavādiṣu ।
akṛteṣu yathāśāstraṃ kṛtvā tantreṇa vaipunaḥ ।।

mantreṇa vā punassūkṣmaṃ kāle avabhṛthamācaret ।
yajñasyāpabhṛtho antassyānnotsavastadanantaram ।।

akṛtotsavakāryāṇi yathoktaṃ pūrvamācaret ।
nityotsavaṃ hareḥ kuryānnityaśrī rnityamaṅgalaḥ ।।

harirnārāyaṇo devo nālaṃ devā stamarcitum ।
ācārye yajamāne vā pūjake anyapadārthini ।।

naṣṭe sadyastadānyantu varayitvā samācaret ।
na daivaṃ pratibadhnāti kāryaṃ yatkarma mānuṣam ।।

deveśamanumānyātha mahāśāntiṃ tu padmake ।
samṛto brahmamedhār'haḥ pūtaṃ tadgātramucyate ।।

sarve padārthinaḥ proktā gurupūrvāḥpadārthinaḥ ।
grāmāntaraṃ prayāte tu dīkṣāmadhye padārthini ।।

aspṛśyasparśadoṣeṇa surāpānādinā tathā ।
anuktadoṣairvā duṣṭe rogācchaucādyasaṃbhave ।।

śāvādyāśausayogye vā śavānugamane tathā ।
vāhane dāhane caiva pretānnaśrāddhabhoktari ।।

śrāddhasya yājake śrāddhaśiṣṭabhoktaribhoktari ।
doṣassyādvidhinā tatra mahāśāntimathācaret ।।

śrāddhakartiri no doṣa statra dātā bhavetsahi ।
parānnena mukhaṃ dagdhaṃ hastau dagdhau pratigrahāt ।।

parastrībhirmanodagdhaṃ brahmaśāpaḥ kutaḥ kalau ।
dīkṣāmadhye nānyadīkṣāṃ garbhadīkṣāṃ vinā caret ।।

vidhure yajamāne tu dīkṣitaḥ puruṣo bhavet ।
sadāro vā pyadārovā dīkṣitassyātkalatravān ।।

daṃpatī yajamāno cedayamabhyudayo bhavet ।
anagnimatyadāre vā gurau taṃ tu na dīkṣayet ।।

anyasmin padabhājī syādyathāsaṃbhavamādaraḥ ।
vaidhuryasaṃbhave tveṣāṃ madhye duṣyanti naiva te ।।

vatsarāśaucamitaraccāśaucaṃ na pravartate ।
mātāpitrormṛtau yattu proktamabhyudaye punaḥ ।।

dhvajārohaṇahīne tu kṛte niṣphala utsavaḥ ।
kṛtvaivārohaṇaṃ tasmāddhvajasyotsavamācaret ।।

dhvajasyārohaṇaṃ kṛtvā nācaredyadi cotsavam ।
ajñānādarthalobhādvāmāse a nyasmintsamācaret ।।

nakuryācceddvitīye tu māse kartā vinaśyati ।
tasmānniṣkṛtimabjāgnau hutvā tūtsavamācaret ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca nṛsūktaṃ caiva gāruḍam ।
dhvājaṃ śāntaṃ ca cakraṃ ca tathaivotsavadaivatam ।।

vyāhṛtyantaṃ ca hutvā tu vaiṣṇavān pūjya cācaret ।
dhvajasya lakṣaṇaṃ vakṣye yena mānena kārayet ।।

vimānena samaṃ vātha pādenār'dhena vādhikam ।
pādenārdhena hīsaṃ vā pañcadhāpi prakalpayet ।।

jayaśrīkīrtivijayamaṅgalākhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।
ardhahīnaṃ na kurvīta tadevāgatikaṃ bhavet ।।

tasmāccahīnaṃ naiva syādadhikaṃ syāttu śaktitaḥ ।
avakramṛjumanyenāsaṃbaddhaṃ kīlitādibhiḥ ।।

ślakṣṇaṃ manoharaṃ dāru gṛhītvākhaṇḍamuttamam ।
taṃ caturdaśadhā kuryāmmālāgre tena kārayet ।।

bhāgamekaṃ vihāyāgre tatra kuryāttrimekhalāḥ ।
mekhalānāmathāyāmastadbhāgena samo bhavet, ।।

tritālavistṛtaṃ kuryāddaṇḍavistṛtameva vā ।
antaraṃ ca samaṃ teṣāṃ tisraḥ kuryāttu yaṣṭikāḥ ।।

yaṣṭī dve purataḥ kuryātpaścādekā vidhīyate ।
sarvatra kiṅkiṇīnāṃ tu kuryācchatama śeṣataḥ ।।

paścāccheṣaṃ tridhā kuryāccaturdhā vā dhvajaṃ budhaḥ ।
aṣṭāśraṃ ca ṣaḍaśraṃ ca caturaśraṃ ca vṛttakam ।।

mūlādārabhya kurvīta caturdhā vihitaṃ dhvajam ।
tridhā kṛte na kuryāttu ṣaḍaśraṃ śeṣamācaret ।।

ādyaṃ bhāgaṃ tridhā kṛtvā kecidevaṃ prakurvate ।
śikharaṃ śira ityāhurardhena śikharaṃ bhavet ।।

pramādātpatitaṃ gṛhya śikharaṃ sthāpayedvidhiḥ ।
spuṭitevātha bhinne vā biṃbasyoktavadācaret ।।

adhiṣṭite tu śikhare dvijairgṛdhrādibhissakṛt ।
viṣṭhādikaraṇe vāpi uṣite vā nirantaram ।।

vāstuhomaṃ ca hutvaiva paryagnikaraṇaṃ caret ।
eṣa eva vidhiḥ prokto vimānaśikharādiṣu ।।

adhiṣṭhānena pādena prastareṇa ca saṃyutam ।
dhvajamūle tviṣṭakābhirvediṃ kuryānmanoharām ।।

na tāmapyadhitiṣṭheta naro dīrghaṃ jijīviṣuḥ ।
kiṃ punastatra vaktavyamālayādyavarohaṇe ।।

vimānaṃ viṣṇurūpaṃ syānna tatpādādivā kramet ।
dhāmapradakṣiṇe pūrvaṃ kuryāttatra namastriyāḥ ।।

na laṅghayeddhvajachāyāṃ pradakṣiṇavidhiṃ vinā ।
gopurasya vimānasya prākārasyālayasya ca ।।

pramādādatilaṅghyaiva prāṇāyāmaśataṃ caret ।
śivadṛṣṭiṃ viṣṇuvṛṣṭhaṃ durgāyāḥ pārśvato dṛśam ।।

vighneśasyordhvadṛṣṭiṃ ca tīkṣṇamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।
yāvacchāvatarec chāyā tāvatī doṣabhūmikā ।।

doṣabhūmiṃ parityajya nivāsaṃ parikalpayet ।
tyāge saṃpatsamṛddhissyādanyathā viparītakṛt ।।

radhyādibhiryathā bhūyādantaraṃ tanna doṣakṛt ।
atha vā śatadaṇḍāntaṃ tyaktvānve vasatiṃ jaguḥ ।।

yāvaddhāmāyataṃ dāvatpṛṣṭhaṃ vā mughameva vā ।
tatodhikaṃ tacca tacca kecidāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।।

dhvajaṃ nityamuśantyeke yatraiko hyanavāyiṣu ।
tatrārohaṇakarmādi necchanti paramarṣayaḥ ।।

autsavaṃ dhvajamāsthāpya tatra kāryaṃ prakurvate ।
dhvajamekaṃ tu sarvatra kecidāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।।

ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi dhvajadaṇḍe tu niṣkṛtim ।
pramādātpatite bhūmyāṃ dhvaje vātādinā dṛḍhe ।।

abhagne vātha bhagne vā dhvajaṃ tatra pūnaḥ kṣipet ।
abhagne taṃ dhvajaṃ gṛhya kṛtvā mantreṇa takṣaṇam ।।

adhivāsādikaṃ kṛtvā tatthsāne sthāpayedbudhaḥ ।
bhagne dhvaje na sagrāhyastamapsu vidhinā tyajet ।।

tato anyaṃ dhvajamādāya sthāpayedavilaṃbitam ।
corādyairbuddhipūrvaṃ vā pātite pūrvavadvidhiḥ ।।

tatrādhikaṃ prakurvīta śilpibhistakṣaṇaṃ punaḥ ।
abhagnadhvajavatkuryādanyatpūrvavadatvaraḥ ।।

bhāgenānupayuktasya dhvajasya tyājyataiva hi ।
duṣṭabhāgasya dānena na kadācitparigrahaḥ ।।

atha vā sudṛḍaṃ gṛhya pratiṣṭhāṃ mahatīṃ caret ।
duṣṭaṃ bhāgaṃ vyapohyaiva pramāṇaṃ lakṣayetpunaḥ ।।

pramāṇamapramāṇaṃ vā dhvajaṃ nānyena dāruṇā ।
saṃyutāṃ vardhitāṃ kuryādeṣa sārvatriko vidhiḥ ।।

yantu tāmrādinā kuryāllohena kavacādikam ।
bālālayaṃ prakalpyaiva tatrakāryaṃ samācaret ।।

sthitameva dhvajaṃ kuryānna tu taṃ cālayetkvacit ।
dagdhaṃ dhvajaṃ parityajya punaranyaṃ samāharet ।।

dhvaje antyajātibhisspṛṣṭe mahāśāntimathācaret ।
taissamīpamupetaintu sahasrāhutimācaret ।।

patite vātyayā caivaṃ dhvajasya śikhare tathā ।
mekhalāsu ca tatsarvaṃ navīkṛtya yathāvidhi ।।

dhvajadaṇḍe tu saṃyojya pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।
dhvajasya calane cāpi pramādādvraścane tathā ।।

bhagnābhagna dhvajasyoktaniṣkṛtiṃ tu samācaret ।
eṣa eva vidhiḥ prokto daṇḍeṣvanveṣu sarvataḥ ।।

aśanyādinipātena dhāmanyantarite yadi ।
deve naṣṭe dhvaje susthe dhvajasyārādhanaṃ bhavet ।।

ālayaṃ ca punaḥkṛtvā tamevārādhayeddhvajam ।
nirīkṣyatrīṇi varṣāṇi devāgāre tvanirmite ।।

tatra devo na ramate taddhvajaṃ tu tyajetsudhīḥ ।
atha vā yatra kutrāpi pratiṣṭhāpya samarcayet ।।

atha vakṣye dhvajasthānaṃ yathāśāstraviniścitam ।
piṭhagopurayormadhye pañcabhāgaṃ prakalpya ca ।।

pīṭhāttyaktyā caturbhāgaṃ pañcame dhvajasaṃsthitiḥ ।
tatsaṃdhau tu praśastaṃ syādyathā saṃphavamācaret ।।

yadi prākārabāhye syāddhvajaśśāstravadācaret ।
anuktasthānanihitaṃ taṃ ca śāstravadācaret ।।

aśaktau punaranyaṃ ca prākāraṃ kārayetkramāt ।
devadṛgviṣayaṃ kuryāddhvajaṃ laivāparokṣayet ।।

yadā cānyālayairvāpi gopurādibhireva vā ।
abhyantaraṃ bhaveccettu chidraṃ kuryāttu dṛkpathe ।।

vṛkṣādyaiḥpatitairnaṣṭe cālite avanate api ca ।
taddhyajaṃ pūrvavatkuryāttrimāsābhyantare atvaraḥ ।।

kṛmyādibhirvihaṅgairvākoṭarādau kṛte dhvaje ।
kṛtvā bālālayaṃ paścātsamīkṛtyārcayetpunaḥ ।।

rajjubandhādikaraṇe dhvajasyārohaṇe kṛte ।
bālālayaṃ na tatra syādvāstuśuddhiṃ samācaret ।।

prākṣayetpañcagavyaistu dhvajamantreṇa hūyate ।
ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi niṣkṛtāvarcanakramam ।।

uktena vidhinā yatra naṣṭe duṣṭe api vā dhvaje ।
punasthsāpanaparyantaṃ kuryādveṇudhvajaṃ śubham ।।

atha vā kārayedvidvān suvarṇarajatādibhiḥ ।
dhvajaṃ tālonnataṃ sthāpya garbhagehe tu pūjayet ।।

adhivāsādi tatsarvaṃ pratiṣṭhoktavadācaret ।
acalo veṇudaṇḍaḥ syādgarbhagehe bhaveccalaḥ ।।

utsavādau tu sarvatra veṇudaṇḍaṃ samācaret ।
caladaṇḍo veṇudaṇḍa iti syādutsavedvayam ।।

utsavādau pravṛtte tu uktadoṣe tvayaṃ vidhiḥ ।
dhvajasthaṃ garuḍaṃ tasmādavamucya samāhitaḥ ।।

nītvātu yāgaśālāyāṃ saṃsthāpya tu samarcayet ।
veṇudaṇḍaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya sadyastasmin prayojayet ।।

mahāśāntiṃ tathā kuryātsahasrāhutimeva ca ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇudaivatyaṃ gāruḍaṃ dhvājameva ca ।।

saudarśanaṃ ca kūśmāṇḍān śatamaṣṭādhikaṃ yajet ।
tathaiva dīpadaṇḍasya bhavetsarvatra cakramaḥ ।।

dhvaje nāropayeddīpaṃ dīpadaṇḍaḥ pṛthagbhavet ।
tatra dīpaṃ samāropya na labhetphalamavyayam ।।

dhvaje dīpaṃ samāropya vaiṣṇavaṃ śataśo yajet ।
āpatkalpaṃ pravakṣyanti dhvaje dīpāvarohaṇam ।।

dīpayukte dhvaje naṣṭe pūrvavanniṣkṛtiṃ caret ।
vīśapratiṣṭhāhīne tu dhvajasyārohaṇe kṛte ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca nṛsūktaṃ dhvājameva ca ।
gāruḍaṃ daśaśo hutvā pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।।

dhvajadevasya cakrasya śāntanandīśayos tathā ।
hīner'cane vaiṣṇavaṃ ca taddaivatyasamanvitam ।।

hutvaiva punarabhyarcya paścātkāryaṃ samācaret ।
bherītāḍanahīne ca raudraṃ ca vyāhṛtīstathā ।।

hutvā mahāvyāhṛtīśca bherītāḍanamācaret ।
arcanādiṣu sarvatra yatra ghaṇṭāninādanam ।।

eṣa eva vidhiḥ proktaḥ prāyaścittaṃ samācaret ।
āropite tu garuḍe hīne caiva nivedane ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ dhvaṃmetrau ca hutvā gāruḍameva ca ।
nivedayettudviguṇaṃ "kṣama'svetyanumānayet ।।

mudgānne tu tathā hīne vaiṣṇavaṃ vāyudaivatam ।
āgneyamīṅkārādīṃśca gāruḍaṃ dhvājameva ca ।।

hutvā yatnena bahuśo maudgikaṃ ca nivedayet ।
varṣavātātapaissamyagupaghātādisaṃbhave ।।

viṣṭhādyupahate caiva pakṣiṇāmasakṛtsakṛt ।
rajjvāditruṭane caiva pramādātpatane api ca ।।

pātite buddhipūrvaṃ vā akāle apyavaropite ।
śūdrādyairanulomairvā spṛṣṭe dhvajagate paṭe ।।

aśuciṃ śodhayitvānyatsamīkṛtyāsamīkṛtam ।
utsavādhipadaivatyaṃ ṣaḍvāraṃ juhuyādguruḥ ।।

gāruḍaṃ dhvajamantraṃ ca sahastaṃ caiva hūyatām ।
tataśśeṣaṃ samāpyeta viparītaṃ na kārayet ।।

pramādādbuddhipūrvaṃ vā paṭe dagdhe anyamāharet ।
śāntiṃ pūrvoditāṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।।

avarohaṇamudvāsantaṃ ca mantreṇa kārayet ।
avarohaṇahīne tu mantreṇodvāsanaṃ bhavet ।।

tataśśeṣaṃ prakūrvīta aśaktāvavarohaṇe ।
apramāṇaṃ paṭaṃ gṛhya mahāśāntiṃ samācaret ।।

punaranyaṃ samādāya karmaśeṣaṃ samācaret ।
hīne tu cotsavāraṃbhasnapane vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।।

viṣṇusūktaṃ nṛsūktaṃ ca vāruṇaṃ caiva hūyate ।
śuddhodadair abhiṣākassyātprāyaścittavidhissmṛtaḥ ।।

hīne kautukabandhe tu vaiṣṇavaṃ śāntameva ca ।
saudarśanaṃ ca hutvā tu kautukaṃ bandhayetpunaḥ ।।

yajñāgāre kuṃbhavedyāhīne vāpyadhike api vā ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ pāvakaṃ bhūmidaivatyaṃ ca hunedbudhaḥ ।।

toraṇānāmalābhe tu huneddauvārikānmanūn ।
hīnāyāṃ darbhamālāyāmārṣaṃ hutvetarāṅkriyāt ।।

alaṅkāravihīne tu śrīdaivatyaṃ tadhā hunet ।
prātarbaliṃ tu nirvāpya hīne nityotsave tathā ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ śāntavīśau ca hutvā cotsavadaivatam ।
sāyaṃ kuryādutsavaṃ tu dviguṇaṃ kārayetkramāt ।।

sāyaṃ hīnaṃ tu dviguṇaṃ prātarutsavamācaret ।
ekakālotsavaścettu kṛtvā kāladvayaṃ balim ।।

sāyāhne cotsavaṃ kuryātkālātīte apyayaṃ vidhiḥ ।
digdevatāssamāvāhya prathame ahani pūjayet ।।

prācyādi balidānaṃ syādīśānāntaṃ pradakṣiṇam ।
devāhvāne vyatyayassyādvyatīhāro atha vā bhavet ।।

pūrvoktāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ kṛtvā dviguṇaṃ tu baliṃ dadet ।
brahmaṇaśca digīśānāṃ balidānaṃ tu naityikam ।।

adāne niṣkṛtiṃ kṛtvā pūrvoktaṃ ṣaḍguṇaṃ baliḥ ।
catuṣpathādhidevānāṃ vṛkṣādīnāmathecchayā ।।

prathamāvāhanādarvāgvyatyaye pūrvaniṣkṛtiḥ ।
prathamaṃ vāstuśuddhissyādya vai dīyate baliḥ ।।

antaṃ śuddhyanti rathyāstāśśurdhyanti samaye punaḥ ।
akṛtāyāṃ vāstuśuddhau dadyādrathyāsu cedbalim ।।

śāntiṃ kṛtvātu pūrvoktāṃ vāstuśuddhiṃ panarbaliḥ ।
antaśśace vāstuni tu na balibhramaṇaṃ caret ।।

śavamuddhṛtya paścāttu paryagni karaṇaṃ bhavet ।
akāle balidānaṃ syādasuraprītivardhanam ।।

akāle tu baliṃ datvā kāle tu triguṇaṃ baliḥ ।
balibhramaṇadeśassyāddevasya bhramaṇāya hi ।।

nānyatra caryā devasya laghuprokṣaṇa manyathā ।
na hi śraddhotsave doṣamuśantyenaṃ sa hītaraḥ ।।

vāstuvṛddhau tathā hrāse grāmasīmānavīkṛtau ।
anumānya ca deveśaṃ śatāṣṭakalaśāplavaḥ ।।

kṛtvā sīmāṃ viniścitya tataḥ kāryaṃ samācaret ।
astarā cotsavaṃ kuryātsahasrakalaśāplavaḥ ।।

devatāvāhanaṃ kṛtvā tathaivotsava mācaret ।
devādīnāṃ balaṃ yasmādvardhate sa balissmṛtaḥ ।।

śvasūkarādibhirduṣṭairnabhakṣyo balirucyate ।
balibhugvāyasaḥ prokto gomukhyā medhyajantavaḥ ।।

viparīte mahān doṣastanmantrairhāvayecchatam ।
baliśeṣaṃ na śūdro adyādarcako baliśeṣabhāk ।।

balāvamantrakaṃ kṣipte saṃkṣipte vidhivarjite ।
bhakṣite cānulomādyaiḥpūrvoktāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ caret ।।

balau paryuṣite atyuṣṇe tathā caivānivedite ।
nivedanātprāgarvāgvādṛṣṭe śūdrādibhirbalau ।।

pūrvoktāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ kṛtvā sarvatra dviguṇaṃ baliḥ ।
devatāvāhanaṃ yatra deśeprāk kriyate tataḥ ।।

tatraiva balidānaṃ syādyāvadudvāsanaṃ bhavet ।
maṇḍalaṃ ca jalaṃ kūrcamāhvānādhāra ucyate ।।

rathyāsu balidānāya pīṭhaṃ śailādibhirbhavet ।
balidānaṃ tu guptaṃ syānna tatbaśyantyavaidikāḥ ।।

tatthsāvaṃ tu tiraskuryātkāle yavanikādibhiḥ ।
balipradānahīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ balirakṣakam ।।

hutvā tu niṣkṛtiṃ kuryādbalidānaṃ punastadā ।
balidravye atha vā pātre patite bhūtale tathā ।।

bhinne naṣṭe ca pūrvoktaṃ hutvānyaṃ balimāharet ।
balidānaṃ tu kṛtvaiva bhutapīṭhe kṣipettataḥ ।।

baliśeṣamanukte tu sthāne buddhyā tu nirvapet ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ cākṣahamanuṃ vaiṣvakcenaṃ ca gāruḍam ।।

saudarśanaṃ ca hutvaiva bhūtapīṭhe bali kṣipet ।
havirnivedane hīnehīne ca dviguṇārcane ।।

śāntiṃ ca vaiṣṇavaṃ hutvā tathābhyarcya nivedayet ।
yathoktahome hīne tu vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

nṛsūktaṃ ca trayastriṃśatkṛtvo hutvā hunetpunaḥ ।
cakravīśāmitānāṃ ca kuṃbhasthānāmathāpivā ।।

devānāmarcane hīne vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।
nṛsūktaṃ sāntamantrau ca gāruḍaṃ cākrameva ca ।।

hutvā punassamabhyarcya viśeṣeṇa nivedayet ।
devālaṅkaraṇe hīne śrīdaivatyaṃ ca vaiṣṇavam ।।

hudvālaṅkāramāsādya vidhīnā bhūṣayedguruḥ ।
alaṅkāreṣu dravyeṣu niryāsaṃ candanaṃ sumam ।।

taddhitvānyatsamādāya dravyaṃ prakṣālyamantrataḥ ।
pañcagavyaissamabhyukṣya tenālaṅkāra ucyate ।।

nṛtte geye atha vā hīne vaiṣṇavaṃ rudradaivatam ।
stotrahīne tathā brāhmaṃ hutvā sārasvataṃ tataḥ ।।

bhaktabṛndaiḥ parivṛtau hīnāyāṃ vāruṇaṃ tathā ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ śāntadaivatyaṃ hīne picchādike tathā ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ juhuyāttadvaddhavirakṣamanuṃ tataḥ ।
yānātkāle yāgaśālāṃ deve na pratigacchati ।।

bhavennityārcanaṃ tatra yatradevo adhivāsitaḥ ।
dhruvārcanaṃ yathā pūrvaṃ na tatrāsti vyatikramaḥ ।।

devaṃ pratyāgataṃ dṛṣṭyā punaranyotsavaṃ caret ।
dinavyapāye kuryācca tatkālaniyatotsavam ।।

atītamutsavaṃ cāpi tantreṇātra samācaret ।
taddinepyapramādāccedbhūyātkālasya yāpanam ।।

na jahyā devakuryācca tatkālocitamutsavam ।
atra pramādetu bhavetpūrvoktaiva hi niṣkṛtiḥ ।।

dīkṣito vastramālyādyaiḥ pañcāgārpitabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।
carennityaṃ viśuddhātmā viparīte tu doṣakṛt ।।

dīkṣāṅgasya tu vastrasya tathā pratisarasya vā ।
nāśe tatra mahān doṣastadānyatpunarāharet ।।

sahasraṃ viṣṇugāyatrīṃ hutvā śāntimathācaret ।
yāvaddīkṣābhavettāvaddīkṣāṅgasya parigrahaḥ ।।

antetu tadgatāśaktissvayamevāvahīyate ।
atha vā mocanaṃ kuryādite ke cidvadantihi ।।

tatra pūrṇāhutiṃ kālaṃ pravadanti vipaścitaḥ ।
pratiṣṭhānte tu sā dīkṣā bhavedutsavasaṃgatā ।।

na tatra dīkṣāsāṃkaryaṃ dvayamekatra cedyadi ।
anyonyaṃ kalahāyante yadyācāryādayaḥkratau ।।

mahānanarthastatra syātpratibhūrgururatra hi ।
guruvākyaṃ ca rājājñāṃ samamāhurmaharṣayaḥ ।।

dīkṣite vartamāne tu nānyaṃ tatra praveśayet ।
nahyekasmin bhavetkārya ācāryadvaya saṃgatiḥ ।।

pramādādbuddhipūrvaṃ vā kalahe kṣatajasrutiḥ ।
kṣatāni vā bhaveyustaṃ visṛjyānyena kārayet ।।

na tasya tu bhaveddīkṣā mahāśāntiṃ tu kārayet ।
sa dīkṣito bhavedeva pūrvasya pkaṇidhissa hi ।।

yāvadāśaucasaṃkrānti rāśaucetvaśucirbhavet ।
punaranyaṃ samādāya śeṣaṃ pūrvavadāyaret ।।

ādau madhye tadhānte ca hīne brāhmaṇabhojane ।
trivākaṃ tu mahāśāntiṃ hutvā brāhmaṇabhojanam, ।।

dviguṇaṃ kārayeccaiva vaiṣṇavānāṃ tu pūjanam ।
punāti pūjitassadyaḥ pāpmabhyo vaiṣṇapassakṛt ।।

avaiṣṇavaiśca pāṣaṇḍairūḍhe deve dvanarthakṛt ।
taddoṣaśāntaye kuryātsahasrakalaśāplavam ।।

avaiṣṇavakṛtāpūjā hanti puṇyaṃ purātanam ।
yānāttu patite deve śīghramuddhṛtya sādaram ।।

"kṣama'svetyanumānyaiva śuddhodairabhiṣicyaca ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca nṛsūktaṃ sahitaṃ kramāt ।।

dinādhipasya daivatyaṃ hutvā cotsavamācaret ।
cakravīśākhamitādīnāṃ biṃbābhāve pṛthak pṛthak ।।

taṇḍuloparipātreṣu kūrceṣvāvāhya mantrataḥ ।
tattadrūpaṃ tu saṃsmṛtya samabhyarcya vidhānataḥ ।।

hutvā ca tattaddaivatyaṃ paścādutsavamācaret ।
patane tu tathaiteṣāmuddhṛtyaiva ca pūrvavat ।।

snāpayitvā hunettattaddaivatyaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।
yānāttu patite biṃbe hīnāṅge doṣagaurave ।।

padmānale mahāśāntiṃ hutvā taddoṣaśāntaye ।
dhruvabere samāropya taccaktiṃ vidhinā tataḥ ।।

kautukaṃ snāpanaṃ vātha baliberamathāpi vā ।
yathārhaṃ samalaṅkṛtya samāvāhya yathāvidhi ।।

samabhyarcyotsavaṃ kuryānna tatrasyādvyatikramaḥ ।
berāntarasyālābhe tu ratnaṃ vā kāñcanaṃ tathā ।।

nyasya pātre samāvāhya samabhyarcya dine dine ।
mahāśāntiṃ ca hutvaiva punarutsavamācaret ।।

hīnāṅgaṃ ca punarberaṃ saṃdhānavidhinā punaḥ ।
saṃdhāya cātvareṇaiva pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।।

patane gāyagādīnāṃ śrīdaivatyaṃ ca vaiṣṇavam ।
vādakānāṃ tu patanai brāhmaṃ raudraṃ tathaiva ca ।।

ācāryādīnāṃ tu patane saṃkṣobhe ca tathākṛte ।
ārṣabhaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tadvaddhvajādīnāṃ ca pātane ।।

dhvājaṃ ca vāruṇaṃ caiva vāyavyaṃ ca hunedvidhiḥ ।
varṣadhārāsu vātyāyāṃ vidyudvrajasamāhatau ।।

kāle na cotsavaṃ kuryātkuryāccedvaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ nṛsūktaṃ ca śrībhūdaivatyameva ca ।।

hutvotsavaṃ prakurvīta viparīte tu doṣakṛt ।
vīthyantare varṣadhārāpraveśe aśanigarjite ।।

tṛṇapāṃsu samāyuktavātasparśe viśeṣataḥ ।
kalahadhvanisaṃyukte devaṃ saṃsnāpya mantravit ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ digdaivatyaṃ ca vāruṇaṃ vāyudaivatam ।
yaddevādīṃśca hutvaiva punarutsavamācaret ।।

kalahe rudhirasrāve dāhe cāpyutsave tataḥ ।
vaiṣṇapaṃ cāgnidaivatyaṃ brāhmaṃ raudraṃ tathaiva ca ।।

taddinādhipadaivatyaṃ juhuyātprārthayeddharim ।
ālayābhyantare caiva śastrādyairmaraṇe sati ।।

tacchīghramapahāyaiva padmāgnau juhuyāttathā ।
mahāśāntiṃ taddinādhidaivatyaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

vīthyāṃ cenmarahaṇādautu tacchīghraṃ tu vyapohya ca ।
śāntihomaṃ ca hutvaiva punarutsavamācaret ।।

nāḍikāyā athāryākcetpunarutsavamācaret ।
ālayasyāśītidaṇḍābhyantare tu śave sati ।।

tatrotsavaṃ na kuryāttu kuryāccetsa vinaśyati ।
tacchīghramapahāyeva prāyaścittaṃ yathoditam ।।

mahāśāntiṃ pārṣadaṃ ca cahutvā cotsavamācaret ।
lagare vidhireṣassyādgrāmenaiṣa vikalpyate ।।

antaśsavenaiva kuryādutsavaṃ grāmavṛddhaye ।
dhvajasvārohaṇādurdhvaṃ yāvattīrthadinaṃ bhavet ।।

anyātsavaṃ śubhaṃ karma kuryāccedābhicārikam ।
taddoṣaśamanāyaiva vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

nṛsūktaṃ pārṣadaṃ caiva hutvā viprāṃstu bhojayet ।
tīrthāhātpūrvarātrau tu hīne kautuka bandhane ।।

śayane vā vaiṣṇavaṃ ca śrībhūdaivatyameva ca ।
saudarśanaṃ ca hutvānte yathoktaṃ tu samācaret ।।

tīrthasnāne tu kālasyātīte hīne ca vaiṣmavam ।
vāruṇaṃ skandadaivatyaṃ hutvā cauktaṃ samācaret ।।

dhvajāvarohaṇe hīne tadrātrau dhvājameva ca ।
gāruḍaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ hutvā deveśaṃ prārthayedguruḥ ।।

avarohaṇakāre tu balau hīne viśeṣataḥ ।
dhvajadevaṃ susaṃpūjya vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

tadālayasthadevānāṃ mantrāṃścaiva viśeṣataḥ ।
hutvā deveśamabhyarchya dhvajaṃ samavarohayet ।।

utsavāntāplavehīne vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।
puruṣasūktaṃ jayādīnaśca mūrtimantrāśca hāvayet ।।

atrānukteṣu doṣeṣu prāyaścittaṃ bhavedidam ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca nṛsūktaṃ ca tathaiva ca ।।

hūyate viṣṇugāyatrī sarvapāpaprāṇāśini ।
evamaṣṭāviṃśatirvā śaktāvaṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre saptaviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

athāṣṭāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

athāṣṭāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ prāyaścittam

athāspṛśyasparśanetuprāyaścittaṃ pravakṣyate ।
sarpamūṣakamaṇḍūkamārjāranakulādiṣu ।।

garbhāgāraṃ praviṣṭeṣu viṇmūtrādivisarjane ।
vyapohya tatpañcagavyaistathābliṅgābhireva ca ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇugāyatrīṃ śatamaṣṭottaraṃ japet ।
dhruvaṃ cai vādhitiṣṭhatsu viṇmūtrādivisarjane ।।

kṣipraṃ vastreṇa saṃśodya mārjayitvā kuśena ca ।
"āpo hiraṇyavarṇā'bhiḥ "pāpamānī'bhireva ca ।।

saṃsrokṣya cārcayeddevamanyatā viparītakṛt ।
sparśetaireva biṃbānāṃ śuddhodaissnāpayedvidhiḥ ।।

udakyayā sūtikayā rajakenāntyajātibhiḥ ।
prathamāvaraṇe viṣṭe cārcāsthāne ca parṣadām ।।

praviṣṭe cātha saṃspṛṣṭe dārbheṇoddīpya vahninā ।
hutvā ca vāstu yajñeva pañcagavyaissamukṣya ca ।।

kṛtvā puṇyāhamante tu nityāgnau juhuyāttataḥ ।
dauvārikamanuṃ caiva dvārapālaṃ ca vaiṣṇavam ।।

bāṅyāvaraṇapakṣe tu mārjanenopalepanaiḥ ।
prokṣaṇairvāstuyajñeva śuddhirbhavati sarvataḥ ।।

arcākāne tu dṛṣṭeṣu caiteṣu vidhinā harim ।
saṃsnāpya pañcagavyaintu śuddhodaissnāpya cātvaraḥ ।।

prokṣaṇaiḥ prokṣya hutvā tu pūrvavacchārcayettataḥ ।
eteṣu saṃpraviṣṭeṣu cālayābhyantare tathā ।।

tatspṛṣṭahaviṣāṃ caiva pramādāttu nivedane ।
śodhayitvātha taddravyaṃ yathāvidhi viśeṣataḥ ।।

vāstuhomaṃ ca hutvātha paryagnikaraṇaṃ caret ।
pañcagavyaissamabhyukṣya puṇyāhamapi vācayet ।।

saṃsnāpya kalaśairdevaṃ hutvā nityānale tataḥ ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca nṛsūktaṃ raudrameva ca ।।

brāhmaṃ ca śrīmahīsūkte brāhmaṇān bhojayettataḥ ।
spṛṣṭetu caitairbiṃbeṣu dhruvādiṣu viśeṣataḥ ।।

kṛtvātu pūrvavacchuddhiṃ vāstuhomaṃ ca kārayet ।
paryagnipañcagavyābhyāṃ śodhayitvā tataḥparam ।।

saṃsnāpya kalaśairdevamabjāgnau vidhivattadā ।
mahāśāntiṃ ca hutvaiva pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।।

śūdrādyairanulomaiśca spṛṣṭaṃ datvā havistataḥ ।
pañca gavyaiśca śuddhodairdevaṃ saṃsnāpya cādarāt ।।

puṇyāhaṃ kārayetpaśchāddviguṇaṃ tu nivedayet ।
mahāpātakibhiścaiva caṇḍālai pulkasādibhiḥ ।।

ālaye saṃpraviṣṭe tu tatspṛṣṭhe vinivedite ।
saptāhaṃ mahatīṃ śāntiṃ hutvābjāgnau vidhānataḥ ।।

saṃsnāpya kalaśairdevaṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।
punaścadhruvabere vā biṃbeṣyanyeṣu mandire ।।

spṛṣṭeṣu pūrvavacchuddhiṃ kṛtvā dviguṇameva ca ।
hutvā tu mahatīṃ śāntiṃ saṃsnāpya kalaśairvibhum ।।

pratiṣṭhoktakrameṇaiva pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।
patite caiva pāṣaṇḍe cānyatantreṇa dīkṣite ।।

praviṣṭe garbhagehe tu vāstuśuddhiṃ vidhāya ca ।
hutvā tu mahatīṃ śāntiṃ pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।।

ukteṣveteṣu satataṃ prathamāvaraṇe tathā ।
dvitīye vā saṃcaratsu māse atīte viśeṣataḥ ।।

māsamekaṃ mahāśāntiṃ hutvā kṛtvā vidhānataḥ ।
karṣaṇādi punaḥkṛtvā pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।।

tathā saṃvatsare atīte tyaktvā cāvāhanādikam ।
kautukādīntsusaṃrakṣya garbhāgārādi sarvataḥ ।।

vāsayedgā viśeṣeṇa māse atīte viśeṣataḥ ।
sarvatra śuddhiṃ kṛtvātu hutvā māsatrayaṃ tataḥ ।।

mahāśāntiṃ tathā kṛtvā karṣaṇādi punaḥkriyāḥ ।
bālālayaṃ ca saṃkalpya biṃbaśuddhimāthācaret ।।

jalādhivāsanādyaiśca tathā vittānusārataḥ ।
aśītyadhikasāhasraissaṃsnāpya kalaśairharivim ।।

brāhmaṇān bhojayitvaiva saṃpūjyāpi ca vaiṣṇavān ।
bālālaye pratiṣṭhāpya deveśaṃ vidhivattataḥ ।।

ālayaṃ caiva sarvatra navīkṛtya viśeṣataḥ ।
mahāpratiṣṭhāṃ kṛtvaiva devadevaṃ samarcayet ।।

etaissaṃsargiṇāṃ sparśe sūtikāktaiva niṣkṛtiḥ ।
sparśe tatsaṃsargiṇāṃ ca śuddhissyātsnapanādinā ।।

tatassaṃsargiṇāṃ caiva na doṣaḥ parikathyate ।
aśaumavaddvijaspṛṣṭahaviṣāṃ ca nivedane ।।

ekāhaṃ tu mahāśāntiṃ hutvā saṃsnāpya caudakaiḥ ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvaiva pūrvavacca samarcayet ।।

spṛṣṭeṣu cātha biṃbeṣu kautukādiṣu vā dhruve ।
pūrvavanmahatīṃ śāntiṃ hutvā saṃsthāpayetpunaḥ ।।

praviṣṭe cālayādbāṅye sarvatra ca yathārhakam ।
gauravaṃ lāghavaṃ jñātvā sarvamūhyaiva kārayet ।।

khadyaitapakṣijātādipraveśe cālayāntare ।
sparśane caiva biṃbānāṃ kṛtvā paryagni pūrvavat ।।

saṃśodya pañcagavyaistu śuddhodairabhiṣicya ca ।
prokṣaṇaiḥ prokṣyanityāgnau chullyāṃ vā vaiṣṇavaṃ hunet ।।

biṃbādīn tatsamīpasthān saṃśodhyaiva ca pūrvavat ।
śuddhodaissnāpya puṇyāhaṃ kṛtvoktaṃ homamācaret ।।

pūrvamukteṣu deśeṣu śvādīnāṃ vā nṛṇāmapi ।
chedane tāḍane caiva raktasrāve mṛtau tathā ।।

tadvyapauhya ca taddeśaśuddhiṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ ।
vāstuhomaṃ ca hutvaiva kalaśaissnāpya saptabhiḥ ।।

taddoṣaśamanārthaṃ ca mahāśāntiṃ hunettataḥ ।
abhyarcya pūrvavaddevaṃ havissamyaṅni vedayet ।।

saṃbhūte tvālayādbāhye kṛtvā paryagni pūrvavat ।
devaṃ śuddhodakaissnāpya śāntiṃ hutvā vidhānataḥ ।।

saṃpūjya vaiṣṇavāṃścaiva pūrvavatsamyagarcayet ।
deveśasya śave dṛṣṭe saṃsnāpya kalaśairharim ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca pauruṣaṃ juhuyāttataḥ ।
gajāśvapaśumukheṣu prathamāvaraṇe punaḥ, ।।

mṛteṣu tadvyapohyaiva khanitvā tādṛśaṃ sthalam ।
vāstuhomaṃ ca hutvā tu śaddhodairabhiṣicya ca ।।

vaiṣṇapaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca pauruṣaṃ juhuyādvidhiḥ ।
prasvede rudhirasrāve rodane jalpane tathā ।।

hāse dṛṣṭe mahābere satsu dhūmādiṣu svataḥ ।
ālayābhimukhe abjāgniṃ sādhayitvātha vaiṣṇavam ।।

viṣṇusūktaṃ nṛsūktaṃ car iṅkārān pāramātmikam ।
hutvā saṃsnāpya deveśaṃ kalaśaissaptabhiḥ kramāt ।।

samabhyarcya havirdatvā brāhmaṇān bhojya sādaram ।
vaiṣṇavāṃśca susaṃpūjya dadyādāyāryadakṣiṇām ।।

tṛṇavalmīkakīṭādāvutpanne tatra pūrvavat ।
śāntiṃ pūrvoditāṃ hutvābhojayitvāpi brāhmaṇān ।।

devaṃ bālālaye sthāpya navīkaraṇamācaret ।
vimāne tu haṭhādbhinne patite vā vidhānataḥ ।।

śāntiṃ māsatrayaṃ hutvā karṣaṇādi vidhāya ca ।
bālālayaṃ ca saṃkalpya kṛtvā cāpsvadhivāsanam ।।

biṃbaśuddhiṃ tu kṛtvaiva saṃsnāpya kalaśairharim ।
aśītyadhikasrāhasrairyathāvibhavavistaram ।।

brāhmaṇān bhojayitvaiva saṃpūjyaiva tu vaiṣṇavān ।
devaṃ bālālaye sthāpya navīkṛtyālayādikam ।।

sarvatra cāviśeṣeṇa pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।
tatrāśanihate caiva makṣikādiphirāvṛte ।।

saṃsnāpya kalaśairdevaṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā viśeṣataḥ ।
prabhūtaṃ tu nivedyaiva hutvā śāntiṃ vidhānataḥ ।।

brāhmaṇān bhaujayitvaiva punassaṃdhānamācaret ।
sthūpikīle vinaṣṭe tu vimānopari saṃsthite ।।

vimānakalpavatkṛtvā punassaṃdhānamācaret ।
akāśe pratisūryasya darśane vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।।

sauraṃ ca daśakṛtvantu hutvābhyarcya viśeṣataḥ ।
digdāhe vaiṣṇavaṃ digdaivatyamāgneyameva ca ।।

śilāvarṣe vāruṇaṃ ca vaiṣṇavaṃ triścatriṃśatā ।
akāle śaśinaḥ pūrtaukṣaye vā pratidarśane ।।

mahotpāte ca mahatīṃ hutvā śāntiṃ vidhānataḥ ।
devaṃ viśeṣato abhyarca brāhmaṇān bhojayettataḥ ।।

ālayābhyantare bāhyaprākāre vā viśeṣataḥ ।
raktastrīdarśanecaivaṃ taṃ deśaṃ pariśodhya ca ।।

devaṃ viśeṣato abhyarcya havissamyaṅnivedayet ।
dhruvabere kautukādau spṛṣṭe caiva dhruvoditām ।।

śuddhiṃ jalādhivāsaṃ ca kṛtvā saṃsthāpayetpunaḥ ।
garbhālaye tu sarpādidarśane tadvyapohya ca ।।

gomayenopalipyaiva gavyairabhyukṣya pañcabhiḥ ।
aupāsanāgnimādhāya vaiṣṇavaṃ śāntimācaret ।।

puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvaiva brāhmaṇān bhojayettataḥ ।
sarpādau tu mṛte tatra tadvyapauhyopalipya ca ।।

pañcagavyaintu saṃprokṣya vāstuśuddhiṃ vidhāya ca ।
saṃsnāpya kalaśair devaṃ caturviṃśatibhistadā ।।

ekāhaṃ paiṇḍarīkāgnau mahāśāntiṃ vidhāya ca ।
dhruvādiṣu tu biṃbeṣu muhusspṛṣṭeṣu taistathā ।।

devaṃ śuddhodakaissnāpya mahāśāntiṃ vidhāya ca ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvaiva viśeṣārcanamācaret ।।

mṛte prāsādabāhye tu tadvyapohya ca pūrvavat ।
prokṣaṇaiḥ prokṣya ca huneddigdaivatyaṃ ca vaiṣṇadam ।।

pākasthāne gopurādau mṛte sarpe vyapohya ca ।
upalipya ca nityāgnau vaiṣṇavaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

tatthsānādhipadaivatyaṃ daśaśo juhuyādvidhiḥ ।
ālayābhyantare caiva sarpatrāvaraṇe api vā ।।

mahāvāte avivṛṣṭau vā śatrucorādyupaplave ।
saṃsmāpya kalaśairdevaṃ vāstuhomaṃ vidhāya ca ।।

paryagni pañcagavyābhyāṃ śodhayitvā vidhānataḥ ।
puṇyāhaṃ vācayitvaiva vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

nṛsūktaṃ śrīmahīmantrān brāhmaṃ raudraṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
prājāpatyaṃ ca hutvaiva brāhmaṇān bhojayedvidhiḥ ।।

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa bhayarakṣārthaniṣkṛtim ।
corairamitrairatha vā paracakreṇa saṃkule ।।

lohajapratimānāṃ ca tirodhānaṃ prakalpayet ।
śucau deśe sugupte tu khanitvā cāvaṭaṃ ghanam ।।

sikatābhiḥ prapūryaiva kuśānāstīrya copari ।
avaṭe abhyarcya bhūdevī "mapo hi'ṣṭheti prokṣya ca ।।

devāgāraṃ praviśyaiva yajamānayuto guruḥ ।
devadevaṃ praṇamyaiva samabhyarcyānumānya ca ।।

"yāvatkālaṃ bhayaṃ bhūyāttāvadīśa janārdana ।
hariśyā sahita statra śayīdhā' iti sanmanum ।।

vījñāpya śaktiṃ biṃbasthāṃ dhruvabere avaropayet ।
berābhāve tu hṛdaye samāropya vidhānataḥ ।।

"paraṃ raṃha' iti procya pīṭhādādāya cātvaraḥ ।
"pratadviṣṇu stavata' ityavaṭe nyasya rakṣitam ।।

"yadvaiṣṇava'miti procya prākchiraśśāyayettataḥ ।
avaṭaṃ sikatābhirvā mṛdā vā pūrva yatnataḥ ।।

acchidraṃ sudṛḍhaṃ kuryādavaṭaṃ parirakṣitam ।
paścādabhyantaraṃ gatvā devadevaṃ praṇamya ca ।।

grathitaṃ pañcadaśabhirdarbhaiḥ kūrcaṃ pragahya ca ।
dvādaśāṃguladīrghantu jīvasthāne nidhāya ca ।।

dhruvaberātsamādāya tatkūrcer'canamācaret ।
bālālayaṃ bhavecchettu arcāpīṭhe viśeṣataḥ ।।

kūrcaṃ sannyasya hṛdayātpraṇidhyāṃ viniveśyaca ।
kūrcaṃ tu biṃbavatsmṛtvā manasaivākṣarāṇi tu ।।

tattatthsāne tu saṃskṛtya sannyasyāvāhya cārcayet ।
snapanādau tu saṃprāpte kuryādabhyukṣaṇaṃ budhaḥ ।।

māsādūrdhvaṃ tu tatkūrcaṃ vyapohyānyaṃ nidhāpayet ।
kāle tu biṃbamuddhṛtya saṃśodhyāmlādibhistadā ।।

puṇyāhāntekṛte aspṛśya sparśane tvavilaṃbitam ।
kṛtvā jalādhivāsādīnaṅkurārpaṇapūrvakam ।।

ālayābhimukhe vāpi dakṣiṇe vā manorame ।
prapāyāṃ maṇḍapekūṭe yatvābjāgniṃ vidhāyaca ।।

taduttare vāstahomaṃ hutvābiṃbasamīpataḥ ।
paryagnikaraṇaṃ kṛtvā gavyaissaṃśodhya pañcabhiḥ ।।

abjāgnau paścime bhāge biṃbārdhādhikavistṛtām ।
bhāgonnatāṃ yathālobhonna tāṃ dhānyairvidhāya ca ।।

vediṃ manoharāṃ caiva vāsāṃsyāstīrya pañca ca ।
saṃsnāpya kalaśairdivyaiścaturdaśabhireva ca ।।

puṇyāhānte pratisaraṃ baddhvā kautukapūrvakam ।
berāṇi devīsahitaṃ śāyayecchayane śubhe ।।

avatārāṇāṃ tu śayanaṃ pṛthageva vidhīyate ।
pariṣicya ca padmāgnau hautraśaṃsanamācaret ।।

deveśasya ca devyāśca avatāragaṇasya ca ।
dakṣiṇapraṇidhau caiva pārṣadānāmathottare ।।

āvāhya kṛtvā nirvāpaṃ hunedājyāhutīḥkramāt ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣasūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

gāyatrī vaiṣṇavī caiva dvādaśākṣarameva ca ।
prājāpatyaṃ mindāhutī vicchinnaṃ juhuyādayam ।।

śāntihoma iti proktā mahāśāntiṃ jaguḥpare ।
ṣaṇmāne samatīte tu hutvā śāntiṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

saktulājatilāpūpairājyamiśraistu vaiṣṇavam ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ ca pratyekaṃ śataśo juhuyādvidhiḥ ।।

śvetaṃ raktaṃ sarojātamalābhe bilvakacchadam ।
ghṛtāplutaṃ tu vaiṣṇavyā gāyatṣājuhuyāttathā ।।

sarvadaivatyamante ca juhuyātpāramātmikam ।
enameke mahāśāntihomamācakṣate budhāḥ ।।

paścādapyavatārāṇāṃ tattanmantraṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
pṛthagaṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā rātriṃ nayettataḥ ।।

snātvā prabhāte deveśaṃ praṇamya praṇavena tu ।
bodhayitvābhivandyaiva "karuṇābdhe kṣamasya me ।।

śataṃ sahasramayutamasaṃkhyeyaṃ muhurmuhuḥ ।
kṛtānāmaparādhānā'miti saṃprārthya bhaktitaḥ ।।

prācīna vastramālyādīn dyapohyanyairvibhūṣya ca ।
sarvavādya samāyuktaṃ śākunaṃ sūktamuccaran ।।

toyadhārāṃ puraskṛtya gacchettu purato guruḥ ।
sthāpakā devamuddhṛta kṛtvā dhāmapradakṣiṇam ।।

abhyantaraṃ praviśyaiva sthāpayeyuśca pūrvavat ।
devapādau gurusspaṣṭvā vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

pauruṣaṃ cātmasūktaṃ ca japtvā dhyātvā vidhānataḥ ।
dhruvādvā hṛdayācchaktiṃ praṇidhyāṃ tu niveśya ca ।।

kṛtvākṣarāṇāṃ vinyāsamāvāhanamathācaret ।
tadālayagatāṃś caiva devānanyāṃ tsamāhvayet ।।

puṇyāhaṃ vācayetpaścādyathoktaṃ pūrvamācaret ।
yajamānopi śuddhātmā dadyādācāryadakṣiṇām ।।

paścādagniṃ paristīrya śāntihomaṃ samācaret ।
yathāvibhavavistāramutsavaṃ snapanaṃ caret ।।

aśaktassnapanaṃ kuryādanyatsarvaṃ ca pūrvavat ।
kūrcādāvarcane hīne tanniṣkṛtimathācaret ।।

evaṃ caidvatsa re atīte punasthsāpanamācaret ।
avatāraviśeṣasya pṛthakkuryāditītare ।।

teṣāṃ punaḥpratiṣṭhā cettattaddhomaṃ tu ke cana ।
idthaṃ syādbhayarakṣārthaniṣkṛtissarvasiddhitā ।।

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa punarbālālayaṃ budhāḥ ।
mahābere vimāne ca patite jarite tathā ।।

bhinneṃgahīne nihate vātyayāśaninātha vā ।
varṇakṣaye sthalabhraṃśe garbhagehasya cānyathā ।।

pīṭhagarbhādināśe vā aspṛśyairvā praveśane ।
unnatasthāpanecchāyāṃ kuryādbālālayaṃ hareḥ ।।

bālālaye abhyarcyamāne saṃbhūte sthānasaṃkaṭe ।
caṇḍālādhiṣṭhite caiva sthānanāśe hradādibhiḥ ।।

anyatra tūcite deśe kṛtvā pūrvoktamārgataḥ ।
karṣaṇādikriyāssarvā biṃbamānīya cādarāt ।।

pratiṣṭhāpya tu tatraiva kuryānmūlālayaṃ tataḥ ।
bāhye caiva vimānasya cāṅgopāṅgakṣatau tathā ।।

makṣikātṛṇavalmīkapādapādyairvibhedane ।
vinā bālālayasthānaṃ śaktiṃ gṛhya vimānagām ।।

tadaṅgadevatānāṃ ca samāropya dhruve punaḥ ।
navīkṛtya vimānoktapratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।।

akṛtvā devatāropaṃ mahābere viśeṣataḥ ।
vimānaṃ nādhitiṣṭheta sarvatrāyaṃ vidhissmṛtaḥ ।।

vimānadhruvayornāśe yugapattatraniṣkṛtiḥ ।
kautukādīn pratiṣṭhāpya vihāya prārthanāmanum ।।

bālālayaṃ prakalpyaiva vidhinā tatra cārcayet ।
tasya kāle apyatīte tu tadā tatra na doṣakṛt ।।

yasyāṅgasya bhaveddhānistatra bālālayaṃ bhavet ।
kṛtvā tasya tu saṃskāraṃ yathoktaṃ tatpunaścaret ।।

kautukādivināśe ca doṣayukte dhruve tathā ।
vimāne ca tathā duṣṭe kṛtvā bālālayaṃ punaḥ ।।

yathālābhena mānena biṃbamāhṛtya dāravam ।
pratiṣṭhāpyādyataruṇālayoktavidhinā tataḥ ।।

kautukādīṃśca saṃkalpya pratiṣṭhāpyārcayetkramāt ।
alābhe kautukādīnāṃ doṣayukte tu dārave ।।

biṃbamasyaṃ samāhṛtya pratiṣṭhāpyaiva dāravam ।
tadberaṃ vidhivattyaktvā kṛtvā mūlālaye punaḥ ।।

vidhinā mūlaberaṃ tu pratiṣṭhāpya samarcayet ।
bālālayasya saṃsthānaṃ vakṣye mūlālayasya tu ।।

madhyasūtrāddakṣiṇe ca prathamāvaraṇe tathā ।
dvitīyāvaraṇe vātha maṇṭapādau manorame ।।

yatrāvakāśastatraivaṃ bālāgāraṃ prakalpayet ।
dvitīyāvaraṇādūrdhvaṃ na bālāgārakalpanam ।।

ekādi tu trihastāntaṃ vistāraṃ tu vidhīyate ।
adhyardhaṃ caiva pādonamutsedhaṃ dviguṇaṃ tu vā ।।

utsedhaṃ pañcadhā kṛtvādhiṣṭhānaṃ caikamaṃśakam ।
bhittyuccaṃ dvyaṃśamatha ca dvyaṃśaṃ tu śikharaṃ matam ।।

lupopare tṛṇācchannaṃ mṛṇmayaṃ kārayetsudhīḥ ।
bhittiviṣkaṃbhamānaṃ syānmūlālayasamaṃ tathā ।।

dviguṇaṃ caturguṇaṃ kṛtvā yacchiṣṭaṃ vidhinā kṛtam ।
nālīgṛhaṃ bhavedvindyāttameva taruṇālayam ।।

maṇḍapādiṣu cedbhittyā saha tasya yathārhakam ।
nālīgṛhaṃ maṇḍapena pramukhe rahitaṃ tu vā ।।

sahite tu samaṃ kuryāttripādaṃ cārdhameva vā ।
pūrvāparayutaṃ vātha dakṣiṇottaramāyatam ।।

samaṃ vā taruṇāgāraṃ śilpaśāstroktavaccaret ।
pañcaviṃśatibhāgaṃ tu kṛtvā garbhālayaṃ tataḥ ।।

madhye brāhmaṃ padaṃ caikaṃ parito aṣṭau tu daivikam ।
mānuṣaṃ tasya paritaḥ padānyanyāni ṣoḍaśa ।।

kautukaṃ brahmaṇasthsāne sthāpayeduttamaṃ bhavet ।
daivike mānuṣe sthāpya madhyamaṃ cādhamaṃ bhavet ।।

trīṇi tu snapanādīni berāṇi sthāpayetsadā ।
antyayoreva nānyatra sthānabhedaḥ praśasyate ।।

prāṇasthānetu pīṭhaṃ syādramyamekatrimekhalam ।
yathālābhāyataṃ tadvadvistāro tsedhasaṃyutam ।।

ratnanyāsavihīnaṃ vā kṛtvā vibhavavistarāt ।
ālayāgre atha vā bālāgārāgre pūrvavadbudhaḥ ।।

yāgaśālāṃ tu kṛtvaiva toraṇādīnvidhāya ca ।
subhṛtyaiva ca saṃbhārānṛtvijovarayetkramāt ।।

śālāmadhye prakalpyaiva śayyāvediṃ manoharam ।
caturaśrāṃ pādahīnāmardhahīnāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

tadbhittyātu samāṃ tatturīyāṃśotsedhasammittām । pañcatrīnathavai kāgniṃ saṃkalpyaiva ca pūrvavat।।

paryagni pañcagavyābhyāṃ saṃśodhya vidhinā tataḥ ।
bālāgāraṃ yajñaśālāṃ puṇyāhamapi vācayet ।।

hutvāgnikuṇḍeṣvāghāraṃ pradhānāgniṃ samindhya ca ।
gāyatrīṃ vaiṣṇavīṃ caiva vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

pauruṣaṃ caikākṣarādi śrībhūsūktaṃ ca vāruṇam ।
pañcamantrān jayānabhyātānān rāṣṭrabhṛtastathā ।।

midāhutī ca vicchinnamṛddhiṃ vaiṣṇavasaṃyutam ।
pratyekaṃ pratimantraṃ ca hutvāṃ ca samanantaram ।।

śvetābjaṃ viṣṇugāyatṣāghṛtāktaṃ bilvapatrakam ।
hunedaṣṭottaraśataṃ sarvadoṣavināśanam ।।

rātripūjāvasāne tu devamabhyarcya yatnataḥ ।
havirnivedya tāṃ śaktiṃ kautukādiṣu saṃgatām ।।

mahābere samāropya kuṃbhamāhṛtya pūrvavat ।
tantunā pariveṣṭyaiva "śucī vo havya'mantrataḥ ।।
