prakṣālyotpavanaṃ kṛtvā "dhārāsvi'ti ca mantrataḥ ।
adbhirāpūryābhimṛśya "idamāpaśśivā' iti ।।

vastrayugmena cāveṣṭya navaratnādi vinyaset ।
uccāryaviṣṇugāyatrīṃ tatra kāryaṃ samācaret ।।

tato abhyantaramāviśya devāgre dhānyamaṇḍale ।
sannyasya kuṃbhamāsitvā devāgre tūttarāmukhaḥ ।।

samāhito hariṃ dhyāyan prārthayenmantramuccaran ।
"anarhametattvadgehaṃ jīrṇaṃ tūrṇaṃ vyapohya ca ।।

kiñcitkālaṃ ca deveśa tvayātra sthīyatāṃ vibho ।
yāvadvayaṃ navaṃ kṛtvā pratiṣṭhāṃ kārayāmahe ।।

prasādaṃ kuru tāvattvamasmin gehe jagatpate' ।
ityuktvābdamatha dvautrīn saṃkalpyāvadhimādarāt ।।

devyādisahitaṃ devamāvāhyāṃbhasi kuṃbhake ।
ācāryaśśirasā kuṃbhaṃ dhārayannagratastviyāt ।।

tadanu sthāpakābiṃbanyādāya snapanāvaṭe ।
yajñālaye pratiṣṭhāpya caturdaśabhireva ca ।।

kalaśaissnāpya vastrādyairalaṅkṛtya samarcyaca ।
śayyāvedyāṃ dhānyapīṭhe śayanāni tu pañcavai ।।

āstīrya cātha vāsāṃsi baddhvā pratisaraṃ tataḥ ।
tathaiva śāyayetkuryāduttarācchādanaṃ punaḥ ।।

pariṣicya pradhānāgniṃ hautraśaṃsanamācaret ।
kṛtvā cāvāhanādīni hunedagniṣu pūrvavat ।।

pradhānāgnau sruveṇājyamādāyaiva tu vaiṣṇavam ।
gāyatrīṃ vaiṣṇapaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ pauruṣameva ca ।।

ekākṣarādisūktaṃ ca śrībhūdaivatyameva ca ।
trirhutvā sarvadaivatyaparṣadāṃ mantrameva ca ।।

hutvā vyapohya vidhinā rātriśeṣaṃ samāhitaḥ ।
snātvā prabhāte deveśaṃ praṇamya pramavena tu ।।

vibodhya dakṣiṇāṃ dadyādyajamāno mudānvitaḥ ।
tato agniṃ sādhayitvā tu gurussviṣṭakṛtaṃ tathā ।।

pūrṇāhutiṃ ca hutvaiva visṛjyāgniṃ vidhānataḥ ।
dhārayan śirasā kuṃbhaṃ śākunaṃ sū"ktamuccaran ।।

ācāryaḥ purategacchetthsāpakāstadanastaram ।
hastābhyāṃ devamādāya sarvavādyasamāyutam ।।

sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ to yadhārāpurassaram ।
ālayaṃ parito gatvā praviśyābhyantaraṃ punaḥ ।।

vihāya sthirarāśiṃ tu sumuhūrteviśeṣataḥ ।
"pratadviṣṇu'riti procya prāṇapīṭhe hariṃsmaran ।।

pratiṣṭhāpya tu deveśaṃ tasya dakṣiṇavāmayoḥ ।
śriyaṃ bhuvaṃ ca mantrābhyāṃ tayossaṃsthāpayetkramāt ।।

devapādau spṛśan paścādviṣṇusūktaṃ japan guruḥ ।
kṛtvākṣarāṇāṃ nyāsādī "nidaṃ viṣṇuṃ'ti bruvan ।।

kūrcenādāya kuṃbhasthāṃ śakti"māyātu' mantrataḥ ।
"viṣṇumāvāhayā'mīti kautukasya tu mūrdhavi ।।

"śriyaṃca "hariṇīṃ'ceti devyau dakṣiṇavāmayoḥ ।
saṃsrāvyāvāhayeddevāṃstataḥ pāriṣadānapi ।।

kautukāddakṣiṇe vāme snapanādīni kautukāt ।
saṃsthāpya tu samāvāhya tāvatkālaṃ samarcayet ।।

sthāpakaissaha puṇyāhaṃ kṛtvābhyarcyāsanādibhiḥ ।
havirnivedya deveśaṃ hutvā homaṃ ca naityikam ।।

baliṃ nirvāpya kurvīta balibhramaṇameva ca ।
snapanaṃ cotsavādīni pūrvavatkārayetkramāt ।।

bālālayārcane kuryādarcanaṃ tu dhruvārcayoḥ ।
āvāhanaṃ visargaṃ ca hitvā sarvaṃ samācaret ।।

mahānasādinirmāṇaṃ bālālayavidhau punaḥ ।
sūlālayoktavatkuryādviparītaṃ na kārayet ।।

ajñānādarthalobhādvā kālasyātikrame sati ।
devaṃ viśeṣato abhyarcyaśāntiṃ vaiṣṇavasaṃyutam ।।

hutvā saṃpūjya pūjyāṃśca yajamāno gurustathā ।
saṃprārthya devaṃ kālasya cāvadhiṃ jñāpayetpunaḥ ।।

bhaktinamra stataḥkutyācchīghraṅkarmedamādarāt ।
evaṃ dvādaśavarṣāntaṃ kārayeccha tataḥ param ।।

na ra meta haristatra tasmā duktaṃ samācaret ।
aśaktaścettathā kartuṃ bālāgālāntaraṃ punaḥ ।।

saṃkalpyasthāpayettatra viparītakṛdanyathā ।
dehāddehāntaraprāptau yathā saṃskriyate naraḥ ।।

tathā sthānāntanaprāptau pratiṣṭhāṃ kārayeddhareḥ ।
prathame atha dvitīye nā naṣṭe bālālaye arcite ।।

duṣṭe vā yena kenāpi maṇḍapādau manoramam ।
deśaṃ tu samalaṅkṛtya saṃśodhya vidhivatpunaḥ ।।

saṃsthāpya kautukādīṃśca samabhyarcyedvidhānataḥ ।
bālālayaṃ navīkṛtya tadeva tvaritaṃ yathā ।।

vāstuśuddhiṃ ca puṇyāhaṃ kṛtvā saṃsthāpya cārcayet ।
ayuktetu tatastasminnidhāyānyatra mandiram ।।
punaḥ pratiṣṭhāmārgeṇa pratiṣṭhāpya samarcayet ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre aṣṭāviṃśo adhyāyaḥ

athaikonatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ 
prāyaścittam
athavakṣye viśeṣeṇa dhruvaberasya niṣkṛtim ।
tāmrajaṃ śailajaṃ caiva mūrtikaṃ dāravaṃ tviti ।।

cāturvidhyaṃ dhruvasyātra pūrvameva mayoditam ।
ṣaṇmānasahitaṃ kṛtvāsanālaṃ pādapadmakam ।।

kṛtvā tu tāmrajaṃ biṃbaṃ kautukasyoktavartmanā ।
kṛtvākṣyunmocanaṃ cādhivāsān saṃsthāpya cācalam ।।

sthāpayetsaha devyauca śuddhyarthaṃ pratiparvatu ।
śuddhodairabhiṣicyaiva bhūṣaṇaiśca vibhūṣyaca ।।

puṣpanyāsaṃ ca kṛtvaiva sarvān pariṣadaḥ kramāt ।
śailāneva prakurvīta yathā śātātapo abravīt ।।

śailaṃ dhruvaṃ tathā citraṃ citrārdhaṃ vā vidhāya ca ।
pūrvoktena vidhānena paraṃ saṃskṛtya tatkramāt ।।

devyāvanyāṃśca devāṃśca tadālayagatānapi ।
taddravyeṇa prakurvīta dhruvaṃ ṣaṇmānasaṃyutam ।।

kṛtvākṣṇośca bhruvostadvadoṣṭhayorubhayorapi ।
karapādatale caiva nakheṣu mukuṭe api ca ।।

bhūṣaṇeṣu vidhānena tattadvarṇena lepayet ।
mṛṇmayaṃ dāravaṃ vā cettaddravyeṇaiva devatāḥ ।।

tadālayagatāḥ kuryādanyathā viparītakṛt ।
atha vā varṇahīnaṃ tu śailaṃ sarvatra kārayet ।।

ardhacitrasya śailasya hīneṣvaṃ geṣu caiva hi ।
pratyaṅgeṣu tathopāṅgeṣvaniṣṭaṃ tadbhavediha ।।

bālāgāre atha tacchaktiṃ nītvā biṃbaṃ samāharet ।
bhūmau pidhāya tasyordhve padmāgniṃ parikalpya ca ।।

hutvā ca mahatīṃ śāntiṃ śilāgrahaṇavattathā ।
tattadaṅgasamutpattiṃ yuktyā takṣṇā tu kārayet ।।

hīne mahāṅge tadberamayuktaṃ cetsamīkṛtau ।
tyaktvā tadvidhinā beraṃ punaranyatsamāharet ।।

beraṃ saṃdhānayogyaṃ yastyajetpāpī bhavetsa hi ।
vinaṣṭaṃ ca bhavetsarvaṃsaṃdhānaṃ śaktitaścaret ।।

dhruvaberamathār'cāṃ ca kartuṃ pūrvamivadvayam ।
aśaktaśceddhruvārcāntu kṛtvā caikaṃ svaśaktitaḥ ।।

pratiṣṭhāpyārcayetsamyagiti ke cinmanīṣiṇaḥ ।
ekaberapratiṣṭhāyāmeṣa eva vidhissmṛtaḥ ।।

aśaktaśceddhruvaṃ beramarcāberamathāpi vā ।
sahitaṃ rahitaṃ vātha devībhyāṃsthāpya cārcayet ।।

mṛdālaye brahmasthāne dhruvārcāberamāharet ।
taṃ devīsahitaṃ kṛtvā vimānaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

śailaṃ tu kartumicchecced devo daivikamāśrayet ।
yathā tathā prakalpyaiva vimānaṃ kautukaṃ punaḥ ।।

lohajaṃ jaṅgamaṃ kṛtvā braṅmasthāne samācaret ।
kautukaṃ śailajaṃ cettu sthāvaraṃ tveva sthāpayet ।।

laghuberaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya vimāne mṛṇmaye arcite ।
kartumiccheddhruvaṃ beraṃ vimānaṃ caiva śailajam ।।

vimānaṃ parikalpyaiva vidhinā hastamānataḥ ।
devībhyāṃ sahitaṃ devaṃ daivikāṃśe vidhāya ca ।।

pūrvārcitāṃ gṛhītvaiva beraṃ kautukakarmaṇi ।
tasyottare cautsavādīn pratiṣṭhāpya samarcayet ।।

pūrvaṃ dhruvārcāberetu arcyamāne mṛdālaye ।
śilābhiriṣṭakābhirvā vimānaṃ kartumicchayā ।।

rakṣārthaṃ tasya berasya śilpisparśanivṛttaye ।
kāṣṭhena pañjaraṃ kṛtvā bālāgāraṃ dṛḍhaṃ tataḥ ।।

saṃśodhya śalyaṃ cādhastādyuktyā paramāyā punaḥ ।
vimānaṃ yugmahastena tadberasya vaśādapi ।।

yathāvibhavavistāraṃ saudhaṃ kṛtvā surakṣayet ।
tadberasamamadhyardhaṃ dviguṇaṃ caturaśrakam ।।

adhamaṃ madhyamaṃ tadvaduttamaṃ trividhoditam ।
kṛtvā tasya caturbhāgaṃ tribhāgaṃ cārdhamevavā ।।

garbhāgāraṃ bhaveccheṣaṃ bhittiviṣkaṃbhameva ca ।
samaṇṭapaṃ vimānaṃ tu pūrvavatkārayedvidhiḥ ।।

śileṣṭakāvimāne tu vargasyānte parasya vā ।
kārayenmiśramatha cedaśaktaḥ kartumīdṛśam ।।

adhiṣṭhānasya cordhvaṃ hi yatheṣṭasthānake punaḥ ।
miśradravyeṇa kuryāttu śaktilobhaṃ na kārayet ।।

varṇakṣayedhruve doṣasaṃphade sphuṭitādibhiḥ ।
alpadoṣe api vāśaktiṃ dhruvaberasthitāṃ tadā ।।

kuṃbhe aṃbhasi samāvāhya tatkuṃbhaṃ kautukādi ca ।
samādāya vidhānena mālikāyāṃ tu maṇḍape ।।

sannyasya kautukādau tu samāvāhya samarcayet ।
kāle kuṃbhe samāropya kriyāssarvāssamācaret ।।

atīte dvidine kuṃbhamanyadādāyacātvaraḥ ।
kuṃbhācchaktiṃ samādāya kuṃbhe anyasmin vidhālataḥ ।।

arcayettridine caivaṃ kuṃbhasaṃśodhanaṃ caret ।
paścācca varṇalepādīn kṛtvā saṃśodya caivahi ।।

vāstuhomaṃ ca puṇyāhaṃ dhruvaśuddhiṃ ca kārayet ।
kuṃbhaṃ biṃbaṃ samādāya praviśyābhyantaraṃ tataḥ ।।

kautukādīn susaṃsthāpya nyāsādīṃśca vidhāya ca ।
kuṃbhasthāṃ śaktimādāya dhruvabere avaropayet ।।

dhruvātpunaḥ kautukādiṣvāvāṅya tu samarcayet ।
doṣāṇāṃ goravānmāsādūrdhvaṃ kāletvapekṣite ।।

devaṃ bālālaye sthāpya śodhayenmṛṇmayaṃ punaḥ ।
yāvacchūlaṃ punaśśailaṃ śilāntaṃ śodhayetkramāt ।।

navaṣaṭpañcamūrtīnāṃ vimāne doṣasaṃyutam ।
yattalaṃ tattalaṃ gṛhya bālasthānaṃ prakalpya ca ।।

kautukādīn susaṃsthāpya vidhinā samyagarcayet ।
paścāttale tu nirduṣṭe kautukādīn pragṛhya ca ।।

sthāpayitvā punaścaiva vidhināpi samarcayet ।
atha vakṣye jīrṇaberaparityāgavidhiṃ kramāt ।।

dhruvasyāṅgavihīne tu tyajettatsadya eva hi ।
kartrārādhakayorgrāhyamanyathā syānmahadbhayam ।।

tasmātsarvaprayatnena jīrṇaṃ saṃśodhya sarvataḥ ।
navavastraissamācchādya baddhvā ca kuśarajjubhiḥ ।।

brāhmaṇairvāhayitvaiva nadīṃ sphārāṃ samudragām ।
aśoṣyaṃ vā jalādhāramanyannītvātha tattaṭe ।।

prapāṃ kṛtvāgnimādhāya caupāsanamatandritaḥ ।
āghārānte tu juhuyādvaiṣṇavaṃ śataśastataḥ ।।

"dadbhyassvā''hetyaṅgahomaṃ vyāhṛtyantaṃ hunedbhudhaḥ ।
vastrabandhaṃ vimocyaiva prāṅmukhodaṅmukho guruḥ ।।

vāruṇaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ caiva prakṣipyaiva ca tajjale ।
snāyātsaṃsmṛtya deveśaṃ dārave tu viśeṣataḥ ।।

dagdhvāgninātha tadbhasma nikṣipettādṛśe jale ।
devyādīnāṃ parṣadāṃ ca tattanmantraṃ savaiṣṇavam ।।

hunejjalekṣipetpaścāddadyādācārya dakṣiṇām ।
atha cetkautukādīnā maṅgahānistaducyate ।।

mahāṅgāni śiraḥ kukṣi vakṣaḥ kaṇṭhān pracakṣate ।
pādauhastau bāhavaścetyaṅgāni pravadantihi ।।

aṅgulyaḥ karṇanāsādyāḥ pratyaṅgāni vidurbudhāḥ ।
śiraścakraṃ ca pīṭhaṃ ca prabhāmaṇḍalameva ca ।।

upāṅgānyūcire bhūṣaṇāyudhāṃbarapūrvakān ।
tatropāṅgasya hīne tu kuṃbhaṃ saṃsādhya pūrvavat ।।

āvāhya kuṃbhe tacchaktiṃ biṃbaṃ saṃdhāya pūrvavat ।
kṛtvā jalādhivāsādīn vāstuhomaṃ vidhāya ca ।।

saṃśodya pañcagavyaiśca kuśodaiśca viśeṣataḥ ।
saptabhiḥ kalaśaisthsāpya kuṃbhasthāṃ śaktimādarāt ।।

samāvāhya punarbiṃbe vidhinā samyagarcayet ।
pratyaṅgahīne tacchaktiṃ mahābere avaropya ca ।।

udhrutya biṃbaṃ saṃprokṣya pañcagavyaiḥ kuśodakaiḥ ।
tulyalohena saṃdhāya cādhivāsya kuśādiṣu ।।

punaḥ pratiṣṭhāmārgeṇa pratiṣṭhāṃ punarācaret ।
aṅgahīnetu saṃdhānayogyaṃ saṃdhāya pūrvavat ।।

arcayedanyathā yuktehīne vāpi mahāṅgake ।
bhūmau pidhāya tadberaṃ tadūrdhve juhuyātkramāt ।।

aṅgahomaṃ mahāśāntimapohyaiva ca taddinam ।
uddhṛtya biṃbaṃ prakṣālya pañcagavyaiḥ kuśodakaiḥ ।।

triragnau saṃparikṣipya śodhayedāmlavāriṇā ।
rājataṃ dvissakṛdraukmaṃ dahedagnāviti kramaḥ ।।

kṛtvātenaiva dravyeṇa biṃbaṃ pūrvavaduttamam ।
punaḥpratiṣṭhāṃ kṛtvaiva kārayedarcanaṃ kramāt ।।

paṭe kuḍye atha vā likhya bere vidhivadarcite ।
jīrṇamālokya tacchaktimāropyaivārkamaṇḍale ।।

navīkṛtya punastasmin pratiṣṭhāpya samarcayet ।
ācāryeṇa ca yenādau karṣaṇādyāḥ kṛtāḥ kriyāḥ ।।

pratiṣṭhā vā kṛtā viṣṇostenaivānyāṃśca kārayet ।
nityārcanotsavādīṃśca prāyaścittādikānapi ।।

tadabhāve ca tatputraṃ pautraṃ naptārameva ca ।
tadvaṃśajaṃ vā tacchiṣyaṃ tanniyuktamathāntataḥ ।।

ācāryasannidhau nānyamācāryaṃ varayetkvacit ।
varayedyadi rāṣṭrasya rājñaścāpi mahadbhayam ।।

bhavecca niṣphalā pūjā sarvaṃ kāryaṃ vinaśyati ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena na kuryādgurusaṃkaram ।।

ajñānādarthalobhādvā kṛte tvācāryasaṃkare ।
abjānale mahāśāntiṃ hutvā saṃprārthyavai gurum ।।

yācayitvā "kṣama''sveti pūjayitvā viśeṣataḥ ।
panastenaiva tatkarma kārayediti śāsanam ।।

ācāryadīnāmalābhe tu tadrūpaṃ lekhayetpaṭe ।
tatsannidhau yuktamanyamācāryaṃ varayettathā ।।

ekasminnālaye syāccetsannipātastu karmaṇām ।
ācāryaṃ saṃpraṇamyaiva tatputrādyairvidhānataḥ ।।

kārayettadalābhetu kārayettantrato guruḥ ।
pūrvaṃ tu yogamārgeṇa pratiṣṭhāpyārcite punaḥ ।।

devībhyāṃ saha paścāttu kārayet sthāpanaṃ yadi ।
ābhicārikameva syādrājarāṣṭravināśakṛt ।।

dhruvakautuka saṃyukte pūjyamāne purā tataḥ ।
vimānadhruvayornāśe brahmasthāne dhruvārcanam, ।।

kautukaṃ cotsavasthāne sthāpayediti ke cana ।
sthānake cāsanaṃ kuryācchayanaṃ vāpi cecchayā ।।

asaneśayanaṃ kuryātthsānakaṃ na tu kārayet ।
śayane nāsanaṃ caiva sthānakaṃ kārayedvidhiḥ ।।

kautukaṃ sthitamāsīna mautsavaṃ kārayettathā ।
asīnaṃ kautukaṃ kuryātthsitamautsavameva vā ।।

snapanaṃ baliberaṃ ca sthitaṃ sarvatra kārayet ।
avatāragaṇasyaiva mūrtīnāṃ pañcakasya ca ।।

anyonyasaṃkareṇaiva sthāpane kautukasya ca ।
mahattaro bhaveddo, staddoṣaśamavāya vai ।।

hutvā tu mahatīṃ śāntiṃ yathāsthāne tu sthāpayet ।
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa śāntipañcakakalpanam ।।

narāṇāṃ pāpabāhulyādaparādhaviśeṣataḥ ।
devāssṛjantyadbhutāni teṣu dṛṣṭeṣu satvaram ।।

kuryācchāntiṃ yathoktāntu viparīte tvanarthakṛt ।
kartrārādhakayoścaiva rājño rāṣṭrasya vāstuvaḥ ।।

saṃkṣobho jāyate sadyo vināśo bhavati dhruvam ।
dvādaśāhāntare tasmācchāntiṃ kuryādvidhānataḥ ।।

atīte dvādaśāhetu mahāśāntipurassaram ।
saṃpūjya vaiṣṇavān śaktyādatvā vai bhūridakṣiṇām ।।

ārabheduttaraṃ karma māse atīte viśeṣataḥ ।
saptāhaṃ tu mahāśāntiṃ hutvā vipraśataṃ tathā ।।

bhojayitvā ca deveśamanumānya tu kārayet ।
ṣaṇmāse samatīte tu ramate tatra nohariḥ ।।

tasmātsarvaprayatnena kuryācchāntiṃ yathoditām ।
bhaumāntarikṣadivyākhyabhedāttrividhamadbhutam ।।

grahayuddhaśca bhedaśca vikāro grahamaṇḍale ।
sarvagrāsoparāgaśca durbhikṣaścākṣabhedanam ।।

evamādīni divyāni tvadbhutāni pracakṣate ।
āntarikṣāṇi cārkendvoḥ pariveṣo nirantaraḥ ।।

varṇāntareṇa bāhulyātpariveṣastathāvidhaḥ ।
rātrāvindradhamardevasadma cākāśamaṇḍale ।।

aśanyulkādipātaśca rāhupucchādidarśanam ।
nakṣatrapatanaṃ ketordhūmasyendrasya darśanam ।।

gandharvanagarasyāpi darśanaṃ patanaṃ tu vā ।
pratisūryābjanakṣatradarśanaṃ saṃpracakṣate ।।

bhaumānyanekathoktāni carasthiravibhedataḥ ।
deśakālasvabhāvādiviruddhaṃ prasavādikam ।।

pṛṣadaṃśakasarpāśvayonijānāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
gonāgamahiṣādyeṣu tiryakṣu jananaṃ tathā ।।

kṛmikīṭapataṅgeṣu viṣkireṣvaṇḍajādiṣu ।
vivarṇākāravāsādirāśrayādistathālaye ।।

raktastrīdarśanādīni cādbhutāni careṣu tu ।
divyāni cāntarikṣāṇi teṣāmatrottamottamam ।।

nārāṇi cottamāni syurmāhiṣādyāni madhyamam ।
sarīsṛpādiṣu bhavānyathamāni vadantihi ।।

rodanaṃ hasanaṃ jalpo jvalanaṃ parivartanam ।
svedaśca rudhirasrāvaḥ kṛmikīnādisaṃbhavaḥ ।।

akālasphoṭanaṃ dhūmaścāṅgakaṃpanameva ca ।
svāpanāsvādanecaiva tṛṇavalmīka saṃbhavaḥ ।।

pratimāyāṃ bhaveccettu raktastrīdarśanaṃ tathā ।
pāṣaṇḍapratilomāntyajātibhiḥ patitaisthathā ।।

sṛgālādibhiraspṛśyaissparśane ca praveśane ।
sthūṇāvirohaṇe caiva calane parivartane ।।

tathāpasarpaṇe caiva kavāṭaśayanāsane ।
bhittyāyudhāṃbare tadvadagnihotrādyupaskare ।।

vimāne ca vikāraśca makṣikāvṛkṣapātane ।
pravartane copasarpe parṇapuṣpaphaleṣu ca ।।

śākhādau viparītasya darśanaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
raktasrāvo jalasrāvaścādbhutāni sthireṣu tu ।।

teṣu garbhakṛhe caiva pīṭhe caiva bhavāni tu ।
rājñorāṣṭrasya viprāṇāṃ nāśakāni viśeṣataḥ ।।

kartrārādhakayornāśa iti śātātapo abravīt ।
prāsādajāni rājñāṃ syuḥ prāsāde api viśeṣataḥ ।।

adhiṣṭhāne ca pāde ca prastare ca gale api ca ।
śikhare ca bhavāni syuḥkṣatriyāṇāṃ krameṇa tu ।।

abhiṣekasya yogyasya yuvarājasya caiva hi ।
abhiṣiktasya samrājaścātyāhitakarāṇi tu ।।

prathamāvaraṇe vaiśyajātīnāṃ mantriṇāṃ tathā ।
purohitasya tanmaṇḍalādhipānāṃ mahadbhayam ।।

śūdrajātivipaddhetdvitīyāvaraṇādiṣu ।
sasyanāśo gajāśvādipaśunāśasca jāyate ।।

purodhasaścāgnikuṇḍe brahmasthāne dvijanmanām ।
rudrālaye tu sarveṣāṃ nṛpasya tu guhālaye ।।

seneśānāṃ vipattiḥ syādvakratuṇḍālaye tathā ।
śṣālaye rājapatnīnāṃ durgāsthāne anyayoṣitām ।।

mātṛsthāne antyajātīnāmoṣadhīnāṃ kuberake ।
nṛpavāhanaśastropajīvināṃ bhāskarālaye ।।

anyadevālaye tattadbhoktānāmapi lakṣayet ।
āsthānamaṇḍapasaṅgamaṇḍabaprāṅgaṇeṣu ca ।।

mahānase nṛpāvāse krīḍāsthāne viśeṣataḥ ।
ācāryayajamānādipadārthinilayeṣu ca ।।

caityavṛkṣādiṣūdbhūtā raktastrīdarśanādayaḥ ।
valmīkādyāśca phaladāstattaddiśyuktamārgataḥ ।।

bhaumeṣu devaberārcāpīṭhagarbhagṛhārte ।
jātādoṣāntu saṃproktā uttamottamasaṃjñitāḥ ।।

uttamāstupunarjātāḥ prākāremukhamaṇḍape ।
madhyamāḥ prathamāvaraṇe śeṣeṣūktāstathādhamāḥ ।।

tathā rājāṅgaṇe cottamottamāḥ paritastataḥ ।
aṅkaṇeṣūttamā antarvāstuke madhyamāssmṛtāḥ ।।

adhamā vāstuno bāhye tāratamyamiti smṛtam ।
divyāntarikṣayornāsti cikitsā śāntiriṣyate ।।

bhaumeṣu tu careṣvatra nimittaṃ ca nimittinam ।
deśāntare vāsayitvā śāntintatra samācaret ।।

sthireṣu pratimānāṃ tu rodane hasane tathā ।
jvalane ca tathā devaṃ saṃsthāpya taruṇālaye ।।

tadberasthāṃ samāropya śaktiṃ tatra vidhānataḥ ।
śāntiṃ kṛtvā punaḥ kuryātthsāpanaṃ cārcanaṃ kramāt ।।

parivṛttau punasthsāpya kuryācchāntyādi pūrvavat ।
svede ca rudhirasrāve sarvaṃ rodanavaccaret ।।

kṛmikīṭapataṅgānāṃ kṛṇādīnāmathodbhave ।
āropya pūrvavacchaktiṃ punassaṃdhāya yuktitaḥ ।।

śāntyādīnācaredevamakālasphoṭanādike ।
berārcāpīṭhake tadvadālayābhyantarepe ca ।।

valmīkādyudbhave devaṃ saṃsthāpya taruṇālaye ।
yāvaddoṣaṃ khanitvaiva gavyairabhyukṣya pañcabhiḥ ।।

saṃśodhya sarvaṃ saṃdhāya punasthsāpana mācaret ।
prāsādabāhye cotpanne vivare viśadīkṛte ।।

peṣayitvā marīcyādijalenāpūrya cāśmanā ।
ālipya śarkarāṃ kuryāc chāntiṃ divyapracoditām ।।

punarapyudite kuryādevameva tuyuktitaḥ ।
makṣikādarśane tattyadvyapohyatvavilaṃbitam ।।

śodhayitvā tataśśāntimārabheta vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
aspṛśyaspakśane tadvatkṛtvā śāntiṃ samācaret ।।

sthūṇāvirohaṇādau ca punassaṃdhāya cācaret ।
haṭhādvṛkṣādhipatine śānti stattyāgapūrvikā ।।

rājāṅgaṇe samutpanne rājānaṃ sabalaṃ punaḥ ।
veśmāntaraṃ vāsayitvā śāntiṃ kṛtvā yathocitām ।।

abhiṣicya punaryuktedine rāṣṭraṃ praveśayet ।
athottamottamasyottamasya syānmadhyamasya ca ।।

adhamasyāpi cāspṛśyasparśanasya yathākramam ।
krameṇādbhutaśāntistu prabhūtā mahatī tathā ।।

śāntiśśuddhiriti prājñaiḥ pañcadhā śāntirucyate ।
ālayābhimukhe tadvadaiśānyāṃ cottare atha vā ।।

parvatāgre taṭākasya tīre vā maṇḍapaṃ prapām ।
kūṭaṃ vā ṣoḍaśastaṃbhasaṃyuktāṃ sumanoharam ।।

caturhastapramāṇāntastsaṃbhāntarasamāyutām ।
tānonnatācalāyuktāṃ? kṛtvā madhye vidhānataḥ ।।

kuṇḍaṃ śrāmaṇakoktaṃ tu kṛtvādho dvādaśāṅgulam ।
khanitvaiva cat prācyāṃ dvihastāyata vistṛtam ।।

hastamātrasamutsedhaṃ kṛtvā sthaṇḍilamuttamam ।
prāgādiṣu caturdhikṣu krameṇāhavanīyakam ।।

anvāhāryaṃ cāvasathyaṃ gārhapatyaṃ ca kārayet ।
agneyādiṣu koṇeṣu kuṇḍānyaupāsanāni ca ।।

kṛtvādvāreṣu vidhinā toraṇādi prakalpayet ।
pūrmakaṃbhairaṅkuraiśca kadalībhirdhvajairapi ।।

staṃbha veṣṭanakādyaiśca darbhamālābhireva ca ।
alaṅkṛtya vitānādyairyathāvibhavastaram ।।

sthaṇḍile dhānyarāśiṃ tu kṛtvā tasya ca madhyame ।
padmamaṣṭadalaṃ kṛtvā taṇḍulaistasya madhyame ।।

sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmraṃ kṛṇmayaṃ vā svaśaktitaḥ ।
dvātriṃśatprasthasaṃpūrṇaṃ kaṃbhamādāya śāstravat ।।

tantunā pariṣṭyaiva yavāntaramanantam ।
vastrayugmena saṃveṣṭya bhūṣaṇaiśca vibhūṣya ca ।।

sauvarṇa maṅgalānyaṣṭau tathā pañcāyudhāni ca ।
varṇacihnāni tādṛṃśi cāhīnānyaṅgulādapi ।।

ratnāni hema rajataṃ tāmraṃ kāṃsyaṃ tathā trapu ।
sīsāyastīkṣṇukāntāni graharūpāṇi caiva hi ।।

nikṣipyāpūrya toyeva śuddhena tu vidhānataḥ ।
karpūracandanośīralavaṅgailādikānapi ।।

gandhadravyāṇi cānyāni nyasya cūtādipallavān ।
tanmukhaṃ tu pidhāneva pidadhyātsadṛśenavai ।।

ācāryamṛtvijaścāpi vṛtvā śāstravidhānataḥ ।
navavastrottarīyādyaiḥ pañcāṅgārpitabhūṣaṇaiḥ ।।

alaṅkṛtyāgnikuṇḍeṣu hutvāghāraṃ yathoditam ।
madhye sūryaṃ tathendrādi bhārgavāṅgārakau tathā ।।

mandaṃ guruṃ pāvakādi candrarāhudhvajān budham ।
pradakṣiṇavaśenaiva dhyātvāvāṅyār'cayet tataḥ ।।

aṣṭākṣareṇāyutaṃ vā sahasraṃ cāṣṭasaṃyutam ।
abhimṛśya vidhānena grahayajñoditena vai ।।

hunecca tattaddaivatyaṃ samiccarughṛtaiḥ kramāt ।
hutvāṣṭottarasāhasraṃ tato vaikhānasānale ।।

ghṛtāplutairbilvadalairaṣṭottara sahasrakam ।
hunedaṣṭākṣaraṃ nityaṃ tathā bilvasamidghetaiḥ ।।

dūrvāpūpavrīhitilacarulājābjasaktubhiḥ ।
vaiṣṇavyācaiva gāyatṣā pūrvavajjuhuyādguruḥ ।।

ghṛtenāṣṭākṣareṇaiva sahasraṃ cāṣṭasaṃyutam ।
hutvānte tu ghṛtenaiva vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktakam ।।

juhuyātpauruṣaṃ sūktaṃ nṛttairgeyaiśca ghoṣayet ।
yathādiśaṃ caturvedānnityamadhyāpayetkramāt ।।

kalpasūtramathaukheyaṃ praṇītaṃ guruṇā purā ।
svādhyāyo yatra yatroktastatrādhyeyaṃ vidhānataḥ ।।

ṛtvigbhyo dakṣiṇāṃ dadyādevaṃ saptāhamācaret ।
yadi devālaye doṣaḥ kuṃbhapārśvetha sthaṇḍile ।।

devaṃ taṃ sthāpya cābhyarchya nivedya ca mahāhaviḥ ।
devasyābhimukhe hutvā homamante yathāvidhi ।।

navāhaṃ vātha stāham utsavaṃ kārayedvidhiḥ ।
divyāntarikṣayoḥ kuṃbhajalenā plāvayennṛpam ।।

bhaumeṣu tatthsalaṃ prākṣya śiṣṭatoyena vai nṛpam ।
tatpatnīṃ cābhiṣiñcecca guruṃ saṃpūjya pārthivaḥ ।।

suvarṇapaśubhūmyādīn dadyādṛtvigbhya eva ca ।
dakṣiṇāṃ bahulāṃ dadyājjīvo yajñasya dakṣiṇā ।।

yadi rājagṛhe doṣaḥ kṛtvā maṇḍapamantike ।
pūrvavadgrahayajñaṃ ca homaṃ śrāmaṇake anale ।।

kuṃbhasya sādhanaṃ kṛtvā saptāhānte prabhuṃ tathā ।
snāpayetkuṃbhatoyena pratiṣṭhāntakrameṇa vai ।।

dakṣiṇāṃ gurupūrvebhyo datvā kṛtvāṃkurār'paṇam ।
śubhe anukūle nakṣatre kṛtvā caivābhiṣecanam ।।

praviśetpūrvagehaṃ tu dharmasiddhyaigurūditaḥ ।
eṣa eva vidhiḥ prokto gṛhiṇāmapi sammataḥ ।।

rājñāṃ parārthavṛttitvātso atra tu prakṛtīkṛtaḥ ।
sarvagrāsoparāgādidivyādbhutaśamāyavai ।।

yathāśakti brāhmaṇebhyassvarṇaṃ bhūmiṃ paśūnapi ।
dadyāttathā viśeṣeṇa dakṣiṇāṃ bhūrisammitām ।।

anāvṛṣṭinivṛttyarthaṃ kuṃbhaṃ saṃgṛhya pūrvavat ।
sarvatīrthaṃ samāvāhya samabhyarcyāgrato hareḥ ।।

dhyānyapīṭhe tu sauvarṇaṃ padmamaṣṭadalairyutam ।
hemapātre tu sannyasya devamāvāhya tatra ca ।।

abhyarcya tasya cordhvetu pīṭhe kuṃbhaṃ nidhāya ca ।
kuṃbhamūle tu suṣiraṃ sūcīmātraṃ vidhāya ca ।।

taddhārayā tvavicchinnarūpayā secayeddharim ।
samidbhirvaitasībhistu pālāśībhirathāpi vā ।।

aṣṭhottarasahastraṃ tu juhuyātpañjavāruṇam ।
agnau śrāmaṇake paścāddiśāhomeṣu pūrvavat ।।

aṣṭāttarasahasraṃ tu pratyekaṃ pañcavāruṇam ।
samidbhirjuhuyādvidvān vaitasībhiryadhāvithi ।।

samidbhiḥ punarājyena vaitasībhiḥ pṛthagghunet ।
aṣṭādhikasahasraṃ tu "indraṃ praṇayanta'' mityapi ।।

śrāmaṇāgniṃ vidhāyaikaṃ dakṣiṇe tasya vajriṇam ।
āvāhya tu samabhyarcya "śacīsahā''yeti homayet ।।

devaṃ viśeṣato abhyarcya kārayetsnapanādikam ।
evaṃ jñātvā vidhānena tattatkarmasu gauravam ।।

tṣahādi triṃśadghasrāntaṃ śrāmaṇāgnau yathāvithi ।
dine dine pūrayitvā kuṃbhaṃ tenaiva secayet ।।

sarvānte devamāsnāpya samabhyarcya havirdadet ।
karmānte syānmahāvṛṣṭistasmādyatnena kārayet ।।

atha vā varṣa kāmī vā mokṣārthī paśukāmanaḥ ।
sarvopadravaśāntyarthī vijayārthī viśeṣataḥ ।।

snapanālayamāsādya alaṅkṛtya ca pūrvavat ।
karmagauravamājñāya saṃbhṛtya bahudhā payaḥ ।।

pūjayetprathamaṃ yatnādācāryaṃ sahi dhārakaḥ ।
ācāryassuprasannātmā śvabhrātprācyāṃ tu taṇḍulaiḥ ।।

kṛtvā paṅktiṃ dakṣiṇottarāyatāṃ vipulāntarām ।
śvabhrāddakṣiṇataḥ kṛtvā kuṇḍaṃ śrāmaṇakasya tu ।।

agnimādhāya kuṃbhāṃ stu nava saṃveṣṭya tantunā ।
adbhiḥ prakṣālya cotpūya kuśakūrcena cātvaraḥ ।।

kṣīreṇa pūrayitvaiva cotbūtena krameṇa vai ।
paṅktiṃ nidhāyāpidhānairapidhāyopari kramāt ।।

vastreṇācchādayecchvabhraṃpūjāntebhyarcya vai harim ।
svastisūktena cānamya saṃsthāpya śvabhramadhyame ।।

arcanoktavidhānena sarvaṃ pūrvanadāyaret ।
tantunā veṣṭite kṣīraṃ kṛhītvākarake pūnaḥ ।।

viṣṇusūktena "ceṣe''tvetyādyairmantraiḥ kramādguruḥ ।
tayā saṃsnāpayeddenamuktayo kṣīradhārayā ।।

tathaiva pariṣicyāgniṃ mantrai"rviṣṇornu''kādibhiḥ ।
"atodevādi''bhistadvadaṣṭārṇa manunā tathā ।।

juhuyādviṣṇugāyatṣā aṣṭādhikasahasrakam ।
atha vā snapanaṃ yāvattāvadudvartya mantrataḥ ।।

hāridrena tu cūrṇena saṃśodhyāmlādibhistataḥ ।
gandhodena susaṃsnāpya plotena vimṛjettataḥ ।।

vastrādibhiralaṅkṛtya samabhyarcya vidhānataḥ ।
pāyasādi havirdadyāddapyādācāryadakṣiṇām ।।

anena sarvān kāmāṃśca labhetāviśayaṃ naraḥ ।
dhruvaberārcane cettu saṃsnāpya pramukhe ghaṭam ।।

tasmādānīya tatraiva snāpayeduktagauravāt ।
saptapañcatṣahānyatra kṣīrasnānaṃ prakalpayet ।।

evaṃ ghṛtābhiṣekaṃ ca kārayetsadṛśaṃ phalam ।
imāmadbhutāśāntintu kāśyapādyāḥ pracakṣate ।।

atha prabhūtaśāntiṃ tu pravakṣyāmi tapodhanāḥ ।
pūrvavanmaṇṭapādīni kārayitvā yathāvidhi ।।

viśāhomaṃ cakṛtvaiva śrāmaṇāgnau yathoditam ।
kuṃbhaṃ saṃsādhya ca prāgvatsaptāhānte viśeṣataḥ ।।

aṣṭottaraśataṃ vāṣṭacatvāriṃśadathātha vā ।
saṃgṛhya kalaśānāntu samabhyarcya'bhiṣecya ca ।।

devaṃ viśeṣato abhyarcya havirdadyādayaṃ vidhiḥ ।
mahāśāntikramaṃ vakṣye vinā kuṃbhasya sādhanam ।।

agnau śrāmaṇake bilvapatrairājyāplutaiḥkramāt ।
aṣṭādhikasahasraṃ vai hunedaṣṭākṣareṇa tu ।।

ājyena vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ pauruṣameva ca ।
hutvā tṣahānte saṃsnāpya śuddhasnapanavartmanā ।।

samabhyarcya havirdadyānmahāśāntiriyaṃ bhavet ।
aupāsanāgnāvekāhaṃ hutvā śāntiṃ vidhānataḥ ।।

brāhmaṇān bhojayitvaiva dadyādācāryadakṣiṇām ।
atha śuddhividhiṃ vakṣye vāstuhomaṃ hunettataḥ ।।

bilvapatrādibhirhutvā pṛthagaṣṭottaraṃ śatam ।
puṇyāhānte guruṃ pūjya bhojayedbrāhmaṇānapi ।।

sarvatratu vikalpena ghaṭasaṃskāramācaret ।
athātassarvaśāntissyādapamṛtyubhaye tathā ।।

grahakope mahāvyādhau paracakrabhaye tathā ।
arthabandhuvināśe ca durbhikṣe ca parājaye ।।

abhicārabhaye caiva tāpatrayanipīḍane ।
viruddhe acātmanaḥ prāpte sarvaśāntiṃ samācaret ।।

saptāhaṃ vā navāhaṃ vā dvādaśārṇena vai pṛthak ।
aṣṭottara sahasraṃ tu juhuyādvidhinā kramāt ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ sihitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre ekonatriṃśo adhyaḥ

athatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ 
prāyaścittam
athavakṣye viśeṣeṇa tantrasaṃkaraniṣkṛtim ।
vaiṣṇavasyānyatantreṇa saṃkare doṣamādiśet ।।

grāmasya yajamānasya rājño rāṣṭrasya saṃkṣayaḥ ।
taddoṣaśamanāyaiva sāṃkaryamapahāya ca ।।

padmāvale vaiṣṇavaṃ ca viṣṇusūktaṃ ca pauruṣam ।
pāramātmikamīṅkārā dyaṣṭāśītiṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

aṣṭottarasahasraṃ vā śatamaṣṭottaraṃ tu vā ।
doṣagauravamuddiśya hutvā pūrvavadācaret ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ dvividhaṃ śāstraṃ munibhiḥ parikīrtitam ।
vaikhānasaṃ pañcarātraṃ vaidikaṃ tāntrikaṃ kramāt ।।

vaikhānasaṃ vaidikaṃ syādvaidikairarcitaṃ dvijaiḥ ।
aihikāmuṣmikaphalapradaṃ saumyaṃ prakīrtitam ।।

pañcarātramathāgneyamavaidikamatāttvikam ।
tāpādipañcasaṃskāradīkṣāvadbhissamarcitam ।।

aśrīkaramatha proktaṅkevalāmuṣmikapradam ।
saumyaṃ sarvatra saṃpūjyaṃ grāmādiṣu viśeṣataḥ ।।

brāhmaṇānāṃ ca geheṣu saumye nai vārcayeddharim ।
āgneyamarcayettadvadavāstvaṅgālaye tathā ।।

parvatādiṣvaraṇyeṣu vivikteṣu sthaleṣuca ।
viprāvāse janāvāse naiva kuryādanena tu ।।

saumye vaikhānase mārge yadyāgne yena saṃkaraḥ ।
pañcarātreṇa saṃprāpto rājā rāṣṭraṃ vinaśyati ।।

taddoṣaśamānāyaiva padmāgnau juhuyātkramāt ।
mahāśāntiṃ vidhānena saptāhaṃ vā tṣahantu vā ।।

aṣṭādhikaśadaiścaiva saṃsnāpya kalaśaistataḥ ।
abhyarcya devadeveśaṃ saṃpūjyaiva tu vaiṣṇavān ।।

bhojayitvā brāhmaṇāṃstu kārayetpūrvavartmanā ।
pañcarātravidhānena pratiṣṭhāpyārcanekṛte ।।

kālenāntarite tasmin kuryātsaumya praveśanam ।
saumyatvādrājarāṣṭrāṇāṃ tatsa mṛddhikaraṃ bhavet ।।

padmānale mahāśāntiṃ hutvādau ca tataḥkramāt ।
vaikhānasena vidhināvimānaṃ biṃbameva ca ।।

saṃskṛtya cocitaissarvaiskaṃskāraiḥ karṣaṇādibhiḥ ।
pratiṣṭhāpya tadārabhya sarvaṃ tenaiva cācaret ।।

ālayāśritadevānāṃ parivārasya parṣadām ।
pūjāyāmapyamukhyāyāṃ saṃkaro naiva sammataḥ ।।

mahātmyaṃ kimuvakṣyāmi śāstrasya mahato asya vai ।
nālaṃ devāstrayassendrā ananto apyupavarṇitum ।।

śruṇantu munayassarve śāstramāhātmyamuttamam ।
yāvacchakti pravakṣyāmi jñātaṃ gurukṛpābalāt ।।

purā caturmukho brahmāsisṛkṣurakhilaṃ jagat ।
suptodthitaściraṃ kālaṃ prākrāmītsargakarmaṇi ।।

visasmāra yadā dhātā nidrayākrāntamānasaḥ ।
vedāntsargapradhānāṃstu sṛṣṭirnaivapravartate ।।

cintātura stadā brahmā mūḍhaḥ kartavyakarmaṇi ।
bahudhā dhyāyamānastuna lebhe kāraṇaṃ svataḥ ।।

svaśaktyā yadvidheyaṃ syātsarvaṃ cakre vimūḍhadhīḥ ।
na hi tatkāraṇaṃ lebhe vedavismaraṇaṃ tu yat ।।

cirācchintāṃ tu tāṃ tyaktvā svasthacittaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
hṛtpadmamadhye puruṣaṃ parameṇa samādhinā ।।

cintayāmāsa vai viṣṇumṛgyajussāmarūpiṇam ।
tuṣṭāva ca tadā brahmā haripravaṇamānasaḥ ।।

nanāma ca tadā viṣṇuṃ śaṅkhacakragaddharam ।
arcayāmāsa deveśaṃ pādyādyairvigrahaissamaiḥ ।।

muhurmuhuḥ praṇamyāthamūrthnā devaṃ jagatpatim ।
nirvyājakaruṇāleśāddevasya vimalāntaraḥ ।।

tuṣṭāvajagadīśānaṃ nārāyaṇamajaṃ vidhiḥ ।
"jitante puṇḍarīkākṣa namaste viśvabhāvana ।।

namaste astu hṛṣīkeśa mahāpuruṣa pūrvaja ।
deśakālaparicchedarahitānanta cinmaya ।।

satyajñānasukhānandasvarūpa parameśvara ।
pañcavyūha caturvyūhāna ntavyūhātmavigraha ।।

viṣṇo puruṣa satyācyutāniruddha jagatpate ।
nityamuktajanāvāsaparamavyomanāyaka ।।

śrībhūnīlādisaṃsevya divyamaṅgalavigraha ।
śaṅkhacakragadāvāṇe bhaktābhayavaraprada ।।

kīrīṭa hāra keyūra kaṭakāṅgadabhūṣita ।
graiveyakapariṣkāra kaṭīsūtravirājita ।।

tulasīmālikārājadviśālorasthsalāṃcita ।
pralaṃbayajñasūtrāḍhya kaustubhābharaṇojjvala ।।

sarvalokeśvarācintya śrīvatsakṛtalakṣaṇa ।
divyāyudhasamāsevya pītāṃbarasuśobhita ।।

nityaniryatnanirandhravisārikaruṇārasa ।
mandasnitamukhāṃbhoja madhurādharapallava ।।

rukmābha raktanetrāsyapāṇipāda sukhodvaha ।
subhrūlalāṭasubhaga sunasa svāyatekṣaṇa ।।

vṛttapīnāyatabhuja tanumadhya mahāhano ।
vilāsavikramākrānta trailokyacaraṇāṃbuja ।।

jñānaśakti balaiśvaryavīrya tejovidhe anagha ।
namaste viṣṇave tubhyaṃ puruṣāya namo namaḥ ।।

samassatyasvarūpāya acyutāya namo namaḥ ।
namo aniruddharūpāya vāsudevāya śārṅgiṇe ।।

namaścidātmane ananta śāntarūpāya dhanvine ।
śāsate nirapekṣāya svatantrāyādhikāriṇe ।।

acyutāyāvikārāya tejasāṃ nidhaye namaḥ ।
pradhāna puruṣeśāya vedavedyāya vedine ।।

namaḥ para vyūharūpa namo vibhavavigraha ।
antaryāminnamaste astu namor'cārūpa śāśvata ।।

sahasraśīrṣaṃ puruṣaṃ sahasrākṣaṃ nirañjanam ।
sahasrapādaṃ trātāraṃ śaraṇaṃ tvāṅgato asmyaham ।।

mātā tvaṃ me pitā tvaṃ me bhrātā tvaṃ me sakhāmama ।
sarvaṃ tvamasi viśvātmaṃstvayi sarvaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।।

saṃsārasāgaraṃ ghoramanantaṃ kleśabhājanam ।
tvāmeva śaraṇaṃ pāpya nistaranti manīṣiṇaḥ ।।

na hi te gopya te kiñcinna hyantyaviditaṃ tava ।
tvaṃ sākṣī dehināmekassarvaṃ vyāpya tvamedhase ।।

na te rūpaṃ na karaṇaṃ kāraṇaṃ nāsti te anagha ।
tvaṃ śāstā sarvalokānāṃ sraṣṭāpātā haran hare ।।

ahaṃ bhavaśca te brahman prasādakrodhajāvubhau ।
tvatto me mānasaṃ janma prathamaṃ dvijapūjitam ।।

vijñānaṃ tadidaṃ prāptaṃ brahmatvaṃ ca yadārjitam ।
sarvaṃ tava kaṭākṣasya leśo ayaṃ madhusūdana ।।

tamasākrāntacittasya vismṛtā nigamā mama ।
avedavihitassargo mayā kartuṃ na śakyate ।।

prasīda parameśāna vedabhikṣāṃ prayaccha me ।
iti cintayatastasya babhūvāvāvilaṃ manaḥ ।।

tatastubhagavān brahmā vedarāśimavāptavān ।
sasmāra nikhilānvedān sāṃgānupaniṣadgaṇam ।।

purāṇanyāyamīmāṃsādharmaśāstrāṇi sarvaśaḥ ।
catuṣṣaṣṭikalāścaiva vidyāsthānāni yāni ca ।।

antarhitānāṃ khananādvedānāntu viśeṣataḥ ।
sa vibhuḥ procyate brahmā vikhanā brahmavādibhiḥ ।।

vaikhānasaśca bhagavān procyate sa pitāmahaḥ ।
jagatsarvamaśeṣeṇa vedadṛṣṭena vartmanā ।।

prāṇācca cakṣuṣastadvadabhimānācca marmaṇaḥ ।
hṛdayācchirasaśśrotrādudānādvyānatastataḥ ।।

samānācca tathāpānādṛṣiśreṣṭhānimān daśa ।
dakṣaṃ marīcinaṃ nīlalohitaṃ bhṛgumena ca ।।

tathāṃgirasamatriñca pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ tathā ।
vasiṣṭhaṃ cakratuṃ caiva kramādasṛjadabjabhūḥ ।।

nava brahmāṇa evai te vināsyurnīlalohitam ।
vedānāṃ vyasanādarpāk prāgrūpaṃ militaṃ tu yat ।।

tāntu vaikhānasīṃ śākhāyetānadhyāpayanmuniḥ ।
nāmnā vikhanasaṃ prāhuryaṃ ca śātātapaṃ tathā ।।

bhṛgvaṅgiromarīcyatripulastyapulahāḥkratuḥ ।
tathā vasiṣṭhodakṣaśca nava brahmāṇar iritā ।।

।
ete vikhanasaśsiṣyāśśrutismṛtividhānataḥ ।
tacchiṣyāstu mahātmāno munayastattvadarśinaḥ ।।

vedānugāni śāstrāṇi cakrurlokahitaiṣiṇaḥ ।
ke cidgṛhyāṇi vai cakrurgṛhyaśrautātmakāni tu ।।

dharmaśāstrāṇi kecittu purāṇāni ca ke cana ।
itihāsāṃs tathākalpān procuranye maharṣaya? ।।

ke cidvyākaraṇaṃ kecinnyāyamanye tathetarat ।
vāṅmayaṃ sakalaṃ sarvaṃ śāstrabaddhaṃ pracakrire ।।

tāntuvākhānasīṃ śākhāṃ svasūtre viniyuktavān ।
padmabhūḥparamo dhātā tasminnārādhanatrayam ।।

tāntu vaikhānasīṃ śākhāṃ svasūtre viniyuktavān ।
cakre ṛgādibhedaistu vyasitvā tu pṛthak pṛthak ।।

ādikāle tu bhagavān brahmātu vikhanā muniḥ ।
yajuśśākhānusāreṇa cakresūtraṃ mahattaram ।।

varṇāśramācārayutaṃ śrautasmārtasamanvitam ।
yatsūtrādyantamadhyeṣu bhagavān viṣṇuravyayaḥ ।।

yaṣṭavyo gīyate yasmātsarvasūtrottamaṃ tu tat ।
vede vaikhānase sūtre yo dharmaḥ parikīrtitaḥ ।।

sarvaissadharmonuṣṭheyo nātra kāryāvicāraṇā ।
svasūtrasya parityāgādanyasūtrasamāśrayāt ।।

sadyaḥpatati vai viprona vedasya samāśraye ।
sūtraṃ vaikhānasaṃ yattu vedassaṃpratipadyate ।।

etadvaikhānasaṃ sūtramanyasūtrānapekṣitam ।
etadvaikhānasaṃ sūtraṃ sarvavedārthasaṃgrahaḥ ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ sarvaviprāṇāṃ sāmnyamabhidhīyate ।
vaikhānasasya sūtrasya cāgneśśrāmaṇakasya ca ।।

nārāyaṇasya devasya māhātmyaṃ nāvabudhyate ।
yathā vedeṣu sarveṣu sāmavedaḥ praśasyate ।।

tathā sarveṣu sūtreṣu sūtrametatpraśasyate ।
agnirvaikhānasaṃ śāstraṃ viṣṇurvedāścaśāśvatāḥ ।।

gāyatrī vaiṣṇavā viprāssaptaite bahupāvanāḥ ।
adhīteṣu ca vedeṣu sāṃgeṣu labhate phalam ।।

tatphalaṃ labhate sadyassūtrametatpaṭhan dvijaḥ ।
agnīṣomādayo devā ye yajñāṃśahavirbhujaḥ ।।

te sarve sūtramāśritya cainaṃ gacchanti mādhavam ।
śārīrāṇyanyasūtrāṇi tathā svargaphalāni ca ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ sūtrametaddhi sarvasiddhikaraṃ param ।
ādyatvātsarvasūtrāṇāṃ vaiṣṇavatvādviśeṣataḥ ।।

mayānuvartitaṃ tadvatkāśyapātrimarīcibhiḥ ।
yasminneva tu saṃprokte sūtre vikhanasā purā ।।

vanasthānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ vidhiśśrāmaṇakābhidhaḥ ।
vānaprasthāstatassvarve yedvijāścānyasūtriṇaḥ ।।

tatsūtravidhyamaṣṭhānātsmṛtā vaikhānasā amī ।
kiṃ bahūktena vidhinā sarvaṃ vaikhānasaṃ jagat ।।

parasmin vyomni yaccār'ke yattejastutrayīmayam ।
tadvaikhānaḥ paraṃ brahma iti vedādadhīmahi ।।

śāstrametacca sūtraṃ ca sarveṣāmapi jīvanam ।
ye vaikhānasasūtreṇa saṃskṛtāstu dvijātayaḥ ।।

te viṣṇusadṛśā jñeyāssarveṣāmuttamottamāḥ ।
vaikhānasānāṃ sarveṣāṃ garbhavaiṣṇavajanmanām ।।

nārāyaṇassvayaṃ garbhemudrāṃ dhārayite nijām ।
viprā vaikhānasākhyāye tebhaktāstattvamucyate ।।

ekāntinassusattvasthā dehāntaṃ nānyayājīnaḥ ।
viṣṇoḥpriyatamā loke catvāraḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।।

aśvadthaḥkapilā gāvastulasī vaiṣṇavā dvijāḥ ।
dvijeṣu brāhmāṇāśśreṣṭhā brāhmaṇeṣu ca caiṣṇavāḥ ।।

vaiṣṇaveṣu paraṃ śreṣṭhā ye vaikhānasasūtriṇaḥ ।
vaiṣṇavīṃ pratimāṃ loke vipraṃ vaikhānasaṃ tathā ।।

gaṅgāṃ viṣṇupadīṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate mūlamasyāpi śāstrasya ।
sārdhakoṭipramāṇataḥ upādiśatsa bhagavān asmabhyaṃ naimiśe vane ।।

iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ mahattvaṃ sūtraśāstrayoḥ ।
tasmādvaikhānasā viprāssaṃpūjyā bhagavatpriyāḥ ।।

pūjānte snapanānte ca tathānte cotsavasya ca ।
ācāryamarcakaṃ cāpi sarvān vaikhānasāṃstathā ।।

prathamaṃ pūjayitvaiva paścātkāryaṃ samācaret ।
yaḥpūjakamanādṛtya vipraṃ vaikhānasaṃ haṭhāt ।।

tīrthaṃ gṛhītuṃ prathamcchetsa patati dhruvam yaḥ ।
pūjakamanādṛtya vipraṃ vaikhānasaṃ punaḥ ।।

prasādaṃ devadevasya prathamaṃ tu jighṛkṣati ।
brahmahatyāmavāpnoti tatbūjā niṣpalā bhavet ।।

yaḥ pūjakamanādṛtya vipraṃ vaikhānasaṃ punaḥ ।
yādṛśīmapi devāgre vāñchatyapacitiṃ janaḥ ।।

caturvedyapi so viprassadyaścaṇḍālatāṃ vrajet ।
tatpūjā niṣphalā ca syādrājarāṣṭraṃ vinaśyati ।।

ṣaṭkālaṃ vā trikālaṃ vā dvikālaṃ kālameva vā ।
ālaye bhagavatpūjā saumyena vidhinā kṛtā ।।

sarvasaṃpatkarī sā syājjagatāmiti śāsanam ।
tatrārcane tu śuddhātmā pūjakaḥ paritoṣitaḥ ।।

tena rājā ca rājyaṃ ca yajamānaśca nānvayaḥ ।
sarvalokaśca saṃtuṣṭo vardhate brahmatejasā ।।

agraṃ vṛkṣasya rājānomūlaṃ vṛkṣasya pūjakāḥ ।
tasmānmūlaṃ na hiṃsīyānmūlādagraṃ prarohati ।।

phalaṃ vṛkṣasya rājānaḥ puṣpaṃ vṛkṣasya pūjakāḥ ।
tasmātpuṣpaṃ na hiṃsīyātpuṣpātsaṃjāyate phalam ।।

devasyaṃ brāhmaṇasvaṃ ca sanmānaṃ pūjakasya ca ।
yastu na trāyate rājā tamāhurbrahmaghātukam ।।

durbalānāmanāthānāṃ bālavṛddhatapasvinām ।
anyāyaiḥ paribhūtānāṃ sarveṣāṃ pārthivo gatiḥ ।।

rājā pitā ca mātā ca rājā ca paramo guruḥ ।
rājā ca sarvabhūtānāṃ paritrātā gururmataḥ ।।

dāvāgnidavadagdhānāṃ rājā pūrṇamivāṃbhasā ।
samudramiva tṛpyanti brāhmaṇā vedavādinaḥ ।।

dahatyagnistejasā ca sūryo dahati raśmibhiḥ ।
rājā dahati diḍena vipro dahati manyuvā ।।

manyupraharaṇā viprāścakra praharaṇo hariḥ ।
cakrāttīkṣṇataro manyustasmādviprānna kopayet ।।

agnidagdhaṃ praroheta sūryadagdhaṃ tathaiva ca ।
daṇḍyastu saṃpraroheta brahmaśāpahato hataḥ ।।

āpadyapi ca kaṣṭāyāṃ nāvamānyo hi pūjakaḥ ।
arcakena tu tuṣṭena yaduktaṃ devasannidhau ।।

tadvākyaṃ tu ha rervākyaṃ nāvamānyo hi pūjakaḥ ।
arcakaṃ kopayedyastu sa hi devasya kopakṛt ।।

deveśaṃ toṣayedyastu sa hi pūjakatoṣakṛt ।
gandhaṃ puṣpaṃ tathā mālyaṃ tāṃbūlaṃ cākṣatādikam ।।

prasādaṃ cāpi devasya prathamaṃ pūjakor'hati ।
ṣaḍaṅgaviduṣāṃ caiva kratupravarayājinām ।।

vaikhānasaḥ punātyagre goṣṭhīṃ vipraśatasya tu ।
phalābhisaṃdhirahitaṃ sarvaṃ karmākhilaṃ kṛtam ।।

brahmārpaṇadhiyā kuryātsa bhavedvaiṣṇavottamaḥ ।
nānyaṃ devaṃ namaskuryānnānyaṃ devaṃ prapūjayet ।।

arcayetsatataṃ dhyāyennārāyaṇamanāyam ।
kāyena manasā vācā sa tu vaiṣṇava ucyate ।।

tiryakpuṇḍradharaṃ caiva pāṣaṇḍinamavaiṣṇavam ।
devāgre pūjaye annaiva tadvaiṣṇavavimānanā ।।

abhyarcyā viṣṇubhaktā hi vaiṣṇavā bhagavatpriyāḥ ।
avaiṣṇavasya pūjā tu teṣāmagre sudāruṇā ।।

tasmātsarvaprayatnena tyajeddūrādavaiṣṇavam ।
yetu sāmānyabhāvena manyante puruṣottamam ।।

rudrādibhissahājñā nātte api jñeyā avaiṣṇavāḥ ।
nareṣu brāhmaṇāśśreṣṭhā brāhmaṇeṣu vipaścitaḥ ।।

vipaścitsu kṛtadhiyasteṣu kartāra eva ca ।
kartṛṣu brahmaviduṣo ye hi bhaktājanākdane ।।

viṣṇubhakteṣu sarvatra śreṣṭhā vaikhānasāssmṛtāḥ ।
tasmātsaṃpūjya sarvādau bhaktyā vaikhānasaṃ dvijam ।।

viṣṇubhaktaṃ tataḥ pūjya yathāvarṇānupūrvyaśaḥ ।
goṣṭhīṃ samarcayetkāle bhojyāścānye dvijātayaḥ ।।

strīyaḥ pūjyā vidhānena vaiṣṇapyo vaiṣṇavāśrayāḥ ।
na hi sādhāraṇi sṛṣyirvaiṣṇavīti vicintayet ।।

janmāntarasahasreṣu tapodhyānasamādhibhiḥ ।
narāṇāṃ kṣīṇapāpānāṃ kṛṣṇe bhaktiḥ prajāyate ।।

na hyabhāgavatairviṣṇurjñrātuṃ stotuṃ ca tattvataḥ ।
draṣṭuṃ vā śakyate mūḍhāḥ praveṣṭuṃ kuta eva hi ।।

tadbhaktibhāvitāḥ pūtā narāstadgatacetasaḥ ।
bhavantivai bhāgavatāste viṣṇuṃ praviśanti ca ।।

aneka janmasaṃsāracite pāpasamuccaye ।
vārṣiṇe jāyate puṃsāṃ govindābhimukhī matiḥ ।।

pradveṣaṃ yāti govinde dvijān vedāṃśca nindati ।
yo narastaṃ vijānīyādāsurāṃśasamudbhavam ।।

pāṣaṇḍeṣu ratiḥ puṃsāṃ hetuvādānukūlatā ।
jāyate viṣṇumāyātaḥ patitānāṃ durātmanām ।।

yadā pāpakṣayaḥ puṃsāṃ tadā devadvijātiṣu ।
viṣṭau ca yajñapuruṣe śraddhā bhavati niścalā ।।

yathā svalpāna śeṣastu narāṇāṃ pāpasaṃcayaḥ ।
bhavanti te bhāgavatā niśśreyaśaparā narāḥ ।।

bhrāmyatāmatra saṃsāre narāṇāṃ karmadurgame ।
hastāvalaṃbano hyeko bhaktikrīto janārdanaḥ ।।

karmaṇā manasā vācā prāṇināṃ yo anasūyakaḥ ।
bhāvasaktaśca govinde viṣṇau bhāgavato hi saḥ ।।

yo brāhmaṇāṃśca vedāṃśca nityameva namasyati ।
na drogdhā paravittādeḥ sahi bhāgavataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

sarvān devān hariṃ vetti sarvān lokāṃśca keśavam ।
tebhyaśca nāsyamātmāvaṃ sa hi bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ ।।

devaṃ manuṣyamanyaṃ vā paśupakṣipipīlikāḥ ।
tarupāṣāṇakāṣṭhādīn bhūmyaṃbhogaganaṃ diśaḥ ।।

ātmānaṃ cāpi deveśādvyatiriktaṃ janārdanāt ।
yo na jānāti puṇyātmā sa hi bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ ।।

sarvaṃ bhagavato bhāgo yadbhūtaṃ bhavyasaṃsthitam ।
iti yo vai vijānāti sa hi bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ ।।

bhavabhītiṃ haratyeṣa bhaktibhāvena bhāvitaḥ ।
bhagavāniti yadbhāvassa tu bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ ।।

bhāvaṃ na kurute yastu sarvabhūteṣu pāpakam ।
karmaṇā manasā vācā sa tu bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ ।।

bāhyārthanirapekṣo yo bhaktyā bhagavataḥ kriyām ।
bhāvena niṣpādayati jñeyo bhāgavato hi saḥ ।।

nārayo yasya susnigdhā na codāsīnavṛttayaḥ ।
paśyatassarvamevedaṃ viṣṇuṃ bhāgavatassa hi ।।

sutapteneha tapasā yajñairvā bahudakṣiṇaiḥ ।
tāṃ gatiṃ na narāyānti yāṃ tu bhāgavatā narāḥ ।।

yogacyutairbhāgavataid devarājaśśatakratuḥ ।
avāṅnirīkṣyate najrīkimu ye yogapāragāḥ ।।

yajñaniṣpattaye vedā devā yajñapateḥ kṛte ।
tattoṣaṇāya yatate sa hi bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ ।।

yena sarvātmanā bhaktyā viṣṇau bhāvo niveśitaḥ ।
yuktatvātkṛtakṛtyatvātsa hi bhāgavatassmṛtaḥ ।।

vratināṃ yajñapuruṣaḥ pūjyo viṣṇurasaṃśayaḥ ।
strīyaśca svaṃ ca bhartāramṛte pūjyanna daivatam ।।

bharturgṛhasthasya sataḥ pūjyo yajñapatirhariḥ ।
vaikhānasānāmārādhyastapobhirmadhusūdanaḥ ।।

dhyeyaḥ parivrājakānāṃ vāsudevo mahātmanām ।
evamāśramiṇāṃ viṣṇussarveṣāṃ ca parāyaṇam ।।

na dānairnatapobhiśca prīyate bhagavān hariḥ ।
varṇāśramācāravatā yathā sa parituṣyati ।।

varṇāśramācāravatā puruṣeṇa paraḥpumān ।
viṣṇurārādhyate panthā nānyastattoṣakārakaḥ ।।

atrānukteṣu doṣeṣu prāyaścittaṃ pravakṣyate ।
paiṇḍarīkāgnimāsādya pariṣicya ca pāvakam ।।

ṣaṭkṛtvo vaiṣṇavaṃ tadvaccatuṣkṛtvaśca vyāhṛtīḥ ।
aṣṭākṣaraṃ cāṣṭakṛtvastathā ca dvādaśākṣaram ।।

hutvā dvādaśakṛtvastu viṣṇusūktaṃ ca pauruṣam ।
ekākṣarādisūktaṃ ca śrībhūsūktadvayaṃ hunet ।।

devaṃ saṃsnāpya cābhyarcya havissamyaṅni vedayet, ।
anena vidhinā tatra śāntirbhavati śobhanā ।।

hādoṣeṣu ca punaruktahomaissahaiva tu ।
pāramātmikamīṅkārādyaṣṭāśītiṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

hutvā ca sarvadaivatyamaṣṭābhiśca śatairghaṭaiḥ ।
devaṃ saṃsnāpya cābhyarcya havissamyaṅni vedayet ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre triṃśo adhyāyaḥ

athaika triṃśo adhyāyaḥ

saṃprokṣaṇatrayam
atha vakṣyāmi tatroktaprāyaścittasya saṃgraham ।
jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caiva laghusaṃprokṣaṇaṃ tathā ।।

mahāsaṃprokṣaṇaṃ ceti prāyaścittaṃ tridhā smṛtam ।
nimitte samanuprāpte jñātvā gauravalāghavam ।।

vakṣyamāṇakrāreṇa sadyassaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret ।
saṃprokṣaṇavidhānasya na kālaniyamassmṛtaḥ ।।

na kuryānmāsanakṣatra tithivārādyavekṣaṇam ।
tasmānnimitte saṃprāpte sadyassaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret ।।

deśakālādyavekṣāyā nimitte sati gauravam ।
bahubereṣu caikasmin sthāvare jaṅgame atha vā ।।

arcanāyāṃ vihīnāyāṃ kālātīte viparyaye ।
nirmālyapūjane caiva niveditanivedane ।।

ekāhe apyarcanāhīne nityasnāpanavarjane ।
balihomādihīneca nityotsavavivarjane ।।

prākārābhyantare prāpte pramādādaśubhe sati ।
aspṛśyāgamane tatra caṇḍālādyaiḥ praveśane ।।

śvakukkuṭa varāhoṣṭragardabhānāṃ praveśane ।
udakyayā sūtikayā pāṣaṇḍādyairathāpi vā ।।

kuṇḍagolavratabhraṣṭaturuṣkādipraveśane ।
anyasūtridvijaisspṛṣṭe mohādajñānato apivā ।।

mahāvātahate biṃbe saṃsikte varṣabindubhiḥ ।
viṇmūtrarudhirasrāve bahujalpe ca maithune ।।

evamādinimitte tu jalasaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret ।
naivāsaṃprokṣite biṃbe harirvasati niścayaḥ ।।

tasmādbiṃbaviśuddhyarthaṃ saṃprokṣyaiva samarcayet ।
doṣādhikye samutpanne laghusaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret ।।

rāṣṭrakṣobhe ca durbhikṣe tantrasaṃkaradūṣaṇe ।
śūdrairvāthānulomairvāpāṣaṇḍairbhramitairapi ।।

udakyayā sūtikayā patitairvātha pātakaiḥ ।
caṇḍālādyaiḥ praviṣṭe ca garbhāgāre viśeṣataḥ ।।

sūtairvā kuṇḍagolādyaistathā devalakādibhiḥ ।
śvakukkuṭa varāhādyaiḥ praviṣṭe gārdabhādibhiḥ ।।

ulūkagṛdhrakākādyaiḥ praviṣṭe antargṛhe tathā ।
turuṣkādyaiḥpraviṣṭe vā śukraṇoṇitayorapi ।।

viṇmūtrādervisarge vā garbhāgārerdhamaṇḍape ।
tṣahādūrdhvaṃ vihīne tu pūjane dīpavarjane ।।

eka rātramatikramya devegrāmāntarasthite ।
āgnidāhe aśanīpāte garbhāgārer'dhamaṇḍape ।।

anyasūtṣarcite biṃbespṛṣṭe vā buddhipūrvakam ।
anyairanuktairdeṣaiśca laghusaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret ।।

mahānimitte saṃprāpte mahāsaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret ।
dvādaśāhātsamārabhya vatsarāntaṃ vidhānataḥ ।।

hīnāyāmarcanāyāṃ ca nitye naimittike tathā ।
kriyāhīne viparyāse hīne māsotsavādike ।।

nityasnapanahīne api mātrādānavihīnake ।
balihomādihīne ca saṃprāpte śāstrasaṃkare ।।

evamādiṣu hīneṣu vatsarāntaṃ pramādataḥ ।
parṣadāṃ parivārāṇāmāśritālayasevinām ।।

dhvajārohaṇapūrvaṃ tu kṛte kālotsavādike ।
viprādimaraṇe prāpte devāgāre viśeṣataḥ ।।

gardabhāśvalulāyoṣṭraśvasūkaramukhe mṛte ।
gajādimṛganāśe ca devāgāre pramādataḥ ।।

caṇḍālādyantyajātīnāṃ maraṇe vā viśeṣataḥ ।
śūdrairvāthānulomairvā pāṣaṇḍaiḥ patitādibhiḥ ।।

saṃspṛṣṭe vaiṣṇave biṃbe turuṣkādyairmalimlucaiḥ ।
spṛṣṭe caṇḍālakādyairvā mahāpātakadūṣitaiḥ ।।

vimāne aśanipāte vā maholkā patane api vā ।
lohito palavarṣe ca vāṃsuvarṣe viśeṣataḥ ।।

bhūkaṃpāccalite biṃbe valmīkasya samudbhave ।
śithilibhavane vāpi cāṣṭabandhe viśeṣataḥ ।।

jīrṇe staṃbhādipatane devāgārena vīkṛte ।
agnisparśe ca berasya manuṣyaprasave tathā ।।

suthākarmaṇi sarvatra garbhagehādike punaḥ ।
biṃbeṣu garbhagehe vā kṛmikīṭādidarśane ।।

hasane rodane caiva bhāṣaṇe ca viśeṣataḥ ।
svedaśoṇitayorvāpi darśane varṇasaṃkṣaye ।।

vimāne maṇḍape vātha yatra kutrāpi vā hareḥ ।
devāgāre samutpanne doṣeṣveteṣu vā pṛthak ।।

durbhikṣe rāṣṭrasaṃkṣobhe durnimitteṣu caiva hi ।
dussvapne bhūmikaṃpe vā pararājādyupadrave ।।

bhūgupte coddhṛte biṃbe ciramanyālaye sthite ।
atikramya trirātraṃ tu deve grāmāntare sthite ।।

kuṇḍagolakasūtādyairdīkṣitairarcane kṛte ।
anuktāni ca karvāṇi duritānyadbhutāni ca ।।

dṛṣṭvātu yajamānaśca ye tatparisare janāḥ ।
grāmasthitā canāścaiva rājā rāṣṭraṃ ca yatnataḥ ।।

jñātvā śāstroktavidhinā doṣajaṃ bhaktitaḥ phalam ।
mahāsaṃprokṣaṇaṃ kuryānmahādoṣāpanuttaye ।।

mahadoṣeṣu sarvatra mahāśāntirvithīyate ।
pūrvaṃ sthāpitabiṃbasya na sādhāraṇahetunā ।।

syātpunasthsāpanaṃ tasmānmahāsaṃprokṣaṇaṃ caret ।
mahāsaṃprokṣaṇavidhernūtanasthāpanasya ca ।।

svalpo bheda iti proktamṛṣibhiḥ kāśyapādibhiḥ ।
jalasaṃprokṣaṇavidhiṃ pravakṣyāmi tapodhanāḥ ।।

yajamānābhyanujñāto gurussnātvā vidhānataḥ ।
ālayābhimukhe vāpi dakṣiṇe vā manorame ।।

sthaṇḍile saikate śuddhe puṇyāhāgnimukhātvaram ।
vāstuhomāvasāne ca doṣaduṣṭaṃ tu yat sthalam ।।

paryagnipañcagavyābhyāṃ saṃskratya vidhinā budhaḥ ।
biṃbaṃ puruṣasūktena kalaśairabhiṣicya ca ।।

ṣaṭdroṇadhānya rāśau tu pañcakuṃbhānnidhāya ca ।
vastrayugnena saṃveṣṭya pratimāsteṣu nikṣipet ।।

nālikerāmrapatrādyairalaṅkṛtya pṛthak ghaṭān ।
pañcasūktaṃ japitvaiva pañcaśāntibhireva ca ।।

pañcamūrtibhirāvāhya samabhyarcyāṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।
paścādagniṃ paristīrya pañcasūktaṃ hunetsudhīḥ r ।।

iṅkārādīṃśca juhuyādaṣṭāśītimataḥ param ।
pañcavāruṇamantraiśca mahāvyāhṛtibhissaha ।।

paścādagniṃ visṛjyaiva gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadet ।
niṣkāhīnasuvarṇaṃ ca vastrābharaṇakuṇḍalān ।।

paścātkuṃbhajalenaiva prokṣayitvā samantrakam ।
prabhūtaṃ ca nivedyaiva nityārcanamathācaret ।।

anena vidhinā doṣā naśyatyeva na saṃśayaḥ ।
tadbiṃbe devasānnidhyaṃ bhavedityāha cāṅgirāḥ ।।

etāvāneva saṃprokto jalasaṃprokṣaṇakramaḥ ।
laghusaṃprokṣaṇaṃ kuryādyajamānena vai guruḥ ।।

yathārhaṃ pūjitaḥ pūrvamāraṃbhadivasādadhaḥ ।
tṣahe vā dviyahe vāpi kṛtvā caivāṅkurārpaṇam ।।

aupāsanāgnau śvobhūte vāstuhomaṃ vidhāya ca ।
paryagni pañcagavyābhyāṃ śodhayitvā samantataḥ ।।

abhiṣicya ca deveśamaṣṭottaraśatairghuṭaiḥ ।
śothayitvā vidhānena vastuvāstuparicchadān ।।

paścātpadmāgnimāsādya kṛtāghāraṃ vidhānataḥ ।
kuṃbhapūjāṃ tataḥ kuryātsamyak dhyānayuto guruḥ ।।

dvātriṃśatprasthasaṃpūrṇān kuṃbhānāhṛtya śobhanān ।
tantunā veṣṭayitvā tu toyairāpūrya mantrata ।।

ṣaḍbhāradhānyarośau tu vedyāṃ saptadaśa kramāt ।
vastrayugmena saṃveṣṭya pratimāsteṣu nikṣipet ।।

niṣkatrayakṛtāṃstatra nava ratnāni yatnataḥ ।
ratnālābhe suvarṇaṃ vā pratyekaṃ nikṣipedghaṭe ।।

gandhapuṣpaissamabhyarcya nālikerāmrapallavaiḥ ।
āyudhaiḥpañcabhistadvattoraṇairaṣṭamaṅgalaiḥ ।।

alaṅkṛtya gururdhīmānt pṛṣṭvā kūrcena tān ghaṭān ।
pañcasūktaṃ pañcaśāntiṃ tato dvādaśasūktakam ।।

sārasvatādisūktaṃ ca diksūktaṃ pañcavāruṇam ।
svastisūktaṃ japitvaiva tathaivauṣadhisūktakam ।।

navamūrtibhirāvāhya devībhyāṃ saha pārṣadaiḥ ।
dvātriṃśadvigrahaissamyagabhyarcya tu nivedayet ।।

paiṇḍarīkāgnimāsādya pariṣicya ca pāvakam ।
pañcasūktena juhuyādvyāpakatrayamantrataḥ ।।

aṣṭottaraśataṃ tadvadaṣṭāviṃśatireva vā ।
r iṅkārādīṃśca juhuyādaṣṭāśītimataḥ param ।।

dhātādiṃ mūlahomaṃ ca pañcavāruṇameva ca ।
hutvā kūśmāṇḍahomaṃ ca pañcavāruṇameva ca ।।

paṅkajairbilvapatrairvā viṣṇugāyatriyā tataḥ ।
aṣṭottaraśataṃ hutvā paścādagniṃ visarcayet ।।

paścādguruḥ pūjitassan vastrābharaṇakuṇḍalaiḥ ।
kuṃbhamādāya śiraso grāmamālayameva vā ।।

pradakṣiṇaṃ parītyātha devadevasya sannidhau ।
kūrcenādāya tattoyaṃ prokṣayetpañcamūrtibhiḥ ।।

"śucī vo havya'' mantreṇa prokṣayetsarvamandiram ।
upacāraissamabhyarcya "kṣama''sveti praṇamya ca ।।

mahāhaviḥ prabhūtaṃ vā deveśāya nivedayet ।
brāhmaṇānāṃ sahasraṃ ca bhojayedguruṇā saha ।।

gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadyātsuvarṇaṃ pañcaniṣkakam ।
pradadyādbhūmimiṣṭāṃ ca pronmiṣatsasyamālinīm ।।

daśadānaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā nityārcanamathācaret ।
evaṃ yaḥ kurute bhaktyā laghusaṃprokṣaṇaṃ hareḥ ।।

viṣṇusānnidhyamāpnoti doṣaśāntiśca jāyate ।
rājarāṣṭrābhivṛddhiśca jagatpuṣṭikaraṃ bhavet ।।

laghusaṃprokṣaṇavidhirmayā prakhyāpitaḥ kila ।
kāśyapādyaiśca munibhirevameva pracoditaḥ ।।

mahāsaṃprokṣaṇa vidhau viśeṣo vakṣyate mayā ।
jalādhivāsarahitaṃ netronmīlanavarjanam ।।

pratiṣṭhoktavidhānena sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret ।
netrayostejane tadvaddṛṣṭidoṣe viśeṣataḥ ।।

jalādhivāsanaṃ kuryādakṣṇorunmīlanaṃ punaḥ ।
mahāśāntividhānasya viśeṣo atra prakīrtitaḥ ।।

jaṅgamapratimāssarvā adhivāsapurassaram ।
prokṣayitvā vidhānena devaṃ pūrvavadarcayet ।।

mahānimitte saṃprāpte yajamānārthito guruḥ ।
pratiṣṭhoktadine vidvān ṛtvigbhirlakṣaṇānvitaiḥ ।।

vastrairābharaṇaiścāpi pūrvoktamiva bhūṣitaḥ ।
prokṣaṇādivasātsūrvamaṅkurārpaṇamācaret ।।

dravyāṇyapi susaṃbhṛtya yāgaśālāṃ praviśya ca ।
kadalīpūgamālādyaiḥ patākādyairalaṅkṛtām ।।

tanmadhyekalpayedvediṃ śayanārthaṃ vidhānataḥ ।
tasyāstu pūrvadigbhāge kuṃbhavediṃ salakṣaṇam ।।

paritaścāgnikuṇḍāṃśca paiṇḍarīkaṃ ca kārayet ।
devālayaṃ ca saṃśodhya mṛṣṭasiktopalepanaiḥ ।।

ācāryassuprasannātmā yajamānārthito muhuḥ ।
snātvāsnānavidhānena gāyatrīṃ ca sahasraśaḥ ।।

japtvā dvādaśasūktāni puṇyāhamapi vācayet ।
vāstuhomaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā kuṇḍe tvaupāsane guruḥ ।।

paryagni pañcagavyābhyāṃ saṃśodhyaiva ca sarvataḥ ।
gārhapatyādikuṇḍeṣu kramādāghāramācaret ।।

pakvabiṃbasamākāraghaṭānāṃ pañcaviṃśatim ।
tantunā trivṛtā veṣṭya śodhayitvā sudhūpitān ।।

ādāya mantravaddivyaṃ jalamāhṛtya yatnataḥ ।
pūtābhiradbhirāpūrya nālikerāmrapallavaiḥ ।।

alaṅkṛtya tathā kūrcairgandhapuṣpākṣatādibhiḥ ।
yavairvāhrīhibhirvātha vedyāṃ dvādaśabhārakaiḥ ।।

āstīrya teṣu saṃsthāpya pṛthagvastreṇa veṣṭayet ।
sauvarṇapratimāstatra pañcaniṣkakṛtāḥ pṛthak ।।

gajakūrmādirūpāṇi navaratnādi ca kṣipet ।
dhyānamārgeṇa kuṃbheṣu madhyamādiṣu cakramāt ।।

navamūrtikrameṇaiva mantreṇāvāhayedguruḥ ।
vedyadhastheṣu kuṃbheṣu ceṃ dādīnaṣṭadikpatīn ।।

āvāhya gandhapuṣpādyaissamabhyarcya nivedayet ।
sahasrakalaśaissnāpya snapanoktaprakārataḥ ।।

sauvarṇaṃ kautukaṃ baddhvā pratiṣṭhoktavidhānataḥ ।
śayyāvediṃ samabhyukṣya pañcatalpān prākalpyaca ।।

śālivrīhiyavaiścāpi ṣaḍbhāraiśca pṛthak pṛthak ।
tadardhaistaṇḍulaiścātha tadardhaiśca tilaistathā ।।

uparyupari cāstīrya carmajādīn samāstaret ।
śayane śāyayedvedyāmautsavaṃ biṃbamuktavat ।।

kūrcādhivāsaṃ kurvīta dhruvamātraṃ yadikramāt ।
vedānadhyāpayeddikṣu "ṛcāṃ prācī''riti śrutiḥ ।।

gārhapatyādikuṇḍeṣu pratiṣṭhoktavidhānataḥ ।
ṛtvigbhiḥ kārayeddhomaṃ tattaddaivatyapūrvakam ।।

gurussabhyāgnimāsādya pariṣicya ca pāvakam ।
pañcasūktaṃ krameṇaiva mahāvyāhṛtipūrvakam ।।

vyāpakatrayamantraṃ ca viṣṇugāyatriyā punaḥ ।
aṣottaraśataṃ hutvā vyāhṛtyā ca tathaiva ca ।।

tato abjāgniṃ samāsādya pañcasūktaissahaiva tu ।
dhātādimūlahomaṃ ca pañcavāruṇasaṃyutam ।।

mahāśāntyuktamantrāṃśca trirāvartya hunettataḥ ।
kuṃbhavediṃ samāsādya samabhyarcyāṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।।

spṛṣṭvā kūrcena tatkuṃbhān ṛtvigbhissaha vai guruḥ ।
ātmasūktaṃ japitvaiva pañcasūktamataḥ param ।।

svastisūktaṃ ca daurgaṃ ca rātrimekākṣaraṃ tathā ।
aṣṭadikpālasūktāni pañcaśāntimataḥ param ।।

"āpo hiraṇyavarṇā''bhyāṃ pāvamānībhireva ca ।
japtvā dvādaśasūktaṃ ca tatassabhyānale kramāt ।।

hautrapraśasanaṃ kuryātsarvaṃ hot tu pūrvavat ।
caturmūrtikrameṇaiva sahasrāhutinā saha ।।

"yaddevā''dyaiśca kūśmāṇḍaissarvadaivatyamantrakaiḥ ।
hutvātu doṣaśāntyarthaṃ lojaistadvattilairapi ।।

sāpūpairviṣṇugāyatṣā hutvākuṇḍeṣu pūrvavat ।
aṣṭottaraśataṃ tadvadaṣṭāviṃśatireva vā ।।

pariṣegaṃ tataḥ kṛtvā paiṇḍarīke viśeṣataḥ ।
padmairvā bilvapatrairvā viṣṇugāyatriyā tataḥ ।।

aṣottarasahasraṃ tu ghṛtenāplutya vai hunet ।
pāramātmikamantraiśca r iṅkārādyaiśca yatnataḥ ।।

aṣṭāśītiṃ tato hutvā mahāvyāhṛtipūrvakam ।
hutvā taddoṣanāśāya rājarāṣṭrābhivṛddhaye ।।
sabhyāgniṃ pauṇḍarīkāgniṃ hitvānyeṣvantahomakam ।।
nṛttagītādivādyaiśca rātriśeṣaṃ nayedguruḥ ।
prātassnātvā vidhānena kalaśaissnapanaṃ caret ।।

pañcasūktaiśca saṃsnāpya pañcaśāntisamanvitam ।
paścāddevamalaṅkṛtya suvastrābharaṇādikaiḥ ।।

gandhapuṣpaissugandhaiśca yāpannetramanaḥpriyam ।
muhūrte samanuprāpte kuṃbhamādāya deśikaḥ ।।

svastisūktaṃ japan grāmamālayaṃ vā pradakṣiṇam ।
kṛtvā devāgrataḥ kuṃbhaṃ dhyānyapīṭhe niveśayet ।।

yajamānena śaktyāvai gurussaṃpūjitastadā ।
kūryādanantaroktāṃśca saṃskārān bhagavatpriyān ।।

vastrerābharaṇaiśśubhraiḥ kuṇḍalaiśca viśeṣataḥ ।
yajamānassusaṃpūjya paśubhūmyādibhirgurum ।।

gurave dakṣiṇāṃ dadyānniṣkāṇāmekaviṃśatim ।
ṛtvigbhyaśca tathā dadyātsuprīto bhagavān hariḥ ।।

guruḥ paścātsamāvāhya samabhyarcyāṣṭavigrahaiḥ ।
mahāhavirni vedyaina pāyasāpūpasaṃyutam ।।

sājyaṃ savyañjanaṃ datvā mukhavāsaṃ nivedayet ।
puṣpāñjaliṃ tato datvā "kṣaya'' sveti praṇamya ca ।।

sahasraṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca bhojayecchāntihetave ।
daśadānaṃ viśeṣeṇa devaprītikaṃ bhavet ।।

evamādvādaśābdāttu pratiṣṭhāmācarettataḥ ।
punasthsāpanasaṃskārātprāyaścittaṃ na hītarat ।।

tasmātsarvaprayatnena śāstroktaṃ sarvamācaret ।
evaṃ yaḥkurute bhaktyā viṣṇossaṃprokṣaṇatrayam ।।
pratiṣṭhāphalamāsādya vaiṣṇavaṃ lokamāpnuyāt ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre ekatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

athadvātriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

prakīrṇakam
ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi jyeṣṭhāyāmutsavakramam ।
jyeṣṭhe māsi tu saṃprāpte jyeṣṭhānakṣatra saṃyute ।।

viṣṇoreva viśeṣassyātsugandhaṃ tailamāharet ।
tailakramaṃ pravakṣyāmi śruṇudhvaṃ munipuṅgavāḥ ।।

yāgaśālāṃ prakalpyaiva sarvālaṅkālasaṃyutām ।
sabhyaṃ ca paiṇḍarīkaṃ ca kārayitvā salakṣaṇam ।।

taddinasya tu pūrvedyustṛtīye pañcame api vā ।
saptame ahani vā cāpi aṅkurārpaṇamācaret ।।

āghāraṃ vidhivatkṛtvā sarvakāryamadaḥ param ।
vedyāstathottare pārśve bhūmyāmapaṭamācaret ।।

catustālapramāṇeva vistāraṃ nimnameva ca ।
nimnetu vinyasedbhāṇḍaṃ dvidroṇaparimāṇakam ।।

"bhūḥ prati'' ṣṭheti mantreṇa nimne bhāṇḍaṃ sunikṣipet ।
malayāgurudārūṇi devadāru tathaiva ca ।।

yāni cātra sugandhīni devayogyāni tāni vai ।
guggulaṃ ca samāhṛtya mardayitvāsakṛt sakṛt ।।

viṣṇu'gāyatriyā bhāṇḍe tāni dravyāṇi nikṣivet ।
śarāveṇa pidhāyātha mṛdā ca parilepayet ।।

gokarīṣāṇi kāṣṭhāni tasyopari vinikṣipet ।
mandāgninā pacettattu yāvattailāgamaṃ bhavet ।।

tāvatkālaṃ pacedvidvān tailamāhṛtya saṃbhṛtam ।
vāsitāni tu vastūni parihṛtya tu tatra vai ।।

sugandhidailabhāṇḍaṃ ca dhyānyapīṭhopari nyaset ।
pūrvoktenaiva mantreṇa tantunā pariveṣṭayet ।।

pitṝn somaṃ tathābhyarcya vanatpatimataḥ param ।
taile tasmin vidhānena arghyāntamabhipūjayet ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca narasūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।
japtvātu viṣṇugāyatrīmaṣṭottarasahasrakam ।।

ācāryastvarito gatvā sabhyāgnestu samīpataḥ ।
dvitālavistṛtaṃ vṛttaṃ caturaṅgulamunnatam ।।
kūrmākṛtivadākāraṃ bilvādyaiḥ parikalpitam ।।
pratiṣṭhāyāmutsave ca japahomārcanādiṣu ।
devakāryeṣu sarveṣu tathānyeṣu ca karmasu ।।

kūrmapīṭhaṃ tu gṛhṇīyādanyathā niṣphalaṃ bhavet ।
asīnaḥ kūrmapīṭhe tu sabhyāgnau juhuyāttathā ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca narasūktaṃ tatheva ca ।
juhuyātsarvadaivatyaṃ pāramātmikameva ca ।।

mahāvyāhṛtibhirhutvā antahomaṃ samācaret ।
praṇidhyāṃ śaṅkhapātre vā agnimāropayetsudhīḥ? ।।

tailasyālepanātpūrvaṃ dhruvādagniṃ samāharet ।
sragvastrakuṇḍalādyaiśca ācāryaṃ pūjayettataḥ ।।

paricārakamāhūya yathārhaṃ pūjya taṃ tataḥ ।
uṣṇīṣaṃ dhārayitvātaṃ paricārakamūrdhani ।।

sugandhitailabhāṇḍaṃ tu yatnenāpi vinikṣipet ।
śanaiśsanaiśca gatvā tu sarvavādyasamanvitam ।।

sarvālaṅkārasaṃyuktaṃ brahmaghoṣasamanvitam ।
vīthiṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya devasyāgretu nikṣipet ।।

arghyāntamabhipūjyaiva deveśaṃ saṃpraṇamya ca ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca narasūktaṃ japetkramāt ।।

tailenālepayeddevamācārya stvaritastathā ।
devībhyāṃ ca tataḥ paścāttattanmantreṇa lepayet ।।

sarveṣāṃ parivārāṇāṃ tattanmantraiśca kārayet ।
ācāryastvaritogatvā cautsavasya samīpataḥ ।।

"parilikhita'miti mantreṇa kavacaṃ pariśodhayet ।
jīrṇe bhinne ca kavace śilpinaina susannayet ।।

prakṣālya pañcagavyena jalena pariśodhayet ।
kṛtvāpi vāstuśuddhiṃ ca yathoktāṃ niṣkṛtiṃ caret ।।

viṣṇornukādimantraiśca saṃdadhyātkavacaṃ tathā ।
dṛḍhīkṛtya tu pūrvoktaṃ yatnena parikalpayet ।।

sahasrakalaśairdevaṃ snāpayitvā yathāvidhe ।
nityapūjāvidhānena devamārādhya pūrvavat ।।

mahāhaviḥprabhūtaṃ vā pāyasaṃ ca nivedayet ।
"kṣamasve''ti vadan bhūyaḥ praṇametpuruṣottamam ।।

brahmaghoṣaṃ tataḥ kuryāddadyādācāryadakṣiṇām ।
dine pakṣe ca māse ca tathā saṃnatsare caret ।।

yadyadrūpaṃ tathādhyāyettattadbiṃbeṣu yojayet ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena biṃbarakṣāṃ samācaret ।।

pavitrāropaṇam atha vakṣye viśeṣaṇa pavitrāropaṇaṃ hareḥ ।।

sarvadoṣopaśamanaṃ sarvayajñaphalapradam ।
sarvakāmapradaṃ caiva sarvatuṣṭikaraṃ param ।।

sarvalokasya vṛddhyarthaṃ sarvalokasya śāntidam ।
yadyanmantrakriyāhīnaṃ dravyahīnaṃ ca yatkṛtam ।।

taddoṣaśamanāyaiva pavitrāropaṇaṃ caret ।
pavitrāropaṇe hīne yā pūjā niṣphalā bhavet ।।

saṃkṣobho jāyate tatra tasmādyatnena kārayet ।
āṣāḍhe śrāvaṇe māsi proṣṭhapadyāṃ viśeṣataḥ ।।

dvādaśyāṃ śuklapakṣe tu viṣṇupañcadine atha vā ।
saṃsarpamadhimāsaṃ ca tithivāraṃ ca śūnyakam ।।

daśamyekādaśīmiśraṃ taddinaṃ ca vivarjayet ।
haritithyāṃ ca nirduṣṭe pavitrāropaṇaṃ śubham ।।

navāhaṃ vātha saptāhaṃ pañcāhamatha vā tṣaham ।
uktalakṣaṇasaṃpannamācāryaṃ varayetkramāt ।।

ṛtvijo varayettadvacchiṣyāṃś ca varayettataḥ ।
taddinātpūrvarātrau tu deveśaṃ prārthayedguruḥ ।।

"bhagavato bale''neti procya namrāṅgassusamāhitaḥ ।
pādyādyaiśca viśeṣeṇa devamabhyarcya satvaraḥ ।।

prārthanāsūktamuccārya vedādhyayanamārabhet ।
parito yāgaśālāyāśśiṣyaiḥ parivṛtoguruḥ ।।

caturṣu dvāradeśeṣu kramātprāgādiṣu svayam ।
caturvedāndimantrāṃśca śaktyādhyayanamācaret ।।

puṇyāhaṃ ca tataḥ kṛtvā mṛtsaṃgrahaṇamācaret ।
aṅkurānalpayitvaiva mudgānnaṃ ca nivedayet ।।

aupāsanāgnikuṇḍe tu āghāraṃ vidhivadyajet ।
vāstuhomaṃ ca hutvā tu gavyaṃ kṛtvā vidhānataḥ ।।

paryagni pañcagavyābhyāṃ yogaśālāṃ viśodhayet ।
"tamekanemi'' mityuktvā "āmāvājasya'' ityapi ।।

"tantuntavva''nniti procya "yanmegarbha'' itīrayan ।
ṣaḍbhiśca vaiṣṇavairmantrairviṣṇugāyatriyā tathā ।।

pavitrāṇi susaṃprokṣya vidhinā pañcagavyakaiḥ ।
"pratadviṣṇustavata'' iti "idaṃ viṣṇu'' ritīrayan ।।
viṣṇugāyatriyā paścāt pavitraṃ saṃpraṇamya ca ।।
uttamaṃ svarṇasūtraṃ ca madhyamaṃ raupyasūtrakam ।
kārpāsamadhamaṃ gṛhya sarvadoṣavivarjitam ।।

sumaṅgalībhiryugmābhirbrāhmaṇībhirviśeṣataḥ ।
alābhe kanyakābhirvā nirmitaṃ sūtramuttamam ।।

gṛhṇīyādbiṃbamānena cāṣṭottarasahasrakam ।
granthayoṃguṣṭhamātrāssyustābhirmālāṃ ca kārayet ।।

vanamālā samākhyātā viṣṇoḥpriyatamā bhavet ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ ca japtvātu "aṇoraṇīyā''niti brurna ।।

prokṣya hāridratoyena "ime dhū'' peti dhūpayet ।
caturvedādimantraiśca toraṇādyairalaṅkṛtam ।।
nabhyāgnikuṇḍaṃ kṛtvaiva āghāraṃ vidhivadyajet ।।
biṃbādhyardhapramāṇena śayyāvediṃ prakalpayet ।
tilataṇḍuladhānyaiśca dhānyapīṭhaṃ prakalpya ca ।।

darbhāṃstatra samāstīrya cāṇḍajādīni cāstaret ।
"pratadviṣṇu''riti procya pavitraṃ sannidhāya ca ।।

pañcamūrtabhirāvāhya samabhyarcya praṇamya ca ।
japtvā pratisaraṃ mantraṃ dhūpadīpādi darśayet? ।।

"ato devā'' dinā paścāddeveśaṃ prārthayedguruḥ ।
pādyādibhissamabhyarcya dhūpadīpādidarśayet ।।

baddhvā pratisaraṃ devaṃ śrībhūmyau ca tathaiva ca ।
ācāryasyartvijāṃ caiva baddhvāpratisaraṃ tathā ।।

"yadvaiṣṇavaṃ samuccārya pavitraṃ śayanaṃ caret ।
sūkṣmavastreṇa cācchādya cārpayetpuṣbamakṣatam ।।

viṣṇusūktaṃ ca godānasūktaṃ caivātmasūktakam ।
ekākṣarādisūktaṃ ca vaiṣṇavaṃ sūktameva ca ।।

nṛsūktaṃ rudra sūktaṃ ca durgāsūktaṃ tathaiva ca ।
sārasvataṃ tathā sūktaṃ rātrisūktamataḥ param ।।

"ṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ'' japtvaiva "sahasraśīrṣa''meva ca ।
śrībhūsūktañca japtvaiva kārayeddeśikottamaḥ ।।

daśānāṃ caiva pañcānāṃ sūktānāṃ japa uttamam ।
madhyamaṃ daśasūktānāṃ pañcānāmadhamaṃ bhavet ।।

prāgādidikṣu ca tathā vidikṣu ca caturṣvapi ।
kramācchāntaṃ khagādhīśaṃ cakraṃ śaṅkhaṃ tathaiva ca ।।

vimānapālāṃścāvāhya samabhyarcya viśeṣataḥ ।
mudgānnaṃ vinivedyaiva praṇāmaṃ muhurācaret ।।

sarvarakṣākaraṃ cakraṃ pavitropari cārcayet ।
nivedayettadānnena śāntādīnāṃ baliṃ dadet ।।

pādau prakṣālya cācamya yathoktena vidhānataḥ ।
hautraṃ praśaṃsya vidhivadāvāhana mathācaret ।।

juṣṭākāraṃ ca kṛtvā tu juhuyācca yathākramam ।
hāvayetpañcabhissuktaistattaddaivatyameva ca ।।

vaścādagniṃ visṛjyaiva rātriśeṣaṃ nayedguruḥ ।
tataḥ prabhāte dharmātmā snātvā snānavidhānataḥ ।।

nityapūjā vidherante deveśaṃ prārthayedguruḥ ।
aṣṭottaraśatairdevaṃ snāpayetkalaśaistataḥ ।।
alaṅkṛtyaca deveśaṃ dhūpadīpādikaṃ dadet ।।
audyantam'' itimantreṇa pavitraṃ mūrdhni dhārayan ।
sarvavādyasamāyuktaṃ to yadhārāpurassaram ।।

pradakṣiṇaṃ śanairgatvādevāgresannidhāyaca ।
"surya'' ca mantreṇa śatañjaptvā tu pallavam ।।

ācāryassuprasannātmā svātmarakṣāṃ vidhāyaca ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ samuccārya kaniṣṭhādi ca ropayet ।।

pādyādyairdevamabhyarcya mukhavāsāntamādarāt ।
kuṃbhāṃstu saptadaśa ca alaṅkṛtya yathāvidhi ।।

vedyāmāropayetkuṃbhān svastike sannidhāya ca ।
śayyāvedi ca tatprācyāṃ sabhyakuṇḍaṃ prakalpyaca ।।

abjāgnikuṇḍamāgneyyāmīśe caupāsasaṃ tathā ।
aupāsanāgnikuṇḍe tu āghāraṃ vidhivadyajet ।।

śayyāvedyāstūttare ca trihastāyatavistṛtām ।
caturaśrāṃ samāṃ kṛtvāyantravediṃ salakṣaṇam ।।

pañcavarṇairviśeṣeṇa yantraṃ vikhya manoharam ।
atha yantraṃ pravakṣyāmi śruṇudhvaṃ munisattamāḥ ।।

sarvarakṣākarasudarśana yantraḥ- ādau ṣaṭkoṇaṃ vilikhya tanmadhye sādhyanāma vilikhya om kṣrām, hrīm, śrīm, vilikhya, tatpārśvayoḥ, irm, im, iti dṛṣṭibījaṃ, um, ūm, iti śrotrabījaṃ ca vilikhya, ṣaṭkoṇeṣu, sahasrārahum phaṭ iti sudarśanaṣaḍakṣarīṃ vilikhya, koṇasaṃdhau om ham lam ram yam? likhitvā, tadbahirvṛttamaṣṭadalaṃ vilikhya, daleṣu om na ma ssu dar śa nā ya iti vilikhya, dalasaṃdhau om ja ya ja ya nṛ siṃ ha iti vilikhya, tadbahirvṛttaṃ ṣodaśadalaṃ vilikhya, dalamadhye om na mo bha ga va te mahā su dar śa nāya svāhā iti vilikhya, dalasaṃdhau om hum na mo bha ga va te va jra va rā hā ya svā hā iti vilikhya, tadupari vṛttadvayaṃ vṛttadvayamadhye akārādikṣakārāntaṃ mātṛkāvarṇān vilikhya, tadupari bhūpuradvayaṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ vilikhya, caturdvāre om ām hrīm krom iti vilikhya, tattaddigdevatābījāni likhitvā, lam ram ham ṣam vam yam sam śam iti bījaṃ likhitvā, āgneyā dīśānāntaṃ prāṇapratiṣṭhāmantraṃ, mantrarājagāyatrīṃ, yantrarājagāyatrīṃ, cavilikhya, tanmantreṇāvāhyabhyarcya sudarśanamūla mantraṃ daśasahasraṃ japitvā, tadgrāyatṣā taddaśāṃśaṃ japitvā mantrarājaṃ ca daśāṃśaṃ japitvā taddaśāṃśaṃ tarpaṇaṃ taddaśāṃśaṃ homaṃ taddaśāṃśaṃ brāhmaṇabhojanaṃ kārayet yantradaśāṅgam- bījaṃ prāṇaṃ ca śaktiśca dṛṣṭirvaśyādikaṃ tathā mantrayantrasya gāyatrī bījasthāpanameva ca bhūtadikpālabījaṃ ca yantrasyāṅgāni vai daśa yantragāyatrī- yantrarājāya vidmahe mahāyantrāya dhīmahi tanno yantraḥ pracodayāt sudarśanagāyatrī- ugraṃ vīraṃ mahāviṣṇuṃ jvalantaṃ sarvatomukham nṛsiṃhaṃ bhīṣaṇaṃ bhadraṃ matyumṛtyuṃ namāmyaham tatra sarvatrānukramaṇikāsu yantrasyāsya pāṭhodṛśyate mūlagranthetvasya mātṛkākośena dṛśyate 
tathāpi bahūnāṃ mātṛkākośānāmanupalaṃ
bhādasyasthitiratra aśaṅkitāpi niveśyate
parastīrya vidhānena pāvakaṃ vidhivadyajet ।।

lājāpūpai rājya miśrairmūlamantraṃ samuccaran ।
aṣṭāttaraśatenaiva homayeddeśikottamaḥ ।।

puruṣasūktaṃ ca juhuyāttato dvātriṃśasaṃkhyayā ।
paścādagniṃ paristīrya "kṣaya''sveti praṇamya ca ।।

evaṃ pratidinaṃ kuryādante devaṃ tu ropayet ।
sāyaṃ saṃdhyāmupāsitvā yāgaśālāṃ praviśya ca ।।

sabhyāgniṃ paiṇḍarīkāgniṃ cāsādyāghāramācaret ।
abjāgnau śāntihomaṃ ca hutvaiva gururatvaraḥ ।।

kuṃbhaṃ vinā mahāśāntihomaṃ ke cidvadantihi ।
vedyāṃ tu puratastiṣṭhan prāṇāyāmādikaṃ caret ।।

navamūrtibhirāvāhya dikpālānāvahetkramāt ।
aṣṭopacārairabhyarchya mudgānnaṃ vinivedayet ।।

pānīyācamanaṃ datvā mukhavāsaṃ dadettataḥ ।
"āpo vā'' iti mantreṇa pavitraṃ dhārayedghaṭam ।।

"agnāvagni''riti procya pavitraṃ cāgnikuṇḍake ।
kuṇḍasyaiva tu mānena samalaṅkṛtya pāvakam ।।

"pavitrantu'' iti procya pavitraṃ dhārayedguruḥ ।
saminthyaiva tu sabhyāgniṃ pariṣicya vidhānataḥ ।।

hautraṃ praśaṃsya vidhivatsamidbhirhāvayedguruḥ ।
tadālayagatān ścaiva devānāvāhayetkramāt ।।

juṣṭākāraṃ tataḥ paścātsvāhākālaṃ tataḥ param ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ suhutvā tu puruṣasūktamataḥ param ।।

caruṃ lājāṃs tathāpūpānājyamiśrāṃśca hāvayet ।
paścāttu vaiṣṇavairmantraiścatamaṣṭottaraṃ yajert ।।

iṅkārādīṃstataḥ paścātpāramātmikasaṃyutam ।
aṣṭāśītiṃ tato hutvā tattaddaivatyameva ca ।।

sarvadaivatyamantrāṃśca dhātādīn pañca vāruṇam ।
mūlahomaṃ tato hutvā tathānte pariṣicya ca ।।

yāgaśālācaturdvāre caturvedānathoccaret ।
aiśānyāṃ tu viśeṣeṇa japedaṣṭākṣaraṃ manum ।।

dvādaśākṣaramantraṃ ca gāyatrīṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ tathā ।
nārāyaṇākhyagāyatrīṃ pāramātmikamityapi ।।

vyāpakatrayasaṃyuktaṃ viṣṇugāyatriyā yutam ।
tataśca vaiṣṇavaṃ japtvā "yo vā bhū'' teti pañcakam ।।

puṣbāñjaliṃ japitvaiva nyaseddevasya pādayoḥ ।
nṛttagītādivādyaiśca rātriśeṣaṃ nayedguruḥ ।।

tataḥ prabhāte dharmātmā snātvā saṃdhyāmupāsya ca ।
yāgaśālāṃ praviśyaiva deveśaṃ prārthayettataḥ ।।

"bhūragnaya'' iti procya vediṃ saṃprokṣya cātvaraḥ ।
kuṃbhārādhanahomādīn sarvaṃ pūrvavadācaret ।।

kuṃbhamārādhayetpūrvaṃ biṃbapūjā tvanantaram ।
paścāddhomaṃ prakurvīta balidānaṃ tataḥ param ।।

evaṃ kuryādvidhānena dinaṃ prati gurūttamaḥ ।
samāpte tu dine sāyaṃ pūrṇāhuti mathācaret ।।
tadagniṃ triyahādūrdhvaṃ sādhayedagnikuṇḍake? ।।
kuṃbhamādāya śirasā toyadhārāpurassaram ।
pradakṣiṇaṃ śanairgatvā devāgre sannidhāya ca ।।

"hiraṇya pavamānā'' dyaiḥkuṃbhatoyena prokṣayet ।
devamabhyarcya pādyādyaiḥ prabhūtaṃ ca nivedayet ।।

pānīyācamalaṃ datvā mukhavāsaṃ dadetpunaḥ ।
kṣamāmantraṃ samuccārya "kṣama'' sveti namenmuhuḥ ।।

yajamāno api śuddhātmā bhaktinamrassamāhitaḥ ।
ācāryaṃ pūjayettatra gandhamāryānulepanaiḥ ।।

pañcāṅgabhūṣaṇaiścaiva dukūlaiśca navaistathā ।
tato guruḥ prasannātmā prayuñjyādāśiṣastadā ।।

taduktaṃ bhagavatproktaṃ pratigṛhṇīyurādarāt ।
evaṃ kurvīta pratyabdaṃ pavitrāropaṇaṃ hareḥ ।।

ihaloke sukhībhūtvā sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।
priyatāṃ bhagavānviṣṇuḥ prārthanāsūktamucyate ।।

"kanikradā''pimantrāśca śākunaṃ sūktamīritam ।
"svastino mimī''tetyuktvā svastisūktamiti smṛtam ।।

"śuddhā ime paśava'' iti gosūktaṃ samudāhṛtam ।
"ṛtaṃ ca satyaṃ'' cetyādi aghamarṣaṇamucyate ।।

"aṇoraṇīyā'' nityuktvāsūktaṃ prokṣaṇamīritam ।
"apo hiraṇyavarṇāśca pavamāna'' iti trayaḥ ।।

prokṣaṇaṃ sūktamiti tu kecidvaikalpikaṃ jaguḥ ।
"yā jātā'' iti mantrāśca oṣadhīsūktamucyate ।।

"kṛṇuṣva pāja'' ityādi sūktaṃ pratisarāhvayam ।
।।

"atodevādi ṣaṇmantrā''ṣ,ḍvaiṣṇavapadāhvayāḥ ।
"viṣṇornu''kādi ṣaṇmantrā viṣṇusūktamudīritam ।।

"sahasraśīrṣā puruṣa'' iti pauruṣasūktakam ।
"hiraṇya varṇā'' ityādi śrīsūktaṃ sarvakāmadam ।।

"bhūmirbhūmne''tyādimantrā bhūmisūktamudāhṛtam ।
"upa śvāsaya'' ityādi dundubhīsūktamucyate ।।

"suparṇo asi garutmā''nityuktaṃ sūktaṃ ca gāruḍam ।
"hiraṇyagarbha''ityādi brahmasūktamudhṛtam ।।

"indraṃ vo viśvata'' iti indrasūktamihocyate ।
"agne nayetyā''diṣaḍbhiragnisūktaṃ pracakṣate ।।

"āyātudeva'' ityādiyamasūktaṃprakīrtitam ।
"namassute nirṛte'' sūktaṃnairṛtamucyate ।।

"astabhnādyāmṛṣabha''iti vāruṇasūktakam ।
"pīvonnāṃrayi vṛdhassumedhā''iti vāyavam ।।

"adbhyastirodhā''ityādi kauveraṃ sūktamucyate ।
"stuhi śrutaṃ garta''iti rudrasūktaṃ prakīrtitam ।।

"omāsaścarṣaṇī''tyādi sūktaṃ sārasvataṃ bhavet ।
"viśvajitedhana''iti viśvajitsūktamucyate ।।

"rātrī vyakhya''dityādi rātrisūktamudāhṛtam ।
"jātavedasa''ityādi ṣaḍdurgāsūktamucyate ।।

"ā godānā''diti procyagodānaṃ sūktamucyate ।
"ekākṣaram'' itiprocya sūktamekākṣarādikam ।।
"ātmātmā parametyādi ātmasūktaṃ prakīrtitam ।।
vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣa sūktamataḥ param ।
śrībhūsūktaṃ ca pañcaitaṃ pañcasūktamihocyate ।।

viṣṇusūktaṃ nṛsūktaṃ ca śrībhūsūktamataḥ param ।
ekākṣarādi sūktaṃ ca pañcasūktaṃ jaguḥpare ।।

viṣṇusūktaṃ nṛsūktaṃ ca śrībhūsūktaṃ ca vaiṣṇavam ।
ekākṣarādisūktaṃ ca viṣṇugāyatriyā sahā ।।

āhatya saptabhiścaitaissaptasūktaṃ samīritam ।
rudrasūktaṃ dhruvasūktaṃ durgāsūktaṃ tataḥ param ।।

rātrisūktaṃ tathā sūktaṃ sārasvatamapi kramāt ।
viśvajitsūktamatha ca sahasraśīrṣamityapi ।।

aghamarṣaṇasūktaṃ ca godānaṃ sūktameva ca ।
ātmasūktena saṃyuktaṃ daśamūktamudāhṛtam ।।

daśasūktaṃ pañcasūktaṃ kṛtvā saṃhṛtameva ca evaṃ ।
bhavetpañca daśasūktamiti saṃjñā prabhāṣitā ।।

ataḥparaṃ pravakṣyāmi śruṇudhvaṃ munisattamāḥ ।
maṇḍalārādhanaṃ nityaṃ puṇyāhaṃ snapanaṃ caret ।।

catpāriṃśaddhinādūrdhvaṃ maṇḍalaṃ dinapañcakam ।
puṇyāhaṃ vidhivatkṛtvā vrīhibhistaṇḍulopari ।।

navaṃ kalaśamādāya pūrvoktena vidhānataḥ ।
samabhyarcya japaṃ kuryādbrāhmaṇairbrahmavādibhiḥ ।।

vaiṣṇavaṃ viṣṇusūktaṃ ca puruṣasūktamataḥ param ।
śrībhūsūktaṃ tathā pañcaśāntiṃ caiva pṛthak pṛthak ।।

caturāvartya japtvā tu snāpayeddhruvamacyutam ।
tathaiva kautukādīṃśca snāpayedvidhinā budhaḥ ।।

dadhyodanaṃ guḍānnaṃ ca pāyasaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
nivedya devadevasya mukhavāsaṃ pradāpayet ।।

ācāryadakṣiṇāṃ dadyādṛtvijāṃ ca tathaiva ca ।
pratiṣṭhādinamārabhya maṇḍalāntaṃ dinaṃ prati ।।

evameva krameṇaiva kārayettu viśeṣataḥ ।
maṇḍalārdhaṃ tu kuryācchenmadhyamaṃ tatpracakṣate ।।

maṇḍalānte viśeṣeṇa kārayeddvijabhojanam ।
sabhyāgnikuṇḍaṃ kṛtvaiva puṇyāhamasi vācayet ।।

āghāraṃ vidhivaddhutvā vaiṣṇavaṃ sūktameva ca ।
viṣṇusūktaṃ tato hutvā puruṣasūkta samanvitam ।।

śrībhūsūktaṃ samuccārya pañcaśāntimataḥ param ।
pāramātmikamīṅkārādyaṣṭāśītiṃ kramāddhunet ।।

aṣṭākṣaraṃ samuccārya tathaiva dvādaśākṣaram ।
pūrṇāhutiṃ tato hutvā antahomaścahūyate ।।

saṃsnāpayeccha kalaśairaṣṭādhikaśataiḥkramāt ।
varṇayuktandhruvaṃ beraṃ prāṅgayet snāpayennatu ।।

dvādaśārādhanaṃ kuryānmadhye madhye vidhānataḥ ।
grāmaṃ pradakṣiṇīkṛtya sarvavādyasamanvitam ।।

pakṣirājopari sthāpya rakṣādīpaṃ ca darśayet ।
jīvasthāne susaṃsthāpya praṇāmaṃ kārayettataḥ ।।

evaṃ yaḥkurute bhaktyā maṇḍalārādhanaṃ hareḥ ।
sarvān kāmānavāpyaiva sa yāti paramāṅgatim ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ saṃhitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre dvātriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

athatrayastriṃśo adhyāyaḥ arcāvatāramahattvam

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa devadevasya śārṅgiṇaḥ ।
pañcadhāvasthitaṃ rūpaṃ paravyūhādibhedataḥ ।।

anugrahāya lokānāṃ bhaktānāmanukaṃpayā ।
paravyūhādibhedena devadevaḥ pravartate ।।

ādyena pararūpeṇa vyūhākhyenetareṇa tu ।
tathāvibhavarūpeṇa nānābhāvamupeyuṣā ।।

antaryāmisvarūpeṇa caturthena tathā punaḥ ।
arcāvatārarūpeṇa pañcadhāvasthito hariḥ ।।

anaupama manirdesyaṃ punassa bhajate param ।
viśvāpyāyanakaṃ kāntyā pūrṇendvayutulyayā ।।

parandhāma parañjyotissarvaśaktimayo amalaḥ ।
nirdvandvo nirvikalpo acchonityo acintyassanātanaḥ ।।

aprameyo nirādyanto dṛśyo adṛśyo hyatīndriyaḥ ।
susūkṣmatvādanirdeśyassarvajñassadasadvibhuḥ ।।

ānādimatparaṃ brahma sarvaheyavivarjitam ।
vyāpi yatsarvabhūteṣu sthitaṃ sadasatoḥ param ।।

śaṅkhacakragadāpadmadivyāyudhapariṣkṛtaḥ ।
sahasrādityasaṃkāśe pakame vyomni saṃsthitaḥ ।।

nityamuktaikasaṃbhāvyaścaturbhujadharohariḥ ।
anyūnānatarigtaissvairguṇaiṣṣaḍbhiralaṅkṛtaḥ ।।

samassamavibhaktāṅgassarvāvayavasundaraḥ ।
divyairābharaṇairyuktassudhākallolasaṃkulaiḥ ।।
śriyā nityānapāyinyā sevyamāno jagatpatiḥ ।।
pañcadhātu punarvyūhaḥ procyate śrutisammataḥ ।
devo viṣṇvādibhedeva pañcadhā vyavatiṣṭhate ।।

sa vā eṣa puruṣaḥ pañcadhā pañcātmeti ca śrutiḥ ।
tathā popūyamānaḥ pañcabhissvaguṇairiti ।।

ādimūrtistu pañcānāṃ viṣṇurbhedāśca tasyatu ।
catasraḥ puruṣādyāssyurmūrtayo bhinnalakṣaṇāḥ ।।

tadviṣṇośśramāpanudāya caturguṇā''yeti caśrutiḥ ।
tasmādbrahma catuṣpādityucyate vedavedibhiḥ ।।

pādādardhāttripādācca kevalācchaktibhedataḥ ।
krameṇa dharmajñānaiśvaryavairāgyākhyairguṇairyutāḥ ।।

bhavantimūrtayastasmāccatasro viṣayairnijaiḥ ।
cāturātmyādādimūrteścatasrastatramūrtayaḥ ।।

viṣṇuścaiva mahāviṣṇussadāviṣṇuriti kramāt ।
vyāpī nārāyaṇa iti tannāmāni tataḥkramāt ।।

viṣṇoraṃśastu puruṣo mahāviṣṇostu satyakaḥ ।
sadāviṣṇoracyutassyādyyāpino aṃśo aniruddhakaḥ ।।

dharmādibhirbrahmaguṇaiścaturdhābheda īritaḥ ।
tṛtīyaṃ vibhavākhyantaṃ viśvamantaramadhyamam? ।।

nānākārakriyākartṛ rūpaṃ vakṣye mahātmanaḥ ।
vibhavā matsyakūrmādyā hayagrīvādayo matāḥ ।।

antaryāmisvarūpaṃ tu turīyamidamucyate ।
nīvāraśūkavattanvī pītābhā syāttanūpamā ।।

tasyāśśikhāyā madhye paramātmā vyavasthitaḥ ।
ityuktaśśrutyabhihito hṛdayāṃbujamadhyame ।।

jvalanmahāgnau viśvārcirjvālānte viśvato mukhe ।
āpādatalacūḍāgraṃ santāpayati santatam ।।

śikhā tatra ca pītābhā tanvī nīvāraśūkavat ।
madhye śikhāyāstasyāśca jyotiḥ prajvalitaṃ mahat ।।

svasaṃkalpaviśeṣeṇa taptajāṃbūnadaprabhaḥ ।
pītāṃbaradharassaumyassuprasannaśśucismitaḥ ।।

padmākṣo raktanetrāsyapāṇipādaścaturbhujaḥ ।
cakraśaṅkhābhayadharaḥ kaṭinyastānyahastakaḥ ।।

śrīvatsāṃko mahābāhussarvābharaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।
hṛdi tiṣṭhati sarvātmā śrībhūmibhyāṃ ca pārṣadaiḥ ।।

bhrāmayan sarvabhūtāni yantrārūḍhāni māyayā ।
antaryāmīti vijñeyassarvakāraṇakāraṇaḥ ।।

anyadarcāsvarūpaṃ tu sarvottaraphalapradam ।
nityamuktopabhogyatvātparavyūhātmanohareḥ ।।

tatkālasannikṛṣṭaikalakṣyatvādvibhavātmanaḥ ।
viśuddhairyogasaṃsiddhaiścintyatvādantarātmanaḥ ।।

arcātmanyeva sarveṣāmadhikāro niraṅkuśaḥ ।
viśeṣabhaktihetutvātpratimārādhanaṃ param ।।

arcāvatārassarveṣāṃ bāndhavo bhaktavatsalaḥ ।
arcāvatāraviṣaye mayāpyuddeśatastathā ।।

uktā guṇā na śakyante vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi ।
vicitrā dehasaṃpattirīśvarāya niveditum ।।

kalpitā brahmaṇā pūrvaṃ hastapādādisaṃyutā ।
mudhaiva jihvā kṛṣṇeti keśaveti na vakṣyati ।।

mudhā cittaṃ natadgāmi yadanyatkimito adhikam ।
sā jihvā yā hariṃ stauti taccittaṃ keśavārpitam ।।

tatkarmacārcanaṃ tasya tadanyattu nirarthakam ।
sattāmātraṃ paraṃ brahma viṣṇvākhyamaviśeṣaṇam ।।

durvicintyaṃ yataḥpūrvaṃ tatprāptyarthamihocyate ।
vātormicañcalaṃ cittamanālaṃbanamasthiram ।।

sūkṣmatvādbrahmaṇo ajasya nigrāhyaṃ grāhmadharmaṇaḥ ।
samyagabhyasyato ajasramupabṛṃhitaśaktimat ।।

janmāntaraśatasyāpi brahmagrāhyeva jāyate ।
yadyastarāyadoṣeṇa nāpakarṣo vicintyate ।।

yogino yogarūḍhasya tālāgrātpatanaṃ yathā ।
tadāpnoti paraṃ brahmakleśena mahatāpi ca ।।

janmāntarābhyāsoddhena vijñānena samādhinā ।
viṣṇvākhyaṃ brahmaduṣprāpaṃ viṣayākrāntacetasā ।।

manuṣyeṇālpasāreṇa tatprāptau sādhanaṃ tvidam ।
surūpāṃ pratimāṃ viṣṇoḥ prasannavadanekṣaṇām ।।

kṛtvātmanaḥ prītikarīṃ suvarṇarajatādibhiḥ ।
tāmarcayettāṃ vraṇamettāṃ namettāṃ vicintayet ।।
viśatyapāstadoṣastu tāmeva brahmarūpiṇīm ।।
iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ sahitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre trayastriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha catustriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

svayaṃvyaktādi sthānapañcakam

ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi sthalapañcakakalpanam ।
devadevo mahābāhurharirnārāyaṇassvayam ।।

yena yena prakāreṇa āvirāstedharātale ।
arcāvatārarūpeṇa bhaktasaulabhyahetave ।।

svayaṃvyaktaṃ ca divyaṃ ca saiddhaṃ paurāṇameva ca ।
pauruṣaṃ ceti kathitaṃ sthalānāṃ pañcakaṃ budhaiḥ ।।

svayaṃvyaktaṃ tu tatproktaṃ yatrāsau harivyayaḥ ।
svecchayā lokarakṣāye bhūmyāmāvirbhavetsvayam ।।

na tatra devadevasya pratiṣṭhā vidhisammatā ।
na cāpi karṣaṇaṃ nāpi biṃbaśuddhyādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।।

biṃbena saha deveśassannidhatte yatassvayam ।
yānadicchā vasedbhūmau tāvatkālaṃ samarcitaḥ ।।

svayaṃvyaktasthale pūjā sarvalokaśubhapradā ।
svayaṃvyaktasthalānyatra catvāryāsata bhūtale ।।

yatra vaikhānasaṃ śāstramāśritya paramaṃ śubham ।
arcayāmo jagadyonimahamanye ca te trayaḥ ।।

marīcirmandhare viṣṇumarcayāmāsa keśavam ।
sarvadevottamaṃ devaṃ śrīnivāse atrirarcayat ।।

kāśyapo viṣṇvadhiṣṭhāne śubhakṣetre apyahaṃ bhṛguḥ ।
yādṛśīvartate pūjā yā biṃbānāṃ ca saṃsthitiḥ ।।

na kiṃ cittāmatikramya pūrvoktāṃ tu samācaret ।
svayamāvirabhūddevo yatra bhaktānukaṃpayā ।।

kartavyamakhilaṃ tatra tannideśena kalpyate ।
na vāpyucchāstrakaraṇaṃ pravartayati mādhavam ।।

tasmātsarvaprayatnena pūrvairācaritaṃ caret ।
anyathā cettu kurvāṇo devāyaivāparādhyati ।।

yanmāyāmohitaṃ sarvaṃ yasyāntaṃ ke api no viduḥ ।
tasya devasya māhātmyaṃ vaktuṃ śaknoti ko bhuvi ।।

yadyadā caritaṃ tatra tatsarvaṃ śāstrameva hi ।
tatrāpi ca viśeṣo asti prāyaścittādidarśane ।।

sarvaṃ prāmādikaṃ kuryāttatra śāstraṃ pravartakam ।
śrutismṛtī ubhetasya paramājñāṃ vadanti hī ।।

svayaṃvyaktasthale pūjā sarvalokaśūbhāvahā ।
svayaṃ vyakto jagannāthastādātmyena śilādiṣu ।।

svayaṃ bhaktajanābhīṣṭān vicāryaiva prayacchati ।
na hyatra sādhanāpekṣā svayaṃnyaktastato varaḥ ।।

devaiḥ pratiṣṭhito yatra harirāvirbabhūva hi ।
taddidyasthalamuddiṣṭaṃ devo divya udīryate ।।

smṛtā devāstrayastriṃśattāvatkoṭīmitā api ।
sarve te phalakāmāssyurve prapadyante yathā harim ।।

tāṃstathā bhajate devo yato asau karuṇānidhiḥ ।
phalārthino yadā devāḥ pratiṣṭhyāpya hariṃ kramāt ।।

samabhyarcya ca saṃprāpya vāṃbhitaṃ tadanantaram ।
lokānugrahahetor vai tādṛśaṃ devamandiram ।।

cirasthāyi ca saṃkalpya yathārhaṃ samapūjayan ।
divyasthalasthadevo hi devānāṃ sannidhāpanāt ।।

atyantaṃ puṣṭivaḥ proktassarvaśāntikarassṛtaḥ ।
divyasthalasthapūjā tu śatayojanavistṛtam ।।

punāti parito deśaṃ nātra saṃdeha iṣyate ।
divyasthalāni kathitānyasaṃkhyeyāni bhūtale ।।

na hi devāssvayaṃ bhūmāvavatīrya kalau kvacit ।
pratiṣṭhāṃ devadevasya kurvanti kuhiciddhruvam ।।

divyasthalāni bhūbhāge kalau tu viralāni vai ।
bhaviṣyanti bahūnyatra luptabūjāni sattamāḥ ।।

divyasthalakṛtā pūjā śāstrasiddhā na saṃśayaḥ ।
nocchāstraṃ tu pratiṣṭhādi kurvantidivi devatāḥ ।।

devāśca devaloke api kṛtvā vaiṣṇavamandiram ।
ārādhya ca jagannāthaṃ prāpnuvanti phalaṃ bahu ।।

yā tu bhūmitale pūjā tādṛśī divijā na vai ।
karmabhūmistu saṃproktā bhūmirdyairna hi tatsamā ।।

saṃcintya puṇyaṃ pāpaṃ vā bhūmau lokāntarenarāḥ ।
gamiṣyantitato jyāyān bhūbhāgassarvakarmasu ।।

tato devāḥ pratiṣṭhāpya cārcayitvā ramāpatim ।
arcāvatārarūpeṇa svayaṃ tīrṇāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।।

bhūmisthānakhilān jantūn tāryayiṣyantyanugrahāt ।
ato viprāssadā yajñairdānaiśca tapasā muhuḥ ।।

toṣayiṣyanti devānvai teṣāmānṛṇyahetave ।
devā nisargaripavo manuṣyeṣu bhavantyapi ।।

ārādhanena devasya copakurvanti mānavān ।
idameva hareḥ pūjābalaṃ saṃpāditaṃ phalam ।।

sarve api sāttvikā yānti tuṣyanti svārjitaiḥ phalaiḥ ।
na dviṣyanti ripūnvāpi tatro dāharaṇaṃ surāḥ ।।

yathā cyavanadharmā syātsvargassvargāśrito atha vā ।
tathādinyasthalāniha na syuśśāśvatikāni tu ।।

divyasthaleṣu sarvatra divyenaivāgamena tu ।
vaikhānasena pūjāsītsāhi śrautī ca sammatā ।।

prāyaścittocitānyatra nimittāni yadātadā ।
śāstroktaṃ kārayedeva nānyathā kārayedvidhiḥ ।।

ye tu pūrvārjitaireva tapobhiḥ paramātmani ।
raktātmānastapassiddhāssaṃkalpya svatapaḥphalam ।।

devadevaṃ jagannāthaṃ nārāyaṇamanāyam ।
pratiṣṭhāpya kvacidbiṃbe samabhyarcya viśeṣataḥ ।।

ujjīvanāya lākānāṃ pradāsyantīha pūjanam ।
sa deśassaiddha ityuktassaiddhā tatrārcanocyate ।।

na hi siddhāstapassiddhiṃ kurvanti vibhalāṃ kvacit ।
yasyānugrahamicchantastapasyantīha sādhavaḥ ।।

yaṃ prasādayituṃ viprā yajñadānādi kurvate ।
tasyaivārādhanaṃ hitvā kiṃ siddhāssaṃprakurvate ।।

te siddhāste mahātmānaste santa nte tapasvinaḥ ।
ye svakarmaphalaṃ devaṃ viditvā śrīpatiṃ harim ।।

pratiṣṭhāpya tu tadrūpamarcayanti nirantaram ।
na hyanyaḥ prāpaṇe heturarcanānmuktihetave ।।

saiddhasthale tu yā pūjā sarvaśāntikarī smṛtā ।
pañcāśadyojanaṃ tasya paritaḥ pāvayenmahīm ।।

siddhapratiṣṭhitā deśā bahavo viditāḥ purā ।
utpadyante bhaviṣyanti santisiddhā dharātale ।।

saiddhasthalāni bhūyāṃsi bhaviṣyanti ca santi ca ।
siddhā vaikhānasaṃ śāstramāśrityaiva svanirmitam ।।

devaṃ saṃpūjayantīha tatprāyaḥ pracalatyapi ।
na hi siddhāḥ prakurvantikiñciducchāstramāpadi ।।

tasmātsarvaprayatnena sarvaṃ siddhāśritasthale ।
kuryādvaikhānasaṃ śāstramāśritya sakalāḥ kriyāḥ ।।

siddhā jānanti śāstrārthān siddhā jānanti cāgamān ।
siddhāssamarcayantyeva vaikhānasavidhānataḥ ।।

yadi siddhāśrito deśaḥpūjyate anyaiḥ pramādataḥ ।
rājā taṃ tu vicāryaiva punarvaikhānasaiḥkramāt ।।

satvaraṃ yājayetkṛtvā prāyaścittaṃ yathāvidhi ।
saiddhameke sthalaṃ prāhurārṣametacca sammatam ।।

atha paurāṇiko deśaḥ kathyate yatra yatra vai ।
gādhā paurāṇikī bhūyāttatpurāṇasthalaṃ matam ।।

ajñātakartṛkāṇyatra smaryante prāyaśo bahu ।
sthalānīmānitattāni?purāṇāni pracakṣate ।।

purāṇāni tvanantāni sthalāni pṛthivītale ।
bhavantyatha kalau prāpte lupyante tānyanekaśaḥ ।।

daśayojanaparyantāṃ bhūmiṃ tu paritassakṛt ।
punāti deśaḥ paurāṇastatra kiṃ cinna hīyate ।।

svayaṃvyaktādayassarve paurāṇāḥ kīrtitā api ।
svayaṃvyaktādibhedena vyavahārasya darśanāt ।।

purāṇatvaṃ ca teṣāṃ syādanyat paurāṇamucyate ।
purāṇasthaladevasya pratiṣṭhā vidhisammatā ।।

pratiṣṭhite tvavidhinā sthare naiva rameddhariḥ ।
na hi vṛddhāssamarcanti biṃbamucchāstranirmitam ।।

na hi paurāṇike deśe yajamānasya gauravam ।
arthasya gauravaṃ cāpi darśanīyaṃ mahātmabhiḥ? ।।

yadi paśyedvisūḍhātmā rauravaṃ narakaṃvrajet ।
eṣa eva viśeṣassyādanyatsaiddhavadācaret ।।

purāṇasthalapūjā tu śāstradṛṣṭena vartmanā ।
pramādetu samīkāryāna tena syādvyatikramaḥ ।।

mānuṣaṃ pañcamaṃ proktaṃ sthalaṃ yatra viśeṣataḥ ।
grāme vā nagare vāpi śāstrokte sumanorame ।।

pratiṣṭāpyārcake viṣṇussarvadeveśvareśvaraḥ ।
brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyaiśśūdrairvānyairnarottamaiḥ ।।

vaikhānasena śāstreṇa pañcarātreṇa vā punaḥ ।
mānuṣasthalapūjā tu yojanaṃ paritasthsalam ।।

pāpayettasya tu proktāśaktiranyātu tāvatī ।
manuṣyāḥ puṇyakarmāṇastatra tatra dine dine ।।

preritā bhagavadbhaktyādhanino nirdhanā api ।
nirmāya bhagavadgehaṃ pratiṣṭhāpya śriyaḥpatim ।।

arcayanti viśeṣeṇa vaikhānasavidhānataḥ ।
viśālaḥ pṛthivībhāgaḥ kālo anādirantakaḥ ।।

śāstraṃ cāpyatigaṃbhīraṃ bhaktāśca bahavo harau ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena sarvasyāpyanuśāsanam ।।

proktaṃ vikhanasā pūrvaṃ bhagavacchāstramuttamam ।
anenaiva prakāreṇa sarvatrārādhayeddharim ।।

bhaktāśca bahudhā śāstraṃ praśaṃsantīdameva hī ।
taduktenaiva vidhinā kalpayedālayādikam ।।

yathā mānādhikaraṇe mayā proktassa vistaraḥ ।
yatra vā dṛśyate bhedo bhagavacchāstraśilpayoḥ ।।

śilpaśāstraṃ parityajya bhagavacchāstrataścaret ।
pradhānametacchāstraṃ syādbhagavadgehakalpane ।।

na tacchāstramanādṛtya kāryaṃ kiṃ citsamācaret ।
lobhānmohādathājñānācchāstre asminna dhṛtaṃ caret ।।

atikramyāpi śāstraṃ tatpūjā niṣbhalā bhavet ।
yajamāno vipadyeta tasmādatroktamācaret ।।

tenaiva tu vidhānena pratiṣṭhādikamācaret ।
aihikāmuṣmikaṃ yasmātphaladvayamavāpyate ।।

grāme viṣṇvarcanāhīne viṣṇvarcāhīnaveśmani ।
tīrthapānaṃ surāpānamannaṃ gomāṃsabhakṣaṇam ।।

devadhāmavihīnaṃ tu śmaśānaṃ grāma ucyate ।
gṛhaṃ ca cititulyaṃ syādyatra nārādhyate hariḥ ।।
