yo mohādatha vālasyādakṛtvā devatārcanam ।
bhuṅkte sa yāti narakān sūkareṣvasi jāyate ।।

keśavārcāgṛhe yasya na tiṣṭhati śūbhapradā ।
tasyānnaṃ naiva bhoktavyamabhakṣyeṇa samaṃ hi tat ।।

biṃbaśuddhyādikaṃ kṛtvā śāstroktavidhinā punaḥ ।
kalānyāsādikaṃ sarvaṃ vidhāya parameśvaraḥ ।।

pratiṣṭhāpyārcyate yatra parito yojanāvadhi ।
pūyate anugrahādviṣṇoḥ sa deśo aprākṛtassmṛtaḥ ।।

tatra pārṣadasaṃyuktaśśriyā lakṣmyā samanvitaḥ ।
yathā ca parame vyomni sannidhatte tathā hariḥ ।।

tatra devāstrayastriṃśatpitaraḥ pannagāśca ye ।
sādhyā vidyādharā yakṣāssarvā vai devayonayaḥ ।।

sarvasaṃvatsamṛddhissyātparjanyo varṣuko bhavet ।
vāyurvāti sukhaṃ tatra sūryastapati tejasā ।।

candramāśśītalairdeśaṃ sevate kiraṇaistathā ।
bhūmissasyavatī ca syātprasannaṃ ca nabho bhavet ।।

nakṣatragrahatārāśca prasādābhimukhāssame ।
rājanvatī prajā ca syātpaśuputrasamanvitā ।।

na vyādhijaṃ bhayaṃ kiṃ cinnāpi jvarakṛtaṃ tathā ।
na vyālajaṃ bhayaṃ vāpi bhavedatrana saṃśayaḥ ।।

nopaplavo nṛpāṇāṃ vā mṛgāṇāṃ vāpyapāṃ bhavet ।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāśśūdrāstatra nivāsinaḥ ।।

sve sve karmaṇyabhiratā bhaveyussukhajīvinaḥ ।
āgnihotrāśca hūyante tapyante atra tapāṃsi ca ।।

dīyante bhūridānāni yatra devo harispvayam ।
aprākṛtamimaṃ deśaṃ sannidhānācchriyaḥ pateḥ ।।

prākṛtaṃ yo vadenmūḍhassa yāti narakaṃ dhruvam ।
aprākṛtamimaṃ devaṃ naro yaścāpanihnute ।।

caṇḍālassa tu vijñeyo niṣkṛtirnāsya dṛśyate ।
mahāpātakīnāṃ tadvaddṛṣṭaṃ pātakināmapi ।।

upapātakināṃ cāpi prāyaścittaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
śāstrāpalāpināṃ naiva prāyaścittaṃ pradṛśyate ।।

yastu sāmānyabhāvena manyate sthalamīdṛśam ।
brahmahatyāmavāpnoti bhrūṇahatyāṃ tathaiva ca ।।

svarṇasteye ca yatpāpaṃ surāpāne ca yadbhavet ।
gurutalpasya gamane yaccapāpamudīritam ।।

vṛṣalīgamane yacca pāpaṃ sarvaṃ tadaśnute ।
nāsti śāstrātparaṃ jñānaṃ nasyāttasmātpravartakam ।।

tasmāttasyāvamānena sadyaḥ patati dūṣakaḥ ।
tasmin deśe viśeṣeṇa sarvebhāgavatā harau ।।

devapādodakādīni pītvā yāsyantisadgatim ।
na hi sarvo api sarvatra svayaṃvyaktasthalādikam ।।

gatvaivārādhayedviṣṇuṃ sadā taccāpyasaṃbhavi ।
ata eva kṛpāsiṃdhurbhagavān bhūtabhāvanaḥ ।।

arcāvatārarūpeṇa grāme grāme gṛhe gṛhe ।
avatīrya mahābāhurbhaktasaulabhyahetave ।।

arcyate śāstravidhinā tatra kāryona saṃśayaḥ ।
tasmādaprākṛtaṃ deśaṃ na brūyātprākṛtaṃ naraḥ ।।

na ca sāmānyabhāvena taṃ paśyedyadi paśyati ।
naśyatyeva na saṃdeha iti śāstraviniścayaḥ ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ sahitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre catustriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha pañcatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

phalaśrutiḥ

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa kriyāyogaśritaṃ phalam ।
yastu devālayaṃ dāruśilālohavilekhanaiḥ ।।

kārayenmṛṇmayaṃ vāpi tasyānantaphalaṃ smṛtam ।
ahanyahani yajñena yajato yanmahatphalam ।।

prāpnoti tatphalaṃ viṣṇoryaḥ kārayati mandiram ।
kulānāṃ śatamāgāmi samatītaṃ tathā śatam ।।

tārayedbhagavadgehamiti buddhiṃ karoti yaḥ ।
saptajanmakṛtaṃ pāpamalpaṃ vā yadi vā bahu ।।

viṣṇorālayavinyāsaprāraṃbhādeva naśyati ।
saptalokamayo viṣṇustasya yaḥkurute gṛham ।।

pratiṣṭhāṃ samapāpnoti sa narassāptalaukikīm ।
praśastadeśe bhūbhāge yo naro bhavanaṃ hareḥ ।।

kārayatyakṣayān lokān sa varaḥ pratipadyate ।
iṣṭakācayavinyāso yāvadvarṣāṇi tiṣṭhati ।।

tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi tatkartādivi modate ।
pratimāṃ lakṣaṇavatīṃ yaḥ kārayati mānavaḥ ।।

kesavasya sa tallokamakṣayaṃ pratipadyate ।
ṣaṣṭiṃ varṣasahasrāṇāṃ sahasrāṇi sa mogate ।।

svargaukasāṃ nivāseṣu pratyekamarisūdanaḥ ।
tataḥ prayāti vaikuṇṭhaṃ nissamābhyadhikaṃ mahaḥ ।।

pratīṣṭhāpya harerarcāṃ supraśaste niveśane ।
puruṣaḥ kṛtakṛtyatvānnainaṃ śvo maraṇaṃ tapet ।।

ye bhaviṣyanti ye atītā ākalpāḥ puruṣāḥ kule ।
tāṃstārayati saṃsthāpya devasya pratiyāṃ hareḥ ।।

berapūjā tviyaṃ proktā pūjānāmuttamottamā ।
atīte yajamāne api ciramasyā avasthite ।।

anuśastāḥ kila purā yameva yamakiṅkarāḥ ।
pāśadhaṇḍadharāḥ krūrāḥ prajāsaṃyamanodyatāḥ ।।

viharadhvaṃ yathānyāyyaṃ niyogo me anupālyatām ।
nājñābhaṅgaṃ kariṣyanti bhavatāṃ jantavaḥ kvacit ।।

kevalaṃ ye jagannāthamanastaṃ samupāśritāḥ ।
bhavadbhiḥ parihartavyāsteṣāṃ nāstyatra saṃsthitiḥ ।।

ye tu bhāgavatā loke taccittāstatparāyaṇāḥ ।
pūjayanti sadā viṣṇuṃ te vastyājyāḥ sudūrataḥ ।।

yastiṣṭhan yassvapan bhuñjan uttiṣṭhan skhaliteṣu ca ।
saṃkīrtayati govindaṃ sa vastyājyassudūrataḥ ।।

nityanaimittikairdevaṃ ye yajante janārdanam ।
nāvalokyā bhavadbhiste tattejo hanti vau gatim ।।

ye dhūpapuṣpavāsobhirbhūṣaṇaiścāpi durlabhaiḥ ।
arcayanti na te grāhyānarāḥ kṛṣṇāśrayoddhatāḥ ।।

upalepanakartārassammārjanakarāśca ye ।
kṛṣṇālaye parityājyāsteṣāṃ tripūruṣaṃ kulam ।।

yena cāyatanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kāritaṃ tatkulodbhavam ।
puṃsāṃ kulaṃ nāvalokyaṃ bhavadbhirduṣṭacakṣuṣā ।।

yenārcā bhagavadbhaktyā vāsudevasya kāritā ।
narāyutaṃ tatkulajaṃ bhavatāṃ śāsanātigam ।।

bhavatāṃ bhramatāmatra viṣṇusaṃśrayamudrayā ।
vinājñābhaṅgakṛnnaiva bhaviṣyati naraḥkvacit ।।

yajñā narāṇāṃ pāpaughakṣālanāḥ sarvakāmadāḥ ।
tathaivejyā jagaddhātussarvayajñamayo hariḥ ।।

sthāpitaṃ pratimā viṣṇossamyak saṃpūjya mānavaḥ ।
yaṃ yaṃ kāmayate kāmaṃ taṃ tamāpnotyasaṃśayam ।।

yathā hi jvalano vahnistamohānintadarthinām ।
śītahānintadanyeṣāṃ svedaṃ svedābhilāṣiṇām ।।

karoti kṣudhitānāṃ ca bhojyāṃ pākakriyāṃ śikhī ।
tathaiva kāmān bhūteśassadadāti yathepsitam ।।

kalpadrumādivahareryadiṣṭaṃ tadavāpyate ।
yassadāyatane viṣṇoḥ kurute mārjanakriyām ।।

sapāṃsubhumyair? dehasya sarvaṃ pāpaṃ vyapohāti ।
yāvantaḥ pāṃsukaṇikā mārjyante keśavālaye ।।

varṣāṇi divi tāvante vasatyastamalo naraḥ ।
ahanyahani yatpāpaṃ kurute viṣayī naraḥ ।।

yo bāhyābhyantaraṃ veśma mārjayetkeśavālaye ।
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ tasya kāyo niṣkalmaṣo bhavet ।।

gocarmamātraṃ sammṛjya hanti tatkeśavālaye ।
sabāhyābhyantaraṃ yacca mārjayedacyutālaye ।।

sabāhyābhyantaraṃ tasya kāyaṃ niṣkalmaṣaṃ viduḥ? ।
udakābhyukṣaṇaṃ viṣṇoryaḥ karoti satā gṛhe ।।

so apigacchati yatrāste bhagavān yādasāṃ patiḥ ।
mṛdā dhātuvikārairvā varṇakairgomayena vā ।।

viṣṇorāyatane nityaṃ yaḥ karotyanu lepanam ।
pravāte vāti guṇavadvarṣāsvatimanoharam ।।

svanuliptaṃ śūbhākāraṃ svakṛhaṃ labhate naraḥ ।
pūrṇadhānyahiraṇyādimaṇimuktāphalojjvalam ।।

pratyāsannajalopetaṃ gṛhaṃ prāpnoti śobhanam ।
sāmantasvajanānāṃ ca sarveṣāmuttamottamam ।।

tadāpnoti gṛhaṃ ramyamupalepanakṛnnaraḥ ।
yenānulipte tiṣṭanti viṣṇvāyatanabhūtale ।।

brāhmaṇāḥkṣatriyā vaiśyāśśūdrassādhvyastriyastathā ।
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ nālaṃ devāssahānugāḥ ।।

apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇaṃ muktāhālaśatojjvalam ।
śreṣṭhaṃ sarvavimānānāṃ svargadhiṣṇyamavāpnuyāt ।।

yāvanta stithayo liptā divyābdāṃstāvato naraḥ ।
tasminvimāne sa narastsrī vā tiṣṭhati śobhane ।।

sraggandhavastrasaṃyuktaḥ sarvabhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ ।
gandharvāpsarasāṃ saṃghaiḥ pūjyamānassa tiṣṭhati ।।

liptā ca yāvatā hastā viṣṇorāyatane mahī ।
tāvadyojanavistīrṇasvargasthānādhipo bhavet ।।

pūjyamānassuragaṇaiśśītoṣṇādivivarjitaḥ ।
manojñagātro viprendraistiṣṭhatyābhūtasaṃplavam ।।

tat kṣayādiha cāgatya viśiṣṭe jāyate kule ।
atyutkṛṣṭagṛhaṃ prāpya martyaloke abhivāñchitam ।।

natatra tāvaddāridṣaṃ nopasargona vākaliḥ ।
na tāvanmṛtaniṣkrāntiryāvajjīvanti sākṣiṇaḥ ।।

viṣṇussamastabhūtāni sasarjaitāni yāni vai ।
teṣāṃ madhye jagaddhāturatīveṣṭā vasuṃdharā ।।

kṛte sammārjane tasyāstathā caivānulepane ।
prayāti paramaṃ toṣaṃ viṣṇurbhūrvaiṣṇavīyataḥ ।।

upoṣito naro nārī yaḥkarotyanulepanam ।
na tasyajāyate bhaṅgo gārhasthye tu kadā ca na ।।

yā ca nārī karotyevaṃ yathāvadanulepanam ।
nāpnoti sāpi vaidhavyaṃ gṛhabhaṅgaṃ kadā ca na ।।

sarvābharaṇasaṃpūrṇassarvopaskaradhānyavān ।
gomahiṣyādisaṃbhāgaṃ gṛhamāpnoti mānava ।।

tasmādabhīpsatā samyaggārhasthyaṃ tadakhaṇḍitam ।
viṣṇorāyatane kāryaṃ sahasai vopalepanam ।।

yaścānulepanaṃ kuryādviṣṇorāyatane naraḥ ।
so api lokaṃ samāsādya modatevai śatakratoḥ ।।

puṣpaprakīrṇamatyarthaṃ sugandhaṃ keśavālaye ।
upalipte naro datvā na durgatimavāpnuyāt ।।

snānapānāṃbhasāṃ viṣṇoḥ pradānāttatsalokabhāk ।
snānīyadravyadānena nīrogaḥ prītya modate ।।

kṣaumādidānādāpnoti paraloke mahatsukham ।
ālepanadravyadānātkāmānāpnoti śāśvatān ।।

elākarpūratāṃbūlītailādi sparśanātpukhī ।
paratreha ca loke syāddīrghakālamasaṃśayaḥ ।।

sarvayajñamayo viṣṇurgavyānāṃ paramassmṛtaḥ ।
jāyate yeṣu lokeṣu pulakassaṃgamomahān ।।

yeṣu kṣīravahā nadyo hradāḥ pāyasakardamāḥ ।
tān lokān puruṣā yāntikṣīrasnānakarā hareḥ ।।

āhgādaṃ nirvṛtiṃ svāsthyamārogyaṃ cārurūpatā ।
saptajanmānyavāpnoti kṣīrasnānakaro hareḥ ।।

dadhyādīnāṃ vikārāṇāṃ kṣīratassaṃbhavo yathā ।
tathaivāśeṣakāmānāṃ kṣīrasnāpanato hareḥ ।।

yathā ca vimalaṃ kṣīraṃ yathā nirvṛtikārakam ।
tathāsya nirmalaṃ jñānaṃ bhavatyatiphalapradam ।।

grahānukūlatāṃ puṣṭiṃ priyaṃ cāpyakhile jane ।
karoti bhagavān viṣṇuḥkṣīrasnāpanatoṣitaḥ ।।

sarvo asyasnigdhatāmeti dṛṣṭimātprātprasīdati ।
yassnāpayati devasya ghṛtena pratimāṃ hareḥ ।।

indraprasthe dvijāgṣāṇāṃ sa dadāti gavāṃ śatam ।
gavāṃ śatasya viprāṇāṃ na dattasya bhavetphalam ।।

ghṛtaprasthena tadviṣṇorlabhetsnānopayoginām ।
purā rājarṣibhiḥ prāptā saptadvīpā vasundharā ।।

ghṛtāḍhakena govinda pratimāsnāpanātkila ।
pratimāsaṃ sitāṣṭamyāṃ ghṛtena jagataḥ patim ।।

snāpayitvā samastebhyaḥ pāpebhyo api pramucyate ।
dvādaśyāṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ ca gavyena haviṣā hareḥ ।।

snāpanaṃ devadevasya mahāpātakanāśanam ।
jñānato ajñānato vāpi yatpāpaṃ kurute naraḥ ।।

tatkṣālayati saṃdhyāyāṃ ghṛtena snāpayan harim ।
ghṛtakṣīreṇa deveśe snāpite madhusūdane ।।

sa gatvāvaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma modate saha sūribhiḥ ।
srajaṃ baddhvā sumanasāṃ yaḥ prayacchati viṣṇave ।।

sa bhuktvā vipulān bhogānnākapṛṣṭhe virājate ।
cāmaravyajana chatradānātsvārājyamaśnu te ।।

dānādābharaṇādīnāṃ tejasvī divimodate ।
dānācca navaratnāvāṃ devasālokyamaśnute ।।

ādarśanapradānena dṛśyassarvairbhaviṣyati ।
gandhadravya pradānena sugandhirdāyate bhṛvet ।।

dhūpadravyapradānena svasthānaṃ svargiṇāṃ bhavet ।
upānahau pāduke ca vāhanaṃ yānameva ca ।।

dadāti yo saṃdayitvā? maṇikāñcanacitritam ।
sa vimānaṃ tu dutprāpaṃ prāpno tyeva na saṃśayaḥ ।।

alaṅkṛtaṃ bhadrapīṭhaṃ prayacchan sarvakāmabhāk ।
vinatānandanasthānaṃ dhvajamutpādya darśayan ।।

sāmīpyaṃ sahasā viṣṇoryāti sadyo sa saṃśayaḥ ।
dhvajaṃ ca vādyamutpādya viṣṇusātkurute tu yaḥ ।।

sa divyadundubhi prāyaṃsthānaṃ prāpya virājate ।
dāsīdāsaṃ tathātmāna mātmīyaṃ ca prayacchali ।।

vāsudevāya dāsyena muktiḥ karatalesthitā ।
nṛttabhedairgītabhedais tathā vādyairanekathā ।।

śrotavyairapi dṛśyaiśca devadevasya sannidhau ।
āsīnamupacāraistairye samārādhayantite ।।

pretya divyeṣu lokeṣu pūjyantetairna saṃśayaḥ ।
dīpaṃ prayacchati naro viṣṇorāyatane hi yaḥ ।।

sadakṣiṇasya yajñasya phalaṃ prāpnotyasaṃśayaḥ ।
āhorātramanirvāṇaṃ dīpamāropayennaraḥ ।।

sarvapāpa viśuddhātmā viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।
dinedine japannāma keśaveti samāhitaḥ ।।

sakṛddadātiyovipraḥpradīpaṃ keśavālaye ।
jātismaratvaṃ prajñāṃ ca prākāśyaṃ sarvavantuṣu ।।

avyāhatendriyatvaṃ ca samāpnoti na saṃśayaḥ ।
sarvakālaṃ ca cakṣuṣmān medhāvī dīpado naraḥ ।।

jāyate narakaṃ cāpi tamassaṃjñaṃ na paśyati ।
suvarṇamaṇimuktāḍhyaṃ manojñamatiśobhanam ।।

dīpamālākulaṃ divyaṃ vimānamadhirohati ।
tasmādāyatane viṣṇordadyāddīpaṃ prayatnataḥ ।।

tāṃś cadatvānnahīnaste? na ca tailaviyojanam ।
kurvīta dīpahartāca mūkū'ndho jāyate jaḍaḥ ।।

andhetamasi duṣpāre narake patitān kila ।
vikrośamānānmanujān vakṣyanti yamakiṅkarāḥ ।।

vilāpairala matrevaṃ kiṃvo vilapite phalam ।
tathā pramādibhiḥ pūrvamātmātyantamupekṣitaḥ ।।

purvamālocitaṃ naitatkathamante bhaviṣyati ।
idānīṃ yātanā bhaugāḥkiṃ vilāpaḥ kariṣyati ।।

dehoditāni svalpāni viṣayāścātikarṣakāḥ ।
etatkona vijānāti yena yūyaṃ pramādinaḥ ।।

janturjanmasahasrebhyo hyekasmin mānuṣo yadi ।
tatrāpyativimāḍhatvātkiṃbhogānabhidhāvati ।।

ko atibhāro harernāmni jihvayā parikīrtite ।
varṇite tulyamūletu yadagnirlabhyate sukham ।।

ato adhikarolābhaḥ kovaścitai'bhavattathā ।
yenāyateṣu hasteṣu svātantṣesati dīpakaḥ ।।

mahāphalo viṣṇugṛhe na datto narakāpahāḥ ।
na vo vilapite kiṃ cididānīṃ dṛśyate phalam ।।

asvātantṣe vilapatāṃ svātantṣe tu pramādinām ।
avaśyaṃpātinaḥ prāṇā bhoktājīvopyaharniśam ।।

dattaṃ calabhate bhoktuṃ kāmayanviṣayāṃstadā ।
etatsvātantṣavadbhirvo yuktamāsītparīkṣitum ।।

idānīṃ kiṃ vilāpena sahadhvaṃ yadupāgatam ।
yadyetadanabhīṣṭaṃ vo yadduḥkhaṃ samupasthitam ।।

yadbhūyo api matiḥ pāpe na kartavyā kathaṃ ca na ।
pāpakarmaṇinirvṛtte apyajñānādaghanāśanam ।।

kartavyamapyavicchinnaṃ smaradbhirmadhusūdanam ।
vimānamatividyoti sarvaratnamayaṃ divi ।।

samāpnoti naro datvā pradīpaṃ keśavālaye ।
haviṣāṃ pāyasādīnāṃ haraye ca nivedanāt ।।

sukhaikarasapūrṇatmā rājate viṣṇusannidhau ।
bhakṣyapānīyabhojyānāmanyeṣāmapi dānataḥ ।।

śvetadvīpe tatsamīpe vasanti sukhinassadā ।
bahunātra kimuktena vāsudevārthamādarāt ।।

dadāti vastudānaṃ? yasthsānaṃ prāpnoti cepsitam ।
karmaṇāṃ mārjanādīnāṃ phalabhogādanantaram ।।

karmaśeṣaiḥ punarjanma karmānuguṇayoniṣu ।
utkṛṣṭāsvena bhoktāro labhante sukhinassadā ।।

ārāmāṇāṃ taṭākānāṃ prapāṇāṃ ca pravartanāt ।
viṣṇorālayasāmīpye tatphalaṃ kena varṇyate ।।

supradarśā balavatī citrā dhātuvibhūṣitā ।
upetā sarvabhūtaiśca śreṣṭhā bhūmirihocyate ।।

tasyāḥ kṣetraviśeṣāśca taṭākānāṃ ca bandhanam ।
audakāni ca sarvāṇi pravakṣyāmyanupūrvaśaḥ ।।

taṭākānāṃ ca vakṣyāmi kṛtānāṃ cāpi ye guṇāḥ ।
triṣu lokeṣu sarvatra pūjanīyaḥ pratāpavān ।।

atha vā mitrasadanaṃ maitraṃ mitravivardhanam ।
kīrtisaṃjananaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ taṭākānāṃ niveśanam ।।

dharmasyārthasya kāmasya phalamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।
taṭākaṃ sukṛtaṃ deśekṣetramekaṃ mahāśrayam ।।

caturvidhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ taṭākamupalakṣayet ।
taṭākāni ca sarvāṇi diśanti śriyamuttamām ।।

devā manuṣyā gandharvāḥ pitaro yakṣarākṣasāḥ ।
sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni saṃśrayanti jalāśayam ।।

tasmāttāṃstu pravakṣyāmi taṭāke ye guṇāssmṛtāḥ ।
yā ca tatra phalāvāptirṛṣibhissamudāhṛtā ।।

varṣākāle taṭāke tu salilaṃ yasya tiṣṭhati ।
agnihotraphalaṃ tasya phalamāhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।।

śaratkā le tu salilaṃ taṭāke yasya tiṣṭhati ।
gosahasrasya saṃpretya labhate phalamuttamam ।।

hemantakāle salilaṃ taṭāke yasya tiṣṭhati ।
sa vai bahusuvarṇasya yajñasya labhate phalam ।।

yasya vai śaiśire kāle taṭāke salilaṃ bhavet ।
tasyāgniṣṭomayajñasya bhalamūhurmanīṣiṇaḥ ।।

taṭākaṃ sukṛtaṃ yasya vasantetaṃ mahāśrayam ।
atirātrasya yajñasya phalaṃ sa samupāśnute ।।

nidāghakāle pānīyaṃ taṭāke yasya tiṣṭhati ।
vājimedhapalaṃ tasya phalaṃ vai munayo viduḥ ।।

sa kulaṃ tārayetsarvaṃ yasya khāte jalāśaye ।
gāvaḥ pibanti salilaṃ sādhavaśca narāssadā ।।

taṭāke yasya gāvastu pibanti tṛṣitā jalam ।
mṛgapakṣimanuṣyāśya so aśvamedhaphalaṃ labhet ।।

yatpibanti jalaṃ tatra styāyante viśramantica ।
taṭākadasya tatsarvaṃ pretyānantyāya kalpate ।।

durlabhaṃ salilaṃ ceha viśeṣeṇa paratra vai ।
pānīyasya pradānena prītirbhavati śāśvatī ।।

taṭāke yasya pānīyaṃ pānīyāya jagatpateḥ ।
tasya puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ nālaṃ devāssahānu gāḥ ।।

taṭāke yasya pānīye sāyaṃ prātardvijātayaḥ ।
snātvā kurvanti karmāṇi tasya nākesthitirbhavet ।।

taṭāke yasya devasya snāpanaṃ cādhivāsanam ।
tasya lokā bhavantyeva pāvanāḥ kṣativarjitāḥ ।।

sarvadānairgurutaraṃ sarvadānairviśiṣyate ।
pānīyāvāsadānaṃ tu devasyāgre praśasyate ।।

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa vṛkṣāṇāmavaropaṇam ।
sthānarāṇāṃ ca bhūtānāṃ jātayaṣṣaṭ prakīrtitāḥ ।।

vṛkṣagulpala tāvallyastvakcārāstṛṇajātayaḥ ।
etā jātyastu vṛkṣāṇāṃ teṣāṃ rope guṇāstvime ।।

kīrtiśca mānave loke pretya caiva phalaṃ śubham ।
labhate nāma loke ca pitṛbhiśca mahīyate ।।

devalokagatasyāpi nāmatasya na naśyati ।
atīte anāgate cobhepitṛvaṃ śe anyatastathā ।।

tārayedvṛkṣarūpī ca tasmādvṛkṣāṃśca ropayet ।
tasya putrā bhavantyete pādapā nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

paralokagatassvargaṃ lokāṃścāpnoti so avyayān ।
puṣpaissuragaṇān vṛkṣāḥ phalaiścāpi tathā pitṛn ।।

cāyayā cātithīṃścāpi pūjayanti mahīruhāḥ ।
kinnaroragarakṣāṃsi devagandharvamānavāḥ ।।

tathā ṛṣigaṇāścaiva saṃśrayanti mahīruhān ।
puṣpitāḥ phalavantaśca tarpayantīha mānavān ।।

vṛkṣadaṃ putravadvṛkṣāstārayanti paratra tu ।
patraṃ phalaṃ vā puṣpaṃ vā yasyārāme avaropite ।।

acyutasya padaṃ prāptaṃ lokāstasyācyutā dhruvam ।
patraiḥphalair vāpuṣpairvā prīyate bhagavān hariḥ ।।

tasmāttaṭāre tadvṛkṣā ropyāśśreyorthinā sadā ।
putravatparipālyāśca putrāstedharmatassmṛtāḥ ।।

taṭākakṛdvṛkṣaropī iṣṭayajñaśca yo naraḥ ।
ete svarge mahīyante ye cānye satyavādinaḥ ।।

tasmāttaṭākān kurvīta ārāmāṃścaiva ropayet ।
yajecca vividhairyajñaissatyaṃ ca satataṃ vadet ।।

gobhūhiraṇyadānāni kṛtvācāryāya viṣṇave ।
arcakāya viśeṣeṇa svargatassukhamedhate ।।

atidānaṃ tu sarveṣāṃ bhūmidānamihocyate ।
acalā hyakṣayo bhūmissarvān kāmān prayacchati ।।

yastudadyādbhūmidānaṃ devanāmnārcakāyahi ।
tasyaihikaṃ bhavetpuṇyaṃ tathā pāratrikaṃ bahu ।।

yastu dadyātsvanāmnaiva pūjakāya vasuṃdharām ।
tasya kāmāḥ prarohanti sarvamaihikamaśnute ।।

devakāryāya vaidadyādyo devāya vasundharām ।
devanāmnaiva tasya syātkevalāmuṣmikaṃ phalam ।।

brahmārpaṇadhiyā yastu guptaṃ dāsyati kiṃ cana ।
devāya devakāryāya brāhmaṇāyādhikāriṇe ।।

yāvajjīvati taddānaṃ svargetasya sthitirbhavet ।
yaṃ yaṃ kāmaṃ tu manasi kṛtvā yadyacca yor'payet ।।

taṃ tameva phalaṃ labdhvākartāsammodate ciram ।
kimalabhyaṃ bhagavati prasanne śrīniketane ।।

ācāryāyārpitā bhūmiratyantaphaladāyinī ।
tator'cakārpitā dadyādanantaṃ phalamucyate ।।

padārthināmathānveṣāṃ tathānyavibhavasya ca ।
sarvameva bhaveddattaṃ vasudhāṃ yaḥ prayacchati ।।

phālakṛṣṭāṃ mahīṃ dadyātsabījāṃ sasyamālinīm ।
yāvatsūryakarā loke tāvatsvarge mahīyate ।।

phālakṛṣṭāṃ mahīṃ dadyātsabījāṃ sasyamālinīm ।
yāvatsūryakarā loke tāvatsvarge mahīyate ।।

yaścāpi kurute pāpaṃ puruṣovṛttikarśitaḥ ।
api gokarṇamātreṇa bhūmidānena śuddhyati ।।

saptahastena vā samyaktriṃśaddaṇḍena vardhanam ।
sa śatānyeva gokarṇamiti vedavido vidaḥ ।।

jitendrayāya guṇine pūjakāya tapasvine ।
dadyānmahīṃ bhadettasya phalamakṣayamacyutam ।।

yathāpsu patitassadyastailabinduḥ prarohati ।
evaṃ bhūmikṛtaṃ dānaṃ sasye sasye prarohati ।।

yathā bījāni rohanti prakīrṇāni mahītale ।
evaṃ kāmāḥprarohanti bhūmidānasamārjitāḥ ।।

yathā gaurbharate vatsaṃ kṣīriṇī kṣīramutsṛjet ।
evaṃ dattāciraṃ kālaṃ bhūmirbharati bhūmidam ।।

ikṣubhissatatāṃ bhūmiṃ yavagodhūmaśādvalaiḥ ।
yo dadāti naraśreṣṭhassa na pracyavate divaḥ ।।

śubhaṃ bhadrāsanaṃ chatraṃ varāśca varayoṣitaḥ ।
bhūmidānasya cihnāni phalametanna saṃśayaḥ ।।

āditya vasavo viṣṇurbrahmā somo hutāśanaḥ ।
śūlapāṇiśca bhagavānabhinandanti bhūmidam ।।

sauvarṇachatrahakmyāṇi vasordhārāśca kāmadāḥ ।
gandharvāpsaraso yatra tatra tiṣṭhanti bhūmidāḥ ।।

iyameva purā bhūmiḥ pālitā bahubhignṛpaiḥ ।
anyaiśca bahubhirdattā rājabhissatyasaṃgaraiḥ ।।

yasya yasya yadā bhūmi stasya tasya tadā phalam ।
bhūmiṃ yaḥ pratigṛhṇāti yaśca bhūmiṃ prayacchati ।।

tāvubhau puṇyakarmāṇau niyatau svargagāminau ।
dānapālanayormadhye dānācchreyo anupālanam ।।

dānātsvargamavāpnoti pālanādacyutaṃ padam ।
svadattāddviguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ paradattānupālanam ।।

bhūmidassvargamāruhya śāsvatīredhate samāḥ ।
punaśca janma saṃpāpya bhavedbhūmi patirdhruvam ।।

yathā bhūmissadā devī dātāraṃ kurute patim ।
evaṃ sadakṣiṇā dattākurute gaurjanādhipam ।।

api pāpakṛtaṃ prāpya pratigṛhṇāti bhūmidam ।
mahīṃ dadatpavitrassyātpuṇyā ca jagatī yataḥ ।।

nāmaiva priyadatteti guhyāmetatsanātanam ।
tadasyāssatataṃ prītyaikīrtanīyā prayacchatā ।।

tapoyajñāśritaṃ śīlamalobhassatyavāditā ।
gurudaivatapūjā ca nātikrāmati bhūmidam ।।

bharturniśśreyase yuktā styaktātmādoraṇe hatāḥ ।
brahmalokagatāssanto nātikrāmantibhūmidam ।।

yathā janitrī kṣīreṇa puṣṇāti svasutaṃ mudā ।
evaṃ sarvaguṇairbhūmirdātāramanupuṣyati ।।

agniṣṭomādibhiryajñairiṣṭvā vipuladakṣiṇaiḥ ।
na tatphalamavāpnoti yaddatvā vasudhāṃ punaḥ ।।

mṛtyorhi kiṅkarā daṇḍā hyagnitāpāssudāruṇāḥ ।
ghorāśca vāruṇāḥ pāśā nopasarpanti bhūmidam ।।

pītaraḥ pitṛlokasthā devaloke divaukasaḥ ।
santarpayanti dātāraṃ bhūmeḥ prabhavatāṃnaraḥ ।।

ādityā iva dīpyante tejasā di mānavāḥ ।
ye prayacchanti vasudhāṃ haraye lokasākṣiṇe ।।

kṛśāya kṛśabhṛtyāya vṛttiṃ kṣīṇāya sīdate ।
devāgrer'pyatu viprāya suśrīrbhavati mānavaḥ ।।

āsphoṭayanti pitaraḥ pranṛtya ni pitāmahāḥ ।
bhūmido naḥ kule jātassavassantārayiṣyati ।।

sa naḥ kulasya puruṣassano bandhussano guruḥ ।
sa dātā sa ca vikrānto yo dadāti vasuṃdharām ।।

lokāṃstu sṛjatā pūrvaṃ gāvassṛṣṭāssvayaṃbhuvā ।
vṛddhyarthaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ tasmāttā mātarassmṛtāḥ ।।

tāstudatvā saurabheyīssvargeloke mahīyate ।
dhenuṃ datvā suvratāṃ ca sopadhānāṃ payasvinīm ।।

savatsāṃ kapilāṃ divyāmācāryāyārcakāya ca ।
devadevasya tuṣṭyarthaṃ devāya brāhmaṇāya vā ।।

na tasya śakyate vaktuṃ phalaṃ varṣaśatairapi ।
yāvanti dhenvālomāni vatsāyāśca viśeṣataḥ ।।

tāvadvarṣa sahasrāṇi kāmān duhyeta sā varā ।
prayacchate yaḥkapilāṃ savatsāṃ kāṃsyajohanām ।।

svarṇaśruṅgīṃ raupyakhurāṃ taistairdravyaguṇaiḥ punaḥ ।
sā gauḥ kāmadughā bhūtvā dātāramupasarpati ।।

gosahasraṃ tu yo dadyātsarvaratnairalaṅkṛtam ।
parāṃ vṛddhiṃśriyaṃ prāpya svargaloke mahīyate ।।

daśa cobhayataḥpretya mātā mahapitāmahāḥ ।
gacchetsukṛtināṃ lokān gāvo datvā yathāvidhi ।।

dāyādyalabdhairyogādyairgāvassampādya yodadet ।
tasyāpi cākṣayā lokā bhavantīha paratra ca ।।

yo vā dyūte dhanaṃ jitvāgāvaḥkrītvā prayacchati ।
sa gacchedvirajān lokān gopradānaphalārjitān ।।

pratigṛhyatu yo dadyādgāvaśśuddhena cetasā ।
sa gatvā durlabhaṃ sthānamamaraissaha modate ।।

yaścātmavikrayaṃ kṛtvā gāvo dadyādyadhāvidhi ।
sa gatvā virajān lokān sukhaṃ vasati devavat ।।

saṃgrāme yastanuṃ tyaktvā tvaktvā gāvaḥprayacchati ।
dehavikraya mūlyāstā śśāśvatāḥ kāmadohanāḥ ।।

jīrṇāṃ caivopabhukrāñca jaradgāṃ śīlavarjitām, ।
tamaḥ praviśate datvā dvijaṃ kleśena yojayet ।।

dānayogyā bhavesnaiva kṛśā duṣṭā palāyinī ।
yuñjyātlkeśaistu yo vipraṃ datvaināṃ tadvṛdhā bhavet ।।

yuvānaṃ balinaṃ śyāmaṃ halena saha yūthapam ।
gopatiṃ haraye dadyādbhūriśruṅgamalaṅkṛtam ।।

brāhmaṇānāṃ gavāṃ caiva kulamekaṃ dvidhā kṛtam ।
ekatra mantrā stiṣṭhanti havirekatra tiṣṭhati ।।

upagamya tu yo dadyādgāvaśśuddhena cetasā ।
yāvantitāsāṃ romāṇi tāvatsvarge mahīyate ।।

pravakṣyāmi gavāṃlokā yādṛśāyatra saṃsthitāḥ ।
manojñā ramaṇīyāśca sarvakāmaduhāssadā ।।

puṇyāḥpāpaharāśceva gavāṃ lokā na saṃśayaḥ ।
atyantasukhinastatra sarvapāpavivarjitāḥ ।।

pramodante mahāsthsāne narā vigatakalmaṣāḥ ।
tulyaprabhāvā devaiste modante psarasāṃ gaṇaiḥ ।।

gandharvairupagīyante gośaraṇyā na saṃśayaḥ ।
brāhmaṇāssādhuvṛttāśca dayāvanto anukaṃpakāḥ ।।

ghṛṇinaśśubhakartāro modantedaivataissaha ।
yathaiva salile matsyassalilena sahoṣya te ।।

gobhiḥ pāpakṛtaṃ karma dṛḍhameva vyapohyate ।
mātarassarvabhūtānāṃ prajānāṃ rakṣaṇe kṛtāḥ ।।

brahmāṇā lokasāreṇa gāvaḥpāpabhayāpahāḥ ।
tānu dattāsu loke asmin kiṃ na dattaṃ bhavediha ।।

deveśāya viśeṣeṇa tatkriyāya tathā punaḥ ।
pratipādyāssadā gāno bhūtiṃ sbhārāmabhīpsubhiḥ ।।

suvarṇaṃ paramaṃ dānaṃ suvarṇaṃ dakṣiṇā parā ।
etatpavitraṃ paramametatsvastyayanaṃ mahat ।।

daśapūrvān parān vaṃśyānātmānaṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।
apipāpaśataṃ kṛtvā dattaṃ vipriṣu tārayet ।।

suvarṇaṃ ye prayacchanti narāśśuddheva cetasā ।
devatāste prayacchanti samastamiti naśśrutam ।।

agnirhi devatāssarvāssuvarṇaṃ ca hutāśanaḥ ।
tasmātsuvarṇaṃ dadatā dattāssarvāśca devatāḥ ।।

agnyabhāve ca kurvanti vahnisthāne ca kāñcanam ।
sarvadevapramāṇajñā vedaśrutinidarśanāt ।।

yastvenaṃ jvalayedagnimādityodayanaṃ prati ।
dadyādvai devamuddiśya sarvānkāmānavāpnuyāt ।।

suvarṇadassarvaloke kāmāniṣṭānavāpnute ।
virajāṃbarasaṃvītaḥ pariyāti tatastataḥ ।।

vimānenārkavarṇena bhāsvareṇa virājatā ।
apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇo bhāsvarastena tejasā ।।

haṃsabarhiṇayuktena kāmagena narottamaḥ ।
divyagandhavahassvarge parigacchannitastataḥ ।।

tasmātsvaśaktyā dātavyaṃ kāñcanaṃ mānavairbhuvi ।
vimānenārkavarṇena sa yāti svargamuttamam ।।

na hyataḥ paramaṃ loke sadyaḥ pāpavināśanam ।
brahmakośasya śuddhasya suvarṇaṃ yaḥ prayacchati ।।

bahūnyabdasahasrāṇi svargeloke mahīyate ।
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ svarṇadānaphalaṃ mayā ।।

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa phalamannasya dāpanāt ।
viṣṇave ca śriyai bhūmyai sarvadevebhya eva ca ।।

tanni vedita śeṣasya dānāccārthibhya ādarāt ।
na śakyate phalaṃ tasya vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi ।।

tathāpi gīyate yattu vistārāt paramarṣibhiḥ ।
saṃkṣepataḥ pravakṣyāmi annadānārjitaṃ phalam ।।

prasādamamṛtaṃ brūyādannaṃ devaniveditam ।
tīrthaṃ cāmṛtamityeva devapādodakaṃ vadet ।।

annameva praśaṃsanti devā ṛṣigaṇāstathā ।
lokatantraṃ hi saṃjñāśca sarvamanne pratiṣṭhitam ।।

annena sadṛśaṃ dānaṃ na bhūto na bhaviṣyati ।
tasmādannaṃ viśeṣeṇa dātumicchanti mānavāḥ ।।

annamūrjaskaraṃ loke prāṇāścānne pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।
annena dhāryate sarvaṃ viśvaṃ jagadidaṃ mahat ।।

annādgṛhasthā lokesmin bhikṣavastāpasāstathā ।
annādbhavanti vai prāṇāḥ pratyakṣaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

kuṭuṃbaṃ pīḍayitvā tu brāhmaṇāya mahātmane ।
dātavyaṃ bhikṣave cānnamātmano bhūtimicchatā ।।

brāhmaṇāyābhirūpāya yo dadyādannamarthine ।
vidadhāti nidhiṃ śreṣṭhaṃ pāralaukikamātmanaḥ ।।

śrāntamadhvani vartantaṃ vṛddhamarhamupasthitam ।
arcayedbhūtimanvicchan gṛhastho gṛhamāgatam ।।

krodhamutpatitaṃ hitvā suśīlo vītamatsaraḥ ।
annadaḥ prāpnute bhū yo bhuvi ceha ca yatsukham ।।

nāvamanyedabhigataṃ na praṇudyātkathaṃ cana ।
api śvapāke śuni vā na dānaṃ vipraṇaśyati ।।

yo dadyādaparikliṣṭamanna madhvani vartate ।
śāntāyādṛṣṭapūrvāya samahaddharmamāpnuyāt ।।

pitṝn devānṛṣīnviprānatithīṃśca viśeṣataḥ ।
yo naraḥprīṇayatyannaistasya puṇyaphalaṃ mahat ।।

kṛtvātipātakaṃ karmayo dadyādanna marthine ।
brāhmaṇāya viśeṣeṇa na sa pāpena muhyate ।।

brāhmaṇeṣvakṣayaṃ nāmnāṃ śūdre mahatbhalam ।
annadāmapi śūdre ca brāhmaṇasya viśiṣyate ।।

na pṛcchedgotracaraṇaṃ svādhyāyaṃ deśamena ca ।
bhikṣito brāhmaṇeneha dadyādannaṃ prayācitaḥ ।।

annadasyānnavṛkṣāśca sarvakāmaphalapradāḥ ।
bhavanti ceha nāmutranṛpaternātrasaṃśayaḥ ।।

āśaṃsate hi pitarassuvṛṣṭimiva karṣakāḥ ।
asmākamapi putro vā pautro vānnaṃ pradāsyati ।।

brāhmaṇohi mahadbhūtaṃ svayaṃ dehīti yācate ।
akāmovā sakāmo vā datvā puṇyamavāpnuyāt ।।

brāhmaṇassarvabhūtānāmatidhiḥ prasṛtāgrabhuk ।
viprā yamadhigacchanti bhikṣamāṇā gṛhaṃ sadā ।।

satkṛtācca nivartante tadatīva pravarthate ।
mahābhoge kule pretya janma cāpnoti nityaśaḥ ।।

datvātvannaṃ naro loke yathāsthānamanuttamam ।
nityaṃ mṛṣṭānnadāyī tu svarge vasati satkṛtaḥ ।।

annaṃ prāṇā narāṇāṃhi sarvamanne pratiṣṭhitam ।
annadaḥ paśumān putrī dhanavān bhogavānapi ।।

prāṇavāṃścāpi bhavati rūpavāṃśca tathā bhavet ।
annadaḥprāṇado loke sarvadaḥ procyate tu saḥ ।।

annaṃ hidatvātithaye brāhmaṇāya yathāvidhi ।
pradātā sukhamāpnoti daivataiścāpi pūjyate ।।

brāhmaṇo hi mahadbhūtaṃ kṣetrabhūtamihocyate ।
upyate yatra tadbījaṃ taddhi puṇyaphalaṃ mahat ।।

pratyakṣaprītijananaṃ bhokturdāturbhavatyuta ।
sarvāṇyanyāni dānāni parokṣaphalavantyuta ।।

annāddhi prasavaṃ yānti ratirannāddhi jāyate ।
dhakmārthāvannato vidyāt roganāśastathānnataḥ ।।

annaṃ hyadbhutamityāha purā kalpe prajāpatiḥ ।
annaṃ bhuvaṃ divaṃ khaṃ ca sarvamanne pratiṣṭhitam ।।

anna praṇāśe bhidyante śarīre pañca dhātavaḥ ।
balaṃ balavato apīha praṇaśyatyannahānitaḥ ।।

āvāhāśca vivāhāśca yajñāścānnakṛte tathā ।
nivartante viśeṣeṇa brahma cātra pradīyate ।।

annatassarvametaddhi yatkiñcit sthāṇu jaṅgamam ।
triṣulokeṣu dharmārthamannaṃ deyaṃ tato budhaiḥ ।।

annadasya manuṣyasya balamojo yaśāṃsi ca ।
āyuśca vardhate tadvatteṣu lokeṣu niścitam ।।

meghādūrdhvaṃ sannidhatteprāṇānāṃ pavanaḥ patiḥ ।
yacca meghagataṃ vāri śakro varṣati harṣitaḥ ।।

ādatte ca rasān bhaumān ādityassvagabhastibhiḥ ।
vāyurādityataptāṃśca rasān devaḥpravarṣati ।।

tadyathā meghato vāri patitaṃ bhavati kṣitau ।
tadā vasumatī devī snigdhā bhavati bhāvitā ।।

tatassasyāni rohanti yena vartayate jagat ।
māṃsamedo asthiśukrāṇāṃ prādurbhāvastataḥ punaḥ ।।

saṃbhavanti tataśśukrātprāṇinaḥ pṛdhivītale ।
agniṣṭomau hi tacchrakraṃ sṛjataḥ puṣyataśca ha ।।

evamannāddhi sūryaśca pavanaśśukramevaca ।
eka eva smṛto rāśistato bhūtāni jaṅgire ।।

prāṇān dadāti bhūtānāṃ tejaśca satataprabham ।
gṛhamabhyāgatāyātha yo dadyādannamarthine ।।

annadānāddhi yelokāstāṃśruṇudhvaṃ samāhitāḥ ।
bhavanāni prakāśante divi teṣāṃ mahātmanām ।।

tārāsaṃsthānarūpāṇi nānā staṃbhānvitāni ca ।
candramaṇḍalaśubhrāṇi kiṅkiṇījālavanti ca ।।

taruṇādityavarṇāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇica ।
anekaśatabhaumāni sāṃtarjalacarāṇi ca ।।

vaiḍūryārkaprakāśāni raukmarūpyamayāni ca ।
sarvakāmaphalāścāpi vṛkṣā bhavanasaṃsthitāḥ ।।

vāpyo vīthyaḥ sabhāḥ kūpādīrghi kāścaiva sarvaśaḥ ।
ghoṣavantyatha yānāni muktānyatha sahasraśaḥ ।।

bhakṣyabhojyamayāśśailā vāsāṃsyābharaṇāni ca ।
kṣīraṃ sravanti saritastathā caivānna parvatāḥ ।।

prāsādāḥ pāṇḍurābhrābhāśśayyāśca kanakojjvalāḥ ।
tānyannadāḥ prapadyante tasmādannaṃ dadetsadā ।।

dadyādadyātsadaivānnaṃ viṣṇave viniveditam ।
haviḥpātrādi sauvarṇaṃ rājataṃ tāmrameva vā ।।

kāṃsyaṃ vāpyatha yo dadyādarghya pātrādikānapi ।
kalaśān karakān kuṃbhānanyāṃścaiva paricchadān ।।

śaktilobhamakṛtvaiva tasya puṇyaphalaṃ mahat ।
sauvarṇānyevayo dadyātsārūpyaṃ labhate phalam ।।

rājatānyatha yodadyātsāmīpyaṃ phalamāpnuyāt ।
dadyāttāmrāṇi kāṃsyāni sārokyaṃ padameti saḥ ।।

dhvacānvicitrān yo dadyānnānāvarṇa samāyutān ।
sarveṣāmuttamo bhūtvā kulaketurbhaviṣyati ।।

śvetaṃ vitānaṃ raktaṃ vā kṛṣṇaṃ pītaṃ ca śyāmalam ।
dukūlenātha paṭṭena tantunānyena vā kṛtam ।।

yo dadyāddevadevasya sa gacchedvaiṣṇavaṃ padam ।
sopadhānāṃ satalpāṃ ca khaṭvāṃ dadyācca yohareḥ ।।

kuberalokamāsādya tatra sammodate ciram ।
ātapatraṃ tathā haimaṃ muktādāmavibhūṣitam ।।

haimadaṇḍayutaṃ dadyādindralokaṃ sa gacchati ।
rājyakāmī tu rājā syātsārvabhaumo api jāyate ।।

mayūracchatradānāttu vāruṇaṃ lokamāpnuyāt ।
cāmaraṃ hemadaṇḍaṃ ca vyajanaṃ ratnabhūṣitam ।।

kevalaṃ hemadaṇḍaṃ vā bhaktyā śaktyā ca saṃyutam ।
arpayeddharaye yastu devaloke mahīyate ।।

mayūravyajanaṃ tadvadrukmadaṇḍaṃ ca śaktitaḥ ।
bhaktyaiva yo harerdadyādvāyuloke mahīyate ।।

vimānaṃ haivasaṃcchannaṃ viṣṇoryaḥ kārayennaraḥ ।
aśakyaṃ tatphalaṃ vaktuṃ sarvairapi surāsuraiḥ ।।

sauvarmaṃ viṣṇurūpantu yo bhaktyaiva tu kārayet ।
tasyāpi yatphalaṃ sarvamanantamiti naśśrutam ।।

maṇḍapaṃ vā prapāṃ vātha ratnamuktopaśobhitam ।
hemalaṃba? samāyuktaṃ haimastaṃbhapariṣkṛtam ।।

kalpayedviṣṇusālokyaṃ prāpnotyamaradurlabham ।
haimaṃ siṃhāsanaṃ śreṣṭhaṃ yo bhaktyaivār'payeddhareḥ ।।

siṃhāsanaṃ samāsthāya māhendrīṃ saṃpadaṃ vrajet ।
haimīryāśśibikāścaiva raṅgādīnyaśca kārayet ।।

haimaṃ yānaṃ tathāruhya viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।
aśaktodāravān vātharaṅgādīn śibikāstathā ।।

siṃhāsanaṃ vā yo dadyātsomalokaṃ sa gacchati ।
yaśca kāṃsyamayīṃ ghaṇṭāṃhṛdyadhvaniyutāṃ dadet ।।

hṛdyavāksusvaro hṛdyo vāgmī sa tu bhavennaraḥ ।
śaṅkhabheryādidānena śakraloke sa pūjyate ।।

nṛttageyādibhirvādyairghoṣaṇaṃ kārayettu yaḥ ।
nartayedapsarobhirvā gāndharvaṃ lokamāpnuyāt ।।

vīṇāveṇuvinādaiśca śaktyā yaḥ pūjayeddharim ।
bhuktvātramahadaiśvaryaṃ vaiṣṇavaṃ padamāpnuyāt ।।

yadyaddravyaṃ mudā yukto dadyāttu haraye naraḥ ।
tadagre pūjakebhyaśca gurave ca viśeṣataḥ ।।

tatprītyai cetarebhyaśca brāhmaṇebhyo vidhānataḥ ।
samṛddhiṃ tasya tasyaiva dravyasyāpnotyasaṃśayam ।।

yaṃ kāmayitvā dadyādyattatsarvaṃ sa labhennaraḥ ।
yadyatkarma tadarthaṃ syātparicaryā ca tasya yā ।।

tasyopacāraṃ yatkarma karoti śraddhayā tu yaḥ ।
sarvayajñaphalaṃ prāpya nāmīpyaṃ padamāpnu yāt ।।

tasmādatra pratiṣṭhāpya devadevasya mandiram ।
śaktilobhamakṛtvaiva vibhavānāñcabhaktitaḥ ।।

bahudhā bahulāṃ vṛttiṃ kalpayeccettaduttamam ।
athār'cane phalaṃ vakṣye viśeṣeṇa madhudviṣaḥ ।।

bhaktyāpradakṣiṇaṃ kurvannityaṃ viṣṇvālaye naraḥ ।
sāyaṃ prātaśca deveśaṃ namasyannatha cintayan ।।

yaḥ pramāmaṃ muhuḥ kuryātsa tu yajñaphalaṃ labhet ।
upacāraviśeṣāṇādvakṣyate phalam ।।

dhyānamāvāhanaṃ kṛtvā sarvān kāmānavāpnuyāt ।
aṣṭāṅgayogamārgeṇa manasā bhāvayan harim ।।

saṃcintya manasā pūrvaṃ pūtakāyo mahāmanāḥ ।
yaḥ kuryātpūjanaṃ viṣṇostatra devo vaseddhruvam ।।

arcakasya tapoyogātpūjāyā ścātiśāyanāt ।
ābhirūpyācca biṃbasya sannidheḥ procyate hareḥ ।।

āsanaṃ haraye datvā pratiṣṭhāṃ labhate ciram ।
svāgatenānumānena yaḥ pūjayati mādhavam ।।

sarvairanumato bhūtvā svāgataṃ so abhipadyate ।
pādyamācamanīyaṃ ca samarpya haraye naraḥ ।।

bāhyamābhyantaraṃ yattu pāpaṃ tena vimucyate ।
nityaṃ puṣpāṇi puṇyāni bhaktyā yastu samarcayet ।।

sūryakoṭinibhaṃ divyaṃ vimānamadhiruhyasaḥ ।
viṣṇulokaṃ gatassatyaṃ viṣṇuvanmodate ciram ।।

deveśaṃ puṣpamālādyairalaṅkuryācca yo budhaḥ ।
tasyānantaphalaṃ prokta mananto bhagavān hariḥ ।।

caṃpakāśokapunnāga jātīmalayapaṅkajam ।
samarpya devadevāya śubhānāmāśrayo bhavet ।।

damanośīralāmajjā ketakyutpalamarpayet ।
maṅgalaṃ tasya niśchidraṃ bhavedeva na saṃśayaḥ ।।

tulasīmarpayedvidvān pādayorbhaktito hareḥ ।
sa cāna ntaphalaṃ prāpya modate viṣṇusannedhau ।।

sugandhipuṣpadānena sugandhirjāyate naraḥ ।
bahupuṣpapradānena bahudhā tuṣyate?hariḥ ।।

bahujātisumānāṃ ca dānena prīyate sa vai ।
pādayorarpaṇādviṣṇoḥ puṣpāṇāṃ saṃcayaṃ sakṛt ।।

padepade cāśvamedhaphalaṃ prāpnotyasaṃśayam ।
tulasīṃ mūrthni devasya samarpya madhuvidviṣaḥ ।।

naraḥ pāpādvimucyeta karmaṇā nopalipyate ।
sarvāṅgeṣvarpayan puṣpaṃ sarvagasya naro hareḥ ।।

sarvadā sarvalokeṣu kāmacoro bhaviṣyati ।
alaṅkṛtya phalairdevaṃ puṣpārpaṇaphalaṃ labhet ।।

saṃgandhacandanadravyaṃ karpūrādiyutaṃ tathā ।
yathārhamarpayedaṅgeślakṣṇaṃ sarvāṅgasundaram ।।

sa naro viṣṇusālokyaṃ prayātyamaradurlabham ।
svayamevāhṛtaiḥ puṣpaiḥ pūjayedyastu mādhavam ।।

sa sarvān samavāpnoti puṣpārpaṇaphalādikān ।
sarveṣāmapi puṣpāṇāṃ tulasī prītidā hareḥ ।।

tulasīdalamādāya yatra gacchati pūjakaḥ ।
anugacchati taṃ devo yathā gorvatsalā bhṛśam ।।

pratyahaṃ pūjayedyastu tulasyā garuḍadhvajam ।
janmamṛtyujarāvyādhimukto muktimavāpnuyāt ।।

maṇikāñcanapuṣpāṇi muktāvaidūryakāni ca ।
tulasīdaladānasya kalāṃ nār'hanti ṣoḍaśīm ।।

sumañjarīdalairyuktaiḥ komalaistulasīdalaiḥ ।
ye kurvanti hareḥ pūjāṃ te kṛtārthāḥ kalau yuge ।।

śuṣkaṃ paryuṣitaṃ vār'draṃ kāṣṭhaṃ vā tulasīdalam ।
arcane vāsudevasya lakṣakoṭiguṇaṃ bhavet ।।

tulasīgrahaṇaṃ śastaṃ viṣṇorarcanahetave ।
varjyaṃ paryuṣitaṃ puṣpaṃ na varjyaṃ tulasīdalam ।।

varjyaṃ paryuṣitaṃ toyaṃ na varjyaṃ jāhnavījalam ।
anyatparyuṣitaṃ varjyaṃ na varjyaṃ padmapuṣpakam ।।

śuṣkaiḥ paryuṣitairvāpi kāṣṭhamūlamṛdādibhiḥ ।
arcanādvāsudevasya mukto bhavati pūruṣaḥ ।।

puṣkarādyāni tīrthāni gaṅgādyāssaritastathā ।
devā divisthitā ye vaitiṣṭhanti tulasīdale ।।

tāvadgarjanti puṣpāṇi mālatyādīni garvataḥ ।
yāvanna prāpyate puṇyā tulasī viṣṇuvallabhā ।।

sakṛdabhyarcya govindaṃ tulasyā caiva mānavaḥ ।
muktibhāgī nirātaṅkaṃ kṛṣṇasyānucaro bhavet ।।

nākṣatairarcayedviṣṇuṃ na śaṃbhuṃ śaṅkhavāriṇā ।
nārcayeddūrvayā durgāṃ na tulasyā surāntaram ।।

dalālābhe tulasyāstu patrairārādhayeddharim ।
patrālābhe śiphābhirvā śiphābhāve śiphālavaiḥ ।।

lavālābhe mṛdā tatra bhaktimānarcayeddharim ।
harerabhyarcanāyāṃ ca tulasī sādhanaṃ param ।।

alābhe tulasī ca tannāmagrahaṇaṃ param ।
bhagavānaravindākṣassantuṣyati sahasradhā ।।

na padmairnāpi kalhārairna hemakusumairapi ।
tathā tuṣyati govindo yathaina tulasīdalaiḥ ।।

saṃgṛhya tulasīṃ bhaktyā sarvāniṣṭa ।
tulasyaiva hareḥ pūjāṃ ye kurvanti sadā bhuvi ।।

tasmāttulasyā sadṛśaṃ sa ca bhūtaṃ na bhāvi ca ।
tulasīkānanāmodavāpitā yatra mārutāḥ ।।

na tatra dharaṇībhāge caranti yamakiṅkarāḥ ।
"tulasī tulasī''tyevaṃ nāmānyāvartayantiye ।।

te viṣṇulokamāsādya paśyanti madhusūdanam ।
darśanācchravaṇātsvarśātsmaraṇātkīrtanādapi ।।

punāti tulasī puṇyā daśapūrvān daśāvarān ।
tulasīkānanaṃ yatra yatra vā harikīrtanam ।।

tatraivāste hariśśrīmān śaṅkhacakragadāyudhaḥ ।
yaḥ pūjayetphalairviṣṇuṃ nupakvairamṛtopamaiḥ ।।

puṇyavṛkṣasamudbhūtaistatphalaṃ kena varṇyate ।
candanāgurukoṣṭhvādyairbhūpamāghrāpayeccayaḥ ।।

sūryalokaṃ sa gatvaiva yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam ।
ghṛtena kāpilenaiva dṛḍhavartiyutaṃ tu yaḥ ।।

darśayeddevadevasya dīpaṃ dṛṣṭimanoharam ।
so andhaṃ naiva praviśati narakaṃ narapuṅgavaḥ ।।

yastu tailena saṃdīptaṃ darśayeddīpamujjvalam ।
vimānamatividyoti yātyāruhya tamaḥparam ।।

karbūradīpaṃ yo bhaktyā darśayeddharaye naraḥ ।
tasya pāpāni naśyanti nirlepassa bhaviṣyati ।।

vidhinār'ghyaṃ harerdadyādaṣṭhāṅgaṃ bhaktito naraḥ ।
candralokaṃ sa gatvaiva yāti viṣṇoḥ paraṃ padam ।।

sugandhi śubhamutpūtaṃ snānatoyaṃ ca yo dadet ।
deveśasya viśeṣaṇa sa bhavedvītakalmaṣaḥ ।।

tataśca vāruṇaṃ lokaṃ prāpya tatraiva modate ।
plotavastrottarīyāṇi viśuddhāni mṛdūni ca ।।

devadevasya datvā tu saumyaṃ lokamavāpnuyāt ।
kārpāsamatha ca kṣaumaṃ kauśeyaṃ rāṅkavaṃ tathā ।।

yathāśakti samarpyaiva phalaṃ cānantamaśnute ।
kārpāsādrāṅgavaṃ tasmātkau śeyaṃ kṣaumamityapi ।।

praśastaṃ kathitaṃ vastraṃ yathā śaktyanurūpataḥ ।
sauvarṇābharaṇānyatra muktāmaṇikṛtāni vā ।।

arpayeddevadevasya bhavedbhūmipatissa hi ।
jāṃbūnadaṃ śātakuṃbhaṃ hāṭakaṃ vaiṇavaṃ tathā ।।

śruṅgī ca śuktijaṃ caiva jātarūpamataḥ param ।
rasaviddhaṃ tathā proktamākarodgatamityapi ।।

proktaṃ bahuvidhaṃ hema pūrvātpūrvātparaṃ param ।
pratyuptāni viśeṣeṇa ratnairnāvāvidhairhareḥ ।।

bhūṣaṇānyarpayedbhaktyā mitrāṇyasya navagrahāḥ ।
rājaśriyaṃ ca bhuktvā nte viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।

upavītaṃ tu yo dadyātsauvarṇaistantubhiḥ kṛtām ।
dvijottamassyādvijñānī brahmalokamavāpnuyāt ।।

sālagrāmaiśca bahubhirnirmitāṃ mālikāṃ tu yaḥ ।
arpayeddevadevasya sa viṣṇoryāti sannidhim ।।

lakṣmīḥ priyatamā viṣṇossā hi nityānapāyinī ।
svasaṃkālpānuviddhā ca śaktissarvātmikā parā ।।

prakṛtermūlabhūtā ca svāminī jagatāṃ satām ।
lakṣmīpratikṛtiṃ kṛtvā maṇimuktādibhirmunā ।।

ābadhya mālikāyāṃ yo deveśāya samarpayet ।
tasya prasannau jāyete daṃpatī jagataḥ patī ।।

mātrāṃ ca devadesya datvā haste viśeṣataḥ ।
sarvān kāmānavāpnoti carāṃśastarpito hareḥ ।।

madhuparkaṃ harerdadyādbhaktyā prītikaraṃ hareḥ ।
virajāṃ' barasaṃvītaśśaśāṅkadhavalo mudā ।।

candralokādhipo bhūtvā yāyādviṣṇupadaṃ mahat ।
havirni vedya devasya pratiṣṭhāphalamaśnute ।।

prabhūtaṃ vinivedyaiva jīrṇoddhāraphalaṃ tathā ।
pāyasaṃ vinidedyaiva harerbhaktyā viśeṣataḥ ।।

payohradaiśca pitarastṛptimāyānti tasyatu ।
kṛsaraṃ vinivedyaiva devasya mudito naraḥ ।।

akṣayaṃ pratipadyeta svagṛhe annaṃ ciraṃ ciram ।
gaulyaṃ nivedya devasya prāpnoti guḍaparvatān ।।

mudgānnasya pradānena mudgarāśiṃ samāpnuyāt ।
yavodanasya donena nīrogo bhavati dhruvam ।।

śuddhānnasya pradānena triśuddhā bhavati prajā ।
apūpādipradānena manasvī jāyate naraḥ ।।

upadaṃśādidānena nopadaṃśo bhaviṣyati? ।
sugandhi svādu śuddhaṃ ca pānīyaṃ yo harerdadet ।।

havirdānaphalasyārdhaṃ phalaṃ samyak samaśnute ।
kadalyā nārikelasya cūtasya panasasya ca ।।

phalāni ca nupakvāni bhaktyā śuddhāni yo dadet ।
havirdānāccaturbhāgaṃ phalaṃ so api samāpnuyāt ।।

karpūrailālavaṅgaiśca tathā jātīphalādibhiḥ ।
mātuluṅgaphalaiśśuddhaissupakvaiśca yutaṃ tathā ।।

tāṃbūlaṃ kramukairyuktaṃ mukhavāsaṃ ca yo dadet ।
sarvaiśvaryamavāpnoti viṣṇulokaṃ ca gacchati ।।

vidhinā balimārādhya kārayedyaḥ pradakṣiṇam ।
balaṃ balavatāṃ labdhvā viṣṇulokaṃ sa gacchati ।।

baliṃ seveta yo bhaktyā so api yajñaphalaṃ labhet ।
devasya maṇḍapaṃ kuryādgandhapuṣpaiḥ prapāntuvā ।।

sarvaiśvaryamavāpyaiva nityapuṣpaphalaṃ vrajet ।
viṣṇoḥ kathāstu saṃkīrtyastotraiḥ stutvā ca vaiṣṇavaiḥ ।।

śrutvābhaktyā hariṃ dhyāyan viṣṇuloke mahīyate ।
saumyān puṇyānimān viṣṇoścaturo apyarcanāvidhīn ।।

śrāvayedyo budho bhaktyā tathā yaśśruṇuyādapi ।
sarvapāpavinirmuktā vaiṣṇavaṃ padamāpnuyuḥ ।।

athotsavādikaraṇe phalaṃ vakṣye madhudviṣaḥ ।
sakāmānāṃ phalaṃ kāmyamakāmānāṃ paraṃ padam ।।

utsavaṃ tu pravakṣyanti devadevārcanāṃ surāḥ ।
utsāha utsavaḥ prokto manuṣyāṇāṃ viśeṣetaḥ ।।

udityutkṛṣṭaśabdo ayaṃ savo yajña udāhṛtaḥ ।
tasmāduttamayajñatvādutsavaḥ paribhāṣyate ।।

vājimedhāstayāgānāṃ tasmāddevotsavo varaḥ ।
utsavaṃ devadevasya yaḥ kuryātsvakulaṃ svakam ।।

uttārayan svayaṃ viṣṇossa yāti paramaṃ padam ।
savāduttāraṇaṃ yasmādutsavaḥ parikīrtyate ।।

sa yajño vo narān yuṣmānuttārayati niścayam ।
iti vedā vadantīti sa utsava udīrya te ।।

vājīmedhasahasreṇa yajato yatphalaṃ bhavet ।
yaścotsavena yajate tayostulyaṃ phalaṃ nmṛtam ।।

yāgānāmapi sarveṣāṃ phalamutsavakarmaṇā ।
devasyāśnuvate sarvaṃ ye yajante saṃśayaḥ ।।

savānutkramate yasmāttasmādutsava uchyate ।
upakurvanti ye martyā devasyotsavakarmaṇi ।।

karmāṇā manasā vācā te api yānti phalaṃ bahu ।
grāme vā ragare va'pi pattane vā mahotsavaḥ ।।

yatra pravartate viṣṇossaṃpadassanti tatra vai ।
yatra deśe janapade rāṣṭre vā pyutsavo hareḥ ।।

nāpamṛtyubhayaṃ tatra naināvagrahasaṃbhavaḥ ।
naiva corādyupahatirna tāpatrayasaṃgatiḥ ।।

dharmaścatuṣpādvarteta kalau tatrādimo yugaḥ ।
dhārmikaśca bhavedrājā prajā dharmaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

bhavanti sukhinassarve sarvaduḥkhavivarjitāḥ ।
mahotsave vartamāne yadarthibhyaḥ pradīyate ।।

pānīyamannaṃ vastraṃ vā tatsahasraguṇaṃ bhavet ।
puṣpamulaphalairijyā devasyābharaṇādikaiḥ ।।

kriyamāṇā yathāśakti nityānantyāya kalpate ।
sevante tatra ye devamaharniśamatandritāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ nālaṃ devāssahāsurāḥ ।
ālepanaṃ mārjanaṃ ca rajaḥ praśamanaṃ tathā ।।

vāribhīrdīpikāropaṃ kṣvelanāsphoṭanādikam ।
kurvantiye brāhmalokaṃ prayāntyamaradurlabham ।।

yānaṃ vahanti ye viprāste yānti brahmaṇaḥ padam ।
rathaṃ vahanti ye cāśvāste api yāntisurālayam ।।

chatrādidhāriṇaścāpi modante divi mānavāḥ ।
ācāryāścārcakāścaiva tathaiva paricārakāḥ ।।

utsave adhikṛtā viṣṇoḥ prāpnuvanti yathepsitam ।
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni ye tatrādhīyate janāḥ ।।

te pare vyomni devasya pārśve vartanti nisspṛhāḥ ।
sarvaśāntikaraṃ sarvaduḥkhotsādanamuttamam ।।

rājño rāṣṭrasya sukhadamāyurārogya vardhanam ।
prajānāṃ vāsudevasya kalyāṇārādhanaṃ mahat ।।

imaṃ devādayassarve viṣṇorutsavamuttamam ।
kṛtvā śāśvatikaṃ sthānaṃ prāpnuvantyatidurlabham ।।

atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa mahāsnapanajaṃ phalam ।
yena dravyeṇa deveśaṃ snāpayedyastubhaktitaḥ ।।

taddravyaṃ varthate tasya naśyaṃ tyevāśubhāni tu ।
rājño rāṣṭrasya taddravyaṃ samṛddhyaiva bhaviṣyati ।।

aśubhāni vinaśyanti śūbhāni prabhavanti ca ।
nirmāti yaḥprapāṃ viṣṇordevasya nnapanāya vai ।।

tasya nirmīyate gehassvarge svarganivāsibhiḥ ।
mṛdbhissaṃsnāpanādbhūmissarvasasyānvitā bhavet ।।

nagaiḥ pradakṣiṇādeva gotrasya sthitirāpyate ।
dhānyaissaṃsnāpanādviṣṇordhānyānāṃ vṛddhirāpyate ।।

aṅkurairarcanādviṣṇoḥ prajāvṛddhirbhaviṣyati ।
maṅgalaiḥ pūjanātsarvamaṅgalāni bhavanti vai ।।

snāpanātpañcabhirgavyaiḥ pāpaṃ saśyati sarvadhā ।
ghṛtena snāpanādbhuyātsāmādhyayanajaṃ phalam ।।

kṣīreṇa snāpayedviṣṇuṃ gāśca kṣīravatīriyāt ।
madhunā snāpayedviṣṇuṃ madhusyandi bhavedvacaḥ ।।

dadhnā saṃsnāpayeddevamacchaṃ tasya bhavedyaśaḥ ।
gandhodasnāpanādviṣṇossarvasaṃpadvṛtobhavet ।।

snāpayedakṣatodaistu prajā tasyākṣatā bhavet ।
phalodakasnāpanena śubhānīyātphalāni tu ।।

snāpanāttu kuśodena brahmavarcasamāpnuyāt ।
ratnodakasnāpanena maṇiratnādi vardhayet ।।

japyodakasya snānena sarvajāpaphalaṃ labhet ।
bhavantyoṣadhayassarvāssarvauṣadhyudakāplavāt ।।

puṇyapuṣpārcanenaiva puṇyavān jāyate naraḥ ।
cūrṇaiśśrīveṣṭakādīnīmarpaṇādvṛddhirāyuṣaḥ ।।

udvartanātkaṣāyeṇa cūrṇenāvāpyate ruciḥ ।
tīrthodasnāpanenaiva tīrthayātrāphalaṃ bhavet ।।

vanauṣadhībhissaṃsparśādbhavennityamarogatā ।
hāridracūrṇasnānena prīto bhavati cācyutaḥ ।।

mārjanātsarvagandhaiśca śrīrbhavatyacalā calā ।
mārjanānmūlagandhaiśca kulamedheta nityaśaḥ ।।

dhātubhiścāpyalaṅkārāddhātuvṛddhirbhaviṣyati ।
anyairanuktairvā yastudravyaiḥ snāpanakarmaṇi ।।

upatiṣṭhejjagadyoniṃ phalaṃ prāpnoti vistṛtam ।
yastu kuryājjaladroṇīṃ snānapīṭhaṃ ca śārṅgiṇaḥ ।।

sa sarvaiḥ pūjyayānantu pīṭhe cātyunna te vaset ।
evaṃ yassnapanaṃ viṣṇoḥ kārayecchaktito naraḥ ।।

yathoktānīha labdhvaivaphalāni suciraṃ bhuvi ।
ante vimāsamāruhya haimaṃ devaiḥ parīvṛtaḥ ।।

kinnarairapsarobhiśca nṛttairgeyaiśca tarpitaḥ ।
yakṣairvṛto atha gandharvaistsūyāmāno mudānvitaḥ ।।

sarvalokātparaṃ puṇyaṃ vaikuṇṭhaṃ lokamāpnuyāt ।
devadevasya viṣṇostu snapanaṃ bhaktimāṃstu yaḥ ।।

seveta so api pāpmabhyo mucyate nātra saṃśayaḥ ।
snāpanāntetu deveśasyotsavaṃ yaśca kārayet ।।

prajāvṛddhiṃ śriyaṃ sphārāṃ samāpnoti viśeṣataḥ ।
utsavaṃ sevateyastu so api yajñaphalaṃ labhet ।।

viṣṇupañcadine yastu deveśaṃ snāpayetprabhum ।
tasya syānmahatī saṃpatpaśuputrādi sammitā ।।

grahaṇe viṣuve tadvatsaṃkramādiṣu caivahi ।
anyeṣvapi ca puṇyeṣu kāryeṣu jagataḥ prabhum ।।

snāpayedyaśca seveta phalamāpnoti so api saḥ ।
yaḥ kuryādvaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma bhaktiśraddhāsamanvitaḥ ।।

khaṇḍite sphaṭite dhāmni dūṣite ca sūdhādibhiḥ ।
samādadhyātpunardhāma sa lokaṃ yāti vaiṣṇavaṃ ।।

corairapahṛte biṃbeyaḥ kuryātpratimāṃ punaḥ ।
sthāpayedbhakti yuktaśca sa yāti paramāṃ gatim ।।

pramādātpatite biṃbe sphuṭate dūṣite atha vā ।
yaḥ sandhāya punaḥ kuryātpritiṣṭhāṃ pūrvavanmudā ।।

tasya taṣyati deveśo varamiṣṭaṃ pradāsyati ।
śīrṇe jīrṇe tathā bhinne bhūṣaṇādau viśeṣataḥ ।।

navīkṛtyār'payedyastu tasya pāpaṃ praṇaśyati ।
yānāni rathaṅgādīnyālokya śithilāni vai ।।

samīkṛtya tu yodadyāttāni bhaktyā harennaraḥ ।
tasya kāyakṛtaṃ pāpaṃ tatkṣaṇādeva naśyati ।।

yastu vīkṣya harerarcāṃ patamānāmanādarāt ।
nardhayeddhanadānena tasya lokā madhudviṣaḥ ।।

sīdatāṃ vṛttihīnānāṃ devasyāghre padārthinām ।
yo dadyāducitāṃ vṛttiṃ sa yamaṃ nopasarpati ।।

yastu devotsavādīni kārayedbhaktisaṃyutaḥ ।
luptaprāyāṇi tasyā āpi bhavetphalamana ntakam ।।

yaḥ kuryāddevatāgāre luptakāryāṇi sattamaḥ ।
na tasya kṛtakṛtyatvādamātyā yamakiṅkarāḥ ।।

devārdhe brāhmaṇasyār'the yastyajettanumuttamām ।
tasya vāso bhavetsvarge cāvadidrāśca turdhaśa ।।

devārthe brāhmaṇasyār'dhe sarvasvaṃ svantyajettu yaḥ ।
tasya tuṣyati deveśassa tu svārājyamaśnu te ।।

prāyaścittanimittāni saṃbhūtānitu dhāmani ।
dṛṣṭvā ca śraddhayā yuktoyo devamupatiṣṭhate ।।

tasya tuṣyati deveśaḥ pra hṛṣṭassaṃprasīdati ।
prāyaścittānyaśeṣāṇi pāpaughadhvaṃsanāya vai ।।

nirdiṣṭāni purākalpe brahmaṇā parameṣṭhinā ।
lokānugrahaletorvai pavṛtto gururatvaraḥ ।।

narāṇāṃ sīdatāṃ dṛṣṭvā cittavṛttīssudurmalāḥ ।
prāyaścittavidhānaṃ tu provāca jagatāṃ hitaḥ ।।

na kaścinnācaretkarma śāstroktaṃ sakalaṃ kramāt ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena prāyaścittaṃ samācaret ।।

prāyaścittaṃ tu kṛtvaiva ya uktāmācaretkriyām ।
tasya syāddviguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ matassyādanupālanam ।।

bhaktiśraddhānvito yastu kuryādvā kārayetkramāt ।
deveśasya pratiṣṭhādi prāyaścittānta satkriyāḥ ।।

tasya puṇyaphalaṃ vaktuṃ na śakyaṃ tridaśairapi ।
iha loke akhilān kāmānanubhūya sukhaṃ cirāt ।।

dehantejāyate sadyaśśaṅkhacakragadādharaḥ ।
śrīvatsāṃkaścaturbāhuśśyāmalāṅgassu sundaraḥ ।।

gagane garuḍārūḍhassarva devanamaskṛtaḥ ।
adityamaṇḍalaṃ bhitvā gatvā śubhrāṃśumaṇḍalam ।।

tato avatīrya nikhilān lokānapi yathākramam ।
satyasthaṃ satyarokasthaṃ jagataḥ prabhavāpyayam ।।

tathāśeṣaviśeṣaṃ ca nityānandaṃ nirañjanam ।
sudhārasasamāsvādatulitaṃ nityatṛptidam ।।

śāśvataṃ tatparañjyotiḥ praviśennātra saṃśayaḥ ।
atha vakṣye viśeṣeṇa kriyālope ca yatphalam ।।

nirmātumālayaṃ yastu saṃkalpya matimānnaraḥ ।
pareṇedbodhito bhūyastasmā darthānni vartate ।।

tāvubhau narakaṃ pretya bhavetāṃ duḥkhabhāginau ।
kartā kārayitā caiva prerakaścānumodakaḥ ।।

sukṛte duṣkṛte caiva vadanti samabhāginaḥ ।
nirmātumicchayā dhāma devasya madhuvidviṣaḥ ।।

svayaṃ nivartate yastu tasya syānmahatī vipat ।
saṃkalpya devatāgāraṃ nirmātuṃ yo viśeṣataḥ ।।

ācāryaṃ vṛṇuyānno cettasya kāryaṃ praṇaśyati ।
ācāryassatataṃ goptā ācāryastu pitā smṛtaḥ ।।

ācāryassarvameveti yo manyeta sa manyate ।
ārabhya gehanirmāṇaṃ devasya jagataḥ pateḥ ।।

asamāpya tu yo mūḍho nivarte pravilobhataḥ ।
tasya saṃpadvināśassyāt kruddho bhavati cāvyayaḥ ।।

pravṛttāyāṃ pratiṣṭhāyāṃ yena kenāpi hetunā ।
yaḥ kuryādantarāyaṃ tu tasya puṇyaṃ vinaśyati ।।

yena vighnastadā bhūyāttaṃ hatvāpi na doṣabhāk ।
yastu śāstroditaṃ karma kurvantaṃ ca padārthinam ।।

śilpinaṃ vivadenmūḍhastasya nāstiphalaṃ kvacit ।
vivadeta ya ucchāstramācāryeṇa padārthinā ।।

tasyāśubhāni bhūyāṃsi bhaveyurnātra saṃśayaḥ ।
adhvare vartamāne tu saṃbhārān śāstracoditān ।।

yo na dadyātsa pāpīyān nāpnuyāt karmajaṃ phalam ।
pratiṣṭhāpya harerbiṃbaṃ yo na satkurute gurum ।।

anyānpadārthinaścāpi sa kiñcinnāpnuyātphalam ।
pratiṣṭhānte tathā nityamavicchinnaṃ tu pūjitum ।।

arcakaṃ vṛṇuyānno cedyajamāno vinaśyati ।
arcakaṃ ca tathācāryamanyāṃścāpi padārthinaḥ ।।

kālāvadhiṃ viniścitya yaḥ karmasu niyojayet ।
sa bhavedbrahmahā caiva dhanaṃ tasya vilupyati ।।

dāyarhāṃ kāyedvrattimarcakasya na cedyadi ।
yajamāno vipadyeta devāvāso naśiṣyati ।।

ācāryamarcakaṃ kuryāt svasthānādyo avaropitam ।
anyaṃ vā yojayettatra tāvubhau vinaśiṣyataḥ ।।

āpadyapi ca kaṣṭhāyāṃ na kadāpyanyamarcakam ।
pūrvāvaropaṇādeva niyuñjyāttu kathaṃ cana ।।

ādyārcakasya vaṃśetu jāyante ye mahāśayāḥ ।
sarve ca kramaśaḥ pūjāṃ kartumarhanti te yataḥ ।।

pitryaṃ bhavati devasya dāyādyaṃ pūjanaṃ svataḥ ।
tasmāttadvaṃśajān hitvā yadyanyaiḥ kāritār'canā ।।

brahmahatyābhavettasya tatbūjā niṣphalā bhavet ।
yastudadyādarcakāya bhṛtyarthaṃ ke valaṃ dhanam ।।

anyadvāpyasthiraṃ vastu na haristena tuṣyati ।
lobhānmohādathājñānādya ādatter'cako dhanam ।।

vetanārdhaṃ tathā dadyādyajamāno vimūḍhadhīḥ ।
ubhautaunarakaṃ yāto yādaccandra divākaram ।।

vittārthaṃ pūjayedyastu niyamyāpyavadhiṃ harim ।
savaidevalako nāma sarvakarma bahirkṛtaḥ ।।

adatvā vasudhāmagre pūjanārtha mathārcake ।
nirmāti brāhmaṇaṃ bhūyo yajamānastu devalam ।।

nahyasmātpātakaṃ kiñci dbrāhmaṇāyā aparādhyati ।
alabdhvādevatāgāranirmāṇasadṛśaṃ phalam ।।

brahmaghnatvamanuprāpya vinaśyati na saṃśayaḥ ।
hartā hārayitā bhūmerdattasya danuśāsinaḥ ।।

tatkiṅkarāṇāmanyeṣāṃ yo mūḍhassa tamovṛtaḥ ।
saṃbaddho vāruṇaiḥ pāśaiḥ kṛṣyamāṇassamantataḥ ।।

duḥkhito narake bhūyastiryagyoniṣu jāyate ।
svadattāṃ varadattāṃ vā yo hareta vasundharām ।।

ṣaṣṭirvarṣasahasrāṇi viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ ।
svadattāddviguṇaṃ puṇyaṃ paradattānu pālanam ।।

paradattāpahāreṇa svadattaṃ niṣpalaṃ bhavet ।
anyāyena hṛtā bhūmiranyāyenaina hāritā ।।

harato hārakasyāpi dahatyāsaptamaṃ kulam ।
pañca kanyānṛte hanti daśa hanti gavānṛte ।।

śatamaśvānṛte hanti sahasraṃ puruṣānṛte ।
hanti jātānajātāṃśca hiraṇyār'dhe anṛtaṃ vadan ।।

sarvaṃ bhūmyanṛte hanti no brūyādanṛtaṃ kvacit ।
vindhyāṭavīṣvatoyāsu śuṣkakojaravāsinaḥ ।।

kṛṣṇasarpāḥ prajāyante devabrahmasvahāriṇaḥ ।
taṭākānāṃ sahasreṇa hayamedhaśatena ca ।।

gavāṃ koṭipradānena bhūmihartāna śuddhyati ।
brahmasvaṃ brahmahatyā ca daridrasya ca yaddhanam ।।

gurumitradhanaṃ caiva svargasthamapi pātayet ।
brahmasve no matiṃ kuryātprāṇaiḥ kaṇṭhagatairapi ।।

agnidagdhāḥ prarohānti brahmadagdho na rohati ।
na viṣaṃ viṣamityāhurbrahmasvaṃ viṣamucyate ।।

viṣamekākinaṃ hanti brahmasvaṃ putrapautrakam ।
brahmasvaṃ praṇayādbhuktaṃ dahatyāsaptamaṃ kulam ।।

vikrameṇa tu bhoktṝṇāṃ daśapūrvān daśāvarān ।
lohacūrṇāṃśca cūrṇāṃśca viṣaṃ vā jarayetpumān ।।

brahmasvaṃ triṣu lokeṣu kaḥpumān jarayiṣyati ।
devasvaṃ brāhmaṇasvaṃ ca lobheno pahinasti yaḥ ।।

sa pāpāttu pareloke gṛdhrocchiṣṭena jīvati ।
devadravyavināśena brahmasvaharaṇena ca ।।

kulānyakulatāṃ yānti brāhmaṇātikrameṇa ca ।
sahasrasammitā dhenuranaḍvān daśadhenavaḥ ।।

daśāvaḍvatsamaṃ yānaṃ daśayānasamo hayaḥ ।
daśavājisamā kanyā bhūmidānena sā samā ।।

ṣaṣṭirvarṣa sahasrāṇi svarge tiṣṭhati bhūmidhaḥ ।
ācchettācānumantā ca tānyena narake vaset ।।

patantyaśrūṇi rudatāṃ dīnānāmavasīdatām ।
brāhmaṇānāṃ hṛte kṣetre hanyādāsaptamaṃ kulam ।।

sādhubhyo bhūmimākṣipya na bhūmiṃ vindatekvacit ।
dadaddhi bhūmiṃ sādhubhyo vindate phūmimuttamām ।।

arcakaḥ praṇidhiryasmāddeveśasya jagatpateḥ ।
sa devo brāhmaṇassādhurmahadbhūtaṃ pracakṣate ।।

tasmāttadarpitāṃ vṛttiṃ naiva śaṅketa buddhimān ।
tadarcakārpitāṃ bhūmiṃ yo hareta yateta vā ।।

kiṃ punastasya vaktavyaṃ na bhavettasya niṣkṛtiḥ ।
na vācā śakyate vaktuṃ gatistasya durātmanaḥ ।।

mriyeta sadya evāsau jāyate atha punaḥ punaḥ ।
na tasya śaraṇaṃ kvāpi labhyate pāpakarmaṇaḥ ।।

devasye api matiṃ kuryātprahmasvaṃ na haretkvacit ।
prāsādamaṇḍapādīnāṃ bhoktāraḥ kaiṭabhadviṣaḥ ।।

temūḍhamatayaḥ pretya narakeṣu niratyayāḥ ।
vasanti bhūyo jāyante nīcayoniṣu ca dhruvam ।।

bhūṣaṇacchatravastrādihartā yo durmatirnaraḥ ।
gale nigalitaḥ pāśaiḥ kṛṣyate nirayeṣu saḥ ।।

vāhanāni ca yānāni vaiṣṇavāni harantiye ।
mohādvasanti te dīrgha maṅgāranarakodare ।।

pretya bhūyo api jāyante gardabhoṣṭrādiyoniṣu ।
candanādīni vastūni puṣpāṇi surabhīṇyapi ।।

vrajanti svāni viṣṇoste vrajante yāmyayātanām? ।
anubhūya punarbhūyo jāyante gandhamūṣikāḥ ।।

upānatpādukāpīṭhavāhanāni harantiye ।
uṣitvā narakeṣvete jāyante phaṇināṃ kule ।।

gobhūhiraṇyavastrādi dhanaṃ viṣṇoḥ parigraham ।
āhṛtya ye anubhuñjante narakeṣu duratyayāḥ ।।

uṣitvā pretya bhūyo api jāyante śvādiyoniṣu ।
sarveṣu narakeṣvevaṃ devabrahmasvahāriṇaḥ ।।

nasanti mūḍhamatayo yāmyaduḥkheṣu yātanāḥ ।
vāsudevapratikṛterbhedanacchedanādiṣu ।।

vikrīḍādīniyānyeṣu yatante pāpacetasaḥ ।
ete yānti kramātsarvāsnarakān bhṛśadāruṇān ।।

anyeṣvapyapacāreṣu sthūlasūkṣmeṣu mānavāḥ ।
kṛtinaḥ pretya narake pacyante duḥkhabhāginaḥ ।।

athanityārcanāyāṃ vai deveśasya viśeṣataḥ ।
upacārādihāno tu pāpasyedaṃ phalaṃ bhavet ।।

āsanasya vihīne tu dharmanāśo bhaviṣyati ।
svāgate buddhināśassyānmūkatvamanumānake ।।

vihīne pādukāyāstu paṅgutvaṃ saṃbhavatyuta ।
pādyahīne mahānrogaḥ kleśaścāpi bhaviṣyati ।।

danta dhāvanahīne ca duṣṭadanto abhijāyate ।
tāṃbūlahīne vidveṣaṃ kuṣṭaṃ tailavihīnake ।।

keśasaṃśodhane hīne galarogo bhaviṣyati ।
snānadravyavihīne ca snānahīne tathaiva ca ।।

rājayakṣmā bhavedrogaḥ pāpiṣṭhaśca sudāruṇaḥ ।
plotahīne vātarogo vastrahīne jalodaraḥ ।।

saṃvyānahīne hṛdrogo yajñasūtravihīnake ।
agnidāhabhayaṃ caiva mandāgnitvaṃ ca jāyate ।।

gandhahīne ca kuṣṭhassyādbhūṣāhīne mahadbhayam ।
puṣpahīne tvalābhassyāttathā ca kaphasaṃbhavaḥ ।।

(śūdrāhṛtaiḥ krayakrītair arcanaṃ niṣphalaṃ sumaiḥ ।
araṇyādvāgṛhādvāpi vikrītānyāpaṇāntarāt ।।

ayācitāni puṣpāṇi labdhānyarhāṇi nār'cane ।
tathā paryuṣitairyāpi jantubhirdūṣitairapi ।।

mlānairaspṛśyasaṃspṛṣṭairdurgandhaiḥ pādalaṅghitaiḥ ।
pratilomāntyajānītairarcanaṃ tvaphalaṃ bhavet ।।

uttamaṃ svārjitaṃ puṣpaṃ madhyamaṃ vanyamucyate ।
adhamaṃ tu krayakrītaṃ pārakyamadhamādhamam ।।

hastānītaṃ paṭānītaṃ svayaṃ patitameva vā ।
anyārāmodbhavaṃ puṣpaṃ nār'payediti ke cana ।।

ārahare ca śukre ca manvādiṣu yugādiṣu ।
nāharettulasīpatraṃ madhyāhnātparatastathā ।।

saṃkrāntyāṃ pakṣayorante dvādaśyorniśi saṃdhyayoḥ ।
tulasīṃ ye vicinvanti te kṛntanti hareśśiraḥ ।।

bhṛgvarkāṃgārake vāre dvādaśyāṃ pañcaparvasu ।
nāharettulasīpatraṃ nandāyāṃ śravaṇe api ca ।।

keśakīṭāpaviddhāni śīrṇaparyuṣitāni ca ।
bhugnapatraṃ na ca grāhyaṃ kṛmiduṣṭaṃ ca nāharet ।।

varjayedūrṇanābhena vāsitaṃ yadi śobhanam ।
sthalajaṃ noddharetpuṣpaṃ chedayejjalajaṃ na tu ।।

niṣiddhairduḥkhadairdevaṃ nār'cayeta kadā cana ।
na śuṣkaiḥpūjayeddevaṃ kunumairna mahīgataiḥ ।।

na viśīrṇataraiśśiṣṭairnāśubhairnāvikāsibhiḥ ।
pūtigandhograndhāni hyugragandhāni varjayet ।।

snānaṃ kṛtvā tu ye ke citpuṣpaṃ gṛhṇanti vaidvijāḥ ।
devatāstanna gṛhṇantitanna gṛhṇanti mānavāḥ ।।

pitarastanna gṛhṇanti bhasmībhavati kāṣṭhavat ।
snānaṃ kṛtvātu madhyāhne puṣpāṇi na samāharet ।।

tebhyaḥkruddho akṣayaṃ duḥkhaṃ krodhādviṣṇuḥ prayacchati ।
anyadevār'thasandiṣṭaiḥ pūjayedyo hariṃ prabhum ।।

sa tu tenaiva pāpena maṇḍūko jāyate naraḥ ।
tatassa narakaṃ yāti yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।।

kusumānāṃ nivedyānāṃ gandhamāghrāti yo naraḥ ।
sa pūti gandhasaṃyuktaḥ kuṣṭhī caiva prajāyate ।।

janmadvayaṃ tu vai mūḍhaśśūdratāṃ yāti mānavaḥ ।
asūtragrathitaṃ puṣpamasnehāktaṃ tathodanam ।।

avālukāyutaṃ toyaṃ sarvaṃ paryuṣitaṃ bhavet ।
etaistu pūjanātsadyo niṣphalāssakalāḥ kriyāḥ ।।

ādarśanavihīne tu kāmilā ca bhaviṣyati ।
bādhiryaṃ dhūpahīne ca dīpahīne andhatāmiyāt ।।

arghyahīne tu devasya kulaṃ bhavati ninditam ।
madhuparkavihīne ca madhumeho bhaviṣyati ।।

mātrādānavihīne tu sarvanāśo bhaviṣyati ।
rakṣānīrājane hīne rāṅgasair āvṛtirbhavet ।।

vedādhyayanahīne tu karmalopo bhaveddhruvam ।
havirnivedane hīne durbhikṣaṃ bhavati dhruvam ।।

upadaṃśavihīne ca dāridṣaṃ grāmavāsinām ।
nālikeraphale hīne hīne kṣīrādike tathā ।।

vināśassarvasasyānāṃ durbhikṣaṃ ca bhavedhdhruvam ।
hīne bhakṣyādike caiva vividhe haviṣī prabho ।।

tadgrāmayajamānasya viśeṣeṇāśubhaṃ bhavet ।
viniyogakramasyātrahīne pūjaiva naśyati ।।

kāle yavanikāhīne kartā caiva vinaśyati ।
dvārapūjāvihīne tu taska rādipraveśanam ।।

dvārapālakapūjāyo hīne caurādyupadravaḥ ।
śāntasya pūjane hīne tathā caivānapāyinām ।।

rājño rāṣṭrasya sarvasya vināśassyānna saṃśayaḥ ।
yajamānasya tatrāpi pararājādyupadravaḥ ।।

pāparogādipīḍā ca bhaviṣyati tathā punaḥ, ।
sarpavṛścikalūtādyairhāniścaiva bhavedbahu ।।

puṣpanyāser'canehīne nyūne vā mantravarjite, ।
tadgrāmavāsināṃ caiva rājadveṣo bhaviṣyati ।।

bhūtapīṭhasya pārśve vā dakṣiṇe vā viśeṣataḥ, ।
bhūtādināgaparyantaṃ balyarcanavihīnake ।।

śākinyādigrahāssarve praviśanti na saṃśayaḥ ।
śrīdevyā arcane hīne saṃpadāṃ tu bhavet kṣayaḥ ।।

hariṇyarcanahīne ca sthānanāśo bhaviṣyati, ।
agnipūjāvihīne tu nyūne vā mantravarjite ।।

nivedanājyahīne vā saṃbhavedvarṇasaṃkaraḥ, ।
varṇāśramādihāniśca brāhmaṇānāṃ vipadbhavet ।।

pānīyahīne devasya bhavettatra tvavagrahaḥ, ।
mukhavāsavihīne tu janavidveṣaṇaṃ bhavet ।।

balidravyavihīne tu nyūne mantravivarjite ।
balakṣayo janānāṃ syātpitṝṇāṃ patanaṃ bhavet ।।

puṣpāṃjalivihīne tu rājakopā bhaviṣyati, ।
praṇāmastutihīne tu sadyo mṛtyurbhaviṣyati, ।।

dhyānahīne kulaṃ hanti nyāsahīne vipadbhavet ।
prāṇāyāmavihīne tu paracakrabhayaṃ bhavet ।।

śaucācāravihīne tu paśuputrādināśanam ।
biṃbanyāsavihīne tu kalatraṃ tasya naśyati ।।

pradakṣiṇavihīne tu pātakī jāyate naraḥ ।
nityamarcāvasānetu pūjakācāryayormude ।।

dakṣiṇādānahīne tu sā pūjā niṣphalā bhavet ।
rāṣṭrasya yajamānasya rājñaścāpi bhavedbhayam ।।

hīne tu pācakādīnāṃ dakṣiṇādānakarmaṇi ।
paśuvāhananāśaśca tadgrāme saṃbhavennṛṇām ।।

prātaḥ pūjāvihīne tu tadgrāme avagraho bhavet ।
brāhmaṇānāṃ kriyāhānissarvakarmavināśanam ।।

madhyāhnapūjāhīne tu rāṣṭrakṣobho bhaviṣyati ।
sāyaṅkālār'cane hīne tadgrāmayajamānayoḥ ।।

arthahāniḥ prajāhānirbhaviṣyati na saṃśayaḥ ।
upasaṃdhyārcane hīne karmalopo bhaviṣyati ।।

viṣṇupañcadine caiva hīne snāner'cane tathā ।
utsave ca viśeṣaṇa yajamānabhayaṃ bhavet ।।

māsapūjāvihīnetu bhrātṛdveṣo bhaviṣyati ।
viṣude cāyane caiva hīne tatroktakarmaṇi ।।

grāmasya yajamānasya yaśohānirbhaviṣyati ।
snapanokte tathānyasmin divase snānavarjite ।।

akāle ca kṛte vāpi bhavet kṣāmabhayaṃ tathā ।
nityotsavavihīne tu nirānando bhavejjanaḥ ।।

anyasminnarcanadravye vihīne doṣa āpatet ।
nimitte yadi saṃprāpte snāpayeccenna mādhavam ।।

tasya pāpaphalaṃ naktuṃ na kenāpi hi śakyate ।
rājño rāṣṭrasya ca bhavetsarvatrātyāhitaṃ dhruvam ।।

gṛhanāśaḥ prapāhīne hīnāyāṃ cāpyalaṅkṛtau ।
mṛtsuhīnānu nāśassyātsasyānāṃ tu na saṃśayaḥ ।।

parvateṣu vihīneṣu sthairyaṃ tasya vilupyate ।
dhānyeṣu tu vihīneṣu dyānyanāśo bhavettathā ।।

aṅkurāṇāmabhāve tu prajāhāniśca saṃbhavet ।
maṅgaleṣvatha hīneṣu tasya bhūyādamaṅgalam ।।

pañcagavyavihīne tu gohatyā samavāpyate ।
ghṛtahīne buddhināśo anāyuṣyaṃ kṣīrahīnake ।।

madhuhīne mahān vyādhirdadhihīne tu saṃjvaraḥ ।
kṣīrahīne bhavettasya malinā kīrtireva hi ।।

gandhodakavihīne tu durgandho jāyate bhṛśam ।
akṣatodakahīne tu kṣatistasya prajāyate ।।

phalodakavihīne tu viphalaṃ tasya jīvitam ।
kuśodakavihīne ca naidheta brahmavarcasam ।।

ratnodakavihīne ca dhanadhyānya vināśanam ।
abhāve cauṣadhīnāntu vyādhipīḍā bhaviṣyati ।।

upasnānavihīne tu malinaṃ jāyate kulam ।
uṣṇāṃbhasāmabhove tu bhaveduṣṇaśarīratā ।।

puṇyapuṣpavihine tu pāpīyān jāyate naraḥ ।
jātīphalādicūrṇasya cābhāve tu vipadbhavet ।।

kaṣāyacūrṇahīne tu kāntihīno bhavennaraḥ ।
vanauṣadhīnāṃ cālābhe rogī bhavati niścayaḥ ।।

hāridracūrṇahīne tu gataśrīrjāyate naraḥ ।
mūlagandhavihīne tu vārdhakyaṃ bhavati dhravam ।।

dhātūnāmapyabhāvetu sirdhāturjāyate naraḥ ।
plotavastrottarīyāṇāṃ bhūṣaṇānāṃ vihīnake ।।

karmanāśo bhavedeva na tuṣṭati ramāpatiḥ ।
ācāryasyartvijāṃ tadvadanyeṣāṃ ca padārthinām ।।

dakṣiṇādānahīne ca sarvanāśo bhaviṣyati ।
hīne haviṣi devasya niṣphalaṃ snapanaṃ bhavet ।।

snapanāntotsave hīne na devaḥparituṣyati ।
śithilaṃ bhagavadgehaṃ dṛṣṭyā śrutvā ca yonaraḥ ।।

tatkriyā lopitā vāpi sa bhaveddevahā dhruvam ।
tadgrāmavāsinassarve rājā cānyodhanī punaḥ ।।

śīghraṃ sarvaṃ samīkṛtya pūrvavatpunarācaret ।
anyathā yadi kuryācchedrājarāṣṭraṃ vinaśyati ।।

dharmasetumimaṃ vindyātsarvasādhāraṇaṃ naraḥ ।
pālanīyassadā so ayaṃ jagatāṃ yatra saṃsthitiḥ ।।

prāyaścittanimittetu saṃprāpte yastu mūḍhadhīḥ ।
akṛtvā niṣkṛtiṃ kuryātkārayetkarma cottaram ।।

lobhānmohadathājñānādanādṛtya ca śāsanam ।
bhagavacchāsanadrohī sa bhavetpātakī janaḥ ।।

pramādināṃ manuṣyāṇāṃ skhalanaṃ niyataṃ yataḥ ।
niṣkṛtirvihitā pūrvairnatāmaticaretkvacit ।।

brahmādyairapi yaddevairaśakyaṃ pūjanaṃ hareḥ ।
taduktā niṣkṛtiḥ pūrvairnatāmatipatetkvacit ।।

nimitte yastvakṛtvaiva prāyaścittaṃ yathocitam ।
nnityaṃ naimittikaṃ kāmyaṃ kuryāttadakṛtaṃ bhavet ।।

tasmānnimitte saṃprāpte niṣkṛtiṃ sadya ācaret ।
iti saṃkṣepataḥ proktaṃ kriyāyogāśritaṃ phalam ।।

iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ sahitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre pañcatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

athaṣaṭtriṃśo adhyāyaḥ apacārāḥ

apacārāstathā viṣṇordvātriṃśatparikīrtitāḥ ।
yānairvā pādukairvāpi gamanaṃ bhagavadgṛhe ।।

devotsavādyasevācāpraṇāmaṃ ca tadagrataḥ ।
ekahastapraṇāmaśca tatpurastātpradakṣiṇam ।।

ucchiṣṭe caiva cāśauce bhagavadvandanādikam ।
pādaprasāraṇaṃ cāgre tathā paryaṅkabandhanam ।।

śayanaṃ bhojanaṃ caiva mudhābhāṣaṇameva ca ।
uccairbhāṣā vṛdhājalpo rodanādyaṃ ca vigrahaḥ ।।

nigraho anugrahaścaiva strīṣu sākūtabhāṣaṇam ।
aślīlakathanaṃ caivāpyadhovāyuvimokṣaṇam ।।

kaṃbalāvaraṇaṃ caiva varanindā parastutiḥ ।
śaktau gauṇopacāraścāpyaniveditabhakṣaṇam ।।

tattatkālodbhavānāṃ ca phalādīnāmanarpaṇam ।
viniyuktāvaśiṣṭasya pradānaṃ vyañjanādiṣu ।।

pṛṣṭhīkṛtyāsanaṃ caiva pareṣāmabhivandanam ।
guraumaunaṃ nijastotraṃ devatānindanaṃ tathā ।।

apacārāṃ stu vividhānīdṛśān parivarjayet ।
apacāreṣvananteṣu satsvanyeṣu pramādataḥ ।।

"kṣama''svetyarthanaivaigā niṣkṛtirnirupadravā ।
anyathā yadi kurvāṇaḥpramādāt jñānato athavā ।।

sa yāti narakān ghorān santataṃ bhṛśadāruṇān ।
yetu smaraṇamātreṇa bhavanti hṛdayacchidaḥ ।।

dvātriṃśannarakāḥ
dvātriṃśannarakāste tu kīrtyantebrahmavādibhiḥ ।
rauravadhvāntaśītoṣṇatāpāṃbujamahāṃbujāḥ ।।

kālasūtro aṣṭamo hyete narakā iti viśrutāḥ ।
sūcyagrakālakhaḍgāśca kṣuradhārāṃcabarīṣakāḥ ।।

taptāṃgāramahādāhau saṃtāpaśceti ke cana ।
bhavantyaṣṭāsu bhībhatkā mahāśabdā bhayānakāḥ ।।

lakṣāpralepamāṃsādanirucchvasanasocchvasāḥ ।
yugmādriśālmalīlohapradīpakṣutpipāsikāḥ ।।

kṛmīṇāṃ nicayaścaiva rājānaḥ parikīrtitāḥ ।
lohastambho atha viṇmūtre tathā vaitaraṇī nadī ।।

tāmisraścāndhatāmisraḥ kumbhīpāko atha rauravaḥ ।
mahāpadānugāmī ca rājarājeśvarāhvayaḥ ।।

trayastrīṃśatpuṭeṣvardhaṃ pārthivaṃ cārdhamāyasam ।
tanmadhye narakā ghorā bahuśastamasi sthitāḥ ।।

teṣāṃ narakabhedānāmaṣṭāviṃśatikoṭayaḥ ।
eteṣāṃ dāruṇānāṃ tu narakāṇāṃ patisthsitaḥ ।।

kūśmāṇḍa iti vikhyātaḥ pralayārkālanadyutiḥ ।
karālavadanaḥ kruddho vṛttakoṭaralocanaḥ ।।

ṭaṅkapāṇistathābhūtairbhūtairbhūyobhirāvṛtaḥ ।
pāpāstveteṣu pacyantenarāḥ karmānurūpataḥ ।।

yātanābhirvicitrābhirāpāpaprakṣayāntakam ।
prāyaścittojghitā dṛptānijadharmaparāṅmukhāḥ ।।

paradharmaratāścorāḥ patanti narakāgniṣu ।
mahāpātakinaḥkalpaṃ tiṣṭhanti narakāgniṣu ।।

manvantaraṃ pātakino devabrahmasvahāriṇaḥ ।
upapātakino martyā devadevāgniyajvanām ।।

dvijagogurudharmāṇāṃ nindakā brahmaṇo dinam ।
anye caturyugaṃ martyāstadardhaṃ ca narādhamāḥ ।।

tiṣṭhanti narake ghore nijapāpānurūpyataḥ ।
dyūtastrīviṣayāsaktā ye dharmavikalāḥkhalāḥ ।।

patanti teṣu ghoreṣu narakeṣu narādhamāḥ ।
na śruṇvanti ca ye mūḍhāssādhūktaṃ dharmagauravam ।।

"pyatyakṣaṃ kena taddṛṣṭaṃ pratyu''teti vadanti ca ।
kāmalobhābhibhūtāśca biḍālavratinastathā ।।

pāpiṣṭhāḥ karmahīnāśca jihvopasthaparāyaṇāḥ ।
yatinindāparā ye ca kṣetratīrthādidūṣakāḥ ।।

patanti teṣu te martyāvivaśāḥ pāpabandhanāḥ ।
ihānubhūyanirdiṣṭamāyurmartyāssvayaṃbhuvā ।।

nimittaṃ kiñcidāsādya vimucyantekalevaraiḥ ।
labhante te punardebaṃ yātanīyaṃ svakarmajam ।।

tanmātraguṇasaṃpannaṃ sukhaduḥkhopabhogadam ।
pāpāḥ pāpakṣayo yāvatpacyante narakāgniṣu ।।

āmalaprakṣayādvahnau dhmāyantedhātavo yathā ।
yāvantojantavassvargabhūpātāleṣu sarvataḥ ।।

tāvanta eva ghoreṣu santyadho narakāgniṣu ।
aṣṭāviṃśatirevoktāḥ kṣiternarakakoṭayaḥ ।।

saptamasya talasyādho ghoretamasi saṃsthitāḥ ।
ghorākhyā pradhamākoṭissu ghoratalasaṃsthitāḥ ।।

atighorā mahāghorā ghoraghorā ca pañcamī ।
ṣaṣṭhī taralatārākhyā saptamī ca bhayāvahā ।।

aṣṭamī kālarātrī ca navamī ca bhayotkaṭā ।
daśamī tadadhaścaṇṇā mahācaṇḍā tato apyadhaḥ ।।

caṇḍakolāhalācānyā pracaṇḍānarakādhikā ।
padmāpadmavatī bhīmā bhīmabhīṣaṇanāyakā ।।

karālā vikarālā ca vajrā viṃśatikāsmṛtā ।
trikoṇā pañcakoṇā ca sudīrghā parivartulā ।।

saptabhaumāṣṭabhaumā ca dīptāyāmeti cāṣṭamī ।
ityetā nāmataḥ proktā ghorā narakakoṭayaḥ ।।

aṣṭāviṃśatirevaitāḥ pāpānāṃ yātanātmanām ।
tāsāṃ krameṇa vijñeyāḥ pañca pañcaikanāyakāḥ ।।

pratyekaṃ sarvakoṭīnāṃ nāmatastānnibodhata ।
rauravaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ rudante yatra dehinaḥ ।।

mahārauravako yatra mahānto api rudantica ।
tamaśśītaṃ yathā coṣṇaṃ pañcādyā nāyakāssmṛtāḥ ।।

sughorassutapastīkṣṇaḥ padmassaṃ jīvanaśśataḥ ।
mahāmāṃso vilomaśca subhīmaśca kaṭaṅkaṭaḥ ।।

tīvraveṣī karālaśca vikarālaḥ prakampanaḥ ।
mahāpadmassupadmaśca kālavakraśca garjanaḥ ।।

sūcīmukhassunemiśca khādakassuprapīḍanaḥ ।
kuṃbhīpākassupākaśca cakrakaścātidāruṇaḥ ।।

aṅgārarāśiphavanamasṛkpūyacahadrastathā ।
tīkṣṇāyastuṇḍaśakunirmahāsaṃvartakastatā ।।

sutaptābjassulopaśca pūtimāṃso dravatrapu ।
ucchvāsaśca nirucchvāso sudīrghaḥ kūṭaśālmalī ।।

darīṣṭassumahānādaprabhāvassuprabhāvanaḥ ।
ṛkṣameṣavṛkāśśalya siṃhavyāghragajānanāḥ ।।

śvasūkarājamahiṣakharameṣahayānanāḥ ।
grahakuṃbhīranakrāsyāḥ sarpakūrmāsyavāyasāḥ ।।

kṛdhrolūkajalūkāśca śārdūlakapikarkaṭāḥ ।
gandhakaḥ pūtivakraśca raktākṣaḥ pūtimṛttikaḥ ।।

kaṇadhūmastuṣāgniśca kṛmīṇāṃ nicayastathā ।
amedhyaścāpratīkāro rudhirānnasyabhojanam ।।

lālābhakṣamabhakṣaśca sarvabhakṣaśca dāruṇaḥ ।
jaṅkaṭassuvilāsaśca vikaṭaḥ kaṭapūtanaḥ ।।

ambarīṣaḥ kaṭāhaśca kaṣṭā vaitaraṇī nadī ।
sutaptalohaśayanamekapādaprataptakam ।।

asitālavanaṃ ghoramasthibhaṅgaprapīḍanam ।
tilātasīkṣuyāntrāṇikūṭapāśapramardanam ।।

mahāchullī suchullī ca taptalohamayī śilā ।
parvatakṣuradhārākhyaṃ tathā ca malaparvataḥ ।।

mūtraviṣṭhāṃdhakūpeṣu kṣārakūpeṣu pātanam ।
musalolūkhalaṃ yantraṃ śilāśakalalāṅgalam ।।

tālapatrāsigahanaṃ mahāmaśakamaṇḍapam ।
sammohano asthibhaṅgaśca tapuḥśūlamayoguḍaḥ ।।

bahuduḥkhaṃ mahāduḥkhaṃ kaśmalaṃ śamalaṃ malam ।
hālāhalo nirūpaśca surūpaśca tamo anugaḥ ।।

ekapādastripādaśca tīvravīciśca rantimaḥ ।
aṣṭāviṃśatirevaitaiḥ kramaśaḥ pañcakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

koṭīnāmānu pūrvyeṇa pañca pañcaiva nāyakāḥ ।
rauravādyaṃ ca vīryaṃ ca śatamekantu sarvataḥ ।।

catvāriṃśatsamadhikaṃ mahānarakamaṇḍalam ।
teṣu pāpāḥ prapacyantenarāḥ karmānurūpataḥ ।।

yātanābhirvicitrābhirākarmaprakṣayādbhṛśam ।
susūḍhaṃ hastayorbaddhvātaptaśṛṅkhalayā narāḥ ।।

mahāvṛṅgaraśākhāsugamyanteyamakiṅkaraiḥ ।
ḍolitāścātivegena nissaṃjñā yāntiyojanam ।।

antarikṣasthitānāṃ ca lohabhāraśataṃ tataḥ ।
pādayorbadhyate teṣāṃ yamadūtairmahābalaiḥ ।।

tena bhāreṇa mahatā bhṛśamātāḍitānarāḥ ।
ākhyāntassvāni karmāṇi tūṣṇīṃ tiṣṭanti vihvalāḥ ।।

tatastaptairagni varṇairlohadaṇḍaissakaṇṭakaiḥ ।
hanyante kiṅkarairghoraissamartātpāpakāriṇaḥ ।।

tataḥ kṣāreṇa dīptena vahnerapi viśeṣataḥ ।
samantataḥ pralipyante tāmreṇa ca punaḥ punaḥ ।।

drutenātyantaliptena kṣatāṅgā jarjarīkṛtāḥ ।
punarvidhāya cāṅgāni śiraḥprabhṛti cakramāt ।।

vārtākavatprapacyante taptataile kaṭāhake ।
niṣṭhāpūrṇe tathākūpe kṛmīṇāṃnicaye punaḥ ।।

medo asṛkpūyapūrṇāyāṃ vāpyāṃ kṣipyanti? te punaḥ ।
bhakṣyante kṛmibhistīvrairlohatuṇḍaiśca vāyasaiḥ ।।

śvabhirdaṃśairvṛkairugrairvyāghraiśca vikṛtairnaraiḥ ।
pacyante caruvadvāpi pradīptāṅgārarāśiṣu ।।

protāstīkṣṇeṣu śūleṣu narāḥ pāpena karmaṇā ।
śailapīṭhairathākramya ghoraiḥ karmabhirātmajaiḥ ।।

tilavatsaṃprapīḍyante cakrākhye narake narāḥ ।
pacyante cātitapteṣu lohabhāṇḍeṣvanekathā ।।

tailapūrṇakaṭāheṣu sutapteṣu punaḥpunaḥ ।
sardendriyāṇi saṃbaddhya kramātpāpena yātanāḥ ।।

bhavanti ghorāḥ pratyekaṃ śarīre tatkṛtena ca ।
ye śruṇvanti harernindāṃ teṣāṃ karṇaḥ prapūryate ।।

agninarṇairayaḥkīlaistaptaistāmrādikadrutaiḥ ।
trapusīsārakūrakūṭādyaiḥkṣāreṇa jatunā punaḥ ।।

sutaptatīkṣṇatailena vajralepena cāntataḥ ।
kramādāpūryate karṇau? narakeṣu ca yātanāḥ ।।

anukrameṇa sarveṣu bhramantyeteṣu yātanāḥ ।
ye tu deva gṛhaṃ gatvā tatra sevārthamāgatāḥ ।।

atha vānyatra tadrūpā madamohaparājitāḥ ।
paradārāṃśca gacchanti lubdhāssnigdhena cakṣuṣā ।।

guroḥkurvanti bhrukuṭīṃ krūranetrāścaye narāḥ ।
sūcībhiragnivarṇābhisteṣāṃ cakṣuḥ pravidhyate ।।

kṣārādyaiśca kramātsarvairdehe sarvāśca yātanāḥ ।
sparśalobhena ye mūḍhāssaṃspṛśanti parastriyaḥ ।।

teṣāṃ taptāgnivarṇābhissūcībhirvidhyate karaḥ ।
tataḥ kṣārādikaissarvaṃ śarīramanulipyate ।।

yātanāśca mahākaṣṭāssarveṣu narakeṣu ca ।
pareṣvajanti cātyugraṃ pradīptaṃ lohaśālmalim ।।

hanyante pṛṣṭhadeśeṣu punarbhīmairmahābalaiḥ ।
dantureṇātikuṇṭhena krakacena balīyasā ।।

śilaḥpṛbhṛti pāṭyanteghoraiḥ karmabhirātmajaiḥ ।
tenatenaiva rūpeṇa hanyante pāradārikāḥ ।।

gāḍhamāliṅgyate nārī jvalantīlohanirmitā ।
pūrvākālaṃ jvalantaṃ taṃ pūruṣaṃ lohanirmitam ।।

duścāriṇyaḥstrīyo gāḍhamāliṅgantivadanti ca ।
kiṃ pradhāvasi vegena na te moho asti saṃprati ।।

laṅghitaste yathā bhartā pāpaṃ bhuṅkṣva tadādhunā ।
lohakuṃbhe vinikṣiptāḥ sāpidhāne śanaiśśanaiḥ ।।

mṛdvagninā prapacyante svapāpairiva mānavāḥ ।
ulūkhalādyaiḥ kṣodyante prapīḍyante śilāsu ca ।।

kṣipyante cāndhakūpeṣu daśyante bhramarairbhṛśam ।
kṛmibhirbhinna sarvāṅgāśśataśo jarjarīkṛtāḥ ।।

sutīkṣṇakṣurakūpeṣu kṣipyante tadanantaram ।
mahajvāle ca narake pāpāḥ pacyanti sarvataḥ ।।

itastataśca dhāvanti dahyamānāstadarciṣā ।
pṛṣṭhenānīya jaṅghe dve vinyaste srandhayojite ।।

tayormadhyena cākṛṣya bāhupṛṣṭhena gāḍhataḥ ।
baddhvā parasparaṃ sarvaṃ sudṛḍhaṃ pāparajjubhiḥ ।।

piṇḍabaddhaṃ daśantyenaṃ bhramārāstīkṣṇalohajāḥ ।
mānināṃ krodhināṃ caiva taskarāṇāṃ ca dāruṇāḥ ।।

piṇḍabaddhāssmṛtā yāmyamahājvāle ca yātanāḥ ।
rijjubhirveṣṭitāṃgāśca praliptāḥ kardamena ca ।।

karīṣavatprapacyante mriyante tena tetathā ।
sutīkṣṇakṣāratoyena karmaśānu śilāsu ca ।।

apāpasaṃkṣayātpāpā ghṛṣyante candanaṃ yathā ।
śarīrābhyantaragataissantataṃ kṛmibhirnarāḥ ।।

bhakṣyante tīvravadanairādeha prakṣayādbhṛśam ।
kṛmīṇāṃ nicaye kṣiptāḥ pūtimāṃsasya rāśiṣu ।।

tiṣṭhantyudvignahṛdayāḥ parvatābhyantarārditāḥ ।
sutaptavajralepena śarīramupalipyate ।।

adhomukhordhvapādāśca vṛtā stapyanti vahninā ।
vadanāntaḥ pravinyastaṃ suprataptamayoguḍam ।।

te khādanti parādhīnā hanyamānāśca mudgaraiḥ ।
ye devārāmapuṣpāṇi lobhātsaṃsṛhya pāṇinā ।।

jighranti mūḍhamanaso śirasā dhārayanti ca ।
āropyate śirasteṣāṃ sutaptairlohaśaṅkubhiḥ ।।

tataḥ kṣāreṇa dīptena tailatāmrādibhiḥ kramāt ।
śarīre ca mahāghorāścitrā narakayātanāḥ ।।

bahudhotpāṭyate jīhvā ye asatya priyavādinaḥ ।
saṃdaṃśena sutaptena prapīḍyorasi pādataḥ ।।

midhyāgamapravaktuśca jīhvā cāsya vinirgatā ।
krośārdhajīhvāvistīrṇairhalaistīkṣṇaiḥ prapāṭyate ।।

nirbhartsayantiye krūrā mātaraṃ pitaraṃ gurum ।
teṣāṃ vajrajalūkābhirmukhamādaśyate yataḥ ।।

tataḥkṣāreṇa tāmreṇa trapuṇā sicyate punaḥ ।
drutair āpūryate atyarthaṃ taptalohaiśca tanmukham ।।

itastataḥ punardhāvan baddhyate yamakiṅkaraiḥ ।
ye nindanti mahātmānamācāryaṃ dharmadeśikam ।।

viṣṇubhaktāṃśca sammūḍhāstaddharmaṃ caiha śāśvatam ।
teṣāmurasi kanthe ca jihmāyāṃ dantasandhiṣu ।।

tālunyoṣṭhe ca nāsāyāṃ mūrdhni sarvāṃgasandhiṣu ।
agnivarṇāssutaptāśca triśikhā lohaśaṅkavaḥ ।।

āropyante subahuśaḥ sthāneṣveteṣu mudgaraiḥ ।
tataḥ kṣāreṇa taptena tāmreṇa trapuṇā punaḥ ।।

taptalohādibhissarvairāpūryante samantataḥ ।
yātanāśca mahācitrāśśarīrasyāpi sarvataḥ ।।

niśśeṣanarakeṣvevaṃ bhramanti kramaśaḥ punaḥ ।
ye gṛhṇanti paradravyaṃ padbhyāṃ vipraṃ spṛśanti ca ।।

devopakaraṇāṃgaṃ ca jñānaṃ ca likhitaṃ kvacit ।
hastapādāghanaiste ṣāmāpūryante samantataḥ ।।

kṣāratāmrādibhirdhīptairdahyante kramaśaḥ punaḥ ।
narakeṣu ca sarveṣu vicitrā dehayātanāḥ ।।

bhavanti bahuśaḥ kaṣṭāḥ pāṇipādasamudbhavāḥ ।
pradattāṃ devadevasya tannāmnā pūjakasya vā ।।

padārdhināmathānyeṣāṃ haṭhādvṛttiṃ harantiye ।
te vai narakakūpeṣu pacyamānāssvakarmabhiḥ ।।

vrajantiyātanā bhūyo nātiyantiyāmāṅgaṇam ।
ye devāyatanārāmavāpīkūpamaṭhāṅgaṇam ।।

upadravanti pāpiṣṭhā nṛpāstatra vasanti ca ।
vyāyāmodvartanābhyaṅgasnānapānānnabhojanam ।।

krīḍanaṃ maithunaṃ dyūtamaśaucādyācaranti ca ।
te nadhairvividhairghorairikṣu yantrādipīḍanaiḥ ।।

nirayāgniṣu pacyante yāvadācandratārakam ।
devāyatanaparyante devārāme ca kutracit ।।

samutsṛjanti ye mūḍhāḥpurīṣaṃ mūtrameva vā ।
teṣāṃ śiśnaṃ savṛṣaṇaṃ hanyate lohamudgaraiḥ, ।।

sūcībhīrnetraparyantair agnivarṇaissakaṇṭakaiḥ ।
aropyante gude teṣāṃ yāvanmūrdhni vinirgataiḥ ।।

tataḥ kṣāreṇa mahatā tāmreṇa trapuṇā punaḥ ।
drutenāpūryate gāḍhaṃ gudaṃ śiśnaṃ ca dehinām ।।

manassarvendriyāṇāṃ ca yasmāduktaṃ pravartanam ।
tasmādindriyaduḥkhena jāyate tatsuduḥkhitam ।।

anna pānamadattaṃ yairmūḍhairnāpyanumoditam ।
dhane satyapi ye dānaṃ na ca yacchanti tṛṣṇayā ।।

atithiṃ cāvamanyante kālaprāptaṃ gṛhāśrame ।
tejohīnā raṇe baddhā hastapādānadhāritāḥ ।।

vistāritāṃgāśśuṣyanti tiṣṭhantyabdaśataṃ narāḥ ।
hastapādalalāṭeṣu kīlitā lohaśaṅkubhiḥ ।।

nityaṃ ca vikṛtaṃ vakraṃ kīlakadvayaghāṭitam ।
kṛmibhiḥprāṇibhiścograirlohatuṇḍaiśca vāyasaiḥ ।।

upadravairbahuvidhairmukhamantaḥ prapīḍyate ।
jihvā tataḥ prabhinnā ca gāḍhaṃ śṛṅkhalayā punaḥ ।।

tiṣṭanti laṃbamānāśca lohākārāssuvartulāḥ ।
tataḥ svamāṃsamutkṛṣya tilamātrapramāṇataḥ ।।

khādituṃ dīyate teṣāṃ sūcyagreṇa ca śoṇitam ।
yathā nirmāṃsatāṃ prāptāḥ kālena bahudhā punaḥ ।।

tataḥ kṣāreṇa dīptena taccharīraṃ pralipyate ।
bhidyante varṣa dhārābhiśśuṣyante vāyunā punaḥ ।।

punastailena sicyante sutaptena samantataḥ ।
iti citravidhairghorairmadhyamānāssvakarmajaiḥ ।।

mriyante naiva pāpiṣṭhā yāvatpāpasya saṃkṣayaḥ ।
tasmātpāpaṃ na kurvīta cañcale jīvite sati ।।

evaṃ kliṣṭā viśiṣṭāśca sāvaśeṣeṇa karmaṇā ।
tataḥ kṣitiṃ samāsādya jāyante dehinaḥ punaḥ ।।

sthāvarā vividhāḥ krūrāstṛṇa gulmādibheditaḥ ।
tatrānubhūya duḥkhāni jāyante kīṭayoniṣu, ।।

niṣkrāntāḥ kīṭayonibhyojāyante pakṣiṇaḥ kramāt ।
saṃkliṣṭāḥ pakṣibhevena bhavanti mṛgajātiṣu ।।

mārgaṃ duḥghamatikramya jāyante paśuyoniṣu ।
kramādgoyonimāsādya jāyante mānuṣe punaḥ ।।

vyutkrameṇāpi mānuṣyaṃ prāpyate puṇyagauravāt ।
tato manuṣyatāṃ prāpya tattatpāpānusārataḥ ।।

saṃyutāṃ pāpacihneśca vartante prāṇinastataḥ ।
devābhigamanam
snāto dhṛtordhvapuṇḍraśca prayataśśāntamānasaḥ ।।

avyagraścānyakāryeṣu gṛhītvā śaktitassvayam ।
phalādīnyupahārāṇi gandhān sumanasastathā ।।

hiraṇyaṃ harimuddiśya yena sarvāḥkṛtā ime ।
upahārādibhissamyagabhisacchejjagadgurum ।।

patraiḥ puṣpaiḥphalair vāpi yathāśakti samarpitaiḥ ।
ayatnasulabhenāpi toyenāpi sa tuṣyati ।।

pādacāryeva gacchettu devālayamatandritaḥ ।
aśakto apyatha vāśakta āḍhyo vā durvidho adha vā ।।

ādhirājye jagaddhāturadhikārī samassmṛtaḥ ।
na hi saṃharate jyotsnāṃ candraścaṇḍālaveśmani ।।

na vā saudheṣu samrājāṃ sudhādhārāḥ pravarṣati ।
bhogāyataname teṣā mekākāraṃ kaleparam ।।

anugṛhṇāti dātā tasya noccānaco vidhiḥ viṣṇupāramyam ।
devateha parañjyotireka eva paraḥ pumān ।।

sa eva bahudhā loke māyayā bhidyate svayā ।
viṣṇvākhyassa svayaṃ māyaṃ prakṛtiṃ vyajya sa dvidhā ।।

sthitastridhā ca sattvādiguṇabhedātpratīyate ।
viṣṇubrahmaśivākhyo asau sthityutpatyantakṛtsmṛtaḥ ।।

viṣṇvādyā mūrtayastasya dharmajñānādibhedataḥ ।
catasra eva vijñeyā vedavarṇa yugāśrayāḥ ।।

viṣṇuśca puruṣassatyo hyacyutaśchāniruddhakaḥ ।
pañcadhopaniṣadbhedānmahābhūtatvamāgataḥ ।।

manaśśrotrādibhiṣṣaḍbhiraṅgaiśca hṛdayādibhiḥ ।
ṣaḍakṣarātmako nityamṛṣibhiścaiṣa bhidyate ।।

saptavyāhṛtibhirlo kaiśchandobhiḥ kratubhistathā ।
saptadhā bhidyamāno asau vijñātavyo vicakṣaṇaiḥ ।।

aṣṭaprakṛtibhiścāsāvaṣṭamūrtibhireva ca ।
aṣṭākṣaramayo nityamaṣṭadhā caiṣa bhidyate ।।

nārāyaṇo nṛsiṃhaśca varāho vāmanastathā ।
rāmabrahmendrasūryāśca candrastairna vadhā sthitiḥ ।।

indro agniśṭa yamaścaiva nirṛtirvaruṇas tathā ।
vāyussomastatheśāno brahmānantaścate daśa ।।

ekādaśendriyairbhinnas tathā dvādaśamānapaiḥ ।
sa trayodaśadhā caiva viśvedevādibhiḥ sthitaḥ ।।

sa caturdaśadhā bhinno manubhiścākṣuṣādibhiḥ ।
tithibhiḥ pañcadaśadhā bhinno jñeyassu vai prabhuḥ ।।

svaraiṣṣoḍaśadhā bhinnodikkoṇāvāntaraistathā ।
mūrtyantaraiśca vijñeyo bahudhā tasya vistaraḥ ।।

ekadvitricatuḥpañcaṣaḍādyā viśvato mukhāḥ ।
mukhabhedāssamākhyātāstasya viśvātmano hareḥ ।।

dvyādayo viśvataḥpāṇerbhujabhedastathā smṛtāḥ ।
vividhābharaṇā dīrghā vividhāyudhadhāriṇaḥ ।।

mūrdhānaścaiva tasyoktā lasanmukuṭakuṇḍalāḥ ।
haimordhvapuḍralāvaṇyaprabhavā vakrakuntalāḥ ।।

smerāruṇādharāssaumyāḥ prasādāmṛtavarṣiṇaḥ ।
sahasraṃ pauruṣe sūkte pādāścākṣīṇyanekaśaḥ ।।

hiraṇyagarbho anekātmā vimalaśśyāma eva ca ।
nīlaḥ pītastathā rakto nānāvarṇaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।

candrasūryausmṛtau tasya nayane vāmadakṣiṇe ।
brahmāṇamāhurmūrdhānaṃ keśāṃścāsya vanaspatīn ।।

āsyaṃ vedāśca ye anantā toyaṃ rudhirameva ca ।
upajihvā tu tasyoktamupaśrutiśataṃ tathā ।।

bhruvormadhye tathā rudraṃ bhṛguṃ manasi saṃsthitam ।
rudrā ekādaśa jñe yā stasya kaṇṭhaṃ samāśritā ।।

nakṣatragrahatārāśca dantāssyurmaruto api ca ।
dharmādharmautathordhvādharoṣṭhau tu parikīrtitau ।।

indrāgnī tāluke tasya jihmācaiva sarasvatī ।
diśaśca vidiśaścaiva śrotrayontasya saṃsmṛtāḥ ।।

vāyuḥprāṇeṣu vijñeyassādhyāścāṃgulayaḥsmṛtāḥ ।
ṛṣayo romakūpeṣu sāgarā vastigocarāḥ ।।

nadyaśca vasudhā cāsya nāgāśca nalake sthitāḥ ।
jānusthāvaśvinau devau parvatāścorusaṃsthitāḥ ।।

guhyo asya guhyakā jñeyā vasavaścorasi sthitāḥ ।
nakhāgreṣu ca vijñeyā divyā oṣadhayas tathā ।।

nāsikāyāḥ puṭau jñeyāvayane dakṣiṇottare ।
ṛtavo bāhumūle tu māsāḥ karataleṣu ca ।।

lalāṭāgre tathā siddhā bhruvormeghāssavidyutaḥ ।
yakṣakinnaragandharvā daiteyā dānavāstathā ।।

rākṣasāścāraṇāścāsya jaṭharaṃ samusāśritāḥ ।
pitaraḥ pretakūśmāṇḍa vetālapramathāstathā ।।

pātālagocarāścāsya pāvayugmaṃ samāśritāḥ ।
pārśvayostasya vijñeyāḥkriyā vedairabhiṣṭutāḥ ।।

agnihotrādikarmāṇi varṇāśramahitāni ca ।
svāhāsvadhāvaṣaṭkā rāssarve asya hṛdaye śritāḥ ।।

nāmnāṃ śataṃ sahasraṃ vā tathānantaṃ paṭhantiyat ।
anantānantarūpasya yathāyogaṃ samanvitam ।।

mūrtayaścāsya sarvāstāssaṃkhyātītāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।
devādīnāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ mūrtayastatra saṃśritāḥ ।।

tasmādanantansaṃproktaḥ puṃsūkte tadudīritam ।
"sahasraśīrṣā puruṣassahasrākṣassahasrapāt'' ।।

brāhmaṇā mukhate yasya kṣatriyā yasya bāhutaḥ ।
ūruto yasya vai jātā vaiśyāśceti narā bhuvi ।।

candramā manaso jātaścakṣuṣormihiras tathā ।
mūkhādindras tathāgniśca prāṇādvāyurajāyata ।।

nābhyāyasyāntarikṣaṃ ca śiraso dyaurajāyata ।
padbhyāṃ bhūmirdiśaśśrotrādyasya devasya saṃbabhau ।।

tamīdṛśaṃ mahāviṣṇumaprameyamanāmayam ।
tatprasādādṛte jñātuṃ vaktuṃ vā naiva śakyate ।।

sarvadevamayo viṣṇuḥ sarve devāstadātmakāḥ ।
aśeṣaṃ vāṅmayaṃ cedaṃ lokālokaṃ carācaram ।।

vaiṣṇavyā vyāpyate śaktyā vāyunevadiśo antaram ।
sarve viṣṇumayādevāssarvaśāstreṣu kīrtitāḥ ।।

ādhārādheyabhāvena dvedhāsa vyāpya tiṣṭhati ।
sarvabhūtahitāyaiva niṣkalassakalaḥsthitaḥ ।।

niṣkalassakalaścaivaṃ jñeyo viṣṇussanātanaḥ ।
sarvataḥpāṇipādaṃ tatsarvato akṣiśiromukham ।।

sarvataśśrutimalloke sarvamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati, ।
sarvendriyaguṇābhāsaṃ sarvendriyavivarjatam ।।

asaktaṃ sarvabhṛccaiva nirguṇaṃ guṇabhoktṛ ca ।
avibhaktaṃ ca bhūteṣu vibhaktamiva ca sthitam ।।

bhūtabhartṛca tad jñeyaṃ grasiṣṇu prabhaviṣṇu ca ।
jyotiṣāmapi tajjyotistamasaḥ paramucyate ।।

jñānaṃ jñeyaṃ jñānagamyaṃ hṛdi sarvasya viṣṭhitam ।
taccādyo jagatāmīśaḥ pareśaḥ parameśvaraḥ ।।

parāvarasvarūpeṇa viṣṇussarvahṛdi sthitaḥ ।
sthūlasūkṣmaparatvena tridhā ca bhagavān sthitaḥ ।।

prabhaviṣṇurmahāviṣṇussadāviṣṇuḥ smṛtaśca saḥ ।
ātmā sa hyantarātmā ca paramātmā ca saṃsmṛtaḥ ।।

vairājaṃ laiṅgikaṃ caiva bahirantaśca sarvaśaḥ ।
śabdādiścinmayaṃ rūpaṃ jāgratsvapna suṣuptigam ।।

mantrānusvāranādeṣu trayamanveṣayedbudhaḥ ।
vede ca bhagavacchāstre sāṃkhye yoge tathaiva ca ।।

dharmaśāstre purāṇe ca munibhirdevamānuṣaiḥ ।
paṭhyate nikhilairnityaṃ viśvaṃ viṣṇumayaṃ jagat ।।

yacca bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyacca vartamānaṃ tu kiṃ cana ।
indriyāṇīndriyārthāśca bhūtāntaḥ karaṇāni ca ।।

avyaktaṃ triguṇā māyā vidyā dharmādayastathā ।
niyatiśca kalā kālaḥ sarvamanyacca tanmayam ।।

viṣṇureva paro devassarva bhūteṣvavasthitaḥ ।
sarvabhūtāni caivācau na tadastīha yanna saḥ ।।

devāsurādayo martyāḥ paśavaśca sarīsṛpāḥ ।
taruvallītṛṇauṣadhyo mahābhrāśanividyutaḥ ।।

śailābdhisaridārāmanagarāṇi sarāṃsi ca ।
lokāścāna ntakālo agni pretāvāsoragālayāḥ ।।

saptabhūrādayo brāhmaśaivavaiṣṇavasaṃjñitāḥ ।
sarve ca viṣṇunaikena vyāptāssarvātmanātmanā ।।

varāho bhārgavassiṃho rāmaśrīdharavāmanāḥ ।
aśvikṛṣṇau ca dikṣveṣāṃ lokairaṇḍaṃ sahākhilam ।।

yaccānuktamaśeṣeṇa viṣṇoretā vibhūtayaḥ ।
viśvavyāpitayevaiṣa viṣṇurvṛddhairudhīritaḥ ।।

purusaṃjñeśarīre asmin śayanātpuruṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
satyaśchābādhitārthatvānnityatvātsa prakīrtitaḥ ।।

acyuto acyavanādeva sa hariḥ samadīritaḥ ।
aniruddhastathā proktassarvasmādanirodhanāt ।।

vasanāstarvabhūteṣu vāsudevatvamīyivān ।
ādimūrtessamākṛṣṭaḥ smṛtassaṃkarṣaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।।

pradyumno dyumna pṛṣṭhatvāttridhāmā dhāmabhistribhiḥ ।
vaikuṇṭhāmalavarṇatvādvaikuṇṭhaśṭāyamucyate ।।

līyete pralaye tvasmin keśāvityeṣa keśavaḥ ।
naranārīprakartṛtvānnarāṇāṃ cāyanādayam ।।

nārāyaṇo naroddhānāmayanatvādapāñca saḥ ।
mādhavo madhuṣūtpattyā dhavatvādvā śriyaḥsmṛtaḥ ।।

govindatīti govindo gāvo vindanti yaṃ tathā ।
asuraṃ madhunāmānaṃ hantīti madhusūdana ।।

tribhiḥsvairvikramairvyāpto jagadeṣa trivikramaḥ ।
vāmano vrāsvatāyogācchrīdharo vahanācchriyaḥ ।।

hṛṣīkasyendriyasyeśo hṛṣīkeśa udīritaḥ ।
padmaṃ nābherabhūdyapya padmanābhastatasmmataḥ ।।

udarālambi dāmāsyetyukto dāmodaro hariḥ ।
