uttamaḥ puruṣoyasmāduktassa puruṣottamaḥ ।।

vilomendriyagamyatvātprocyate sa tvadhokṣajaḥ ।
ardhamardhaṃ larassiṃho narasiṃhā udāhṛtaḥ ।।

janārdanassa pāpiṣṭhān janānardayatīti saḥ ।
indrasyāvarajo bhūta upendraḥ procyate hariḥ ।।

haraṇātsarvapāpānāṃ harirnāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
karṣaṇātpāparāśīnāṃ kṛṣṇassarvātmako hariḥ ।।

rudro rodayate tasmāt brahmā bṛṃhaṇakarmaṇā ।
indraśca paramaiśvaryādvahanādvahnirucyate ।।

yamassaṃyamanātpuṃsāṃ varaṇādvaruṇastathā ।
vāyurvānātsavātsomar iśaśceṣṭe janeṣu yaḥ ।।

ādityo aditiputratvāccandraścandayate yataḥ ।
ityevaṃ guṇavṛttyohyaiḥ śabdereko apyanekathā ।।

śrutibhiḥ procyate brahma viṣṇvākhyaṃ jātu netarat ।
tasyeśvarasya caiśvaryātsarvametatpravartate ।।

seśvaraṃ hi jagatsarvaṃ bhavennānīśvaraṃ kvacit ।
tanmayatvena govinde nyastasarvabharā narāḥ ।।

tadyājīno mahābhāgāstaranti bhavavāridhim ।
taṃ prasādhayituṃ yatnaḥ kāryassarātmanā naraiḥ ।।

bhaktinamrassadā gacchetsarvo api jagataḥ patim ।
taddevasya priyaṃ bhūyādyatassammānanaṃ tu tat ।।

tasya sannihito devo yasya citte janārdanaḥ ।
dānena tapasā nānyaistyasya tuṣṭobhaveddhariḥ ।।

āruhya śakaṭaṃ gacchedyo viṣṇormandiraṃ naraḥ ।
nārī vā bālako vātha vṛddha ātura eva vā ।।

tasya puṇyaphalaṃ nāsti pretya yugyaśca jāyate ।
ye vāhayanti tānmartyānnarā vā prāṇinaśca ye ।।

te yāsyanti padaṃ viṣṇoryasmātpādaca rāstu te ।
ye vāhayanti jantūṃstān ste apimūḍhāḥ patanti vai ।।

yastodayati tāneva gamane mūḍhacetanaḥ ।
sa yāmīryātanāḥ prāpya todyate yamakiṅkaraiḥ ।।

punaḥ paśutvamāpannastodyate paśubhirnaraiḥ ।
yo vā bhṛtakadānena vāhanena tu mānavaḥ ।।

vāhayatyatha voheta so api yāsyati durgatim ।
apāre durgasaṃsāre karmabaddhe viśeṣataḥ ।।

svīyaṃ karma samutsṛjya patanti narake aśucau ।
tataḥpaśutvamāpannāściraṃ tiṣṭhanti bhūtale ।।

pādukāmadhiruhyāpi yo devālayamāprajet ।
sa paśurjoyate pretya rogī cehaprajāyate ।।

pādukāṃ vāhanaṃ cāpi yo adhiṣṭhitya vimūḍhadhīḥ ।
praṇāmaṃ haraye kuryātta sya dūrataro hariḥ ।।

devadarṇanamuddiśya naivedaṃ vidha āvrajet ।
ayatnādgamane jāte apyavaruhya ca vāhanāt ।।

pādukādi vimucyaiva samupaspṛśya vāriṇā ।
praviśetprayato bhūtvā prākāraṃ prathamaṃ punaḥ ।।

na viśeddhāma devasya yādatā vāhanādibhiḥ ।
tādṛśaṃ puruṣaṃ dṛṣṭvā yathāśaktyavabodhayet ।।

ādyastveṣo apacārassyādyatnahāryobhavettataḥ ।
śmaśānamadhye gatvātu yo gaccheddevatāgṛham ।।

saptajanmakṛtātpuṇyāttat kṣaṇānmucyate naraḥ ।
sārgālīṃ yonimāśritya pasejjanmatrayaṃ tataḥ ।।

daridrāścaiva mārkhāśca bhaviṣyanti trijanmakam ।
anyadevagṛhaṃ gadvāhyasnātvā yo vrajedgṛham ।।

devadevasya mohāttu tasya pāpaṃ mahādbhavet ।
gṛhādgṛhaṃ tathā gadvā bhikṣārthī kṣudhitassvayam ।।

bhikṣāmalabdhvā kutrāpi daridro jāyate naraḥ ।
catvāri caiva janmāni teṣāmante ca yo budhaḥ? ।।

caṇḍālayoni māpnoti janmāni daśa pañca ca ।
atra codāharantīmaṃ viśeṣaṃ kāśyapādayaḥ ।।

sarvadevamayo viṣṇussarvavedamayo hariḥ ।
tasyātiriktaṃ no kiñcidviśeṣastatra vakṣyate ।।

sarve apyadhikṛtā loke tattatkarmānurūpataḥ ।
ābrahmastaṃbaparyantaṃ jagadantarvyavasthitāḥ ।।

tasmādeva jagatsarvaṃ sargakāle prajāyate ।
tasminneva punastacca pralaye saṃpralīyate ।।

yaḥ varaḥ prakṛteḥ proktaḥ purāṇaḥ puruṣo avyayaḥ ।
sa eva sarvabhūtātmā nara ityabhidhīyate ।।

narājjātāni tattvāni nārāṇīti pracakṣate ।
tānyeva cāyanaṃ yasya sa tu nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

nārāyaṇaḥ paraṃ brahma tattvaṃ nārāyaṇaḥ paraḥ ।
viṣṇvādibhistathā kecidvāsudevādibhiḥ pare ।।

saṃjñābhedairmahātmānassadaivārādhayantitam ।
sarvatra paripūrṇasya sarvadhā sarvavastuṣu ।।

na jātu labhyate kiñcidyenāvyāptaṃ tu kiṃ cana ।
tasmāttasmin samāropya sarvaṃ deveśvareśvare ।।

upāsanaṃ bhavedyattu tadbhaveducitaṃ budhaiḥ ।
anyatra taṃ samāropya yadi copāsanaṃ bhavet ।।

tadbhavedanyadevārcā tasmātparimitaṃ phalam ।
ye apyanyadevatābhaktāyajante śraddhayo anvitāḥ ।।

yajante te api deveśaṃ tamevāvidhi pūrvakam ।
anye te brahmarudrendrāstadādyā devatāssmṛtāḥ ।।

vaiṣṇavā avatārāśca ye tu śāstroditāḥ purā ।
paramārthe na bhidyante nānyatvaṃ syātparasparam ।।

viṣṇvālayādathaikasmādanyaviṣṇvālayasya tu ।
tat sthānāṃ daivatānāṃ vā nānyatvaṃ jātu saṃbhavet ।।

atha śāstravidhirbhinno yatra nāpyupalabhyate ।
tatrānyatvaṃ vijānīyānna cecchecchāstrasaṃkaram ।।

hariṃ devaṃ tu saṃsevya vāhanasthaṃ dvijottamaḥ ।
yadanyaṃ sedate vīthyāṃ tatkāle vāhanasthitam ।।

so api pāpamavāpnoti viṣṇudhyānena śuddhyati ।
deveśasyotsavo yatra grāme vā nagare api vā ।।

parvatāgre mahānadyāstīre durgāṭavīṣuvā ।
tatra gacchennaro bhaktyā sevetotsavamādarāt ।।

saha puttressahāmātyaissarvaiḥ parijanairvṛtaḥ ।
vaiṣṇavaṃ kratudeśantu gatvā seveta mānavaḥ ।।

yathār'hamupayuñjīta svaśaktiṃ tatkriyāsu ca ।
śrutvā devotsavāraṃbhaṃ paṅgūbhāvena yo naraḥ ।।

tiṣṭhetsa janmasāhasraṃ paṅgureva bhaviṣyati ।
tadbhavedviphalaṃ janma bhūbhārastasya jīvitam ।।

deveśasyotsave samyagvartamāne mahāphale ।
yo anyatra vyāpṛtastatra na gaccheddurmanā naraḥ ।।

na tasya niṣkṛtiḥ proktā sa pāpī narakaṃ vrajet ।
anāhūto adhvaraṃ gacchettathā gurukulaṃ vrajet ।।

yo adhvaraṃ gantukāmo atra pratīkṣetārṅgaṇādikam ।
tanya pūrvārjitaṃ puṇyaṃ tat kṣaṇādeva naśyati ।।

devotsavaṃ tu yo martyo yatamānaṃ tu sevitum ।
vārayedyena kenāpi hetunā sa tu durmatiḥ ।।

aphalassaphalo vāpi patatyeva na saṃśayaḥ ।
viṣṇupañcadine vāpi puṇyāheṣvitareṣvapi ।।

upoṣitastu śrutvaiva deveśasyotsavaṃ haṭhāt ।
tat kṣaṇādyo na gacchettu tasya pāpaṃ mahadbhavet ।।

khaṭvāmāsthāya yaśśete vartamāne tadutsave ।
āsīnasthsita evātra sa yāmīryātanā vrajet ।।

deveśābhimukhaṃ gatvā na kuryādyo namaskriyām ।
sa pāpiṣṭhataro loke niṣkṛtirnāsya vidyate ।।

utkramiṣyanti yatprāṇāḥ prāṇade samupasthite ।
pratyudthānābhivādābhyāṃ punastān pratipādayet ।।

sarveṣāṃ prāṇabhūto asau bhagavān hariravyayaḥ ।
prāṇinaścetanāssarve prāṇyekaḥ prāṇado aparaḥ ।।

anyathā cenmahādoṣaḥ saṃkṣuphyante ca mānavāḥ ।
ekahastapraṇāmena yatpāpaṃ na tadanyataḥ ।।

hastau dvau nirmitau dhātrā kiṃ tena sukṛtaṃ bhavet ।
prāñjalīkṛtya hastautu yāceta madhusūdanam ।।

ya ekenaiva hastena praṇamenmandadhīrharim ।
tasyahasto bhavedekaḥ paścājjanmaśatairapi ।।

iha vai jāyate paṅgū rogī caiva na saṃśayaḥ ।
kimidaṃ bahulaiścitraiḥ karaṇairdehakalpanam ।।

yadyekaikaṃ na cettasya kaiṅkaryāyopayujyate ।
kiṃ svādhīnena hastena svādhīnaṃ karma sevitum ।।

aśaknu vānāssvātantṣahatāḥ pāpahatā hatāḥ ।
ekahastapraṇāmastu parihāryo viśeṣataḥ ।।

praṇataṃ caikahastena yastu pratyabhivādayet ।
tāvubhau narakaṃ yātastayoryasmātsamāgamaḥ ।।

devatāstādṛśaṃ mūḍhaṃ śapanti ca viśaṅkitāḥ ।
purastādyastu devasya kuryādātmapradakṣiṇam ।।

ātmanā sa bhavedvāpassa druhyedātmane budhaḥ ।
purastāddevabiṃbe tu devyamaṅgalavigrahe ।।

vartamāne tvanādṛtya na hyanyasya pradakṣiṇam ।
yatra mānasikārcā syāttacca mānasikaṃ bhavet ।।

antaryāmī ya evāste hṛdaye niṣkalo hariḥ ।
sa eva sakalo bhūtvā biṃbe yatsannidhāpitaḥ ।।

tasmātsakalapūjāyāṃ naiva kuryādvyatikramam ।
na kadāpi bhavetprājña ucbhiṣṭassveṣu karmasu ।।

viṇmūtraṃ pathi kṛtvātu śaucaṃ yāvanna cācaret ।
ucchiṣṭastāvadeva syādanarhassarvakarmasu ।।

nakharomāṇi yaścaiva keśāsthīni tathaiva ca ।
kṣipettu devatāgāre sa bhavedbrahmahā naraḥ ।।

mākṣikīṃ yonimśritya jāyate mriyate punaḥ ।
sapta janmāni tatraiva vrajennarakamastataḥ ।।

tāṃbūlaṃ carvitaṃ yastu prakṣipeddevamantire ।
sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।।

tato mukto mahāpāpī śunako aparajanmani ।
saṃsthitastrīṇi janmāni vasatyeva na saṃśayaḥ ।।

niṣṭhīvanakaro yastu mandire madhuvidviṣaḥ ।
kṛmibhakṣye patedghore narake pāpakṛnnaraḥ ।।

śleṣmātakatarurbhūtvā jāyate janmapañcakam ।
mūtrayenmandire yastu keśavasya vimūḍhadhīḥ ।।

sa mūtragartanarake patatyeva hyavākchirāḥ ।
tasmānmuktasturaktādiniṃbakadrumamāsthitaḥ ।।

janiṣyati na sandehassaptajanmasu saukarīm ।
purīṣaṃ vātra kurvīta yo naro bhagavadgṛhe ।।

sa yāti narakān ghorān paryāyeṇaikaviṃśatim ।
tato muktastu pāpātmā viṣṭhāyāṃ jāyate kṛmiḥ ।।

samīpe mandirasyāpi sakṛnmūtraṃ karoti yaḥ ।
sa tiṣṭhedraurave ghore varṣāṇāmayutaṃ śatam ।।

tato api manujo mukto grāmasūkarajātitām ।
grāme janmaśataṃ prāpya viṣṭhābhūsūkarastathā ।।

yastu retovisargaṃ ca kṛtvā kāmādakāmataḥ ।
asnāto devatāgāramiyātsadyassa naśyati ।।

yo yatra devatāgehe dantadhāvanamācaret ।
tathā nirlekhayejjihvāṃ sa pāpī naśyati dhruvam ।।

tailenābhyaktasarvāṅgaḥ kaṣāyodvartitastathā ।
yo naraḥpraviśedgehaṃ devasya paramātmanaḥ ।।

sa yāti gṛhagodhātvaṃ navajanmāni pañca ca ।
anugamya yathā pretaṃ yāti devālayaṃ tu yaḥ ।।

ārādhitumathecchedvāsa gacchennarāyutam ।
balibhugyonitāṃ yāti janmāni subahūni vai ।।

bharaṇaṃ tu tathā kṛtvā mṛtakasya viśeṣataḥ ।
mandiraṃ na praveṣṭavyaṃ praviṣṭastu praṇaśyati ।।

cāṇḍālīṃ yonimāśritya janmakṛnnava pañca ca ।
bhaviṣyati tathā bhūyaḥ pṛthak krūro atha niṣṭhuraḥ ।।

bhuktvāśrāddhaṃ paragṛhe yāyādviṣṇugṛhantu yaḥ ।
arcayedvā viśeṣeṇa caṭako jāyate khalaḥ ।।

tatra janmaśataṃ prāpya tato godhāvapurgataḥ ।
chāyāmākramya yo mohādyāti viṣṇostu mandiram ।।

pradakṣiṇamakurvanvā yastiṣṭhenmatipūrvakam ।
so apyucchiṣṭobhavenmūḍhastasya pāpaphalaṃ tvidam ।।

tiṣsetsa kānane śūnye kaṇṭakair bahubhirvṛtaḥ ।
phalapuhpādihīnaśca śmaśāne? śūnyavṛkṣatām ।।

yajña sūtramadhaḥkṛtya karṇe kṛtvā viśeṣataḥ ।
apasavyaṃ ca dhṛtvaiva dhṛtvā caiva nivītavat ।।

na gaccheddevatāgāraṃ na vā muktaśikho naraḥ ।
akacchaḥ pucchakacchaśca nagnaḥ kaupīnamātṛdhṛk ।।

riktahastaśśūnyaphālastyaktasaṃvyāna eva ca ।
khādannapi ca tāṃbūlamupahārādi bhakṣayan ।।

devālayaṃ viśennaiva tasya pāpaṃ mahadbhavet ।
durācāro hi puruṣo nehāyurvindate mahat ।।

trasyanti cāsya bhūtāni tathā paribhanantica ।
tasmādācāravāneva kuryādvaivaidikīḥ kriyāḥ ।।

api pāpaśarīrasya ācāro hantyalakṣaṇam ।
ācāralakṣaṇo dharmaḥ santaścāritralakṣaṇāḥ ।।

sādhūnāṃ ca yathāvṛttametadācāralakṣaṇam ।
apyadṛṣṭaṃ śravādeva puruṣaṃ dharmacāriṇam ।।

svāni karmāṇi kurvāṇaṃ taṃ janāḥ kurvate priyam ।
ye nāstikā niṣkriyāśca guruśāstrātilaṅghinaḥ ।।

adharmajñā durācārāste bhavantigatāyuṣaḥ ।
viśīlā dharmamaryādā nityaṃ saṃkīrṇamaithunāḥ ।।

alpāyuṣo bhavantīhanarā nirayagāminaḥ ।
loṣṭhamardī tṛṇacchedī nakhakhādī ca yo naraḥ ।।

nityocchiṣṭassaṃkusuko nehayurvindate kvacit ।
viṣṇusthānasamīpasthān viṣṇusevārthamāgatān ।।

śvapacān patitānvāpi spṛṣṭvā na snānamācaret ।
utsave vāsudevasya yaḥsnāti sparśaśaṅkayā ।।

svargasthāḥ pitarastasya patanti narake aśucau ।
pibetpādodakaṃ viṣṇorgurūṇāṃ vā viśeṣataḥ ।।

tatra nācamanaṃ kuryāttadvatsome dvijottamaḥ ।
anyadevārthasandiṣṭhaiḥ pūjayeyuśca ye harim ।।

saptajanmāni pañcāpi muḍūkatvaṃ vrajanti te ।
janmadvayantu vai mūḍhāśśūdratāṃ yānti te narāḥ ।।

kusumānāṃ nivedyāhaṃ gandhamāghrāti yo naraḥ ।
sa pūtigandhasaṃyuktaḥ kuṣṭhī caiva bhaveddhruvam ।।

tadante trīṇi janmāni tādṛśāni bhavantyuta ।
jātakaṃ mṛtakaṃ vāpi yasyāśaucaṃ vidhīyate ।।

anarhassarvakarmabhyo sa neyāddevatā gṛham ।
puṃprasūtau smṛtaṃ pūrvaissāpiṇḍyaṃ saptapūruṣam ।।

kanyakājanane tadvatsāpiṇḍantu tripūruṣam ।
vratināṃ satriṇāṃ tadvadyatīnāṃ brahmacāriṇām ।।

nāśaucaḥ kathyate prājñairyathā śātātapo abravīt ।
vratasaṃkalpamātreṇa vratitvaṃ vratino bhavet ।।

vṛtamātrastathartvikca satre satrī prakīrtitaḥ ।
kāṣāyadaṇḍamātreṇa yatitvañca yatermatam ।।

upanīto vasenmā vā tathā gurukule kramāt ।
brahmādhyeti nacādhyeti brahmacārī kumārakaḥ ।।

rājājñākāriṇāṃ tadvadrājñāṃ ca snātakasya car ।
idṛśānāmathānyeṣāmatrāstarbhāvar iritaḥ ।।

na kuryācca namaskāraṃ naiva pratyabhivādayet ।
nār'payedupahārāṃśca tīrthādīnnāpi sevate ।।

āśaucī brāhmaṇo yastu mohāddevaṃ prapūjayet ।
saptajanmasu dāridṣamatyantaṃ samavāpnuyāt ।।

śvānayoniśataṃ prāpya tataścaṇḍālatāmiyāt ।
yobhuktvā devatāgāre nikṣipyocchiṣṭamatra tu ।।

gacchedanyatra vā prāsyātsopi mūḍho vipadyate ।
yastu devagṛhadvāre prasārya caraṇau kvacit ।।

śete nidrāti sammohātsa yāti narakāyutam ।
punaśca janma saṃprāpya nīcayoniṣvanekaśaḥ ।।

yātanāścānubhūyeva daurbrāhmaṇyaṃ vrajettu saḥ ।
yastu devagṛhe mūḍhaśsayīta madamohitaḥ ।।

tatrocchiṣṭanidhānena bhṛśaṃ niśśvāsamārutaiḥ ।
durgandhī jāyate martyojāyate janmapañcakam ।।

tatassūkaratāṃ prāpya janmāni nava pañca ca ।
kliśyate bahubhiḥ kaṣṭairna śayīta harergṛhe ।।

upadhānādisahitaṃ ya stalpamadhitiṣṭhati ।
devālaye viśeṣeṇa prākāre vāpi mūḍhadhīḥ ।।

sa bhaveddurbhagaścaiva sarpayauniṣu jāyate ।
sapta pañca ca janmāni tato mānuṣatāṃ vrajet ।।

śayīta devatāgehe vyādhito yastu durmatiḥ ।
sa bhaveddurmanā dīno pretya ceha ca janmani ।।

yaḥstriyā sahito mūḍhaśśayīta bhagavadgṛhe ।
sa bhavedduritaṣṣaṇḍassaptajanmāni pañca ca ।।

yogibhiryogasiddhyarthamabhyasyante viśeṣataḥ ।
āsanāni tvasaṃkhyāni devāgāre na cācaret ।।

mantrayogaparaistadvallayayogaparāyaṇaiḥ ।
haṭhayogibhiretāni kriyante rājayogibhiḥ ।।

svastikaṃ sarvatobhadraṃ siddhaṃ siṃhāsanaṃ tathā ।
savyaṃ khūlaṃ sukhaṃ caiva gomukhaṃ garuḍaṃ tathā ।।

mayūraṃ matsyamatsyendraṃ maṇḍūkaṃ mudgaraṃ mṛgam ।
kuñjaraṃ kukkuṭaṃ nāgaṃ kāṣṭhaṃ kraiñcaṃ ca kūrmakam ।।

khaḍgaṃ ca kāmadahanaṃ vaiyāghraṃ veṇukāsanam ।
yonyāsanaṃ vāsakaṃ ca dhīraṃ padmāsanaṃ tathā ।।

vārāhaṃ caiva paryaṅkaṃ patagāsanameva ca ।
tripadaṃ hastikarṇaṃ ca hemamardhāsanaṃ tathā ।।

ityādīnā māsanā nāmaśītiśca turuttarā ।
anyāni śāstrasiddhāni yāni santi viśeṣataḥ ।।

tānyāsthāyi tu devāgreno patiṣṭheta buddhimān ।
bhuñjīyāddevatāgāre yaḥ pāpassa tu durmanāḥ ।।

kukṣirogārdito bhūtvā janmāni daśa pañca ca ।
tatassṛgālatāṃ prāpya pateddhi narake aśucau ।।

yo vā mūḍhamatirmohātkārayeddvijabhojanam ।
devāgāre viśeṣeṇa sa bhavennindito janaḥ ।।

garbhāgāre cāntarāle tathā caivārdhamaṇḍape ।
mahāmaṇḍapamadhye ca nānnamadyādviśeṣataḥ ।।

annaṃ pātre vinikṣipya puṭapatrādinirmite ।
āpośanaṃ tu kṛtvaiva yadadyādbhojanaṃ tutat ।।

na devatāprasādasya gṛhītasyāñjalau tathā ।
na caivāpośanaṃ kuryātkuryāccettadasammatam ।।

yastu pānīyapātrāṇi pītānyatra tu vinyaset ।
sa gacchennarakān krūrān yāvanta udabindavaḥ ।।

pātre tiṣṭhanti śaradastāvatīrnātra saṃśayaḥ ।
niveditaṃ tu devasya devasyāgre viśeṣataḥ ।।

pradadyāttu krameṇaiva varṇāśramavidhānataḥ ।
aśnantibhaktāssarve apigṛhītvaivāṃjalau punaḥ ।।

brahmaṇyadevamuddiśya puruṣaṃ brāhmaṇapriyam ।
nārāyaṇamanādyantaṃ viṣṇuṃ sarveśvareśvaram ।।

brāhmaṇān bhojayedyastu karmasādguṇyasiddhaye ।
tathā niṣkṛtiniṣpattyaiśāstroktena vidhānataḥ ।।

kārayennoktadeśeṣu kadāpi dvijabhojanam ।
yastvannaṃ dāpayedvipro dvijebhyo bhaktisaṃyutaḥ ।।

niveditaṃ tu devasya saṃtuṣṭyaisvasya tasya ca ।
tasya tuṣyati deveśa ādātā tu vipadyate ।।

dātustu sakalaṃ pāpaṃ manovākkāyakarmabhiḥ ।
bahuśassaṃcitaṃ pūrvamādātā samavāpnuyāt ।।

prasādo apihi devasya parapākaruciṃ naram ।
na jātu pāvayennaiva pāvayetpāvayenna tu ।।

yadṛcchālābhasaṃtuṣṭaṃ yathā bhaktavaraṃ tathā ।
mahimānaṃ prasādasya yo avajānāti mūḍhadhīḥ ।।

tena bhuktaṃ bhavetpāpaṃ dātureva na saṃśayaḥ ।
ayutaṃ brāhmaṇānāntu tarpayitvātu yatphalam ।।

tatphalaṃ naśyati kṣipramucchiṣṭasya kaṇena tu ।
athānnavikrayedoṣaḥ kathyate vidhivittamaiḥ ।।

annavikrayiṇaḥ pāpā vrajanti yamayātanāḥ ।
pretya sṛgālatāṃ yānti nava janmāni pañca ca ।।

yastvannaṃ bhagavadgehe vikrīṇāti viśeṣataḥ ।
caṇḍālo jāyate pretya kṣudhitaśca carenmuhuḥ ।।

vikrīṇate tu ye viprā vāṇijye dattacakṣuṣaḥ ।
ye apyannamupahārādi cetaraddevamandire ।।

te api yānti mahāghoraṃ narakaṃ bhṛśadāruṇam ।
yatra naivabhaveṣyanti pālīyāyodabindavaḥ ।।

kaṇamannasya vāna syāttapyante tatra te janāḥ ।
ye gṛhītvā tadannādi bhuñjate kṣudhitā janāḥ ।।

upakurvantiye vā tānucyante abhakṣyabhojanāḥ ।
annaṃ prāṇā manuṣyāṇāṃ sarvamanne pratiṣṭhitam ।।

annaṃ brahmātmakaṃ vindyādvindyādannamayīṃ tanum ।
annaṃ vikrīṇate ye tu prāṇavikrayiṇaḥ smṛtāḥ ।।

tasmātsarvaprayatnena tyajettatkraya vikrayau ।
na kuryāddevatā gehe abhyudayaṃ śrāddhabhojanam ।।

kuryānna cāpi śrāddhādīnvihāyāpi dvijāśanam ।
tasmātsarvaprayatnena nāśnīyāddharimandire ।।

mudhā saṃbhāṣate yastu praviśya harimandiram ।
sa nidhiṃ puratassiddhaṃ tyaktvā bhikṣati kākiṇīm ।।

yastu saṃbhāṣate vyarthaṃ devālayamupāśritaḥ ।
siddhamannaṃ parityajya bhikṣāmaṭati durjanaḥ ।।

yanmuhūrtaṃ kṣaṇaṃ vāpi paramātmāna cintyate ।
sā hānistanmamahacchidraṃ sā bhrāntissā tu vikriyā ।।

dasyubhirmuṣiteneva dagdheneva davāgninā ।
vyādhibhiḥpīḍiteneva cākṛṣṭeneva mṛtyunā ।।

bhītenevottamarṇena dharṣiteneva rājabhiḥ ।
magneneva mahāsiṃdhau hateneva ca vātyayā ।।

saṃpiṣṭeneva pāṣāṇairākrandedyassa mucyate ।
santyanekā pradeśāśca samayāśca viśeṣataḥ ।।

lokayātrāviniṣpattyai dehayātropayoginaḥ ।
tasmāddevagṛhaṃ gatvā naro nānyaparo bhavet ।।

yatprasaṃge harernāma tanmamahattvaṃ ca nāpyate ।
sa sarvo api mudhā proktomithyetyeke vadantitam ।।

na hi devasya purataḥ kvacidapyanṛtaṃ vadet ।
satyasvarūpī bhagavān satyaṃ tasmaina gūhayet ।।

satyameva paraṃ brahma satyameva paraṃ tapaḥ ।
satyameva paro yajñassatyameva paraṃ śrutam ।।

satyaṃ deveṣu jāgarti satyaṃ dharmataroḥ phalam ।
tapoyajñaśca puṇyaṃ ca devarṣipitṛpūjanam ।।

ādyo vidhiśca vidyā ca sarvaṃ satye pratiṣṭhitam ।
satyaṃ yajñantathā vedāssatyā devī sarasvatī ।।

vratacaryā tathā satyamoṅkārassatyameva ca ।
satyena vāyurāvāti satyenār'kaḥ prakāśate ।।

dahatyagniśca satyena yāyātsatyena sadgatim ।
parjanyo dharaṇībhāge satyenāpaḥ pravarṣati ।।

svādhyāyassarvavedānāṃ sarvatīrthāvagāhanam ।
satyaṃ tu vadato loke tulitaṃ syānna saṃśayaḥ ।।

aśvamedhasahasraṃ ca satyaṃ ca tulayā kṛtam ।
aśvamedhasahasrāttu bhārassatye viśiṣyate ।।

satyena devāḥ prīṇanti pitaro brāhmaṇāstathā ।
satyamāhuḥparaṃ dharmaṃ satyamāhuḥ paraṃ padam ।।

satyamāhuḥ paraṃ brahma tasmātsatyaṃ na lobhayet ।
ye satyaniratāssatyaśapathāssatyavikramāḥ ।।

mahatmāno muniśreṣṭhāste parāṃ siddhimāpnuvan ।
daivataissaha modante svarge satyaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

apcarogaṇasaṃkīrṇairvimānaissaṃcaranti ca ।
vaktavyaṃ ca sadā satyaṃ na satyādvidyate param ।।

agodhe vimale śuddhe satyatīrthe śucihrade ।
snātavyaṃ manasā yuktaistatsnānaṃ paramaṃ smṛtam ।।

devārthe vā parārthe vā putrārthe vā ātmane tathā ।
ye anṛtaṃ nābhibhāṣante te svargaṃ yāntimānavāḥ ।।

yassatyavādī puruṣo nānṛtaṃ paribhāṣate ।
saṃprāpya virajān lokānuṣitvā śāśvatīssamāḥ ।।

bhagavadbhaktimuktānāṃ jāyate śrīmatāṃ kule ।
sākṣiṇassantisarvete devatā bhāskarādayaḥ ।।

parīkṣante ca sarvāsu daśāsu puruṣaṃ sadā ।
na vācyamanṛtaṃ tasmātprāṇaiḥ kaṇṭhagatairapi ।।

ye anṛtaṃ bruvate mūḍhāśśapathāni ca kurvate ।
devāgāre viśeṣeṇa te praṇaśyanti sānvayam ।।

punarjanmaśataṃ yānti kīṭaḍayoniṣvanekaśaḥ ।
gītavāditranṛttādīn puṇyākhyānakathāśca ye ।।

lopayantyatha pāruṣyairmandire madhuvidviṣaḥ ।
te yānti narakaṃ pāpā jāyante nīcayoniṣu ।।

tathā te api durātmāno gārdabhīṃ yonimāpnuyuḥ ।
tathānte krūrā nava janmāni pañca ca ।।

anibaddhapralāpān ye kurvate devamandire ।
te api tittiritāṃ bhūtvā jāyante janmapañcakam ।।

devabhāṣāṃ parityajya deśabhāṣāsu yo naraḥ ।
stuvīta devatāgehe devasyāgre viśeṣataḥ ।।

tasya doṣomahānāśu naiva pūjāphalaṃ bhavet ।
asārāṇi tu śāstrāṇi bhūyāṃsi pṛthivītale ।।

yatra devasya mahātmyakathanaṃ na prapañcyate ।
teṣu śāstreṣu ye jātāśśāstrārthāśca viśeṣataḥ ।।

vādāśca prativādāśca saṃskārāssarva eva hi ।
citraśilpā na saṃdeho narastena na mucyate ।।

sā vidyā yā hariṃ stauti sā kriyā yattadarcanam ।
yā nyā yadanyadakhilaṃ duṣṭodarkā hi jīvikā ।।

na hi devagṛhaṃ gatvā śāstrārthairnī rasairnaraḥ ।
muhūrtaṃ kṣapayetkālaṃ taddevasya vimānanā ।।

viśālaṃ vāṅmayaṃ sarvaṃ sṛṣṭvā sraṣṭā hariḥ prabhuḥ ।
tadantassaṃpraviśyaiva vācyavācakabhedataḥ ।।

vijñānāya manuṣyāṇāṃ vijñānaghanavigrahaḥ ।
sadopakurute yasmātsarve bhaktavarāḥ sadā ।।

sarvā vāco vimucyānyāścintayānāśca sādaram ।
tanmahattvakathāgandhadaridraṃ vācanaṃ tathā ।।

pāṭhanaṃ lekhanādyaṃ ca naiva kuryādgṛhe hareḥ ।
sa bhavedakṣaradroṅī yastu kuryādvyatikramam ।।

druhyetsa vāṅmayāyāpi tasmādyuktataro bhavet ।
yastu devagṛhaṃ gatvā roditi praṇayādyathā ।।

duḥkhitaḥ stauti vā devaṃ tatsyānmānasikaṃ malam ।
nirvāṇaparamaṃ sthānaṃ mlānena manasā tu yaḥ ।।

sevate sa na jānāti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।
nārī vā puruṣo vāpi gatvā devagṛhaṃ kvacit ।।

na rodetpātayennāśru naivānyaṃ rodayedapi ।
yāvantyaśrūṇi rudatāṃ pateyurdevamandire ।।

tāvantyabdasahasrāṇi te vasanti yamālaye ।
anubhūya punastatra yātanāstīvracodanāḥ ।।

prāpya tit tiritāṃ kālaṃ vasiṣyanti ciraṃ bhuvi ।
naivātra hiṃsāṃ kurvīta prāṇināṃ duḥkhadāṃ kvacit ।।

ahiṃsā vaidikaṃ karma dhyānamindriyanigrahaḥ ।
tapo atha guruśuśrūṣā dharmadvārāṣṣaḍīritāḥ ।।

ahiṃsāpāśrayaṃ dharmaṃ dānto vidvān samācaret ।
trīdaṇḍaṃ sarvabhūteṣu nidhāya puruṣaśśuciḥ ।।

kāmakrodhau ca saṃyamya tataḥ siddhimavāpnu te ।
ahiṃsakāni bhūtāni daṇḍena vinihantiyaḥ ।।

ātmanassukhamanvicchan sa pretya na sukhī bhavet ।
ātmopamastu bhūteṣu yo vaibhavati pūruṣaḥ ।।

tyaktadaṇḍo jitakrodhassa pretya sukhamedhate ।
sarvabhūtātmabhūtasya sarvabhūtāni paśyataḥ ।।

muhyanti mārge devāśca hyapadasya padaiṣiṇaḥ ।
na tatparasya saṃdadhyātpratikūlaṃ yadātmanaḥ ।।

eṣa sāṃgrāhiko dharmaḥkāmādanyaḥ pravartate ।
prakhyāpane ca dāne ca sukhaduḥkhe priyāpriye ।।

ātmauvamyena puruṣaḥ pramāṇamadhigacchati ।
ṛṣayo brāhmaṇā devāḥ praśaṃsanti viśeṣataḥ ।।

ahiṃsālakṣaṇaṃ dharmaṃ vedaprāmāṇyadarṇanāt ।
karmaṇā na naraḥ kurvan hiṃsāṃ jātu vicakṣaṇaḥ, ।।

vācā ca manasā caiva tato duḥkhātpramucyate ।
caturvidheyaṃ nirdiṣṭā hyahiṃsā brahmavādibhiḥ ।।

ekaikato api vibhraṣṭā na bhavennātra saṃśayaḥ ।
yathā sarvaścatuṣpādvai tribhiḥ pādairna tiṣṭhati ।।

tathaiveyaṃ viśeṣeṇa kāraṇaiḥ procyate tribhiḥ ।
yathā nāgapade anyāni padāni padagāminām ।।

sarvāṇyevāpidhīyante padajātāni kaiñjare ।
evaṃ lokeṣvahiṃsā tu nirdiṣṭādharmataḥ purā ।।

na hyatassadṛśaṃ kiñcidihaloke paratra ca ।
yatsarveṣviha bhūteṣu dayāhiṃsātmikā tu yā ।।

na bhayaṃ vidyate jātu narasyeha dayāvataḥ ।
dayāvatāmime lokāḥ paratrāpi tapasvinām ।।

abhayaṃ sarvabhūtebhyo yo dadāti dayāparaḥ ।
abhayaṃ sarvabhūtāni dadatīti jagau śrutiḥ ।।

kṣataṃ ca patitaṃ caiva skhalitaṃ klinnamāhatam ।
sarvabhūtāni rakṣanti sameṣu viṣameṣu ca ।।

nainaṃ vyālamṛgā ghnanti na piśācā na rākṣasāḥ ।
mucyate bhayakāleṣu mokṣayedyo bhaye parān ।।

prāṇadānātparaṃ dānaṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati ।
na hyātmanaḥ priyakaraṃ kiṃ cidastīha niścitam ।।

aniṣṭaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ maraṇaṃ nāma kathyate ।
mṛtyukāle hi bhūtānāṃ sadyo jāyeta vepathuḥ ।।

vyādhijanmajarāduḥkhairnityaṃ saṃsārasāgare ।
jantavaḥ parivartante maraṇādudvijanti ca ।।

garbhavāseṣu pacyante kṣārāmlakaṭukai rasaiḥ ।
mūtrasvedapurīṣāṇāṃ paruṣairbhṛśadāruṇaiḥ ।।

jātāścāpyavaśāstatra chidyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
hanyamānāśca dṛśyante vivaśā ghātukā narāḥ ।।

kuṃbhīpākeca pacyantetāṃ tāṃ yonimupāgatāḥ ।
ākramya māryamāṇāśca trāsyantyanye punaḥ punaḥ ।।

nātmano asti priyatamaḥ pṛthivīmanusṛtya ha ।
tasmātrāṇeṣu sarveṣu dayāvānātmavān bhavet ।।

yena yena śarīraṇa yadyatkarmakaroti yaḥ ।
tena tena śarīraṇa tattatphalamupāśnute ।।

ahiṃsā paramo dharmastathāhiṃsā paro damaḥ ।
ahiṃsā paramaṃ dānamahiṃsā paramaṃ tapaḥ ।।

ahiṃsā paramo yajñastathāhiṃsā paraṃ phalam ।
ahiṃsā paramaṃ mitramahiṃsā paramaṃ sukham ।।

sarvayajñeṣu vā dānaṃ sarvatīrtheṣu vā plutam ।
sarvadānaphalaṃ vāpi naitattulyamahiṃsayā ।।

ahiṃsrasya tapo akṣayyamahiṃsro jayate sadā ।
ahiṃsrassarvabhūtānāṃ yathā mātā yathā pitā ।।

tasmādahiṃsrassatatamupavāsa vrataṃ caret ।
phalamaṅgirasāproktamupavāsasya vistarāt ।।

trirātraṃ pañcarātraṃ vā saptarātramathāpi vā ।
dhānyānyapi na hiṃseta yassa bhūyādahiṃsakaḥ ।।

nāśnāti yāvato jīvastāvatpuṇyena yajyate ।
āhārasya viyogena śarīraṃ paritapyate ।।

tapyamāne śarīre tu śarīre cendriyāṇi tu ।
tiṣṭhanti svavaśe tasya nṛpāṇāmiva kiṅkarāḥ ।।

niruṇaddhīndriyāṇyeva sa sukhī sa vicakṣaṇaḥ ।
indriyāṇāṃ nirodhena dānena ca damena ca ।।

narassarvamavāpnoti manasā yadyadicchati ।
evaṃ mūlamahiṃsāyā upavāsaḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।।

kāmānyānyānnaro bhaktyā manasecchati mādhavāt ।
vratopavāsanātprītastān prayacchatyasau hariḥ ।।
māse māse tathaikasminnekasminniyataṃ caret ।।
upavāsavratamidaṃ tasyānantaṃ phalaṃ bhavet ।
ekādaśyāṃ nirāhārassaṃpūjya harimavyayam ।।

tatpādasalilaṃ tadvattulasīṃ ca tadarpitāmā ।
pītvā ca bhakṣayitvā ca upavāsavrataṃ caret ।।

upavāsadine yastu tīrdhaṃ śrītulasīyutam ।
na prāśnīyādvimūḍhātmā rauravaṃ narakaṃ vrajet ।।

na hi devagṛhaṃ gatvā vivadeta naraḥ kvacit ।
na tat sthānaṃ vivādasya tasmāttaṃ dūrata styajet ।।

mano anavasthitaṃ yasya sa nālaṃ pūjitaṃ harim ।
yasyaiva nirmalaṃ cittaṃ sor'hassarveṣu karmasu ।।

rāgādyapetaṃ hṛdayaṃ vāgaduṣṭānṛtādinā ।
hiṃsādirahitaḥ kāyaḥ keśavārādhane trayam ।।

rāgādidūṣite cittaṃ nāspadaṃ kurute hariḥ ।
na badhnāti padaṃ haṃsaḥ kadācitkardamāṃbhasi ।।

na yogyā mādhavaṃ stotuṃ vāgduṣṭā cānṛtādinā ।
tamaso nāśanāyālaṃ meghacchannona candrayāḥ ।।

hiṃsādidūṣitaḥ kāyaḥ prabhavennārcane hareḥ ।
janacittaprasādāya yathā kāśastamovṛtaḥ ।।

manodoṣavihīnānāṃ na doṣassyātkathaṃ ca na ।
anyathāliṅgyate kāntā snehena duhitānyathā ।।

yateśca kāmukānāṃ ca yoṣidrūbe anyathā matiḥ ।
aśikṣayaiva manasaḥ prāyo lokaśca vañcyate ।।

lāletyudvijate loko vaktrāsava iti spṛhā ।
viśuddhaiḥ karaṇaistasmādvrajeddevagṛhaṃ naraḥ ।।

vivādaḥ krodhajo yasmāttasmāttaṃ parivarjayet ।
kruddhaḥ pāpaṃ na kuryātkaḥ kruddho hanyādgurūnapi ।।

kruddhaḥ paruṣayā vācā narassādhūnadhikṣipet ।
sādhusajjanasantāpaḥ sādhūnāṃ ca vimānanā ।।

dahatyāsaptamaṃ tasya kulaṃ nātra vicāraṇā ।
vācyāvācyaṃ prakupito na vicānāti karhi cit ।।

nākāryamaste kruddhasya nāvācyaṃ vidyate kvacit ।
yassamutpatitaṃ krodhaṃ kṣamayā tu nirasyati ।।

yathoragastvacaṃ jīrṇāṃ sa vai puruṣa ucyate ।
te mānyāḥpuruṣaśreṣṭhāḥ kṣamayā krodhamuddhitam ।।

nirvāpayante ye nityaṃ dīptamagnimivāṃbhasā ।
parāpavādaṃ na brūyānnāpriyaṃ ca kadā cana ।।

na manyuḥ kaścidutpādyo mahatāṃ devasannidhau ।
svayaṃ dattāvadhānastu devakārye viśeṣataḥ ।।

manyeta bhagavatsarge svātmānaṃ cāpyakiñcanam ।
sa eva bhagavān devassarvajñaḥ sarvaśaktiyuk ।।

sarveśassarvavitsarvonigrahānugrahe rataḥ ।
tasmānnānyasya jātvasti śaktiḥ krodhaprasādayoḥ ।।

iti saṃcintya bhūyo api sarveṣvapi ca jantuṣu ।
bhagavatsannidhau sthitvā ānṛśaṃsyaṃ prayojayet ।।

yadyadbhāvi bhavadbhūtaṃ vidyāttattasya ceṣṭhitam ।
yadyahaṅkāramāśritya svātantṣamadamohitaḥ ।।

nigrahe anugrahe vāpi śaktiṃ svasyāvabodhayet ।
sa yāti narakaṃ ghoraṃ na daivaṃ tasya mṛṣyati ।।

tathā strīṇāṃ viśeṣaṇa tyājyā syādatisaṃgatiḥ ।
devatāmandiraṃ prāpya kāleṣvanyeṣu vā tathā ।।

āyuryaśastapohāniḥ puṃsāṃ strīṣvatisaṃginām ।
puruṣeṣvatisaktānāṃ tulyā sā yoṣitāmapi ।।

kulīnā rūpavatyaśca nāthavatyaśca yoṣitaḥ ।
maryādāsu sa tiṣṭhanti sa doṣaḥ strīṣu garhitaḥ ।।

na strībhyaḥ paramanyadvai pāpīyastaramasti vai ।
striyo hi mūlaṃ doṣāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।।

samājñātānṛddhimataḥ pratirūpān va śesthitān ।
patīnantaramāsādya nālaṃ nāryaḥ parīkṣitum ।।

asaddharmastvayaṃ strīṇāṃ prāyeṇa hi bhavedbhuvi ।
pāpīyaso narān yadvai tyaktalajjā bhajantitāḥ ।।

strīyaṃ hi yaḥ prārthayate sannikarṣaṃ ca gacchatir ।
iṣacca kurute sevāṃ tamevecchanti yoṣitaḥ ।।

anarthitvānmanuṣyāṇāṃ bhayātparijanasya ca ।
maryādāyāmamaryādāḥ strīyastiṣṭhanti bhartṛṣu ।।

nāsāṃ kaścidagamyo astināsāṃ vayasi saṃsthitiḥ ।
rūpavantaṃ virūpaṃ vā pumānityeva bhuñjate ।।

na bhayānnāpyanukrośnānnār'thahetoḥ kathaṃ ca na ।
na jñātikulasaṃbandhāt tsriyastiṣṭhanti bhartṛṣu ।।

yauvane vartamānānāṃ mṛṣṭābharaṇavāsasām ।
nārīṇāṃ svairavṛttīnāṃ spṛhayanti kulastrīyaḥ ।।

yāśca śasvadbahumatā rakṣyante dayitāḥstrīyaḥ ।
api tāḥ saṃprasajjante kubjāndhajūvāmanaiḥ ।।

paṅguṣvanyeṣu kuṣṭheṣu ye cānye kutsitā narāḥ ।
strīṇāmagamyo loke asminnāsti kaśchidihodyate ।।

yadi puṃsāṃ gatistatra kathaṃ cinnopapadyate ।
apyanyonyaṃ pravartantena hi tiṣṭhanti bhartṛṣu ।।

duṣṭhācārāḥ pāparatā asatyā māyayā vṛtāḥ ।
adṛṣṭabuddhibahulāḥ prāyeṇetyavadhāryate ।।

alābhātpuruṣāṇāṃ hi bhayātparijanasya ca ।
vadhabandhabhayāccāpi svayaṃ guptā bhavanti tāḥ ।।

calasvabhāvā dussevyā durgrāhyā bhāvatastathā ।
prājasya puruṣasyeva yathā bhāvās tathā strīyaḥ ।।

nāgnistṛpyati kāṣṭhānāṃ nāpagānāṃ mahodadhiḥ ।
nāntakassarvabhūtānāṃ na puṃsāṃ vāmalocanāḥ ।।

rahasyamidamanyacca vijñeyaṃ sarvayoṣitām ।
dṛṣṭvaiva puruṣaṃ hyanyaṃ yoniḥ praklidyate striyāḥ ।।

kāmānāmapi dātāraṃ kartāraṃ mānasāntvayoḥ ।
rakṣitāraṃ na mṛṣyanti svabhartāramasat striyaḥ ।।

na kāmabhogān vipulān nālaṅkārārtha saṃcayān ।
tathaiva bahumanyante yathā ratyāmanugraham ।।

antakaḥ śamano mṛtyuḥ pātālaṃ baḍabāmukham ।
kṣuradhārā viṣaḥ sarpo vahnirityekataḥ striyaḥ ।।

etā hi svīyamāyābhirvañcayantīha mānavān ।
na cāsāṃ mucyate kaścitpuruṣo hastamāgataḥ ।।

gāvo navatṛṇānīva gṛhṇantyetā navaṃ navam ।
śaṃbarasya ca yā māyā yā māyā namucerapi ।।

baleḥ kuṃbhīnaseścaiva tāssarvāyoṣito viduḥ ।
hasantaṃ prahasantyetā rudantaṃ prarudanti ca ।।

apriyaṃ priyavākyaiśca gṛhṇate kālayogataḥ ।
yadi jihmā sahasraṃ syājjīvecca śaradāṃ śatam ।।

ananyakarmā strīdoṣānanuktvā nidhanaṃ vrajet ।
uśanā veda yacchāstraṃ yacca veda bṛhaspatiḥ ।।

strībuddhyā na viśiṣyeta surakṣyā na bhavantitāḥ ।
anṛtaṃ satyamityāhussatyaṃ cāpi tathānṛtam ।।

iti yāstāḥ kathaṃ rakṣyāḥ puruṣairdurbharāḥ striyaḥ ।
saṃpūjyamānāḥ puruṣairvikurvanti mano nṛṣu ।।

apāstāśca tathā sadyo vikurvanti manaḥ striyaḥ ।
na ca strīṇāṃ kriyāḥ kāściditi dharmo vyavasthitaḥ ।।

nirindriyā hyaśāstrāśca strīyo anṛtamiti śrutiḥ ।
śayyāsanamalaṅkāramanna pānamanāryatām ।।

durvāgarbhavaṃ ratiṃ caiva dadau strībhyaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
na tāsāṃ rakṣaṇaṃ śakyaṃ kartuṃ puṃsāṃ kathaṃ cana ।।

api viśvakṛtā caiva kutastu puruṣairiha ।
vācā ca vadhabandhairvā kleśairvā vividhaistathā ।।

na śakyā rakṣitāṃ nāryastā hi nityamasaṃyatāḥ ।
avidvāṃsamalaṃloke vidvāṃsamapi vā punaḥ ।।

pramadāhyutpathaṃ netuṃ kāmakrodhavaśānugam ।
nātaḥ paraṃ hi nārīṇāṃ vidyate ca kadā cana ।।

yathā puruṣa saṃsargaḥ parametatphalaṃ viduḥ ।
ātmacchandena vartante nāryo manmathacoditāḥ ।।

na ca dahyanti gacchantyaḥ sutaptairapi pāṃsubhiḥ ।
nānilo agnirna varuṇo na cānye tridaśāntathā ।।

priyāḥ strīṇāṃ yathā kāmo ratiśīlā hi yoṣitaḥ ।
sahasrekila nārīṇāṃ prāpyetaikā kadā cana ।।

tathā śatasahasreṣu yadi kācitpativratā ।
naitā jānanti pitaraṃ na kulaṃ na ca mātaram ।।

na bhrātṝnna ca bhartāraṃ na ca putrān na devarān ।
līlāyantyaḥ kulaṃ ghnanti kūlānīva saridvarāḥ ।।

strīṣvāyāsasametasya ye puṃsaśśakrabindavaḥ ।
na te sukhāya mantavyāḥ svedajā iva bindavaḥ ।।

kṛmibhistudyamānasya kuṣṭhinaḥ pāmanasya vā ।
kaṇḍūyanāgnitāpābhyāṃ yatsukhaṃ strīṣu tadviduḥ ।।

yādṛśaṃ vidyate saukhyaṃ kaṇḍūpūyavinirgame ।
tādṛśaṃ strīṣu vijñeyaṃ nādhikaṃ tāsu vidyate ।।

granthestu vedanā yadvat sphuṭitasya nivartane ।
tadvat strīṣvapi vijñeyaṃ na saukhyaṃ paramārthataḥ ।।

varcomūtravisargāttu sukhaṃ bhavati yādṛśam ।
tādṛśaṃ strīṣu vijñeyaṃ nādhikaṃ tāsu vidyate ।।

na cāṇumātramapyeve sukhamasti vicārataḥ ।
tathā devotsavādīnāṃ sevā tāsāṃ niṣidhyate ।।

na hi svatantrato yoṣijjātu gacchet sthalāntaram ।
na hi nirmimate vṛddhā līlayā devamandirān ।।

kāmukānāṃ vilāsārthaṃ tasmādyuktataro bhavet ।
anugacchetpitā bhrātā bhartā putro atha vā yadi ।।

tadā devagṛhaṃ yāyānnānyathā jātu kāminī ।
dhyāyato viṣayān puṃsassaṃgasteṣūpajāyate ।।

saṃgātsaṃjāyate kāmaḥ kāmātkrodho abhijāyate ।
krodhādbhavati sammohassammohātsmṛtivibhramaḥ ।।

smṛtibhraṃśādbuddhināśo buddhināśātpraṇaśyati ।
balavānindriyagrāmo vidvāṃsamapikarṣati ।।

tasmāt strīyā bhavedvidvānnātisaktaḥ kathaṃ cana ।
tasmāt strīṣu na kartavyaḥ prasaṃgo devatākṛhe ।।

tathaiva paradārebhyo manaḥ prahiṇuyānna ca ।
paradārā na gantavyā narairṛddhimabhīpsubhiḥ ।।

na hīdṛśamanāyuṣyaṃ loke kiṃ cana vidyate ।
yādṛśaṃ puruṣasyeha paradāraniṣevanam ।।

tādṛśaṃ vidyate kiñci danāyuṣyaṃ nṛṇāmiha ।
yāvanto romakūpāḥ syuḥ strīṇāṃ gātreṣu nirmitāḥ ।।

tāvadvarṣasahasrāṇi narakaṃ paryupāsate ।
atisaṃgaṃ tyajettasmādyoṣitāṃ devamandire ।।

yairasabhyaḥ padairarthaḥ padenaikena vā tathā ।
gamyate kathanaṃ tādṛgaślīlaṃ parivarjayet ।।

aślīlakathanāccaiva bhavedudvejanaṃ nṛṇām ।
bhaktānāṃ bhagavadgehe bhaveccittamathāvilam ।।

nivarteta manastatra niviṣṭaṃ paramātmani ।
tasmādaślīlamābhāṣṭa naraḥ pāpaparo bhavet ।।

sa tu caṇḍālatāṃ prāpya jāyate janmanāṃ śatam ।
artona praviśedgehaṃ devasya paramātmanaḥ ।।

vāyubhūte śarīre asmin vāyusaṃcārakarmaṇi ।
malavāyuvisargastu devagehe viśeṣataḥ ।।

pātayetpuruṣaṃ satyamapi vedāntapāragam ।
tasmādapānagandhasya visargaṃ naiva cācaret ।।

atha vāyunirodhetu vyādhikopo bhaviṣyati ।
tasmādvāyuvisargaṃ tu kuryādevāvicārayan ।।

iti devagṛhaṃ gantuṃ vyādhito naiva cārhati ।
tathā kuṣṭhī viśeṣeṇa pāparogārditāssame ।।

udvīkṣituṃ ca deveśaṃ mandire madhusūdanam ।
arcituṃ sevituṃ cāpi dātuṃ dravyacayaṃ tathā ।।

nārhantiyasmāttatsaktaṃ pāpaṃ sāṃkrāmikaṃ bhavet ।
yadyanyathā bhavetsadyassa pāpī saṃprajāyate ।।

janmāni nava pañcāpi jāyate malabhuk kṛmiḥ ।
yadā viśedgṛhaṃ viṣṇossevārdhaṃ madhuvidviṣaḥ ।।

kṛtvopavītavatsamyaguttarīyaṃ manoharam ।
seveta devadevaśamupavītaḥ sadā śuciḥ ।।

kañcukenāvṛtāṅgastu na gaccheddharimandiram ।
naivābhivādanaṃ kuryānnābhivādyaḥ sa uccate ।।

uṣṇīṣī na ca seveta naiva pāṇau dhṛtāyudhaḥ ।
vastreṇācchādya dehantukambalenetareṇa vā ।।

yogacchedvaiṣṇavaṃ dhāma yo vāpi praṇameddharim ।
śvitrī saṃjāyate mūḍho navajanmāni pañca ca ।।

kṣaumādibhirvā saṃvīto yo naraḥpraṇameddharim ।
caṇḍālayonitāṃ yāti nava janmāni pañca ca ।।

na jātu tvamitabrūyādāpannopi mahattaram ।
tvaṅkāro vā vadho veti vidvatsu na niśiṣyate ।।

paranindā parasyaiva puṃso nindā bhaviṣyati ।
paranindā ca śāstrasya parasya tu vinindanam ।।

paranindā bhavetkrodhātkrodhātsadyo vinaśyati ।
nindayā vai pareṣāṃ tu ninditāste punassmṛtāḥ ।।

tasmānnidāṃ pareṣāṃ tudevāgre parivarjayet ।
tathā parastutiṃ caiva vidhinā saṃtyajennaraḥ ।।

paraḥ parātmā puruṣaḥ purāṇaḥ procyate tu yaḥ ।
tadagre anyasya devasya na stutiṃ stāvayennaraḥ ।।

yastu sarveśvarādanyamadhikaṃ tasya cāgrataḥ ।
pūjayedyadi manyeta pūjārhaṃ vāsa naśyati ।।

sarvaṃ jagacca tasyaiva svarūpaṃ paramātmanaḥ ।
tathāpi tattadrūṣeṇa tāratamyajuṣā punaḥ ।।

pūjyate bhagavān bhaktaistatra śāstroditā gatiḥ ।
tasmāddeveśvarādanyadyatkiñcitthsāṇu jaṅgamam ।।

pūjārhaṃ vidyate vastu taddhāmani viśeṣataḥ ।
tasmātpūjāṃ stutiṃ cānyāmitareṣāmasaṃśayam ।।

tyajeddevagṛhe yastu sukhaṃ manyeta jīvitum ।
śaktau satyāṃ viśeṣeṇa yastulobhādinā naraḥ ।।

gauṇairarcayate viṣṇamupacārairudīritaiḥ ।
na tasya vidyate puṇyaṃ sa tūcchāstraṃ vravartate ।।

yāvatā kīrtyateśāstre phalamāḍhyadaridrayoḥ ।
tattacchaktyarpitaireva yathārhaṃ ca dhanādikaiḥ ।।

yathā tuṣyatideveśo muktāhāreṇa bhūbhujām ।
tathaiva tulasīdāmnā durvidhasyāpi tuṣyati ।।

tasmātkurvīta yatnena śaktilobhaṃ na jātu cit ।
anyathā yadi kurvāṇaḥ phalaṃ naiva prapadyate ।।

pretya mārjāratāṃ prāpya jāyate janmapañcakam ।
viṣaṃ prāśnāti sammūḍho yassvasmai pacate naraḥ ।।

yo adyādannaṃ kaṇaṃ vāpi yadviṣṇoraniveditam ।
sa bhavedbrahmahābhūyaḥ sa bhuṅktepūyaśoṇitam ।।

yatpibecca yadaśnīyāt yaccajighrecca dhārayet ।
anuliṃpecca yattattannivedyāgre madhudviṣe ।।

tanniveditaśeṣaṃ tu bhuñjīyādvopayojayet ।
viṣṇorniveditaṃ yastu na bhuṅkte manujādhamaḥ ।।

kalpakoṭiśatenāpi niṣkṛtirnāsya vidyate ।
niveditaṃ tu yadviṣṇorbhaktebhyastasya dāpanāt ।।

prīyat bhagavān devastatparastu bhavennaraḥ ।
niveditaṃ yadi brūyāducchiṣṭamiti mandadhīḥ ।।

sa tu durgatimāsādya vindate yamayātanāḥ ।
vibhūtiṃ samupāśritya yasyānantasya śāśvatam ।।

samṛddhā dharaṇī seyaṃ saśailavanakānanā ।
yā ca bhūyāṃsi loke asminnutpādayati santatam ।।

oṣadhīrnikhilā stadvatpuṣpāṇi ca phalāni ca ।
tasyānṛṇyasyahetorvaiya teta vidhinā naraḥ ।।

yastu nār'payate viṣṇostattatkālodbhavāni tu ।
sasyāni cauṣadhīstadvatphalāni kusumāni ca ।।

saṃbhṛtāni yathāśakti sabhavedbrahmah naraḥ ।
navāni kāle jātāni sasyādīni viśeṣataḥ ।।

dhyāyanti devadeveśamabhigantuṃ yatanti ca ।
kadarthayantoye mūḍhāsteṣāmabhyarthanaṃ param ।।

audāsīnyena tiṣṭhanti svayaṃ vāpyupayuñjate ।
teyāntinarakān ghorān kṛtaghnā yāntiyān bahūn ।।

śapantyauṣadhayassarvāstasmādbhaktyā viśeṣataḥ ।
navaṃ sasyaṃ phalaṃ puṣpaṃ dadhikṣīraṃ ghṛtaṃ madhu ।।

yadarhamarpaṇe sarvamagre tasmai samarpayet ।
lobhānmohādathājñānādya ucchiṣṭaṃ nivedayet ।।

deveśāya viśeṣeṇa sa bhavetpātakī naraḥ ।
ucchiṣṭa manyadevasya yo devāya nivedayet ।।

so api caṇḍālatāṃ prāpya naśyedeva na saṃśayaḥ ।
niveditaṃ tu devasya ya ucchiṣṭena yojayet ।।

devānāmita reṣāṃ vā manuṣyāṇāmathāpi vā ।
sa pāpī janmasāhasraṃ śvānayoniṣu jāyate ।।

na hi devagṛhaṃ gatvā pṛṣṭī kṛtyāsanaṃ caret ।
devābhimukha eva syādbhaktassarvātmanānaraḥ ।।

na pṛṣṭhaṃ darśayejjātu devāgre hitacintakaḥ ।
pārśvatastu caranneva nivartetālayaṃ prati ।।

naivānyaṃ praṇamejjātu praviśya harimandiram ।
sa hi sarveśvara śśeṣī yastatrāste ramādhavaḥ ।।

pūjārhaśca praṇāmārhaḥ pūjārhastatra netaraḥ ।
yastathā praṇamenmūḍhassa yāti narakāyutam ।।

caṇḍālayonimāsādya bhajate yātanā muhuḥ ।
yastu devagṛhaṃ prāptān vaiṣṇavān bhagavatpriyān ।।

ācāryamṛtvijaścātha pūjakān paricārakān ।
nār'cayenmaunamāsthāya sa vinaśyati sānvayaḥ ।।

yadiṣṭaṃ yājakebhyassyātpūraṇāyeva tasyatu ।
bhaktāḥ paricareyuśca viśeṣādgrāmavāsinaḥ ।।

anyathā cenmadoṣassarveṣāṃ ca vipacadbhavet ।
atmānaṃ yo viśeṣeṇastautyahaṅkāra bhāvidaḥ ।।

anādṛtya gurūn daivamanibaddhaṃ ca saṃpadet ।
avalīptona jānāti doṣamātmani saṃgatam ।।

kulavidyātapassampatpramukhairgarvite naraḥ ।
na sukhaṃ na ca saubhāgyaṃ yenātmāntūyate svayam ।।

tasmādātmastutiṃ kṛtvā naraḥ patati niścayam ।
tato janmaśataṃ prāpya mṛgayonau viśeṣataḥ ।।

jāyate mriyate abhīkṣṇaṃ tasya pāpaṃ mahadbhavet ।
yasdevagṛhaṃ gatvā vāñchatyapacitiṃ janaḥ ।।

sa tu tit tiritāṃ yāti navajanmāni pañca ca ।
deveśasyatu sevārthaṃ varṇānāmānupūrvyaśaḥ ।।

adhikāraḥ samākhyātastatkramaṃ na vimānayet ।
viśanti garbhagehetu ye vaikhānasasūtriṇaḥ ।।

garbhāgāre praveṣṭavyo na hyavaikhānasaḥ kvacit ।
antarāle tathā yeṣāṃ sthānaṃ tattu pravakṣyate ।।

anye dvijāśca tiṣṭhanti yathā syādāśramakramaḥ ।
te dvijāstat strīyaścāpi sevante tatra saṃgatāḥ ।।

kṣatrajātā viśeṣaṇa sthitvā caivār'dhamaṇḍape ।
deveśamabhisevante tadīyā yāśca yoṣitaḥ ।।

saṃgatāśśūdrajātāśca pratilomabhavāścaye ।
mahāmaṇḍapamāsthāya sevante puruṣottamam ।।

anulomabhuvaścaivaye cānye mlecchajātayaḥ ।
gopurādbāhyataḥ sthitvā sevante mandiraṃ hareḥ ।।

tāratamyamidaṃ jñātvā seveta satataṃ harim ।
devatānindanaṃ kuryādyassa pāpīna mucyate ।।

anyadevasamaṃ yastu manyate puruṣottamam ।
caṇḍālayonitāmeti nava janmāni pañca ca ।।

apahnutya punardevāṃ staddravyādi harettu yaḥ ।
sa bhaveddevahā satyaṃ jāyate śvādiyoniṣu, ।।

tiraskṛtya tathā devān bhagavacchāstrameva ca ।
karmāṇi svecchayā kuryātso api syāddevahā naraḥ ।।

kathāyāṃ kathyamānāyāṃ devasya madhuvidviṣaḥ ।
anādṛtya ca ye yānti te narāḥ pāpakāriṇaḥ ।।

toyahīne atiraudre ca vane vai śūnyavṛkṣatām ।
jāyante saptajanmāni tataścaṇḍālatāṃ yayuḥ ।।

deveṣu goṣu vipreṣu devāgāreṣu caiva hi ।
vahennaivādhipatyaṃ yannāsāvṛddhimavāpnuyāt ।।

doṣāśca bahulā stasminnādhipatye smṛtā budhaiḥ ।
kāmato akāmataścāpi sarvaṃ tasya viceṣṭitam ।।

pāpāyaiva bhavettasmādbhūtikāmastu taṃ tyajet ।
sevārthināṃ sakāśāttu balātkāreṇa yaḥ prabhuḥ ।।

gṛhṇīyāttukaraṃ sadyaḥ patetsa saha tena ca ।
devasya sannidhau bhaktairbhaktyāyattu samarpyate ।।

patraṃ phalaṃ vā mūlaṃ vā svarṇaṃ vāsāṃsi cetarat ।
dāyādyamarcakānāṃ tu yo mohādapanihnute ।।

svayaṃ vāpyupayuñjīta sa pāpī narakaṃ vrajet ।
viśrāṇayanti haraye yadbhaktā bhaktibhāvitāḥ ।।

tannāmnā pūjakāneva jānanti phalabhāginaḥ ।
sthirajaṅgamayoḥ pūjā yatassampāditā bhavet ।।

tasmādbhagavato nāmnā dattaṃ yaddevamandire ।
vihāyābharaṇādīni vāsāṃsyanyatparicchadam ।।

devālaṅkārayogyāni mūlyavanti viśeṣataḥ ।
arcakā eva gṛhṇīyuḥ pratibadhnīta netaraḥ ।।

yastvadhīkāragarveṇa devāgāramupāśritaḥ ।
akāle sevituṃ cecchetso api yāsyati durgatim ।।

atha vā sevituṃ cecchetkāraṇenāpi kena cit ।
ukteṣveva tu kāleṣu seveta matimānnaraḥ ।।

antyārcanāvasāne yat kavāṭo badhyate tataḥ ।
punarudghāṭanaṃ yāvatpratyūṣe ca bhaviṣyati ।।

tāvannaiva hariṃ sevedakālassa viśeṣataḥ ।
pratyūṣādyantyakālāntapūjane api tu mantrataḥ ।।

tattatkāle kavāṭasya bandhane vihite api ca ।
na tadā tāvatī hāniravabaddhe apyamantrakam ।।

athār'canārhakālepi bhaktānāṃ sevanāya tu ।
akālā bahavaḥ proktāstathā yavasikoditā ।।

tasmādakālasevāṃ tu vidhinā parivarjayet ।
viṣayākrāntacittānāṃ viṣṇvarcanamakurvatām ।।

karmabhūmau nṛṇāṃ janma karmāpi vibhalaṃ dhruvam ।
yo gurau mānuṣaṃ bhāvaṃ śilābhāvaṃ ca daivate ।।

mantreṣu jīvikābhāvaṃ hiṃsābhāvaṃ makheṣu ca ।
pūjakeṣu ca pūjāyāṃ nīrasaṃ bhāvameti saḥ ।।

sarvadhā ninditavyo hi jīvitaṃ tasya niṣphalam ।
kṣamāmantraḥ
atha vakṣye viśeṣaṇa kṣamāmantravidhiṃ param ।।

apacāreṣu sarveṣu yaṃ japtvā mucyate naraḥ ।
aparādhaḥ kṛto yena jānatā svavaśena saḥ ।।

kṣamāmantrasahasrasya jāpenāpi na mucyate ।
kṣamāmantrastvaśeṣāghadhvaṃsanakṣama ucyate ।।

"nārāyaṇa namaste astu namo bhaktaparāyaṇa ।
namo namo namaste astu namaste astu namo namaḥ ।।

ajñānādarthalobhādvā rāgāddveṣātpramādataḥ ।
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

saṃdhyayośca divā rātrau jāgratsvapnasuṣuptiṣu ।
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

kāyena manasā vācā sarvairvāpi samuccitaiḥ ।
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

tiṣṭhatā prajatā caiva śayyāsanagatena ca ।
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

snāsyatā japatā vāpi yajatā juhvatā mayā ।
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

bhujatā dhyāyatā nūnaṃ viṣayānupasevatā ।
aparādhāḥ kṛtā ye tān kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

mayā vā majjanairvāpi mama bandhubhirevavā ।
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

rājñā vā tadamātyairvā rājabhṛtyairathāpivā ।
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

ācāryeṇār'cakenāpi bhaktairvāparicārakaiḥ ।
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

gāyakairnartakairvātha vāditrāṇāṃ ca vādakaiḥ ।
aparādhaḥ kṛto yastaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

praṇavādivisargāntaṃ kriyāsu vidhipūrvakam ।
amantramarcane doṣaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

uddhānācchayanā ntantu kriyāsu vividhāsu ca ।
śraddhālopakṛtaṃ doṣaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

kaśśaknotyarcituṃ devaṃ tvāmanādyantamavyayam ।
tasmādajñānacaritaṃ kṣamasva puruṣottama ।।

prārthaye devadevaṃ tvāṃ prasīda bhagavanmayi ।
prasīdatu ram mahyaṃ tava vakṣaḥsthalālayā ।।

iśānā jagato devī mātā nityānapāyinī ।
prasīdantu surāḥ sarve prasādādyuvayormayi ।।

svastyastu kṛpayāsmākaṃ yuvayoḥ suprasannayoḥ ।
upacārāpadeśena kṛtānaharaharmayā ।।

apacārānimān tsarvān kṣamasva puruṣottama ।
iti vijñāpayedbhūyo bhaktisādhvasabhāvitaḥ ।।

tadarthanātparaṃ prītaḥ prasīdati khagadhvajaḥ ।
kṣamāmantramimaṃ deyānna cāśuśrūṣave kvacit ।।

guhyādguhyatamo gopyassarvadā gurubhiḥ sadā iti śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ sihitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre ṣaṭtriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

atha saptatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ 
triyugadharma prapañcaḥ
atha vakṣye laghūktena yugadharmāṃstataḥ param ।
kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaśca kaliśceti caturyugam ।।

kṛtameva ca kartavyaṃ tasmin kāle yadīpsitam ।
na tatradharmāḥsīdanti na ca kṣīyantivai prajāḥ ।।

tataḥ kṛtayugaṃ proktamanvarthena guṇena vai ।
na tasmin yugasaṃsargevyavāyo nendriyakṣayaḥ ।।

nānūyā nāpi ruditaṃ na darpo na ca paiśunam ।
na vigraho na vidveṣona mithyā nāpi vañcanam ।।

na bhayaṃ na ca santāpo na lobho na ca mānitā ।
tadā jyotiḥparaṃ brahma vaikhānasamanāmayam ।।

yā gatir yogināmekā hyapunarbhavakāṅkṣiṇām ।
viṣṇussarvātmako devaḥ śuklo nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।

antaryāmiṇi tasmiṃstu sarvalokamaye harau ।
svayaṃ śuklatvamāpanne sarvamacchaṃ bhaviṣyati ।।

brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāśśūdrāśca bhagavatparāḥ ।
svakarmaniratāssarvebhavanti manujāḥ kṛte ।।

samāśramaṃ samācāraṃ satyabhūtaṃ taporatam ।
vijñānabharitaṃ sarvaṃ jagadbhavati santatam ।।

eka vedasamāyuktā ekadharmavidhikriyāḥ ।
pṛthagdharmāstveka vedā dharmamekamanuvratāḥ ।।

caturāśramayustena karmaṇā kālayoginā ।
akāmabhalasaṃyogāḥ prāpnuvanti parāṃ gatim ।।

kṛte yuge catuṣpādaścāturvarṇyasya śāśvataḥ ।
etatkṛtayugaṃ nāma traiguṇyaguṇavarjitam ।।

tatastretāyugaṃ nāma yatra dharmastrī pādbhavet ।
raktatāṃ tu samabhyeti harirnārāyaṇaḥ prabhuḥ ।।

satyapravṛttāśca narāḥ dānadharmaparāyaṇāḥ ।
yajante vividhairyajñairnārāyaṇamanāmayam ।।

brāhmaṇādyāssvadharmeṣu pravartante nirantaram ।
yato dharmapade vṛddhā dvāparaṃ pratipedare ।।

yugaṃ saṃśīnadharmatvāddvāparaṃ paricakṣate ।
viṣṇuḥ pītatvamabhyeti vedaścāpi vibhajyate ।।

dvipādbhavati vaidharmo dvāpare samupasthite ।
dvivedāścaikavedāśca nirvedāśca tathā pare ।।

vibhinnaśāstraniṣṭhāśca bhavanti vividhakriyāḥ ।
prajā dānaparā bhūtvā dānaṃ śaṃsanti santatam ।।

rājasaṃ bhāvamāśritya rājasī bhavati prajā ।
sattvātpracyavamānānāṃ vyādhayo bhṛśadāruṇāḥ ।।

atyāhitāni cānyāni bhaveṣyantyadharottaram ।
kālasya hrasvatāyogāccaturthaṃ syādyugaṃ kaliḥ ।।

pratyakṣarūpadhṛgdevo na kalau dṛśyate yataḥ ।
kṛtādiṣviva tenaiva triyugaḥ kalirucyate ।।

padenaikena vai dharmaḥ pravarteta kalau yuge ।
tasmiṃstu samanuprāpte na dharmassaṃpravartate ।।

tāmasaṃ yugamāsādya hariḥ kṛṣṇatvameti ca ।
yaḥ kaścidatra dharmātmā kriyoyogarato bhavet ।।

naraṃ dharmaparaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve asūyāṃ prakurvate ।
varṇāśramāśritācārāḥ praṇaśyantina saṃśayaḥ ।।

vratācārāḥ praṇaśyanti dhyānayajñādayastathā ।
upadravā janiṣyanti hyadharmasya pravartanāt ।।

asūyāniratāssarve daṃbhācāraparāyaṇāḥ ।
prajāścālpāyuṣassarve bhaviṣyantikalau yuge ।।

sarvedharmāḥ praṇaśyanti kṛṣṇe kṛṣmatvamāgate ।
yasmātkalirmahāghorassarvapāpasya sādhakaḥ ।।

brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāśśūdrā dharmaparāṅmukhāḥ ।
ghore kaliyuge prāpte dvijā vedaparāṅmukhāḥ ।।

vyājadharmaparāssarve vṛdhāhaṅkāra dūṣitāḥ ।
sarvamākṣipyate nityaṃ naraiḥ paṇḍitamānibhiḥ ।।

ahamevādhika iti sarvo vivadate janaḥ ।
adharmalolupāssarve tathā caiva dvijātayaḥ ।।

atastvalpāyuṣassarve bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।
alpāyuṣṭvānmanuṣyāṇāṃ na vidyāgrahaṇaṃ bhavet ।।

vidyāgrahaṇaśūnyatvādadharmassaṃpravartate ।
vyutkrameṇa prajāssarvā mriyante pāpatarparāḥ ।।

brāhmaṇādyāstathā varṇāssaṃkīryante parasbaram ।
kāmakrodhaparā mūḍhā vṛdhāhaṃ kārapūritāḥ ।।

baddhavairā bhaviṣyanti parasparavadhepsavaḥ ।
janāssarve dayāhīnā dākṣiṇya parivarjitā ।।

śūdratulyā bhaviṣyanti tapassatyavivarjitāḥ ।
uttamā nīcatāṃ yānti nīcāścottamatāṃ tathā ।।

rājāno dravyaniratā lobhamohaparāyaṇāḥ ।
dharmakañcukasaṃvītā dharmavidhvaṃsakāriṇaḥ ।।

yo yo aśvarathanāgāḍhyassa sa rājā bhaviṣyati ।
kiṅkarāśca bhaviṣyanti śūdrāṇāṃ cadvijātayaḥ ।।

mlecchāśca yunādyāśca pālayanti vasuṃdharām ।
anāvṛṣṭibhayātprāyo gaganādattacakṣuṣaḥ ।।

bhaviṣyanti narāssarve sadā kṣudbhayakātarāḥ ।
kalau narābhaviṣyanti svalpabhāgyā bahuprajāḥ ।।

pativākyamanādṛtya sadānyagṛhatatparāḥ ।
duśśīlā duṣṭaśīleṣu kariṣyanti spṛhāṃ striyaḥ ।।

paruṣānṛtabhāṣiṇyo dehasaṃskāra varjitāḥ ।
vācālāśca bhaviṣyantikalau prāpte sadā striyaḥ ।।

nagareṣu ca grāmeṣu prākārāṭṭādikān janāḥ ।
corādibhayabhītāśca kāṣṭhayantrāṇi kurvate ।।

durbhikṣakarapīḍābhiratīvopadrutā janāḥ ।
godhūmānnayavānnāḍhyān deśān prāpsyanti duḥkhitāḥ ।।

svakāryasiddhiparyantaṃ snihyantyanyeṣu mānavāḥ ।
bhikṣavaścāpi mitrādisnehasaṃbandhayantritāḥ ।।

annopādhinimittena śiṣyān gṛhṇanti sarvataḥ ।
ubhābhyāmapi hastābhyāṃ śiraḥkaṇḍūyanaṃ striyaḥ ।।

kurvantyo bhartṛmukhyānāmājñāṃ bhetsyantyānādṛtāḥ ।
pāṣaṇḍālāpaniratāḥ pāṣaṇḍijanasaṃginaḥ ।।

bhaviṣyanti yadā viprā stadā vṛddhimiyātkaliḥ ।
alpodakāstathā meghā alpasasyā vasuṃdharā ।।

alpakṣīrāstathā gāvaḥ kṣīrātsarpirna jāyate ।
ekavarṇā bhaviṣyanti varṇāścatvāra eva ca ।।

nāsti varṇāntaraṃ tatralayaṃ yāsyanti mānavāḥ ।
santassīdantyasantaśca vilasantisamantataḥ ।।

maitrī parajane bhūyādvairaṃ ca svajane bhavet ।
putrāḥ pitṛṣu jīvatsu mriyante ca tadagrataḥ ।।

kalau kākiṇike apyarthe vigṛhya tyaktasauhṛdāḥ ।
tyakṣyantihi priyān prāṇān haniṣyanti svabāndhavān ।।

pāṣaṇḍapracuredharme dasyuprāyeṣu rājasu ।
cauryānṛtavṛdhāhiṃsānānāvṛttiṣu vai nṛṣu ।।

śūdraprāyeṣu varṇeṣu chāgaprāyeṣu goṣu ca ।
kariṣyanti tathā śūdrāḥ pravrajyāliṅginau'dhamāḥ ।।

kāṣāyaparinītāśca jaṭilā bhakmadhūsarāḥ ।
aśaucāvakramatayaḥ parapākānnajīvinaḥ ।।

devadvijanivāseṣu pūjāmicchanti pāpinaḥ ।
bhaviṣyanti durātmānaḥ śūdrāḥ pravrajitās tathā ।।

utkoca jīvinastatra mahāpāparatāstathā ।
bhaviṣyantyatha pāṣaṇḍāḥ kāpālā bhikṣavodhamāḥ ।।

dharmavidhvaṃsaśīlānāṃ dvijanāṃ rājavallabhāḥ ।
śūdrā dharmān pravakṣyanti pravrajyāliṅgino adhamāḥ ।।

gītavādyaparā viprā vedavādaparāṅmukhāḥ ।
bhaviṣyanti kalau prāpte śūdramārga pravartinaḥ ।।

hartāro na ca dātārobhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।
viśvāsahīnāḥ piśunā vedadevadvijātiṣu ।।

asaṃskṛto ktivaktāro rāgadveṣaparāstathā ।
paramāyuścateṣāṃ syāttadā varṣāṇi ṣoḍaśa ।।

pañcame vāthaḥvaṣṭhe vā varṣekanyā prasūyate ।
sartpavarṣāṣṭavarṣāśca prasūyante tathā narāḥ ।।

svakarmatyāginassarve kṛtaghnā bhinnavṛttayaḥ ।
yācakāḥ piśunāścaiva bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।।

parāvamānaniratā ātmastutiparāyaṇāḥ ।
parasvaharaṇopāyacintakāḥ sarvadā narāḥ ।।

nindāṃ kurvanti satataṃ pitṛmātṛkuleṣu tu ।
vadanti vācā dharmāṃśca cetasā pāpalolupāḥ ।।

chādayanti prayatnena svadoṣaṃ pāpakarmajam ।
apāpe duṣkṛtaṃ samyagvivṛṇvanti narādhamāḥ ।।

dharmamārgapravaktāraṃ tiraskurvanti pāpinaḥ ।
bhaviṣyanti kalau prāpti rājāno mlecchajātayaḥ ।।

dvijāśca kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥ śūdrāścānyāśca jātayaḥ ।
atyantakāminassarve saṃkīryante parasparam ।।

na śiṣyo na guruḥ kaścinna putro na tathā pitā ।
na bhāryā na patistatra bhavitā sarvasaṃkaraḥ ।।

kalau ca te bhaviṣyanti dhanāḍhyā api yācakāḥ ।
rasavikrayiṇaścāpi bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।।

dharmapatnīṣu yacchanti patayo jāralakṣaṇam ।
dviṣyanti pitaraṃ putrā guruṃ śiṣyādviṣanti ca ।।

patiṃ ca vanitā dveṣṭi kalau prāptena saṃśayaḥ ।
lobhābhibhūtamanasassarve duṣkarmaśālinaḥ ।।

parānnalolupā nityaṃ bhaviṣyanti dvijātayaḥ ।
parastrīniratāssarve paradravyaparāyaṇāḥ ।।

martyāmiṣeṇa jīvanti duhantaścāpyajāvikān ।
sarittīreṣu kuddālairopayiṣyanti cauṣadhīḥ ।।

atyalpāni phalānyāsāṃ bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।
veśyālāvaṇyaśīleṣu spṛhāṃ kurvanti yoṣitaḥ ।।

dharmavighnā bhaviṣyanti striyaśca puruṣeṣu ca ।
na kanyāṃ yācate kaścinna ca kanyāprado naraḥ ।।

kanyā varāṃśca chandena grahīṣṭanti parasparam ।
prāyaśaḥ kṛpaṇānāṃ ca bandhūnāṃ ca tadhā dvijāḥ ।।

sādhūnāṃ vividhānāṃ ca vittānyapaharanti ca ।
na yakṣyanti na hoṣyantina tapasyanti vai janāḥ ।।

naiva dāsyanti dānādi nār'cayiṣyanti vā harim ।
na dharme niviśiṣyanti hetuvādakathāśrayāḥ ।।

apātreṣveva dānāni kurvanti ca tathā narāḥ ।
kṣīropādhinimittena goṣu prītiṃ prakurvate ।।

na kurvanti tathā viprāḥ snānaśaucādikāḥ kriyāḥ ।
akālakarmaniratāḥ kūṭayuktiviśāradāḥ ।।

devanindāparāścaiva vipranindāparāstathā ।
tyaktapuṇḍraśikhāsūtrāścariṣyantidvijātayaḥ ।।

viṣṇubhaktiparaṃ na syānmanaḥ kasyāpi jātu cit ।
devapūjāparaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarve parihasanti ca ।।

śāstroditāśca ye devāḥparivārā madhudviṣaḥ ।
tān parityajya mohena narāḥ kālabalātkṛtāḥ ।।

hetuvādaparān devān kariṣyantyaparāṃ stadā ।
nirbadhnanti dvijāneva karārthaṃ rājakiṅkarāḥ ।।

nādriyante dvijānanye kalau pāpasamākule ।
dānayajña japādīnāṃ vikrīṇante phalaṃ dvijāḥ ।।

pratigrahaṃ ca kurvante caṇḍālāderapi dvijāḥ ।
śūdrastrīmaṅganiratā vidhavāsaṃgalolupāḥ ।।

rajassvalānāṃ voḍhāro bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।
śūdrānna pānaniratāḥ śūdraprāyā bhavanti ca ।।

aṭṭaśūlājanapadāḥ śivaśūlāścatuṣpathāḥ ।
pramadāḥ keśaśūlinyo bhaviṣyanti kalau yuge ।।

kuhakāśca janāstatra hetuvādaviśāradāḥ ।
pāṣaṇḍino bhaviṣyanti tiṣṭantyāśramanindakāḥ ।।

na ca dvijātiśuśrūṣāṃ sarvadharmanivartinīm ।
gṛhaprāyeṣvāśrameṣu yogiprāyeṣu bandhuṣu ।।

tataśchānudinaṃ dharmassatyaṃ śaucaṃ dayā kṣamā ।
kālena balinā sarvaṃ naśyatyāyurbalaṃ smṛtiḥ ।।

vīttameva kalau nṝṇāṃ janmācāraguṇodayam ।
dāṃpatye abhirucirheturmāyaiva vyavahārake ।।

dharmanyāyavyavasthānāṃ kāraṇaṃ balameva hi ।
strītvamevopabhoge svādvipratve sūtrameva hi ।।

liṅgamevāśramakhyātāvanyāyo vṛttikāraṇam ।
avṛttau cāpi daurbalyaṃ pāṇḍitye cāphalaṃ vacaḥ ।।

svīkāra eva codvāhe snānamevāśucau smṛtam ।
udaraṃbharitā svārthesatyatve dhārṣṭyameva hi ।।

dākṣye kuṭuṃbabharaṇe yaśorthe dharmasevanam ।
itthaṃ kaliyuge prāpte dharmassarvo api jīryate ।।

yadā māyānṛtaṃ tandrā nidrā hiṃsā viṣāyanam ।
śoko moho bhayaṃ dainyaṃ sa kalistāmasaḥsmṛtaḥ ।।

yadāyadā satāṃ hānirvaidikānāṃ dvijanmanām ।
tadā tadā kaliṃprāptamavabuddhyeta paṇḍitaḥ ।।

aho duḥkhamahoduḥkhamahoduḥkhamaho mahat ।
svarūpamatibhīmasya saṃsārasya sudurbharam ।।

viṇmūtrapūyakalite garbhavāse nipīḍanāt ।
aśucāvatibhībhatse duḥkhamatyantadussaham ।।

duḥkhaṃ ca jāyamānānāṃ gātrabhaṅgādipīḍane ।
vātena preryamāṇānāṃ mūrchanāyātibhītidam ।।

bālake nirvivekānāṃ bhūtadaivātmasaṃbhavam ।
yauvane vārdhake caiva maraṇe cāti dāruṇe ।।

ekauttaraṃ mṛtyuśataṃ dehe jñeyaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।
tatraikaḥ kālasaṃjñaḥ syāccheṣāstvāgantukāḥsmṛtāḥ ।।

ye cātrāgantukāḥ proktāste tu śāmyanti bheṣajaiḥ ।
japahomapradānaiśca kālamṛtyurna śāmyati ।।

vividhā vyādhayaśśastraṃ sarpādyāḥ prāṇinas tathā ।
viṣāṇi cābhicārāśca mṛtyordvārāṇi dehinām ।।

nauṣadhaṃ na tapo dānaṃ na mantrāna ca bāndhavāḥ ।
śaknuvanti naraṃ trātuṃ kālamṛtyuprapīḍitam ।।

rasāyanatapojapyayogasiddhairmahātmabhiḥ ।
kālamṛtyurapi prāpto jīyate analasairnaraiḥ ।।

nāsti mṛtyusamaṃ duḥkhaṃ nāsti mṛtyusamaṃ bhayam ।
sadbhāryāṃ putramitrāṇi rājyaiśvaryasukhāni ca ।।

ābaddhāni ca vairāṇi mṛtyussarvaṃ vināśayet ।
yadduḥkhaṃ maraṇe jantorna tasyeha samaṃ kvacit ।।

maṇḍūka iva sarpeṇa grasyate mṛtyunā jagat ।
bāndhavaiśca pariṣvaktaḥ priyaiśca parivāritaḥ ।।

niśśvapan dīrghamuṣṇaṃ ca mukhena pariśuṣyatā ।
caturṣvanteṣu khaṭvāyāḥ parivṛtya mūhurmuhuḥ ।।

sammūḍhaḥ kṣipate atyardhaṃ hastapādamitastataḥ ।
khaṭvāyā vāñchate bhūmiṃ bhūmeḥ khaṭvāṃ tato mahīm ।।

vivastrastyaktalajjaśca mūtraviṣṭhāpariplutaḥ ।
yācamānaśca salilaṃ śuṣkakaṇṭhāsyatālukaḥ ।।

cintayānaścavittāni kasyaitānimṛtemayi ।
nakhāgraiśca spṛśan bhūmiṃ kālapāśena karṣitaḥ ।।

mriyate paśyatāmeva gale khurakhurāyate ।
jīvastṛṇajalūkāvaddehāddehaṃ viśedasau ।।

saṃprāpyottaravaṃśe ca tanuṃ tyajati paurvikīm ।
dehabhedena yaḥ puṃsāṃ viyogaḥ karmasaṃkṣayāt ।।

maraṇaṃ tadvinirdiṣṭaṃ na nāśaḥ paramārthataḥ ।
jāyate mriyate caivaṃ karmabhiḥ svayamārjitaiḥ ।।

śītoṣṇatṛṣṇākṣudrograjvarādiparivāritaḥ ।
sarvadaivapumānāste yāvajjanmānta saṃsthitiḥ ।।

duḥkhātiśayabhūtaṃ hi yadante nāsukhaṃ nṛṇām ।
tasyopamānaṃ naivāsti kāryeṇaivānu mīyate ।।

kṛṣyamāṇasya puruṣairyadyamasyātidussaham ।
duḥkhaṃ tatsaṃsmṛtiṃ prāptaṃ karoti mama vepathum ।।

tataścaiva punastasya yonisaṃkramaṇe ca yat ।
garbhasthasya ca yadduḥkhamatidussahamulbaṇam ।।

punaśca jāyamānasya bālyayauvanajaṃ ca yat ।
duḥkhānyetānyanantāni saṃsārāntaravartibhiḥ ।।

puruṣairanubhūyante sukhabhrāntivimohitaiḥ ।
na vai sukhakalā kācidatrāstyatyantaduḥkhade ।।

saṃsārasaṃkaṭe saṃgamupetānāṃ kadā cana ।
viṣayāsaktamanasassatataṃ pāmarā janāḥ ।।

na matiṃ kurvate viṣṇau sarvalokeśvareśvare ।
athāpi nātra bibhyanti vaiṣṇavā bhagavatpriyāḥ ।।

viṣṇudhyānaparāssanto viṣvarcanaparāyaṇāḥ ।
te viṣṇusadṛśā jñeyā na hi tān bādhate kaliḥ ।।

māyeyaṃ vaiṣṇavī bhūyaḥ pātayetprāṇinastadā ।
dustarāpi bhavetsādhyā yairnyastaṃ mādhavemanaḥ ।।

asaṃtyajya ca gārhasthyamataptvā catathā tapaḥ ।
chinatti vaiṣṇavīṃ māyāṃ keśavārādhane rataḥ ।।

viṣayānavirodhena sevamāno api mādhavam ।
arcayānastarantyenāṃ viṣṇumāyāṃ duratyayām ।।

yata evamato labdhvāśarīraṃ karmasādhanam ।
śubhaṃ karmaiva kartadyaṃ tatprasādāya mānavaiḥ, ।।

prasādite asmin sarveṣāṃ svavarṇāśramakarmabhiḥ ।
sarvehastagatāḥ kāmā muktiścānte karasthitā ।।

kāryārthā mūrtayastasya lokakalyāṇakārakāḥ ।
atassākārameveṣṭvā bhaktyemaṃ siddhimāpnuyāt ।।

idaṃ ca śāstramālaṃbya pūjayedviṣṇumavyayam ।
yaddhyānaṃ kevalaṃ proktaṃ śāstre kvacidanāśrayam ।।

na tatrendriyadaurbalyātkarmasthasyādhikāritā ।
yathā giritaṭāgrasthavanaspatiphalecchayā ।।

upāye vartate aśrāntastathāsau yatnamācaret ।
sarvatra kramavān yatnaḥkāryo naicchaiva kevalā ।।

tatkāyavāṅmanoyogaiḥkramādicchetparāṃ gatim ।
nirākāretu yā bhaktyā pūjeṣṭā dhyānameva vā ।।

ramaṇīyamivābhāti tadanarthasya kāraṇam ।
sthūlabhāvaprasaṃdīni janmanāsyendriyāṇi tu ।।

sūkṣmāccha na prapadyante cirācca kimutācirāt ।
na ca rūpaṃ vinā dovo dhyātuṃ kenāpi śakyate ।।

sarvarūpanivṛttā hi buddhiḥ kutrāsya tiṣṭhati ।
nivṛttāglāyate buddhirnidrayāhi parīyate ।।

tasmādvidvānupāsīta buddhyā sākālameva tam ।
astitasya parokṣaṃ taditi kiñcidanusmaret ।।

sarvadhākāramuddiṣṭaṃ na parityajya paṇḍitaḥ ।
paraṃ devamupāsīta muktaye vā phalāyavā ।।

bhaktyākṛtenārcanena tuṣṭodevaḥ prajāpateḥ ।
pūjādyanugrahāyā adāvāvirbhūtaścaturbhujaḥ ।।

tasmāttenaiva rūpeṇa hriyā lakṣmyā samāyutaḥ ।
dhyeyassevyor'caniyaśca sadā nārāyaṇo budhaiḥ ।।

sākāre asmin kṛtā pūjā stutirvā dhyānameva vā ।
vidhinā śāstradṛṣṭena tasminneva kṛtā bhavet ।।

tadevārādhanaṃ viṣṇoravajñātaṃ viśeṣataḥ ।
khyāpanārthaṃ kalau kaścidbhaviṣyati mahāmatiḥ ।।

dharmaglāniradharmasya vṛddhiryāvadbhaviṣyati ।
tāvavbhartā mahāviṣṇuḥ sṛjatyātmānamātmanā ।।

śrīnivāse janāvāne śrīnivāsaḥ svayaṃ hariḥ ।
śrīnivāsassamākhyāto bhūmāvavatariṣyati ।।

utpatsyamāna evāsau bhrājamānassvatejasā ।
jagadāvaraṇaṃ krūraṃ tamaḥ puñjaṃ haniṣyati ।।

pañcahāyana evātha prāptasarvakalākulaḥ ।
saṃskṛto akhilasaṃskārair brahmavarcasasevitaḥ ।।

sarvalokeśvaraṃ devaṃ śrīnivākaṃ śriyaḥ patim ।
caturbhujamudārāṅgaṃ divyābharaṇabhūṣitam ।।

śrīvatsāṃkaṃ mahābāhuṃ śaṅkhacakragadādharam ।
kirīṭamukuṭopetaṃ varadābhayacihnitam ।।

haimordhvapuṇḍralāvaṇyalasadvadanapaṅkajam ।
vaikhānasairmahābhāgairarcyamānaṃ nirantaram ।।

kṛtāspadaṃ kaliyuge tadīyaṃ kuladaivatam ।
"arāyi kāṇa'' ityādyaiśśrutivākyairabhiṣṭutam ।।

"rayiḥ kakudmā''nityādyairmantrairvaikhānasaiḥ paraiḥ ।
ijyamānaṃ viśeṣeṇa vividhaiḥ pāramātmikaiḥ ।।

kalyāṇaguṇasaṃpūrṇaṃ divyamaṅgalavigraham ।
svayaṃvyaktaṃ parañjyotiḥ paraṃ brahma parātparam ।।

vidhinā śāstradṛṣṭena devamārādhayiṣyati ।
prasādasumukho devassvātmabhūte śiśau svayam ।।

avanamya ca mūrdhānaṃ gṛhīṣyati gale srajam ।
divyaiḥprasannairgrathitāṃ kusumaistulasīdalaiḥ ।।

svayaṃ sārdhaṃ kumāreṇa havīṃṣi ca bhujiṣyati ।
saṃtuṣṭena kumāreṇa prārthitaḥ karuṇānidhiḥ ।।

vaikhānasairmahābhāgairupetaiḥ saha mandire ।
havīṃṣyaśiṣyatyadhyakṣaṃ kumāraṃ sāntvayiṣyati ।।

arcāvatāramahātmyaṃ lokebhyaḥkhyāpayiṣyati ।
devor'cakaparādhīnaḥ sarvaṃ tebhyaḥ kariṣyati ।।

tathā sammānitaḥ premṇā śrīnivāsena sādaram ।
yajñairbahuvidhair anyairyajñeśaṃ saṃyajiṣyati ।।

viśāle bahusaṃskārasaṃkule vasudhātale ।
sthāpayiṣyati viṣṇvarcāṃ grāme grāme gṛhe gṛhe ।।

purāṇi ca janāvāsā gṛhāṇi gṛhiṇāṃ tathā ।
mandirairindireśasya sundarairnatibhandhuraiḥ ।।

maṇḍitāni bhaviṣyanti jagattattvaṃ bhajiṣyati ।
ita ācārya nirdeśa itaśśiṣyopasarpaṇam ।।

ihaiva gṛhiṇāṃ bhūyaḥ prasaṃga iha mantraṇam ।
acāryavaraṇaṃ ceha śilpināmiha mārgaṇam ।।

iha prastarasaṃgrāha iha dārugrahastathā ।
iha diksāthanaṃ caiha vasudhāsaṃparīkṣaṇam ।।

ito maṅgalaghoṣaśca itaḥpuṇyāhavācanam ।
ita ādyeṣṭakānyāsa ito mūrdheṣṭakāvidhiḥ ।।

itaśśūlagrahaśceta ito vairajjubandhanam ।
itaśca mṛtsnāsaṃskāra ito varṇavilekhanam ।।

ito madhūcchiṣṭavidhirito alaṅkārakalpanam ।
ito dhvajasya nirmāṇamito bhaktasamāgamaḥ ।।

itaḥpratiṣṭhāsaṃkalpa nāto nayanamokṣaṇam ।
ito adhivāsanaṃ ceto prabhūtabalidāpanam ।।

ito agnimanthanaṃ ceto homa ānandavardhanaḥ ।
iha gītaṃ nṛttamiha vādyaṃ śrutimanoharam ।।

iha pratiṣṭhā devasya iha ca dvijabhojanam ।
iha kālotsavaśceha dhanuṣi prātarutsavaḥ ।।

mudgānnasya guḍānnasya prasādasya nivedanam ।
adyottiṣṭhati vaikuṇṭhaḥ śayitaḥ kṣīrasāgare? ।।

adya vratasyāpavargo saṃśitassa bhuvo hareḥ ।
adya vaivāhikaṃ devyāvratānte lokamaṅgalam ।।

adya pauṣī pūrṇimāhocādya caikādaśī śubhā ।
adya devasya kuryanti snapanaṃ kalaśaiśśataiḥ ।।

adya dāśarathirjāto dvādaśī māghasaṃbhavā ।
adya cātā jaganmātā phālgune revatī tithau ।।

adyakurvanti devasya damanotsavamīśvarāḥ ।
caitramāsasta devasya mahāprītikaraḥ kila ।।

kurvanti manujādhīśā vasante divyamutsavam ।
jalakrīḍotsavo hyadya caitrayātrā hareḥkvacit ।।

ketakīmālatījātīmallikādolikotsavaḥ ।
gandhotsavo adya kriyate paurṇamāsī kadā dinam ।।

kadā caikādaśī puṇyā kadā vā dvādaśītidhiḥ ।
kadā nṛsiṃhassaṃjātaḥ smṛtamadyatrayodaśī ।।

vaiśākhe śuklapakṣe tu kriyate vārṣikotsavaḥ ।
kadā bhavetpaurṇamāsī kriyate candrikotsavaḥ ।।

kadā jyeṣṭhotsavo bhūyātkadā vā pūrṇimā śubhā ।
prapotsavaḥ kadā bhūyādāṣāḍhī ca bhaviṣyati ।।

kadā ca śravaṇaṃ bhūyānnakṣatraṃ yatra mārutiḥ ।
rāmasevādhuraṃ dhṛtvā jātassākṣānmahāmatiḥ ।।

kadā ca śrāvaṇī bhūyādyatra nārāyaṇo hariḥ ।
svātmānaṃ janayāmāsa lokakalyāṇahetave ।।

vaikhānasaṃ vikhanasaṃ viriñcamiti yaṃ viduḥ ।
kadā bhādrapado māsastatra caikādaśī bhavet ।।

kadā vā dvādaśī bhūyātsarvapāpa praṇāśinī ।
tiladhenuṃ pradāsyanti yatra devasya sannidhau ।।

kadāśvino bhavenmāsastatrāpi daśamī śubhā ।
aśvayātrā harerbhūyādanuyāsyāmahe harim ।।

kadā bhavedamāvāsyā yasyāṃ sa narakohataḥ ।
kadā vā kārtikomāso bhaviṣyati haripriyaḥ ।।

dīpāropo bhavettatra kadā vā kārtikī śubhā ।
kadāyugādaya stadvatpuṇyakālā viśeṣataḥ ।।

kadā bhaviṣyati hare rathayātrā mahātmanaḥ ।
kadā vā gajayātrā syātkadā vīśādhirohaṇam ।।

kadā bhramati deveśo grāmavīthiṣu sundaram ।
kadā labhiṣṭati harestīrthaṃ paramapāvanam ।।

kadā prasādaṃ devasya kaṇasyāpi labhiṣyati ।
kadā śaṅkharathāṅgādidivyalāñchanalāñchitā ।।

pādukā devadevasya saṃskariṣyati me śiraḥ ।
kadā vā tulasīṃ puṇyāmarpitāṃ tasya pādayoḥ ।।

aśnāmi śirasā caiva dhārayiṣyāmi vaiṣṇavīm ।
kadā vā puṇyapuṣpāṇāmekaṃ devasamarpitam ।।

śirasā dhārayiṣyāmi jighrāmi bhahugandhavat ।
devadevasya drakṣyāmi kadā sarvāṅgasuṃdaram ।।

āpādamauliparyantaṃ lāvaṇyamadhuraṃ vapuḥ ।
ityādikāḥ kathāstatra bhaviṣyanti prajāsu ca ।।

sarve dharmaparāssarve nārāyaṇa parāyaṇāḥ ।
arcane vāsudevasya bhaviṣyanti ratā narāḥ ।।

ityeva kālaṃ kāleyaṃ gururujjīvayiṣyati ।
śrīnivāsaṃ śriyovāsamarciṣyati ciraṃ bhuvi ।।

pāṣaṇḍopaplutaṃ dharmamuddhariṣyati vaiṣṇavam ।
idaṃ ca bhagavacchāstraṃ cirasthāyi kariṣyati ।।

sarvatantrasvatantro asau bahūn grandhān praṇeṣyati ।
asaṃkhyebhyaśca śiṣyebhyastattārthamupadekṣyati ।।

dharmavyavasthāṃ kṛtvaivaṃ kalāvatibhayaṅkare ।
sameṣyati paraṃ sthānaṃ tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।।

yugānte ca punarnāmaharernaiko gṛhīṣyati ।
tadā harirmahāvīraḥ kalkī nāma bhaviṣyati ।।

adharmanidhanaṃ kṛtvā dharmaṃ saṃsthāpayiṣyati ।
harerdivyāvatārāṇāmavatārakathāmimām ।।

yaḥ paṭhec chruṇuyādvāpi so api yāsyati sadgatim ।
dhanyāste puruṣaśreṣṭhā durante bhavasāgare ।।

ye nāmāpi kalau viṣṇossmariṣyintyavyayātmavaḥ ।
dhyāyan kṛtayuge viṣṇuṃ tretāyāṃ dāpare yajan ।।

yattatphalamavāpnoti kalau smaraṇamātrataḥ ।
harerharati pāpāni nāmasaṃkīrtitaṃ sakṛt ।।

pāṣaṇḍabahule loke kalāvatibhayaṅkare ।
tannāmakīrtayedyastu taṃ vidyātkṛtināṃ varam ।।

tasmātsarvaprayatnena bhaktyā paramayā yutaḥ ।
samūrtārādhanaṃ kuryānnānyathā muktimāpnuyāt ।।

nāthamādyaistu navabhiradhyāyairīḍyate kramāt ।
bhūparīkṣādikarmāṇi vimānānāṃ ca kalpanam ।।

vividhānāṃ ca berāṇāṃ nirmāṇavidhivistaraḥ ।
daśame nāṃkurāropaḥ paścāddvābhyāmudīritaḥ ।।

pratiṣṭhā vidhiratyanta phalado jagataḥ pateḥ ।
paścāddaśāvatārāṇāṃ caturbhiḥ procyate vidhiḥ ।।

tathā saptadaśe cokta ādimūrti vidhistataḥ ।
aṣṭādaśer'canaṃ sāṃgamuktaṃ madhuvidāriṇaḥ ।।

dvābhyāmuktastato pūjādravya saṃgrahaṇa kramaḥ ।
ekaviṃśe viśeṣārcāvidhissamyagudīritaḥ ।।

dvāviṃśesnapanaṃ coktaṃ trayoviṃśe viśeṣataḥ ।
vidhirutsavacakrasya prokto dvābhyāmathotsavaḥ ।।

tataśca ṣaḍbhiradhyāyaiḥ prāyaścittasya vistaraḥ ।
proktastataśca dvātriṃśe saṃkīrṇaṃśā udīritāḥ ।।

arcāvatāramahimā trayastriṃśe prakīrtitaḥ ।
svayaṃvyaktādibhedaśca catustriṃśe prakāśitaḥ ।।

pañcatriṃśe tu saṃproktaṃ kriyāyogāśritaṃ phalam ।
ṣaṭtriṃśetvapacārāśca kathitā devakopanāḥ ।।

kalidharmāśca saṃproktāssaptatriṃśe viśeṣataḥ ।
saptatriṃśadbhiradhyāyairevaṃ gurukṛpābalāt ।।
ṣaḍbhiḥ sahasraiḥ ślokaistu kriyāṅgamupavarṇitam ।।
ityārṣe śrīvaikhānase bhagavacchāstre bhṛguproktāyāṃ caturviṃśatsahānrikāyāṃ sahitāyāṃ prakīrṇādhikāre saptatriṃśo adhyāyaḥ

iti śrīmati prakīrṇādhikāre kriyāpādaḥ śrī vikhanasamahāgurave namaḥ śrautasmārtādikaṃ karma nikhilaṃ yena sūtritam tasmai samastavedārthavide vikhanase namaḥ jayatyātmeśvarosni dradhyāna saudhapriyātithiḥ śrīmatpatrapurīvāsaḥ śrīrāmassītayā gṛhī śrīrāmacandrāya namaḥ
